<1>
{1.1}
<prathamaḥ pādaḥ — pakṣadharmādhikāraḥ>
[1,1]
namo buddhāya ||
[1,2]
ādityabandhoḥ kiraṇairivānyairātanyamāne kṣaṇabhāji loke | suptā ivāniṣṭavilāpino'tastalaprahārādiva cetayadhvam || 1 ||
[1,3]
yat sat tat kṣaṇikaṃ yathā jaladharaḥ santastu bhāvā ime sattā śaktirihārthakarmaṇi miteḥ siddheṣu siddhā na sā | nāpyekaiva vidhānyadāpi parakṛnnaiva kriyā vā bhaved dvedhāpi kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃgatirataḥ sādhye ca viśrāsyati || 2 ||
[1,4]
atra prathamapādopadarśitaḥ svabhāvahetuḥ | ayaṃ na tāvadasiddhaḥ | tathā hi yadi nāma pratidarśanaṃ sattvalakṣaṇabhedaḥ, tathāpi ihāthaṃkriyāsāmarthyameva sattvamabhipretaṃ hetutayopāttam |
tatra nāsaṃbhavi sarvathā śakyamabhidhātumabhimataṃ vā keṣāñcit | tallakṣaṇāsahiṣṇavo hi yadi paramavyāptamasmaddūṣaṇamabhidadhyuḥ, tatra ya evaite bhāvāḥ pramāṇasamadhigatārthakriyāviśeṣavyāpārāḥ, ta eva pakṣīkṛtā iti svarūpeṇāśrayadvāreṇa vā nāsiddhiśaṅkā | ye punararthakriyāsāmarthyasaṃbhave'pi tattvato'navadhāritatadbhāvāḥ, teṣāmidānīṃ pakṣād bahirbhāve'pi paścānnirūpayato yadyarthakriyopalambho bhaviṣyati, bhaviṣyatyevānumānāntaram | tadabhāve tu sādhyāpratipattiriṣṭaiva liṅgāntaravat |
[2,1]
nanvevamavyāpinī kṣaṇikatāsiddhiriti cet — na, yatkiñcit kadācit kvacidarthakriyāyāmupayogi, tasya sarvasya tadbhāvasādhanāyeṣṭatvācca kvacidupayoginyeva, viśeṣacintāyāḥ prakramārhatvāt | tasmānnāniṣṭarūpaparihāreṇa | na ca hetunirūpaṇāśaktau | nāpi sarvatra sādhyadharmavati dharmiṇi sakṛdanumānapravṛttivirahakṛtaṃ prādeśikatvaṃ sādhyasiddherīśvarādyanumānavat | etena niścitārthakriyāśaktayo bhāvabhedāḥ dharmiṇo'rthakriyāsāmarthyasāmānyaṃ heturiti darśitam | athavā ime pratyakṣādigocarāḥ sarva eva bhāvā dharmiṇo'rthakriyāsāmarthyaṃ hetuḥ, tatra pramāṇāviṣayasya kvacidapi vidhisādhanānumāne dharmīkartumaśakyatvāt, pramāṇaviṣaye ca sarvatrānumānapravṛtteḥ, kā aparā vyāptiḥ sādhyasiddheḥ ? pramāṇagocaratayā dharmiṇo nāśrayāsiddhiḥ sādhanasya | nāpi svarūpāsiddhiḥ, yato yeṣu tāvadavivādena bahirarthakriyopalambhaḥ, teṣu cintaiva nāsti | yeṣvapi na sākṣāt tadavadhāraṇam, tatrāpi pramāṇajananādevārthakriyāsāmarthyavyavasthāpanamanavadyam | adhyakṣe sākṣādanumāne ca kārye pāramparyeṇeti |
[2,2]
atra kecidācakṣate — yatkāryakāriṇaḥ kāraṇasya sāmarthyavyavasthāpanaṃ tasyaiva kathaṃ sattvasiddhiḥ ? tadasiddhau mūlasyāpi nārthasāmarthyam | atha yathāṅkurāpekṣayā bījasya sāmarthyam, tathā aṅkurasyāpi patrakāṇḍādyapekṣayāstu | buddherapi buddhyantarasmṛtyabhilāpapravṛttyādyapekṣayā svaparopakārādyapekṣayā veti |
[2,3]
syādetat | kevalaṃ kāryaparamparānusaraṇaparyavasānābhāve yadekamapi kiñcidarthakriyākāri kalayitvā kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanam, tanna syāt | yadeva ca kāryaṃ paryavasāne'narthakriyākāri tenaiva pūrveṣāṃ tadbhāvaprasaṅge naikamapyarthakriyāśaktaṃ siddhyatīti nāsiddhiparihāraḥ |
[2,4]
yat punaretadbhinnavyāvṛttikatayā sattāsiddhāvapi na kāryatvakṣatirityucyate, tadapi na samyak | vyāvṛttibhede'pi hi sattvasiddhau kṛtakatvasyāpi kathaṃ siddhiḥ ? abhūtvā bhavanaṃ hi kṛtakatvam, bhavanaṃ ca bhavatāmarthakriyākāritvameva | tato'rthakāritvasaṃdehe bhavatotyeva na śakyam | apekṣitaparavyāpāratvaṃ svabhāvaniṣpattau kṛtakatvamityapi nāsato dharmaḥ | sattā cārthakriyaiva | evaṃ pratyayabhede bheditvādayo'pi saddharmā na sattāniścaye'bhidhātuṃ śakyanta iti |
[3,1]
atrocyate | na tāvadaṅkurādayaḥ parito nirastavibhramāśaṅke'bhyāsaviśeṣāsāditapaṭimni pratyakṣacetasi parisphuranto na santaḥ śakyante'bhidhātumadarśane'pi phalasya | anyathā arthakriyāyāmapi na kaścidāśvāsa iti saditaravyavahāravirahānnirīhaṃ jagajjāyeta |
[3,2]
atha sattvalakṣaṇaṃ tāvad bhavatāmarthakriyāsāmarthyameveti cet ? tat kimidānīṃ samayasiddhena lakṣaṇena pratyakṣabādho'bhidheyaḥ ? tad yadi bhavato'pi lakṣaṇadoṣa evānena krameṇa vaktumiṣṭo'bhidhīyatām | asmākaṃ tu na tallakṣaṇaprasādhanāya parikarabandhaḥ, kiṃ tu tallakṣaṇena kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanāya | atastallakṣaṇānavadhāraṇaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhipratibandhamādadhīta kārye | kāryāntaradarśane tu tatrāpi tadanumānaprasavaḥ krameṇa kena vāryate ? idānīṃ tvarthakriyāsamarthasyaiva pakṣīkaraṇāt pakṣabahirbhūte sādhyasādhanayorasiddhāvapi na kaścid doṣa ityuktaprāyam |
[3,3]
tasmāt sāmayikalakṣaṇakṣatāvapi kiṃ punaraniścayamātre paṭutarapratyakṣabalāvalambitavastubhāve aṅkurādivastuni vastudharmasya kāryatvasya virodha iti | tadapekṣayā bījādikamarthakriyāsāmarthyasamarthanasahameva, kathamasiddhiḥ ?
[3,4]
nanvarthakriyāsāmarthyamitaradvā vastulakṣaṇamaspṛśatendriyajñānena kathaṃ vastutvamupasthāpitamityucyate ? tadapi yat kiñcit, anubhave pramāṇāntaracintāyā niravakāśatvāt | dṛśyate hi śāstrīyalakṣaṇānullekhepyabhyāsabhāvitapratyakṣodayamātrād vastutvamavasāya pravṛttiravisaṃvādabhāginīti kimatra kriyatām ? evaṃ tu syāt | yadi paramārthato'rthakriyāsāmarthyameva vastutvaṃ tadā idamato jāyata iti janmādhiraṇaṃ vastūllikhatā adhyakṣeṇārthakriyāsāmarthyamevollikhitam | athānyadeva vastulakṣaṇaṃ tadā tadevollikhitam | yathā triguṇamayatvamitaradvā'nullikhitā tadabahirbhūtaṃ nīlaṃ nīlagrāhiṇā gṛhītamevātatsiddhamadhyakṣeṇa vastutvamaṅkurādeḥ kāryatāsaṃvāde'pi kāryāntarādarśane'pi kāraṇasya bījāderarthasāmarthyamavasthāpayatīti | kāryavat tarhi bījādikamapi pratyakṣodayādevāstu vastusat, kimarthasāmarthyagaveṣaṇeneti cet — na vai vastuvyavahāre pratyakṣapāṭavaṃ paribhūyārthaśaktimanusarāmaḥ, tasyā api pratyakṣādhīnatvāt | kiṃ tu kṣaṇabhaṅgamaṅgīkārayitum |
pratyakṣakṛto hi vastuvyavahāra uktakrameṇa tadatallakṣaṇasādhāraṇo na kṣaṇikatvasādhanāya niyamena prabhavati | arthakriyāsāmarthyaṃ tu vastulakṣaṇamabhavadapi yatra svayaṃ vartate, tatrāvaśyaṃ tadanupanīya na svarūpasattāmāviśati | tataḥ sādhanatvenāsya prastāvo'tra na vastulakṣaṇatveneti sthitam ||
[4,1]
evaṃ jñāne'pi svarūpasaṃvedanaṃ sattvāvyabhicārīti sarvaṃ pūrvavat | tadanenāpi viṣayasya sāmarthyasiddhiravyāhateti veditavyam | pareṇa hi paravedane bhrāntiśaṅkāvakāśaḥ |
svarūpavedane punaḥ sarvathā tadabhāva eva | atha svavedane vipratipadyeta, tadaikārthasamavāyināpi jñānena vedanasvīkāre'ṅkurādivadeva pareṇāpi svarūpopadhānānna kaścid doṣaḥ | anyathā dṛṣṭārthavyavahārahāniḥ sarvathā prasajyeta |
[4,2]
nanu viṣayajñānayorhetuphalabhāva eva kathamavagantavyaḥ, upalambhāt pūrvaṃ viṣayasyānupalambhāt ? vyatirekabalāditi brūmaḥ | sati ca bāhye'rthe sthiretaratvanirṇayārambhaḥ |
tasmādarthakriyākārikadambakapakṣīkaraṇavat pramāṇagocaracakrapakṣīkaraṇe'pi nāśrayasvarūpadvārā dvividhāpyasiddhirasthirasādhanasya ||
[4,3]
athārthaśakteḥ sarvathā sūkṣmavicārāsahatvād arthaśaktaṃ sarvamiti kva pakṣīkaraṇam, kiṃ vā sādhanamiti cet — nanu bījāderaṅkurādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ, nahi dṛṣṭe anupapannaṃ nāma |
sarvasya hi vicāranāmnaḥ pramāṇasyānubhava eva sīmā | kiṃ caivamanicchan prāmāṇikaḥ kathaṃ dhūmādapi dahanamanumāsyati ? jalajvalanayorvātātapaśītārtaḥ sadṛśīṃ pravṛttimālambeta, apravṛttiṃ vā | bhavāneva kathaṃ vā mithyāśaktimāropayatā pareṇa sādhana upanyaste tadabhāvaṃ vidvānevaitatparājayāśaṃsī dūṣaṇopanyāsottarito'sti ? tatrāpyasiddhyādikameva vaktumādriyase, na tu jātyuttaram ? tadetadāyātam, nātmanāpi pratyaya iti | tasmād brūyāḥ kiñcit kenacit pratāritaḥ | durapahnavā tu śaktirartheṣu | sābhāsā cet — saṃvṛttyā, na paramārthena |
astu yathā tathā saṃvṛttyā paramārthena vā, kimatra nirbandhena ?
[5,1]
athabhāvasāṃvṛtaśaktisamanvayinī kṣaṇikatāpi sāṃvṛtī syānna pāramārthikīti matiḥ, tatrāpyucyate | iha tattvābhyāso'bhyudayaniḥśreyasaphalaheturiti nityānityādivicāramārabhante santaḥ, tadaniścaye'bhyāsānupapatteḥ | sa cābhyāso nityeśvarādidattasāhāyakastannirapekṣo vā tatphalahetuḥ syāditīdṛśi prakaraṇe pramāṇaparīkṣādakṣāṇāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgāvatāraḥ | atra yadi paramapuruṣārthasādhanamaniṣṭaparihāreṇa śaktisthitināntarīyakatayā saṃvṛtireveyam, kṣaṇikatāpi saṃvṛtirevāstu, paramapuruṣārthopayogenaiva kṣaṇikatāyāmādarāt | kimasmākaṃ paramārthacintayā, yatra na pramāṇaprameyavibhāgaḥ sādhyasādhanavyavahāro vā kaścit ? atha paramārthe'pyevaṃ saṃbhavati, tadā tadākṛṣṭaḥ śaktisambhavaḥ, tadanvayī vā kṣaṇabhaṅgo na pāramārthikatvamāpatati | pramāṇaprameyavibhāgādyabhāve tu sarvathā caitanyavyāvṛttau svacinmātravyavasthitau vā pakṣadharmatvādyabhāvaniścayakālavat kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirabhavantyapi na pīḍayati | tatra kṣaṇikatāsiddhiratāttvikīti yastrāsayati, sa svargāpavargaphalaprāptirapāramārthikīti kiṃ na trasyati ?
[5,2]
tasmād yāvat sādhyasādhanabhāvavyavahāraḥ, tāvat parīkṣākṣamamityeva pāramārthikatvam, mūladūṣaṇaṃ prati sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāsatkalpatvāditi | alamativistareṇa ||
[5,3]
etena yadasthānābhiniveśinā nyāyabhūṣaṇakāreṇa bhāṣyakārīyaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvadūṣaṇaprabandhamutthāpya varṇitam, tat sarvaṃ nirupayogamiti pratipāditam | tathāhi yadyetāvataḥ śramasyāsiddhatodbhāvanāyāmevopayogaḥ, kimanena kartavyam ? asiddhiśca parihṛtā, puruṣārthasamīhayā vastutattvanirūpaṇapravṛttasya śaktisiddhināntarīyakavyāpāratvāt | tata eva tathā kramākramābhyāṃ kāryotpattirvyāptetyetadapyasiddhamiti yaduktaṃ tadapi niravakāśam | yadapyanena tattadāśaṅkyottarābhimānāt paryante sāṃvṛtatvārthakriyāpātāt — arthakriyāsamarthaṃ yat tadatra paramārthasat | (pra0 vā0 1. 3.) ityuktivaiyarthyamudbhāvya likhitam | yathā saṃvṛtyārthakriyāsamarthaṃ, tathā tat paramārthasaditi cet — sāmānyāvayavisaṃyogādeḥ kiṃ na tathā sattvamiṣṭam ? tasya saṃvṛttyāpyasāmarthyamiti cet — na, anvayavyatirekapratibhāsasyobhayathā tulyatvāt | tathāhi yatra yatra cakṣuḥ pravartate tatra tatra taimirikakeśādivanna stambhādipratibhāso bhavatīti stambhādeḥ sāmarthyagatiḥ |
tathā mahiṣādiṣu gavādyanvayabuddhirna bhavati | paramāṇumātreṣu saṃyogādirahiteṣu cāvayavisaṃyogabuddhirna bhavatīti sāmānyāderapi sāmarthyagatiriti | tadapyasāram |
nahi saṃvṛtirityeva parigrahastyāgo vā, bālasaṃvṛterapi grahaṇaprasaṅgāt | paṇḍitasaṃvṛterapi paramapuruṣārthasādhanapravaṇāyāstyāgaprasaṅgāt | avicāritaramyā hi pratītiḥ saṃvṛtiḥ | asti ca bālakasya darpaṇatalāvalīnasatyavadanagraho vicāravidhuraḥ puruṣārthasādhanagraho vā paṇḍitānāṃ tvadvicāreṇa vidhurito na ca tyājyaḥ, tatparityāge kṣaṇabhaṅgaparīkṣānapekṣāyā iṣṭatvāt |
[6,1]
atha bauddhasyāyaṃ vicāro mama tvatrāniṣṭireva | tato bauddhasyaiva siddhāntavirodhaḥ, sādhanasya ca vādyasiddhatā doṣa iti cet — sa tāvadayaṃ vicāraḥ pramāṇam apramāṇaṃ vā ? pramāṇatve tavaivāyaṃ na mameti vibhāgānupapattiḥ | pratyuta pramāṇād bahirbhāvasvīkāre nādhikāraḥ prativāde'pi tavetyāyātam | athāpramāṇam, tadā yadi nāmāgamapradeśapratipādito'rthaḥ kaścinna samarthaḥ prakṛtasya tu na kṣatiḥ | tadetadāyātam —
[6,2]
yadi kiñcit kvacicchāstre na yuktaṃ pratiṣidhyate | bruvāṇo yuktamapyanyaditi rājakulasthitiḥ || (pra0 vā0 4. 63)
[6,3]
iti | sautrāntikasamayasthitasya hi kṣaṇabhaṅgaṃ prasādhayataḥ sthityantaravirodho na bādhakaḥ | anyathā
[6,4]
ākāśaṃ dvau nirodhau ca nityaṃ trayamasaṃskṛtam, (abhidharmakośe 2. 5)
[6,5]
ityanena kiṃ navābhidhānam ? naiyāyikasya copamānaṃ pramāṇamicchato vaiśeṣikāpekṣayā kathaṃ na siddhāntavirodhaḥ ? bhinnaprasthānatvaṃ tu samānam | śaktisaṃśrayaśca na sautrāntikanītimatikramya | yadi tu tatrāpi na syāt śaktisthitiḥ, tadā svapratibhāsamātramācaṣṭe na bauddhasiddhāntasthita iti syāt | tasmānnayāntaravirodhe'pi na siddhāntavirodhayogaḥ | nāpi vādyasiddhiḥ | na ca vastubalapravṛttānumāne śāstrānurodhaḥ kaścit |
tadvicāraprāmāṇye tu sāṃvṛtatve'pyarthaśakteravaśyābhyupagantavyatayā tadupanītakṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhibādhitanityābhimatasāmānyasamavāyādikalpanamadharasaṃvṛtitvād bālasaṃvṛtivannopādeyam arthakriyāśaktau | aśaktau svaviṣayajñānajanane'pyayogyasya sattvābhyupagamaḥ saṃvṛtirastu kiṃ tvadharato'pyadhareti niścayaḥ | ataevādharādharasaṃvṛtyapekṣayottarottarāsu paramārthatvenavyavasthāpyamānāvaśyābhyupagantavyā, niruttarārthakriyaiva saṃvṛtiḥ paramārtha iti tayā sat paramārthasaducyate | tathāhi bālasya darpaṇatale vadanagrahamapekṣyāsadeva vadanamatra khyātīti paramārtha iti ucyate | tadapekṣayā ca darpaṇapratihativyāvṛttyā netrāṃśavaḥ svamukhameva gṛhṇātīti paramārthaḥ | evamuttarottaraparikalpeṣu balavatsu pūrvapūrvaḥ saṃvṛtiruttarottaraḥ paramārtho yāvadarthakriyāsthitiḥ | tadatikrame hi grāhyagrāhakabhaṅgādāyātaṃ pratibhāsamātravyavasthānamiti kva saṃvṛtervārtā ? tasmāt saṃvṛtīnāmantimārthakriyāśaktireva paramārthaśabdavācyeti na saṃvṛtimātratvena sāmānyādisaṃvṛtistatkalām adhirohati |
tadvicāraprāmāṇyaṃ tu gajanimīlikayāvadhīrya tattvata eva śaktiḥ paramārthastatra tatrocyate, sāmānyādayaśca saṃvṛtisanta iti | evamavayavisaṃyogādayo'pi saṃvṛtisantastadvadubhayathā veditavyāḥ — śakteḥ paramārthatayā nityatābhyupagamatvāt kṣaṇasthitidharmatāyāḥ |
aṇava eva hi viśiṣṭotpannā dravyadvayaṃ vā saṃyogaśūnyaṃ tattadbuddhisādhanamiti kimavayavyādinā ? tat kathaṃ sāmānyādiparigrahaḥ saṃvṛtimātratvenārthakriyā samīkriyate |
yadi ca tāvataiva sāmyaṃ kimupapattighoṣaṇena ? mā bhūdadharasaṃvṛtitvamiti niyamopanyāsaḥ | tacca śaktisamanvayinaḥ tadādhārasya vā kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgamena durnivāram | yathoktaṃ prākśaktisamanvayābhāve tadādhārasyāpi saṃvṛtisattve kutastaddharmasya sāmānyāderadharasaṃvṛtitvaparihāraḥ ? tasmāt saṃvṛtimātratvameva sāmyam | tatra cokto doṣaḥ | yā ceyamupapattirbuddhivyatireko nāma sāpyapohe cintayiṣyate |
[8,1]
yaccedamūce — kiṃ ca yadyanirūpitatattvā pratītiḥ saṃvṛtiḥ, tata eva kāryakāraṇavyavasthitiriṣṭā, tathā satyakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ sarvavyavahāriprasiddho'nvartho jñeyaḥ, kiṃ tatra sūkṣmavicāreṇeti — tadapyayuktam | tathāhi yastāvat tattvata eva kṣaṇabhaṅgurabhāvagrāmasādhanāya sādhanamāha sautrāntikaḥ, svacinmātrāsthitau sādhanadūṣaṇāvadhānābhāvāt tasya tāttvikameva sāmarthyaṃ trividhaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhopalabhyam | kathaṃ tasyāyamupālambhaḥ ? paraviṣayapramāṇopasthāpitamanyaṃ vā parihṛtya kathamāsitumasau samarthaḥ ? tāvatā ca tāttvikī kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirakṣaṇikānāmeva kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ sāṃvṛtamupapādayati iti kimasyāṅgīkaraṇaprayāsena ? na ca vicāraḥ parisphuranneva parihartuṃ śakyaḥ, chāyādravyatādiniṣedheśvarasiddhyādiṣvapyanādaraprasaṅgāt | tadaniṣṭavādinaḥ pratītasyāpi vicārasya sūkṣmatvāditi kṛtamidānīṃ śāstraparamparāpariśrameṇa | tataśca kiṃ tatra sūkṣmavicāreṇeti vimucya vicāraścārurasau na bhavati, yenākṣaṇikakṣepa iti vaktumucitam |
tacca na pratijñāmātreṇa sidhyati | asmābhistu nityamatyetuṃ sādhanamupanyastam | na ca tatra doṣaḥ |
[8,2]
atha prastutasūkṣmavicārādare sūkṣmavicārāntarasyāpyavakāśaprasaṅgo doṣa eva |
yadāha — sūkṣmekṣikayā hi kāryakāraṇabhāvād bheda eva syāt, tvaduktāt nyāyāditi |
idamapi śraddhājaḍasyaiva śobhate | yāvaddhi bhāvānāmarthakriyāśaktiparityāgaṃ na sahāmahe tāvadavyāhataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgāṅgīkāro nityanigrahaśca | yadā tu śaktivivecanavi cārāntare ca balavati cetaḥ kramiṣyate tadā kṣaṇikatāvimokṣamapītyakṣamaḥ, samānatvāddaṇḍasya | na caivaṃ śakterupagamo nityatāmanityatāṃ ca pratyujjīvayituṃ śaknoti, asādhāraṇatvāt | tathāhi na khalu śaktiriti pramāṇaśūnyameva kiñcit kvacit kadācid astītyavimokṣaḥ | kiṃ tarhi ? etadvījādikamaṅkurādisamarthamityanenākāreṇa pratyakṣaprativedyatayaiva | tacca pratyakṣaṃ yathānvayavyatireke pramāṇamiṣṭaṃ tathā kāryāṇāṃ kramītaratvepītyevaṃ prakāreṇa nyāyena śaktiḥ kṣaṇikatāyāṃ viśrāmyantī na nityasādhāraṇīti kathamubhayorapi pratyujjīvanam ? tadevaṃ balavati hetuphalatābhraṃśaśaṃsinī vicāre śaktisiddhā kṣaṇikataivāsti | sā saṃvṛtiḥ | nityatā tvadharasaṃvṛtireveti sāmānyavad bhāvyam | tadvicārabalane tu na kiñcidāśaṃkāsthānamiti siddhaiva śaktiḥ |
[9,1]
tatkathamucyate — tathāpyasiddhatvānna sattvena kṣaṇikatvasiddhiḥ | nāpyarthakriyāyāḥ kramākramābhyāṃ vyāptisiddhiriti, sāṃvṛtaśaktipakṣe'pi nirvāhasya darśitatvāt ?
[9,2]
nanu yathā saṃvṛtau paramapuruṣārthaṃ prārthayamānasyopāyānveṣaṇapravṛttasya nārthaśaktimanāśritya sthātuṃ śaktiḥ, tathā mayā tatphalalābhinā bhāvyamityupāyānveṣaṇānnityatāgraho'pyavaśyamāyāta iti nityo'pi satsaṃvṛtisanna bhavatu kathamadharasaṃvṛtiviṣayaḥ ? nityātmā tu cintāntaramarhati | na ca tanmātreṇopagamārhaḥ, yataḥ saṃvṛtiviśeṣaviṣayaḥ syāt | evaṃ śaktigraho'nveṣaṇe prayojako'stu | śaktyā kiṃ kartavyamityabhidadhīta nāma | na tu śaktivyatikramo'nena vacasā dalitaḥ, śaktigrahasyopāyānveṣaṇa hetutvasvīkārāt | natvevamātmani śakyam | śaktigraho'pi saṃvṛttyeva prayojaka iti cet — astu saṃvṛttayā tattvena vā | śaktisiddhau ca punarātmagrahasyāpi prayojakatvasiddhernāvaśyamātmasiddherākṣepa iti | nirṇayāpekṣaṇe kṣaṇikatvasiddhistadbādhanītyuktaprāyam | hetuphalagrahaṇe vyavasthitapratisandhātṛsiddhivādastu prastoṣyate'nekāntacintāyām |
[9,3]
yadapīdamuktam, sūkṣmekṣikayāpi tvanmata eva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaṃ naṣṭaṃ bhavati, anyenānyasyāpratibaddhasya grahaṇānabhyupagamāt | pratibandhaśca dviṣṭhaḥ pratyakṣeṇādvayagrāhiṇā na gṛhyata ityanumānasya tatrāpravṛtteḥ | asmanmate tu kāryakāraṇabhāvasyāpi na grahaṇānupapattiḥ, pratyakṣasyaikakṣaṇaviṣayatvaniyamānabhyupagamāt | tathā ca vyāptigrahaṇasamarthanaprastāve'smadādipratyakṣamapyatotānāgatādiviṣayaṃ kadācidadṛṣṭādihetuvaśāt pravartata iti samarthitam | na hyanyathā kāraṇatāvādapratītiḥ saṃbhavatīti | tadapi sakalaṃ viphalam | tathāhi pareṇa parasya vedanaṃ tāvadubhayorapi kṣaṇiketaravādinoriṣṭam | tatra ca yadi pratyakṣeṇādvayagrahaṇaṃ nāma, nyāyaviruddhametat | dvayagrahaṇameva nyāyyam | tathā ca sati kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇasya na vyāghātaḥ | kṣaṇabhaṅgavādyapi tathopagacchan kiyatīṃ kṣatimāsādayet | na hyadṛṣṭamaniṣṭamevāsya |
[10,1]
pūrvamapyeṣa siddhāntaṃ svecchayaiva gṛhītavān | kathañcidanyaṃ sa punargrahītuṃ labhate na kim || (pra0 vā0 4. 74)
[10,2]
atha kathañcidadvayagrahaṇameva nyāyyam, tadā tadviparītaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravaṇamapi tvadiṣṭimātraṃ kutropayogi ?
[10,3]
atha kṣaṇabhaṅgavāde kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇamapi na prāpnotītyākūtam, tarhyasti kāryakāraṇabhāva iti virodha udbhāvyatām, nāsiddhiḥ | tatra ca vakṣyāmaḥ | yadapīdamuktam — anādivāsanāta eveyaṃ pratītiriti cet — na, atrāpi pramāṇābhāvāditi, tatrāpi kāyacittavyatiriktātmadravyasamavāye vastvantaradharmādharmalakṣaṇaguṇaprasādhakamayaṃ pramāṇamupanyasituṃ śakto nāparaścetaḥśaktiviśeṣaḥ karmetyasya prasādhakamiti mahatī śraddhā |
cittaśaktireva hi vāsanetyabhidhīyate | tasmādasaṃsṛṣṭakṣaṇamātravedanavādino hi vyavahārasyānādirabhyāsaḥ | tato vāsanā | tato mithyā pratītiriti | etat sarvamandhaparamparāvadapramāṇakamityapi dhandhāndhavilasitamiti mantavyam | asaṃsṛṣṭakṣaṇamātravedanavādī hi prastutaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgavādī sautrāntika ityarthaḥ | tasya kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītiḥ mithyā pratītiriti mahatī bhrāntiḥ | kāryakāraṇabhāvāpalāpī tu yogācāraḥ svasaṃvinmātravedanavādīti vaditumucitam | na ca tasya dūṣaṇena kṣaṇabhaṅgavādinaḥ kiñcit | hetuphalāpalāpino'pi yadi tadapalāpāya nyāyasaṃbhavaḥ tadā tadapi na dūramiti kimatra nirbandhena ? iti |
sthitametat yadi kāryakriyāśaktistāttvikī, taditarā vā, ubhayathāpi nāsiddhidūṣaṇāvatāra iti ||
{1.2}
<kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ — anvayādhikāraḥ>
[11,1]
nāpyayaṃ viruddho hetuḥ, sapakṣīkṛte jalabhṛti darśanāt, sādhyaviparyayavyāptilakṣaṇasya viruddhasya sādhyavati darśanānupapatteḥ | nanu sāhasametat, kvacidapi dhiyaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgagocarīkaraṇasāmarthyānupalabdheḥ, tathāvasāyābhāvāt | na ca pramāṇabalāvalambanād ambude kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiḥ | pratyakṣato hi sa evāyaṃ toyada iti pratyabhijñānamasya kālāntarasthāyitāmevopasthāpayati | tadbādhitatvāccānumānamanavakāśam | na cānumānamanyadasti | sattvānumāne ca punarnidarśanāntarasamīkṣāyāmanavasthāprasaṃgaḥ | tasmāt sapakṣe'darśanāt na virodhaparihāraḥ | vipakṣībhūte'mbhobhṛti bhāvācca avirodha evānaikāntikatvasyāsattvasya | pakṣe ca kṣaṇabhaṅgapratijñāyāḥ pratyakṣabādhā |
[11,2]
yadāha śaṃkaraḥ, pratyakṣeṇaiva sthitiviparyayābhāvasya siddhatvāditi | na cāyamekatāgrahaḥ pūrvāparakālayorapramāṇam, saṃvāditvāt | tathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ, yathā cedamasatkāryamityasyāḥ pratītervisaṃvādābhāvādeva prāmāṇyaṃ, tathā'nenaitāni krameṇa kṛtāni na yugapaditi pratīteḥ, sa evāhaṃ sa evāyaṃ sphaṭika ityevamādipratyabhijñāyāśca visaṃvādābhāvādeva prāmāṇyameṣṭavyam, tulyayogakṣematvāditi | tadetadasaṃgatam |
aliṅgasya hi vikalpasyā visaṃvādo nāmārthakriyāprāptiḥ, pramāṇāntarasaṃgatirvā syāt |
tatra sa evetyadhyavasāyamātrānnāparapramāṇavṛttiratra | arthakriyāpi naikapratibaddhā siddhā kācit, bhinnenāpi tatsamānaśaktinā tādṛgarthakriyāyāḥ karaṇāvirodhāt, tathāhi yathaiko ghaṭo vāri dhārayatīti tatkālabhāvino'pyanyasya na vāridhāraṇam, tathā dvitīyakṣaṇe'pyanyo yadi vāri dhārayati tadā kīdṛśo doṣaḥ syāt ? visadṛśakriyāyāṃ tu cintaiva nāsti | tasmāt yathā pāvakādeḥ pākādikriyā pratibaddhā siddhānubhūyamānā dahanajñānasya saṃvādamāpādayati, na tathā prathamacaramakālayorekībhāvapratibaddhā kācit kriyopalabdhigocarā, yayaikabhāvagraho'pi saṃvādī syāt |
[12,1]
sarveṣāṃ sarvadaikādhyavasāyasāmyāt kimaparasaṃvādāpekṣayeti cet — na, asiddhatvāt | yadyapi hi samānaśaktibhirekatvamavaseyaṃ tathāpi sarvairiti na śakyamasarvavidā | atīndriyadarśināṃ suramuniyogināmullaṃghanīyatayā teṣu kaścit kadācit kṣaṇabhaṅgadarśī yadi syāt, na virodhaḥ | adhikādhikaśaktidarśanaṃ ca saṃbhāvanābījam | yadi tu svabhāva evāyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅganāmā na bhavati na tairgrahaṇamiti, yuktametat | tacca nirūpayitumārabdham | ato yāvanna svabhāvasiddhiḥ, tāvanna sarveṣāṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsaniṣedhādhyavasāyasiddhiḥ | atīndriyadarśidveṣiṇo hi nānupalabdhimātreṇa niṣedhamabhidadhānāḥ sādhavaḥ, atiprasaṅgāt | yogyānupalabdhistu deśādiviprakarṣiṇyasamarthetyāstāṃ tāvat | katipayasaṃpratipattistu taimirikakalitakeśādiṣvapi saṃbhavinī na saṃvādamavasthāpayituṃ śaknoti | etacca pratyakṣāpekṣayocyate |
anumānatastu kṣaṇabhede bhāvabhedaṃ pratiyantaḥ kimihāpi pariṣadi niṣeddhuṃ śakyante, tatsādhanābhyāsasya kvacidanivāraṇāt ? tasmānna sarveṣāmadhyakṣakṛto'numānātmā vā ekādhyavasāyo niyamena bhedādhyavasāyaniṣedho veti na pramāṇāntaravat saṃvādasaṃvāditamasya prāmāṇyam, lūnapunarjātakeśakuśakadalakāṇḍādiṣu vyabhicārācca | yat punaranena viśeṣavacanābhimāninābhihitam, atha visaṃvādinyapi pratyabhijñā dṛśyate |
kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītiḥ kiṃ visaṃvādinyapi na dṛśyate ? yā visaṃvādinī sā kāryakāraṇapratītireva na bhavati, apramāṇatvāditi cet ? samānamatrāpi | visaṃvādinī yā sā pratyabhijñaiva na bhavati tadābhāsatvāditi |
[12,2]
syādetat, yadi kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītivallakṣaṇabhedaḥ pratipādayituṃ śakyeta |
tathāhi kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītāvapi yadi vastumātreṇa jananaṃ dhūmādergṛhṇīyāt, gardabhādivyabhicāreṇa vahnāvapi hastakaṃ tyajet | evamanvayamātreṇa vyatirekamātreṇa vā yathāyogaṃ bhāvyam | yadā punaranvayavyatirekagrahaṇapravaṇapratyakṣānupalambhasambhavaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvapratyayaḥ puraskriyate, yathā nirṇītamasmābhiḥ trikapañcakacintāyām — na sthitaṃ tatra nānyasmājjātaṃ nāyātamanyataḥ | yasya bhāve bhavet kāryaṃ na cettasya na kasyacit || (kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhau 4)
iti, tadā tvavyabhicāraḥ |
[13,1]
evaṃ yadi pratyabhijñāne'pi lakṣaṇabhedo darśitaḥ syād darśayituṃ vā śakyo vyabhicārāvyabhicāropayogī, tadā yuktametat | na caivamasti, sarvatrātyantasadṛśavastuni pṛthagjanapratyabhijñāyā ekarasatvāt | yadi cāvaśyametāvatā kālena bhrāntibhraṃśo bhavatīti kālaniyamaḥ syāt, tadāpyucitametat | yāvatā chinnodbhinnakeśapāśādau puruṣāyuṣakṣayeṇāpi naikatābhramabhraṃśo'vaśyaṃ yatnavato bhavatyeveti cet — na, tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt | prayatamānasyāpi hi vacanamātramapramāṇamupapattyantaraṃ ca durlabham |
yadi copapattyantaraṃ pratyabhijñāsiddhaikatvabādhakam, prastute'pi kiṃ naivamāsthīyate ? kevalaṃ pratyabhijñayātītamanumānaṃ varākamasamarthamidānīṃ keśādau tava vacanamātramapi samarthamiti mahatī parāmarśaśaktiḥ | bhinne'pi keśādāvabhedādhyavasāyadarśanād bhavatu tatra yathākathañcid bhedasaṃpratyaya iti cet — na, anyatrāpi bahulaṃ tathā darśanāt | na hi stambhamekamapanīya niveśite sadṛśe stambhāntare na bhavatyeva pratyabhijñānam ||
[13,2]
evaṃ ghaṭapaṭasphaṭikādiṣvapi yatra yāvadatyantasadṛśalābhaḥ | bhinnakāladarśane cāyaṃ nyāyaḥ | samasamayaṃ tu ayogolakayugalopalambhe'pi bhavatyeva bhedavyavasāyaḥ |
tasmāt kālabhedenaikābhimate'pi stambhādau bhinna eva kimayamekatvādhyavasāyaḥ stambhāntareṇeva ? athābhinna iti saṃśayaḥ pratyabhijñāyāḥ prāmāṇyapratiṣedhī kathaṃ niṣedhyaḥ ?
[13,3]
atha kṣaṇabhedenābhedasyādṛṣṭapūrvatvānna saṃśaya iti cet — naitadapi sādhu |
na hyadṛṣṭamityeva nāstīti śakyate vaktum, sato'pi sūkṣmatayā'nupalakṣaṇāt | tatkṣaṇodayavyaya dehopacayāpacayavat | tato'nupalakṣaṇe'pi bhedasya sattāṅgollekhaśekharo durnivāraḥ saṃśayaḥ | etāvadvimarśābhāve tu itarajanasya niścala ekāvasāyaḥ syāt |
yauktastu so'pi saṃśaya eva | kiṃ ca kṣaṇabhedenāpi bhedaḥ pramāṇaparidṛṣṭatvād dṛṣṭa eva |
yathā dhārādau kiyatyapi nabhobhāge'parāparapayaḥpāte'pi tadevedamudakamityavadhāraṇasya viparyayasthiteśca saṃbhavāt |
[14,1]
anabhyāsadaśāyāmekatāgrahaḥ tatra stambhādau tvabhyāsavato'pīti cet ? nanu kṣaṇabhedabhāvini viśeṣe sarvatraivāsmādṛśo'nabhyāsa ityupapāditameva | ambhaḥstambhādau tu tatkriyāsārthasāmānyālambanaḥ sarvatrābhyāsaḥ sthūlaviṣayaḥ | tasmānna pratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇadvaye abhedasādhanavyāpāraḥ svīkartuṃ śakyaḥ | ekāvasāyamātraṃ tu sadapi vyabhicārādasamartham |
[14,2]
nanu sarvatra nīlādau pṛṣṭhabhāvinā vikalpena pratyakṣasya vyāpāro'nugamyamānaḥ prāmāṇyamupanayati | tadekatāvasāyo'pyekaviṣayameva prāmāṇyamasya dīpayatviti cet — na khalu sarvatra pṛṣṭhabhāvivikalpaviṣaye prāmāṇyamindriyajñānasya | marīciviṣayasyāpi jalāvasāye jalaviṣaye prāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt | vikalpāpekṣaṃ tu prāmāṇyamiti tadanudaye na prāmāṇyamiti nyāyaḥ | tadudaye tu saṃvādāpekṣameva tat | na caikādhyavasāyasya saṃvādaḥ sa ityāveditametat |
[14,3]
nanu yatra bādhaḥ, tatrāprāmāṇyamabādhite prāmāṇyamiti kiṃ na paryāptam ? iyaṃ gatiravanatagaganapratibhāse'pi deśakālanarāntaravyāpinī saṃbhavati, nirūpyamāṇā truṭyatīti pratyabhijñāyāmapi samānam |
[14,4]
kiṃ cāyamabādho nāma bādhāviraho bādhānupalabdhirveti vikalpayoḥ kramād asiddhiranekāntaśca duṣpratividhānaḥ | anupalabdhimātreṇa niṣedhāsiddheḥ, bādhakasya cānumānasyābhidhāsyamānatvāt | atha pratyakṣasamākhyāteyaṃ pratyabhijñā, kathamanumānena bādhyate ? na cābādhyatvapratijñānādvādhakasya sadbhāvacintāvakāśe'numānasyāpyavakāśaḥ svayameva dattaḥ | prāmāṇyasyaiva siddhibādhanayoradhikārāt, pratyakṣamevāsyā bādhakam astviti cet — saṃvādadraḍhimni pratyakṣaśatenāpi kimasyāḥ ? tataḥ pratyakṣeṇāpi bādhanamasyāḥ saṃvādaśaithilyaṃ saṃbhāvayadanumānamapi sannidhāpayati |
[15,1]
apica māyākaraḥ śirasi nimajjitaṃ golakamāsyena niḥsārayatīti pratyabhijñā śirasi chidraprasaṅgasaṅgatenānumānena bādhyamānā kiṃ nopalabdhā ? bādhyamānā na pratyakṣamiti prastute'pyastu | ataḥ pratyakṣatvakīrtanamasyā yācitakamaṇḍanamātramatrāṇam | yathā cāvanatākāśapratibhāsaḥ sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nābādhya eva, tathā nāvisaṃvādyevetyapi vyaktam | tadvadeva caikatāgrahaḥ sarvasaṃpratipattāvapi nāvisaṃvādī |
nahi tadaparādhyavasāyodayamantareṇa praṇatāmbarasaṃvedane sa evāyamiti pratyaye'paraḥ saṃvādo'rthakriyādisvabhāvaḥ saṃbhavati | ataśca bādhakābhāve'pi nāmāprāmāṇyavyavahāro'śakyasādhanaḥ | tadvadeva saṃvādena prāmāṇyamanvaśāsataḥ tadabhāvāt prāmāṇyavyavahāro'pi kutaḥ pratyabhijñāyāḥ ? ubhayaniścayābhāve ca tadubhayāvalambī saṃśayaḥ siddhaḥ | tallakṣaṇe kadalakāṇḍādau vyabhicāradarśanāt paripuṣṭāniṣṭāṅgaśca | tatkutaḥ prāmāṇyam ?
[15,2]
kiṃ ca, ya evamāha visaṃvādinī yā sā pratyabhijñaiva na bhavati tadābhāsatvāditi, tena śabdādau prameyatvaṃ hetūkṛtya yat sādhyavyabhicāri prameyatvaṃ, tatprameyatvameva na bhavati tadābhāsatvādityapi vaktavyameva |
[15,3]
atha pramāṇaviṣayatvamātraṃ prameyatvam, tacca vyabhicāriṇo'pyakṣīṇam | evaṃ tarhi pūrvāparaikīkaraṇamātraṃ pratyabhijñārthaḥ | tacca vyabhicāriṇyā apyasti | pratyabhijñā nāma kriyatāṃ mā vā, kevalaṃ sā pramāṇameva na bhavatīti vaktavyam | prameyatvamapi yadvyabhicāri, tat liṅgameva na bhavatītyapi brūhi | ekalakṣaṇatayā yathaikatra vyabhicārastathānyatrāpi saṃbhavanna nivāryata iti pratyabhijñāne'pi nāśakyam ||
[15,4]
nanvagniratretyanumānamananumānaṃ ca hetvābhāsakāle samānākāram | tatkatham ekatrāśvāso nānyatra ? hetudvāreṇa viśeṣāt | yathā hi ekaṃ trirūpaliṅganiścayajanitam anyadanyathā, yathā kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītireva kācitpariśuddhā yā adhyakṣānupalabdhisādhanā, kācidanyatheti darśitam | tathā ca sati bhinnalakṣaṇatvāt nāśvāsānāśvāsasaṅkaraḥ |
tathā na pratyabhijñāyāṃ śakyam, anupahatendriyasyeva tajjñānasya vā vyabhicāriṇyāmapi vyāpārāt | nāparaḥ parairapi paridīpite viśeṣaḥ | dīrghakālānubandhamātraṃ tu bahalavyāmohād adṛṣṭādihetuprabhāvād viparyayasāmagrīsamavadhānaparilambe'pyupapattimat, yathoktaṃ prāk | yad vā yataḥ kutaścit parokṣārthapratipattimanumānamanumatya yatra vyabhicāraḥ, talliṅgameva na bhavati, anumānaṃ veti nirvṛttimālambamānaḥ pakṣadharmatvādikaṃ liṅgalakṣaṇaṃ tatprabhavamanumānaṃ kimarthamabhidadhyāt ?
[16,1]
atha vyabhicāriṇo'pi vyabhicāradarśanamasamartham, sāmagrīlābhavilambe vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa liṅgatvaprasaṅgād vaktavyameva lakṣaṇam, yadīkṣaṇānnirvṛttiranīkṣaṇādanāśvāsaśca jāyate ? tato na prekṣastadanurūpānuṣṭhānaprārambhamāsādayet | santi hi pratyanīkadarśanasthānāṃ sādhanāni cirakālābhyāsabhāvitā samasamādhibalonmīladadhyakṣagocaravyabhicārāṇi kṣaṇikatādisādhanavat | tatkimidānīṃ vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇa bhāvinyāḥ pramāṇānupapatteḥ sādhanānyeva bhavantu tadanurūpānuṣṭhānena vā viphalamāyāsamāviśatu prekṣaḥ | pakṣadharmatvādilakṣaṇe tu tallakṣaṇanirūpaṇāyāṃ tadaprāptau tadaiva hastakatyāgānnāyāsamāviśati | tallakṣaṇaprāptau vā tadeva upādadīta | tanna vyabhicārāvalambanaṃ sādhu, vyatirekanirākaraṇāyaiva vivekārambhāt | tatkathaṃ lakṣaṇamavācyamiti cet — etat sarvaṃ pratyabhijñāyāmapi ālocayan yāvanna lakṣaṇabhedaṃ paśyasi, tāvannaikasyāṃvyabhicārādarśī vyabhicārādarśanamātreṇāparasyāmāśvāsamekāntena kartumarhasi | tasmāllakṣaṇayukte bādhāsaṃbhave tallakṣaṇameva dūṣitaṃ syāditi sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ | tadiyaṃ pratyabhijñā vyapanayatu vyabhicāraśaṅkāṃ, kalaṅkitā tayā na kālāntarasthitimarthasya sthāpayituṃ prabhavati, nāpyanumānamanavakāśayitum | tatkathaṃ tadapekṣayā pratyakṣabādhitaḥ pakṣa ucyate ? sapakṣe vā jaladhare kathamanvayābhāvaḥ ?
[16,2]
atha mā bhūt pratyabhijñāyāḥ prāmāṇyam, tadanusārī sthiratāniścayo vā | kṣaṇikatvāvadhāraṇaṃ tu sapakṣīkṛte kathaṃ yataḥ sapakṣe sattvaṃ hetorupapadyate ? ucyate, iha jaladharasya jaladhāraṇakriyāsamarthastāvadekārthasvabhāvo'śakyaparihāraḥ | kṣaṇāntare ca dvitīyādau tatkriyāyāḥ kṛtatvāt punaḥ kartumaśakyatvāt tajjātīyāmanyajātīyāṃ vā kuryāt | na kuryād vā kāmapi kriyāmiti pakṣaḥ | evaṃ tat kriyākaraṇakṣaṇāt prāgapi vaktavyam | tatra yadi tatkaraṇasamarthasvabhāvo'mbhodharaḥ, tatkṣaṇavat kṣaṇāntare'pi kathaṃ kadācit kriyāvicchedaḥ ? kṣaṇāntaranivartanīyakriyāsamarthasvabhāvatve vā kṣaṇāntaravat tatrāpi kṣaṇe sajātīyetarakriyāprasavaprasaṅgaḥ | kṣaṇāntare'pi hi tacchāmarthyasya saṃbhavājjananaṃ taccānyadāpyakṣīṇam |
[17,1]
kāryāṇi hi vilambante kāraṇāsannidhānataḥ | samarthahetusadbhāve kṣepasteṣāṃ tu kiṃkṛtaḥ || (tattvasaṃgrahe 395)
[17,2]
etenākaraṇapakṣo'pi pratikṣiptaḥ | yadā vilambo'pyasahyaḥ, tadā dūrotsāditam akaraṇam | asāmarthye vā samīhitasamaye'pyakaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ, sadaikasvabhāvatvāt | svabhāvabhraṃśe ca pratikṣaṇaṃ kṣayaḥ siddho jaladharasya | tatra prayogaḥ, yad yadā yajjananasamarthaṃ tattadā tajjanayatyeva | yathā'ntyā kāraṇasāmagrī svakāryam | sa eva vā jaladharastadavasthāyāṃ vāri dhārayan kṛṣībalavilocanotsavādikāryam, vārivitaraṇakāle vā tatkriyām, śaktaścāyamubhayadaśāyāmubhayakāryamarjitumiti svabhāvahetuprasaṅgaḥ | jananamantareṇa sāmarthyavyavasthāyāṃ sarvasya sarvatra śaktivyavahāraprasaṅgaḥ | niyataścāyaṃ pratipanno vyavahāraḥ |
na cāsya jananādanyannimittamupapadyate | tato jananavinābhāve vipakṣe niyamavattvena kṣaṇavyāpakaviyogenātmasattayā viyujyamāno janana eva viśrāmyatīti samarthavyavahāragocaratvamātrānubandhi janakatvaṃ siddhamiti vyāptisiddhiḥ ||
[17,3]
evaṃ yad yadā yatkaraṇasamarthaṃ tattadā tatkarotyeva | yathā'ntyā kāraṇasāmagrī |
śaktaścāyaṃ sakalakriyātikramakāle'pīti | anyadā sarvathā'karaṇapakṣe yojyam |
asamarthasvabhāvatve tu yad yatrāśaktaṃ na tat tatkaroti, yathā śālyaṅkuraṃ kodravaḥ |
aśaktaścāyamudavāhano'karaṇakṣaṇavat kṣaṇāntare'pīti vyāpakavirudvopalabdheḥ na kadācit kuryāditi hetvarthaḥ |
[17,4]
viparyayaprayogaśca, yad yanna karoti na tat tatra śaktam, yathā śālyaṅkuramakurvan kodravaḥ | na karoti ca prathamakṣaṇasādhyāṃ kriyāṃ dvitīyādikṣaṇe, dvitīyādikṣaṇasādhyāṃ vā prathamakṣaṇa iti vyāpakānupalabdhirjaladharasya tattatkriyāsu samarthāsamarthasvabhāvatayā pratikṣaṇaṃ bhedamutpādayatīti ||
[18,1]
evaṃ sarvathā'karaṇāpekṣayā yad yanna karoti na tattatra samarthaṃ yathā śālyaṅkuramakurvan kodravaḥ | na karoti cākaraṇakāle karaṇakālakāryāṃ kriyāmiti | sāmarthyāpekṣayā, yad yat karoti na tat tatrāśaktam, antyasāmagrīvat | karoti cāyaṃ toyadharastoyadhāraṇamiti viruddhavyāptopalabdhirasamarthakṣaṇād bhinatti karaṇasamartham | yathā hi jananena vyāpyate samarthasthitiyogyatā, tathā jananaṃ tayāpi | tadasāmarthyaviruddhaṃ yat sāmarthyaṃ tena vyāptaṃ karaṇamupalabhyamānasāmarthyaṃ kadarthayatīti samarthāsamarthasvabhāvatayā svabhāvabhedaḥ siddhastoyadasya | tatkathaṃ sattvādanyadanumānaṃ nāstītyucyate ?
[18,2]
atra ca samarthavyavahārayogyatājananayorbhinnavyāvṛttikatayā sādhyāviśiṣṭatā hetorityavāntaraiḥ kīrtitaṃ dūṣaṇamanavakāśaṃ veditavyam | tasmādekārthakāriṇaḥ kṣaṇāntarāpekṣayā samarthetarasvabhāvatayā bheda eveti kṣaṇabhaṅgitayā sapakṣatāmāvahati | balāhake sattvasiddhiraviruddhā |
[18,3]
nanu kṣaṇabhedeṣvavatiṣṭhamānasyāpi bhāvasya sahakārisaṃgamāpekṣayā karaṇākaraṇamupapadyamānaṃ kathaṃ svabhāvabhedamāpādayituṃ prabhavati ? tato yathoktaprasaṅgamaulahetuṣvanekāntaḥ | kiṃ punarasya samarthasvabhāvasya sahakāribhiḥ kartavyam, yadayamanapekṣya sahakāriṇo na svakāryakarmaṇi pravṛttimālambate ? anupakāriṇyapekṣāyā ayogāt | svayam asamarthastu sāmarthyamarthayamānaḥ sahakāriṇo'pekṣata iti yuktametat | tato'kiñcitkarāḥ ca sahakāriṇo'pekṣāgocarāśceti vyāhatam |
[18,4]
atra śakaraḥ, sahakāriviraho hi tasyāsāmarthyamucyate | taccāsya sahakārisākalyahetubhirapanīyate, tayorekatra sahasthitivirodhāt | sākalyahetubhyaśca vaikalyasyaiva vyāvṛttiḥ, na tadvataḥ sākalyasya sahakārivirahavyāvṛttirūpatvāt | na ca sahakārisākalyavaikalyayorāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāṃ tadvatastadbhāvasiddhiḥ, tasya tābhyāmanyatvāt | ataeva sahakārivirahavyāvṛttihetorna tadvatastirobhāvasiddhiriti ||
[19,1]
etadeva nyāyabhūṣaṇakāro'pyāha — sahakāriṇastasya kamupakāraṃ kurvanti yena tairvinā na karotīti cet — kāryameva kurvanti | anyopakārakaraṇe hi sahakāritvameva na syāt |
tathāhi yadi tameva kurvanti tadā tatkāriṇa eva syuḥ na tatsahakāriṇaḥ | tena sahaikaṃ kāryaṃ kurvanto hi tatsahakāriṇo'bhidhīyanta iti | tathā bhavatu nāmānupakārako'pi sahakārī, tathā yadi tasya prāgeva śaktirasti kiṃ na karoti ? nāsti cet — paścādaśaktaḥ kathaṃ karoti ? paścācchaktaścet — śaktāśaktayoḥ kathaṃ na nānātvam ? viruddhadharmādhyāsasya bhedakatvādityāśaṃkya sahakārisākalyaṃ hi tasya śaktiḥ | tadvaikalyaṃ cāśaktiḥ | tena sahakārivaikalye prāgaśakta ucyate | paścāt sākalye ca śaktaḥ |
dharmadharmiṇośca bhedaḥ prasādhitaḥ | tena śaktyutpāde'pi nāvaśyaṃ tadutpādaḥ | aśaktinivṛttāvapi nāvaśyaṃ tadvato nivṛttiḥ, pratibandhābhāvāditi |
[19,2]
tadetat sarvamapohaprastāve dharmadharmiṇorabhedapratipādanenaiva nirastaṃ veditavyam, sākalyavekalyayorāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāṃ dharmiṇa eva tathāvasthānāt | astu vā dharmadharmiṇorbheda eva | nāpi sahakāriṇāmakiñcitkaratve vipratipadyāmahe | kevalaṃ na tāvanta eva sahakāriṇaḥ kāryakāriṇaḥ | nāpi sākalyameva kāryamarjati, kiṃ tu so'pi bhāvaḥ | tadarthaṃ taireva prayattamiti na vistareṇopayogaḥ | tasya ca bhāvasya yādṛśaścaramakṣaṇe'kṣepakriyādharmā svabhāvaḥ, tādṛśa eva cet prathamakṣaṇe'pi, tadaiva prasahya kurvāṇo gīrvāṇaśāpenāpi nāpahastayituṃ śaktaḥ | kiṃ punastavāmunā marmapīḍājanitaviklavavikrośamātreṇa ? yathāhi śaktāśaktatayā bhaṅgaprasaṅgaparihārāya sākalyavaikalyalakṣaṇadharmāntarasvabhāve śaktyaśaktī bhinnasvabhāve kalpite, tathā na so'pyakṣepakriyādharmā svabhāvo bhāvād bhinna evābhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ, bhāvasyākartṛtvaprasaṅgāt |
[19,3]
atha yathā śaktyaśaktī bhinnau dharmau pratijānīmahe, na ca tayorudayavyayābhyāṃ bhāvasya kiñcit, tathā'kṣepakriyādharmatvaṃ kṣepakriyādharmatvaṃ ca dharmāntarameva | tacca sahakārisannidhānapratyayabhāvākṣepamudeti vyeti ceti | tathaiva bhāvasya na kiñcidityucyate |
[19,4]
ucyatām | kevalamastu nedānīṃ kāryajanma, kāraṇābhimatasya tādavasthyāt |
tathāhi yathā na sahakāriṇa eva, nāpi sākalyameva janakaṃ tathā sākalye sati jātamakṣepakriyādharmatvamapi na prakṛtaṃ bhāvamanapekṣya janakam, janakatve'pi svayameva bhāvasya janakatvasvīkārāt | kiṃ tu prakṛto'pi bhāvaḥ kartā svīkartavyaḥ | sa ca prācīnadaśāto'natiricyamānamūrtiḥ kurvan pūrvamapi kuryāt, akurvan vā paścādapi na kuryāditi tadavasthaḥ paribhavaḥ | yadi tu kādācitkaṃ sākalyādivastvantarameva hetuḥ, tadā kāryamapi tadapekṣaṃ kādācitkamiti nyāyyametat | evaṃ yāvad yāvad dharmāntaraparikalpaḥ, tāvat tāvadudāsīno bhāvaḥ | atha akṣepakriyādharmatvaṃ jātaṃ, kāryaṃ tu tato notpadyata iti ko'yaṃ nyāyaḥ ? tadavaśyaṃ kāryeṇa janitavyam | taccākṣepakriyādharmatvaṃ prāṅnāsoditi kāryodayasyāpi nāvakāśaḥ | evaṃ tarhi kāryātpādanāntarīyakamakṣepakāritvam, akṣepakāritvanāntarīyakaśca kāryotpāda iti vyaktamitaretarāśrayatvam |
anyathā na yadi kāryotpādanāntaroyakamakṣepakāritvam, nākṣepakāritvena kāryodayākṣepaḥ | yadi ca nākṣepakāritvanāntaroyakaḥ kāryotpādo'kṣepakāritvāt prāgapi syāt | ekārthatve tu sākalye jāte satyakṣepakāritvaṃ dharmāntaraṃ jātamiti kimanayā bhāṣayābhihitaṃ kāryamutpannamiti ? tathā ca sati na prakṛtadoṣaparihāraḥ | nahi kāryajanmani vivādaḥ, yatsvarūpāpekṣastu kāryodayaḥ tasya sarvadā tādavasthyāt kathaṃ kadācitkateti cintyate |
[20,1]
tasmādakṣepakriyādharmeti janayatīti vā yatsvarūpapuraskāreṇeyamabhikhyā tasya prāgapi sattve kathamajani kadācit ? akṣepakriyādharmakapratyanokasvabhāvasya vā prācyasya paścādanuvṛttau kathaṃ kadācidapi kāryasaṃbhavaḥ ? atha yadi sa evaikaḥ kartā syāt ?
yuktametat, kiṃ tu sāmagrī janikā tatsahakāryantaravirahavelāyāṃ balīyaso'pi na kāryaprasava iti kimatra viruddham ? ekārthakaraṇācca sahakāritvamuktam, nopakāreṇeti |
[20,2]
atrocyate | yadi militāḥ santaḥ kāryaṃ kurvate, tadaikārthakaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ sahakāritvameṣāmastu, ko niṣeddhā ? militaireva tu tat kāryaṃ kartavyamiti kuto labhyate ? pūrvāparakāryayorekatve tāvad bhāvasya sarvadā jananājananayoranyataraniyamaprasaṅgasya durnivāratvāt | tasmāt sāmagrī janikā, naikaṃ janakamiti sthiravādināṃ manorathasyānyaviṣayaḥ | dṛśyate tāvadevamiti cet — ataeva na sthairyapakṣaḥ kṣama iti brūmaḥ | sarvo hi prasaṅgo viparyayaparyavasānaḥ | tato yadi nityatā syāt janayituḥ, janyaṃ sarvadā syānna vā kadācidapīti | na caivam, sākalya eva kadācitkāryotpattiriti niyamena svabhāvabhaṅgaḥ |
[21,1]
nanu yadi kvacinnityaṃ sarvadā kāraṇamupalabdhaṃ syāt, tadā kvacinnityatvābhyupagame sadā kartṛtvaprasaṅgaḥ saṃgacchate | yāvatā sarvadā tasyābhāvāt kathametādṛśaṃ prasañjayituṃ śakyate ?
[21,2]
tadetadapi grāmyam | tathāhi nityatve satīti | asyāyamarthaḥ | parakālabhāvī janako yaḥ svabhāvo bhāvasya, sa eva yadi pūrvakālabhāvī, pūrvakālabhāvī vā yo'janakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa eva yadi parakālabhāvī, tadā tadupalabdhameva jananamajananaṃ vā syāditi | tathā ca sati siddhayorekatvārope siddhameva jananamajananaṃ vā prasajyeta |
na pūvaparasvabhāvayorekatvasaṃbhavānnityatve satītyucyata iti kimatra viruddham ?
[21,3]
atha pūrvaparayorekatvaṃ nopalabdhaṃ kathamāropyata iti manīṣā ? evaṃ sati śuktāvapi rajatāropeṇa na bhāvyam | nahi rajatasvarūpā śuktiḥ kvacidupalabdhigocaraḥ | āropyamāṇaṃ tu rajataṃ kadācidupalabdhameveti nāropakṣatiriti bhavatāmapi kṛtāntaḥ | tathā prastute'pi pūrvāparasvabhāvayorekatvaṃ nopalabhe | āropyamāṇau tu mithaḥ pūrvāparasvabhāvau siddhāveva | tadārope karaṇākaraṇe api prasajyamāne samañjase eva, guñjāpuñje jvalanāropavidhau dāhavat |
[21,4]
tadetadatilāghavamāviṣkṛtamātmanaḥ śaṅkareṇa | tadayaṃ jātyandhānāṃ nīlādiprativedhavadasaṃbandho niṣedhaḥ saugatānāmasanto'kṣaṇikā ityabhidadhānena | tasmāt sthitametat, sthirātmatve militvaiva kāryakaraṇaniyamo bhāgyahīnamanorājyasthānīya iti | tathā ca sati sahakārisākalye śaktiśabdasamayamapākurvāṇaḥ kamarthaṃ paripuṣṇāti paravyāmohanādanyamanupayuktāprastutābhidhānāt ? kṣaṇikatvavādinā hi śaktāśaktasvabhāvatayā viruddhadharmādhyāsād bhedamāropayatā yādṛśī śaktiraśaktiśca vivakṣitā tatpratividhānamācaritumucitamasya | tadapahāya svayaṃ kṛtasaṅketena parihāramāracayatīti mahannepuṇyaṃ naiyāyikapravarasya | yo hi dhūmādatrāgninā bhāvyamityāha — tatrāpi yadi kaścid gardabhādau dhūmaśabdaṃ saṃketya vahnimapahnavīta, na kaścid doṣaḥ | kṣaṇikavādī hi yajjanayatīti samākhyayā yadanantarabhāvi kāryaṃ tatsvarūpaṃ śaktamityāha | na cedamapūrvaṃ saketamātram | loke'pi hi jananadvāraka eva śaktavyavahāraḥ | yadyapi ca sākalyavata eva jananaṃ tathāpi na sākalyadvāreṇa śaktaucyate, kiṃ tu jananāt | kṣepavati sākalye'pi śaktavyavahārasyāñjasasyābhāvāt, anadhyavasitasahakāriviśeṣasākalyasyāpi jananadarśane idamatra śaktamiti vyavahārāt |
tādṛśaṃ ca svarūpaṃ śaktirucyate | asya śaktiriti bhedanirdeśe'pyasya svarūpamitivadabhinnaiva | sa ca janayitā svabhāvaḥ prāgapyasti, na ca janayatīti niyataṃ mātā ca bandhyā ceti prāptamiti | atra prakaraṇe yadi nāma tvayā kvacit śaktiśabdaniveśanaṃ kṛtam, tadāvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyā ca na bhāvasya kiñcit | tataḥ prastute kimāyātam ?
yat khalu janayitṛrūpajanayitṛbhāvādabhinnaṃ tayoyād nīdayavyayā kutaḥ kādācitkatā kāryasya ? udayavyayayoge vā svabhāvabhadastadavasthaḥ |
[22,1]
yadi tu tadapi na janayadrūpaṃ bhinnameva, tadā tasyāpi nodayavyayābhyāṃ bhāvatruṭiḥ |
kevalamajanaka eva bhāvaḥ syāditi mūlanāśaḥ | tasmād brūyāḥ kiñcit kiñcitkarasya kvacit kāryakālabhadena śaktāśaktasvabhāvayorviruddhadharmādhyāsād bheda eva |
[22,2]
ataeva yadāha bhūṣaṇakāraḥ, tatra kālabhedenāvirodhāt | yathā kriyotpatteḥ pūrvaṃ niṣkriyaḥ sphaṭikaḥ, sa eva paścāt sakriyaḥ | sādhyatvādadṛṣṭānta iti cet — na pramāṇasiddhasya sādhyatvāyogāt | evaṃ hi viruddhadharmādhyāsād bhedo'pyasiddha ityapi bruvāṇaḥ kathaṃ vāryate ? tasmād yayordharmayoryathā virodho dṛṣṭaḥ, tayostathaivābhyupagantavyaḥ | yathā sa eva hetuḥ svakāryaṃ prati śaktaḥ, kāryāntaraṃ pratyaśakta ityekasyaiva viṣayabhedaṃ prati śaktyaśaktī na viruddhe, tathā kālabhedenāpi śaktibhede śaktimadabhedasya pramāṇasiddherubhayatrāviśeṣāditi | etadapyasāram | etayā hiṇḍārapiṇḍāḍambaraṃ viḍambayate | tathāhi na khalu pramāṇasiddhirnāma pratyakṣānumāne paribhūyābhidhātuṃ śakyate | tatra ca pratyakṣamiti na pratyabhijñāvikalpādanyat | sā ca nivāritā |
[23,1]
yaccānumānamāha śaṃkaraḥ sthirasiddhau notpattyanantaraṃ vināśī bhāvaḥ prameyatvāt | vastuvyāvṛttivaditi | avidyamānavipakṣatvādanvayyeva hetuḥ | prameyatvasya kṣaṇikatvena virodhābhāvāt sandigdhavyatirekamiti cet — na khalu kṣaṇikatve kasyacit prameyatvaṃ sidhyati, kṣaṇasthitidharmaṇaḥ pramāṇakāle'tipātāt, atītasya ca pratyakṣatve'tiprasaṅgāt | tadapi manorathamātram | tathāhi | mā bhūdatītasya grahaṇam | vartamānasya ca kṣaṇikasyaiva kṣaṇikena jñānena grahaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tasmādavirodha eva prameyatvakṣaṇikatvayoḥ |
[23,2]
atha kāraṇaṃ viṣaya iti jñānāt prāgapekṣitasattāko'rthaḥ kṣaṇāntare'nanuvartamāno na grāhya eva syāt, kṣaṇāntarānuvṛttau vā akṣaṇikatvameveti cet — tat kimiyaṃ rājñāmājñā yadajanakena grāhyeṇa na bhavitavyamiti ? ayamasya samaya eveti cet — nyāyasyāyamavasaro na samayasya | tasmāt samayamanapekṣya vādavyasaninā nyāyopanyāsena paro bodhayitavyaḥ | samayasya hi sādhanatve sarvasiddhernyāyo nāma na kiñcit | nyāyastu samayabādhanāyaiva kathaṃ samayameva śaraṇīkuryāt ||
kathamajanitena grahaṇamatiprasaṅgaścaivamiti cet ? janitenāpi kathaṃ grahaṇam ? jāyamānaṃ hi jñānaṃ viṣayamanubhavadupajāyate | tacca janmaviṣayakṛtamanyakṛtaṃ vā syāt, ko viśeṣaḥ ? atiprasaṅgastu sādhāraṇaḥ, cakṣurādināpi tasya jananāt | tasyāviṣayasvabhāvatvāditi cet — nanu gṛhyamāṇa eva viṣayo vyavahriyate, na jātiniyataḥ kaścid viṣayo nāma | tato'viṣayatvādityagṛhyamāṇatvānna gṛhyata iti kvedamuttaraṃ saṃbadhyate | tathāhi svabhāvādeva nendriyaṃ gṛhyata iti cet — na, yogināṃ darśanasvīkārāt | pṛthagjanāpekṣayā niyama eṣa iti cet ? pṛthagjanāpekṣayā tarhi sūkṣmādayo'pi svabhāvenaiva gṛhyanta iti nātiprasaṅgaḥ | athavā,
[23,3]
pūrvikaiva tu sāmagrī sajñānaṃ viṣayakṣaṇam | sālokarūpavat kuryād yena syāt sahavedanam ||
[24,1]
tena vā svaviṣayaniyatamutpāditaṃ jñānaṃ tadekagrāhi, tatkāraṇasāmagryā vā tanniyatamutpāditamiti nirviśeṣaḥ | atastasyā eva te arthajñāne grāhyagrāhakabhāvaniyatajanmanī kathamatiprasajyeyātām ?
[24,2]
atha sākāravedanavādino hi viṣayādeva tatsvarūpasaṃvitterutpattirabhimatā, tatrātītagrahaṇe'tiprasaṅgaḥ, grahaṇakṣaṇānuvṛttau ca sthirasiddhiriti vivakṣitam | tat kimayaṃ prasaṅgaheturyatparopagamanamanapekṣya na bhavati ? tathā ca sati viparyayaparyavasānāt tava sthirasiddhiratītagrahaṇaṃ veti na grāhyāttatsvarūpajñānotpattiriti syāt | evaṃ ca sati vyaktamanyad bhuktamanyad vāntamiti nyāyaḥ | sthiramārabdhaḥ sādhayituṃ tadviparyayeṇa sākārabodhaṃ vidhurayatīti |
[24,3]
atha sautrāntikasyedamubhayamasamañjasamitīyanmātramucyate, tadapi nāsti |
sākāravedanodayapakṣasthitau hi dvitīyakṣaṇānuvṛttāvapyarthasya jaḍatayā prakāśānupapatteḥ viparyayasarūpasvarūpasaṃvedanameva jñānasya viṣayavedanam | evaṃ ca na vartamānānurodhaḥ, atīte'pi tatpratyayāsatterapracyuteḥ | na cātiprasaṅgaḥ, viṣayāntareṇāpi sārūpyasamarpaṇāt | na ca tanmatanirvāhaḥ prakṛtaḥ | bhavatastu tanmatāśrayeṇāpi prameyatvahetuḥ sthirasiddhaye na prabhavatīti siddhamanekāntaparihārāditi | tataḥ sthiravapuṣi pramāṇāntarasiddherayogāt vajro'pi pakṣakukṣau nikṣiptaḥ, kiṃ punaḥ sphaṭiko varākaḥ ? tadayaṃ sakriyākriyāvasthayorbhidyamānaḥ kathaṃ kāmabhedenāvirodhe dṛṣṭāntībhavitumarhatīti ?
yacca viṣayabhedeneva kālabhedenāpi śaktyaśaktyoravirodhapratipādanam, tadapyanaupayikam |
pratiyogī hi dharmo virodhakaḥ sarvatra | na ca svakāryakaraṇasya parakāryākaraṇaṃ pratyanīkam | kiṃ tu svakāryākaraṇameva | evaṃ parakāryākaraṇasyāpi parakāryakaraṇaṃ pratyanīkam |
na svakāryakaraṇam | svakāryaṃ na karotīti vyavacchettumeva hi svakāryaṃ karotītyucyate |
pratyakṣavyāpāraśca te svakāryakāriṇaṃ parakāryakāriṇaṃ ca bhāvabhedenāvasthāpayati |
kālabhede tu naikatāvyavasthāpakaṃ pratyakṣam, pratyabhijñāyā dūṣitatvāt | tataḥ svakāryasya karaṇamakaraṇaṃ ca pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na virodhaparihārāya paryāpnoti |
[25,1]
kālānekatvāpekṣasvakāryakaraṇākaraṇaṃ viruddhamiti cet ? syādiyamapekṣā parabhāgabhāgino yadi viṣayabhedavadabhedāpādakapramāṇavṛttiḥ syādityuktaprāyam | bhavato'pi tadanapekṣya virodhasthitau kiṃ pramāṇamiti cet — uktameva, yad yadā yajjananasamarthaṃ tattadā janayatyevetyādi, sahakāryapekṣāyāśca tatsannidhānāsannidhānayoḥ kāryārjjanaprasaṅgena nirastatvāt | tasmāt janayadrūpameva śaktirvivakṣitā kṣaṇabhaṅgavādinaḥ | tasyāśca bhede kathaṃ na bhāvabhraṃśaḥ ?
[25,2]
yacca nyāyabhūṣaṇena pralapitam, yadyasya bhinnā śaktiḥ śaktimato'bhyupagamyate, tathāpi nāvaśyaṃ śaktāśaktayorbhedaḥ | kasmāt ? tvanmate'pi dharmabhedād dharmibhedaniyamāsiddheḥ | tathā ca bhinne'pi kārye sahakāriṇāṃ pṛthagupayogaṃ darśayatā'bhihitam — mṛtpiṇḍādermṛtsvabhāvebhya ityādi hetubinduṃ lekhitvā | yathā ca tatra mṛdātmatādisvabhāvabhede'pi na kāryabhedaḥ, tathā śaktāśaktādisvabhāvabhede'pyabhedo bhaviṣyati, abādhitatvādhyavasāyasya samānatvāditi, tadapyanena pratyādiṣṭam | santi hi dharmā ye parasparavirodhino'virodhinaśca | na tu dharmā ityeva virodhāvirodhaḥ | na hi brāhmaṇyaṃ vaiyākaraṇatvenāviruddhamiti cāṇḍālatvenāpyaviruddhamityabhidhātuṃ śakyam | na cātra brāhmaṇyavyāptaṃ cāṇḍālatvam | na ca vaiyākaraṇatvenāpi viruddham | yathā cātra svapratiyogibrāhmaṇyetaratvameva virodhamādhatte na vaiyākaraṇatvena, tathā janayadrūpamajananatayaivaviruddhabhāvānna vastusantānabhedena | nīlacaturasrāditā tu śvetaparimaṇḍalatādibhirvirodhamāsādayatu, na tu kvacit kāryakāraṇādibhiḥ | ato yadi virodhagandhāsaṃbhavāt saṃsthānamṛtsvabhāvayorabhinnena dharmiṇā bhāvyam, tat kimatyantapratyanīkayorekakāryaṃ prati janayadrūpetarayorapīti kaḥ sacetanakaścintayet ? viruddhāviruddhatvameva kathamavagantavyamiti cet ? yadvyavacchedena yadvidhānam, yadvidhānena vā yadvyavacchedaḥ, tattena viruddham | na ca mṛnmayamiti vidhānena pṛthūdaratāvyavacchedaśaṅkāpi saṃbhavati | tajjanakābhidhānena cātajjanakatvaṃ vyavacchidyata eva, atajjanakatvena ca tajjanakatvam | na tajjanakamityeva hyatajjanakamiti nañsamāsavākyamapi vismāri |
tasmād yayordharmayoryathā virodho dṛṣṭaḥ tathaivābhyupagantavya ityevameva viśeṣamabhipretya yuktaḥ, naikakālāpekṣayā, samānapramāṇayorapravṛtteḥ | yena hi kālabhedenābhinnameva vastu sakriyākriyanīlānīlatvādiyuktamabhyupagataṃ, yasya vā tadātmani pramāṇaṃ pravṛttaṃ, tasya kvacidvivādasaṃbhave kālabhedenāvirodhaḥ tadvatīti yuktam | tacca dvayamapi nāstīti vyaktam | ata ekatvādhyavasāyasyābādhitaviṣayaviśeṣaṇamasiddham | ekatvādhyavasāyamātraṃ punaranaikāntikaṃ bādhakāpekṣameva | anyathā keśādāvapi na bādhakamapekṣeta | bādhakaṃ coktam | yadapyayaṃ svapnāyamāna iva viplavate |
[26,1]
atha naivābhinnātmanaḥ kasyacit svabhāvabheda iṣyate, evaṃ tarhi sahakāripṛthagupapayogakathanaṃ bālonmattapralapitaṃ syāditi | tena yadi dharmadharmiṇostādātmyatiraskāreṇa bhedāpādanamātramiṣṭam, tadā na prakṛtopayogi | tathāhi dharmiṇaḥ sakāśād dharmā bhedabhāgino bhavantu na vā ? santi tāvatkecidanyonyavirodhino ye svādhikaraṇaṃ dharmiṇamabhittvā nocchvasituṃ śaknuvantīti vivakṣitaṃ kṣaṇikavādinaḥ | tatrānena tādṛśā dharmā eva na santi, santo'pi vā kālādyupādhisāpekṣā bhedasādhava ityeva vaktuṃ nyāyyam | pṛthagupayogāt sahakāriṇāṃ dharmiṇaḥ pṛthageva ta iti kimanena ?
[26,2]
yadi tu svābhāvyabhāja eva bhedakā na bhidyamānā iti samayo'sya syāt, yuktametat | yāvatā valanādayo'pyavalanato bhedakā dṛṣṭā eva | te ca kriyādirūpatvād bhinnā eva | tasmāt kalpanoparacitavibhāgā bhavantu saugatamatena, bhavanmatena vā, tāttvikabhedo dharmadharmiṇoḥ kimidānīṃ naikāntena ? prastāvāntaraṃ hi tat | duṣpariharāstu dharmā dharmiṇaṃ bhindānā ye virodhasthāyina iti siddhaṃ sādhyam |
[26,3]
atha kāryādabhedaśca svabhāvānāṃ pṛthak sahakārikāraṇakalāpopayogaviṣayatvaṃ ceti duḥśliṣṭatāmātramudbhāvyate paranayasya ? tadāpi prastutakṣaterabhāvāt kimanena ?
bhedavatāmapi bhedakatvād dharmāṇāṃ duḥśliṣṭatābhāsatā ca bhinnasamayasthānāṃ parasparamagaṇiteṣu sthāneṣu saṃbhavati | tattvaṃ tu kīdṛgiti tattatsthānanirūpaṇe vyaktībhaviṣyati |
tatra yadi prastutānupayogiyatkiñcidvistārayatā sthātavyamityabhimatam, sarvasya śakyametat | na caitāvataiva dharmadharmivādaparisamāptiḥ | tat kimasya garbhārbhakamanatiśayānasya nindāvacane nirbandhena ? tathā ca sati tasmānna dharmabhedādeva dharmibheda iti nigamanamapyasyāyuktam | bauddhaḥ kila na dharmāṇāṃ bhedamātreṇa dharmibhedamāha |
kiṃ tu virodhena | anyathā kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāmapi dharmabhedamācakṣīta | anenāpi svayaṃ viruddhadharmādhyāsādityakṣaramutthāpitam | tad yadi virodhabhedamātrayorviśeṣaṃ na paśyati, yuktamāheti kimaparaṃ vaktavyam ?
[27,1]
yadapyayamevāha — yo hyanantarakāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ sa kathamādau tat kāryaṃ kuryāt ?
atha kuryānna tarhi uttarakāryakaraṇasvabhāvaḥ | na hi nīlotpādanasvabhāvaḥ pītādikamapi karoti | na ca prathamottarakāryotpādanasvabhāvabhedāt tadvato'pi bhedaḥ, svabhāvabhedasya vyabhicāritvenoktatvāditi | tadapi niḥsāram | yadi hi svabhāvaśabdena svalakṣaṇamabhipretam, tadā tadbhede bheda eva vastūnām, kva vyabhicāravārtā ? tasmāt svabhāvabheda iti kalpitadharmānnānātvaṃ yuktam | na ca tanmātreṇa dharmibhedamāpādayati paraḥ | kiṃ tu virodhena | na ca tadvirodhe'pi dharmibhedavyabhicāro'sti | virodho hi na bhedaṃ vyabhicarati | bhedastu virodhaṃ vyabhicaratītyuktaprāyam |
[27,2]
nanu yadi kalpitā eva te dharmāḥ kva virodhaḥ, kva vā bheda iti cet ?
iha dvividhamabhidheyaṃ kalpitaśabdasya, tattadvyāvṛttavastusaṃbhave bhedamātraṃ kalpanāvabhāsi, tadapi kalpitaṃ kuvalayanīlatvādivat | kalpanāmātraniveśi ca kalpitaṃ karikeśaratriguṇīmayatvādivat | tatra yadyantimaḥ kalpitārthaḥ syāt, na bhedanirodhāditi yuktam | prācīne tu kalpitārthe vastusvabhāvasyaivādhyavasānād bhedo virodho vā vyavasthāpyamānaḥ saṃvādamādāyaiva vartata iti na doṣaḥ |
[27,3]
yaccedam, uttarakṣaṇe yatkāryaṃ kartumasya svabhāvaḥ, tatkathaṃ prathamakṣaṇe kuryāt ?
anyathottarakāryakāritaiva na svabhāvasyeti, tadapyaparibhāvya bhāṣitam | sthirasvabhāvatve hi bhāvasyottarakālamevedaṃ kāryam, na pūrvakālamiti kuta etat ? tadabhāvācca kāraṇamapyuttarakāryakaraṇasvabhāvamiti kutaḥ ? arthānurodhinyo hi vācaḥ śobhābhājaḥ, na vāganurodhādarthatathābhāvo rājavat | kiṃ kurmaḥ, uttarameva tasya janmeti cet — astu |
sthiratve tu tadanupapadyamānamasthiratāmādiśatu | sthiratvepyeṣa eva svabhāvaḥ, tasya yaduttarakṣaṇa eva karotīti cet — hatedānīṃ pramāṇapratyāśā, pramāṇabādhite'pi svabhāvālambanena nistaraṇāt | dhūmādatrāgniragnerabhāvād vā neha dhūma ityukte'pi hi śakyamabhidhātuṃ, svabhāva evāyamasya yadidānīmatra niragnirapi dhūma iti | tasmāt pramāṇasiddhe svabhāvāvalambanam, na svabhāvāvalambanena pramāṇavilopaḥ | pramāṇanirṇayaśca vihita eva | nīlotpādanasvabhāvaśca na pītādikaṃ karotītyasamīkṣākhyānam | upādānatvena hi tatkaraṇaniṣedho, na tu sahakārikāraṇatvenāpi, sahakāritayā tatrāpi kathañcidupayogasyāśakyabādhanatvāt | na cānyavarṇasyānyavarṇopādānatāniṣedha eva | dṛśyate hi pītaiva haridrā cūrṇasahakārikā raktasyopādānaṃ bhavantīti nidarśanamasaṅgatam | yadi ca yathā na nīlaḥ pītamutpādayati tathā nottarajanakaḥ pūrvamutpādayati | evaṃ tarhi yaścottarajanakaḥ, yaśca nottarajanakaḥ, tayorbhedo'pi kiṃ neṣyate, yathā yannīlaṃ tannānīlamiti ?
tadalamevaṃvidhapralāpeṣu nirbandhena | sthitametat parasparaviruddhadharmādhyāsād deśabhedavat kālabhede'pi janakājanakasvabhāvayorbheda eva ||
[28,1]
etena yadapi nyāyamañjarīkāraḥ prāha, nanu kāryotpattiheturyeṣāṃ sannidhimapekṣate te khalvapekṣitasannidhayaḥ, sahakāripratyayāstasya kiṃ kurvanti ? na kiñcit | kevalaṃ kāryameva yeṣāṃ bhāvābhāvāvanuvidhatte te kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhayaḥ sannipatantaḥ tadeva kāryaṃ vivakṣitaṃ hetunā saha kurvantīti sahakāriṇa ucyante na tu yena saha kurvanti tasyaiva kartāro bhavantaḥ sahakāriṇo bhavitumarhanti | tasmādakṣaṇikasya svakāryanimāṇe dvividhaṃ sāmarthyam, ekaṃ nijaṃ sāmarthyam, dvitīyaṃ cāgantukaṃ sahakāryantaram, tayorabhāve tatkāryānutpatteḥ | tasmādeva hi dvividhāt sāmarthyāt kāryotpatterabhyupagamāt | ekamakṣaṇikaṃ gṛhītvā tasmādeva kāryotpattiṃ saṃbhāvayantaḥ sāmarthyameva hetūnāmavijñātavantaḥ pare | yasmādakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu tāsu tāsvarthakriyāsu kartavyāsu kramavatsahakāryantarameva sāmarthyamaṅgīkurmaḥ | tathā ca kramavatsahakārinānātvādapi kramavatkāryanānātvopapatteraśakyaṃ bhāvānāṃ pratikṣaṇamanyatvamupapādayitumiti |
[29,1]
tadapyapāstam | yadyapi hetvantarakalpitaṃ sāmarthyamavijñātamasmākaṃ tathāpi yajjanayatīti vyavahāragocarībhūyamāpannaṃ svarūpamavaśyamabhyupagantavyam, bhāvasya svalakṣaṇākhyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ saṃkhyātamasmanmate | tat kiṃ prāgapi paścādeva veti vikalpya dūṣaṇamudīritam ? tatra kimanenoktaṃ bhavatīti niveditameva | yattu kāryeṇaivāpekṣitasannidhaya ityupaskṛtam, tadapi nirupayogam | yadi hi kāryameva svajanmani svatantraṃ syāt, yuktametat, kevalamevaṃ sati sahakāriṇāmapi sāmarthyarūpatākalpanamaphalamiti, hetoḥ sāmarthyamanapekṣya svātantryādeva kāryaṃ kadācid bhavati kadācinna bhavatīti kiṃ hetusāmarthyasamarthanavyasanena, vyavahāramātraṃ vā sāmarthyamiti, na tu kvacit kiñcit samarthaṃ nāmeti prāptam | astu ko doṣa iti cet ? santo hetavaḥ sarvathā'samarthāḥ, asattu kāryaṃ svatantramiti viśuddhā buddhiḥ | utpattau tu sadrūpaṃ kāryaṃ kimarthamarthāntaramapekṣata iti nirūpaya tāvat |
[29,2]
tasmāt sāmagrīmapekṣate kāryamityanenākṣareṇa sāmagryeva jananasamarthā kāryasyetyevārthaḥ na ca sā samagrebhyo bhinnā | tataḥ samagrā eva janakāḥ | bhinnatve'pi vā'rthāntaramiva sākalyamapi sahakārīti na viśeṣaḥ | tato yāvantaḥ sahakāriṇastāvantaḥ pratyekaṃ samarthā iti prāgvidyamānānāṃ kathaṃ kriyātikramaḥ ? sākalyameva hi paścādupapattimaditi samayaḥ, tadapi vā tebhya eva sahakāribhyo labhyasaṃbhavaṃ prāgapi teṣvasatsu kathaṃ sattāviyuktaṃ kadācid yāvadekasyāpi prāgbhāvaḥ ? atha kāryasyaivāyamaparādho yadamīṣvasamartheṣu kadācinnotpadyata iti cet ? sarvāvasthāsamāne'pi kāraṇe yadyakāryatā | svatantraṃ kāryamevaṃ syāttanna kāryaṃ tathā sati || (vārtikālaṅkāre 1. 396)
iti kiṃ na paśyasi ?
[29,3]
syādetat | na tadbhāve'vaśyaṃ bhavatīti tatkāryamucyate kiṃ tu tadabhāve na bhavatyeveti vyatirekaprādhānyāditi cet ?
[30,1]
tadbhāve'pi na bhāvaścedabhāve bhāvitā kutaḥ | tadabhāvaprayuktasya so'bhāva iti tatkutaḥ || (vārtikālaṅkāre 1. 411)
[30,2]
yadi hi svayaṃ bhavanaṃ bhāvayadeva kāryaṃ hetuḥ, tadā tadabhāvaprayukto'syābhāva ityapi syāt | yadā tu hetau jananonmukhe'pi svātantryādeva na bhūtamiti kathaṃ tadabhāvaprayojako'syābhāva iti pratītiḥ ? tasmād yadi kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ tadā niyataṃ yathaiva tadabhāve niyamena na bhavati, tathaiva tadbhāve'pi niyamena bhavet | abhavacca na tatkāraṇatāmātmanaḥ kṣamate | tadayaṃ prayatnaparamparayāpi hetūnāṃ samarthāsamarthalakṣaṇodayavyayayogo jāragarbha iva gopayitumaśakyaścaturabuddhiṣu ||
[30,3]
yadapyāha śaṅkaraḥ | na ca sarvatra sahakāribhedena kāryabhedādapi kāraṇasya bhedaḥ sidhyati | yathaikatve'pi sahakāribhedād vijñānavartivikārajvālāntarāṇi pradīpaḥ karoti, na cāsau bhidyate, tadabhedasya pramāṇasiddhatvāditi |
[30,4]
apūrvo'yamasya dambhārambhaḥ | yadayamakṣepakriyādharmā svabhāvaḥ śaktiśabdavācyaḥ, sa kiṃ prāgapyasti, yadi vā saṃpratyeveti vikalpya codyaśaktivācyaṃ mama sahakārisākalyamiti bravīti, śaktyaśaktilakṣaṇaviruddhadharmādhyāsād bheda ityabhimatena kāryabhedāt kāraṇabheda iti samādhatte — kaḥ khalu kāryabhedāt kāraṇabhedaṃ vaktumupakrānto yatraivamucyate, sahakāribhadena yaḥ kāryabhedaḥ sa na kāraṇabheda iti, api tu yasya yadā yajjananasvabhāvaḥ so'vaśyaṃ tatkarotyeva | na hi pradopa eva vijñānādikāryāṇi sakṛt kartuṃ samarthaḥ kṣepeṇa janayati | tadvad vā kramabhāvinyapi kāryāṇi sajātīyavijātīyāni kiṃ na tadaiva karoti ? atasteṣāmanya eva kārako dīpa iti yuktam | evamanyatrāpyeṣa eva nyāyaḥ |
[30,5]
yatpunarāha, pradīpādivyaktīnāmiva pratyekamutpattivināśakāraṇānupalabdherabhrāntaṃ sphaṭikāderavasthitivijñānamiti, tadapyandhaśarakṣepāyate, pradīpe'pyanyānyasyotpattikāraṇasyānupalabdheḥ | vartisnehādayo hi pradīpahetavaḥ, te ca pratikṣaṇaṃ pratilavādi vānyānyībhavantītyadhyavasāyaḥ kasya saṃbhavati ? anyathā sphaṭike'pyanyānyībhavati pūrvapūrvamanyadanyaduttarottarasya kāraṇamanvayavyatirekānuvṛtteriti kiṃ na gṛhyate ? yadyapi ca pradīpe kālabhedenānyabuddhirasti tathāpi na tailavartyoḥ, tatkathaṃ pradīpādivyaktīnāmutpattikāraṇopalabdhirna sphaṭikasyetyucyate ? vināśakāraṇaṃ tu cintayiṣyāmaḥ | nāpi pradīpabhaṅguratayā tatkāraṇabhaṅgaḥ saṅgato vaktum, kāraṇābhedātkāryasyāpi pradīpasyābhedaprasaṅgāt |
[31,1]
atha vartisnehayoḥ kṣaya upalabhyate, pradīpasyāpi kṣīyamāṇadeśavyāptiviyogāt, sa eva kṣaya iti cet ? tailaṃ prabalamāsīdidānīmalpaṃ vartate | vartirapyevam |
pradīpo'pyanyānyatailavartibhāgaparihāreṇānyānyatadbhāgavyāpīti, sarvathā nivṛttistu kathamavasātuṃ śakyā, pratyabhijñānasya tadavasthatvāt ?
[31,2]
atha vartyādīnāmapacayakāle'vayave kriyotpadyate | tato vibhāgodayaḥ | tataḥ saṃyoganāśaḥ | tato'pi tadārabdhadravyanāśaḥ | punaḥ kriyā, saṃyogāt itaradravyodayaśceti naikadravyanirvāhasiddhiriti cet ? anubhavabhuvamavatarannapi yadyayaṃ prapañcam ādriyate, bauddho'pyevaṃ svaprakriyāmudghoṣayan kathaṃ vāryaḥ ? pūrvakebhyaḥ sabhāgahetubhyaḥ sahakāriṇamaparamarthamantato vātātapatimirādi samāsādya tebhyaḥ parasya samānaparimāṇasya yathā sahakāribalasaṅketaṃ nyūnasyādhikasya vā saṃbhava iti na sphaṭikaśatakoṭiprabhṛtīnāmekatānirvāhasiddhiḥ | yadā punaranena sādhanamevopanyastaṃ tadā nāsya prakriyayā siddhiḥ, tvatprakriyayā bādhā vā | vātādayaḥ kimupacinvanti apacinvanti vā sphaṭikādau, yena sahakāritayā kalpyante, prāgbhāvitvamātreṇa kāraṇatve'tiprasaṅgād iti cet — na vai sthūlaḥ kaścidupacayo'pacayo vā kriyate taistasya | ataevātyantasadṛśodayaḥ | sūkṣmastu aśakyopalakṣaṇatayā yathedaṃtayā nirdeṣṭumayogyaḥ, tathā niṣedhamapyayogya eva | evamanekavastusaṃkare kadācitkenacidupayoge na kiñcid vastu prastutopādānasya sahakāri syāditi na sarvathā sahakāryantaravirahādekasya jananasaṅgatiravagantavyā ityupanyāsasyārthaḥ | sthiratvasiddhau tu yadi tvamapi svaprakriyāṃ nirvāhayitumīśiṣe, īṣiṣya | bauddhasādhanavicārastāvat prastuto'yam | tatra ca prastute'nekakāryeṇānekena bhāvyamiti kena karṇe bhavato niveśitam, yataḥ pradīpadṛṣṭāntīkaraṇaṃ bhavataḥ śobheta ?
tadidamucyate, anyo vyādhiranyadauṣadhamiti |
[32,1]
yadapyāha, yadeva ca sahakāribhedena kāryabhede pradīpasyābhedasiddhau sādhanaṃ, tadeva kramavatsahakāribhedena kāryabhede'kramasyāpīti, tadapyatyantamasaṃbaddham | advayākāramindriyapratyakṣameva hi bhedabhraṃśamāśaṃsati pradīpe | sapratighasya hi pradīpasya naikasthānam |
bhinnadeśasya cātyantasadṛśasyāpi bhedopalakṣaṇamanivāryaṃ māyāgolakavat | ata ekākāramindriyajñānamekatāyāmeva pradīpamavasthāpayati | kālabhede hi bhinne'pi vastunyatyantasadṛśe pratyabhijñānamupajāyamānamupalabdham | na ca pratyabhijñānādanyadekatāsādhanam |
tatkathaṃ tadeva sādhanamiti na plavate ? na ca sadṛśatayā kālabhedena pratyabhijñānasya saṃśayāṅgatvaṃ vyabhicāradarśanāt, lakṣaṇabhedavirahāt | sakṛdabhedabhāsinyapi pratyakṣe'nāśvāsaḥ, tathā kvacidadarśanāt | indriyajñāne hi kramadarśane'pi na yogyamarthadvayaṃ pratighāti, ekībhūyopalabhyamānamupalabdham | tatkathaṃ sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ ? tasmādanupayogi pradīpadṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam |
[32,2]
etadeva rūpaṃ dṛṣṭāntīkṛtyābhiprāyāntaramasya dyotayan nyāyabhūṣaṇe'pi yadāha — api ca yena svabhāvena rūpaṃ rūpāntaraṃ karoti, na tenaiva rasādikam, rasāderapi rūpasvabhāvatāprasaṅgāt | tataḥ sarvaṃ rūpakāryaṃ cakṣuṣā gṛhyate | na caitadiṣṭam | tasmād yathā rūpaṃ rūpāntarotpādanasvabhāvena tadeva karoti, vijñānotpādanasvabhāvena vijñānameva karoti, na rūpādikam | rasotpādanasvabhāvena ca rasam evaṃ gandhasparśanajananasvabhāvābhyāṃ tābeva janayati | tadvadakṣaṇiko'pyādyakāryotpādanasvabhāvena tadeva karoti | taduttarakāryajananasvabhāvena taduttarameva janayati | nādyamuttarottaraṃ vā |
evamuttarottarakāryeṣvanantakālabhāviṣvapi pratiniyatāḥ svabhāvā draṣṭavyāḥ | svabhāvā eva hetavo na svabhāvītyapyayuktam, rūpasyāhetutvaprasaṅgāt, svabhāvānāmeva hetutvāt |
atha na rūpasya svabhāvabheda iṣyate, kiṃ tveka eva tathābhūtasvabhāvo, yena bhinnākāraṃ bhinnadeśaṃ kāryamutpādayati ? tasya bhinnasvabhāvakāryotpādānurodhena svabhāvabhedaḥ kathita iti |
[33,1]
nanvevaṃ paro'pyabhinnasvabhāvasyaivākṣaṇikasya kramabhāvyanekasvabhāvakāryotpādanānurodhena bhāvasvabhāvaṃ kalpayannopālambhamarhatīti |
[33,2]
etadapīrṣyākaṣāyitadhiyaḥ paradhandhīkaraṇamātram | tathāhi yadi tāvadabhinnātmāpi dīpavadanekamarthamandhakāranāśādi karoti kalpitasvabhāvabheda itīyanmātraṃ vivakṣitam, hanta ko niṣeddhā ? astyeṣa saṃbhavo yadanekamekaḥ karotīti | evaṃ pūrvāparakālayorapyekasvabhāvo yadyanekaṃ kuryānna vivādaḥ | kevalaṃ kvacit kāryavilambaḥ kvacidakṣepakarmeti na yuktam, pradīpavat sakṛdanekakaraṇamastviti vyarthaṃ pradīpanidarśanam | atha kramabhāvyanekamekātmanaḥ kāryamastviti vivakṣitam, tadā samartham | na khalvadyāpi dīpo dṛṣṭāntayituṃ śakyaḥ | evaṃ rūpe'pi nidarśane kriyamāṇe vaktavyam | nacaivaṃ nirvahati yadanekaṃ tadanekenaiva kartavyam, dīpakāryavat kālabhedabhāvi cānekaṃ kāryamiti, na hyanekaṃ jāyamānamekasyaiva kāryamāpadyate, ekakarturapāye bānekajanmaiva na syādityupapādayituṃ śakyam | dāhagāhanāderanekasyānekenaiva jalajvalanādinā karaṇadarśanāt | kālabhedābhinnamekaṃ vivakṣitamiti cet ? anekakālāntaritairekātmabhiranekaṃ na kriyamāṇamupalakṣayasi | evaṃ tu brūyāḥ, ekamanekaṃ vā bhinnakālamabhinnakālaṃ vā nityādeva jāyata iti | tacca pratijñāmātrāviṣkaraṇamabhīṣṭātmanaḥ kasyacidarthasya na sādhanaṃ, nāpi paraprayuktasādhanabādhanamiti kimanena ? tathāpi na dīparūpaduṣṭāntena kiñcit |
yadi ca kāryabhedenāpi bhāvaṃ bhindyādasthiravādī, tathāpi rūpamevābhidyamānaṃ bhidyamānau rūparasau kathaṃ janayatītīyanmātreṇānekāntamudbhāvya svastho bhava | rūpasyāpi punarekatvasādhanena ka upayogaḥ, siddhatvāt ?
[33,3]
tataḥ śaṃkaro'pi, na hi yena svabhāvena vartivikārasya hetuḥ, tenaiva jvālopalambhayorapi tatsvabhāvatāprasaṅgādityabhidadhāno na kiñciccetayata iti upalakṣyate, ekasyānekakaraṇāvirodhāt |
[33,4]
atha yathā bauddho'bhyadhāt kṣaṇāntare'pi yadi sa eva svabhāvo bhāvasya, tadā saṃpratīva prāgapi jananaprasaṅgaḥ | na ca janayati | tataḥ svabhāvabhedo bhāvasyeti | tathāhi, yadi jñānajanakenaiva rūpeṇa vartivikāraṃ karoti dīpaḥ, tadā tasyāpi tattvaprasaṅgaḥ | na ca tattvamasti | tato dīpo'pi kiṃ bhinnasvabhāvo'stu ? yathā ca kāryāṇāṃ tādātmyavirahe'pi hetubhedābhāvaḥ, tathā kāryāṇāṃ bhinnakālatve'pi na hetubheda iti vivakṣitam | tadāpi bauddhena pramāṇabalamālambya janakājanakāvasthayoḥ bhāvabheda āropitaḥ | tatra ca yadyakṣamā, tadā'siddhyādidūṣaṇameva vaktuṃ sāmpratam |
tāvataiva tasya nirāśe kimanena prabandhena ?
[34,1]
atha duṣṭameva tatsādhanam ? tathāpi tena yat siddhaṃ tat siddhameva tāvat |
pradīpasya svabhāvabhedo bhavatu, mā vā bhūt, tathāpi kimasyopanyāsena ? yacca dīpasya svabhāvabhedasādhanāya sādhanaṃ kāryāṇāṃ tādātmyaviraho nāma, so'pi yadi siddhasvasādhyapratibandhaḥ, tadā tena yadi yugapadapi bhedasiddhiḥ kasyacit, tadā tadorṣyayā kimanena bauddhasādhanena ? prayāgavaṭaprayātāyātayoḥ dvitīyamūḍhakarṇāṭeneva svasādhyasādhanāya pravṛttinirāśaḥ kartavyaḥ | anyathā'nena bhede sādhite pradīpabhedasādhanameva kiṃ pravartate, na vā kiñcidapi sādhanaṃ sādhyasādhanāya pravarteta dhūmādisādhanaṃ svasādhyasādhakaṃ dṛṣṭvā ||
[34,2]
athedaṃ pradīpasvabhāvabhedasādhanamadhyakṣādhikṣiptaṃ, svasādhyapratibandhavidhuraṃ vā, tadā tadeva naśyatu | na tadā bauddhasādhanasya kṣatiḥ | tathāpi kiṃ tasyopanyāsena ?
yadi bauddhasparddhayā tadvimarśamasārīkartumupamānabhūtaṃ vimarśāntaramevedamupanītam, tadāyamasthitaḥ pakṣaḥ svabhāvabhedo dīpasyeti | evaṃ sati eka evāsau śaktiviśeṣo yasteṣāmutpādaka iti cet ? etadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayābhyupagamyamānamapi na nītiśīlān prīṇāti | pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānābhāve teṣāṃ sarvatrotpatteradṛṣṭapūrvatvādityādinā | tathā svabhāvabhedābhāve ca kāraṇasya kāryabhedabhāve tasyākasmikatvaṃ prasajyeta | tathā cākaraṇaṃ viśvasya vaiśvarūpyaṃ syādityanena ca kathaṃ svabhāvabhedameva svabhāṣayā draḍhayet ? na cāyaṃ nyāyyaḥ | tathā hi yattāvaducyate, yadi yenaiva svabhāvena dīpo vartivikārahetustenaiva jvālādeḥ, tadā jvālāderapi vartivikāratvaprasaṅgaḥ, na caivam |
tasmādbhinnenaiva svabhāvena vartivikāre bhinnena ca jvālādau dīpaḥ pravartate iti viparyayārthaḥ | tatra ca pratyakṣabādhaiva, niraṃśasya dīpādestatra bhāsanāt | anyathā kadambagolakavadanantasvabhāvaparikaritasyābhāsaprasaṅgāt | na cānupalabhyatvameṣāmabhidhātuṃ śakyam, pradīpasvabhāvatve'nupalabhyatāyā virodhāt | yadi ca pradīpasvabhāvatve'pyadṛśyatvaṃ viruddhamanurudhyase vartivikārakāraṇatve'pi jvālādihetutāṃ kiṃ na saṃbhāvayasi, yataḥ svarūparāśiparikalpanavyagro'si ? tasmānnānupalabhyamānasya pradīpasvabhāvatā | upalabhyatve ca nādhyakṣadhikṣepaparihāraḥ | dīpādanyadeva dṛśyamadṛśyaṃ vā vastu dīpasvabhāva iti tu nāgalokabhāṣā | ananyarūpe hi svabhāvasvarūpasvalakṣaṇaśabdāḥ prasiddhāḥ | kalpanopasthāpite tu dharme bhinna ivābhāsamāne'pi tadadhyavasāyādeva svabhāvaśabdaprayogaḥ, yathā nityatvaṃ śabdasya svabhāva iti | tato yadi sahakāriṇi śaktiśabdavadbhinne'pi kvacit svabhāvaśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ, tathāpi svabhāvāntareṇa karotīti vastvantareṇa sahakāriṇā karotīti yāvat | na ca svabhāvinaḥ karaṇavāraṇamabhimatam |
tataḥ svabhāviśabdo bāhyo'rthaḥ | tena svabhāvenābhinnenaiva bhinnāni kāryāṇi karotītyāyātam | kevalamanekasahakāriparivārita iti viśeṣaḥ | sa ca kasya neṣṭaḥ ? na ca sahakāriṇo'pi svamanīṣikayā kalpanīyāḥ, kiṃ tu yāvanto'nvayavyatirekagrāhakapramāṇavyāpārāstāvanta eva | sa ca vyāpāraḥ tejastailavartyādivyatiriktasya nāstīti kimadhikavidhānena ? pratyuta svabhāvaśabdābhidheyānarthān parikalpya ṣaṭpadārthyāmantarbhāvayan kiṃ viphalamāyāsyasi ? yadā caivaṃ paryante svabhāvaśabdābhidheyaṃ nijaṃ rūpamekamevānekakāryaheturiti upapāditam tadā, yadekena rūpeṇa janitaṃ, tadekameveti na siddhā vyāptiḥ |
tathā sati prasaṅgavadviparyayasyāpi nānekāntaparihāraḥ | pratiniyatasvabhāvopādānatāpi teṣāṃ na pradīpasyaiva tāttvikānekasvabhāvatayā, kiṃ tu tatsāmagryāmapoddhāradvāreṇānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ kasyacittailaṃ kasyacid vartiḥ kasyacid dīpa iti kathaṃ sarvatrotpattireṣāmupalabhyate ?
[35,1]
yattu kāraṇabhedād bheda iti, tatra sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇavaijātyāt kāryavaijātyanimittābhyupagamaḥ, tathaiva pramāṇenārpaṇāt | na tu sāmagryantargatakāraṇanānātvamekasyānekasvabhāvatayeti śāstra eva vipañcitam | tadalameṣāṃ pramāṇanirapekṣasvotprekṣāmātreṇa vikalpeṣu nirbandhena | na ca taiḥ svabhāvabhedairbhāvikaḥ siddharapyeṣāṃ kācidarthasiddhirityuktamevetyaphala evaiṣa bhāvaḥ |
[36,1]
yathā tarhi trilocanaścaryayati tathānayorapi nīyatāmabhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca nyāyamañjarī, asādhāraṇamapi sattvaṃ mādhyamikanyāyena śakyamudbhāvayitum |
tathā hi, kṣaṇavāde'pi pūrvarūpakṣaṇo yena svabhāvenānantarakṣaṇamutpādayati, kiṃ tenaiva rasakṣaṇamapyāhosvit svabhāvāntareṇa ? yadi tenaiva, rasasyāpi rūpatvaprasaṅgaḥ |
na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāmaḥ, viśvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt | atha svabhāvāntareṇa karoti ? yadyevamekasya viruddhaṃ, svabhāvadvayaṃ prasajyeta | rūpajananasvabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvānnāvyabhicārī | tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavet, bhavettatraiva tasya bhāvo'bhāvaśca | bhāvābhāvau ca sākṣādviruddhau pūrvakaṃ rūpalakṣaṇaṃ bhintaḥ | na ca bhinno dṛśyate saḥ |
[36,2]
syādetat | pūrvakasya rūpakṣaṇasya rase kartavye svabhāvāntaraṃ pūrvaka eva rasakṣaṇo, na ca viruddhaṃ svabhāvāntaramastīti | yadyevamakṣaṇikasyāpi kramavatīṣu kāryavyaktiṣu svabhāvāntaraṃ kramavat sahakāryantarameveti sarvaṃ samānamanyatrābhiniveśāt |
tasmādasādhāraṇamupādadānasya svabhāvabhedāpatteḥ kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvam | yena ca prakāreṇa svabhāvabhedo nirākriyate, tasyākṣaṇikatve'pi samānatvāt sattvamakṣaṇikānna nivartate | ato vyatirekāsiddheḥ pratibandhāsiddhiriti |
[36,3]
tatra tāvad yogācāraniṣṭhāmanālocayannayaṃ saugatasamayajñānābhimānī mādhyamikanyāyenetyāha — ubhayorapi hetuphalāpavādasya tattvato'bhimatatvādityadharasiddhimuddhūya sākārasiddhau darśitameva | sthite ca hetuphalabhāve'smākamiyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgacintetyuktam |
sā ca sthitigrahyigrāhakabhāvasya tāttvikatve gṛhīte | tadā ca yadeva yasyānvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi, tadeva kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca bhavatu bījāṅkuravat | yathā ca kasyacidekamanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi dṛśyamānaṃ kāryaṃ, tathā yadyanekamapi kasyacidekasyānvayavyatirekāvanuvidhīyamānamupalabhyate, tadā kimanekenāpyekakāryeṇa bhavitavyam ?
paravedanāpalāpe hi ekamapyekasya kāryaṃ na syāt | anapalāpe tvanekamapi kāryamekasya kena vāryate ? ataḥ paravedanāpavādivādimatāvatāraṇena na kiñcit | grāhyagrāhakasthitau tvekavadanekasyāpyekakāryatānyāyaḥ samānaḥ | tatkathamekātmanā janyamānamekākārameva bhavediti plavate ?
[37,1]
yattūktam — nahyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇātkāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti, tadatisāhasam | kiṃ vā na paśyati pradīpamekaṃ vikārakāriṇamandhakārahāriṇaṃ ca, taraṇiṃ vā tamaḥkamalayornidhanapravodhavidhāyinam ? sarvadāndhakāramagno vā bhavān paśyati vā sahasramaṃśumālinaḥ kāryasahasrakāriṇaḥ ? ekasvabhāvāt tu kāraṇānna kāryabheda iti samānasāmagryā na kāryavaijātyamityarthaḥ | ataeva na viśvasyāhetukatvam | tasmādekasmādanekotpattiravirodhinī | kāryadvāreṇa tu rūpaṃ rūpakāraṇaṃ rasakāraṇaṃ ceti samuccayena svabhāvadvayavyavahāraḥ | ataeva na virodhavārtā | nahi samuccaye pramāṇasiddhe virodhagandhaḥ | vātātapayorivaikasminnākāśadeśe ||
[37,2]
yattūktam — rūpajananasvabhāvo hi rasajananasvabhāvatāvyabhicārīti, tāvatāpi bhedamātraṃ sidhyati, na tu virodhaḥ, kṛtakānityavat | yathāhi nīlābhāvāvyabhicāri pītaṃ na nīlaṃ bhavitumarhati, na tu tanmātreṇa virodhaḥ | na hi yad yato bhidyate tadaśeṣaṃ tena viruddhamabhidhātuṃ śakyam | virodhastu yadyapyekasmin dharmiṇi dvayorasaṃbhavayorniyamaḥ, sa ca kadācid vastunorekasya bhāve'nyaparyādānād dahanatuhinavat | kadāciddharmayoḥ svabhāvenaiva ekādhiṣṭhite'nyāsaṃbhavāt bhāvābhāvavat, nīlatvānīlatvavad vā | tatra yadi nīlapītadravyayorapyekabhāve'nyaparyādānamāpādayet, syādeva sahānavasthānanāmā virodhaḥ | na tu tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa | bhedamātraṃ tu tāvatā | evaṃ nīlatvapītatvayorapyabhāvavyabhicāramātreṇa bhedamātraṃ tu na tu virodhaḥ | virodhastu nīlatvasvīkṛte dharmiṇi svayamevānīlatvabhedasya pītatvasyābhāvāt | anyathā kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāmapi tadabhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodhaprasaṅgāt |
[37,3]
atha kathamatra tadabhāvāvyabhicāraḥ ? na hi kṛtakena satā nānityena bhāvyamityupapattirasti | yadyevaṃ rūpajanakena satā rasajanakena na bhāvyamityatrāpi kopapattiḥ ?
rūpajanakatvādeveti cet — na, ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇe kṣīṇatvādupapatteḥ, anyayogavyavacchedasyāsiddhatvāt | tathāhi kiṃ rūpasya janakameva ? atha rūpasyaiva janakamiti rūpajanakam ? tatra prathamapakṣe rūpaṃ pratyajanakatvasyaiva vyavacchedo na punaranyajanakatvasya vyavacchedo vidhirveti, sādhanāntaramapekṣya tenaiva virodhe vyavacchedasyaiva asiddheḥ |
dvitīye tu pakṣe, anyajananakṣepasiddhirasandigdhā | kevalaṃ na tatra pramāṇavyāpāraḥ | yathā hyekasya tannāntaroyakatvaṃ tathā dvitīyasyāpi yadi syānna doṣaḥ, pradīpavat | na tu rūpajanakamityeva rasajanakapratikṣepo, rūpajanakatvasyāyogavyavacchedenāpi caritārthatvāditi na kāpyupapattiratrāpi | kevalaṃ kalpanābuddhau yathārthāntaramiva rūpajanakatvaṃ pratibhāti, tathā tadabhāvāvyabhicāri ca pṛthageva rasajanakatvamavasīyate | yataḥ pṛthak śabdapramāṇavṛttiḥ apekṣyate, tāvataiva virodhamadhyavasyati | sāvagatiḥkṛtakatvānityatvayorapi na vyavasīyate kenāpi | nāpi tatra virodhābhidhānena kaścidupayogaḥ | ekatra dharmiṇyaparaparihārārthameva hi virodhaḥ sādhyate | tad yadi virodhe'pyekadharmisamparkaḥ, kṛtaṃ virodhacintayā | nīlatvānīlatvādiṣu tu prayujyate parasparaparihārātmā virodhaḥ |
[38,1]
nanuparasparābhāvāvyabhicārāviśeṣe'pi kathaṃ keṣāñcid dharmāṇāmekadharmiṇyanavasthānātmā virodhaḥ, keṣāñcit punarbhedamātraṃ na virodhaḥ ? uktamatra, yadvyavacchedena yasya vidhānaṃ yadvidhānena vā yasya vyavacchedo niyamena, tattena pratiyoginā viruddham | yatra neyaṃ gatiḥ, tadaviruddhamityalaṃ punaḥ pariśrameṇa | tadevaṃ rūpajananarasajananayoḥ parasparābhāvāvyabhicāre'pi kṛtakatvānityatvavad bhedamātraṃ śabdapramāṇāntarākarṣi, na tu virodha iti sthitam |
[38,2]
yattūktam — tatra yadi svabhāvāntaraṃ bhavedityādi | sa tarhi nyāyaḥ kiṃ kṛtakānityatvābhyāṃ bibheti ? prasaṅga eva tatrāpi bhavatviti cet ? nanu parābhyupagamena prasaṅgaḥ, na ca mayedamaṅgīkṛtaṃ parasparābhāvāvyabhicāramātreṇa virodha ekatrānavasthānaheturiti | kiṃ tavaiṣo'bhyupagamaḥ pramāṇavṛttirvā ? ubhayathā'pi na mamāparādhaḥ |
sidhyatutarāṃ ca kṛtakatvānityādīnāṃ virodho, na caivaṃ tasmātparasparāvyabhicārasya tādātmyaniṣedhe vyāpārāt na kṛtakatvamevānityatvam | aniṣedhe tvekasyaiva kṛtakatvasya bhāvo'bhāvaśca syāt | yathā vastuno nīlādanīlasyāvyavacchede tasyaiva bhāvo'bhāvaśca svīkṛtaḥ syādityucyate | nīlamiti hi tasya bhāvaḥ | anīlamiti cābhāvaḥ tadabhāvavyāptasyānīlasya bhāvo na vyāpakaṃ tadabhāvamanākṛṣya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ, bhāvābhāvayośca virodhaḥ prasādhita evetyekadharmiṇyanavasthānamiti yannīlaṃ tannānīlaṃ pītādivastu, tathā dharmo'pi yatkṛtakatvaṃ, tannākṛtakatvamanityatvādi | yadrūpajananaṃ tannārūpajananaṃ rasajananādi | anyathaikatra kṛtakatvarūpajananādau śabdapramāṇapravṛttāvanyatrānityatvarasajananādau pramāṇāntarānapekṣāprasaṅgaḥ |
[39,1]
tasmāt tādātmye bhāvo'bhāvaścaikatra syāditi doṣaḥ | na tadādhāratve |
tau hi parasparaṃ bhinnau dharmau yadyekatra syātāṃ, kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? bhāvābhāvadoṣasya bhedasādhanenaiva caritārthatvāt | śāstre'pi hi viruddhadharmādhyāso bheda ukto, na virodhaḥ | virodhalakṣaṇaṃ tvanyat prasiddhameva | tādātmyaniṣedho'pi viśeṣaṇānapekṣasvabhāvānupalambhādukto na viruddhopalambhāt | tadevaṃ bhāvābhāvalakṣaṇaviruddhadharmasaṃsargāt taddharmitvena bhāsamānau dharmāveva bhinnau bhavata iti na tayorapi dharmivastunornānādharmayogamātreṇa bhedavārtā | yadā punastathā bhidyamānāveva dharmau yathoktaparasparapratidvandvinau bhavatastadā taddharmiṇo'pi bhedaḥ, nīlatvānīlatvabhāvābhāvadharmivat, ekakāryaṃ prati jananājananavacca | tasmād bhāvābhāvau sākṣād viruddhau rūpajanakatvarasajanakatvalakṣaṇau dharmāveva svadharmitvenābhāsamānau bhintaḥ | na tayorapyādhāraṃ prācīnavirūpalakṣaṇam, svayaṃ virodhābhāvāt | ata eva na bhinnau dṛśyate saḥ, ekakāryajanakājanakatve ca svayaṃ pratyanīkatayā svadharmiṇaṃ bhinta eva, abhedadarśanaṃ ca pratyanīkāvasāyena virodhī yata iti anumānavṛttiśceti sarvamanavadyam ||
[39,2]
ayaṃ tu svayameva na hyekasvabhāvāt kāraṇāt kāryabhedaṃ paśyāma iti, na ca bhinno dṛśyate sa iti ca brūvannasvastha eva na nirbandhayogyaḥ | tasmānnaikasvabhāvāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ kāryavaijātyamityavirodhaḥ | na tu svabhāvaparamparārahitāditi | tadevaṃ svabhāvasandehāpohād yaduktam, kṣaṇikebhyo nivartamānaṃ sattvamasādhāraṇamupādadānasya svabhāvabhedāpattiriti tannirastam |
[40,1]
kālpanika iva bhedapratibhāso na tāttviko bhedaḥ | kiṃ ca tāttvikasvabhāvabhedāpattāvapi sattvamasādhāraṇamiti śraddhāvadheyameva | na hi vastūnāṃ parimāṇātirekeṇa nityādiva kṣaṇikādapi vyāvṛttaṃ bhavati sattvam, yato'sādhāraṇamavadhāryeta | svabhāvabhūmani kaścinnityo'pi syāditi cet ? tamanupatattarhi sattvaṃ sādhāraṇamanaikāntikamāśaṅkyatām | tacca cintyam | bādhakānāṃ vyāttavadanānāṃ saṃbhavāt |
[40,2]
atha svabhāvaparamparāsaṃbhave bhāvasyeva paribhavāt kasya kṣaṇikatvamiti kṣaṇikādapi vyāvṛttamucyate, tadapi nāsti | svayameva svabhāvebhyo bhinnasya svabhāvinaḥ kriyāsamarthanena rakṣāvidhānāt | na ca svabhāvabhedasaṃbhave mūlasya kṣayo'pi yuktaḥ, aparimitopādhisaṃbhave'pi tadvato vyayāniṣṭaḥ | asmaddarśane'pi yadi nāma vastvantararāśerudayaḥ, tathāpi prakṛtabhāvasya kīdṛśī kṣayopapattiriti vyaktametat | sa tu rāśiḥ pramāṇamanviyānnaveti cintyam | bhavatu vā mūlāpalāpaḥ | ye tu svabhāvā bhāvikā iṣṭāḥ tadātmani magnatvānmūlasyaikaṃ pṛthak sat kṣaṇikaṃ mā bhūt | bhūyāṃsastu kṣaṇikāḥ santa ityupacaya eva kṣaṇikatāyāḥ, kathaṃ kṣaṇikatāyāḥ sattvavyāvṛttiḥ ?
tadevamevaṃvidhāḥ pralāpā grāmyajanajanitamahimānasteṣveva śobhante, na tarkakarkaśakuśāgrīyabuddhiṣu bauddheṣu | yā tu śikṣā svabhāvabhedasādhanāya syādetadityādiḥ saiṣāmevāstu, anyo'nyasya svabhāva iti svasthasya vaktumaśakteḥ | svabhāvabhedastu sādhanāsaṃbhavādadhyakṣabādhanācca parihṛta eva | na ca bhavannapi prakṛtadoṣasaṃsparśī | nāpi sahakāryantarameva svabhāvāntaramiti dantaniṣkoṣikayā svabhāvabhedasādhanā hetavo viparyāsayituṃ śakyante | kṣaṇikavādī hi sahakāriṇaḥ paśyanneva prasiddhasvabhāvabhedasādhanāya sādhanamupanyasya na kathamapyanena vacasā pratārayituṃ śakyaḥ | tadvaraṃ tatsādhanamasādhanameveti mukhyamākhyāyatāniṣṭasiddhavyāghātāditi |
[41,1]
tatra coktamasmābhiḥ | na ca sahakārisādhanāyaiva pratyavasthāturayaṃ prayatnaḥ | kāryeṇānubhūtānvayavyatirekā hi sahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣādipramāṇasiddhā eva kimatra sādhyam ? tato'kṣaṇikābhimatasya kramavatīṣu kāryavyaktiṣu svalakṣaṇabhedasādhana upanyaste dūṣaṇamanuktvā sahakāryantarameva svabhāvabheda iti lapanaṃ yadi svahṛdayasantoṣamālambeta, ālambatām | na tu parasādhyaṃ bādhitamanena | tasmāt siddhamarthakriyākāritvamasthairyeṇa vyāptamiti ||
[41,2]
yadapyanenoktam — kiṃ cedaṃ tāvadayaṃ kṣaṇikavādī praṣṭavyaḥ | pūrvasya kṣaṇasyottarasminnekasantānavartini kṣaṇe kartavye nānyat kiñcidapekṣaṇīyamasti | tataśca parotpatti pratyanapekṣatvāt tanmātrānubaddhenottareṇāpi satyeva tasmin bhavitavyam | abhavan vā tanmātrānubaddho na syāt, api tu nimittāntarāpekṣo vijñāyeta | asabhāgotpattau tu pūrve samānasantānavartina ekasantānāntarbhūtatvāviśeṣāt samarthā asamarthā vā bhaveyuḥ | tena santānāntaravartikṣaṇapratibandhasāmarthyaḥ sāpekṣaḥ kṣaṇaḥ syāt | na tu sabhāgakṣaṇapratibandhotpattau | tathā ca sati pūrvakṣaṇasattāmātrānubandhitvāviśeṣāduttarottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ paurvāparyaṃ tyaktvā yugapadutpadyeta | tataśca prabandhāpekṣakāryakṣaṇakālabhāvināṃ kṣaṇānāṃ prabandha ucchidyeta | tataśca trailokyavartisakalavastusantānabhāvināmanenaiva paryāyeṇa prabandhocchedādanyonyasaṃpīḍitā kṛtsnā trilokī prasajyeta |
[41,3]
athāpi samayasamayabhāvitvāt savyetaragoviṣāṇayoriva kāryakāraṇabhāvo nāstītyucyate, yadyevamatīte kṣaṇe pūrvasmin vastvantara utpadyeta, sati ca notpadyeta ityapūrvo'yamanvayavyatirekānugamaprakāraḥ | etayāpi dvārā kṣaṇikānāmarthakriyākāritvamevānupapannamiti ||
[41,4]
tadapi sarvamasaṃbaddham | tathāhi yat tāvat pūrvasyottare kartavye nānyatra kvacidapekṣeti, tatra sabhāgā uttare sarva eva kṣaṇā abhipretā bhavataḥ | anyathā sarveṣāṃ yaugapadyaprasañjanamanupapannaṃ syāt | tatra yadi svābhiprāye dūṣaṇaṃ tadā na kaścid vipakṣaḥ |
atha saugata eva praṣṭavyaḥ, tadā pūrvasya uttarasminnanantara eva kṣaṇe kartavye nirapekṣatvaṃ, nottare kṣaṇe | sa eva tarhi tasya svabhāvo nāsti yastadutpādakaḥ | tataḥ svabhāvasāpekṣatvātkathamanapekṣaḥ ? sa tarhi svabhāvaḥ kadācidasya bhāvī, na bhāvī tarhi tadapekṣa iti vācoyukteḥ ko'rthaḥ ? ayamarthaḥ | yaducyate devadatto'tra kārye yajñadattāpekṣaḥ samartha iti | tatra dvayaṃ pratīyate, svayamasamartha iti, yajñadattena saha samartha iti ca | na ca sarvo vyavahārastattvānurodhī | kiṃ tu kvacit kiñcit satyam | tadatrāpi svayamasamartha ityayamaṃśa ubhayasaṃmatatvād durapahnavaḥ | sa eva paścādanyena saha samartha ityatra tu vivādaḥ | ataeva sādhane bādhanāvatāraḥ | atastadaṃśāsiddheḥ tadapekṣaṃ svayaṃśabdamapyapanīya kvacit sāpekṣa ityasamartha ityevārthaḥ | tata uttarottare karttavye asaṃbhavini tadutpādanasvabhāve sāpekṣa iti ko'rthaḥ ? uttarottarakartavye samarthaḥ | tadatra yad dūṣaṇaṃ taducyatām |
[42,1]
syādetat | uttarasvarūpāviśiṣṭamuttarottaram, tataḥ pūrvaṃ yathottare śaktaṃ tathottarottare'pi | uttarottare aśaktaḥ taduttare'pi kathaṃ śaktaḥ syāt, ekasvabhāvatvād dvayoriti ?
[42,2]
