tadapyasaṃgatam, ekasvabhāvatvāsiddheḥ | sabhāgakṣaṇaparamparāpekṣayā siddhamekasvabhāvatvamiti cet — na, sarvathā sabhāgatvāsiddheḥ | sajātīyārtho hi sabhāgārthaḥ |
sajātīyatvaṃ ca vividham | rūpataḥ śaktita ubhayataśceti | tatra yadyapi rūpamātrakṛtaṃ sajātīyatvamuttarasyottareṇa, tathāpi sāmarthyakṛtaṃ nāsti | tataḥ kṛtaṃ vijātīyatvameva |
ataeva bījādīnāṃ svabhāvapariṇāmaparamparayā kiyatyāpyaṅkurakāryaniṣpattiḥ | tatra hi antimasya bījakṣaṇasyāṅkure śaktiḥ | antime punarupāntyasyopāntye ca tatpūrvasyetyevaṃ yāvatprathamabījasaṃbhavaḥ | evaṃ sahakārisāmagryapi tatrāparāparāviśiṣṭaiveti veditavyam |
ataevāparāparapratyayayogena pratikṣaṇabhinnaśaktayaḥ saṃtanvantaḥ saṃskārā yadyapi kutaścit sāmyāt sarūpāḥ pratīyante, tathāpi bhinna evaiṣāṃ svabhāvastena kiñcideva kasyacit kāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ veti nyāyaḥ | tataḥ sarvathā sabhāgatvavirahāt pūrvasyottarakṣaṇajananasāmarthye'pi nottarottarajananamasya, tataḥ śaktiviśeṣeṇa viśeṣāt | tathā tasyāpyanyasmāt śakterupacayo'pacayo vā ? ubhayorapi viśeṣa evocyate | viśiṣyate'nyasmāditi | tat kathamekakṣaṇa eva sarveṣāṃ sabhāgābhimatakṣaṇānāmupanipātacodyāvakāśaḥ ?
anvayavyatirekotprāso'pi paścimo duścaritameva | kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanasāmarthyākadarthane hi yadekānantaramanyajanma, sa evānvayaḥ | yacca tatkāraṇasya prāgasaṃbhave'saṃbhava eva deśakālāntare kāryasya, sa eva vyatireka iti kimatra kriyatāmanicchatāpi ? nityavādino'pi hi na sahaiva hetuphalayorjanma | kiṃ tu hetujanmānantaraṃ phalasya janma |
yatkṣaṇācca kāraṇasya kāryamudayavat tataḥ prāk paścād vā saṃbhave kāraṇasya kāryasya ka upakāraḥ ? tatkṣaṇāntaramasya janmeti tāvataiva kṛtārthatvāt kāryasya tāvataivānvayaḥ, tadabhāve'bhāvaśceti vyatirekaśca | kevalaṃ tatkṣaṇāt prāk paścādapi kāraṇābhimatasya bhāvaḥ pramāṇopanītena kāryānupayogamātreṇa parihartuṃ śakya iti tāvannityavādino viśeṣaḥ | sa ca vicāritaḥ | anvayavyatirekau tu yathoktamātreṇeti sthitam ||
[43,1]
yadapi sattvasyāsādhāraṇatāṃ pratijñāya ekasmādanekasmādekamanekaṃ votpadyata iti vimṛśyānekasmādanekotpattipakṣaṃ sthitamādāyovāca vācaspatiḥ, kiṃ pūrve kṣaṇā uttareṣāṃ kṣaṇānāṃ parasparaṃ nirapekṣā eva janakā āhosvit sāpekṣā iti |
[43,2]
nanūktamantyakṣaṇaprāptāḥ parasparamanapekṣāḥ kāryāṇi janayantīti | tat kimanabhyupetāropaprapañcena ? tat kimidānīṃ samarthabījakṣaṇajanako'pi tajjanane bījakṣaṇo'napekṣa eva ? omiti brūmaḥ | hantānena prakāreṇa sarva eva bījakṣaṇā nirapekṣāḥ kāryajanana iti kṛtaṃ sahakāribhiḥ | nanūktaṃ naite prekṣāvantaḥ kiṃ tu svapratyayādhīnaniyatasannidhayo na kṣaṇamapi vyavadherīśata iti | tat kimayaṃ kṛṣībalo'pi na prekṣāvān, yaḥ kuśūlādapanīya bījamāvapati bhūmau parikarṣitāyāṃ kṣityādisahabhāvena evātiśayītpādaparamparayā aṅku rajananasāmarthyād bījasya | kuśūlasthād vatsaraśatenāpi tadadarśanāt tatrāvapatīti cet ? atha kimayaṃ na svasantānamātraprabhavaḥ samartho bījakṣaṇaḥ ? tathā cet, kathaṃ santānāntaraṃ sahakāri nāpekṣeta kāryakaraṇe ?
[44,1]
nanvapekṣata eva kiṃ tu svotpāde, na punaḥ svakārye | tatra tasyānapekṣatvamucyate, na tu svotpattau | nanu svotpattāvapyasya svasantānavartī jāgarti pūrva eva nirapekṣaḥ kṣaṇaḥ ?
evaṃ tasya tasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ svasantānapatita evānapekṣo jāgarti janana iti kuśūlanihitabīja eva syāt kṛtī kṛṣīvalaḥ | kṛtamasya prekṣāvataḥ kṛṣikarmaṇā duḥkhākareṇeti |
[44,2]
yadi manyeta dvividhamiha kāryaṃ, ekaṃ sahakāribhirāhitātiśayaviśeṣaparamparāprasavadharmakam, dvitīyaṃ sahakāryatiśayanirapekṣajanakam | yatrāṅkaro'tiśayaviśeṣaparamparāpekṣajanmā | ādyātiśayastu sahakārikṛtātiśayaparamparānirapekṣotpādaḥ |
na caitadubhayavidhamapi kāryaṃ bījasya svasantānamātrādutpattimarhati | kṣityādisantānāntarāpekṣameva bījaṃ svasantānavarti, bhinnasantānavarti vā kādācitkaṃ kāryaṃ karotīti kalpate kṛṣikarmaṃ, santānāntarāṇi tu kādācitkakāryotpattau ye sahakāripratyayāḥ, ta eva yathāṅkurotpattau sahakāriṇo bījasya sāmarthyaprabodhe hetavaḥ kadācit teṣāṃ kṣityādīnāṃ ye'pi jananahetavaḥ ta eva sāmarthyahetavo bhavanti, yathā bījādīnāmādyātiśayotpādane sāmarthyaprabodhahetava upasarpaṇapratyayāḥ | sarvathā santānāntarairanāhitātiśayaṃ na bījaṃ kāryaviśeṣaṃ kādācitkaṃ karoti | sāmarthyaprabodhahetavaśca dvaye sahakāripratyayā upasarpaṇapratyayāśceti |
[44,3]
tadanupapannam | tathāhi bhavatu tathā dvividhaṃ kāryam | astu ca tatkādācitkatvāt santānāntarāpekṣam | apekṣārthaśca vaktavyaḥ | kāraṇasya svasāmarthyaprabodha iti cet ? nanu sāmarthyatatprabodhayoḥ samarthabhāvatattvāvyatirekāt samarthapratyayotpāda ityuktaṃ bhavati | tathā ca svotpādāpekṣitakāraṇaṃ sahakāripratyayāt satyam abhyupagama eva doṣatvena codyate | athāyamaṅkurajananasamartho vā kṣaṇaḥ, ādyātiśayo vā kiṃ nirapekṣeṇa svasantānamātrajanmanā pūrvakṣaṇena janyate, na punaḥ svasantānamātrajanmanā, asyāpi pūrvasmādeva puñjādutpatteḥ |
[45,1]
nanu samānaśaktyā kuśūlajanmasu bījasantāneṣu kasmāt kiñcideva bījaṃ paramparayā'ṅkuropajananānuguṇamupajanayati bījakṣaṇam, nānye bījakṣaṇā bhinnasantānāntaḥpātinaḥ ? na khalūpasarpaṇapratyayāt prāgeteṣāṃ samānāsamānasantānavartināṃ kaścit paramparātiśayo bījakṣaṇānām | arthopasarpaṇapratyayāt prāṅ na tatsantānavartino janayanti paramparayāpyaṅkuropajananānuguṇaṃ bījakṣaṇam, bījamātrajananātteṣām | kasyacid bījakṣaṇasyopasarpaṇapratyayasahabhuva ādyātiśayotpādaḥ | hanta tarhi tadabhāve satyutpanno'pi janayedeva | na cāsyopasarpaṇapratyayena sahabhāvaniyamaḥ, atatsantānānāṃ kuśūlavartināṃ bījakṣaṇānāṃ tena saha samānayogakṣemāṇāmabhyupasarpaṇapratyayasahabhāvābhāvāt, kṣaṇasya caikasya kṣaṇāntareṇaikena kāryakāraṇaniścayābhāvāt | sāmānyaviṣayotpādānvayavyatirekayostatraivopapatteḥ | tathā ca kevalānāṃ vyabhicārasaṃbhavādādyātiśayotpādamaṅkuraṃ vā prati kṣityādīnāṃ parasparāpekṣatvamevotpādakatvamakāmenāpyaṅgīkartavyamiti |
[45,2]
tadapi prācīnacarcayā nirastaprāyam | tathāhi yadi nāma parasparāpekṣāṇāmevotpādakatvametāvatā samarthitaṃ, prastute kimāyātam ? atha samānakālabhāvināṃ parasparopakāramantareṇāpi parasparāpekṣatvamupalabdham ? evamakṣaṇikasyāpi sahakāriṣvanupakāriṣu tyakṣyate iti kadācit kasyacit karaṇasaṃbhāvanāyāmāyāsasaṃbhavinī nityād vyāvṛttiḥ satyasyetyabhiprāyaḥ | yadyevaṃ kathamasādhāraṇatāpratijñānirvāhaḥ ? sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamevābhidhātumucitam ||
[45,3]
atha kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣu nāpekṣā nānapekṣā yukteti vyavasthitam, vakṣyate ca purastādayamabhiprāyaḥ, tato'pekṣānapekṣābhyāṃ vyāptamarthakriyākāritvamanityācca tadabhāvād vyāvartate | sthirācca kramayaugapadyavirahād vyāvartate tvanmateneti vyaktamasādhāraṇam | tathā ca na kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣvapekṣā upakārābhāvāt, nāpyanapekṣā, tāmantareṇa kāraṇābhāvāditi siddho vyāpakābhāvaḥ |
[45,4]
tadapi yatkiñcit | tathā hi kīdṛśamapekṣārthamādāyedamucyate ? yadi tāvat sahakāriṇamapekṣata iti sahakāriṇopakartavya ityarthaḥ, tadā tadabhāvādanapekṣaiva kṣaṇikasya kathamubhayavyāvṛttiḥ ? sahakāribhedamantareṇa karaṇānupapattistu kṣaṇāntare svayamabhāvādeva |
[46,1]
atha tadvā tādṛgvā āsīditi na kaścidviśeṣaḥ, tataḥ tādṛksvabhāvasaṃbhave'pyakaraṇaṃ sahakāriṇi nirapekṣānna kṣamata iti cet — asaṃbaddhametat, akartustādṛksvabhāvatāyā virahāt | yadevānantarakāryamaparyāsitaśaktisakalasahakārimadhyamadhyāsīnasya svarūpaṃ tadeva yadi deśakālāntare'pi, hanta tadvadeva karaṇakṣamatvam | na ca varṇasaṃsthānamātrasāmye ca sāmyaṃ bījāntarāṇāṃ bhavitumarhati | dṛśyante hyākārasāmye'pi phalasadbhāvādibhedena bhāvānāṃ bhinnavyavasthitayaḥ, tathā śaktibhedenāpi syuḥ |
pākopacaye harītakīvat | sa tu svabhāvabhedasteṣāṃ bījatve sādhāraṇe'pi kuta iti praśne'pi kāraṇasāmagrīśaktibheda eva śaraṇaṃ kathañcit sāmyapratītāvapīti darśitamaparāparapratyayetyādiprastāve |
[46,2]
tato yaduktam, nanu samānakuśūlajanmasvityādi, tadapāstam | yasya hi dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagrīpariṇāme paramparāyātaḥ svabhāvabhedo bījasyopasarpaṇapratyayasahakāribhāvabhūmiḥ, tat pariṇāmaparamparayā janayatyādyamatiśayamaṅkuraṃ vā | nānye bījakṣaṇāstathābhūtahetuparamparāviraheṇa tatsvabhāvābhāvāt | nanvekatra kṣetre niṣpattilavanādipūrvakamānīya kuśūle kṣiptāni sarvāṇyeva bījāni sādhāraṇarūpāṇi pratīyante tat kutastyo'mukabījasaṃbhavī viśeṣo nānyeṣām ? ataścaivaṃ, yato hi kṣetralavanāya karasparśastasyaiva sa svabhāvaḥ, paścādanyeṣāmapi nayane taddarśanāt | tat kathamasya samasvabhāvatvamapahnotuṃ śakyate ? iti |
[46,3]
atrocyate | kāraṇaṃ khalu sarvatra dvividham — dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ ceti sarvāstikasiddhametat | tatrādṛṣṭaṃ karmasvabhāvamanyajanmajanitamadarśanaikaniyataṃ kāryavaicitryadarśanādanumitavaicitryam | dṛṣṭaṃ punaraihalaukikasvabhāvaṃ dṛśyamadṛśyaṃ ceti dvedhā | tacca pratyekam acetanasamavetaṃ ceti caturdhā bhavati | tadevaṃ na hetusāmagrī sarvā sarvākāreṇa pratyakṣā puruṣamātrasya |
[46,4]
tathā ca trilocanaḥ | kaścit sahakāripratyayaḥ pratyakṣaḥ parokṣaścetaraḥ | tataśca pratyakṣaparokṣasahakāripratyayasākalyamasarvavidā pratyakṣato na śakyaṃ pratipattumiti |
yadaṃśenāpi sā sāmagrī pratyakṣā tatrāpyavāntarasūkṣmabhedaparigaṇanāya na samarthaḥ pṛthagjanaḥ sthuladarśitvāt | tato bhavedapi tādṛśasvabhāvabhedaḥ keṣāñcidvījānāmupalabdhakarmakarapāṇipraṇayānāṃ yaḥ paramparayā prakṛtakāryamarjitumūrjasvī, yaśca nānyeṣāṃ tadekakuśūlasthānāmapi, na cainamanviyāllokaḥ | na cānavadhāraṇamātreṇa tadabhāvaḥ, saṃśayastu syāt | sa ca kāryeṇa karasparśeṇa na bhavatā paribhūyate | tathācaikaśarīrāvayavānāmavibhaktamātāpitṛsaṃyogādisāmagrīsaṃbhavānāṃ kvacideva tilakaścitrakaciṇṭikādaya udayamāsādayantaḥ sahajāḥ kramajā vopalabhyante | asti ca tvaṅmāṃsādisāmyamanyāvayaveṣvapi | tadamī tilakādayo vibhāgena bhavanto dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagrīpariṇativibhāgamanupalakṣyamapi khyāpayantaḥ kathamiva niṣeddhuṃ śakyāḥ | evaṃ bāhyeṣvapi bhāveṣu | sarvakāryagrāmasya hi sādhāraṇasādhāraṇakarmaṇi jātatvamiṣṭaṃ śiṣṭānām ||
[47,1]
athāpi syāt, śarīre dakṣiṇetaragopyāgopyasthāneṣu bhavantastilakādayo'vaśyaṃ sukhāsukhādikamupanayantīti satsaṃvartanīyakarmādhipatyāducitaḥ sthānaniyamaḥ | kuśūle tu bījavisareṇa tenānyena vā parikarmitabhūmāvupyamāne na kaścid viśeṣa iti vaiṣamyāt na karmaśaktikalpanamiti cet ?
[47,2]
hantaivaṃ sākṣādupayogadarśanādarśanābhyāṃ karmādisādhanaśaktikalpanākalpanayoralpīyaḥ kiścitkāryaṃ jagati karmanirmeyamanumantavyamīśvarādisādhyaṃ vā ? na hi śiśupaśuviśeṣasādhāraṇavyāvṛttyā chāgādīnāṃ purīṣādervartulīkaraṇena kiñcitprayojanamupalabhase | anupabhuktaviśīrṇeṣu vāṭavīviṭapaphalaprasūnapallavādiṣu | ta eva tilakādimantaḥ puruṣāḥ aparicitasvakīyakāyatilakādayaḥ | paricaye'pi vānudīrṇaduḥkhadaurmanasyādayo dṛśyante maraṇamupagacchanta iti kastatrāpyupayogaḥ ? savyāsavyagopyetarasthāneṣu vā sthavīyassu tilakādisaṃbhavayogyasthānīyasya deśasya bhūyasaḥ saṃbhavāt kathamudbhatisthānaniyamastilakādīnām ? mṛgādiṣu ca varṇamātravaikṛtyena kvacidaṅge daurmanasyādiśaṅkayāpyalaṃ kiṃ teṣu kīdṛśamupayogavarṇanam ? kiyadvā śakyametādṛśamupadarśayitum ? kiyati vā tvayāpi pratividheyam ? tat kiṃ viphalamāyāsyasi ? upayogābhyūhavirahe'pi pratiniyatadeśakālasvabhāveṣu bhāveṣu kāryabhedopalambhaḥ sarvatrāvāntarabhedaṃ durlakṣyakarmādisādhanaśaktibhedabhāvitam | sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā dṛśyādṛśyacetanācetanārthakarmaṇyupayoginaṃ yogibhirapyavāntarairaśakyaparicchedamidantayā niyamena sāmānyato vyavasthāpayatīti galepādikayāpi svīkārayitavyo nyāyānveṣī nyāyavidā | tathā ca sati kasyacideva bījasyāpasarpaṇapratyayasamparkakarkaśaḥ svabhāvaḥ, anyeṣāṃ tu tadviśeṣaviśleṣamasṛṇa ityavāntarāvāntaraviśeṣāt sa eva bījakṣaṇaḥ paramparayāpi prakṛtakāryopayogī, nānye bījakṣaṇāḥ | sa cāvāntaro viśeṣaḥ karasparśādanumīyamāno na karmādisādhanaśaktiviśeṣānabhyūhādupayogaviśeṣānabhyūhād vā śakyapratikṣepaḥ | tilakādisaṃbhavādiva dehāṃśaviśeṣaḥ, vṛkṣādyaṃśaviśeṣo vā kutaścidekadeśikavikāraleśāt | tatrāpi hi vikārabindusthānasyāṃśasyedaṃ dṛṣṭamadṛṣṭaṃ vā kāraṇamāsādyopādānabhāgaviśeṣaparamparayāyaṃ svabhāvabheda idamanyabhāgāsādhyamarthaṃ kartuṃ samartha iti viśeṣānavadhāraṇe'pyasti kiñcidviśiṣṭaṃ kāraṇamupayogo vā'nyāsaṃbhavīti sāmānyato vikārakāraṇayogādaṅgasya svabhāvabhedaniścayaḥ | evamatrāpi bīje puruṣabuddhiprayuktakarasparśādasti svabhāvabhedaḥ sūkṣmahetuphalabhedabhāgīti sāmānyato durnivāro niścayaḥ |
tataḥ svābhavabhedasaṃbhavāt tadeva bījamupayujyate paramparayāpyaṅkuropajananānuguṇe viśeṣe nānye bījakṣaṇā iti siddhametat |
[48,1]
yattūktaṃ na khalūpasarpaṇetyādi | tadetat kasya pramāṇasya vyāpāramālocyate ?
na tāvat pratyakṣasya, ākārasāmyena sthūlaikajātīyatāniścaye'pyavāntarabhedasya sūkṣmatayānavasitasyāśakyaniṣedhatvāt | dṛṣṭaṃ ca tiktetaratrapuṣādau sadṛśākāre sthūlajātibhedavatyapi praskhaladadhyakṣamekāvasāyajananāt | tannaikāvasāyamātreṇa tattvasthitiḥ, tadaṃśe bādhakasya darśitatvāt | atyantābhyāsabhāvite tu saṃvādini bādhakābhāvādekatāsthitiraviruddheti na pratyakṣīkṛtaḥ prastute parasparātiśayaniṣedhaḥ | nāpyanumānāt, yadyucyeta kṣityādau janayitavye tadupādānaṃ pūrvameva kṣityādibījasya rūpāntaramiti, na tarhi bījaṃ tadapekṣaṃ kṣityādīnāṃ janakam, tadanapekṣatve teṣāmaṅkurād bhedānupapatteḥ | na cānupakārakā apekṣanta iti tvayaivoktam | na ca kṣaṇasyopakārasaṃbhavo'nyatra jananāt, tasyābhedyatvāt | tathā cārthakriyāyā ekatvānekatvasāpekṣatvānapekṣatvavyāptatvāt, tṛtīyaprakāravirahāt | anayoranyataraniṣedhasyānyataravidhānanāntarīyakatvāt | akṣaṇike ca tadvyāpakayorekatvānekatvayoḥ sāpekṣatvānapekṣatvayoḥ prakārayorabhāvāt uktena krameṇa sattvaṃ nivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikāntādavyabhicāriṇo liṅgasyānupadarśanādupadarśayitumaśakyatvācca | bādhakasyaiva vidyamānatvāt | tasmānnāniṣṭamātraghoṣaṇena kiñcit |
[49,1]
etena nopakāro'pekṣārtha ityanapekṣaiva kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣu, nobhayavyāvṛtiḥ |
[49,2]
atha saṃbhūyakaraṇamapekṣārthaḥ | tadapi yadi pūrvasthitasyeti viśeṣaṇāpekṣā tadāpi kṣaṇikasya naiva kācidityanapekṣaivākṣīṇā |
[49,3]
atha pūrvasthitasyeti nāpekṣate militāvasthitasya karaṇamātramapekṣārthaḥ, tadā sāpekṣataiva nānapekṣā | tathāpi nobhayavyāvṛttiḥ |
[49,4]
athāsmatsamayāpekṣayā apekṣāsthitiḥ | tadā sāpekṣamasamarthameva samarthitavanto vayamiti yatkāryaṃ prati yadasamarthaṃ tatsāpekṣam, yattu samarthaṃ tadanapekṣamiti vyavasthā | tadā caikaniṣedhenāparavidhānāt sāmarthyarahitaṃ samarthameva bhavatyasāmarthyam | uktaṃ ca,
[49,5]
samarthameveti natarāmubhayavyāvṛttiḥ kṣaṇikatve ||
[49,6]
yaccāvocat, api cāntyakṣaṇaprāptaṃ bījamanapekṣyāṅkurāvanipavanapāthastejāṃsi janayat kiṃ yenaiva rūpeṇāṅkuraṃ janayati tenaiva taditarāṇyapi, kiṃ vā rūpāntareṇa ?
na tāvattenaiva, kṣityādīnāmapyaṅkurasvābhāvyāpatteḥ | na khalu kāraṇābhede bhedavat kāryaṃ bhavitumarhati, kāryabhedasyākasmikatvaprasaṅgāt |
[49,7]
yadāha, ayameva hi bhedo bhedaheturvā yaduta viruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ, kāraṇabhedaśceti | nāpi sāmagrībhedaḥ, tasyā apyekatvāt | anyathā sahabhāvaniyamābhāvāt, rūpāntareṇa taditareṣāṃ janakam | tathā hi bījamaṅkuraṃ janayadupādānam, tadvikriyayā tadutpatteḥ | taditareṣu punarasya sahakāripratyayatā, teṣāṃ tu pūrve pavanādayo yathā svamupādānāni, tadvikriyayā tadutpādāditi cet ? nanu sahakāritopādānate kimekaṃ tattvaṃ nānā vā ? ekaṃ cet, kathaṃ rūpāntareṇa janakam ? nānātve tu anayorbījād bhedo'bhedo vā ? bhede kathaṃ bījasya janakatvam, tābhyāmevāṅkurādīnāmupapatteḥ ? abhede vā kathaṃ bījasya na nānātvam, bhinnatādātmyāt | etayorvaikatvamekatādātmyāt |
[50,1]
yadyucyeta, kṣityādau janayitavye tadupādānaṃ pūrvameva kṣityādi bījasya rūpāntaramiti ? na tarhi bījaṃ tadanapekṣaṃ kṣityādīnāṃ janakam | tadanapekṣatve teṣāmaṅkurād bhedānupapatteḥ | na cānupakārakāriṇo'pekṣanta iti tvayaivoktam | na ca kṣaṇasyopakārasaṃbhavo'nyatra jananāt, tasyābhedyatvāt | tathā cārthakriyāyā ekatvānekatvasāpekṣatvānapekṣatvavyāptatvāt | tṛtoyaprakāravirahāt | anayoranyataraniṣedhasyānyataravidhānanāntarīyakatvāt | kṣaṇikavad vyāpakayorekatvānekatvayoḥ sāpekṣatvānapekṣatvayoḥ prakārayorabhāvāduktena krameṇa sattvaṃ nivṛttamityasādhāraṇānaikāntikatvaṃ gandhavattvāderiveti |
[50,2]
yadi manyeta, anupakāriṇo'pi bhavanti sahakāriṇo'pekṣaṇīyāśca, kāryeṇānuvihitabhāvābhāvatvāt | sahakāryakaraṇācca | nanvanena krameṇākṣaṇiko'pi bhāvo'nupakārakānapi sahakāriṇaḥ kramavataḥ kāryeṇānukṛtānvayavyatirekānapekṣiṣyate, kariṣyate ca kramavatsahakārisamavadhānavaśāt krameṇa kāryāṇīti vyāpakānupalabdherasiddheḥ sandigdhavyatirekamanaikāntikaṃ sattvaṃ kṣaṇikatvasiddhāviti | tadapi pūrvameva nirastam |
yatpunarayamadhikamāha — nāpi sāmagrībhedaḥ, tasyā apyekatvāditi | tatrāpi brūmaḥ — yathā sāmagryā abhedaḥ, tathā kāryāṇāmapyabhedāt kathaṃ na kāraṇābhedānukāraḥ ?
[50,3]
nanu pratiniyatānekarūpāṇāṃ kāryāṇāmabheda iti keyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ ? yadyebaṃ na khalu samagrebhyo bhinnā kācidadhyakṣagocaraḥ | saugatamate ca cinteyam | tato'bhinnā sāmagrīti samagrā eva pratiniyatānekamūrtayo'bhinnā ityapi kīdṛśī vācoyuktiḥ ?
sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇabhedābhedācca kāryabhedābhedamāśaṅkamānasya ayamabhinnasāmagrīvādo vācaspaterucitaḥ | anyathā bījamekaṃ kathamaṅkurasarodharaṇidhāmādi janayedityetāvataiva gatametat | na cedaṃ codyam, yato yadi pramāṇavṛttimanuvṛttya ekasmādanekotpattiniṣedho'bhipretaḥ, tadā ekasmādapi dīpād vartivikārādyanekaṃ kāryamupajāyamānamadhigacchadadhyakṣamakhilatadviparītamatiṣvāsthāṃ dusthayati |
[51,1]
tadapi kathamiti cet ? nanu pramāṇapuraskāreṇa vicāre pratyakṣamādāvādāya pariśiṣṭagaṇanāttena sādhite bādhite vā nāparasya bādhanasādhanayoradhikāraḥ | pramāṇamārgollaṅghinastu tādṛśaiva deyamuttaramityāstāṃ tāvat |
[51,2]
athāṅkurakāri kathaṃ dharaṇikṣaṇahetuḥ ? na hyatrāpi pratyakṣabādhābhidhānaṃ yuktimat, kṣaṇasya tadgocarātikrāntatvāt | tadāpi yadyekakārako'nyakārako na bhavatīti vyāptiḥ, tadā dīpenaiva vyabhicāraḥ | athāṅkurakārako na pṛthvīheturiti tadā'sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ | athāṅkurasya hetuḥ kathamanyasya bhavitumarhatīti cet ? kimaṅkurasyaivāthāṅkurasyāpi, yadvā aṅkurasya tāvad bhavati, anyatrāniścayaḥ ? atra ca pakṣatraye'pyasiddhaviruddhānaikāntikatvaṃ krameṇa duṣpariharam | tasmānnātra pramāṇavṛttiḥ | prasaṅgodbhāvanamapi parābhyupagamena bhavati, na caikamanekasyājanakamiti kṣaṇikavādināmabhyupagamaḥ | tanna sāmagryantargatavastvekatvena kāryaikatvaprasañjanamabālasya | sāmagrīlakṣaṇakāraṇāpekṣaṇe ca bhinnānāmapyaṅkurādīnāṃ kāraṇabhedābhedānuvidhānaṃ siddhamiti nābhedānuvidhānānurodhādaṅkurādīnāmekatāpattiḥ | yathā hyaṅkurādayaḥ pratyekakāryatve'pi bhinnābhinnātmānaḥ, tathā sāmagrośabdavācyā bījādayaḥ pratyekaṃ kāraṇībhavanto bhinnābhinnā eveti siddhaḥ kāraṇabhedād bhedaḥ |
[51,3]
atha bhinnātmāno'pi bījādayaḥ kayācit pratyāsattyā ekavyavahāragocarīkriyante, evamaṅkurādayopīti kāraṇābhede'bhedo'pi siddhaḥ | tatra kāraṇānāmekaikārthajanakatvamekavyavahārahetuḥ | kāryāṇāṃ tvekaikajanyatvamiti samānam | tat kimarthamekībhavitavyamaṅkurādibhiḥ, sāmagryapekṣāyāmapi tāvataiva hetubhedābhedānuvidhānasya paryāptatvāt | etacca kāraṇaśabdena sāmagrīṃ vyutpadyamānasyāpi parasya bhedābhedayoravyutpattirevabuddhyanurodhādabhidhīyate | tattvatastu yathā kāraṇaṃ sāmagrī vivakṣitā, tathā bhedābhedāvapi vaijātyāvaijātye vivakṣite iti darśitaprāyam |
[52,1]
nanvadyāpi na samagrebhyo'nyā sāmagrīti teṣāmeva samagrāṇāṃ sādṛśye vaisadṛśye vā kāryāṇāṃ sādṛśyaṃ vaisadṛśyaṃ veti prāptam | evametat | na tu tatpuñjasthānāṃ parasparaṃ sādṛśyādinirūpaṇam | kiṃ tu puñjāntarasthaiḥ saha svajātyapekṣayā senāyāḥ senāntareṇa saha sādṛśyetaranirūpaṇavat | tatra yāvanto yādṛśā ekasāmagrīprajñaptigocarā arthā hetusaṃmatāḥ, tāvantastādṛśā eva yadi deśakālāntaravartinastadāsau sadṛśī sāmagrī, kāryaṃ ca sadṛśamasyā iti kāryaśabdenāpi puñja eva | yāvanti yādṛśāni kāryāṇi jātānyekatra tāvanti tādṛśānyevānyatrāpi jāyanta ityarthaḥ | vaisadṛśye tu tāratamyabhedena bhidyamāne kāryamapi tāratamyabhedena bhidyata ityapi kāryapuñjasyaiva tāratamyabhedena vaisadṛśyamityarthaḥ | bhedamātrabivakṣāyāmapyayameva nyāyaḥ | satyāṃ bipratipattau bhinnāyāḥ sāmagryā bhinnameva kāryaṃ bhavatīti etādṛśameva kāraṇabhedānuvidhānaṃ kāryasya pramāṇānusāri | tadatikrame ca viśvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgatimavatarati | na pramāṇabādhitasya ekakāraṇaikakaraṇaniyamasyātikrame | tadiyaṃ bhedābhedānukaraṇavārtā naiyāyikānāṃ gopamukhātpāyasamiṣṭatāśrutimanuharati |
[52,2]
tasmādekameva bījamaṅkurādikamanekaṃ janayati, evaṃ kṣityādikamapi pratyekam |
ato naikānekayorubhayorapi vyāvṛttiryato vyāpakānupalambhā'yamaparaḥ kṣaṇikapakṣe'pi kriyābādhanaṃ sattayā asādhāraṇīkaraṇārthamupanyasyate | rūpāntareṇa jananapakṣastu pratikṣipta evāsmābhiriti na taddūṣaṇaparamparāyāḥ parihārābhiyogaḥ | etacca tattvāpekṣayocyate | kalpanāvilāse tu yadaṅkurajananaṃ na tat kṣitijananam | tathā na sahakāritvamevopādānatvamityevaṃ prakāraprapañcasaṃbhave'pi nāparādho vastunaḥ kaścit kriyāvirahalakṣaṇaḥ, tāttvikenaiva rūpeṇa sarvanirvāhāt | ataeva kṣityādau janayitavye tadupādānaṃ pūrvameva kṣityādibījasya rūpāntaramiti kimarthaṃ baktavyamasmābhiḥ, yaduttaraḥ prabandhaḥ sādhuḥ syāt | anapekṣā caikā sahakāriṣvapi sādhiteti prakaraṇārthanigamanaṃ sakalamākulamākuladhiyaḥ parasya |
[53,1]
kiṃ ca yenaiva rūpeṇa bījamaṅkuramutpādayati kiṃ tenaiva kṣauṇīkṣaṇamiti paryanuyuñjānāḥ te'pi paryanuyujyante rūpaśabdena kimatra vivakṣitamiti ? kiṃ tāvat kalpanātalpaśāyino bhinnā iva bhāsamānā dharmāḥ kṛtakatvānityatvādivadaṅkuretarajanakatvādayaḥ svarūpaśabdenāpi labdhavyavahṛtayaḥ ? atha rūpaṃ svarūpaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ yadbhedāt nāparo vastubhedaḥ yadadhikāreṇocyate, yadādau vastunaḥ svarūpaṃ tadeva yadi paścādapi prāgiva paścādapi na janayedityādi ?
[53,2]
yadvā naiyāyikaiḥ patyurnāmāvijānatyā bhrātṛśabdena vyavahāravat sahakāriṇa eva svarūpaśabdena vyavahṛtā rūpamityuktam | tatra prathamapakṣe tāvanna paryanuyogasaṃgatiḥ |
kalpanānirmitā hi dharmāḥ parasparaṃ dharmiṇaśca sakāśād vidyamānā iva bhānto'pi yathā pratibhāsamasattvāt pramāṇasahatayā na kvacit kriyāyāṃ karaṇabhāvabhājo bhavitumarhati |
yadeva hi svalakṣaṇamadhyakṣagocarīkṛtamanaṅgaṃ tata evānvayavyatirekābhyāmarthakriyāniṣpattiniścaye'pyanādivāsanāvaśādupajāyamāna vikalpacetasi tatastato vyāvṛttavastuvyavasāyabalāvalambisaṃvādeṣudharmaṣvapoddhāreṇāsyāmasyāṃ kriyāyāmayamayaṃ dharma upayujyata iti vyavahāramātramātanyate | na tu teṣā kvacit karaṇabhāvaḥ, svayamasattvāt | vivakṣākṛtastu na vāryate | yathā prakāśe piśaṅgātmani pradopepyayamakhaṇḍenaiva rūpeṇa tamaso nāśamavakāśapiñjaraṇaṃ ca kurvati tathaiva niścite ca yadayaṃ dīpaḥ prakāśarūpaḥ, tato'ndhakāraṃ harati hariṇāṅkavat | piśaṅgatvācca piñjaraṇaheturharidrādivaditivyavahāraḥ | na ca tatra prakāśapiśaṅgabhāvau bhinnau | vikalpacetasi tu bhinnavadbhāsamānāvekaikamapoddhṛtya bhinnakriyākaraṇatvena vyavasthitau vivakṣitau, na vyavasthitau vā na ca vivakṣāmātreṇa pradīpasyākārakatvaṃ bhedo vā | tathā bījasyāpyaṅkurajananena rūpeṇa kalpitenāṅkurakaṇaṃ pṛthvījanakena ca tatkaraṇamiti vyavahāre'pi tattvato naikasyāpyanekakarmaṇi niṣedho bhedopapattirvā akriyaiva vā | tato vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayānekena rūpeṇānekakaraṇamiti vyavahāramātraṃ na vastu | vāstavī ca cinteyam | tat kimanena vikalpitena, kiṃ tena rūpeṇānyena veti ? vikalpe'pi vānekenaiva visarjanaṃ vyavahāramātreṇa | na ca kaścid doṣaḥ | dvitīyapakṣastvanekasvalakṣaṇadarśane satyupapadyate | na ca bīcasvalakṣaṇāni api sakṛdekasaṃkhyā nirīkṣāviṣayaḥ | na hyaparidṛṣṭabhūmani manuṣye kimayamatra karmaṇi niyojyo naraḥ, kimayaṃ veti praśnāvatāraḥ |
[54,1]
tṛtīyavikalpe tvayamarthaḥ syāt, yenaiva rūpeṇāṅkuraṃ karoti kiṃ tenaiva kṣitimiti ? yenaiva sahakāriṇāṅkuraṃ janayati kiṃ tenaiva bhuvamiti ? etacca kadocyate yadi bījasyāṅkurakaraṇe nirjāte niyatarūpaḥ kaścit sahakārī vyāpāravān pariniṣṭhito'nyakaraṇe sandigdhavyāpāraḥ | na caivaṃ śakyopadarśanam |
[54,2]
athaivaṃ sati bījasyāṅkurakaraṇe pṛthvīpāthaḥprabhṛtayaḥ sahakāriṇasya eva kiṃ tasya pṛthvījanane'pīti vikalpārthaḥ ? tenāpi nopayogaḥ | sarveṣāṃ sarvatra parasparaṃ sahakāribhāvasya suprasiddhatvāt kimatra praśnena ? na cottaraḥ prabandho'trānurūpaḥ | nahi tadāpi kāraṇabhedābhedābhyāṃ kāryabhedābhedāviti śliṣṭatā kācit | tasmādīrṣyāśalyakadarthitanirarthakaiḥ pralāpaiḥ paramākulayitumicchanti nyāyavinmānina ityalamatra nirbandhena |
[54,3]
api cāpūrvo'yamasādhāraṇānaikāntikakīrtanaprakāraḥ | vidyamāno hi bhāvaḥ sādhyetarayoraniścitānvayavyatireko gandhavattvādivadasādhāraṇo yuktaḥ | prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhabalācca sarvathārthakriyaivāsatīti tat kathamasādhāraṇānaikāntikī bhavitumarhati ? asiddhidūṣaṇaṃ tu vaktumucitam | tatra coktameva |
[54,4]
atha kṣaṇikatve vyāpakābhāva ityuktam, tanna sarvathāsattvamiti cet ? evaṃ tarhi vidyamānaivārthakriyā kṣaṇikādeva vyāvartate, tato niyamenākṣaṇike viśrāmyantīti tena vyāpyata iti viruddhatāpyastu |
[54,5]
atha sākṣādakṣaṇike tasyā bādhakasya sādhakasya vā virahāt sandeha iti cet ?
vidyamānatve kṣaṇikād vyāvṛttireva sādhanī tasyāḥ sandehamanavakāśayati | vidyamānatāsandehe ca sandigdhāsiddhireva dūṣaṇam |
[54,6]
kiṃ ca prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhasya kṣaṇikavadakṣaṇike'pi sāmarthyānapāyāt kathaṃ bādhakasiddhirityasiddhireva sarvathāyātā | śakyaṃ hi nitye'pi vaktuṃ na sahakāriṇi sāpekṣasya karaṇamupakārābhāvāt | na nirapekṣasya, tena vinā karaṇāt | sthiraṃ ca bījamaṅkurajanakenaiva rūpeṇa kṣitimutpādayati bhinnena vetyādi yadā visadṛśakṣityādijanmopālambhaḥ pradīpo'pi cākṣaṇika eva bhavatām | tatra vartivikāratailakṣayāvekena bhinnena vā rūpeṇa kriyetāmiti samānam | yastu samādhiḥ sahakāriṇa eva bhinnāḥ tasya svarūpabheda iti, evaṃ ca bruvatā paro'pyātmā ātmāpi para iti nivṛttedānīmātmaparādiśabdebhyaḥ pratiniyatārthapratyāyanapratyāśā | na ca devadattasya svarūpaṃ yajñadattaḥ śuklasya vā nīlamityucitaṃ kvacidekakarmaṇi vyāpāre'pi |
[55,1]
tadetadapetāgamayuktikaṃ paraspardhayā'bhidhīyamānaṃ niyatamupahāsabhājanīkaroti |
sahakāriṇo'vadhīrya ca svarūpaśabdavācyamarthaṃ pṛcchataḥ sahakāriṇottaramiti vyaktaṃ na tena nānyena vātmanā janayati sthiro'pi bhāva iti niyatamanujñātaiva vyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | anyasyāpi hi sa evātmā janako na svayamiti na kaścijjanakaḥ | tadayaṃ sthirāsthirayoḥ sādhāraṇo nyāyaḥ kriyāniṣedhasādhana iti | tasya dṛḍhatve sarvathā kriyaiva nāstītyasiddhireva, antataḥ kramayaugapadyavirahalakṣaṇasyāpi doṣasyāparihārāt | sthire'pi kriyānivṛttiravaśyābhyupeyā | kathamanyathā kṣaṇike kriyāniṣedhābhidhānena kevalenāsādhāraṇatāpratijñā nivṛttimālambeta ? na hi sādhyād vyāvṛttirityevāsādhāraṇatā |
anyathā vipakṣād vyāvṛttirityeva kiṃ nāsādhāraṇatvamucyate, kimiyatā prayāsena ? nanu vipakṣād vyāvṛttyā sādhye niyamāddhetureva syāditi cet ? sādhyād vyāvṛttyā vipakṣe niyamād viruddha eva syāditi samānam | tasmādarthakriyāyāḥ pratijñāmātre'pyasiddhireva |
[55,2]
athānyena prakāreṇa ubhayoraniścayamātraṃ sattāyāḥ khyāpyate, tathā ca satyasādhāraṇatā yuktaiva | tadayuktam | vyāpakānupalambho hyekāntato'bhāvaniścayakara eva kathamaniścayaḥ ? tatra yadi nāma kramādyanupalambhasya nityāt sattānivartakasya dārḍhyam asaṃgatam, tathāpi prakṛtasya kṣaṇinityatābādhanasya dṛḍhatvamabhipretameva, anyathopanyāsāyogāt | tataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgarāt kriyāyā aikāntikī vyāvṛttireva vyāvṛttirasādhāraṇatāyāḥ | nahi gandhavattvaṃ kutaścidekāntena vyāvṛttamavasātuṃ śakyam | tadayaṃ vyāpakānupalambhaḥ sthire'pi vyāpakānupalambhamapekṣamāṇo na sādhurasādhāraṇatāsādhane |
apekṣamāṇaśca sarvathā kriyāmevonmūlayatītyasiddhireva na sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ | tasmād bāhyavedanaṃ bāhyavedakapramāṇasiddhāṃ cārthakriyāṃ vastusatīmāśritya vādaprakrame tasyāsādhāraṇatāvādinā na sādhyetarayorekatra vṛttirekato vyāvṛttirvopadarśayitavyā, kiṃ tūbhayatra saṃśayamātraṃ śaraṇīkaraṇīyam | na ca vyāpakānupalambhe saṃbhavastasya | tasmānna sādhurasādhāraṇatopanyāsa iti sthitam |
[56,1]
syādetat | yadi bhinnakālakāryajanmani janakasya svabhāvabhedaḥ, tadā bhinnadeśakāryotpāde'pyeṣa prasaṅgaḥ | tadavaśyaṃ sahakāryapekṣayaiva deśabhedaḥ kāryāṇām | na ca kiñcitkaraḥ sahakārotikālabhedo'pyeṣāmakiñcitkaraḥ sahakāryapekṣayaivāstu |
athopādānabhedād deśabhedaḥ ? kālabhede tu naivaṃ śakyamabhidhātum | kālāntarajanyānāmupādānasya sthirapakṣe tadānīmapi prāptisaṃbhavāt | tasmāt kāraṇabhedarūpabhedanibandhana eva kāryasya kālabheda iti cet ? tadapi nāsti, upādānasahakāribhedasya tattvato'tāttvikatvāt | tāttvikatve'pyupādeyasahakāryabhedena dīpāderupādānasahakāribhāvabhedādanekasvabhāvatāprasaṅgaḥ | tadayamāropitasvabhāva upādānasahakāribhāvabhedena bhedaḥ kāraṇasya kathaṃ kāryasya deśabhedāya prabhavet ? yadi cāropito'pi kāraṇasya bhedaḥ kāryasya deśabhedāya prabhavedevaṃ satyāropita eva kāraṇabhedaḥ kālabhedāya kāryāṇāṃ paryāpta ityalaṃ tāttvikabhedapratyāśayā |
[56,2]
na caitad vaktavyam, yathā kālabhede yadyadā yajjanakamityādi bādhakamasti na tathā deśabheda iti, etādṛśasya bādhakasya deśabhede'pi vaktuṃ śakyatvāt | yathā yat yatkāryaṃ tat taddeśaṃ yathopādeyābhimataṃ, tatkāryaṃ ca kāryāntaramapīti ||
[56,3]
yadapīdamucyate, sarvāvasthāsamāne'pītyādi (vārtikālaṅkāre 1. 396)
tatrāpi śakyamevaṃ paṭhitum
[57,1]
sarvadeśasamāne'pi kāraṇe yadyakāryatetyādi |
[57,2]
atha kāraṇasya vaibhavābhyupagame syādeṣa doṣaḥ | tadabhāve tu kiṃkṛtamasya sarvadeśasamānatvam ? evaṃ tarhi deśāntare'pi kāryaṃ na kuryāt, tatra svayamapravṛtteḥ |
yogyatāmātreṇa tu taddeśavṛttimanapekṣya tatra kāryakāriṇaḥ samāno'sya deśaḥ upakārasyaikato'pyalābhāt | tasmāt taddeśe karotīti na svāpekṣayā deśasyādhārabhāvaḥ kiṃ tu kāryāpekṣayā | ayogavyavacchedena ca tatkaraṇam | anyathā deśāntaravataḥ kāryasya karaṇaprasaṅgāt | evaṃ tarhi kāle karotīti sa kālaḥ kāryasyaivādhāro niyamena |
hetostu sa cāsacca syāt | ayogavyavacchedena tvekakālakāryakaraṇamiti kālāntaravato'pi kāryasya karaṇamavirodhi | tasmāt kuśūlādisarvāvasthāsamānasvabhāvasyāpi tadatatkālakāryajananamupapannam, bhinnadeśānekakāryārjanavaditi |
[57,3]
tadetanna saṅgatam, bādhakabhāvābhāvābhyāṃ viśeṣāt | yattu tatkāryatvaṃ taddeśatāsādhanāyopanyastaṃ tadviparyayabādhakapramāṇābhāvādasādhanameva | anvayavyatirekasamadhigamyaśca kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ | tau ca yathā taddeśakāryajanmani dṛṣṭau tathā bhinnadeśakāryasaṃbhave'pi | na caivaṃ sthitenāpi kāraṇena saha tatkālakāryasyānyakālakāryasya vānvayavyatirekau samānāviti yuktam | kālāntare'pi tadeva kāraṇamanuvartata iti na pratyabhijñāto'nyatpramāṇam, sā ca dūṣiteti kathaṃ sthireṇānvayavyatirekagrahaṇaṃ kāryāṇāṃ kālabhedavatāmiti nāyaṃ nyāyaḥ samānaḥ | tato viparyayabādhakavikalatayā deśabhede bhedasādhano heturyadi svasādhyasādhanasamarthaḥ kimāyātaṃ tadvalavataḥ kālabhede bhedasādhanasya | nahi vṛṣabhasyādohayogyatve dhenorapi tatheti yuktam |
[57,4]
astu vā deśabhedena bhedasādhanasyāpi viparyayabādhā balam, kālabhede bhedasādhanasya tu kimetāvatā dūṣaṇam ? anaikāntikatvamupapādyata iti cet ? kimayaṃ mantrapāṭhaḥ ?
kadācijjananasamarthasyājananasyānvayadarśanāt sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamabhimatamiti cet ? tathāpi kimanena śrameṇa ? samarthaṃ ca syāt, na ca janayatītīyataiva tatsiddheḥ | deśodāharaṇena saṃśayapuṣṭiḥ kriyata iti cet ? yadi viparyayabādhā balamasya na puṣṭyāpi saṃśayamanullaṅghayantyā kiñcit, viparyayabādhāvaidhurye tu saṃśayamātreṇāpi hetorviparyāsanāt kimaparaṃ puṣṭyā ? yadi ca tanmātraṃ vivakṣitam, tadā viparyayabādhakena niraste'smin kiṃ punarupanyāsena ?
[58,1]
atha kāladeśayoḥ sarvatra samānanyāyopalabdherekayogakṣematvād deśabhedavadeva kāryeṇa kālabhedavatāpi na hetubheda ityucyate ? tadapyayuktam | tathāhi na paramāṇoḥ kālavyāptisadṛśī deśavyāptiriṣyate nityavādibhiḥ | nāpi vidyududdyotasya deśavyāptisadṛśī kālavyāptirevaṃ ghaṭāderapīti kathaṃ sarvatra samānanyāyatā ? na cānyatra samānanyāyatādarśane'pi sarvatra tathābhāvaḥ, prastute vaiparītyasaṃbhave bādhakābhāvāt ||
[58,2]
upādānabhedācca deśabhede yaduktamupādānasahakāribhāvo'vāntara iti, tadapyayuktam | yadyapi vikalpe pratibhāsamānau tāvupādānasahakāribhāvau bhinnāviva na vastu, tathāpi vastunastattadvyāvṛttisaṃbhavānnāvāstavavyavasthā, anyānyāpekṣayā ca na virodhaḥ | yathaikasyānyāpekṣayā pitṛputratvasya na vāstavatvaṃ, na ca virodhaḥ |
na ca rūpadvayena kāryadvayasya karaṇam, yena kalpanābhāsino rūpayoravāstavatvāt dvayākaraṇam | yathā caikarūpeṇa dvayākaraṇaṃ tathā svopādeyaṃ svadeśe paropādeyaṃ ca paradeśe karotīti upādānabhedādupapanno'pi deśabhedaḥ | yataśca nāropitasvabhāvabhedādeva deśabhedaḥ kāryasya, kiṃ tu svopādeyaṃ svasvadeśaṃ janayadbhirevārthād bhinnadeśaṃ sahakāryaṃ kāryamiti nyāyaḥ | tato na vikalpitasvabhāvabhedādeva bhinnakālakāryakaraṇamabhinnasya, bādhakasāmarthyena bhedasādhanāt | ata eva na sarvadeśasamānatvaṃ kāraṇasya | svasahakāryupādeye hi sahakāritā asya, tasya ca kāryasya svopādānadeśa eva saṃbhavāt tatraiva asya sahakriyāsāmarthyaṃ na deśāntara iti kathamasya sarvaḥ samāno deśaḥ kutaścidupakārābhāve'pi ?
[58,3]
yaccoktam, kāryasyaiva sa kāla ādhāro niyamena, hetostu sa cāsacceti, tadapi deśasāmyena pratihatam | tathāhi yathaikadeśastha eva heturbhinnadeśāni kāryāṇi karoti, tathā ekakālastha eva bhinnakālāni kāryāṇi karotītyaprāpyaiva kāryakālaṃ deśavat |
tataśca kadācijjātanaṣṭo'pi sahakāryapekṣayā sakalakālakalitāni kāryāṇi kuryāditi sthāne saṃbhūyaikārthakaraṇapratijñānirvāhaḥ |
[59,1]
atha deśamapi kāryasya prāpyaiva jananānna deśadṛṣṭāntasiddhiriti cet — na, puruṣāntarbhuvo jñānasya deśaprāpterabhāvād dīpasya jñānādhikaraṇasyātmanaḥ pradīpasaṃyoge'pi na jñānasukhādisaṃbhavadeśe dehāntaḥprabhāpraveśāvakāśa iti kāśakuśāvalambanametat |
yaścāyaṃ taddeśatvasādhanastatkāryatvaheturupanyastaḥ, sa na svatantraḥ, pratibandhābhāvād |
bhāve'pi nāsmākaṃ kṣatirityuktam ||
[59,2]
na ca prasaṅgo bhavitumarhati, tatkāryatāyāḥ pramāṇasiddhatvena paropagamamātrābhāvāt, viparyayaparyavasāyitāvirahācca | tadāhi na ca taddeśatvamatastatkāryatvamapi nāstīti syāt, na caivaṃ śakyam | śakyatve'pi nāsmākaṃ mūlaprasaṅgayoḥ kṣatiḥ |
na coktadoṣaḥ, yato jananasāmarthyamanyadā paropagamamātreṇaiva, na pramāṇāt | viparyaye ca jananābhāvaḥ pramāṇasiddhaḥ kṣaṇāntare tatkāryasāmarthyaṃ nivartayan jaladharasya anyakriyākriyāpakṣayordvayorapi kṣaṇabhaṅgaṃ sādhayatīti sapakṣe bhāvānna viruddhaḥ sattvaheturiti ||
{1.3}
<kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ — vyatirekādhikāraḥ>
[60,1]
nāpyanaikāntikaśaṅkā, sarvopasaṃhāravatyā vyāpteḥ prasādhanāt | nanu viparyayabādhakapramāṇavaśād vyāptisiddhiḥ, tasya ca nopanyāsavārtā | tat kathaṃ vyāptiḥ prasādhitetyucyate ? tadetaduparipariplavamānataralatarabuddhivilasitam | tathā hyaktametat, kartuḥ sā na kriyā anyadāpi, kiṃ tu parakriyā akriyaiva vā | ataeva prakāradvaye'pi kṣaṇabhaṅgasya saṅgatiravaśyambhāvastanmātrānubandha iti yāvat | tacca prasādhitamataḥ sādhyena vyāptaiva sā arthakriyāśaktiriti |
[60,2]
nanvevamanvayamātramastu, vipakṣātpunarekāntena vyatireka iti kathaṃ labhyamiti cet ? vyāptisiddhereva | vyatireke vyāptisiddhireva kathamiti cet — na, dvividhā hi vyāptiḥ, anvayarūpā ca kartṛdharmaḥ sādhanavati dharmiṇi sādhyasyāvaśyambhāvo yaḥ, vyatirekarūpā ca karmadharmaḥ sādhyābhāve sādhanasyāvaśyamabhāvo yaḥ, vyāptirvyāpakasya tatra bhāva eva vyāpyasya vā tatraiva bhāva iti nyāyāt | enayoścaikasiddhirniyamena dvitīyapratītimākṣipati | anyathā ekasyāpyasiddheḥ | kevalaṃ sākṣādekatra pramāṇavyāpāro'nyatra nāntarīyakatayā pratītiriti tāvataivaikavyapadeśaḥ | tathā ca satyekatra pramāṇapravṛtteḥ pūrvamanyatra saṃśayaḥ pravartamāno'pi paścāttanyā tayā nirasyate | yathā viparyayabādhakapramāṇavādināmanvayaḥ sandihyamāno'pi vipakṣādekāntena vyāvṛttibalāt nirastasaṃśayaḥ paryavasyatyakṣaṇike sarvathā'nupapadyamāneyaṃ sattā kṣaṇabhaṅganiyataiveti, evaṃ sattāvataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ niyatasvabhāvabhedopasthāpanāt tadabhāve'pi sattāsaṃśayakṣaṇaḥ pūrvapravṛtto'pi svayameva parigalati | kriyāvatā cedavaśyaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgureṇa bhāvyam, kṣaṇikatvavyatireke na bhavatyeva niyataṃ satteti |
[61,1]
yadi tu tadabhāve'pi syāt, tadā tasyāṃ satyāṃ niyamena kṣaṇikatvamityanvayo'pi katham ? tasmāt sādhyābhāve sādhanasyaikāntiko vyatirekaḥ, sādhane sati sādhyasyāvaśyamanvayo veti na kaścidarthato bhedaḥ | pramāṇavyāpārastu mukhyato'rthataśceti dvidhā vyavahāraḥ | ataeva yatra yatra sādhyaviparyaye bādhakapramāṇaparyeṣaṇā, tatra sādhane sati sādhyānvayaḥ, sādhakapramāṇaparyeṣaṇāpi tayopalakṣitā veditavyā | viparyayabādhakaśabdena punarubhayasaṃgraha eva | vyatirekarūpavyāptau hi sādhyaviparyaye bādhakaṃ sādhanasya, anvayarūpāyāṃ tu sādhyaviparyayasya bādhakaṃ sādhane satīti | tadubhayābhāve sādhanasya sādhyapratibandhānupapattirityayamarthaḥ | anyathā vyatirekaniścāyakapramāṇasya sākṣādalābhe'pi yadi sādhanasya sādhyenānvayaniyamaprasādhakaṃ pramāṇamupadarśayet, kastasya sādhyasiddhau pratibandho vyatirekasyānvayasyāpi sāmarthyākṣepāt |
anyathā sādharmyaprayogo'nupādeya eva syāt, sākṣād vyatirekānupadarśanāt | tad yadi sāmarthyagamyo'pi na vyatirekātmā, tadā'pi yatra yatra sādhanaṃ tatra tatra sādhyamitīyataiva sādhane satisādhyapratyāśāprayuktaḥ kṛtī kṛtārthaḥ | tadabhāve'bhāvinyapi hi sādhane sati yadi tadbhāve'vaśyaṃbhāvi sādhyaṃ tadā phalitaḥ sādhanasvīkāraḥ |
tasmāt sādhanavādinā dvayamapi paryeṣaṇīyaṃ vikalpena, vādinā caiko'pi prakāraḥ pramāṇasiddha upadarśayitavyaḥ, parasādhaneṣu ca vyatirekavadanvayo'pi niyamavān durlabha eveti veditavyam |
[61,2]
asmābhistu prakṛtasādhane niyamavānanvayaḥ prasaṅgaviparyayābhyāṃ paurastyābhyāṃ darśita eva, tau ca yadyapi sapakṣīkṛte jalabhṛti pravartitau, tathāpi yo yatkaraṇasvabhāvaḥ sa tajjanayatyeva, yo yanna janayati na sa tatkaraṇasvabhāvaḥ, ityevaṃ pravartamānau sarvameva kriyāśaktiyuktaṃ kṣaṇikatve niyataṃ darśayata iti sarvopasaṃhāro vyatirekākṣepabījaṃ dhūmādivat | yathā cādhyakṣaṃ dhūmasya, dhūmadhvajena vyāptiṃ pratiyato na vahnermahānase sattāmanupasaṃharat pratyeti, tathā jalabhṛti kṣaṇikatāṃ pratiyadeva yathoktānumānaṃ sāmānyena kriyāvataḥ sādhāraṇanyāyatayā kṣaṇikatayā vyāptimātanotīti | yaduktaṃ prāk na sattvādanyadanumānasthirasiddhau yato'navasthā na syāditi, tadapāstam yathoktaprasaṅgaviparyayayorapi tatsādhakatvāditi |
[62,1]
yadyevamanarthakaḥ sattvahetūpanyāsa iti cet ? brūmaḥ | kiṃ hetvantarasattāmātreṇa bandhyaṃ sādhanāntaraṃ, uta pakṣīkṛte tasyāpyupanyāsāt, athopanyasituṃ śakyatvāt, yadi vāvaśyopanyasanīyatvāt, yad vā yadarthakāri tadavaśyaṃ kṣaṇikamiti vyāptisiddhau jaladharavat kṣitidharāderapyarthakāriṇaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiriti pakṣāḥ |
[62,2]
tatra prathamastāvat na yuktaḥ, anekasādhanasaṃbhave'pi vivakṣopanītasyaiva paropayogāt | ataeva śakyopanyāsatvamapi nānarthakyahetuḥ, tādṛśasyāpyupanyāsāt prāgaprāgalbhyāt | sādhyadharmiṇyupanyāsaścāsiddhau dṛṣṭāntadharmimātre upanyāsāt |
ataeva pakṣe'vaśyamupanyāsāpekṣāpyasiddhā, tadbalād vyāptisiddhau saṃścāyaṃ capalacāmara ityetāvataiva sādhyasiddheḥ | antimastu doṣaḥ sarvatra sarvopasaṃhāravatyāṃ vyāptau asiddhāyāṃ śaṅkāmavakāśayati, na ca tatra viparyayabādhakasyāpi viśeṣaḥ, kevalaṃ sāmānyena kriyāvati kṣaṇabhaṅgitayā vyāpteḥ siddhe'pi viśeṣe pravṛttyarthinaḥ saccedamityavaśyopanyasanīyatvāditi kimatra nirbandhena ? nanu tathāpi dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇi tāvattadanumānamavaśyāśrayaṇīyaṃ vyāptisādhanāya, tadeva ca kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ svadharmiṇaḥ, evaṃ sati sādhyadharmiṇyapi tadupanyasyaiva nirvṛtirālambyatām, kimiyatā prayāsena vibhāgena tadanumānāvatāraṇam ? tena ca vyāptaṃ sattvaṃ pratītya sattvāt pakṣe kṣaṇabhaṅga iti |
[62,3]
yadyevaṃ viparyayabādhakapramāṇavādino'pi samānaḥ paryanuyogaḥ, tenāpi yad yadā yajjananasvabhāvamityādiprayogasya vyāptisiddhāvapekṣaṇāt, sādhyadharmiṇi sāmarthyānapāyācca tasya | tasmāt pratipattuḥ pravṛttibhedamāśritya vibhāgo'tra kartavyaḥ, yo hi prativastu yo yajjananasamarthaḥ ityādikamavatārayan kṣaṇikatāparīkṣaṇakṣamaḥ, tasya tata eva kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiḥ kimanyahetunā ? evaṃ parapratipādane'pi pratyekavastuṣu tathaiva sādhayataḥ kṛtamanyahetūpanyāsena | yastu tadapekṣayā pratibuddhabuddhiḥ sa ekatra tatsādhanavyāpāreṇa nyāyena sarvasya kriyāvata iyameva gatiriti kṣaṇikatayā tadvyāptimanavadhārayan pratyekaṃ tannyāyāvatāraṇaprayāsamanāviśanneva yathā svayaṃ yaṃ yamarthakriyāsamarthaṃ paśyati, taṃ tamasthiraṃ sthāpayatīti sattvahetorupayogaḥ, tathā parapratipādane'pi tannyāyasiddhavyāptikaṃ sattvameva vyāpārayatīti na doṣaḥ | tadatra prativastu tannyāyāvatāraṇaprayāsaḥ asahya eva | agatikatayā tvādyaḥ pratipattā tamevāśrayet | dvitīyastu saprajñatayā ekatra pravṛttena tannyāyena jhaṭityeva kriyāmātramasthairyaparatantramavadhārayan sattvenaiva paramapi pratipādayati, na tu tannyāyasya kvacit kriyāvati kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanasāmarthyapratighātaḥ, nāpi sattvādisādhanabandhyataiva, sādhyadharmiṇyapravartitatannyāyapratyupanyāsādityalaṃ bahunā |
[63,1]
tadevaṃ vyāptirvyāpakasya vyāpyavati bhāva eveti kartṛdharmānvayarūpavyāptisaṃpāditasāmarthyādeva sattvahetoḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirapratihateti kimatra viparyaye bādhakapramāṇopanyāseneti samarthitam ? ataeva tadupanyāsāśakyatāpi na pīḍayati, viparyayasyaiva bādhakena sādhyasya siddhatvāt | śāstre'pi prathamaniyame ca vyāptiranvayarūpā bījādivadanekāntaparihāravyājena vistarataḥ prasādhitā | sphuṭataramanudbhedāttu vyatirekalakṣaṇāyāḥ parikaramātrametadāropayati loka iti ||
[63,2]
atrāpi tīrthikavacanavikrāntikṛtaṃ kautukamasti vyatirekarūpāyāmeva vyāptau |
tadāpi nāpyekaiva vidhā'nyadāpi kiṃ tuparakṛd, vā bhavet sthirābhimatasyānyadā pūrvaṃ paścād veti kramanirdeśaḥ | naiva kriyā vā bhavet anyadā naivetyabadhāraṇānna pūrva nāpi paścāt kriyetyakramanirdeśaḥ, yadi tu prāk paścād vā syāt kadācit kriyā, tadā krama evetyasaṅkīrṇamanayorlakṣaṇamākhyātaṃ bhavati | yadyapi caikasyā eva samasamayāṃ kriyāmapekṣya yaugapadyaṃ bhinnasamayamapekṣya kramaḥ, tathāpyapekṣaṇīyabhedādasaṅkara eva pitāputravat | akriyāgrahaṇena ca vastvabhāva eva vā sarvathāstu, kriyāśūnyaṃ vā svarūpamavaśiṣyatāṃ matabhedena, nātra nirbandhaḥ | tatra nāpyekaiveti pūrvaparayorekatvamātravivakṣayā jātinirdeśaḥ, pūrvā parā vā punarekānekā vā kriyā syāt | ekadā kriyāpakṣe vobhayamapyakramaśabdavācyatāṃ nātipatati |
tatrāpyanekakriyaiva tāttvikī, puñjātpuñjotpattestāttvikatvāt | śaṅkāmātreṇānavakḷptyā vā ekakriyābhidhānam | ataeva yaugapadyaśabdena tasyāpyupalakṣaṇādakramasaṃgṛhīta evārtho yaugapadyapade'pyavagantavyaḥ śāstre | etasya ca kāryagatasya prakāradvayasya kartuḥ kṣaṇabhaṅga eva saṅgatirityatyantībhāvāvadhāraṇayā vṛttyā nityād vyāvṛttiruktā | prādhānyena kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgatirityakṣaraṃ tu nityādiva kṣaṇikādapi sā vyāvṛttiḥ śaknoti lakṣayitum |
athavā vyāpyasya vā tatraiva bhāva ityanukaraṇārtham | etena nityasya kramayaugapadyābhyām arthakriyāvirodhāt tallakṣaṇaṃ sattvamavahīyate, ataḥ kṣaṇikatva eva viśrāmyati tena vyāpyata iti kramayaugapadyalakṣaṇavyāpakānupalambhād viparyaye bādhakāt sattvasyārthakriyāśaktilakṣaṇasya kṣaṇikatvena vyāptisiddhirityuktaṃ bhavati | tatra kartṛdharmo yadārthakriyā, tadārthakriyā śaktiriti vā vyavahāra ekārthaḥ | kevalaṃ karmadharmasya kramayaugapadyābhyāṃ vyāptau kathaṃ kartṛdharmasya vyāptivyavahāra iti syādāśaṅkā | tatrāpi kramākramikakāryaviṣayatayā vyāpyamānā kāraṇaśaktiḥ kramākramavyāptetyucyate vyavahāralāghavārthamiti ||
[64,1]
etena kṛtvā karaṇalakṣaṇaṃ kramamāśritya kṣaṇikādayaṃ kramo nivartayituṃ śakya ityasāraprabandhaṃ trilocanacodyaṃ nirastam | arthakriyāvirodhādityatra cārthakriyā kartṛdharma eva veditavyaḥ, tallakṣaṇaṃ sattvamiti vacanāt |
[64,2]
athavā lakṣaṇamupalakṣaṇaṃ na svabhāva iti karmadharmo'pyastu | tadatra pakṣe kramākramābhyāmupalakṣitārthakriyā nityasya virudhyata ityarthaḥ | prathamapakṣe tu kramākrameṇopalakṣitārthakāritvaṃ nityasya virodhītyarthaḥ | kramayaugapadyābhyāmiti tu viśeṣaṇānna śeṣābhyanujñāśaṅkā, hetutvārthamupādānāt | yasmāt kramākramābhyāmevārthakriyā tato nityasya virodhinī, kramākramātikramādityarthāt ||
[65,1]
kaḥ punaratra virodhaḥ ? na tāvat sahānavasthānamubhayovastutvaprāpternityaṃ sadeva syāt |
[65,2]
nāpi dvitīyaḥ | nityaṃ hi tadviparītenānityena virudhyeta | kramākramavyāptā cārthakriyā anarthakriyayaiva virudhyata iti cet ? pramāṇabalena nitye'tyantaṃ tasyā bādhasādhanād virodha eva pramāṇāntarabādhādveti vacanāt | vastutastu parasparaparihāra eva niṣṭhāsyati | kiṃ punaḥ pramāṇaṃ akṣaṇike'rthakriyābādhakamiti cet ?
yadyat kramayaugapadyavatyāmarthakriyāyāṃ nopayujyate tannārthakriyāśaktam, yathā haripadāravindam | nopayujyate ca nityābhimato bhāvaḥ kramākramadharmiṇi karmaṇīti vyāpakānupalambhaḥ | na hi kramākramābhyāmanyaḥ prakāro'sti, yenārthakriyāsaṃbhāvanāyāṃ tābhyāmavyāptirasyā bhavet | tasmādarthakriyāmātrānubaddhatayā tayoranyatarasya prakārasya ubhayorabhāve cābhāvāttābhyāmasyā vyāptisiddhiriti pakṣīkṛte tayorabhāve cārthakriyāśaktyabhāvasiddhau nānekāntastāvat |
[65,3]
tatra yat śaṅkaraḥ kramākramābhyāmarthakriyāniṣedhe prakārāntareṇa saṃbhāvayannāha — na ca tṛtīyasya prakārāntarasyābhāvasiddhiḥ, viśeṣaniṣedhasya śeṣābhyanujñāviṣayatvāditi, tannirastam | hetutvārthavacanena yattūpalabhyasvabhāvatve nātyantābhāvasiddhirupalabhyasvabhāvatvādeva paṭādivat, anupalabhyasvabhāvatve tu nāsattāniścayo viprakarṣiṇāmiti kathaṃ prakārāntarābhāvaniścayastannimittāyogāditi viplavate ? tatra yadyādaraḥ, hanta hataḥ prakāreyattāparicchedadvāreṇa tattvavyavasthānanibandhanaḥ svargāpavargamārgānuṣṭhānabhedaḥ |
yadā hi prakāradvaye tṛtīyaḥ śaṅkyate, traye caturthaścatuṣṭayādau pañcamādiḥ, tadā sarvatrānantaprakāratve prakāradvayatrayādiniyamakṛtaṃ tattvavyavasthānaṃ kutaḥ, yathā catvāri pramāṇāni, ṣaṭ padārthāḥ ? yadā ca pramāṇaprakāraśatamanyadapi saṃbhāvyate, tadā caturbhiryanna siddhaṃ tadanyena siddhaṃ, catuḥsiddhaṃ cānyena bādhitamiti kathaṃ taddvāreṇa tattvavyavasthitiḥ ?
evaṃ yadārthasahasre dravyādivyatirekiṇi sidhyati tattvapariniṣṭhāviplavāt kimabhyudayaniḥśreyasayorvātmā'nuṣṭeyamastu ? kathaṃ cānityasya jñānakāritvākāritvapakṣau dūṣayitvā nirvṛtamanena svayamevaṃ prakāreṇa prakāraśatasya niṣeddhumaśakyatvāt ?
[66,1]
kiṃ ca paśavo'pi yadayuktaṃ paśyanti na tadaiva tadācarantīti kathamanena sāhasamidamanuṣṭhitam ? anupalabdherdṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpekṣābhyāṃ prakāradvaitaṃ niyamya kramākramābhyāṃ dvaitanirākaraṇaṃ nāma, prakārāntarasyopadarśayitumaśakyatvāditi tu kramākrame'pi dvaitavādināṃ nāśakyam | tasmāt kimapyayaṃ jalpamahodadhināmaparipuṣṭaye viceṣṭatām, ekaniṣedhenāparavidhāne tāvadaśakyābhidhānaḥ prakārāntarasaṃbhavaḥ ?
[66,2]
kiṃ ca ekakālakriyānantaraṃ kriyāntarasya bhāve kramavyavahāro'bhāve cākrama iti bhāvābhāvayorapi tṛtīyaśaṅketi mahattārkikatvam, tadalaṃ nirbandhena | sthitametat kramākramābhyāmarthakriyāśaktervyāptireveti |
[66,3]
yadapi trilocanaḥ kaścit sahakāripratyayaḥ pratyakṣaḥ | parokṣaścetaraḥ | tataḥ pratyakṣaparokṣasahakāripratyayasākalyamasarvavidā pratyakṣato na śakyaṃ pratyetum | tathā ca sati sādṛśasahakāripratyayasākalyavataḥ kramayaugapadyasyātyantaparokṣatvāt tena vyāptaṃ sattvamapi parokṣameveti kathaṃ pratibandhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa sidhyatītyāha, tadapi nirupayogam |
kāryadharmau hi kramākramau pratipāditau | tataḥ kāraṇasāmagryāḥ sākalyāsākalyaniścayābhāve'pi kramayaugapadyaniyamaḥ kāryāṇāmadhyakṣagocara eva | ekadaiva kāryotpattiranyadāpi neti kathamagocaraḥ pratyakṣasya ? tadāpi hi kāryamekamanekaṃ vā syāt | pratyakṣeṇa vā tathā gṛhītamanekasaṃbhave'pi caikaṃ gṛhītamastu, sarvathā kramākramābhyāmeva vyāptā kāryaniṣpatiriti siddhametat |
[66,4]
nanu kṣaṇabhaṅgapakṣe nārthakriyāpratītiḥ, nāpi kramākramapratītiriti kathaṃ vyāptivyavasthā ? tathā ca śaṅkaraḥ, kṣaṇikatve sati sarvasaṃvittīnāṃ svabhāvaniyamena hetuphalayoḥ svarūpānvayavyatirekāsiddhau sarvatra tadbhāvasyāvagantumaśakyatvāt, na hi kāryasaṃvittyā tasya hetubhāve bhāvaḥ pratīyate, tadā tasya hetoratītatvāt | nāpi hetusaṃvittyā kāryasya tadbhāve bhāvo'vasīyate, tadā tasyānupapattereva, na cātītānāgatayorvartamānena siddhiratiprasaṅgāt | nāpi kāryasaṃvittyaiva hetusvabhāvasaṃvittiḥ, adṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasyāpi dhūme'gnijanyatvaviniścayaprasaṅgāt | etena hetumātrasaṃvittyā kāryasaṃvittirapāstā | hetuvyatireke tu kāryavyatirekaḥ svasaṃvittivādino manorathasyāpyaviṣayaḥ, tasya hetvabhāve kāryābhāvapratipattāvupāyāsaṃbhavāt | nahi tacca nāsti tena ca pratipattiriti nyāyyam | tadayaṃ kāryasya hetusadbhāve bhāvaṃ tadabhāve cābhāvaṃ pratipadyamāno'vasthitaṃ pratisandhātāraṃ prasādhayatīti | evaṃ ca yadyavasthikartṛsiddhiḥ, tadā sādharaṇānekānta eva maulaḥ sattvahetuḥ, kimatra viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsaḥ kariṣyati ? tadaniṣṭau tu vyāptigrahānupapatteḥ sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamubhayorapi |
yathā ca kramiṇī hetuphale pratyetumaśakye evaṃ phale apīti na kramapratītiḥ, nāpi yaugapadyasya |
[67,1]
yathāha sa eva, nāpi yaugapadyasya, bhinnākāreṇa jñānena pratiniyatākārāṇāṃ yaugapadyasyāśakyasādhanatvāt | na tāvadbhireva jñāne yaugapadyaṃ pratyetavyam, teṣāmitaretarāsaṃvedyatve santānāntaravat yugapadbhāvasyāsiddheḥ | na caikamanekākāram, svabhāvabhūtākārabhede bhedasyāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāt | bhede tu vijñānasyākārebhyo'rthāntaratvaprasaṅge na viṣayasya tadākāratvaṃ samarthitaṃ bhaviṣyatīti |
[67,2]
atrocyate, pratisandhātṛsvīkārastāvadasaṃbaddhaḥ, pratisandheyābhimatābhirbuddhibhirbhedābhedavikalpākṣamatvāt | abhede hi sa eva vā syād buddhaya eva vā ? atra ca prathamapakṣe karmaṇaḥ, pakṣāntare karturabhāvāt kaḥ pratisandhānārthaḥ ? bhede'pi buddhibhyo bhidyamānasya jaḍasya kaḥ pratisandhānārthaḥ ? buddhiyogād draṣṭṛvat pratisandhātṛtvamiti cet ? buddhireva tarhi draṣṭrī pratisandhātrī ceti niyatasvīkāre tadyogādanyasya tathātvamiti kimanena yācitakamaṇḍanena ? buddhīnāṃ kartṛtvābhāvāditi cet ? taddvāreṇāpi tarhi tasyātmano draṣṭṛtvādivyavahārānupapattiḥ | yadi hi buddhirhetoḥ phalasya vā draṣṭrī syāt, tadānantaryapratiniyamasya cānusandhātrī kalpikā, tadyogāttasya draṣṭṛtvaṃ pratisandhātṛtvaṃ vocyata iti syādapi | prativiṣayamalabdhaviśeṣāyāṃ ca buddhau saṃbandho'pi na viśeṣaṃ vyavahārayitumīśaḥ, adhunā nibandhanādhigantā, adhunā phalasya, idānīṃ pratisandhāteti | tathāvidhabuddhigataviśeṣasvīkāre tu kimapareṇa kartavyam tāvataiva paryāptatvād vyavahārasya | sthirātmānamantareṇa saiva buddhirna syāditi cet ?
[68,1]
kenaivaṃ pratārito'si ? aho mohamāhātmyaṃ yadīdṛśānapi paravaśīkaroti |
tathāhi nedamidamantareṇeti yaducyate tat khalvanyatra pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ sāmarthyāvadhāraṇe sati yujyate, vahneriva dhūme | cakṣurādivad vā dṛṣṭakāraṇasāmagrye kāryādarśane paścād darśane ca kiñcidanyadapekṣaṇīyamastīti sāmānyākāreṇa | ādyaḥ pakṣastāvannāstīti vyaktam | dvitīyo'pi na saṃbhavī | nahi kāraṇabuddhisamanantaraṃ kāryabuddhau satyāṃ niścayapravṛttasya idamasyānantaraṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mayeti pratisandhānamadṛṣṭapūrvaṃ, kadācid, yato'nyasya sāmarthyaparikalpanaṃ syāt | evaṃ smaraṇamapyanubhavāt kutaścit paramparayā śaktipariṇāmadvāreṇa, kutaścit sākṣāt tat paripākabalāditi | anyasyānubhave tarhi kathamanyasya na smṛtiḥ | anyasyeti na saṃbandhī siddhaścodyaṃ kimīdṛśam ||
anubhavādibhyo bhinnasaṃbandhisiddhyadhikaraṇavivādaprakrame tameva siddhamāsthāya paryanuyoga ityasaṃbaddhametat | tatsiddhau hi vivādaparyavasānāt kā parāpekṣā ? tasmādanyasyeti vivādapadatvādapanīyānubhave kathaṃ na smṛtiriti pariśiṣyamāṇaṃ na prakṛtopayogi |
evaṃ tu yujyate codyārthaḥ | yaddehasaṃbaddho'nubhavastadanyatra dehe kasmānna smṛterudaya iti ?
evaṃ ca vadatā yatkṣetrasambandhi bījaṃ tadanyatra kṣetre kiṃ nāṅkurajanmetyuktaṃ bhavati | sa ca kutastyo nyāyaḥ ?
[68,2]
nanu kāryakāraṇabhāvamātrādanubhavasmaraṇayorna kācidaparā pratyāsattiḥ, na ca kāryakāraṇabhāve'yaṃ niyamo, yadādhārameva kāraṇaṃ tadādhārameva kāryamiti, viṣayādatyantadūre'pi jñānakāryadarśanāt | evaṃ tarhi nāṅkurasyāpi kāryatāmātrādaparā pratyāsattiriti jñānamivāṅkuraṃ dūre'pi bījaṃ janayet | nanu bījārambhiṇaḥ eva paramāṇavaḥ kecidaṅkure samavāyikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyamānāḥ kathaṃ kṣetrāntare'ṅkuramutpādayitumīśate ?
bhavatastu tathāvidhapratyāsattivirahāt | vijñānādinā sādhāraṇaṃ kāryatvamasyeti dūre'pi jananaprasaṅgo'nivārya iti cet ? kasmāt punaraṅkura eva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāyikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante na jñānādau, kāryatvena sarveṣāmekarasatvāt ? tataḥ sarveṣāmaṅkuravat taddeśa eva jananaṃ, jñānādivad vāṅkurasyāpi dūre jananaṃ, kāryatvenāviśeṣāt, tadvadevāṅkure'pi nimittakāraṇatvād bījasya |
[69,1]
nanu yatraiva kārye bījaparamāṇavaḥ samavāyikāraṇatāṃ pratipadyante sa evāṅkuraḥ, tat kathamaṅkurādanyatra teṣāṃ samavāyikāraṇatā codyate ? evaṃ tarhi kāryatvenaikarasatayā samavāyikāraṇatāyā duṣpariharatvādaṅkuraikarūpatvaṃ sarveṣāmekadeśatā caprasahyāyāteti sthāne phalitaṃ parihārapratyāśayā | yadi ca kāryatvena sarveṣāmaviśeṣaḥ kāryāṇām, kāraṇānāmapi sarveṣāṃ kāraṇatvenāviśeṣa iti viśvasya vaicitryamatrāṇam |
tasmātkāryatve satyapi na rītirekaiva sarveṣāmiti | yathā nisargabhedāt kvacit kiñcit samavāyikāraṇatvena kvacidasamavāyikāraṇatvena kvacinnimittakāraṇatvenopayujyate bhavataḥ, tathāsmākamapi kiñcit kāryaṃ samānadeśameva heturutpādayati, kiñcid vyavahitadeśam, kāryaṃ ca kiñcinniyamena hetudeśa evotpattidharmakaṃ kiñcidanyathā | tathaikatra kārye pratyabhijñāsaṃbhavo nānyatra kāryatvāviśeṣe'pi dīpāntaravat jñānavacca | tādṛk kāryāpekṣayā ca yatra bhavataḥ samavāyikāraṇavyavasthā, tatropādānakāraṇavyavahāro'smākamātmāderanyatra | tathāvidhahetuphalaparamparāyāṃ ca ekatra santānavyavasthānamanyatra sahakāritvamātramiti prakriyābhede'pi kāryadvaitaṃ tādṛg nisargasiddhamastīti bhavato'pyaśakyamatikramitumiti sthitametat | tathābhūtabhedasaṃbhave ca yatkāryakaraṇādhikaraṇa evotpattidharmakaṃ tatkathamitaratrotpadyate ? kāraṇaṃ vā svādhikaraṇa eva śakyotpādanaṃ kāryaṃ kathamanyatra janayet ? tadayamanubhavo'pi svādhikaraṇajanyaṃ smaraṇamaṅkuramiva bījāt kathamanyatrotpādayet ? smṛtirvānubhavādhikaraṇaniyatotpattiraṅkuravat kathamanyatrotpadyeta, yato dehāntare smaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ codyamavakāśamāsādayet ? ātmavāde tu duṣpariharametat, vyāpinastasya tenaiva smṛtijananarūpeṇa dehāntare'pi sthānāt | adṛṣṭāśrayaṇaṃ ca nityasyaiveti | bījāṅkuravadanubhavasmaraṇayornyāyo nānyavaditi kathamavagantavyamiti cet ?
bījāṅkurayorapi sa nyāyastathādarśanādevāvasīyate, tathā niyamadarśanaṃ cānubhavasmaraṇayorapyasti, na hyanyadehe'nubhavavati anyamūrtiḥ smṛtimatī nāma |
[70,1]
nanu dehaḥ kathamanubhavavān ? tadādhāratayā tatkāraṇatayā tena saha samānakāraṇatayā vā saṃbandhavivakṣāstīti na kṣatiḥ | kiṃ cātmano'pi kathamanubhavavattvam ? samavāyabalāditi cet ? nanu samavāyo'pīhetibuddhiheturiṣyamāṇa ihetibuddhinibandhanakalpana eva | asti ceha śarīre buddhiḥ, ataḥ kiṃ na samavāyakalpanāpi ? ayutasiddhatvābhāvāt śarīrabuddhyoḥ pṛthageva pratīyamānatvāditi cet ? nanu pṛthakpratīyamānayorihedamiti pratītiniyamaḥ, uparyadhobhāvena hi bhāvadvaye paridṛśyamāne parasparāsaṅkareṇa saptamīprathamayornirdeśa upapadyeta, yadā tu pṛthagdarśanameva nāsti tadā kathamihedamiti bhedena nirdiśan prekṣāvattāyā na hīyate ? samavāyaviṣaye kvacidapi bhedasyādṛṣṭeriti cet ? ataeva svayamiheti buddhiṃ vikalpamātratvena icchayānirvartanayogyāmutpādya samavāyo nāma kalpyate | iheti buddheḥ samavāyasiddhirihetidhīśca dvayadarśane syāt | na ca kvacittadviṣaye dvayekṣā svakalpanāmātramato'bhyupāyaḥ ||
tena cāsaṃvidyamānasyaivātmano buddhimattāvyavahāra iti bandhyāputreṇa turagaśṛṅgasya kholighaṭanavṛttāntamanuharati | yat khalu yāvatopayogena kalpitaṃ tāvata upayogasya anyena siddhireva tasyābhāvaḥ, siddhaścātmano'pi smṛtyādyupayogo'nyatheti | tasmāt naikakāyastho'nubhavaḥ kāyāntare smaraṇakaraṇāya prabhavati |
[70,2]
nanu kṣaṇikatve dehāntara eva smṛterudayāt kathamidaṃ śakyaparihāram, janmāntaraparigrahe vā tataḥ santānāntaratvenābhimate'pi dehe kiṃ na prasaṅgo'nyatvasyāviśeṣāditi cet ? īdṛśaṃ dehāntare smṛtijananamātmano'pi duṣpariharam, tato'nyatrāpi tatprasaṅgo'nyatvasyāviśeṣāditi samānam | yadyapi ca kāyasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ neṣṭam, āśunāśitvaṃ punastairiṣṭameva, tataḥ samāno doṣo yadbhayādātmavādasvīkāraḥ | athātmavāde tasyātmanaḥ karmaṇābhisaṃskṛta eva dehe smṛtijananamiti na doṣaḥ, nairātmyavāde tu kasya tat karma ? śārīrātiriktā hi buddhireva kṣaṇikā saṃbhavati | ataeva ca na kartṛkṣaṇasya tatkarmasukhaduḥkhādi saṃvartanīyam, tasya tadupabhogābhāvāt | yasya ca kṣaṇasyopabhogaḥ so'karteti kṛtanāśākṛtābhyāgamadoṣastvatirikto bhavatu, na tu kasyacit karmasiddhiryataḥ prakṛtadoṣaparihāraḥ syāt | na ca santāno'pi gīyamāno bhinnaḥ kaścidasti | na ca karmāpi bhinnaṃ bhavatāmastītyabhitti citrakarma ||
[71,1]
atrocyate | kartṛkṣaṇasya tāvat tatkarma tatphalopabhogābhāve'pi nāpahnavasaham |
nahi dāhādikamakurvatotpāditena vahninā tadvān na bhavati naraḥ | antimakṣaṇasyāpi tatkarmopakārakatayā saṃbadhyate paramparayā, tata evopabhogabhāgitvāt |
ekakālatā tu kāryakāraṇayorapi na saṃbhavati, saṃbhavati ca merumandarayoḥ | tasmādupakāradvārakameva bhede tasyedamiti ghaṭanam, sa copakāro'ntimasya tatkṛto mahānasti, tanmadhyavartināṃ ca tatsantānavartināṃ kṣaṇānāṃ tādṛgantimakṣaṇaprasūtisāmarthyaṃ sākṣātparaṃparayā vā, tata eva karmaṇa ityupakāradvāraka eva teṣāmapi tatsambandhaḥ | evaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ karmasambandhavyavasthitau sthitāyāṃ tatkarmādhipatyenopanīyamāna eva śarīre tatkarmābhisaṃbhūtānāṃ buddhidehakṣaṇānāmudayaḥ, nānyatra tādṛk pratyāsatterabhāvāt | karma ca kāmaṃ na bhinnamasti vyatirekī ca nirdeśo'pi vyavahārānurodhena | yastu prāktanaḥ karmasaṃbaddha ityucyate kṣaṇaḥ, sa tādṛg viśeṣabhūto jātaḥ, yataḥ paryante tatphalopabhoktṛkṣaṇaprasavasamarthasantānasaṃbhavaḥ, tadanurūpaśarīrasantatisaṃbhavaśca | tatrādyād viśiṣṭād yau buddhidehakṣaṇau alpatamaviśeṣayogināvupajātau saṃbhūyottarāvalpataraviśeṣau janayataḥ, tau cālpaviśeṣāvuttarau janayata ityanayā diśā tāvacchaktilakṣaṇaviśeṣaprakarṣastaratamādibhāvenopacīyate yāvadantimajananasamarthodayastato'ntima iti |
ekasāmagryadhīnatayā parasparānubaddhayorbuddhidehayoranyaparamparāṃ prati viśiṣṭayornaikavyatirekeṇa dvaitīyikaśaṅkāvakāśaḥ | janmāntaraparigrahe'pi tadāyuḥsaṃskārakṣīṇe kṣīyamāṇamūrtikṣaṇāntarasahakāriṇā manaḥkṣaṇena janitaṃ tasyānurūpaṃ vapuranyat pūrvavanmanasaḥ sāhāyakamātanotīti na dehāntare smṛtibhoktṛtvacintāvakāśaḥ | na cātra santānanāmnā bhinnena kiñcit, kṣaṇānāṃ karmasaṃbandhasiddhidvāreṇaiva santāne'pi siddherapratibandhāt, tebhyastasya vyatirekāt | na ca mukhyataḥ santānadvāreṇa siddhāntopakramaḥ, kiṃ tu kṣaṇadvāreṇeti sarvamavadātaṃ mūlapariśodhanāditi ||
[72,1]
yaduktam, yasminneva hi santāne āhitā karmavāsanā | phalaṃ tatraiva badhnāti karpāse raktatā yathā ||
iti, tat svābhimatasantānalakṣaṇaprasiddhau ||
[72,2]
yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇakāra etad dūṣayānnāha — na, sādhanadūṣaṇāsaṃbhavāt, anvayādyabhāvānna sādhanam | na hi kāryakāraṇabhāvāt smṛtiḥ karpāse raktatādivadityanvayaḥ saṃbhavati | nāpi yatra na smṛtiḥ tatra na kāryakāraṇabhāva iti vyatireko'sti | asiddhatvādyanudbhāvanānna dūṣaṇam | na hi pūrvabuddhyanubhūte'rthe uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtiḥ saṃbhavati, tato'nyatvāt santānāntarabuddhivadityasya hetoḥ karpāse raktatāvadityanena na kaściddoṣaḥ pratipādyata iti | tadasamīkṣyābhidhānam, sādhanārthāparijñānāt | na hīha śloke kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ smṛtau hetutvenopanyastaḥ pratīyate | kiṃ tarhi ? karmavāsanā |
vāsanā hi karmaṇābhisaṃskāraḥ | vasitaṃ hyabhisaṃskṛtamucyate | karmakṛto viśeṣo yatra santāne utpāditastatraiva bhogādiphalabandho, nānyatra | yatra nāsau viśeṣa iti pratijñāya karpāse raktatā yathā iti vadataḥ saṃskārasantānabhedo vā heturabhipretaḥ, sādhyaṃ cānyatra bhogādiphalaniṣedhaḥ, tatsantāne tatphalayogyatā ca pratīyate | tadayaṃ prayogaḥ, yo yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kvacitsantāne āhitaḥ sa tatraiva phaladānayogyo nānyatra | yathā karpāsasantāne bījāvasthāyāṃ rāgadravyayogajanitaḥ puṣpāvasthāyāṃ phalāvasthāyāṃ vā rāgaṃ phalamunmīlayituṃ yogyo nānyasantāne |
[72,3]
saṃskāraścāyaṃ dānādikarmajanitaścittasantāna iti | svabhāvahetureva samudāyasādhyāpekṣayā | saṃskāramātrānubandhinī hi tatsantāne phaladānayogyatā anyasantāne sarvathā tadayogyatā ceti nimittāntarānapekṣaṇāt | ekaikasādhyatve tu prathame svabhāvahetuḥ | dvitīye tu viruddhavyāptopalabdhiḥ, svādhārādanyasantāne phaladānaviruddhena svādhārasantāna eva phaladānena vyāptasya saṃskāratvasyopalabdheḥ | tatra yadi saṃskāre'pi sati tatra santāne phaladānayogyatā nimittāntaramapekṣeta, prayatnena saṃskāraghaṭanamanarthakaṃ syāt | anyasantāne'pi phaladānasāmarthye ca dvitīyaprayatnavaiyarthyam | na caikāmalakyāṃ kṣīrāvaseke sarvāmalakī madhuraphalā | tasmātsvasantāna eva phaladānena vyāptiḥ saṃskārasyeti nānekāntaḥ | saṃskāraśca karmakṛto viśeṣaścetasa ityāgamasiddhamabhyupagamyaiva codyavat samādhānamapīti nāsiddhiḥ | sapakṣe bhāvānna virodho vyāptyasiddhervā | athavā, yo yaḥ santānaḥ sa svādhikaraṇa eva saṃskāre phaladānayogyo yathā karpāsasantānaḥ, santānaścāyaṃ cittasantāna iti pūrvavat ||
[73,1]
smṛtthādiphalāpekṣayā'pyayameva nyāyaḥ | yadi santānadvāreṇeyaṃ vyavasthā, tadā vidyāyonisaṃbandhaprasiddhe'pi santāne prasaṃgaḥ | tato guruṇānubhūtādau śiṣyasya smṛtyādiḥ syāt, evaṃ pituranubhavādau putrasya bhavet | naitādṛśaḥ santāno'tra vivakṣitaḥ upādānopādeyabhūtahetuphalaparamparārūpaḥ | kiṃ punarupādānopādeyalakṣaṇam ? ekādhāratāniyamo'sati vicārakāraṇe, vicāre'pi tadyogyatāniyamaḥ | vicitrā hi kāryakāraṇaparamparopapāditā pūrvam, tatraivaṃlakṣaṇā paramparā santāna ucyata ityapi sūcitameva | na caivaṃ guruśiṣyacetasoḥ pitāputramanasorvā astīti nātiprasaṅgadoṣo nyāyabhūṣaṇīyaḥ | santānopādānavyavasthayorvānyonyāśrayadoṣaḥ, upādānavyavasthāyāstadanāśrayatvapratipādanāt |
[73,2]
athavā abhrānta saṃmataikāvasāyaḥ prakṛtivikriye ubhau hetuphalasyopādānopādeyalakṣaṇam | hetuphalasantatau idamupādānamidamupādeyamiti pratyabhijñāpratyayena lakṣitaṃ veditavyam | visabhāgotpattau tu prakṛtirupādānasya vikṛtirupādeyasya lakṣaṇaṃ svabhāva eva | prakṛtivikṛtitvaṃ vā lakṣaṇamiti bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ, kāṣṭhayūpavat kāṣṭhāṅgāravacca | anekotpattāvapi bhinnā eva bhāgā upādānam | yathā dhūma uṣmādīnāmaṅgārāṇām, buddhāvapyekapuruṣaprajñaptirekāvasāyaḥ | asti ca viṣayoparāgaṃ vivecya caitanyamātramāmṛśata ekapuruṣābhimatāyāṃ santatau saiveyaṃ buddhirityavasāyaḥ | te punaratrāśeṣasvarūpānanukārāt, anukārasaṃbhave'pi stambhāntaravadekāvasāyo bhrānta iti na pitāputrādāvupādānādivyavasthā | tadevamupādānādilakṣaṇamanapekṣya tādṛksantatau upādānādivyavasthāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ kīdṛśe santāne āhitā karmavāsaneti jijñāsāyāṃ yatropādānādivyavastheti bhaṇitau na doṣaḥ |
[74,1]
yat punarayamevāha — na, sambandhaviśeṣābhāve kāraṇamātraviśeṣādupādānetaravibhāgānupapatteḥ, yathāsmākaṃ janakatvāviśeṣe'pi samavāyyasamavāyinimittakāraṇavibhāgaḥ saṃbandhaviśeṣāt, na tathā tava kāraṇānāmupādānetaravibhāgaṃ paśyāma iti |
etadapi dūṣitameva, kāraṇatvasāmānye'pi kāryāpekṣayā vibhāgasya darśitatvāt | kāryakāraṇayoranyonyaviśeṣānapekṣaṇe hi saṃbandhadvāreṇāpi vyavasthādausthyamāpāditam |
na ca samavāyaḥ kṣama ityapi leśena sūcitameva | tasmānna saṃskārasantānayordūṣaṇaṃ kiñcit |
[74,2]
yadyapi cātra śloke karmavāsanāśabdaḥ prayukto na cāsyārthaḥ karpāsamanveti, tathāpi vāsanārtho'bhisaṃskārastāvadanvetīti sa eva hetuḥ sūcito grāhyaḥ | athavā karmaśabdenāpi kriyā | yatra santāne yayā kayācit kriyayā kṛto'bhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ |
etena vyāptipradarśanam, pakṣadharmastu prastāvād boddhavyaḥ | tataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ sākṣāt smṛtau pratipādakamādāya yaduktaṃ tatsarvaṃ viplutam, kāryakāraṇabhāvāśrayaviśeṣānvayinī tu smṛtirityanavadyam |
[74,3]
yatpunarasya sādhanaṃ na pūrvabuddhyānubhūte'rthe uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtirbhavatyanyatvāt, santānāntarabuddhivaditi, tatrotrarabuddhīnāṃ dharmiṇīnāṃ bhinnasmṛtirūpabuddhisambandho niṣidhyata uta smṛtirūpatvameva tāsāṃ vāryate, atha smṛtyā phalavatyastā na bhavantīti pratipādyate ? prathamapakṣastāvadayuktaḥ | na hyanyā smṛtiranyā ca smṛtimatī matiriṣyate asmābhiryanniṣedhaḥ syāt, api tu smṛtirūpaiva sā matiriti | athāśvasya smarato gavekṣaṇakāle taddarśanaṃ smṛtimad bhavatīti cet ? tat kiṃ tadavasthāyā eva smṛterniṣedho vivakṣitaḥ ? kevalā tu yadi smṛtirbhavati tadā bhavatu | naivaṃ cet ?
kimanena tarhi uttarabuddhīnāmiti sahacāranirdeśena ? athānumānārthaṃ dharminirdeśa eva iti cet — na, prakṛtābhimatasākalyasiddheḥ sarvathottarakālaṃ smṛtiniṣedhasyeṣṭatvāt pakṣaikadeśāsiddhiḥ sādhanasya | athāśaktidaśāyāṃ kevalasmṛtikāle niṣedho neṣṭa eva |
tarhi vinātmānamuttarakālaṃ smṛtisaṃbhave buddhyantarasahacārakālena kimaparāddhaṃ yat tatraiva niṣedhaḥ ? nāpi vyāptiviṣaye kiñcidasti bādhakam |
[75,1]
dvitīyapakṣe tu uttarabuddhīnāṃ smṛtitvaniṣedhe kimanubhavasyaiva smṛtitvamatha pūrvabuddhīnām ? sarvathā niṣedhe tu kiṃ viśeṣanirdeśeneti pūrvavat |
[75,2]
tṛtīye tu vikalpe evameva viśeṣanirdeśavaiyarthyaṃ samarthanīyam | atha viśeṣanirdeśasyopalakṣaṇatvāt sarvaivānubhavādanyā buddhirna smṛtirūpā, nāpi smṛtimutpādayati ityabhimatam | anubhavasya na hi tathātvaṃ niṣiddham, tatto'nubhavaḥ smṛtirūpaḥ smṛtiṃ cotpādayatītyubhayamapyaniṣṭamāsaktam | anyathā'nubhavādanyatayā viśeṣaṇamanarthakam |
anarthakamevāstu, sarveṣāmeva jñānānāṃ dharmitvamastu | tadāpyanubhavādanyatvaṃ hetuḥ pakṣaikadeśāsiddhaḥ, anubhavasyaiva tadanyathābhāvāt | athottaragrahaṇaṃ vivādapadatvena na tvanyavyavacchedena, anyāsāṃ tu buddhīnāṃ bauddhenāpi smṛtibhāvāniṣṭeḥ | tathāpi tṛtīyapakṣe nedamuttaram, anubhavasyāpi vivādapadatvāt | nairātmyapakṣe hyanubhavo'pi sākṣāt smṛtimutpādayatītyaniṣṭameva bhavataḥ | bauddhasya punariṣṭam | tadayamanubhavasya smṛtijanakatvaṃ na svīkartuṃ śakto'priyatvāt, na parihartum, hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśāsiddheriti |
[75,3]
astu caivamubhayapakṣe'pi tu vyāptirna śakyā | tathā hi yasyā uttarabuddheḥ smṛtitvaṃ smṛtijanakatvaṃ veṣyate, tasyā yadi tadubhayaprāptāvanubhavādanyatvahānirupapādayituṃ pāryate na paryavasyatu vyāptistadanyatvasya tadubhayaniṣedhena | na caivaṃ śakyam | anubhavādanyatvahānāvanubhavatvameva, tacca kathaṃ smṛtitve vaktuṃ śakyam ? smṛtijanakatve ca taducyamānamanubhavasya smaraṇahetutvamanapanīya na viśrāmyati | pratibandhasiddhau hi prasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ | evamuttarakālabhāvitvādayo'pi nāśaṅkyāḥ, śakyapratīkāratvāt tadvadeva |
anekāntastu hetudoṣo vyāpterabhāvāt | tasmād yadi codyacuñcutāyāṃ bharastadaivaṃ brūyāḥ |
anubhavamātrāt karmamātrād vā smaraṇabhogādi janyaṃ cet — bhinnasantāne'pi janmaprasaṅgaḥ, na cābhimate'pi | yad yenāviśiṣṭasāmarthyāsāmarthyaṃ tat tenāviśiṣṭaphalāphalatvam, yathā bījorvījalajvalanapavanādisāmagrīdvayam | aviśiṣṭasāmarthyāsāmarthyaṃ ca santānadvayamanubhavādapīti svabhāvahetuḥ | atra ca siddhiḥ yasminneva hi ityādinā darśitaiva, karmavāsanā ityādinā karpāsavat saṃskāraviśeṣasya vyaktamuktatvāt | yathā prathamaṃ prathitamasmābhiḥ | evamanubhavāt smṛtiriti samānanyāyam |
[76,1]
athavā pūrvoktahetāvayaṃ paryanuyogaḥ, kimanubhavasmaraṇādereva paramparayā hetuphalasaṃmatasyāyaṃ nyāyo'nyatvānna jananamiti, athānyasyāpi ? yadi tāvat prakṛtasyaivāyaṃ yautukalabdho nyāyaḥ tadā yuktiḥ kācidabhidhīyatām, yataḥ sāmānyasiddhaṃ kramamatikramyāyamatra viśeṣo gamyeta | santānāntare'darśanāditi cet ? yadviśeṣaparamparayā jananamanyatve tadabhāve tadadarśanaṃ bhavet, yathāraktabījakarpāse rāgādarśanam | na ca tāvatā sarvatrājananamiti śakyam ||
[76,2]
dvitīyapakṣe tvasiddherudbhāvanametat | rakte bīje'nyasyāpi tatsantānabhuvaḥ puṣpasya phalasya vā tatphalarāgadarśanāt | yat punaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvena smṛtimāśaṅkya nānātvasyāvañcanādityuktam, atrāpi trapā tapasvino ekataḥ kṣiptā tadvacanena, yadi saṃskṛtakarpāse kārya vāryeta sarvaṃ śobhate | tadayaṃ sāmānyasiddho nyāyaḥ | pṛthaktve'pi viśeṣāntarāpekṣaṃ phalamekatra santāne bhavati nānyatreti prakṛte'pi vārayitumaśakyaḥ |
ślokena cānena sādhanaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ vā saṃpāditamityāstāṃ tāvat | tat siddhamavasthitaikābhāve'pyanubhavabhāvitasantānasaṃskāreṇa smaraṇam | na ca pratyakṣeṇānubhavasmaraṇayoḥ kvacidekādhāratvaṃ dṛṣṭam |
[76,3]
yadapyatroktam, na, dṛṣṭatvāt | tathā hi pūrvaṃ yamarthamevānubhūtavānahaṃ tametarhi smarāmi, yo'hamanubhavitā so'haṃ smarteti anubhavasmaraṇayorabhinnādhāratvaṃ liṅgasambandhasmṛtthanapekṣamāptopadeśānapekṣaṃ ca niścinoti | na ceyaṃ bhrāntirvisaṃvādābhāvāt | sukhāderapi pratyakṣatvamapahnavāno nākṣajena pratibodhayitavyaḥ | tathā cānusandhānecchādveṣādīnāmapyekakāraṇatvaṃ pratyakṣato gṛhyate, yamahamadrākṣaṃ tamahaṃ paśyāmīti | taṃ dṛṣṭvāhamicchāmi dveṣmi vā | tamicchan dviṣan vā prayate | yatamāno'haṃ tamarthaṃ prāpya sukhī duḥkhī vā saṃvṛtto'smīti | tadevamahamityetasmin jñāne yo'rthaścakāsti tadadhikaraṇaḥ smṛtyanusandhānecchādayaḥ pratyakṣataḥ pratibhāntītyataḥ pratyakṣeṇātmā gṛhyate | na hyahamiti jñānaṃ sandigdhaṃ bhrāntaṃ vā | nāpi laiṅgikaṃ śābdaṃ veti | tadapi mithyāparitoṣamātram | tathā hi vikalpastāvadayamastyahameva draṣṭā smartā ceti | na ca sarvo vikalpa āśvāsaviṣayaḥ |
tathā cāyaṃ caturdhā darśitaḥ trilocanenāpi |
[77,1]
tatra pratyakṣapṛṣṭhabhāvī tāvanna bhavati, pratyakṣāntarasya tadgrāhakasya svayamapyanaṅgīkārāt, yasyāyaṃ pṛṣṭabhāvī varṇyeta | laiṅgikatvamapi svayameva nirastam | tad yadi avastukaḥ sandigdhavastuko vā bhavan bhavatā pramāṇīkriyate, kasya kiyatī kṣatiḥ ?
[77,2]
athaibhyo bhinnaḥ pañcamo'yaṃ pratyakṣa iṣyate | sarvasya tarhi svābhimate pramāṇavirahiṇi viṣaye sulabha eva nyāyaḥ iti na kvacit siddhipratibandhaḥ |
saṃvādena viśeṣa iti cet ? sa punaḥ saṃvādo'rthakriyāprāptiḥ pramāṇāntaravṛttirvā syāditi nirūpitaprāyam | pramāṇāntarabhāve ca tadevāstu kimanena ? arthakriyā ca nāvasthitasādhyā kācinniścitā, sarvasyā buddhiśarīrābhyāṃ siddheḥ | nāpi tadatiriktagocaro'haṃpratyayaḥ | yathā hi so'yaṃ caitra ityatra caitraśarīre eva upādhyavasthākṛtaṃ bhedamavigaṇayya pūrvāparakālayorekatvena pratyabhijñāyete, tathā ahameva draṣṭā smartā cetyanenāpi pratyayena | kevalamayaṃ buddhidvārakaḥ samudāyavyapadeśaḥ, yathā yo'haṃ mūrkha āsaṃ sa paṇḍito'smīti | kaścit punardehadvāreṇa vyapadeśo yathā gauraḥ pīno vā'hamiti, ekadeśena samudāyavyapadeśasya prasiddhatvāt | kaścit punarubhayadvārako yathā mayā rājyaṃ kṛtaṃ mama durgatirityādi yathāyathamūhyam | sukhaduḥkhecchādveṣaprayatnadharmādharmadvārakā api buddhikārakā eva vyapadeśāḥ, ahaṃ sukhī yāvadahaṃ dhārmika iti buddhivyatirekābhāvāt teṣām | mukhaṃ śarīraṃ vā'syāstīti bhedanirdeśo'pi samudāyaikadeśabhedavivakṣayā, yathā vṛkṣasya śākhā | ata eva mukhamahamiti na bhavati |
[77,3]
kathaṃ tarhi mama matimūrtī iti ? yathā śilāputrakasya śarīram | tarhi buddhiśarīre ityapi syāt, śilāputrakaḥ śarīraṃ rāhoḥ śira ityapi kiṃ dṛṣṭam ? yathā ca tatraiva dvitīyātmābhāve'pi mamātmeti vyavahārastathā samānaṃ prathamātmābhāve'pi mama buddhidehāviti | yathā ca nāhamātmeti tathā nāhaṃ buddhiśarīre iti | ahamātmetyuktārthatvānna prayogārhamiti cet ? evamevāhaṃ buddhiśarīre ityuktārtham | na ceṣṭāmātraparādhīneṣu dhvaniṣu nirbandho budhānāmityāstāṃ tāvat |
[78,1]
tadayamasmacchabdo vaktuḥ paraniṣedhaparaḥ, natu mativigrahau vihāya vastvantaraparaḥ |
tayośca buddhivigrahayorbhūtabhaviṣyatorapi vartamānena ekādhyavasāyānmayaiva dṛṣṭaṃ mayaiva spṛṣṭaṃ smṛtaṃ ceti prayujyate | tasmāt so'yaṃ caitra itivadubhayapuñjasya pūrvāparakālayorekatāropamātrametat, nārthāntarollekhaḥ | caitrepyātmaiva pratyabhijñāyata iti cet — na, adṛṣṭe pratyabhijñānābhāvāt, buddhivigrahāveva hi dṛṣṭau | yadyapi ca parabuddhiranumeyā tathāpiatyantābhyāsādasyāmadhyakṣavad vyavahāradarśanānna doṣaḥ | mitrāmitrayordarśanamātrādeva hi tadanurūpānuṣṭhānamupalabdham | na ca tatra liṅgarūpānusaraṇādiparilambho'sti | nāpi kalevaramātrapratipattau tādṛganuṣṭhānam, mṛtamūrtāvapi prasaṅgāt | sarvaśarīravyāpāraprayojakatayā ca janmanaḥ prabhṛti buddherātmani darśanameva paratrāpi tatsahacarābhyāsabījaṃ satataṃ sannihitamasti | na caivamātmano darśanamabhyāsabījamasti, sarvavyāpārasya śarīracaitanyābhyāmeva paryavasānāt | tasmāccaitraśabdagocarau cittakāyāveva so'yamiti pratyabhijñāyete | tathāsmacchabdaviṣayayostayoreva pratyabhijñānamātrametanmayā dṛṣṭaṃ mayā smṛtamiti | mayā kṛtaṃ mayā mokṣyata ityapi ekatvādhyavasāyamātraṃ tayoreva |
tadatra pakṣe pratyakṣapṛṣṭhabhāvī vikalpo'yamāśvāsaviṣayaḥ, sattāmātre ekatve pūrvaparakṣaṇānāmavastukaḥ, atiriktaviṣayatve tu sphuratyapyarthe alīkānalīkaśaṅkāsaṃkarāt sandigdhavastukaḥ kathaṃ pratyakṣasiddhatāmātmanaḥ prayojayet ?
[78,2]
yaccānenāpyudghuṣyate, abhinnasaṃbandhina icchādibhedā mametyakapratisandhānaviṣayatvādekanartakīpratisandhānaviṣayā iva prekṣakā ityanumānam | tadapyatitaralahṛdayatāmeva dyotayati | nahi nartakī tattvata ekarūpā kācit, caitanyādhiṣṭhitaparamāṇusamūhamātratvāt | vyavahārasiddhamekatvamupādāya dṛṣṭāntasiddhau dārṣṭāntike'pi vyavahārasiddhamekatvaṃ kena bāryata iti | na ca sarvātmanā dṛṣṭānta iti cet ? satyametat |
tāttvikaṃ punarekatvaṃ kasya sāmarthyena samarthyatām, dṛṣṭānte tadanvayadarśanāttena vyāptyasiddheḥ | dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭenāpi hi pramāṇabalāvalambinī vyāptiḥ siddhyati | adṛṣṭena tu tatsiddhiśaṅkāpi nāsti | tasmānna sarvātmanā sādhāraṇo dṛṣṭānta iti vārtāyāmapi sādhyasādhanābhyāṃ sādhāraṇastāvadavaśyakartavyaḥ | na hi vyāptipradarśanādanyo dṛṣṭāntasya arthaḥ, na cānupadarśitena dṛṣṭānte sādhyena vyāptisādhanamādarśitaṃ bhavati | na caikāvayavisiddhyā sādhyaśūnyatāparihāro hārī | śarīrabuddhyādirāśitayā nartakyā'vayavitvābhāvāt | śarīrāpekṣayā tvavayavidūṣaṇameva jāgarti | ātmāpekṣāyāṃ tu so'dyāpi na sidhyati, viparyayabādhakābhāvācca nānekāntaśāntiḥ | mameti pratisandhānaṃ hi vikalpatayā anādyavidyāvaśādapi pratyabhijñānavat saṃbhavatkathamekasaṃbandhādhīnatāṃ svīkuryāditi ?
[79,1]
tadevaṃ yathāsmṛti karmaphalasaṃbandhādikamaśeṣamavasthātāramantareṇāpi na vipattimāsādayati kṣaṇikavādinaḥ, tathā kāryakāraṇabhāvabuddhirapīti na sādhāraṇānekāntaśaṅkākalaṅkaḥ |
[79,2]
śaṅkarastu vācāṭatayā kimapi nāṭayati | tathā hi, kadācidupalambhapūrvikā dhūmabuddhiḥ tejaḥkāryamidaṃ kapotakaṇṭhadhūsaraṃ vastviti niścayamutpādayati, kadācit tadubhayopalambhapūrvakastadanupalambhaḥ | anupalambho'pi pratiyogivastūpalambhasvabhāvatayā adhyakṣarūpa eva anvayaḥ punaranupalabdhiniṣṭhāyāṃ vihita iti tatraivāvadhāryaḥ | anvayavyatirekagrāhakapratyakṣānupalambhanītirapi trikapañcakacintāyāṃ darśitetyāstāṃ tāvat |
[79,3]
prakṛtaṃ tū brūmaḥ | ubhayathāpi kramabhāvinīṣu buddhiṣu pūrvapūrvayā saṃskāraviśeṣādhānādantimā buddhiretasyedaṃ kāryamiti matimutpādayituṃ pūrvavannirvahatīti nāvasthitasyānurodhaḥ pratisandhātuḥ |
[79,4]
yatpunaruktam, vyatireko manorathasyāpyaviṣaya iti, tadatisāhasam | nahi yadeva pratyakṣaṃ vastugrāhiṃ vastudvayanivṛttau tadeva tayorvyatirekamapi gṛhṇātītyucyate, kiṃ tu tadviviktapratiyogivastūpalambhasvabhāvaṃ pratyakṣāntarameva | tato yaduktaṃ tacca nāsti tena ca pratipattiriti na nyāyyamiti kvopayujyate ? na caivaṃ svasaṃvittivādopalambhasaṃgatiḥ |
yadapyuktaṃ pūrvottarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ saṃvittī, tābhyāṃ vāsanā, tayā hetuphalādhyavasāyī vikalpa iti cet ? tat kimidānīṃ yatkiñcidāśaṅkitena vaktavyamityevaṃ vidhiranuṣṭhīyate bhavatā ? vikalpo hi gṛhītānusandhānamatadrūpasamāropo vā syāt ? na tāvat pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, adṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasya puruṣasya hetuphalabhāvāgrahe'nusandhānapratyayahetorvāsanāviśeṣasyaivānupapatteḥ | agṛhītasya cānusandhāne'tiprasaṅgāditi |
[80,1]
tadetanna samīcīnamālocitam | yato hetuphalabhūtapūrvottarakṣaṇayoranubhavena kramiṇāpi svarūpasākṣātkaraṇāt hetuphalatve gṛhīte eva, kevalaṃ hetukāle phalābhāvāt tadviṣayasāmarthyagrahaṇe'pi phalādarśanāt tadavasāya evāpravṛttaḥ kāryadarśane pravartate |
tathā phalāvalokane'pi tatkāryatā gṛhītaiva vikalpenānusandhīyata iti gṛhītānusandhānarūpa evāyaṃ vikalpaḥ anvayavyatirekagrahaṇaṃ ca pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ pratipāditamiti yatkiñcidetat |
[80,2]
etena tadapi pratyuktam, yaduktaṃ na cādṛṣṭānvayavyatirekasya hetuphalabhāvo vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau ca sidhyati | tatrāpi paryanuyogasyāviśeṣādanavastheti |
[80,3]
anvayavyatirekadarśanaṃ hi prastutaviṣayaṃ tāvadupapāditameva | vāsanāvikalpayoranvayavyatirekasiddhiradhyakṣānupalambheṣvantimādevānusandhānavikalpapravṛtteḥ, ekākinaḥ pratyakṣādanupalambhād vā pravṛttyabhāvāt, śaktisvabhāvatvād vāsanāyāḥ kāryamantareṇa vyavasthānupapatteḥ | tathā vyavasthitāyāśca tasyāḥ svahetunānubhavenāpi sahānvayavyatirekasiddhiḥ kāryānvayavyatirekadvāreṇaiva | na cādyaṃ codyam — yāvannānusandhānavikalpaḥ tāvanna vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau vānvayavyatirekasiddhiḥ, yāvacca na vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau vānvayavyatirekasiddhistāvannānusandhānavikalpa iti | na hyanusandhānavikalpo vāsanāyāṃ vāsanāhetau vānvayavyatirekaniścayamapekṣate, api tvanubhayavāsanayoranvayavyatirekavatyoḥ svasantāne sattāmātram, tadanvayavyatirekaniścayastvanusandhānavikalpamapekṣata eva | tatra yathā dahanendhanavikārānvayavyatirekaniścayānapekṣastadapekṣaṇīyo dhūma iti netaretarāśrayastathā prastute'pītyalaṃ bahubhāṣitayā |
[80,4]
atadrūpasamāropapakṣe tu dūṣaṇaprasaṅgāgatamaprastutatayā tadanaṅgīkāreṇāvadhīritaṃ tāvat | tasmādavyākulā kāryakāraṇabhāvapratītirasthiratva iti sthitam ||
[81,1]
tatsthitau ca kramapratītiranivāritā, asmin satīdamasmādupajātamiti pratīteḥ kramāvasāyanāntarīyakatvāt | anyathā siddhasādhyavibhaktiprayogasya viṣayaniyamānupapatteḥ | yasmāddhetuphalayorvā kramapratītiḥ phalayorveti na kaścidviśeṣaḥ kramāpekṣayā | yaugapadye śaṅkāpi nāsti, aikakālikānekāvalokanānantarameva sakṛdimāni jātānīti vikalpasya baujādivāṅkurasyotpatteḥ | na hi tadanekakāryodayagrahaṇakṛtaḥ kaścidaparādho virodho kṣaṇikatāyāḥ | kramikadarśane hi sthirāpekṣā syādapyanusandhānāyāpātataḥ, sakṛddarśane tu kiṃ sthireṇa ? evaṃ tu syāt — sakṛddarśane'nantaramapi smartānyaḥ prāpnotīti, tacca parihṛtaṃ prāk | tadeva vā vācyamastu, kimavraṇakaṇḍūyāsthānīyena sākāravedanadūṣaṇodgīraṇena aprastutatvāt ? grahaṇaṃ cedasti sakṛdanekasya sākāreṇa nirākāreṇa vā jñānena bhaviṣyati, kimidānīmeva sakalatattvaniṣṭhāyā anuṣṭhānam ? yadi tu sakṛjjāyamānānekagrahaṇameva nāstītyabhimatam, tadā yathā sākāranirākaraṇaṃ tathā nirākārasyāpyastu |
anyathā tenaiva grahaṇamāśaṅkyeta |
[81,2]
kiṃ cānekagrahaṇābhāvo'pi sakṛt kathamabhimataḥ ? kiṃ sakṛdanekasaṃbhavābhāvāt ?
grahaṇaprakārāsaṃbhavād vā ?
[81,3]
prathamakalpe tāvat kathaṃ pradīpasya vartivikārāndhakārakṣayādayaḥ tadā kriyante svayamapi ? asmākaṃ punarevaṃ sati prayāsalāghavameva na kṣatiḥ, nitye kramadūṣaṇenaiva sādhyasiddheḥ |
[81,4]
dvitīye tu anekasaṃbhavavyavahāraḥ kiṃkṛto'stu ? anumānakṛto'stu | kiṃ tadanumānamiti pṛṣṭo yadi vyākaroṣi tadānumānasiddhameva yaugapadyaṃ kramasahāyamarthakriyāvyāpakamastu, kathaṃ prakṛtivirahadoṣaḥ ? atha na vyākaroṣi, tāvataiva hato'si | yugapadanekagrahanigrahe ca varamantaḥkaraṇasya manaso yugapadanekatra pravṛttyasaṃbhava eva pratipadyatām, kimanena ?
[81,5]
athānekākārānekasaṃvedanasaṃkalayitā eka eṣitavya iti matiḥ ? tataḥ kim ?
sthirasvīkāro hi kramavān naḥ saṃprati pīḍayati, anyathā tu vādāntarāvatāra eṣaḥ | tadvat krame'pi saṃkalayitā sidhyatīti cet ? tadapi yadi sākāranāntarīyakaṃ grahaṇamiti pramāṇasiddhaṃ syāt tadā sidhyet, anyathopagamamātrasya sukaratyāgatvādanākārasvīkāreṇa nirvahet paraḥ | na cākārasādhanayatno'sti, viṣayasyaiva tadākāratvaṃ samarthitaṃ syāditi tannirapekṣamakṣaraṃ vā kathamāvakṣīta ? na cātra pratisandhāturasthiratvāvirodhinaḥ svīkāre'pi krame'vaśyaṃ svīkāraḥ, yathā bhinnadeśamabhinnasvabhāvasya kāryakaraṇamicchannapi na bhinnakālamicchati | tasmāt krame pratisandhātṛsvīkārārthamanya eva prakāra āśrayaṇīyaḥ | tataḥ kimanena ? tasmāt kathañcit gaṇḍollāsaḥ kartavya ityevaṃvidhimanuṣṭhito'nena | na cedānīmākāradūṣaṇapratividheravasara iti nedaṃ pratiṣidhyata iti ||
[82,1]
nanu tathāpi,
[82,2]
matiḥ sākārā cenna ca bhidi mitho vedanamataḥ sphuratyekaivāsau tadiha na virodhaḥ prabhavati | ataḥ śaktāśakto'pyabhiditi nirastā kṣaṇikatā na vācyo doṣaścāvayavini na vā sākṛtinayaḥ ||
[82,3]
nanvata evoktaṃ nāyaṃ tatpratividheravasara iti | na hi tadasiddhiravayavisiddhirvā bādhikāsmākam |
[82,4]
nityatrayānugamanādiguṇena kāntaḥ sautrāntikasya samayo'pi na bādhitoṃ'śe | nocenna pudgalanirākaraṇena bauddha siddhāntabādhakṛta eva kṛtāparādhaḥ ||
[82,5]
tasmāt,
[82,6]
dhiyaḥ sākāratvaṃ yadi mama ya evaiṣa samayo bhaved duṣṭo mānābhyupanatahatiḥ syātkathamiva | pramāsiddhaṃ tacced bhavatu dhiya evaiṣa samayo bahiścitre'pyekasthitiriti viluptaṃ khalu bahiḥ ||
[83,1]
arthakriyābhedanāntarīyako hyākārabhedaḥ padārtheṣu | tatra yadyākārabhede'pi nārthakriyābhedaḥ, hanta pratibhāsamātrabhedānnātiriktaṃ kiñciditi bāhyapadārthāpalāpa eva prasaktaḥ | tadavaśyamanena bāhyavastuna ākārabhedādbheda eva svīkartavyo, buddhirbhidyatāṃ mā vā | nahi samakakṣatāpi dhiyo'dhigantumalam | anyathā svasaṃvedanamanyaprakāśanaṃ ca bāhyasyāpi prasajyamānaṃ grāhyagrāhakabhāvameva viplāvayet | tad yadi pramāṇasiddhaṃ buddherekatvaṃ citrākārāyāstasyā evāstu, bāhyaṃ tu bhinnākāraṃ bhinnameva | bāhyamapi bhinnākāraṃ kathaṃ bhinnamiti cet ? bhavatu tribhuvanamekameva vastu kimasmākaṃ kṣīṇam ?
pṛthagarthakarmaniyogādyabhāve tu na gandharvanagarādivat pratibhāsamātratāmatiśayītetyuktam |
kvacidekatā kvacid bheda iti vibhāgasyāpi naiṣa prastāvaḥ |
[83,2]
atha buddherapyekatvaṃ samayamātraṃ na pramāṇasiddham | tadānīṃ bādhavirodhī samaya iti sa eva duṣyatu, pramāṇopanītastu prastuto vastubhedaḥ parasparavirodhāt kathaṃ tyājyaḥ ?
[83,3]
kiṃ ca,
[83,4]
hato heturvakturyadi samayamāśritya samaye tavāstveṣa śreyānatha samayacintā pravadituḥ | na vai śāstre sthitvā vacanamiti vaktuśca samayaḥ pramāsiddhai rūpairanumitividhau nāgamaguṇaḥ ||
[83,5]
api ca na virodhamātraṃ bhedamasmākaṃ, kiṃ tu śaktāśaktatvena | taccāvaśyaṃ svīkāryam, anyathā sādhanadūṣaṇasamarthānusaraṇavisaraṇāt paryavasito vāda iti kimapareṇa ? tasmācchaktyaśaktidvāreṇa bhedo duṣpariharaḥ | tato virodhamātrasya bhedavyabhicāre'pi prakṛtaviśeṣasya na vyabhicāraḥ, vastumātrasya vahnivyabhicāre'pi dhūmalakṣaṇavastvavyabhicāravat |
[83,6]
nanu śaktāśaktatvenāpi bhedo virodhādeva, sa ca vyabhicārīti cet ? dhūmo'pi vastutvādeva heturgamako, vastutvaṃ ca vyabhicārīti samānam | tasmād vastutvādeva dahanasya gamako dhūma iti na vastutvaṃ parihṛtyetyarthaḥ | na tu yāvad vastu tāvad gamakam | evaṃ śaktāśaktatvaṃ virodhādeva bhedasādhanamiti na virodhaṃ vidhūyetyarthaḥ | na tu yāvad virodhastāvad bhedasādhakaḥ |
[84,1]
āha ca,
[84,2]
virodhaśced bhedaṃ vyabhicarati bhedapratipade viśiṣṭo'sāviṣṭaḥ prabhavati ca śaktetaratayā | aśakte sāmānye yadi ca viśeṣo'pi balavān na dhūmādagnyāśā vyabhicarati yadvastu śikhinam ||
[84,3]
virodhādevālaṃ balavadabalatvaṃ yadi bhide na vastutvaṃ hitvā hutabhuji sa dhūmo'pi balavān | atho vahniṃ vastu vyabhicaratu bhedo'sya tu balī pramāsiddhāpattiḥ prakṛtaviṣaye'pyeṣa samayaḥ ||
[84,4]
abhede hi śaktāśaktayoḥ sakalamākulam trailokyamapravṛttinivṛttikamāsaktamiti śaktetarayorvirodho'vaśyaṃ bhedasādhaka eṣitavyaḥ, ākāradvāreṇa bhavatu mā vā |
[84,5]
