nanvākārabhedo'pi śaktibhedanāntarīka eveti kiṃkṛto vibhāgaḥ ? satyam, bāhyeṣu tāvadevameva, jalānalādiṣu tathaivopalabdheḥ | anyathā ca na bāhyaṃ nāma kiñcit pratibhāsamātrāvaśeṣāt | buddhestvākārā na tāvad dāhagāhanādiṣvevopayogino, bāhyakāryatvātteṣām | yatpunaravasāyādikāryaṃ tadapyākārāntareṇa saha bhedābhedavivādārūḍhameveti kathamekatraikavyāpāro darśitaḥ ? bhavatu vā kiñcidekamapi kāryam, tatrāpi kimapoddhāradvāreṇa ekākāravyāpārakalpanamatha bhedādeveti cintyam | na cāsmākaṃ citrabuddherekānekatvasādhane nirbandhaḥ, icchāpi sākāratāmātre, kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhane tu tasyāpi na kaścidanurodhaḥ | anāntarīyake cārthe badhite'nyasya kā kṣatiḥ | (pra. vā. 4. 47)
iti nyāyāt | tasmānnāpratītikṛto'rthasāmarthyasya kramākramasya ca vyāpyavyāpakabhāvaniścayaḥ |
[85,1]
yatpunarucyate, yadi krameṇa vyāptam, tadā kathamakrameṇa ? athākrameṇa, na tarhi krameṇa | kramākramābhyāṃ vyāptamiti bruvatā vyāpterevābhāvaḥ pradarśito bhavati | sā hi vyāpyasya tatraiva bhāvo vyāpakasya tatra bhāva evetyevaṃrūpā, ubhayorvyāpakatvena svarūpaṃ jahāti | na hi bhavatyagnirdhūmadhūmābhāvābhyāṃ vyāpta iti | kimevaṃ vaktari vaktavyam ?
datto hi jalāñjaliramunā krameṇa sakalatārkikavartmani vartamānairātmanā ca anena bahudhā dattasya vikalpya dūṣaṇarāśeḥ | api nāmaitatprakārāṇāṃ dūṣaṇenāsattāpratipādanāt tatprameyamasatsyāditi vikalpya dūṣaṇāni pratīyante, tatprakārairavyāptau ca dūṣyaprameyasya teṣāmabhāve'pināsyābhāvaniyama iti dūṣaṇābhidhāne'pi prāgiva saṃśayaḥ, tadalamupanyāsena | tatprakārāṇāmabhāve'bhāvaniyame vā sa eva vyāptyartha iti kasya niṣedhaḥ ? tathā ca santānasya vastutvamanicchan bhinno'bhinno veti vikalpya dūṣaṇamārabhate, tadubhayābhāvavibhāvane ca nirvṛṇvīteti na bhedābhedābhyāṃ vastuvyāptimanaṅgīkurvannirvahati | evaṃ trayādivikalpeṣvapīti sthitam | tasmādekaikenāvyāptiḥ, samudāyena tu vyāptireveti nyāyaḥ | yathā yudhiṣṭhirādiṣvanyatamo'bhavan pāṇḍava eva na bhavati | ekanivṛttau hi tadanyaprakāramāśrityāsīt tattvam | sarvaprakārābhāve tu kvāstām ? ato niyamavatī nivṛttirvyāptireva |
[85,2]
yadapyuktam, na hi bhavatyagnirdhūmadhūmābhāvābhyāṃ vyāpta iti, tadapi pāpīyaḥ |
kramākramābhyāṃ hi kāryodayavyāptivādino rāśyantaravirahavatā taddharmadvayena vyāptiḥ prastutā, tat kvedamupayujyate ? na hi kramākramāviva kāryāṇāṃ vahnerapi dhūmadhūmābhāvo dharmaḥ | svabhāva eva hi dharmiṇo dharmaśabdavācyaḥ prakṛtaḥ | tad yadi dhūmadhūmābhāvābhyāmiti dhūmavattvādhūmavattvābhyāmiti vivakṣitam, tadā kaḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibandhabodhasya ? na hi dahanastadavasthādvayavirahitaḥ kvacidupapannaḥ |
[85,3]
atha yathā yathoktadharmo nāntarīyakatvamagnestathāparabhūte dhūme dhūmābhāvaśabdavācye ca niścitamiti tābhyāmapi kathaṃ na vyāptirasya, sāmānyalakṣaṇasyākṣīṇatvāt ? asti hi dhūmadhūmābhāvayoryatrābhāvastatra vahnerapi, yatra ca vahnistatra tayoranyatarasya saṃbhavaḥ dhūme sati hutāśanaprakārāṇāmivānyatamasyeti cet ? yadyeṣa nirbandhaḥ kastāvadevaṃ doṣaḥ, aniṣṭimātrasyānaṅgatvāt ? vyāptirhi vyāpyasaṃbhave vyāpakaprabhedānyatamasaṃbhavāya vyāpakābhāvena niyamena vyāpyanivṛttyarthamarthyamānā tadubhayavyāpāravyabhicāraśaṅkāyāmeva duṣyati | tacca nāstīti kimaniṣṭimātreṇa bhavataḥ ? kevalaṃ viśeṣalakṣaṇāyogānna sākṣād dhūmatadabhāvābhyāmanalasya vyāptirabhidhīyate | tathā hi dahanadhūmaryorbhedānna tādātmyam, dhūmādibhāvābhāvābhyāmasyānutpattiśca na kāryakāraṇabhāva iti dhūmavattvetarābhyāmeva svagatadharmābhyāmāśrayabhujo'ñjasā vyāptiḥ |
tadarthasvīkāradvārā tu dhūmatadabhāvābhyāmapyabhidhīyamānā na doṣamāvahati | tad yadi bhavata īdṛśī vyāptiranabhimatā viparyayo vā'bhimataḥ, astu | asmākaṃ tāvadayameva vyāptikramo vivakṣitaḥ, sa eva ca prakṛtopayogī, vipakṣādatyantaṃ hetorvyāvartanasamīhayā kramākramābhyāmarthaśakteḥ vyāptivādaprakramāt, taccaivameva siddhamityalametāvati skhalite nirbandhena | tadevaṃ kramākramābhyāmarthakriyāvyāptisiddhāvevārthakriyābhāvena kramākramābhāvasyāpi vyāptisiddhiḥ, na hi vyāpyavyāpakayāstadbhāvasiddhimuddhūya vyāpyābhāvena vyāpakābhāvasya vyāptāvupāyāntaramastīti nānekāntaḥ | prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhasya vyāptisiddhau ca na virodhagandhaḥ, sapakṣe bhāvācca ||
[86,1]
nāpyasiddhiḥ, nityasya sādhyadharmiṇaḥ kramayaugapadyābhyāṃ virodhasiddheḥ | atra nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ, yadi tāvadakṣaṇikānāmasattvaṃ prasādhayitumabhipretaṃ, tadā kasyātra dharmitvam ?
tasyaiva dharmitve tasyaivābhāvasādhanamayuktam | na hyasati dharmiṇi hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvam |
na cāsati pakṣadharmatve gamakatvam | tasmādasanto'kṣaṇikā ityayuktā pratijñā | atha santo'kṣaṇikā na bhavantīti pratijñārthaḥ, tathāpi tasyāṃ kramākramavirodhādityasya kathaṃ pakṣadharmatvamiti ? kiṃ cārthakriyāśakternityena saha virodho vyāpakānupalambhādeva mataḥ, vyāpakasya tu kramākramasya katham ? api caivaṃ sattvameva nityasya prasajyate |
tathā ca sarvaḥ prayāso viphalaḥ |
[87,1]
yadāha śaṅkaraḥ, virodhasiddhimanusaratā virodhyapi pratipattavyaḥ, tatpratipattināntarīyakatvādvirodhasiddheḥ | yathā dahanatuhinayoḥ, sāpekṣadhruvabhāvayośca | pratiyogī cākṣaṇikaḥ pratīyamānaḥ kathaṃ bādhakoparodhenārthakriyākāritvaṃ jahāti, pratipattirūpārthakriyākāritvāt ? atatkāritve kathaṃ pratīyeta, ajanakasyāprameyatvāditi bāhyeṣu yathāsārametallikhitam |
[87,2]
tathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ, virodhyapratītau virodhasya pratyetumaśakyatvāt, na hi dahanatuhinayoranyatarāpratītau virodhapratītirasti | kramākramavirodhādakṣaṇikaṃ yadi pratīyate tataḥ kathamasat, pratītirūpārthakriyākāritvāt ? atatkāritve kathaṃ pratīyate ? na hi tvayārthāntaramajanakaṃ pratītiviṣayatveneṣṭam | athākṣaṇikaṃ naiva pratīyate, kathaṃ tasya kramākramābhyāṃ virodho'vagamyata iti ? tadevaṃ nityasya sarvathā'bhāvāt pratītyaviṣayatvāt āśrayāsiddhirvyāpakānupalambhasya | tathā svarūpāsiddhiśca ||
[87,3]
yadāha śaṅkaraḥ, atha kramayaugapadyāyogādakṣaṇikābhāvaḥ sidhyati, sattātaḥ kṣaṇikatvam, evaṃ tarhi tasya pratipattijanakatvāt tadavasthamanaikāntikatvamarthakriyākāritvasya, tasyābhāve'pi bhāvāt | vyāpakābhāvasiddhau hi vyāpyābhāvo'nyaḥ pratipattavyo yathā agnyabhāve dhūmābhāvastoyādiḥ, vṛkṣābhāve śiṃśapābhāvastadrahito deśādiḥ | evaṃ kramayaugapadyābhāve sāmarthyābhāvaścānyaḥ pratipattavyaḥ, tadasiddhāvaniścitavyatirekeṇa hetunā sādhyasiddherayogāt | pratipattau tu vyāpyavyāpakabhāvasya pratītirūpārthakriyākāritvamiti durnivāraḥ prasaṅga iti |
[87,4]
ataeva sapakṣe sattvamapyasya vaktumaśakyam | ākāśakuśeśayasya kramākramābhāvasyārthakriyāśaktyabhāvasya ca pratītyabhāvāt | pratītau sarveṣāṃ vastutvena mūlahetoḥ pakṣasapakṣayorantarbhāvaprasaṅgāt |
[87,5]
yannyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ, vyatirekabalenaivāsya gamakatvamiti cet — na, vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntasyāpyabhāvāt | śaśaviṣāṇādirdṛṣṭānta iti cet — na, tasya pratipattyaviṣayatvāt | na hi svarūpeṇāpi yanna pratīyate tat sādhyasādhanadharmarahitaṃ pratipattuṃ śakyate, na cāpratipannasya dṛṣṭāntatvaṃ yuktamiti | kiṃ ca nityasyārthasāmarthyābhāvasādhanamasattāsādhanametat, tacca sattāsādhanavanna trayīṃ doṣajātimatipatati |
[88,1]
tathā hyaktena krameṇa
[88,2]
nāsiddhe bhāvadharmo'sti vyabhicāryubhayāśrayaḥ | dharmo viruddho'bhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham || (pra0 vā0 3. 190)
[88,3]
iti śaṅkaranyāyabhūṣaṇau darśayataḥ | trilocano'pi tadeva prameyajātamupaskurvannāha, kramayaugapadyarahitatvaṃ bādhakaṃ kimakṣaṇikānāmasattāṃ sādhayati, āhosvid vyatirekam arthapratibandham ? na tāvat pūrvo vikalpaḥ, ākāśakāladigātmamanasāṃ paramāṇūnāṃ ca rūpāsiddhau hetorāśrayāsiddherasiddhatvāt | so'pi vyāpakānupalambho na trayīṃ doṣajātimatipatati | tatra kramayaugapadyarahitatvamabhāvadharmo na sidhyatyāśrayāsiddherityuktam | na hi kramayaugapadyarahitatvasya śaśaviṣāṇadharmatvaṃ prekṣāvantaḥ pratipadyante |
kiṃ ca yāvatteṣāmasattvaṃ pramāṇāntarānnāvagamyate tāvadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na sidhyati, anyathā pakṣadharmatvasiddhau teṣāmasattvasiddhiḥ, asatvasiddhau ca satyāmabhāvadharmatvasiddhiriti itaretarāśrayatvaṃ durnivāram | bhāvadharmatve cāsya viruddhatvaṃ syāt, ubhayadharmatve cānaikāntikatvam, sattāyāmiva so'yamasattāyāmapi tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ |
[88,4]
nāpi dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ tatrāpi hi vyāpakanivṛttisahitā vyāpyanivṛttiḥ vyatirekaśabdasyārthaḥ | sā ca nivṛttirgamakāṅgatvādavaśyaṃ pratipattavyā bhavatīti yadyanubhavād gamyate tasya hetuḥ syādahetoragrāhyatvāditi heturanaikāntikaḥ syāt, vyatirekasyānubhavakāritayā bhāvarūpatve sādhyakoṭinikṣiptatvāt | anvayavyatirekayorabhāvādasādhāraṇo heturagamakaḥ | tasmād vyatireko'vaśyāṅgīkartavyo'vaśyajñātavyaśca jñātavyatve tajjñānaprasaṅgo darśitaḥ |
[88,5]
syādetat | vyatireko na sākṣātkārivijñānagrāhya iṣṭo yataḥ sākṣātkāriṇo vijñānasya janakaḥ syādapi tu vikalpayitavyaḥ, na ca vikalpyamāno'rthaḥ svakīyasamanantarapratyayādhīnotpādasya vikalpasya heturupapadyate, tat kimucyate heturanaikāntika iti ?
[89,1]
tadapyasaṅgatam, yataḥ sarva eva vikalpo na catuṣṭayīṃ gatimatikrāmati | tathā hi kaścidanubhavapṛṣṭhabhāvī nīlādivikalpaḥ, aparaḥ sandigdhaviṣayaḥ piśācādivikalpaḥ, anyaḥ punarasadarthaḥ śaśaviṣāṇādivikalpaḥ, vikalpaḥ punariha kaścilliṅgajaḥ | tatra liṅgajādārabhya sarvo vikalpaḥ avastunirbhāsād iti bruvatā pratyakṣābha uktaḥ, yato vastupratibhāsaṃ pratyakṣaṃ, svalakṣaṇābhāve tatpratibhāsapracyuteḥ | na caivaṃ vikalpaḥ, tatpratibhāsasya vastunyananurodhāt | tasmāt pratyakṣābho vikalpaḥ | liṅgajastu yathādhyavaseyamarthaṃ prāpayatīti pramāṇam | na ca vyatireko vikalpyamāno liṅgābhāvālliṅgajena vikalpena vikalpyate anubhavapūrvakasya ca vikalpasya pāramparyeṇa vastujanmano'pi na vastuni prāmāṇyam, anubhavasyaiva pramāṇatvāt | anubhavaśca vyatirekāśrayaḥ saṃpratyeva nirasta iti pāriśeṣyādasadarthaḥ sandigdhavastuko vā vikalpo niścāyayatīti sattvamavidyamānavyatirekaṃ sandigdhavyatirekaṃ vā na kṣaṇikatvasādhanāya paryāptam |
[89,2]
nāpi tṛtīyo vikalpaḥ | yataḥ kramayaugapadyamakṣaṇikāt sattvamupādāya vyāvartamānaṃ svena vyāpyena saha kṣaṇikatve vyavatiṣṭhata iti pratibandhasiddhirvyatirekasiddhipūrvikā gamyate, vyatirekaśca pūrvoktena krameṇa nirākṛta iti |
[89,3]
tadevam,
[89,4]
nityaṃ nāsti na vā pratītiviṣayaṃ tenāśrayāsiddhatā hetoḥ svānubhavasya cākṣatirataḥ kṣiptaḥ svapakṣo'pi ca | śūnyaṃ ca dvitayena sidhyati na vā sattāpi sattā yathā no nityena virodhasiddhirasatā śakyā kramāderapi ||
[89,5]
iti dūṣaṇasaṃgrahaḥ |
[89,6]
tatrāmī evaṃ paryanuyujyante,
[89,7]
dharmasya kasyacidavastuni mānasiddhā bādhāvidhivyavahṛtiḥ kimihāsti no vā | kvāpyasti cet kathamiyanti na dūṣaṇāni nāstyeva cet svavacanapratirodhasiddhiḥ ||
[90,1]
na hi kasyacid dharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahāro nāma saṃvādavān vastvekaniyataḥ, kiṃ tvavastunyapi | athāvastuni nāstyeveti bhaktiḥ, tatra kathametaditi paryanuyukto na rājaśāsanamāśrityaiva stheyamiti yadi kiñciddhetumupādadīta kathamāśrayāsiddhiparihāraḥ ? mūkībhūyāvasthānaṃ sati vacanasāmarthye nocita iti yat kiñcillapato na pratimallaḥ |
nāpi pararatena pratipādito bhavati |
[90,2]
kiṃ cāvastuni nāstyeva vidhipratiṣedhavyavahāra ityevaṃ vadataiva avastuni niṣedhavyavahāraḥ svīkṛtaḥ, hetau paraṃ paro vañcitaḥ, na hi niṣedhamavadhūya naño'nyadarthasaṃbhāvanā, sa ca niṣedho yadi na pramāṇasiddhaḥ, kathamādriyate ? kiṃ vāsya vacanena ? pramāṇasiddhisvīkāre ca na tāvadadhyakṣamevāvastuniṣedhayoḥ sādhanam, adhyakṣasya tadviṣayavirodhādarthasāmarthyāpekṣaṇāt | anumānāśraye tu āśrayāsiddhiraśakyaparihāreti |
ato'vastuprastāve mūkataiva prāptā | na ca pratijñāmātrasyāpyavakāśaḥ | na caivaṃ śakyaṃ yāvanna rājadaṇḍenāvastuprastāvavāraṇam | prastāve tvavaśyaṃ satā saṃbhavino vacanamanuṣaṅgi paryanuyogasaṃbhavāt | vacanasya ca vidhiniṣedhābhyāṃ nāparo vyāpāraḥ | tato na vacanaṃ nāvacanamiti mahati kaṣṭasaṅkaṭe praveśaḥ |
[90,3]
tathā ca saṃpratyeva nitye'ntarālakamalavat kramākramābhāvāt nārthasāmarthyamiti prastāvenāvastuni kasyaciddharmasya vidhiniṣedhāviti viduṣāpi bhavatā na mūkībhūya sthātuṃ śakyam, kiṃ tu kṛta eva niṣedho bauddhābhimatāyā asati kramākramābhāvena sāmarthyanivṛtteḥ || nivṛttyabhāvastu vidhirvastubhāvo'sato'pi san | tadabhāvastu nāstīti paśya dhārṣṭyavijṛmbhitam || (pra. vā. 4. 553)
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[90,4]
atha nityasya koṣṭhaśuddhyā vastutvānna pramāṇānniṣedhavirodhaḥ kasyaciddharmasya, tat kimidānīṃ gagananalinasyāpi koṣṭhaśuddhyā vastutvameva ? vastutve vā nāvastuko vikalpaḥ saṅkalpayituṃ śakyaḥ | tadavastuni nabhastāmarase kramādivirahādarthakriyāsāmarthyaviraho'stu na vā ? ubhayathāpi nāvastuni vidhiḥ pratiṣedho vetyasyāḥ pratijñāyā nirvāhaḥ | kathametaditi pramāṇagaveṣaṇe ca pratyakṣābhāve'numānamāśrīyamāṇamāśrayāsiddhigrastaṃ samastam, apramāṇavacanamātrasya cānapekṣitatvāt praśnakṛtā prekṣeṇa | na cobhayābhāvo'bhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ, vidhiniṣedhayorbhāvābhāvasvabhāvādekaniṣedhenāparavidhānāt |
vidhiniṣedho hi niṣedhaḥ pratiṣedhaśca vidhistat kīdṛśo'paraḥ ? astu cobhayaniṣedhapratijñāhetorupādīyamānasya nāśrayāsiddhiparihāraḥ |
[91,1]
yaccedamuktam, koṣṭhaśuddhyā vastveva nityamiti, tataḥ kim ? na hi tadvastutvenaiva dharmi, āśrayāsiddhidūṣaṇasyānavakāśaprasaṅgāt | paropagamāpekṣayedamucyata iti cet ? prasaṅgahetustarhi avastutvānnityāśrayāsiddhaḥ kramādiviraho na heturityarthaḥ |
evaṃ ca satyavastuni heturāśrayāsiddhatvena vyāpto vaktavyaḥ, na hi pratibandhamantareṇa kaściddhetuḥ | pakṣadharmatāmātre paropagamāpekṣayā tu prasaṅga ucyate, na tu vyāptāvapi tadupagama eva | kadācidevamapi syāditi cet ? tathāpi na pareṇāvastuni heturāśrayāsiddhatvena vyāpto'bhyupagataḥ, nitya evāvastuni hetupraṇayanāt | tataśca yatravāvastuni vastutvāt hetorāśrayāsiddhirupanīyate, tatreva pratijñāyāḥ paribhavo nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhāvityasyāḥ |
yadi ca paropagamādeva vyāptirapi vivakṣitā, avastunyavastutvānnapakṣadharmatāprayukto heturiti, tarhi tava nedamanumatamiti, tathāpi nāvastuni vidhipratiṣedhāviti vyāhatam, pratiṣedhasya svayaṃ svīkriyamāṇatvāt, naño'nyārthābhāvāt |
[91,2]
kiṃ ca sarvaḥ prasaṅgo viparyayaparyavasitavyāpāra iti nyāyāt yadyavastu nityaṃ tadāśrayāsiddhiḥ | na cāśrayāsiddhiḥ, tannāvastu nityamiti kiṃ vivakṣitam ? tadāpi yathāśrayāsiddhirdoṣaḥ prastuto nāsti siddhamavastutvaṃ nityasya dharmiṇa iti nāvastu nityamiti kathaṃ na viplavate ? tasmāt svatantra evāyamavastutvādāśrayāsiddhiravastuni hetoriti hetudūṣaṇapravṛttasya prakṛtaḥ | tathā ca nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhāviti dūrīkṛtametat |
vyāpakānupalambhaścāyaṃ svabhāṣayā prayujyate, āśrayatvasya vastutvena vyāptyabhimānāt |
sa cābhimānaḥ svavacanavirodhānavabodhāt | na hi nāvastuni vidhiniṣedhādhāratvamiti svavacanavirodhaṃ manyamānasya vastutvena dharmitvasya vyāptyabhimāno mānasaṃ spṛśati, kiṃ svaparibhāvakatayeti sāmānyanyāyaḥ | kiṃ cāmī svayamavastuni vidhiniṣedhavyavahāramātanvanto vyāpakānupalambhaṃ cāpramāṇayantaḥ paraṃ pratikṣipantīti ka eṣa kramaḥ ?
[92,1]
nyāyabhūṣaṇakāro hi na hyasati dharmiṇi hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvamiti bruvāṇo'vastuni hetoḥ pakṣadharmatāniṣedhaṃ vyaktamāha | kathametaditi yuktigaveṣaṇe ca dharmiṇo'sattvāditi hetumabhipraiti | anyathā ca vacanamātre ka ādaraḥ ? athākṣaṇikaṃ naiva pratīyate kathaṃ tasya kramākramābhyāṃ virodho'vagamyata iti bruvāṇaśca vyaktaṃ pratītyaviṣayatvena virodhāvagamābhāvamāha | sa cāvastvantarasādhāraṇo dharmo nitye'pyavastusaṃmate āsajyate, anyathā anyatrāvastuni yadyayaṃ na nyāyo nitye'pi kathamabhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ ?
[92,2]
śaṅkaropyetadeva sphuṭayati, avastuni pratītyaviṣayatvena na virodhāsiddhiriti |
anyathā prabandhavaiyarthyāt |
[92,3]
nanvasya ṣaṣṭhīsaptamīnirdeśābhāvādasatā saha sato na virodha ityabhiprāyāt na doṣa iti cet ? adyāpyasato'pratīyamānatvāditi svayamabhivyakto heturapekṣaṇīya eveti kathamasato dharmibhāvavyāpakānupalambhayoḥ paribhavaḥ ? tena saha virodhāsiddhau hi tasya pratītiviṣayatvābhāvo hetuḥ | yadi ca tṛtīyānirdeśenāśrayāsiddhiparihāramanumanyate bhavān, kramākramayorapi nityena saha yogābhāvādarthakriyāśakterapi nityena saha yogābhāva iti na kṣatiḥ | evaṃ pakṣeṇa yoga eva sapakṣeṇaiva yogo vipakṣeṇāyoga eveti hetostrairūpyaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | śāntirastvāśrayāsiddhiprahārasya | tasmāt vivakṣāmātrabheda eva na vastubheda iti kimanena kāyavratena ?
[92,4]
kiṃ ca asatā saha tāvad virodhabādhanamevamastu, yadā punaḥ sata eva satā saha virodhaḥ kimastu na veti praśne'stvitisvīkāraḥ, sthitaṃ bauddhasiddhānteneti viphala upanyāsaḥ | atha neti svīkāraḥ, tadā sa evāpratīyamānatvāditi heturapekṣitavya ityavastuni niṣedhanaṃ virodhasya vyāpakānupalambheneti punarbauddhasiddhāntasiddhiḥ | tathā, nāsiddhe bhāvadharmo'sti (pra. vā 4. 190)
ityatrāpi eṣa eva nyāyaḥ śaraṇam |
[93,1]
tathā ca trilocanaḥ svākṣareṇa sphuṭayati, kramayaugapadyarahitatvamabhāvadharmo na sidhyati, āśrayānupalabdheriti | atra hi vyaktamabhāvo dharmī, kramādirahitatvamasya dharmo niṣidhyate, āśrayānupalabdheriti hetoriti | evamasato dharmitvaṃ pratijānāna evānantaraṃ na hi kramayaugapadyarahitaśaśaviṣāṇadharmatvaṃ prekṣāvantaḥ pratipadyanta iti evaṃ bruvan mahān sāhasiko yadayamātmānamātmanaiva nopahasati | abhāvādeva hi śaśaviṣāṇasya dharmitvaṃ niṣeddhavyam, svīkṛtaṃ cābhāvasyāpi dharmitvamiti kaḥ pratirodhasturaṅgaśṛṅgādeḥ ?
athābhāvasya dharmitā kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena svīkṛtā, kathaṃ kramādirahitatvenaivāstu ?
aho buddhivaibhavam ! abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇasya kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena dharmitvaṃ manyate, na kramādirahitatvena | ubhayathāpyavastuni vidhiniṣedhavyavahārasvīkārād durnivāraḥ saugatakṛtānta iti varaṃ kramādirahitvenaiva dharmitvamubhayatrāstu, kimuttarāpathaṃ praviśya tāvataiva mūlyena turagatyāgino gardabhakrayaṇavṛttānta āśriyate ?
[93,2]
athavātisūkṣmā buddhiḥ sthavīyāṃsamasamañjasaviśeṣamiyantaṃ na paśyatīti kimatra kriyatām ? tathāpyakṣiṇo nimīlya cintaya tāvat kiṃ śaśaviṣāṇaṃ kramādiyogi bhavati na vā ? yadi bhavatīti bhaṇasi, kimatra vaktavyamasmābhiḥ ? sabhyādayaḥ pramāṇam |
atha neti pakṣaḥ, tadā kramādirahitaṃ tattatkathaṃ kramādirahitatvaniṣedhena dharmīkaroṣi ?
ubhayathā ca hetuṃ paryanuyujyāvaśyamavastutvāditi vakṣyāmītyalaṃ vistareṇa |
[93,3]
evaṃ bandhyāsuto vaktā na vetyevaṃvidhe'pi prastāve niṣedhamapratijñāya na sthātuṃ śakyamacetanatvādavastutvādityādisādhanamanupanyasya vā na kaścidevamāśaṅkate | yadīdṛśamuttarayitavyamiti cet ? kutaḥ ? tadavastu tāyāḥ prasiddhatvāditi cet ? punastadevāyātam bandhāsutasya dharmiṇo vaktṛtvenāśaṅkanoyatāniṣedhaḥ, suprasiddhāvastutvāditi heturiti | na ca suprasiddhatve'pi sarvathā śaṅkāvirahaḥ | niḥsīmo hi mohamahimā | dṛṣṭo hi śāstrakārāṇāmapi kramādirahitatvaniṣedhaḥ śaśaviṣāṇe ityevaṃprakāro bhramaḥ | tato yathā śabde cākṣuṣatvādanityatvaṃ saṃbhāvayannasiddhatvena niṣidhyate tathehāpi syātāṃ śaṅkāniṣedhau, na virodhaḥ | tasmād vastunīvāvastunyapi kasyaciddharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahāro durvāraḥ, āhatya vipratipannānāmapi śāstrakārāṇāṃ niṣedhavākyenaiva svīkārāt |
tatredānīmavastuṣu bandhyāsutaparyanteṣu kathaṃ dharmitvam ? pratītyabhāve kathaṃ vyavahāraḥ ? pratītijanakatve kathaṃ na vastutvam ? na ca vacanamātrapramāṇamupādeyamiti yaḥ kaściddheturupādīyate, sa sarvaḥ kathaṃ nāśrayāsiddhaḥ ? tadetadāyātam, yaścobhayoḥ samo doṣa ityādi |
yadi ca niścitāvastubhāveṣvapi naite doṣāḥ, tat kiṃ sādhanātprāgasandigdhasattāke nitye bhaviṣyati ? kaḥ punaratra paramārthaḥ ? na hyavastuni kasyaciddharmasya vidhiniṣedhavyavahāraḥ śakyaparihāraḥ prāmāṇikasya | na caite doṣāḥ sānuṣaṅgiṇa iti ceducyate, na tāvadavastuno dharmitvābhāvaḥ | yatraiva hi idamevamiti parāmarśaḥ tadevedamityanenākāreṇa dharmi | evamiti dharmaviśeṣayāgaḥ | yathā ghaṭo nīla evaṃ bandhyāsuto na vakteti ghaṭasya nīlatvamiva bandhyāsutasya vaktṛtvaṃ dharmaḥ pratoyata iti na dharmitvābhāvo'bhāve |
kevalaṃ kaściddharmo vastuniyatā nīlatvādiḥ, kaścidavastuniyataḥ sarvopākhyāvirahādiḥ, kaścidubhayasādhāraṇo'nupalambhamātram | tatra vastudharmiṇāvastudharmitvaniṣedha iti yuktam | na tu dharmamātrāṇām, svavacanavirodhasya bādhakatvāt | pratītyabhāvena vyavahāra ityapyayuktam | na punarubhayārekaprakāraiva pratītiraṅgaṃ vyavahārasya | vastuno hi svasāmarthyabhāvinī pratītiḥ | vikalpaścādhyakṣaliṅgābhyāṃ pāramparyakāryaḥ | avastunastu sandigdhavastubhāvasya vā vikalpamātram | sāmarthyābhāve hi tayorabhāve vikalpamātramapi yadi na tatpratītiravasthāpyate sarvathāvyavahārya eva syāt | iṣṭaśca vyavahāraḥ, ato vikalpanamātraṃ tatra pratātiḥ, tadupasthāpitameva ca tayoḥ svarūpaṃ nānyat | yathā vastunaḥ pratyakṣānumānopanītameva svarūpam, evamavastunaḥ sandigdhavastubhāvasya vā vikalpāpasthāpita evātmā nānya iti | nātaḥ samayādaṅgamākaṣantaḥ santā bhavitumarhanti |
[94,1]
yattu, grāhyatāṃ viduḥhetutvameva yuktijñāḥ (pra. vā. 2. 247)
ityuktam, tanmānasapratyakṣaprastāve grāhakād bhinnameva grāhyamapekṣya | na hi svasaṃvedane'pyeṣa eva nyāya iti sthitametat |
[95,1]
tathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇa evāha, na hi tvayārthāntaramajanakaṃ pratītiviṣayatveneṣṭamiti | na cāvastvarthāntaram | artha eva hyanyamarthamapekṣyārthāntaramucyate, na tvavastu | tadbhāvaniṣedhamātraṃ tat | tasmādarthāntaratvābhāvānna svajanyajñānāpekṣānarthasya | tato vikalpamātramatra śaraṇam | tadākārollikhitaścāsya svabhāvo nāpara ityapyavaśyaṃ svīkartavyam | anyathā śaśaviṣāṇādiśabdānāmanuccāraṇameva prasajyeteti kathaṃ vyavahāraḥ ? tathā hi kharaśṛṅgādiśabdena śabditamarthamanūdyāvaśyaṃ kiñcidvidheyam, yathā na kramādirahitatvaṃ śaśaviṣāṇadharmastatsahitaṃ vā, yathā vā nāsatā kasyacidvirodhabodhaḥ, nāvastudharmīti vā | tatra śaśaviṣāṇāsadavastuśabdairyadi nābhimato'rthaḥ pratyāyyate, abhimatādanya evārtho dhvanijanitavikalpasya, tadā vidhīyamānaḥ kramākramaniṣedhādiḥ kasya pratīyatām ? tatpratītyabhāve ca śabdoccāraṇamanarthakamāyātam | asti ca kūrmaromādiśabdavyavahāraḥ, tasmāt sa eva tasyārthaḥ, arthasyāpi sa eva niścayaḥ | dṛṣṭe'pi vikalpa eva niścayaḥ | evaṃ tarhi vikalpa evāstu sarvatrāśrayaṇīyaḥ, kiṃ darśanena ? naivaṃ darśananirākṛte vikalpacetasyākāramātrasphuraṇād vastutvasādhanārthaṃ bādhanārthaṃ vā pramāṇāntarāpekṣaṇam | darśanena tu viṣayīkṛte vastuni yāvati rūpe vikalpaḥ, tāvati sa eva niścayaḥ, asati sādṛśyād vipralambhe | tasmānna vastunyapi vikalpamātraṃ śaraṇam, avastuni tu tadeva śaraṇam | tadākārabāhyādhyavasānameva hi pramāṇāntarasāpekṣaṃ tatra prārthyate | tacca vikalpenaiva siddham | pramāṇavṛttau tu na pramāṇāntarāpekṣā | tatastena vikalpena yat svarūpamullikhitaṃ tatparāmarśena yathā kramākramarahitatvaniṣedhādikamupasthāpayanti santastadarhatayā, tathā tadrūpapratyanīkākāreṇa saha virodhavyavasthāyāṃ kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? yathā vā bandhyāsutasya saundaryādiniṣedho'nurūpaḥ, tathā ca vastutāvirodhasya ko virodhaḥ yadi cānubhavābhāvādvirodhapratirodho'nubhavābhāvādeva saundaryaniṣedho'pi mābhūt, tato vidheyasya kasyaciddharmasyābhāve'bhāvābhidhāyināmanuccāraṇaprasaṅgastadavasthaḥ, na ca tacchakyamityapi niveditam |
[96,1]
atha bandhyāsutādīnāṃ vikalpanīyād rūpād rūpāntaravirahāt tanmātrasya ca vikalpena viṣayīkaraṇe tadanurūpavyavahārasya na kṣatiḥ ? evaṃ sati virodhavyavahārasyāpi tadanurūpasya kā kṣatiḥ ? yathā ca vastutayā bandhyāsutasya virodhaḥ, evaṃ nityasyāpi yo dharmaḥ pratyanīka upapādayituṃ śakyastena kathaṃ na virodhaḥ ? tat kathamanubhavābhāvamātraṃ virodhabādhanesādhanamanabhidhīyamānaṃ sādhu syāt ? yadi tu vikalpo'pi tadviṣayo na syāt, tatpratyanīkākāraparāmarśo vā na syāt, sahānavasthānābhidhāno vā virodhaḥ sādhayitumiṣṭo bhavet, bhaved virodhasiddhiḥ | ekasya hi bhavato'nyabhāve abhāvāt sahānavasthānavyavasthā | bhāvaśca pratyakṣagocara iti kathamekasyānyavastutve ghaṭeta ?
parasparaparihārasthitilakṣaṇatvaṃ tu pratyanīkākāraparāmarśamātrasādhyam vikalpamātreṇa viṣayīkaraṇe'pi sannidhīyamānavyavasthānimittaṃ nāvaśyaṃ vastvanurodhi, kathamanyathā bhāvābhāvayoreva virodhaḥ parasparaparihāralakṣaṇaḥ ? tatra ca virodhe pradhānamudāharaṇaṃ tāveva |
abhāvasya vastutvasvīkāre'pi na bhāvasya bhāvo'bhāvābhidhāne vastuni, nāpyabhāvasya bhāvo'bhāva iti nābhāvavastuparamparāmupagantuṃ śakyamiti svapracyutimātramavastuvyavahartavyaikasvabhāvamiṣyamāṇaṃ kathaṃ tadvirodhi vyavasthāpyatām ? virodhāvyavasthāne ca tatra svātmā ca svapracyutiścetyekameva vastu svātmanaivāsti ca nāsti ceti syāt, na caivaṃ niyamenetyayameva virodhārthaḥ | kṣaṇikākṣaṇikavad vā | yathā hyekasya nākṣaṇikaṃ tathā nānyasya kṣaṇikamiti | tasmād vastvavastunorna parasparaparihāralakṣaṇavirodhabādheti sthitam ||
[96,2]
nanvevaṃ virodhasyāpāramārthikatve taddvāreṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhirapyavāstavī syāt, na hyapāramārthikādhāraḥ pāramārthiko bhavitumarhati virodhaḥ | yadāha śaṅkaraḥ, evaṃ tarhi virodhakalpanayā bādhakamapi kalpitavirodhatvānna vāstavavyatirekasādhanamityavāstavavyatirekatvāt sattāyāḥ, tadāyattaṃ kṣaṇikatvamapyavāstavameveti |
[96,3]
nyāyabhūṣaṇo'pi tadevamupaskurvannāha, saṃvṛtisiddhenākṣaṇikena virodhāsiddhiriti cet ? saṃvṛtisiddhamapi vāstavaṃ kālpanikaṃ vā syāt | yadi vāstavam, tataḥ kathaṃ tasyāsattvam ? kathaṃ vārthakriyāvirodhaḥ ? arthakriyāṃ kurvaddhi vāstavamucyate | atha kālpanikam, tadvirodhaḥ kiṃ vāstavaḥ kālpaniko vā ? na tāvad vāstavaḥ, kalpitavirodhivirodhatvād bandhyāputravirodhavat | atha virodho'pi kālpanika eva, na tarhi paramārthato'kṣaṇikasyārthakriyāyāṃ kramākramābhyāṃ virodha ityato'kṣaṇikāt sattvasya vyatirekasiddhirapyapāramārthikītyavāstavavyatirekatvāt sattāyāḥ, tadāyattaṃ kṣaṇikatvamapyavāstavameveti |
[97,1]
abaddhapralapitametat | na hi virodho nāma vastvantaraṃ kiñcidubhayakoṭidattapādaṃ sambandhābhidhānamiṣyate'smābhiḥ, upapadyate vā, yenaikasaṃbandhino vastutvābhāve apāramārthikaḥ syāt | yathā tviṣyate tathā pāramārthika eva | viruddhābhimatayoranyonyasvarūpaparihāramātraṃ virodhārthaḥ | tacca bhāvabhāvayoḥ pāramārthikameva | na hi bhāvo'bhāvarūpamāviśati, nāpyabhāvo bhāvarūpamiti yo'yamanayorasaṅkaraniyamaḥ sa eva virodhaḥ | sa ca niyamaḥ svātmānaṃ virodhamapi pāramārthikapade niveśayati | evaṃ na nityaṃ kramayaugapadyarūpamāviśati, nāpi kramayaugapadyaṃ nityarūpamāviśatīti yo'yaṃ niyamaḥ sa eva virodhastayoḥ | na ca kadācidanyatheti pramāṇasiddhireva pāramārthikateti kathamucyate, virodhasyāpāramārthikatayā sattvahetorvyatireko'pyatāttvika iti ? nityasya punarapāramārthikatvamaṅgīkṛ yaiva sarvamavasthāpitamiti na kaściddoṣaḥ | yacca kalpitavirodhivirodhasya vāstavatvaniṣedhāya kalpitavirodhivirodhatvād bandhyāsutavirodhavadityuktam, tatraiva anena tapasvinā kathamāśrayāsiddhitvādidūṣaṇaṃ sthavīyo'pi nopalabdhamityāstāṃ tāvadasya marmodghāṭanam |
[97,2]
etacca cintyate | kalpitavirodhivirodhatvameva vāstavatvena viruddhaṃ na vā ?
yadi tāvanna viruddhaṃ, tadā kalpitāvirodhiviruddhatvamapi bhavati, vāstavatvamapi syāditi kathaṃ tadupanyāsastannirākaraṇaikāntikaḥ syāt ? nāviruddhavidheḥ kasyacit pratiṣedhasiddhiḥ |
atha viruddham, sa virodho vāstavo'vāstavo vā ? tatrāvāstavo virodhaḥ paraparābhave'tiprasaṅgāt asamartha iti, vāstavapakṣe kalpitavirodhivirodho'pi svayaṃ vāstava iṣṭaḥ, na cāsmākamiva svaviruddhaniṣedhāmidhāyīti paśya dhārṣṭyavijṛmbhitam | yathā hi nityakramayaugapadyayorvirodhaḥ kalpitavirodhivirodho nityasya kalpitatvāttathā vāstavatvakalpitavirodhe virodhayorvirodhaḥ kalpitavirodhavirodho vartate kalpitasya virodhino virodha iti kṛtvā kalpito virodhī tasyeti vā, kalpitasya hi virodhino virodho'pi kalpita eva na vāstava ityeva bhavatpauruṣeṇa sādhyamānamīkṣāmahe | tasmāttasya kalpitasya virodhasya virodhino vāstavatvena saha yo virodhaḥ so'pi kalpitavirodhivirodhaḥ siddhaḥ | tasya vāstavatve svavacanavirodhaḥ | avāstavatve dūṣaṇamuktameva |
[98,1]
api ca | virodho nāmaikatra dvayoḥ saṃvāsaniṣedhārthamarthyate | na tu dvayorvastutvasiddhirnāma virodhaphalam | yatra tu dvayorvastutvasiddhistatra sāmarthyādekena vastunā vastvantaratiraskārāt kvacid deśe, yathā sahānavasthāne yathoktaṃ prāk | prakṛtastu virodho dharmayorekatra dharmiṇi sadbhāvaniṣedhaphalaḥ |
[98,2]
tatra yathā dvāvapi dharmau santau niṣidhyete, yatra nīlatvaṃ na tatrānīlatvam |
ato na nīlānīlamekamiti | tathā sadasattvarūpāvapi vipratiṣiddhau dharmāvekatra dharmiṇi samāropitau pratiṣiddhāveva | na hi jananyāḥ tanaye bandhyātanayatvamāropitaṃ tattvato'saditi na niṣedhyam | bandhyātanaye vā vikalpaikagocare jananītanayatvamāropitaṃ na niṣedhyam | na hi jananītanayo bandhyātanayo vaikātmā, tāvataiva virodhakāryaparyavasanāt, kimapareṇa virodhanāmnā yo vastudharmāvanapekṣya nātmalābhamāsādayati ?
evaṃ yatra nityatvaṃ na tatra kramayaugapadyavattvam, yatra kramayaugapadyavattvaṃ tatra na nityatvamato na nityaṃ kramayaugapadyayogi paramārthataḥ | tataśca sattāyuktamapi naiva niyamena paramārthataḥ | tataḥ kṣaṇika eva viśrāmyat tadāyattasattākameva sattvamiti sattvāt kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddheravirodhaḥ | yadi caivamapi virodhavyatirekapratisandhānena mātṛmodakakrameṇa gṛhītvā girikuharakoṇamāviśya ghoṣayitumicchasi ced, ghoṣaya | na punarasmadārabdhasiddhipratibandhe kiñcidupayujyase | tadalamabhiniveśaparavaśībhūya vāstavā evaite virodhādaya ityeva sādhu | nanu nityatvaṃ kramayaugapadyavattvaṃ ca viruddhau dharmau vidhūya nāparo virodho nāma, kasya vāstavatvamiti cet ? tadapi yatkiñcit | na hi dharmāntarasaṃbhavena virodhasya pāramārthikatvaṃ brūmaḥ | kiṃ tu yato viruddhau dharmau dharmāntarasaṃbhave'pi hi yadi na viruddhau na pāramārthiko'pi virodhaḥ | viruddhau cet ? tāvataiva tāttviko virodha iti vyavahāraḥ, kimapareṇa dharmeṇa ? yadapi bandhyāputravirodhavadityuktam, tatra kimekādhāra evāyaṃ virodho dṛṣṭāntīkṛtaḥ, atha dvitīyāpekṣaḥ ? dvitīyo'pi pratiyogirūpo'nyamātraṃ vā ?
prathamapakṣastāvadayuktaḥ, na hi kaścidekādhāraṃ virodhaṃ pratijānīte | tato yadi bandhyāputravirodhasyābhinnadharmiṇo'pāramārthikatvaṃ tadobhayadharmiṇo'pi pāramārthikena virodhena na bhāvyamiti ko'yaṃ nyāyaḥ ? evamanyamātreṇāpi na virodhaḥ, kṛtakānityatvavat |
pratiyoginā tu tatrāpīṣyata eva | bandhyāputrasya hi abandhyāputratvena virodho'styeva |
ekātmaniṣedhaścābhimata eva |
[99,1]
nanu dharmayorvirodhe dharmiṇoraikātmyaniṣedha iti yuktaṃ, banyāputrasyābandhyāputratvena virodho dharmidharmayorvartate | naiṣa doṣaḥ | dharmiṇo'pi dharmadvāreṇaiva vyavahriyante evaṃ dharmiṇorapi kadācidbhāvapradhāno vā nirdeśa iti | yaśca vaidharmyeṇa dahanatuhinayorupanyāsaḥ, so'pyayuktaḥ, parasparaparihārasya vivakṣitatvāt | yau ca tadviṣayatayā sāpekṣadhruvabhāvābuktau, tatrāpi sāpekṣatayā kādācitkatvamanityatvamuktam | dhruvabhāvo'pyavaśyambhāva iti yadi bhāvaniyamatvam, tadā nityatvameva | tato nityānityayoriyaṃ virodhasthitiḥ kathamanubhavapūrvakatayopadarśayantaṃ nopahāsayati ?
nityena kathaṃ virodhapratītirityeva hi prakṛtam | athāvaśyaṃ bhaviṣyattā dhruvabhāvaḥ, sāpi na kasyacidanubhavaviṣaya iti nityavadeva doṣaḥ |
[99,2]
syādetat | yacca kadācidavaśyambhūtamupalabdhaṃ tadapekṣayedamucyata iti | tadapekṣayā tarhi virodha eva nāsti, taddhi sāpekṣaṃ ca dhruvabhūtaṃ ca | atha tadā sāpekṣatvaṃ nāsti siddhatvāt, anyadā tadā sutarāṃ nāsti, asiddhatvādeva | asiddhadharmaṃ evāpekṣeti cet ? ananubhūte tarhi na virodhavyavastheti sa eva doṣaḥ | asiddhasyaiva siddhikālāpekṣayā anubhūtenaiva virodha iti cet ? siddhikālāpekṣāsvīkāre tarhi virodha eva nāstītyeva sādhu |
[99,3]
etenānubhavābhāvād virodhavyavasthābhāve sādhye vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntābhimataḥ sādhyāvyatirekī, asatā virodhaprasañjane tu sādhanāvyatirekī | dhruvabhāvasya nityatārthapakṣe tu sādhyakoṭinikṣepa eveti | bhedābhedādikaṃ tu bhavatu vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ | na ca tāvatāpi vastunoreva nākṣaṇiko virodha iti niyamaḥ, anyathāpi samarthitatvāditi | yadapi nāsiddhe bhāvadharmo'stīti (pra0 vā0 3. 190)
vācyam, tadapyāśrayāsiddhicodyasya dūrīkṛtatvānnirākṛtam | asato'pi dharmitvasādhanāt, avastuni vikalpasya pratītivyavasthāsiddheśca vyomādisvarūpāpratītirapi parihṛtā |
[100,1]
syādetat, yadi vikalparūpāṃ pratītimāśrityāśrayāsiddhiparihāraḥ sattāsādhane'pi samānam, tataḥ kathamucyate nāsiddhe bhāvadharmo'stītyādi ? kathaṃ cātmano vibhutvasādhanaṃ sarvatropalabhyamānaguṇatvamāśrayāsiddhābudāhriyata iti cet ? sādhanānurodhādubhayatrāpi hi bhāvadharma eva heturupātta āśaṅkitaśca | na ca bhāvadharmasyāvastu dharmī bhavitumarhati |
na hi dhūmarśiśapātvādayo'vastuni vasanti | tasmād yatra bhāvadharmaḥ sādhanaṃ tatra niyamena vastveva dharmī | na ca vikalpamātraviṣayasya vastutāśvāsaḥ, avastunyapi vikalpamātrānapāyāt | tato vastu dharmīkurvatā pratyakṣānumānarūpe ca siddhirabhidhātavyā | tadanabhidhāne tu vikalpamātragocarito'rthaḥ sandigdhasattāko nirastasattāko vā dharmīkriyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ vastutayā niścitaḥ kṛtaḥ syāt ? tathā ca sati yāvān vastudharmo hetuḥ sarvo'sau nāśrayāsiddhimatikrāmati, ekatra sandehādanyatra viparyayāt | tataḥ pratyakṣānumānābhyāṃ vastuviṣayābhyāmasiddhe bhāvadharmo na heturastyāśrayāsiddhatvāditi yuktametat sattāsādhane | asattāsādhane tvavastudharmo heturavastuni vikalpamātrasiddha eva nāśrayāsiddhidoṣeṇa dūṣayituṃ śakyaḥ | na hi tasya vastvāśrayāpekṣā, avastudharmādeva |
na ca tadādhārasya pratyakṣānumānāpekṣā, avastutvādeva | bhāvadharme tu sādhane vastvevāśrayo vastudharmatvāt | vastunaśca niścayaḥ pratyakṣānumānābhyāmeva, tatastayorabhāve niyamenāśrayāsiddhiriti sadasattāsādhanayoḥ kathaṃ samāno doṣaḥ ?
[100,2]
yattu trilocanena pramāṇāntaraṃ nityānāmasattāsiddhau kramādivirahasyābhāvadharmatā na sidhyatītyuktam, tad bālasyāpi durabhidhānam | nityā hi dharmiṇaḥ | asattvaṃ sādhyam | kramādiviraho hetuḥ | asya cābhāvadharmatvaṃ nāma svasādhyābinābhāvitvamucyate, abhāvānāṃ śaśaśṛṅgādīnāṃ dharmo na bhāvānāmiti kṛtvā | tadanena vacasā yāvat pramāṇāntareṇa pakṣe sādhyaṃ na sidhyati, na tāvaddhetorvyāptirityuktaṃ bhavati |
tacca kutra hetāvupalabdhamaneneti na vidmaḥ | yathā cānyatra sādhyanāntarīyakatā anyadā pravṛttapramāṇāntarasiddhā dṛṣṭāntena smāritā pakṣīkṛte sādhyasiddhyarthamupayujyate, nānyataḥ sādhyasiddhimapekṣate, tathā kramādyabhāve'bhāvadharmatā vyāptisvabhāvānyadaiva kramākrameṇa siddhatvasya | vyāptigrahaṇakāle pravṛttapramāṇasiddhākāśakamaladṛṣṭāntena smāritā sādhyasiddhāvupayujyate, nānyataḥ sādhyasiddhimapekṣate | anyathā sarvānumānavaiyarthyāt |
kramayaugapadyena hi sattvasya vyāptisiddhau sattvasya vyāpyasyābhāvena kramayaugapadyasya vyāpakasya viraho vyāptaḥ sidhyatītyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramayaugapadyaviṣayaḥ | yathā ca vyāptirūpaṃ tathā pūrvameva niścitaṃ, sadabhāvadharmatvaṃ na pakṣe pramāṇāntareṇa sādhyasiddhyā vyavasthāpyate, tathā kramākramābhāvābhāvenāpi sādhyaṃ prasādhya vyavasthāpyata iti naḥ pakṣaḥ, pūrvameva vyavasthāpitatvāt | tat kuta itaretarāśrayatvam ?
[101,1]
kiṃ ca, itaretarāśrayatvamapyevaṃ yujyate | kramādivirahasyābhāvadharmatvasiddhau teṣāmasattvasiddhiḥ asattvasiddhau cābhāvadharmatvasiddhiriti | viṣamadṛṣṭinā punarabhāvadharmasiddherasattvāsiddhau na prayājakatvamuktaṃ, kiṃ tu pakṣadharmatāsiddheḥ | tat kīdṛśamitaretarāśrayatvam ? na ca pakṣadharmataivābhāvadharmatā, sādhyāvinābhāvarūpatvādabhāvadharmatāyāḥ |
atha yadyabhāvadharmatvaṃ kramādyabhāvasya syāt, tadā pakṣīkṛtānāmasatāṃ nityānāṃ dharmaḥ syādityabhiprāyāt pakṣadharmatāvyāpāradvāreṇa tadavyāpāro darśitaḥ, tathāpi cakrakaṃ vaktumucitam | tadapi prācīnacarcayā carcitameva |
[101,2]
kiṃ ca, abhāvadharmatve vyāptirūpe sati pakṣadharmatvamiti nāyaṃ hetvantarasādhāraṇo nyāyaḥ | na cāsyāpi hetorevam, abhāvadharmatvaṃ hi vyāptirbhavatu mā vā, kramādivirahastu kena nityānāṃ niṣidhyate ? na caite'pyasattārūpeṇa dharmiṇaḥ, kiṃ tu sadasattvasandehavattveneti yatkiñcidetat bhāvadharmatvamubhayadharmatvaṃ ca neṣṭamasya kramādivirahasya hetoriti na prathamavikalpe doṣaḥ | nāpi dvitīye, vyatirekasyābhāvarūpatve'pi vikalpena pratīteḥ samarthitatvāt | na hyabhāvarūpāṇāṃ vikalpādanyā pratītirapratītirvā, ubhayathāpyabhāvavyavahārahāniprasaṅgāt | tato'nubhavāpekṣāvirahānna tajjananaprasaṅge doṣāvakāśaḥ |
anāśvāsastu śāsitumucitaḥ | so'pi kramayaugapadyavirahalakṣaṇavyāpakānupalambhasaṃbhavālliṅgajatvena dūrīkṛtaḥ |
[102,1]
tathā hi tathaiva trairūpyapariśodhanametadārabdham, siddhaṃ ca kimiti vismaryate, yato liṅgābhāvādityucyate ? tasmāt kramādivyāpyasattāvyatirekavikalpe kathamanāśvāsaḥ ?
avyatirekaśaṅkā hyanāśvāsasyārthaḥ | vyāpyavyāpakabhāvaniścaye cāsthānametaditi nityānniyamena vyatiricyamānaṃ sattvaṃ kṣaṇikatvena vyāptaṃ siddhamiti na doṣaḥ |
[102,2]
tṛtīye'pi vikalpe vyatirekaniścayasya dṛḍhīkṛtatvāt, so'yaṃ vyāpakānupalambho nitye svāśraye kramādyabhāvaṃ sādhayanneva sattāyāstato niyamena vyatirekaṃ, kṣaṇikatāyāṃ ca pratibandhamasyāḥ sādhayatīti trayo'sya vyāpārāḥ ekavyāpārasaṃgṛhītāśca, na ca doṣaleśena lipyante | tritvaṃ cārthaśakteḥ sattālakṣaṇatve, hetumātratve tu vyatirekamātrasādhanamasattāsādhanārtha iti vyāpāradvaitameveti sthitam ||
[102,3]
nanu vyāpakābhāvasyābhāvarūpatvena vastudharmatayā āśrayāsiddhiparihāre'pi sa kathamabhāvaḥ kasyacit pratipattiḥ, pratipattiheturvā tasyāpi vā kathaṃ pratipattiriti kiṃ na dṛśyate ? talliṅgajanmā ca saṃpratyeva vyatirekavikalpo na visaṃvādaśaṅkāmaṅke nidhatta ityuktam | avaśyaṃ ca sādhyabuddhiṃ sādhayatā sādhanena bhāvavyavahāraḥ svīkartavyo nānyathā |
taccābhāvarūpatve sarvaṃ virudhyate | vyāpakānupalabdhirityapi yadyapyanupalabdhimātraṃ sa eva doṣaḥ, na cānyopalabdhirvyāpakānupalabdhirabhidhātuṃ śakyā, anyasyāpi kasyacidanupalabdhiriti | tadapi yatkiñcit, dharmyupalabdherevānyatrāpyanupalabdhitayā vyavasthāpanāt |
yathā hi neha śiṃśapā vṛkṣābhāvādityatra vṛkṣāpekṣayā kevalapradeśasya dharmiṇa upalabdhiḥ vṛkṣānupalabdhiḥ, śiṃśapāpekṣayā ca kevalapratītireva śiṃśapābhāvapratītiriti svabhāvahetuparyavasāyivyāpāro vyāpakānupalambhaḥ | tathā nityasya dharmiṇo vikalpabuddhau parisphurataḥ kramādyapekṣayā kevalasphuraṇameva kramādyanupalambhaḥ, arthakriyāpekṣayā ca kevalapratītirevārthakriyāviyogapratītiriti viśeṣaḥ | adhyavasāyāpekṣayā ca yathā neha śiṃśapā vṛkṣabhāvādityabhāvasya hetupañcamyā nirdeśaḥ, tathā bhāvaḥ sādhanamityapi vyavahāraḥ, na tvabhāvaḥ sādhanameva kvacit | sa ca vyavahāraḥ avasitārthāvisaṃvādānna parihartuṃ śakyaḥ | yat khalu vyāpakena virahitaṃ tadavaśyaṃ vyāpyenāpītyetāvata evārthasya saṃvādinaḥ tenāpi prakāreṇa pratipādanāt | ayaṃ ca nyāyo yathā satye dharmiṇi tathāsatye'pīti ko viśeṣaḥ ?
[103,1]
nanvayameva mahān viśeṣaḥ | satye hi dharmiṇi vyāpakasyaikajñānasaṃsargī sa eva dharmīti tasyopalabdhiranupalabdhirvyāpakasyāstu, asatyastu dharmī naikajñānasaṃsargī kenaciditi cet ? tenaiva svasaṃbandhinā dharmeṇa vyāpakasaṃmatena | tathā hyekajñānamatra vikalpa eva | sa hi nityagrāhī vikalpaḥ tadākārāntaramiva kramayaugapadyadharmasaṃbandhe nityasya kramādyākāramapyullikhediti saṃbhāvanayā ekajñānasaṃsargitvamubhayoranivāryam |
yadi na nityamanādheyātiśayatvādinā dharmāntareṇa saha pratītigocarībhavet, yaugapadyāyaugapadyaṃ vāstavadharmiṇā saha na pratītiviṣayaḥ syādapyevam | na caivam, na ca niṣedhyasya saṃbhāvanāṃ vinā kvacidekajñānasaṃsargaḥ tadaiva syāllabhyaḥ | tatra yathā hariṇaśirasi tenaikajñānasaṃsargi śṛṅgamupalabdham, harivarāṅge'pi tatsaṃbhāvanayaiva tatsaṃsargānniṣidhyate, tathā nīlādāvapariniṣṭhitanityānityabhāve tāvat kramākramau svadharmiṇā sārdhamekajñānasaṃsargiṇau dṛṣṭau nitye'pi yadi bhavato nityagrāhiṇā jñānena svadharmiṇā nityena sahaiva gṛhyeyātāmiti saṃbhāvanayaikajñānasaṃsargadvāraka eva pratiṣedhamāviśataḥ |
[103,2]
kathaṃ punaretannityajñāne kramāderasphuraṇamiti, yāvatā kramākramakroḍīkṛtameva nityaṃ vikalpayāma iti cet ? ataeva bādhakāvatāraḥ, viparītarūpāvataraṇaṃ vinā tasya vaiyarthyāt | so'yaṃ nityātmani kramākramāropau bhavatastadvādhakopanyāsaṃ prayojayennāma, na tu nitye kramākramāvantarbhāvayituṃ prabhavati, virodhāt | kālāntaraikarūpatayā hi nityatvaṃ, kramākramau ca kṣaṇadvaye'pi bhinnarūpatayā, tato nityasya kramākramikārthakriyāśakteśca parasparapratyanīkarūpatayā durnivāro virodha iti kathaṃ nitye'ntarbhāvaḥ kramādeḥ ? anantarbhāvācca śuddhanityavikalpena dūrīkṛtasamāropeṇa kathamullekhaḥ kramākramasya ? sarvasya ca vikalpamātragocarasya vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayā viruddhaniyatāniyatadharmavyavasthānaṃ, yathā treguṇyasyaikatvaṃ viruddhaṃ dharmaḥ prasādatāpadainyakriyā niyatā, nairātmyetarayogo'niyataḥ, tathehāpi pūrvāparakālayorekātmatayā yadyakārakamakārakameva, sarvadā kārakatveṃ ca kārakatvameva nityaṃ, kramākramau tu kadācit kriyāśaktisvabhāvau, yaugapadye hi vyaktamekadaiva karaṇamiti kādācitkakriyatvam, krame'pi kṛtāyāḥ kariṣyamāṇāyāśca karaṇāt kādācitkyeva kriyā, sahakāryapekṣāyāḥ kṣiptatvāt | tataḥ kādācitkākādācitkakriyatvayoḥ parasparaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayā virodhaḥ siddhaḥ |
evaṃ sati pratiyogini nitye vikalpyamāne ekajñānasaṃsargilakṣaṇaprāpte viruddhasyānupalabhyamānasya kramākramasya tadupalabdhirevānupalabdhiḥ | saiva vārthakriyāśaktervyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | tasmād vyāpakadharmyupalabdhitayā na vyāpakānupalambhāntarādasya viśeṣaḥ | yadi ca dharmitve'pi vastvavastutayā vibhāgo bhāgyahīnasya bhavato matimadyāpi duḥsthayati, vastunyapi dharmiṇi ekatra pradeśaḥ kaṭhino dharmī dravarūpamanyatra jalamityādayo vibhāgā bhaṅgavantastadanviṣyantaḥ kena vāraṇīyāḥ ? tasmād vastvavastutayāpi bhedacintā kopayoginī ?
[104,1]
nanu mahānasyā upayogaḥ | tathā hi vastuni dharmiṇi paramparayā tatpratibaddhaṃ vyāpakānupalambhalakṣaṇamanumānaṃ pramāṇaṃ pramāṇabhājanībhavati, vastvadhiṣṭhānatvātpramāṇavyavasthāyāḥ | na caivamavastuni śakyamiti cet ? kiṃ tāvatparamparayāpi vastunaḥ sakāśādāgatatvameva vastvadhiṣṭhānatvam tadā kramākramasyārthakriyāyāśca vyāptigrahaṇagocaravastupratibaddhatvamasyāpi na kṣīṇam, dharmivikalpavastupratibaddhatvaṃ vā |
[104,2]
atha vastuni kenacid rūpeṇa vyavahārakāraṇatvaṃ vastvadhiṣṭhānatvam ? tadapi kṣaṇabhaṅgivastusādhanopāyatvena pratiṣṭhitamasya, tasyaiva vā dharmivikalpasya vastuno'vastūpādānatvavyavahārakāraṇatvena dharmivastunaiva tu vastvadhiṣṭhānatvamiti kimanena ? yadi caiṣa grahaṇa eva tat kimanumāna eva vastvadhiṣṭhānatvaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ vā ? na pratyakṣe, liṅgāśrayaṇameva hi dharmicintāmavakāśayati | tadanāśrayaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ vastuna āgataṃ vastunimittavyavahārakamityeva vastvadhiṣṭhānam, evamanumānamapi tathaiva vastvadhiṣṭhānamiti gṛhyatām | kevalaṃ paramparayā pratyakṣasyāpi hi janmaiva sākṣāt, vyavaharaṇaṃ tu vikalpādivyavadhānenaiva | anumānasya punarubhayamapi paramparayā | vyavahārāṇāmapi smṛtyabhilāṣādinā vyavadhānāt | evaṃ vastvadhiṣṭhānatvamanumāne vyavadhānena dūṣaṇameva |
kevalamanumāne'pyanyatra sādhyadharmāpekṣayā yadvyavadhānaṃ tato'tiriktamidaṃ vyāptigrahaṇāpekṣaṃ vartata iti dhāndhyaṃ dhiyaḥ | tatrāpi na sarvo'numānāntarasādhāraṇo'yaṃ dharmaḥ |
svasādhye hi sākṣātpratibandhamavadhūya viparyayavyāptyā gamakatvaṃ kāryakāraṇavyāpakānupalabdhiṣu | tadvad vastvadhiṣṭhānatvamapi yadi yathoktavyavadhānena viṣayaviśeṣe bhavet kīdṛśo doṣaḥ, kasyacid bādhakasyābhāvāt ? dharmivikalpāpekṣayā tu na tāvato'pi vyavadhānasya saṃbhavaḥ, asādhāraṇī ca pratyāsattirdharmiṇo vikalpākāreṇa sahaikīkaraṇāt | nirākārapakṣe'pi hi vikalpāyattaprakāśatvādalīkanityākārasya dharmiṇaḥ | tasmād dharmiṇo vastvadhiṣṭhānaparyeṣaṇaṃ pratyāsattiviśeṣāśrayatayā vikalpabapuṣāpi kṛtārthībhavediti na doṣaḥ kaścit | ayameva nyāyo na vaktā bandhyāsutaścaitanyābhāvāt, na kharaṃ kharaśṛṅgaṃ dravyatāviyogādityādau yojyaḥ, nāvastuni virodhaḥ pratītyaviṣayatvādityādau ca śaraṇam |
[105,1]
yadi pratītimātrāpekṣayā pratītyaviṣayatvaṃ tadā asiddhiḥ anubhavāpekṣayānekāntaḥ |
ityevaṃprakāradūṣaṇaparihāraśaktiḥ, na punarāśrayāsiddhyādidūṣaṇagaṇagaṇanā kācit |
etena vyāpakānupalabdhau hi vyāpyābhāvo'nyaḥ pratipattavya iti helayāpahastitam, dharmirūpasya bhinnasya pratipattiviṣayasya pratipādāt, gaṇḍaśaile vṛkṣatvābhāvena śiṃśapātvābhāvavat | tadevaṃ na prakṛtavyāpakānupalambhasya svarūpāsiddhiḥ, nityakramayaugapadyayoḥ virodhapratipādanāt | yadāha, kramākramavirodha iti, tad vyāpakadvāreṇa punararthakriyāvirodhādityāha | nāpyāśrayāsiddhiravastuno'pi dharmitvapratipādanāt, vikalpena pratipattipratipādanācca | ataeva śāstre, tasya dharmiṇi pratyakṣato'numānato vā prasiddhiniścayaḥ ityutsargasya parairanutpādyāpūrvarūpaṃ nakhādikaṃ sakṛt śabdādyahetutvādikamavastuni sādhyasādhanapratijñānamapavādo veditavya iti vyaktametat |
[106,1]
evaṃ dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇo'pi asiddhiparihāraḥ | vyāpyavyāpakābhāvau ca siddhāveva, nityavat tatra vimaterabhāvāt | tataḥ sapakṣe sattvaniṣedho'pi dhvastaḥ | atha mañcānekāntakrāntiḥ kṛteti, tadanena siddhasādhyapratibandhāt sattvahetoḥ siddhaḥ sādhyadharmiṇāṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgāṅgīkāra iti ||
{1.4}
<kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye caturthaḥ pādaḥ — ahetukavināśādhikāraḥ>
[107,1]
anvītivyatirekamākalayatā'dhyakṣeṇa dhūmāgnivad dṛśyādṛṣṭiprabhūtahetuphalatā siddhā vināśāṅgayoḥ | tatprāk kāraṇasannidheḥ phalamasannāśastanoti sthitiṃ tāvantaṃ kila kālamityapi mṛṣā nāśaḥ svarūpādṛśaḥ ||
[107,2]
nahīdantayā nāśasya svarūpamupalabdhigocaraṃ yenānvayavyatirekaniścayāt kāraṇābhimatamudgarādisannidheḥ prāk nāśākhyaṃ kāryamabhavat tāvantaṃ kālaṃ bhāvasya sthairyamāpādayet, yāvatā nāśasya svabhāvānupalabdhermṛṣaiva kalpaneyamiti kutaḥ kāraṇānupalabdhyā sthairyasiddhiḥ ?
[107,3]
nanu ghaṭamudgarādayo dṛśyante tāvat teṣveva kaścinnāśo nāmeti nāśasvarūpānupalabdhirasiddheti cet ?
[107,4]
dṛṣṭasyāvadayaṃ ghaṭo'tra ca patan dṛṣṭastathā mudgaro dṛṣṭā karparasaṃhatiḥ paramato'bhāvo na dṛṣṭo'paraḥ | tenābhāva itiśrutiḥ kva nihitā kiṃ vātra tatkāraṇaṃ svādhīnā paridhasya kevalamiyaṃ dṛṣṭā kapālāvaliḥ ||
[107,5]
sunipuṇaṃ nirūpayanto'pi māṃsacakṣuṣā vayaṃ tāvannāparamatra vastujātamīkṣāmahe, yadabhāvaśrutyā viṣayīkriyate | taddarśanābhāvācca tatkāraṇamapi kimavadhārayāmo, yadabhāvena pūrvapūrvamasannāśa iti syāt ? yaśca tatkāraṇaṃ kalpito daṇḍastasyāpyanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyinī kapālapaṃktireva dṛṣṭā, nānyā kācit | vaidharmyadṛṣṭāntatayeyamupanyastā punaḥ, yatheyamadhyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekāvanuvidadhatī dṛśyatayā daṇḍasya kāryamavasthāpyate, tathā yadi nāśākhyamapi vastu dṛśyaṃ syādanātmarūpavivekena tasyāpi tarasvidaṇḍakāryatā avāryaiva, na caivam | tasmāt kalpanaiveyam |
[108,1]
syādetat, āstāṃ karparapaṃktireva kalasadhvaṃso na ceyaṃ purātena sthairyamapi prasidhyatu tato bhinnena nāśena kim |
atrottaram,
[108,2]
nāśaḥ saiva yathocyate yadi tathābhāvo'pi kumbhāntaranyāse'bhāvaravaḥ kathaṃ matamataḥ sidhyatyabhāve'pi naḥ ||
[108,3]
ayamarthaḥ | yathā vegavanmudgaraprahārāt pūrvaṃ ghaṭasya nāśo nāstīti pratipādayituṃ śakyaṃ bhavatastatsvabhāvabhūtāyāḥ kapālapaṃkteradarśanāt, tathā nābhāvaparamparāparicayo'pi nāstīti śakyam | na hyabhāvo'pi kapālapaṃktirevocyate, yena svabhāvānupalabdhiravalambanaṃ tadvadeva syāt | atha nāśavadabhāvo'pi kapālapaṃktirevocyate, tadā kvaciddeśe kumbhamekamapanīya kumbhāntaranyāse kathamabhāvavyavahāraḥ, kapālāvalerabhāvāt ? asti ca kathañcidbhedamākalayataḥ tatrāpyabhāvavyavahāraḥ ekasyānyasya sādṛśyavipralabdhasya prācīnāvasthānavyavasāye'pi, tat kathaṃ kapālapālirevābhāvaḥ ? tadasyāṃ dhvaṃsaśabdaṃ saṅketayato yadi pūrvaṃ dhvaṃso nāstīti śakyamapyabhidhātu, kapāladaśāvirahāt, abhāvastu nāstīti na śakyam, sadṛśāparasaṃbhavena durupalakṣaṇāt | tasmāt prahārātprāgabhāve'pi kumbhasya saṃbhāvyamāne siddhamabhimatamasmākam | dṛśyānupalambhānavatāraṇaṃ nāma, ato na karparāṇāṃ dhvaṃsasaṃjñayopayogaḥ | na cānyanmudgarānvayavyatirekānukāri dṛṣṭamiti vyavahāramātraparāyaṇa eva nāśo na vastuto'sti |
[108,4]
nāśo nāsti yadi svahetuniyataḥ kiṃ deśakāle kvacit kumbho naṣṭa iti pratotiniyamastenāsti kāryaśca saḥ | nāpyanyat kila kāraṇaṃ rayavato daṇḍāt purāpyanyathā nāśotthānakṛtā vinaṣṭaghaṭadhīḥ kenoddhurā vāryate ||
[109,1]
evaṃ tarhi kāryāntaravat kāraṇānvayavyatirekānuvidhānaṃ dhvaṃsasyotphullagallamullapitaṃ luptaṃ, kāryāntaravadanubhavābhāvāt | kevalamupapattyā prasādhya pradhvaṃsamasthābhimatanibandhanādhīnatā sādhyā | sā copapattiḥ kṣīṇā, yataḥ
[109,2]
dṛṣṭe'mbhobhṛti mudgarādijanitāṃ dṛṣṭvā kapālāvaliṃ saṃketānugamādvinaṣṭaghaṭadhīstāvat samutpādyate | sāmagryāmiha nāśanāma na kimapyaṅgaṃ na vāsyāmapi syādeṣā na kadāpi nāpi ca purāpyeṣā samagrā sthitiḥ ||
[109,3]
pūrvārdhena naṣṭaghaṭabuddherjanmasāmagrīmādarśya paścārdhenādhikasya nāśanāmno nānvayo na vyatirekastadvivekasāmagryāstūbhayamanukṛtaṃ bhavediti darśitam | tatra nāśākhyaṃ na kiñcidiha sāmagryāṃ nimittamastītyanvayo nirastaḥ, na cāsyāṃ satyāmapi sāmagryāṃ kadācinna syādeṣā buddhiriti vyatirekāvalambanamapāstam | pūrvaṃ tarhi kasmānneyaṃ buddhiriti vyatirekapratyayāśātanaṃ śeṣeṇa ? yadi purāpyeṣā sāmagrī syāt, niyatamiyaṃ bhavantī buddhirarthāntarasāpekṣatāṃ sūcayet | na ceyaṃ sāmagrī purāpyasti, vikalakapālapaṃkteḥ parighapātādikāraṇābhāvenābhāvāt | tat kuto vyatirekamātramapi ? uktasāmagryāstu na vāsyāmapi syādeṣā na kadāciditi niṣedhadvayenānvayaḥ | śeṣeṇa vyatirekaśca vyaktaḥ |
tad buddhyabhāvakāle sāmagryā evābhāvapratipādanādasau sāmagryabhāvo buddhyabhāvavyāpta ityarthaḥ | yastu pratyakṣetarasahakārisākalyarūpatayā sarvaiva sāmagrī parokṣeti samarthayate viṣamadṛṣṭiḥ tataśca parokṣatayā tasyā nānvayavyatirekaniścaya ityucyate, hanta hutavahendhanādisāmagrīpratibandho'pi dhūmāderastamita ityapravṛttinivṛttikaṃ jagat prasajyeta |
tasmānnādṛṣṭābhyupagamo dṛṣṭasādhanasāmarthyapratirodhenetyalaṃ vistareṇa | tadayaṃ ghaṭāmarśavataḥ kapālānubhava eva naṣṭaghaṭāvasāyasādhana iti siddham | arthāpattirato gatā kṣayamiyaṃ na dhvaṃsasiddhau prabhuḥ na viśeṣabuddhirviśeṣaṇamantareṇeti cet — na, bhāve bhinnakālatvād viśeṣaṇatvāsiddherdhvaṃsasya yataḥ,
[110,1]
svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tadviśeṣaṇam |
[110,2]
kālabhedena pūrvāparakālayornāśabhāvayorabhāvāt kena kaḥ syāt ? kvacit pratītiviṣayīkriyate | na ca bhāve sthitidharmo dhvaṃsaḥ, kiṃ tu pradeśe | na cānyatra sthitaḥ anyasya viśeṣaṇaṃ, daṇḍavat | bhedādevamapi syāditi cet ? bhede tarhi sarvānyarūpavivekena pratibhāsamānameva viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ svānuraktapratītiviṣayīkuryāt, na svarūpeṇāpratibhāsamānaṃ, daṇḍavadeva | anumānasiddhenāpi daṇḍena daṇḍipratīterutpādādanekānta iti cet — na, sarvathā yasya na svarūpāvabhāsa ityabhiprāyāt | daṇḍasya punaranumānakāle'pratibhāsane'pi niścāyakābhimataliṅgena saha saṃbandhagrahaṇakāle'styeva svarūpanirbhāsaḥ | tatastadanusmaraṇādanumānakāle'pi tadrūpānuraktāṃ buddhimādadhīta daṇḍaḥ |
na ca sarvathā adṛṣṭadaṇḍasya daṇḍo'pyanumānabhājanaṃ svarūpānuraktapratītiheturvā dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ |
evaṃ nāśanāmāpyarthaḥ kathaṃ tathā syāt, sarvathā adarśanāditi ? na ca daṇḍānumānādbhinnā daṇḍipratītiḥ, daṇḍo'tra daṇḍo'sya daṇḍavānayamiti cānarthāntaratvāt | na ceyaṃ liṅgatyāge na bhavantī pratijñāmātratayānumānaṃ bhavitumarhati, yannaṣṭapratītirapi nāśanāmārthasādhakaṃ niścayamapekṣamāṇā kathaṃ svayameva sādhanatvenābhidhīyeta ? na cānyaliṅgamasti, sarvathā adṛśyatayā tasmin kasyacit pratibandhāsiddheḥ | ataeva hi saṃva buddhistatsiddhaya śaraṇamāśrīyate | ato'numānasiddhanānakāntaḥ | anumānasyāpi viśeṣaṇasvarūpanirbhāsanāntarīyakatvādapṛthaksiddhaścānumānaviśeṣaṇapratītyoriti, yasya na svarūpanirbhāsastanna kasyacit svānuraktapratītinimittam, yathā karikeśaraḥ | nāsti ca svarūpapratibhāso dhvaṃsasyeti vyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | svānuraktapratītinimittatvaṃ nirbhāsabhaṅge bhavadatiprasaṅgabādhitaṃ pratibhāsavattayeva vyāptam | na cāsiddhiḥ, idantayā darśayitumaśakyasya bāhyavastunaḥ pratibhāsavyavahārābhāvāt, idantayā nirdeśanoye ca vivādābhāvāt | na hi daṇḍo'pi daṇḍipratītyā sādhyo'dhyakṣasiddhatvāt | mūḍhaṃ prati vyavahārasādhane'pi nedantayā nirdeśaḥ, viśeṣato locanagocare |
[110,3]
atha sarvaṃ vastu svarūpeṇa pratibhāti, na pararūpeṇa, yathā bhāva eva nābhāvarūpeṇa, evamabhāvo'pi bhāvarūpeṇāpratibhāsamāno'pi svarūpeṇa pratibhātyeva | idantayā pratibhāsanaṃ nayanaviṣayasyāpi bhāvasyaiva | ato nedantayā pratibhāsābhāve'pyapratibhāsa eveti cet ? navai pararūpeṇa pratibhāso mṛgyate, tasyābhāvaṃ prati siddhatvāt | svarūpaṃ punarasya kiṃ tatpratibhātīti nibhālayanto na labhāmahe, idantayā nirdeśastu bhāveṣvetyapi na rājakīyo niyamaḥ | tad yadi bhāveṣvapi keṣucideva netrapātreṣvidantayā nirdeśo na sarveṣviti brūyāt, tadā ṭaṅkavakādayo'pi puraḥ pratibhāsina evedantayā paraṃ nirdeṣṭumaśakyā iti kimatra vaktavyam ? tasmād yāvaccakṣurgocaracāri vastu tāvadidantayā nirdeśapratibhāsameva, yatpunaridantayā nirdeśavirahitaṃ tadapratibhāsameva nayanagrāhyamiti nyāyaḥ |
[111,1]
atha viśeṣabuddhyaiva pratibhāso'pi sādhyaḥ, yathā hi na daṇḍibuddhirdaṇḍabuddhimantareṇa tathā daṇḍapratibhāsamantareṇāpi, evaṃ naṣṭabuddhirapi viśeṣabuddhitvānna nāśaṃ nāśapratibhāsamantareṇeti kathamapratibhāsaghoṣamiti cet ? bhavatyeva vikāro na punaretādṛśaḥ | svasantānavartipratibhāso'smābhirapyanumānena pratipattavya iti ghaṭādipratibhāse'pyevamidānīmāyātam | tat kimahaṃ paśyāmi kiñcidityanumānamanāptavatā āptavacanenāpi pratyetavyamityarthamapratikurvāṇo'pi vaidyaḥ kṛtārthaḥ syāt | antataḥ śapathenāpi nirvṛttirālambyeta | parokṣe hi viṣaye'mīṣāṃ prakārāṇāmavakāśaḥ, na jñāne | yatpunarapaśyantamātmānaṃ vedayamāna eva paśyasīti grāhyate vyaktamiyaṃ bhaṇḍavidyā paśyantamapi vāhayati | yo'pyapaśyannapi tadvacanena paśyāmīti gṛhṇīta sa khalu paśorapi paśuḥ |
[111,2]
jñānaparokṣatāvāde'pi hi,
[111,3]
kasyacitpratibhāsena sādhyate'pratibhāsi yat | pratibhāso'sya nāsyeti sādhyate nopapattibhiḥ ||
[111,4]
tasmāt pratibhāso'pi sādhya ityasaṃbaddhametat | nāśastvapratibhāsamāno yadi sādhyate, sādhyatām, na tu naṣṭaghaṭapratītyeti sthitametat,
[111,5]
nāśo vā'stu na tu pratītijanako yadvadghaṭe naṣṭadhīḥ |
[111,6]
abhyupagamyāpi brūmaḥ | astu vā nāśo nāma, na punarasyāvaśyaṃ pratītameva janakaṃ mudgarādīti śakyam, yathā naṣṭaghaṭabuddhereva na pratītaḥ kapālānubhavo heturiṣṭaḥ, tathā nāśasyāpi mudgarādiparihāreṇa kāraṇamanyadevādṛṣṭaṃ kiñcit syāt, yato na purā kāraṇānupalabdhisiddhiḥ | yathā adṛṣṭameva nāśākhyaṃ vastu svīkārasiddhaṃ naṣṭabuddhernibandhanam, tathā nāśasyāpyadṛṣṭameva kiñcit kāraṇaṃ na mudgarādīti kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi niyamena nāśanivṛttiḥ ? ayaṃ tu viśeṣo yathā mudgarasya kapāle kapālānubhavasya ca naṣṭabuddhāvanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ sāmarthyasiddhistathā na mudgarasya nāśe na nāśasya naṣṭabuddhāviti, yadi paraṃ bhavaduparodhādayamarthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ |
[112,1]
atha kapālānubhavāt kapālakalpanaiba syāt, na naṣṭaghaṭabuddhiriti cet ?
tadetajjīvato vyāghrasya daṃṣṭrotpāṭanam | kalasāmarśavataḥ kapālavalayavīkṣaṇādeva naṣṭaghaṭabuddherudayaḥ sākṣādanubhūyamāno'palapyate iti, evaṃ tarhi sarvasyānvayavyatirekāvadhāritārthasyāpalāpaḥ prasaktaḥ | yadā punaranarthitvādinā ghaṭāmarśena śūnyatā puruṣasya, tadā kapālāvalokanāt kapālakalpanaiva jāyate, sāmagrībhedasya bhedakatvāt | yadi punarbhavadabhiprayānuvartino bhāvā bhaveyurna bhavedapyevam, tathāpi yadīcchasi kapālānubhavādeva naṣṭaghaṭabuddhirastviti, tadā tathaiva syāditi na nāśaḥ prayojakaḥ |
tadalaṃ svamanīṣikāsaṃpratyayena karparadarśanameva tadbuddhinibandhanam | yadā tu kalasavimarśamapekṣate tathā saṅketasmaraṇamapi, tato nātiprasaṅgaḥ | na ca saṅketo'pi nāśamupadarśya kartuṃ śakyaḥ, tasyādṛśyatvādeva, kiṃ tu visabhāgotpattirūpaṃ vikāramupadarśya etādṛśāvasthāyāṃ naśyataḥ prayoga iti |
[112,2]
etenābhāvadarśanameva bhāvānupalambhaṃ saṃbhāvayanto nirastāḥ, abhāvarūpādarśanādeva |
tasmānna dhvaṃso nāma kaścit paścādbhāvī |
[112,3]
kiṃ cānyaprakṛti pratikṣaṇamidaṃ saṃsādhitaṃ cejjagat | prauḍhanyāyabalād vilambi nidhanaṃ syād vā navā kiṃ tataḥ ||
[112,4]
syādetat |
[112,5]
na dhvaṃsena vinānyataiva hi bhaved bhāvena sārdhaṃ sa cet | saccāsacca kimastu vastuniyataṃ bhāvānujo'sau tataḥ || bhāvāttena vibhinnakāraṇatayā tatkāraṇāsaṃbhavebhāvāttena kṛtānyatāpi galitā bhaṅgaḥ kuto'nukṣaṇam ||
[113,1]
bhāvahetoḥ sakāśādabhāvodayavarṇanā bhāvena sārdhaṃ sa cedityuktam | atra dhvaṃsādanyateti ko'rthaḥ ? kimeko bhāvastena khaṇḍakhaṇḍīkriyate ? atha bhāvāntarotpādanamātramasmāt ? uta prācīnanivartanaṃ ca bhāvāntarotpādanaṃ ca ? yadvā prācīnanivartanamātram ? tatra, naikātmānamanekatāṃ gamayati dhvaṃso virodhāttayorekānekatayoḥ | nanu kālabhedenaikamapyanekaṃ bhavanna duṣyatīti cet ? svabhedavirahe kālasya bhede'pi kim |
yadi hi kālabhedako bhāvabhedako bhaved, bhavedetat | bhāvasya tu tādavasthye kāśakuśāvalambanamupayuktamevaitādṛśāmiti prathamapakṣaniṣedhaḥ | bhinnaṃ cet kurute na tasya dalanam iti dvitīyo doṣaḥ | arthāntarakaraṇe hi tatprācīnaṃ na khaṇḍitamiti kṛte'pi karparādau kumbhopalambhaprasaṅgaḥ | bhinnena taddālanekiṃ nāśena ?
arthāntareṇa kapālādinā tasya kalasasya darśane'bhyupagamyamāne nopayogaḥ | nāśākhyasya tasyaivārthāntarasyotpādane upayoga iti cet ? vibhinnajanma tu bhavannāśasya hetorna kim ||
yata eva mudgarādernāśastata eva karparasyāstu janma, kiṃ sādhye dhvaṃsamutkṣipya ?
[113,2]
etena tṛtīye'pi vikalpe'nyotpādanabhāgaḥ pratyukta iti caturtho'vaśiṣyate | nāśena tasya nivṛttiḥ kriyata iti | tadāpi,
[114,1]
pradhvaṃsena vināśajanmani mate tenāpi nāśāntarotpāde nāśaparampareti vibhavedbhāvaḥ kadācinna saḥ | na dhvaṃsādaparā nivṛttiriti cedanyo'nyanāśaḥ kathaṃ tasmin vastuvilokanāditi na sannāśādṛśaḥ khyāpanāt ||
[114,2]
dhvaṃso hi vastutāṃ bhāvatāṃ vā atikramituṃ nārhati, anubhavajananasāmarthyādanyata upapatteśca | sa kathamanyo'rtho'nyasya nāśa ityucyate ? yattvetasmin sati vastuno'darśanādityuttaram, tanna sat, yato nāśasya darśanaṃ nāstīti khyāpitam, tatastasminnasatīti kathaṃ kathayituṃ pāryate ? yadi ca tasmin sati vastvadarśanād dhvaṃsākhyavastunivṛttirucyate, tadā —
[114,3]
nāśo mudgara eva vāstu śakalānyevāthavā,
[114,4]
tadubhayatra tasmin satīti vivakṣāghaṭanāt mudgarasya prāgbhāvāt, khaṇḍānāṃ samasamayatvāt, bīje satyaṅkuro goṣu duhyamānāsu satīṣu gata itivat | nāśa iti nivṛttiḥ dhvaṃsākhyo vā, dhvaṃso'pi mudgarādirevāstu | alaṃ pṛthak dhvaṃsakalpanayā, tāvatāpi tadabhāvāt purā sthiro bhāva iti siddheḥ |
[114,5]
atrocyate,
[114,6]
tad dvayaṃbhāvatvena na bhāvarodhi,
[114,7]
na hi bhāva eva bhāvasya virodhī bhavitumarhati | aviruddhabhāve ca kathamanyasya nivṛttiradarśanaṃ vā ? atrottaraṃ,
[114,8]
bhavato bhāṣaiva bhāvānyatā |
[114,9]
nātra bhāvānāṃ sāmarthyam, kiṃ tu bhavata eva bhāratyā bhāvatā abhāvatā vā |
tathā hi bhavatīti bhāvaḥ, bhavanaṃ cotpattistāvadasya svīkṛtā | yadāpyastīti bhāvaḥ, tadāpi vidyamānatā bhāvārthaḥ | sāpi svarūpasattvalakṣaṇā svīkṛtaiva nityatālaṃkṛtā yāvat | yaccāstīti na bhavati tat kimutpadyatinā saṃbadhyate bandhyāsutavadaṅkuravacca ?
[115,1]
atha sarvasāmarthyopākhyāviraheṇābhāvavyavahārāt śaktirapi sattvamanumanyate, sāpi svajñānajanane'bhyupagataiva, niḥśaṅkagamanādikaṃ ca tatkāryameva | svābhyupagataḥ sattvasamavāyaḥ svakāraṇasamavāyo vā paraṃ nāsti | na ca sarveṇa bhāvadharmeṇa sarvatra bhāve bhavitavyam, nāpi sarvabhāvadharmābhāvena bhāvāntarasyāpi na bhāvatvam | evaṃ sati sāmānyaviśeṣasamavāyānāmapyabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ | tebhyo'pyadhiko dhvaṃsasyotpattirevāparādhaḥ |
vastu cāvaśyaṃ nāśo vasatyarthakriyā asminniti na bhāva iti kaṣṭo vatāyaṃ siddhāntaviṣamagrahaḥ | tasmād bhavato'tra svātantryam | yadi bhaṇasi dhvaṃso'pi bhāvaḥ syāt, mudgarādirapi kumbhasyābhāvaḥ syāt |
[115,2]
na khalu mudgarādikaṃ bhāvamabhāvaṃ vā kaścid vyavaharatīti cet ? nanu dhvaṃsamapi yadi kenacid rūpeṇa jāyamānamupalabheta kaścid viśeṣato nityasthitaṃ kimabhāvaṃ vyavaharet ? dṛśyante hi tanudhūmādayo vyavadhānānavadhānādinā anupalabdhamūrtayaḥ punarupalabhyamānā bhāvavyavahārabhājaḥ | tasmād bhāvavyavahārahānirasyādarśanādeva pratyātmaṃ vedyate pratiyogidarśanasvabhāvāt | taccādarśanamanubhavābhyupagame bhāva eva, anupalabhyatve tu janmādikīrtanamākāśacitraṇam | svarūpajanmanorupalambhe tu bhāvavyavahāraḥ prasahyāyāta iti kathamasyāpi virodhitvam ? na ca mudgarādāvapyabhāvaśabdāpravṛttireva, bhāvāntaraparyudāsena tatsiddheḥ | na cātiprasaṅgo, dhvaṃsavat | yayā hi pratyāsattyā dhvaṃsākhyameva vastu ghaṭasya nivṛttirucyate, tasyā na karparaparidhayorvighātaḥ |
virodhitvamapi tayoreva ramaṇīyam, aṇīyasāpyaṃśena darśanākhyena tayorutkarṣāt |
tayoḥ satoḥ kumbhābhāvavyavahāra ityasyātiprasaṅgasaṅgamādbhaṅganimittasya puṣṭatvāt | na ca bhāvo bhāvāntaravirodhī na bhavatyeva, kathamanyathā gotvamagotvasya, dahanastuhinasya vā ? kiṃ ca virodho'pi dvividhaḥ prasiddhaḥ | tatra,rodhaḥ so'pi sahāsthitiryadi tadā bhāvadvayasyaiva sā dahanatuhinavat | avikalakāraṇasya bhavato'nyabhāve'bhāvāddhi sahānasthānavyavasthānam |
na ceyaṃ gatirbhāvābhāvayoḥ saṃbhavatīti vyaktam |
[116,1]
naikenānyahatiḥ parasparaparīhārasthite lakṣaṇe ||
[116,2]
na khalvalākṣaṇikavirodhasya sadvastubādhana vyāpāraḥ, kiṃ tu sahānavasthānasyaiva, lākṣaṇikasya tu dharmayoreva vyavasthānāt | vyavasthita eva vastuni vastunā avastunā vā svarūpasaṃkaravyatikaraniṣedhaḥ | tato yathā nīlamanīlaṃ na bhavati ubhayoranyonyasvabhāvatvāt, tathā kalasanāśayorapi syāt | na ca tāvateṣṭasiddhiḥ mudgarasannidhimātra iva tasya tādavasthyānapāyāt |
[116,3]
nanu kalasakuliśādau dharmayoreva virodhāt tadadhyāsitasya bhedamātram, kalasanāśau tu bhāvābhāvarūpatayā svayaṃ viruddhāviti kathaṃ saha syātām ? na, bhāvābhāvayorhi bhavanābhavanarūpatayā dharmayoreva parasparaparihāraḥ, yato na bhāvādhyāsitasyābhāvo'bhāvādhiṣṭhitasya vā bhāvaḥ, yato vā kumbhanabho'mbhoruhādernaikatvam | kalasanāśarūpasya padārthadvitayasya dharmirūpasya kva parasparaparihāraḥ ? virodhamātraṃ tu na vāryate, kebalamekena bhavatā bhavataḥ paribhave sati | tāvatā ca sahānavasthānavyāpāraḥ |
tasmāddharmayoreva parasparaparihāraḥ | nīlānīlayoḥ kathamiti cet ? nīlānīlayoḥ parasparaparihāra iti naikatvamanayorityevārthaḥ | tato dharmavirodha evānenāpi prakāreṇa prakāśyate | anyathā tuhinahutabhujoriva nīlānīlavāsasorapi militayoranavasthitiprasaṅgaḥ | tādātmyaṃ tu tadāpi nāstyeva |
[116,4]
deśo'pi nīlānīlayorbhinna eveti cet ? kāmaṃ bhinnaḥ, na tu vastunorvirodhaḥ tāvatā deśabhedena kṛtārthaḥ | anyathā jalajvalanayorapi tadvadeva militayoḥ prabandhasthitiḥ prasajyeta, sūkṣmadeśaparihāreṇa virodhasya phalavattvāt | ataeva viruddhopalabdhau kalpitaikabhāvaḥ sthūla eva deśo dharmī | evaṃ nīlamanīlatvena virudhyata ityapi nīlamanīlaṃ na bhavatītyevārthaḥ |
[116,5]
yadi tu dharmidharmayorapi sākṣādvirodhaḥ syāt, tadā yatra dharmiṇyanīlatvaṃ tatra nīlatvaṃ na syāt | asti ca yathā ratnāntaraṃ tapanīyamātre, tathā nāśasyābhāvarūpadharmamātratve'pi bhāvadharmā ghaṭo nāsannabhāvadharmā ca na sannityevārthaḥ, tataḥ siddhenābhāvena dharmeṇāsanneva ghaṭo'sanniti vyavahriyate, na tu sanneva nivartyate |
sattānivartane tu sarvatra sahānavasthānavyāpāraḥ | kathaṃ punarghaṭasyābhāvo dharmaḥ ? kasya punarasau dharmo'stu ? dharmatvena svīkārād dharmiṇo'vaśyamākṣepāt kṣmātalasyaivāstviti cet ? tataḥ kiṃ bhūtalasyaivābhāvo vivakṣitaḥ ?
[117,1]
nanu ghaṭasya nivartyanivarttakabhāvasaṃbaddho'bhāvo bhūtalasya dharmamātramucyate, na tu bhūtalasya nivartaka iti cet ? bhavatu bhūtalasyānibartakastaddharmo vā kevalam, yathā nīlaviruddhānīlatvayukte bhūtale nīlavastusthitiraviruddhā, tathā ghaṭaviruddhābhimatenābhāvena yukte'pi ghaṭasthiteravirodhaḥ syāt, tato'bhimānamātravyavasthita evaiṣāṃ nivartyanivartakabhāvaḥ | tasmād bhūtale kalasasyābhāva iti bhūtalādhārasya ghaṭasya saṃbandhitvenābhāsayantī vikalpabuddhirabhāvaṃ taddharmatvena vyavahārayatīti nyāyyam | adhyavasitāpekṣayā tu saṃvādetarau, tadevaṃ parasparaparihāraviruddho dharmaḥ svaviruddhasyāsata evāsattāmātmadharmiṇi vyavahārayati | na tu nivartayatīti dharmiṇo bhedavyavahārahetureva | tathā ca jalānalādiṣu sparśasyoṣṇetaratvaṃ dūre'pi pratyanīkākāravattayā anyonyāpanayanamanapekṣya svarūpavimarśamātreṇa virodhavyavahāragocarībhavati | sahānavasthānaṃ punarekenānyasya, sattānivartanadarśanādeva vyavasthāpyate | tad yadi sahānavasthānamabhimato virodhaḥ, tadā sidhyatu bhāvasya sattopalambhayornivṛttiḥ | kevalaṃ bhāvayorevāsau na bhāvābhāvayoḥ |
[117,2]
nanu tasmin sati tannivṛttiritīyatā sahānavasthānamabhimato virodhaḥ, taccābhāvenāpi bhāvasya labhyata iti na bhāvayoreveti yukto niyama iti cet ? uktamatrāsmin satītyeva durlabhamabhāve iti | kiṃ caivamabhāvatvasamarthanamanupayogi, bhāvayorapi tadvirodhasyāvirodhāt | mudgarādinaiva virodhasiddheśca dhvaṃsasyānupayogāt | atha lākṣaṇiko virodha iṣṭaḥ, tadā svarūpāsaṃkareṇaiva tasya kṛtārthatvād bhāvasyāvasthānamanivāryam |
[117,3]
kiṃ ca, sahānavasthānalakṣaṇapakṣe nānutpannena virodhinā paro viroddhavyaḥ, śītahutāśavat | prathamamutpattiḥ, tato vyāpāraḥ, vyāpārapāṭavatāratamyāpekṣayā kiyatāpi kṣaṇena paroparodha itīyantaṃ kālamuparodhāt prāgabhāvena saha saṃvaset | athotpattikṣaṇa eva vyāpārastathāpyutpadyamānena dhvaṃsena sahakāriṇā bhāvaḥ svopādeyaṃ bandhamādadhīta, tato nivṛttiriti durnivāraḥ sahabhāvaḥ | bandhakṣaṇādhānānapekṣāyāmapi svasantānakṣaṇānantaraṃ nāśanāt kṣaṇamapi sahabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ | etacca kathaṃ cetanāvataḥ soḍhuṃ śakyamekasminneva kṣaṇe bhāvasya bhāvābhāvāviti ?
[118,1]
api ca sahānavasthānasvīkārāt kṛśānunā śītamiva dhvaṃsamaparamutpādayatā dhvaṃsenāpi nipādi nivartanīyamiti, tenāpi dhvaṃsamaparamutpādayatā pratiyogī pratihantavya ityanavasthānāt puruṣāyuṣaśatenāpi na kasyacidabhāvavyavahāraḥ syāt | atha dvitīyo virodhaḥ, tadā yatra bhāvastatrābhāvasyāvakāśa eva nāsti | ayameva hi lākṣaṇikavirodhasya svabhāvo yadviruddhayordharmayoranyatarādhiṣṭhite dharmiṇi netarasyāvakāśa iti anutpattireva dhvaṃsasya | atha hetusāmarthyāt kathamabhūtvā āsituṃ śaknotītyavaśyaṃ bhāvyaṃ dhvaṃseneti cet — na, pramāṇabādhite'rthe hetusāmarthyakalpanānupapatteratiprasaṅgāt |
yāvat khalu bhāvasya śvāsaḥ calati na tāvadabhāvagandhaḥ | anyathā viruddhābhimatayoḥ dharmayorekatra dharmiṇi kṣaṇamapi saṃbhave kva parasparaparihāravirodhaḥ ? tathā hi hetubalādbhavatu nāma, sahabhāvastu vastunyekatra bhāvābhāvayorduṣpariharaḥ | sa hi bhāvaḥ pūrvavyavasthito, na bhavanaprayāsakhinno yannivarteta | mudgarādeśca dhvaṃsa eva vyāpāraḥ |
ubhayatra vyāpāre'pi kimaṅga dhvaṃsena ? nāpi dhvaṃsenaiva nivartanīyaḥ, tasyodayāt pūrvamavyāpārāt | tato bhāvasya sthitirabhāvasyotpattiriti siddhaḥ sahabhāvaḥ, gireriva keśariṇotpadyamānena |
[118,2]
paścāttarhi varhiṣevendhanadhvaṃsena nirākariṣyate tāvaditi cet ? bhāvābhāvayoḥ sahabhāvaprasaṅgadūṣaṇādavibhyadabhyastadurnītiruttaraṃ kila vilapati | paścād vidhvaṃsena bhāvo nirākariṣyate na vā, bhāvābhāvayostu sahabhāvaḥ prasakta ityeva pakṣakṣatirāyātā |
kimaparagaveṣaṇena ? yadi ca vyavasthito bhāvastena dhvaṃsena dhvaṃsanīyaḥ, tadā vyaktamayaṃ sahānavasthānavirodhavyāpāra iti prakṛtakṣatiḥ | parasparaparihāravirodho hi vicārayitumupakrāntaḥ | tataḥ prakaraṇavismaraṇād vyutthāpayatyadyāpi parasparaparihāravirodhābhimataḥ, tadā na vyavasthitāpanayanavyāpāraḥ spraṣṭavya iti drādhīyānasahabhāvaḥ |
saṃprati svahetubalāvalambinoḥ kalasanāśayorupanatau bhāvābhāvau caikatra dharmiṇi dhīyete ciramiti paryavasitaṃ virodhakathayā |
[119,1]
atha dhvaṃsena svodayāt prāgeva bhāvo nirbadhyamāno nivartate pravartate cānantaraṃ dhvaṃsa iti noktadoṣaḥ | na caiṣa vyāpāraḥ sahānabasthānasyeti cet ? na śakyamevam |
vyavasthite hi vastuni,
[119,2]
paścātpravartamāno'pi dhvaṃsātmā tasya kiṅkaraḥ | apravṛtteyatastvasmin vastveva balavattaram ||
[119,3]
vyāpārastu yathā naiṣa sahānavasthānasya tathā parasparaparihārasyāpīti niveditametat | nāpi bhaviṣyataḥ kācicchaktiḥ | svayameva tarhi nivartatām ? evaṃ sati kimatrānyena dhvaṃsena mudgareṇa vā ? tatsannidhānāpekṣāyāṃ ca svayaṃśabdārtho riktaḥ |
yathā bījamapekṣya svayameva jāyate'ṅkura iti na tāvatā tatprayuktatvaparihāraḥ | atha parihāra eva, tadā tadapekṣyeti na vaktavyam | tāvatā ca siddhaṃ sādhyamityanena kimiha kartavyam ? dhvaṃsamudgarādikamanapekṣya svayameva bhāvo nitratata iti prāgapi nivṛttisiddhiḥ | vastumātrānubandhī ca dhvaṃso nibandhanāntaranirapekṣa iti, sahasthānābhāvo yadi tava virodho'rthavipadoḥ sahasthānāsaṅgaṃ kṣaṇamapi yathā śītaśikhinoḥ | sahadhvaṃso dhvaṃsāntaramupanayan saṃprati bhaved virodhī so'pyanyaṃ kṣayamiti na nāśaḥ kathamapi || athānyonyābhāvaprakṛtikatayā'rthe sati tadā kṣayasyaivābhāvaḥ saha bhavatu vā hetubalataḥ | anena dhvaṃsena prakṛtihatirasya tvanudaye balīyānevārthaḥ svayamapacaye'nyena kimiha ||
iti saṃgrahaślokau ||
[120,1]
etena yat śaṅkarasyābhavanotpattividhānena kathaṃ bhāvasya niṣedha iti cet ?
abhavanotpattereva saha sthitivirodhena bhāvapratiṣedharūpatvādityevaṃ prakāramabhidhānam, tadvirodhabodhavaidhuryādiyuktamiti darśitam | ata evābhāvotpattividhānena ca bhāvasya tādavasthyaprasaṅga iti pramattabhāṣitamityabhidadhānaḥ sphuṭamayaṃ tapasvī prativātakṣiptabhasmanātmānameva cchurayatīti mahāmohamagnatayā kṛpāpātraṃ mahatāmavagantavyaḥ |
yadyevaṃ bhavatāmapyabhāvo vyavahriyate sa kiṃsvabhāvo yadi na vastu bhāvena vā satyaṃ na virudhyata evāyam ? kathaṃ vā virodhadvayavyavasthā ? ko vāsya hetuḥ ? kādācitkatve akādācitkatve ca bhāvasya samakālaṃ kathaṃ na vyavahriyate ? kathaṃ vā prāgiva paścādapi na kṣaṇaparamparāprasavaḥ ? prasave ca na sahaḥ sahānavasthānavirodhaḥ |
[120,2]
parasparaparihāro'pi bhāvābhāvayorabhāvasyāvastutvenāvāstavaḥ prāpta iti cet ?
yata evaṃ paramataṃ vicārakṣamam,
[120,3]
tasmātpracyutimātrakaṃ vyavahṛteḥ pātraṃ prasajyāhvayaṃ bhūyo'rthasya virudhyate na tu janistasyeti kiṃ hetunā | rodhādeva sakṛnna tadvyavahṛtirhetukṣayānnodayo rodhastāttvika eva tāttvikamithaḥ svābhāvyabhaṅgasthiteḥ ||
[120,4]
bhāvapracyutimātraṃ prasajyapratiṣedhasaṃjñakamiti svarūpanirdeśaḥ | tatra pratiṣedhe pratiṣedhameva vastvicchantīti pracyutimātramuktam | pracyutirnāma kiṃsvit tṛtīyo bhāvaniṣedha iti śaṅkāyāṃ prasajyāhvayamityuktam, tacca tathā vyavahāramātraviṣayo na punaranubhavaviṣayaḥ anyathā vastveva syāt |
[120,5]
na ca yat kiñcid vyavahriyate vikalpabuddhyā tāvad vastu, kharaśṛṅgāderapi vastutvaprasaṅgāt, nirvastukavikalpavyavasthānupapatteśca | taccābhāvasya bhūtyā dharmeṇa virudhyata eveti dvitīyapraśnavisarjanam | bhūtiśca sattārthasāmarthyaṃ, svarūpeṇāvasthānaṃ vā ? ubhayathāpyanyonyapratyanīkarūpatayā pracyutimātreṇa virudhyata iti parasparaparihārasthitilakṣaṇavirodhavyavasthoktā |
[121,1]
nanu pracyutimātraṃ na kiñcit, tacca kathaṃ kenacid birudhyate ? yata eva pracyutimātraṃ na kiñcit, bhāvastu nañarthapratyanīkastata eva virudhyate |
virodho'pyeṣa nānyonyapratighātaḥ, sattānavasthānavat, kiṃ tvanyonyarūpānanupraveśamātram | tacca vikalpitānubhūtayorapyastīti na doṣaḥ | pracyutimātrasya ca kadācid bhāvatvābhāvāt kiṃ hetuneti caturthe visarjanam | kenacid rūpeṇonmajjato hi janakaḥ kalpyeta, akādācitkaṃ ca sarvadāsti vā nāsti vā ? tatrāstipakṣakṣepāt sarvadā nāstyeva tat | vyavahārastu kādācitkaḥ, bhāvakāle tadapravṛtteḥ | kathaṃ virodhādeva ?
bhāvavirodho hyabhāvaḥ pracyutisvabhāvaḥ kalpanāviparivartī kathaṃ bhāvakāle vyavahriyate ?
bhavanadharmā hi nirhetuko vā, bhavanahetujanito vā, hetvantarakṛto vā bhāvakāle'pi bhavennāma, bhāvānvayaṃ ca vyavahāramasyāsādayet | yadā tu nāsya bhāvo na tadā bhāvānuyāyī vyavahāraḥ | vāsanānugastu virodho niścayavato vastudarśane vāsanāprabodhavaidhuryāt kathaṃ pravarteta ?
[121,2]
ataeva yāvatsa eva vastvātmāstīti vyavasāyaḥ, tāvadanavakāśa evābhāvavyavahāraḥ, kṣaṇabhaṅgabhāve'pi tattvataḥ | yadā tu pramāṇabalādekakṣaṇasthitadharmaiva bhāvasvabhāva ityavadhārayati tadā dvitīye kṣaṇe tadvastūpādeyakṣaṇasamakālaṃ tadabhāvaṃ vyavaharati | tatpramāṇālābhe tu karparādivikāradarśanamapekṣyaivābhāvavyavahārā iti pañcame visarjanam | ṣaṣṭhe'pi hetukṣayānnodayaḥ sajātīyakṣaṇadhārāyā iti |
[121,3]
etaduktaṃ svarasanirodheṣu pūrvapūrvakṣaṇeṣu mudgarasahakāriṇā kṣaṇena sāmagrīvaisadṛśyād bandhyakṣaṇasyotpādanādupādānaṃ kṣīṇamiti nāparasyotpattiḥ | yatkṛte ca kasyacid bandhyakṣaṇādhāne sajātīyakṣaṇāntarāpratisandhānam, so'pi bhāvastasya bhāvasya virodhī siddha iti sahānavasthānavirodhavyavasthā | tenaiva saptame'pi caturthapādena yadi nāma vastvavastunoḥ parasparaparihāro virodhaḥ tathāpi na tāttvikatvahāniḥ |
na hi tayoḥ kadācit svabhāvasāṅkaryamasti | etāvāneva dharmavirodhasyārthaḥ | ataeva sthitigrahaṇaṃ niyamasūcanaparam | etena tṛtīyo'pi vikalpo nirastaḥ | tasmānnāśo nāma na prasajyātmā kartavyarūpo yato hetusāpekṣaḥ syāt, nāpyetāvanti dūṣaṇānīti sthitam ||
[122,1]
kiṃ cārthasya vinaśvaretaratayoḥ kiṃ nāśane kāraṇaiḥ
[122,2]
svayaṃ vinaśvarasvabhāvasyotpattau vaiyarthyamanarthahetūnām, avinaśvarasvabhāvatve tvasāmarthyam |
[122,3]
evaṃ tarhi bhaviṣṇutetaratayoḥ kiṃ kāraṇairjanmani |
[122,4]
śakyaṃ hi vaktumarthasya bhaviṣṇutāyāṃ vyarthā janmahetavaḥ, abhaviṣṇutāyāmasamarthā iti |
[122,5]
tathā ca nyāyabhūṣaṇakāraḥ — tanna, hetuvādocchedaprasaṅgāt, vikalpasya sarvatra saṃbhavāt | tathā hi hetutaḥ kiṃ bhavanasvabhāvo bhavatvāhosvit abhavanasvabhāva iti ? yadyādyaḥ pakṣastadā svayameva bhavati, tatsvabhāvatvāditi vyartho hetuḥ | dvitīyapakṣe tvasamartho na hyabhavanasvabhāvaṃ śaśaviṣāṇādi kenacidutpādayituṃ śakyam | tathā cchedadāhādihetavo'pi tatsvabhāvatvāt tatsvabhāvatvātatsvabhāvatvapakṣayoḥ vaiyarthyāsāmarthyābhyāmanupapannā draṣṭavyāḥ | tathā caivaṃ hetuṣu sarvahetupratikṣepasaṃbhavānmokṣādau prayāsaḥ śāstraśravaṇād vyartha iti, atrāyaṃ paryanuyujyate — kimanena mūle paraśunipātaprakāreṇa ? sarvathā kvacidapi hetutayopanīte'sāmarthyavaiyarthyalakṣaṇaṃ dūṣaṇameva na vācyamityucyate | tattāvadayuktam, dṛśyate hi nakhacchedye kuṭhāravaiyarthyam, kuṭhāracchedye ca nakhasyāsāmarthyam | tathā devadattenaiva yat sādhyaṃ tatra devadattasahāyasya yajñadattasya vyāpāravaiyarthyam | tadvinākṛtasya punarasāmarthyam | dahanendhanasāmagryāṃ satyāṃ rāsabhasya dhūme vaiyarthyamasatyāmasāmarthyam | yatra vā siddhasādhanapoṣaṇaṃ tatra vaiyarthyam | asiddhaviruddhānaikāntikeṣvanyatamasattve asāmarthyamiti | ye tu siddhasādhanasyāpyeteṣvantarbhāvamicchanti, tatprayāsaphalaṃ na kiñcit, vaiyarthyasya hetudūṣaṇasya sarvathāśakyāpahnavatvāt, jñāpakahetorapi pratītiṃ prati kārakatvācca | yadi cāsāmarthyavaiyarthyamadūṣaṇaṃ hetoranyadūṣaṇābhāvāt sarvasya sarvasiddhiryataḥ kutaścit |
[123,1]
atha tatsvabhāvātatsvabhāvavikalpadvārakaṃ dūṣaṇamasadityucyate, tadapyasat |
pradīpe hi yo hetuḥ prakāśakaraṇe'ndhakārakāraṇe vā upanīyate, sa kiṃ vaiyarthyāsāmarthyābhyāṃ na nigṛhyate ?
[123,2]
yat punarayamevāha, prakāśādidṛṣṭānto'pyayuktaḥ | tathā hi na tāvadasmanmate pradīpaprakāśādīnāmekatvaṃ siddham, nāpyekahetutvam | dravyotpattyanantaraṃ hi sāmagryantarataḥ prakāśādayo guṇā utpadyanta iti naḥ siddhānta iti | tadapyasambaddham | yataḥ yadyapi dravyotpattyanantaraṃ prakāśo guṇa utpannaḥ, tathāpi tadeva dravyamutpannaṃ na tadrūpaniṣpattau hetvantaramapekṣate, paścād vā prakāśo guṇo na prakāśaguṇarūpatve iti na dṛṣṭāntakṣatiḥ |
[123,3]
atha dravyarūpamapi dravyatvasāmānyāt tatsamavāyāt pūrvaṃ na dravyaṃ nādravyamiti cet ? tat tarhi dravyarūpaṃ dravyatvasāmānyāt jñāyate, atha dravyamiti vikalpavacasorvā gocarībhavatīti pakṣaḥ | prathamapakṣe tāvanna doṣaḥ | sāmānyādeva dravyaṃ jāyatāṃ yataḥ kutaścid yenātmanā jātaṃ na punastadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣata iti hi prakṛtam | dvitīyapakṣe'pi sutarāṃ na doṣaḥ, dravyarūpaṃ hi jātameva prāgapi dravyadhīdhvaniprasava eva sāmānyāt, na caitāvatā tadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣitaṃ bhavati | na hi kāryeṇa kāraṇasya svaviṣayasāmarthyavyavahāre prāganiṣpannameva tatsāmarthyaṃ tadbhāve vā kāraṇam, tadeva kāryaṃ hetvantaramapekṣitavat |
[123,4]
kiṃ ca, bhinnena paścāt jāyamānenāpi prakāśaguṇena yadā tāvat prakāśaguṇayuktaḥ saṃpanno dīpaḥ, tadā kiṃ punastadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣate yato dṛṣṭāntakṣatiḥ syāt ? tanna prakriyāpoṣaṇatrāṇamapramāṇaparāyaṇena | anubhavānurodhena tu yathābhimatameva dṛṣṭāntaḥ |
na hi prathamadvitīyakṣaṇayoḥ sāmānyayogāyogābhyāṃ viśeṣapratītirasti | nāpi dravyasāmānyayorbhedānubhava iti prakṛtasya tvanyathāpi siddhernātra nirbandhaḥ | tasmānna prakāśaḥ svahetoḥ prakāśarūpaniṣpannastadbhāve hetvantaramapekṣate, vaiyarthyāt | andhakārīkaraṇe'pyasāmarthyāditi siddham |
[124,1]
nanu śulkamambaraṃ rāgadravyayogena raktīkriyamāṇamupalabdham, tatra raktasvabhāvāsvabhāvatve vastrasya vaiyarthyāsāmarthye codyaṃ rāgadravyasya kiṃ nopakramyata iti cet ? na khalvasya vikalpasya sarvatrāvatāro vivakṣitaḥ, kiṃ tu tatsvabhāvātatsvabhāvavikalpadvārakamapi dūṣaṇaṃ hetorasti tāvadityatyantāyoganiṣedha upakrāntaḥ | tato yatraitaddūṣaṇamupapādayituṃ śakyate, tatra dūṣaṇabhāvamāviśati | kimanyacintayā yadi yuktibhedaḥ ?
tathā ca vinaśvaratvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikatvaṃ kanīyaḥkālatvaṃ vā ? avinaśvaratvamapi drādhīyasā kālena sadāsthāyitayā vā ? sarvathā yāvatkālāvasthitiko bhāvaḥ svahetorudapādi tadabhyantare yadi kenacinnāśyeta, tadā yāvatkālāvasthitireva notpannaḥ | na hi saṃvatsarasthāyī cāsau divasanāśī ceti svabhāvadvayaṃ parasparaviruddhamasya sādhu |
[124,2]
nanu vināśakāraṇamantareṇa saṃvatsarasthāyī, avāntaraṃ tu vināśakāraṇasamavadhāne'vāntaranāśīti ko virodhaḥ ? virodha eva niścaye hi yadyarthānupraveśo na svabhāve, yathā yadyatra patrapāte dhūmaḥ saṃbhavenniyatamiyamaṅgārā, anyathā tu guñjāpuñja iti na svabhāvabhedaḥ | tathā yadi divase vinaśyati tadavadhikameva hetunā janitam, saṃvatsaranāśe tu tadavadhikamiti bhavatu | na tu parasparavirodhisvarūpe dvitīyasyaikatra samuccayaḥ | na hi tatrāhani vinaśyanneva saṃvatsarasthāyī, ardhārdhena vā tadubhayaṃ bhavitumarhati | vikalpastu saṃśayātmā jñānasyaiva, na vastuno dharmaḥ | tasmād vastvekasvabhāvameva na viruddhasvabhāvāntarayogi | etacca divasādisthāyitvaṃ pramāṇena nirūpaṇamarhati satyaṃ na veti | abhyupagamya tu cintitametat, pramāṇavyāhate hetusāmarthyāśrayaṇasya durlabhatvāt | tato yadyakṣaṇikatāpi tathāpi yāvānasya kālaḥ sthiteravadhistadabhyantare hetvantarasyāsāmarthyaṃ tasya purastādvaiyarthyamiti sthitam | kṣaṇikatve'pi na tatkṣaṇe nāśakāraṇena kiñcit śakyamiti vyaktam, kṣaṇāntare tu svayameva nāstīti nārtho'narthahetunā | sadātane tvasamartha evāyam |
[124,3]
tasmād vināśe kartavye na kaścit heturasāmarthyavaiyarthyadūṣaṇamatikrāmati |
yadārthāntare tu karparādau sa eva mudgarastābhyāṃ dūṣaṇābhyāṃ na lipyate, tadvyāpārānantarameva janmalābhāt karparasya, evaṃ rāgadravyasyāpi tadvyāpārāntaramudayabhāji raktavāsasi na sāmarthyavaiyarthyam | pāṇḍucaṇḍātakanivartane punaḥ kastannivartayati ?
yadāpi daśādvaye ekameva vastravastu tadāpi taddoṣānativṛttireva | na hi raktāvasthāyāmapi śubhrameva taditi nirvahati | tato yadi tadāpi śubhrameva tadvastu na raktatāyā avakāśa ityasamarthaṃ rāgadravyaṃ, pūrvarakte tu tanmātrarāgāpekṣāyāṃ vyartham | tasmāt sthairyāpekṣayā doṣāvatārāt samayāparādha evaṃvidho na vastunaḥ | pūrvasya svarasanirodhe tadupādānāpekṣayā rāgadravyeṇāpūrvaraktavastrotpādane taddoṣasya parihārasiddheḥ | naivaṃ vastusthitiriti cet ? nanu tadeva cintyate kīdṛśī vastusthitiriti | kimatra kośapānena paraḥ pratyāyanīyaḥ ? tat kimakāṇḍenaivaṃ vastusthitiriti ucyate, pratyabhijñāprāmāṇyāvalambanasya nirastatvāt ?
[125,1]
nanu samayāparādho'pi kathamabhidhīyate, vyavasthite dharmiṇi guṇadvayasya tirobhāvāvirbhāvasvīkārāt ? yadyevaṃ tadā prācīnaguṇanirākaraṇe'sāmarthyavaiyarthyaprāptāvapyapūrvaraktatāguṇotpādanenaiva caritārtho rāgadravyavyāpāra iti kathamuktadūṣaṇasparśaḥ ? pūrvaniṣpannarūpāpekṣayā hi vaiyarthyāsāmarthyacintā prakrāntā, nāpūrvāpekṣayā |
na hyapūrve'pi kartavye yadyevaṃ rūpaṃ svahetorjātaṃ tadā vaiyarthyam, evaṃ jāte tvasāmarthyamiti nirṇayāvakāśaḥ | nāśanīyaśca sarvaḥ pūrvasiddha eva bhāvaḥ | sa ca vinaśvaretarayoḥ, prakārāntaratiraskārādanyatarasvarūpamanativartamāno na vināśahetoḥ kalpitasyāsāmarthyamānarthakyaṃ vā sthātuṃ prabhavati | na caivaṃ hetuvādocchedaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ |
asiddhe hi kārye hetorāśrayaṇam, siddhe ceyaṃ cintā | tadaiva ca yadi hetorevaṃrūpo niṣpanna iti hetupuraskāreṇaiva vādapravṛtteḥ | na caivamasiddhe śakyamityuktam | tatkathaṃ prakṛtāsmadvikalpasya sarvatra saṃbhavaḥ ? vikalpamātrasya sarvatra hetuphalasaṃmate saṃbhave'pi nāsmadīyayukteraparādhabodhaḥ kṛto bhavati |
[125,2]
yadi tu siddhe'pi vastuni vyāpakasvabhāvadvaye'sāmarthyavaiyarthyāvatāre'pi hetvantaramapekṣamāṇamupadarśayituṃ śakyate syādaparādhaḥ | na caivam | tasmādvikalpamātrasyāparādhe'pi nāparādhaḥ saviśeṣaṇasya, anupalambhavaditi vyarthaḥ tanmātropanyāsaḥ |
[126,1]
athānupalambhamātrasya svasādhyasādhanasāmarthyaśūnyataivāparādhaḥ, vikalpamātrasya punarasāmarthyavaiyarthyollekhaśekharasya na hetuvādāpavādaśaktiśūnyateti viṣama upanyāsaḥ | aho puruṣakāro bhasmabhūṣaṇasya ! evaṃ hi sarvathā hetuphalāpalāpe sādhu sādhitaṃ dhvaṃsasya hetumattvamiti vyaktamayamātmānamātmanaiva viḍambayati | tadayaṃ bhavanasvabhāvādivikalpaḥ saṃkalpaniveśitaśaktirapi viṣaye ca parihāryaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvavyavasthitena, anyathā mūlocchedāt prakaraṇapravṛtteḥ | siddhopādhistu vikalpo vināśakaraṇameva kavalayati, na kāraṇamātram | atiprasaṅgabhaṅgabhīruṇā tu bhavatā nādriyate iti yuktamevaitat | tasmāt hantu hetuphale śramo'yamaphalaḥ saṃsthāpya sāmānyatastattvaṃ kvāpi vimarśa evaviṣaye prārambhasaṃbhāvitaḥ ||
prārambha upakramaḥ prastāvaḥ tena saṃbhāvita ādṛtaḥ | sāmānyena kāryakāraṇabhāvasattāṃ vyavasthāpya vināśādau viṣayaviśeṣe kvaciddhetusattā kimastu navetyatra vimarśa eṣo'smadīyaḥ prastāvānurūpaḥ | hetuphalonmūlanāya tu viphalaḥ prayāsaḥ, sāmānyena vyavasthāpyaiva prakaraṇapravṛtteḥ | na cāyaṃ vikalpaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvakṣepāya kṣamaḥ bhavanasvabhāvo'bhavanasvabhāvo vā hetuto bhavatīti | tathā hi abhavanadharmā tāvad bandhyā prasūtīti bhavanasvabhāvaśca, tvanmatena gaganāderabhavanasya kadācidapyabhāvāt, tayostāvadasāmarthyavaiyarthyagrasto bhavati hetuvyāpāraḥ | kādācitkaṃ bhāvaṃ bhavanadharmāṇamabhavanadharmakaṃ vā brūhi, na punarayaṃ kiñcidanapekṣamāṇaḥ kādācitka eva bhavitumarhati, yaścāpekṣo'rthaḥ kāladeśasvabhāvaniyamāya sa eva hetuḥ | atha bhavanasvabhāva iti na sattādharmā kiṃ tu utpattidharmeti vivakṣitam, tadāpyutpattirityasata ātmalābho na kādācitkatvādanya iti tadvadevottaram | vināśasya tu kādācitkatvaniṣedha uktaḥ |
[126,2]
atha hetuto bhavanadharmā yaḥ sa kiṃ bhavatītaro veti vikalpārthaḥ ? tadā ādyavikalpa eva viśrānto vādaḥ | tathā hi hetuto bhavati, na pūrvamiti na vaiyarthyam, bhavati hetuto nānyato bhavatīti kuto'sāmarthyam ? atra ca nirbandho bandhya iti diṅmātramabhidhīyate, ubhayoḥ siddhatvāt hetuphalabhāvasya aprastutatvācca | yataścāyaṃ siddhopādhiko vikalpaḥ sannāśasyaiva hetorbādhako nāsadutpādakasya, asamānatvāt nyāyasya yathoktaṃ prāk | tataśchedadāhādihetavo raktadukūlakāraṇavadupapannā eva, mokṣākhyadaśāviśeṣahetuśceti saphala eva tatra prayāsaḥ | tasmānna sato nāśahetuḥ kaścit | svahetuta eva tāvaddeśākāravat kālatayāpi niṣpattiḥ ||
[127,1]
kiṃ ca,
[127,2]
dhvaṃso vāstu vidherbalātparighavad yad vā yathā śarkarā bhāvo'sau tadavastha eva tu na yatkiñcitkarāstasya te | vyāpārāviratistataḥ kṣaṇinaye dattvādabandhyaṃ kathaṃ deśākāravadasya hetuniyataḥ kālo'pi yasmānmataḥ ||
[127,3]
