yathā hi mudgaraḥ śarkarānikaro vā yastasmātsyānmataḥ, nāśahetoranupapatteḥ notpattirnāśasyetyuktam | astu vā nāśābhidhānamarthāntaraṃ kāraṇabalāt | daṇḍavat śarkarāraktatānāśe'pi koṣāntarakamadhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhatu, santu bhāvāstadavasthā eva, na hi te tasya kiñcitkarāḥ | yathā hi mudgaraḥ śarkarānikaro vā tasyākiñcitkaraḥ, anyathā nāśābhyupagamaverthyaprasaṅgāt, tathā nāśo'pi sthitimati bhāve svakāraṇādutpadyamānastasya kimaṅga kartumasamarthaḥ ? yathā hi tasya hetubalabhāvino na sarvathā nāśaḥ śakyo vā sāmarthyavaiyarthyābhyām, tathānurūpāṃśe nāśo'pyaśakya eva | tatrāpi svabhāvabhede pūrvavannaśvaretaravikalpasyāvatāravāraṇābhāvāt, niraṃśe'pi ca vastuni kalpanānurodhādetaducyate | tattvatastvaṃśanāśane'pi sarvathā nāśa eva, sa cāśakya iti sādhitam apūrvanirvartanam | vastunastu vāryate | tataḥ yo'pyapūrvaḥ pūrvavat koṣāntaratirohitaḥ kalpamāstāṃ tatkṛto vā punaraparo nāśābhidhāno'rthastadvadastu | na tu bhāvasya kiñciditi svajñānajananajaladhāraṇādivyāpārānuparamaprasaṅgo durnivāraḥ |
[128,1]
etena yadavocad vācaspatiḥ, nanvasminnutpanne'pi bhinnamūrtau kimāyātaṃ bhāvasya ?
na kiñcidāyātam, astvayamāyuṣmān bhāvaḥ | svakāraṇādhīnajanmanā tadabhāvena tatsvarūpavirahalakṣaṇena svalakṣaṇaśālinārthānurūpavyavahāraṃ pravartayatā nirastasamastārthakriyā kiṃ naśchinnamiti, tadapahastitam, samastārthakriyānirasanasyaiva tadavasthe tasminnaśakyasādhanatvāt |
[128,2]
tadabhāvenaiva tādavasthyakhaṇḍanamiti cet ? nanu bhāve tāvat tadavastha eva svakāraṇaprabhāvādabhāvo jātastato vyāvṛttya tatkhaṇḍanamanena kartavyamiti samasamayatāprasaṅgaḥ prācīno duṣpariharaḥ | tathā ca sati tatsvarūpavirahalakṣaṇenetyanupapannam, na hi tadviraharūpatve tatkālasaṃbhavo nāma | tato mudgarādipadārthāntarasādhāraṇasya abhāvasaṃjñākaraṇe nābhimatasvalakṣaṇaśālitābhivyaktisiddhiḥ, yataḥ tadanurūpavyavahārapravartanamabhidhīyamānaṃ śobheta | tena ca svarūpasyārthakriyāyāṃ tādavasthyasya cākhaṇḍanamiti parasparākarṣī nāśāntarakaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ |
[128,3]
svayaṃnivṛttirūpatayā na nāśāntarāvakāśa iti cet — na, samānakālasaṃbhavāt nivṛttirūpatāyāḥ pratikṣiptatvāt, padārthāntaravat paryudastameva rūpamavaśiṣyate | tena ca vināśena niyataṃ parabhūtavināśākhyavastukaraṇaṃ mudgareṇeva, ko hi viśeṣo'sya tatparyudastarūpatvena mudgarāt, yadayaṃ paramanapekṣamāṇa eva nāśayati ? mudgarastvenamanapekṣamāṇo nāśa iti syāt | vināśasaṃjñākaraṇapratilambhastu bhavet | tāmantareṇa tasyāpi mudgarādaviśeṣāt, ākārabhedamātrasya maṇimantrādiṣvapi bhāvāt |
[128,4]
yadi tu pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ śaktisādhanamekaniyataṃ bhaved, bhaved viśeṣaḥ |
tacca nāstīti pratipāditam ||
[128,5]
tasmāt, prasajyapakṣe'sti na tulyakālatā na paryudāse paranāśavarjanam | sthite'nyadanyatrabhavad bhavet sakṛnniyogato'nyakṣaṇatānurodhini ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ | sthite'pi hetau bhavadekadā na cet prayojanaṃ tatkṣaṇabhaṅgasaṃbhavāt | sthitena kiṃ vyomni samakṣaṇaṃ phalaṃ phalena nāśo'pi yathaiva lakṣayet || ityantaraślokaḥ |
[129,1]
yadi tu nāśākhyaṃ kāryaṃ na tasya nivartakaṃ kiṃ tvanyadeva daṇḍādi, tadā bhāvaśca nivartate, abhāvaśca pravartata iti bhavati kālabhedaḥ, kiṃ tu nopayogo nāśasya | nāpi tadabhāvena nirastasamastārthakriya iti vācyam | asāmarthyavaiyarthyaṃ ca prastutam | tato'pi rikteyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ |
[129,2]
yatpunaratra tenotprekṣitam — yathoktaṃ svahetuto bhāvo naśvaro'naśvaro vā jāyate iti, tatrocyate — na vayaṃ vinaśvaramavinaśvaraṃ vā jānīmaḥ, kiṃ tu santaḥ svahetubhyo jāyante, dhvaṃsante ca hetvantarebhyaḥ svapratyayādhīnasannidhānebhyaḥ, dhvaṃsaśca dhvaṃsamānādbhinno hetubhedataḥ svabhāvabhedācceti, tatrāpyucyate — yadi naśvarānaśvarasvarūpamavidvāneva bhavānevamāha, tadā kva nāśo nāma padārthaḥ ? kuto vā vyāvṛttyā bhavati vyavasthāpyo yo dhvaṃsamānād bhinnaḥ saṃpratyeva pratijñātaḥ, sa idānīṃ vinaśvarāvinaśvarasvarūpāparijñānena vyavasthāpyamāna ākāśādiṣvapi kiṃ na vyavasthāpyate ? teṣu nāśādarśanāditi cet ?
nanvanyatrāpi nāśo nāma dṛśyata iti śapathagamyametat | tato vinaśvaretarasvabhāvāviṣkaraṇaṃ bhavataḥ prasahyāyātaṃ kimatra śapathena ? tathā ca sati svahetoreva tadatadrūpajanmani niyatāvatāramasāmarthyavaiyarthyadūṣaṇaṃ paśyato'pi tatra hetvantarapratijñānaṃ kathamiti vayamapi na jānīmaḥ | athedamākūtaṃ vaidarbhyagarbhayā girā pratyakṣata eva kutaścidutpādaḥ kutaścinnāśa upalabhyamāno vinaśvaretaravikalpena kathamapohituṃ śakyaḥ ? na hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ vikalpaśatenāpi śātayituṃ śakyam, sarvapramāṇavyāpārasya pratyakṣa eva viśrāmāditi ||
[130,1]
tatrāpi nāśa iti yadi padārthāntaraṃ svasamayaprasiddhamucyate, yo mudgarādijanmā ghaṭādipadārthamarthaḥ kadarthayati, tasya janmavyāpārau pratyakṣagocarāviti mahatsāhasamityupapāditaṃ prāk | tat kathaṃ na vikalpāvakāśaḥ ?
[130,2]
atha naśyataḥ svayameva rūpaṃ bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇa tanmātrajijñāsāyāṃ pṛthagivādarśyamāno nāśo'bhipretaḥ, tathā ca dhvaṃsante hetvantarebhyaḥ ityabhītvaivoktam | evaṃ tarhi daṇḍādibhyaḥ kuṇḍādayo vinaśyanti, na svayamiti siddhāntaniṣṭhāyāṃ dhvaṃsaśca nirastasamastārthakriya ityapi suptavilapitameva | tat kimanayā vācaspatiḥ abhipraitīti na vidmaḥ | evaṃ tarhi yāvati pratyakṣavyāpāraḥ tāvato'pi kathamapahnavaḥ ?
kiyati cāsau pratyakṣavyāpāraḥ ? utpadyamāne ca hetvantarāddhetvantarānnirudhyamāne ca bhāvetadutpattihetorvināśaheturanya iti siddham |
[130,3]
na ca nāśo nāmānyo yataḥ pratyakṣagocaracodyāvakāśa iti | dhigetat ! vināśasya bhāvādananyatve taddhetūrbhāvahetureva, bhāvahetureva, na bhāvotpattihetuḥ |
tatkathamutpattihetoranyo vināśahetuḥ ? kathaṃ ca pūrvaniṣpannasya paścāttano hettuḥ ? pūrvaparabhāvaścāyamadhyakṣasiddha eva |
[130,4]
kiṃ cotpadyamānaṃ nirudhyamānaṃ ca vastvekamanekaṃ vā ? ekatvaṃ tāvadviruddhadharmādhyāsādayuktam | atha pratyakṣeṇa tathā vyavasthānāt kiṃ kurmaṃ iti cet ? ekapratyakṣeṇa ekadaikādhārayorupalabdhau sādhuravirodhaḥ, nīlacaturasratāvat | yadā tu bhinnakālamadhyakṣadvayamekaikarūpagrāhi, tadā pratyabhijñānamātrameva miśrayati | taccāpramāṇamityuktam |
tato viddhadharmādhyāsād bheda eva | ekatra tu kṣaṇe vibhāgābhāvānna virodho vyāvṛttibhedamātreṇaikatra bhāvāt | tathā hi sa eva bhāvakṣaṇaḥ prāgabhāvādutpadyamāna ucyate, paścādbhāvānnirudhyamāna ucyate | kṣaṇaparamparāvyāpinyapi vastunyevamastīti cet — na, vyāpakadvāreṇa virodhasyaiva siddheḥ | prathamakṣaṇe'pyutpadyamāno bhāvo vā bhāvikṣaṇāntarāvasthānena vyāpto na prācīnāvasthitiṃ kṣaṇamapi spṛśati, nirudhyamānaścāsau caramakṣaṇe prācyakṣaṇāntarāvasthānena vyāpto, na ca bhāvinīmavasthitiṃ kṣaṇamapi spṛśatīti virodha eva | kṣaṇe punarekasminneṣa vibhāga iti vyāvṛttimātrabhedo na virodhaḥ | tasmāt kṣaṇadvayamapi sthitivivakṣāyāmudayanidhanadharmayorvirodhānnaikatvam |
anekatvapakṣe ca prācīnaṃ vastu mudgarādiparigaṇitavināśahetuvyatirekeṇāpi nirudhyamānaṃ svahetoreva niyatakālasthitidānasāmarthyamuddopayatīti na vināśahetuḥ kaścit | athāparigaṇitā eva vināśahetavaḥ, tatra durupalakṣaḥ kaściddheturanirjñāyamānaḥ svanibandhanaṃ nidhanamādadhīteti kimayuktam ? evaṃ tarhi pratikṣaṇamapi vināśasaṃbhāvanāyā na pracyutiriti vyarthaṃ vināśahetuvyavasthāpanam | parigaṇitasya hi bhūyo lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ prasiddhapradhvaṃsalakṣaṇāt prāgabhāvaniścayena vināśavyavasthā mābhūditi sahetukatvaṃ vināśasya sādhayitumārabdham | sūkṣmatayā tu durupalakṣaṇasyāpi hetoḥ svīkāre prayatnavaiyarthyamāyātamityalaṃ mithyāvikalpena | tasmāt sthitimati vastuni sarvasyākiñcitkaratvapratipādanāt santaḥ svahetubhyo jāyante dhvaṃsante ca hetvantarebhya ityarthapadametat | tat kutaḥ idaṃ maṇimantrauṣadhamindrajālaṃ bhāvena śikṣitaṃ yadayamavikalānyadarśanapratyayastadavastha eva kadācidadhyakṣaḥ atyakṣaśceti ?
[131,1]
nanu kṣaṇikanītāvevāyaṃ doṣa ukto yuktaśca | yadāha śaṅkaraḥ — na hi bhāvasya nivṛtterutpattimantareṇa prāgiva paścādapi svarūpahāniḥ, yenāyaṃ tadaivānupalambhaviṣayo na pūrvaṃ hānau vā paścāt saivāsya nivṛtterutpattiriti | tadayuktam, kṣaṇikapakṣe hi prāgiva paścādapi na svarūpahāniriti sāhasametat | nivṛtterutpattimantareṇa svīkriyamāṇā'pi svarūpahānirasaṅgataiveti cet ? nivṛttyādināmnaḥ padārthāntarasyotpattiḥ bhavatu mā vā bhūt, yata evāsau kṣaṇasthitiniyato'rthaḥ, tata eva kṣaṇāntaramavyāpnuvan kṣaṇāntare nāstītyucyate, sa evārtho bhāvasya kṣaṇāntare nāśo jāta ityanena vacasocyate | nāpūrvavastūtpādo vidhīyate | chandato hi vacasāṃ pravṛttiḥ | arthastu nirūpaṇīyaḥ |
tatra yadyekakṣaṇādhīnatayā kṣaṇāntare niyatasattāvasāyasiddhiḥ, tāvataiva caritārtho vināśavādaḥ, kimatra kasyacidutpattiparyeṣaṇayā ? na hi gṛhe eva devadatto'stīti sarvatrānyatra vastvantaramabhidhānanirodhabodhanamiti nyāyaḥ |
[132,1]
tatrāpi pradeśāntare'bhāvavidhirastīti cet ? astu, tadarthameva niyamanibandhananipātaprayogāt | kevalaṃ kiñcid vastu vidyamānamutpadyamānaṃ vā na pratītipathaprasthāyi, niṣedhamātrasyaiva pratīteḥ | tāvataiva ca devadattamanusarataḥ pravṛtinivṛttipāṭavamāpanīpadyate | vastvantarapratītāvapi hi vihitāyāṃ gṛhādanyatra yāvanna niyamānusāreṇa devadattasya prasajyātmānaṃ niṣedhamavasthāpayati tāvanna susthaḥ | tasmādaspṛṣṭavasturūpamabhāvamātramavaśyapratipādyam |
[132,2]
na cānyatra nāstītyanena vasturūpaṃ kiñcid vidhāya tadeva paramasti na devadatta iti kramavatī pratītiranubhavaviṣayaḥ, yathā gṛha evāstītyanena nānyatreti | bhavatu caivam, tathāpi paścādabhāvamātrapratītyaiva viśrāmaḥ | anyathā parāparavasturūpapratipattāveva puruṣāyuṣamupayujyet, na prakṛtaniṣedhabodhasiddhiḥ | tasmād yathātra niṣedhamātraṃ mandirādanyatra devadattasya vyavahriyate, tanmātrameva ca devadattasyānyatrābhāvaḥ pratītigocara ityādi vyavahārasyāpyarthaḥ, tathā ekatraiva kṣaṇe'sti bhāvaḥ, kṣaṇāntare nāsti |
kṣaṇāntare tasyābhāvaḥ pratīyata iti niṣedhamātramanyatra kṣaṇe khyāpyate, na vasturūpasaṃsparśaḥ |
nāpi tadapekṣāniṣedhasiddhaye'pi | evaṃ svarūpahānirityapi niṣedhamātravyavahāra eva |
tatra ca na kasyacidutpattyā sattayā vopayoga iti kathamucyate nivṛtteḥ utpattimantareṇa svarūpahāniriti ? ataeva hānau vā paścāt saivāsya nivṛtterutpattiḥ ityapi pravāhāpātaḥ pātakavatparihāryaḥ | paścāt svarūpahānirityapi hi paścānniṣedhavyavahāramātram, na tu kasyacid vasturūpasyotpattiriti | sa ca niṣedhavyavahāro devadattasyaivānyatra kvacit sattāniyamapratibandhādavyavasthitasaṃvādī |
[132,3]
etena yat nyāyabhūṣaṇo'pyāha, ko hyevaṃ śraddadhīta pratyutpannāvasthāyāmeva san bhāvaḥ paścāttvasan, na ca paścānnaśyatīti ? tatrāpi kaḥ punarevamāha, na paścāt naśyatīti ? yadi paścānnaśyati tadā paścānnāśotpattiḥ svīkṛteti cet ? yadi tvameva vacasāmartheṣu svāmī |
[133,1]
syādetat | dvidhā tvarthasthitiḥ, pramāṇānusāriṇī samayānusāriṇī ca | prathamāyāṃ paścānnaśyatīti paścādasanniti vyavahriyata ityevārthaḥ samarthitaḥ | ataḥ pramāṇaparāyaṇena kathamabhidhātuṃ śakyaṃ paścādasanna ca paścānnaśyatīti | dvitīyāyāṃ tu na virodhaḥ | yasya hi paścānnaśyatīti paścānnāśotpattiriṣṭā taṃ prati paścādasan | na san vyavahartavyo na ca paścānnaśyati | na cāsya paścānnāśavastūtpattiriti kathamaśraddhāviṣayaḥ ? tadapariniṣṭhitārthatattvavacanavibhramamātreṇa grāmyajanamanohareṇa samayanirvāhamanoratha iti kaṣṭam |
[133,2]
tasmāt svahetorekakṣaṇaniyatasthitirudabhūdbhāva ityeva nānyadā san, na tu kasyacidutpattyā hetostu tādṛk sāmarthyaṃ kiṃ saṃbhāvanāviṣaya iti yadi cintayasi, tadāpi yadi janane sāmarthyaṃ tadāvaśyaṃ kenacid rūpeṇa kāryamutpādayan kṣaṇamātrasthāyināpi rūpeṇa kiṃ notpādayet ? sarvaṃ tu rūpamaspṛśan kāryaṃ kuryāddheturiti kasya śraddhāviṣayaḥ ? tato yathāyaṃ bhāvo niyatadeśo niyatavastusaṃsthānādyākāraḥ svahetoreva samutpadyate, tathā niyatakālo'pīti kimasaṃbhāvyamatra ? na ca deśādiniyamena svarūpasaṃkocamabhāva eva bhāvasya bhāvayatīti vācyam | na hyabhāvo bhāvamutpannaṃ vā saṅkocayet | kāraṇena saha saṃbhūya saṅkucitameva cotpādayet | atra pakṣe pṛthak pauruṣarahitaḥ kāraṇasāmagryantarbhūto'bhāvo'pi nāma yadi bhāvasādhakaḥ kaścidupapādayituṃ śakyaḥ, kiṃ naśchinnam ? yādṛśī tādṛśī vā kāraṇasāmagrī kāryaṃ kuryāt | yathā tu niyatadeśākāraṃ kurute tathā niyatakālamapi kartuṃ kastasyāḥ śaktivighāta iti brūmaḥ, yatastadarthamarthyate parotpattiḥ paścāt | prathamapakṣe'pi kiṃ tāvat sa bhāvaḥ svahetorviśvarūpa utpanno niyataḥ kriyate'bhāvena ? na vā kenāpi rūpeṇa niṣpannaḥ kenacid vā niṣpanna eva na tu deśākārakālairiti vikalpāḥ |
[133,3]
antyastāvadayuktaḥ | yena hi rūpeṇa niṣpannaḥ sa eva tasyākāraḥ, sa ca na kvacid bhāvamantareṇa, kvacid bhāvo'pi na kadācidabhavata iti kathamākārādiparihāraḥ ?
[133,4]
mābhūt tathaivaṃ kevalaṃ kenacid rūpeṇotpādayituṃ śaknuvataḥ svahetoranyatra kimālasyamīrṣyā vā, pramāṇenaikatra śaktiniyamānirvāhāt ? madhyamīye tu kiṃkṛtaḥ kāraṇabhāvaḥ, rājaprasādo vā ? ādye'pi kalpe sakalatribhuvanākāracchedanasahābhāvakarṣiṇaḥ kṣaṇāntarāvasthiticchedanamātre aṇīyasi kārye paryāloca eva nāsti | tato deśādisaṅkocakāriṇaivābhāvanāmnā pūrvasiddhena siddhe kālasaṅkoce'pi kimakāraṇamanyaḥ kālāntarabhāvī kāraṇāntarāpekṣaḥ siddho yaḥ sthāyī gaveṣyate ityuktaprāyam |
[134,1]
pratyarthaṃ bhedo'bhāvasyeti cet ? sarvathā'nupalabhyasvabhāvatve sāhasametat |
ato vyomādeḥ sarvadharmanirmāṇavat sarvato vyāvartanamapi kiṃ neṣyate ? na ca prācīnamevaṃ vyāpārabhāvamanubhavaḥ kṣamate | tasmāt svakāraṇādeva deśādiniyata iva kālaniyato'pi jāta iti na sthirapakṣavat kṣaṇikapakṣe'pi vīkṣaṇādiprasaṅgaḥ, bhāvasyaivābhāvāt |
sthirapakṣe tu sa cāsti tadavasthaśceti na nivartate prasaṅgaḥ padārthāntarotpattāvapi tasya tatrākiñcitkaratvāt | aprastutābhidhānaṃ ca bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ vastvantarodayavarjanāt |
[134,2]
na nu bhāvanivṛttau prastutāyāṃ nivṛtterudayo'padiśyate iti kimaprastutamatra ?
na nu tāvadeva nivṛttiḥ prasajyātmā yāvannodayopadeśaḥ | udaye tu tatparyudastavastvantaravidhānāt punararthāpattyā nivṛttyākṛṣṭiḥ, na tu saiva nivṛtirvastutvādeva, anyathātiprasaṅgāt |
[134,3]
yattu śaṅkaraḥ, bhāvādbhāvāntaravadarthāntaratvāviśeṣe kathaṃ sa eva tasyaiva nivṛttiriti cet ? atra vastusvabhāvairuttaraṃ vācyaṃ yeṣāṃ svahetubhyaḥ sahasthitivirodhenaivotpattiḥ, na hyarthāntaratvādanyatra sahasthitivirodhābhāve bhāvatannivṛttyorapi tasyābhāva iti nyāyyam, tayoreva sahasthitivirodhasya pramāṇena siddhatvāt | na hi yathā kaścidarthāntaratayā anyeṣāmaheturevaṃ svakāryasyāpi mābhūt tādṛgetadapīti |
[134,4]
etadeva nyāyabhūṣaṇo'pi, tadapi dvividhasyāpi virodhasya ghaṭanādapāstam |
yadi ca virodhādarthāntarasyāpi nivṛttibhāvo varaṃ mudgarasyaivāstvityapi darśitam | na ca pratyakṣamanumānaṃ vā nivṛttau pravṛttam | tadvirodhaśca pramāṇasiddho'vaśyavaktavya iti sundaram |
vahnidhūmādau tu hetuphalabhāvaḥ pramāṇasiddha eveti nārthāntarodayavarṇane'pi tannivṛttikhyātiḥ |
tasmāt, agnerarthāntarotpattau bhavet kāṣṭhasya darśanam | (pra. vā. 1. 272) na tasya kiñcidbhavati na bhavatyeva kevalam | (pra. vā. 3. 277)
iti duratikramo nyāyaḥ |
[135,1]
yattu nyāyabhūṣaṇaḥ, yadi tasya na kiñcid bhavati tataḥ pratiṣedho'pi na tasya bhavatītyapratiṣiddhasvarūpastadavasthatvāt prāgivopalabhyeteti, prāgeva prarihṛtametat | tathā hi pratiṣedho'pi na tasya bhavatīti yadi pratiṣedhākhyo'pi padārtho notpadyata ityarthaḥ, tadā satyametat, na tu tāvataivāpratiṣiddhasvarūpatvamarthasya, svahetutaiva kṣaṇāntare pratiṣiddhatāpratipādanāt | atha vācanikapratiṣedho vivakṣitastadā kastamapahastayati ?
kevalamatra pakṣe prāgivopalabhyetetyasaṃbaddham, na hi yo yadā nāsti sa tadopalabhyaḥ | anyathā kānyakubjasthito'pi pāṭaliputre dṛśyeta | māndhātā'pi vādyopalabhyeta |
[135,2]
nanvadya māndhāturabhāvastena nīpalambhaḥ | ko vai anyathā prāha ? kevalaṣaṣṭhīnirdeśād bhedāvasāye'pi na tato bhinnaḥ padārtho vidhīyate, yāvānevārtho māndhātādya nāsti tatkālaniyatasattākatvāt, tāvāneva māndhāturadyābhāva iti | na nu samānametadapi yāvānevārtho māndhāturadyābhāva iti tāvāneva māndhātādya nāstīti |
[135,3]
yadapyucyate — tatkālaniyatasattākatvāditi, tatrāpi tatkāla evāstīti kālāntare abhāva eva pratipādyata iti kimatrādhikamabhihitam ? uktamevaitat | tathāpyucyate, bhedābhedanideśayoreka evārthastattvataḥ kevalaṃ yadi bhinnavastusiddhiḥ pramāṇabalāvalambinī, tadādya nāstītyasyāpi vākyasyādyābhāvo'stītyayamevārthaḥ |
[135,4]
atha bhinnavastubādhaiva pramāṇānvayinī, tadābhāvo'stīti tāvadastu | adyābhāvo jāta ityasyāpi vākyasyādya nāstītyevārtho veditavyaḥ | pramāṇānveṣaṇe ca dṛśyatayā svīkṛtasyādarśanameva bādhakamuktaṃ ca sādhakaṃ ca kiñcinnetyapi | adyānupalambhe'pi tatkālavartinaḥ kālāntare vastvantararūpamaspṛśatā virahamātreṇa siddhatvamityupapāditam | na ca virahamātreṇeti karaṇaśaktinirdeśād vastutvapratyāśā, vivakṣāparatantratvāt kriyākārakavyavahārasya, yāti gandharvanagarādeṣa bandhyāsutaḥ padā | mṛgatṛṣṇāmbhasi snātvā pitre dātuṃ jalāñjalim ||
iti | sakalakārakaśaktiyoge'pi vastutvābhāvāt sarvathā mithyedamiti cet ? vivakṣāparatantratāmātreṇa dṛṣṭāntīkṛtatvāt |
[136,1]
ka evaṃ sādhurabhidadhīteti cet ? na ko'pyabhidhattāṃ prakṛtasiddheravirodhāt | na ca sādhorapyetatpāṭho'saṃbhavī sarvathā kiṃ tat sādhurnābhidadhīteti tadaśrutavataḥ praśne tatpāṭhamātreṇa sādhutākṣaterabhāvāt | kūrmaromṇāṃ tu mithyātvaṃ svīkṛtamityapi kimasādhunaiva vaktavyam ? nāpi sarvathā mithyaivedam | tathā māndhātā nāstīti nādya sthīyate māndhātreti vā vyaktā kartṛśaktirna vastutāṃ pratyujjīvayati |
[136,2]
niṣedha eva tasyā vartata iti cet ? ata eva vivakṣāpāratantryamapetasandeham |
tasmāt kārakaśaktinirdeśena vastutāsiddhipratyāśā phenasaṃghātena toyataraṇamanorathamanuharati |
[136,3]
tadevaṃ nābhidhānādhīnamarthatattvavaśenedaṃ tvabhidhānamiti bhedanirdeśa evādya abhāvo'sya jāta iti bhinnavastūtpattimivāsaṃśan adyedaṃ nāstītyasya prasajyapratiṣedhamātrasūcakasyārthe sthāpyo, na viparyaye, pramāṇāśaraṇatvādasya vibhāgasya | tatkālaniyamena kālāntare'bhāvābhidhānaṃ ca siddhasādhanam, vastvantarotpattireva hi niṣidhyate kālāntare, na ca prasajyapratiṣedhavyavahāramātraṃ pratiṣidhyate | tadasya bādhavidhānapratipādane'pi na paramārthasat padārthāntarasiddhiḥ |
[136,4]
tena yadudvartya vārtikaślokasya nyāyabhūṣaṇaścakāra kāvyam, abhāvo yadi paścānna bhāvastasya kimiṣyate | so'pi na pratiṣedho'yamabhāvasya kimiṣyate ||
iti, tat siddhasādhanaṃ bādhāniścayena vā paścādabhāvavyavahārapravartanamātrasyeṣṭatvād vastūtpattereva pratiṣiddhitvāt |
[137,1]
nanu keyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ, abhāvavyavahāramātramiṣyate paścānnābhāva iti ? evaṃ hi sati visaṃvāditāprasaṅgo'bhāvavyavahārasya, abhāvaśca mithyeti bhāva eva pratiṣedhyasya syāt | pratiṣedhaniṣedhaśca vidhānāt kīdṛśo'paraḥ | (pra. vā. 4. 221)
iti nyāyasya svayaṃ pratijñānāt | sa cābhāvo bhavan paścādeveti sphuṭataramasya kādācitkatvāt sahetutvaṃ vastutvaṃ ceti | tathā ca saha evāha, yasya bhāvasya paścādabhāvaḥ sa eva nāśa ityucyate | kathaṃ bhāvasya vināśo'nyo vā kaścinnopalabhyate ? atha bhāvasya vināśa ucyate, kiṃ tu sa bhavatīti nocyate, bhavatītyabhidhāne ko doṣaḥ ? bhāva eva syāditi cet ? tatkimidānīmabhidhānādevārthasya rūpaparivarto bhavati ? yadi ca bhavet tato jāyata ityucyatām | janmāpyabhāvasya kuta iti cet ? kādācitkatvāt |
akādācitkatve tu pratyutpannāvasthāyāmapyabhāvaḥ syāditi |
[137,2]
atrocyate, vyavahāraśabdena tāvadasmākaṃ niścayavacasī abhimate, vacanaṃ ca vikalpena sahaikaviṣayameva | vikalpasya ca grāhyādhyavasāyabhedena dvividho viṣayaḥ |
tatra yatpratibhāsaṃ vikalpajñānamājāyate tad grāhyamucyate | yadāśraye tu pravṛttinivṛttī tadadhyavaseyam, yathā paścādabhāvā bhāvasyaiva jāta ityasyaiva vikalpasyārthāntarotpattiḥ sākṣānnirbhāsamānā grāhyā tadbhāvārthakriyārthino nivṛtterāśrayabhūtā ca tadviviktatatkāladeśasvabhāvavastvavasthādhyavaseyā, yatastadvikalpodaye vināśākhyavastūtpattiparāmarśavimukhaḥ pratiṣedhyabhāvārthakriyārthī taddeśakālātmani vastuni na pravartate, api tu nivartate | tatastaddeśakālavastvavasthādhyavaseya ucyate | tatra pratibhāsamānavastvantarāpekṣayā vyavahāramātramucyate, yatnena nirūpatayā nayanasahasreṇāpyudīyamānapadārthāntarasyānupalabdheḥ | tatastadvisaṃvāde'pi yatra pravṛttinivṛttibhyāṃ pariniṣṭhitavyāpāro vikalpaḥ saṃpadyate, tamadhyavaseyaṃ viṣayamapekṣya na visaṃvādasaṃvādaḥ | adhyavaseye ca saṃvādetaracintā, na pratibhāsini | tadayamavyāpako'pi yadi nyāyaḥ prakṛte tāvadavaseyasaṃvādenaiva saṃvādamanuśiṣmaḥ | pratibhāsinī tu visaṃvādaḥ sādhya eva yadi sidhyati prasannāḥ devatāḥ, kimatrabhavataḥ kopena ?
[138,1]
tasmādabhāvavikalpapratibhāsinaḥ kāryarūpasya mithyātve'pi nābhāvavyavahārasya visaṃvāditā, adhyavasitārthayāthātmyasya sattvāt | tasya ca kalpitarūpasya mithyātve'pi bhāvavirodhinaḥ pracyutimātrasya vyavahartavyaikarūpasya mithyātvamiti na vastuniṣedhe bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ | tasya tu pracyutimātrasya niṣedhe syāt | na cā sā tena rūpeṇa pracyutimātrātmanā pratiṣidhyate | kiṃ tu vasturūpatayā kalpitayā |
[138,2]
nanu vastu na bhavatītyayameva pratiṣedhaḥ tathā ca sā pratyutirasti na veti praśne yadyasti kathaṃ na vastu ? nāsti cet kathamapratiṣedhaḥ ? ucyate, vastuvirahamātrasya vastutvāropa eva niṣedhaḥ | na vastutvaniṣedhastanniṣedhaḥ | tataḥ pracyutirastīti na pracyutirūpātpracyavata ityayamevārthaḥ | ghaṭo'stītyapi hi ghaṭarūpāpracyutimātramāpadyate | na tvasti prayogamātreṇa kalpitasyāpi traiguṇyamayatvādervidhiḥ | yathā ca pratiṣiddhaghaṭarūpādatiriktarūpāpekṣaiva nāsti ghaṭo nityatayā kṣaṇikatayā veti sādhu, tathā nāsti pracyutirityapi vastutvenetyapekṣaiva sādhu | nirupādhistvasti pracyutiriti tatsvarūpāpracyutau na duṣyati | yāvacca na pratiṣedhyabhāvastāvatpracyutiḥ, svarūpāpracyutiḥ, parasparābhāvarūpatvādanayoḥ | ataeva, nivṛttiryadi tasminna hetorvṛttiḥ kimiṣyate | sāpi na pratiṣedho'yaṃ nivṛttiḥ kiṃ niṣidhyate || (pra. vā. 4. 224)
iti durlaṅgho'yaṃ nyāyaḥ | evam, abhāvo yadi paścānna ityanena paścādabhāvākhyavirahamāśaṅkya, bhāvastasya kimiṣyate ityucyate yadi tadā na doṣaḥ | yasya hi yadāstītyasya pratyanīkaṃ nāstīti virahamātramavasturūpaṃ kalpanāviparivarti pratiṣidhyate, tasya tadā niyamenāstītyevaṃ rūpamantarmātrāyāmupasthānamāsādayati | yadā tu paścādvirahamātramapratikṣipya paścād bhavati jāyate ceti vikalpavivartavaśād vāsanāvaśagādvasturūpasya kalpitasya niṣedhaḥ, tadā kathaṃ virahamātrapratikṣepaprabhavo bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ, yato bhāvastasya kimiṣyate ityucyate ? na hi ghaṭaḥ kalpitarūpaniṣedhe svarūpāt pracyavamāsādayati, udakadhāraṇādyarthakriyāvirahaprasaṅgāt | na ca pracyuteḥ svarūpollekho vastutvapratyāśāyāḥ pūrakaḥ, asatsvabhāvo bandhyāsuta ityādivat, svabhāvāvasthānaniveśane'pi tadayogāt |
asiddho heturityādivad vā |
[139,1]
tasmāt nāśaḥ paścād bhavati jāyate mudgarādibhya iti bālavyavahāramātramapalapyate | tat pratibhāṣitaṃ tu kādācitkatvādi vasturūpaṃ nāstīti brūmaḥ |
[139,2]
na ca vastu yāvad vyavahāropasthāpitaṃ tatsarvaṃ vastutattvamiti śakyam, śāstrapraṇayanānarthakyaprasaṅgāt | vyavahāraṃ tu vitathamupadarśayannapi mūlabalābalābhyāṃ kaścidupādeyo heyaśca kaściditi vibhāgaḥ subhagaḥ | mūlaṃ cādhyavaseyamiti darśitam | tasmāt tattvacintāyām, na bhāvo bhavatītyuktamabhāvo bhavatītyapi | paścādabhāvo bhavati bhāvasyaivānapāyi vā || (tula0 pra. vā. 3. 278) tathā ca paścānna bhavati bhāvaḥ svakālamātraniyata ityeva kathyate | ato nārthāntarotpattiriti na kṣaṇabhaṅgapakṣe tādavasthyādupalambhādisaṃbhavaḥ | kiṃ tu sthirapakṣa eveti sthitam || nārthastāvatsvayamuparato nāśahetormudhātvaprāpterdaṇḍādapi na nidhane vyāpṛtestasya gīteḥ | nāpi dhvaṃsāt parighavadato bhinnanāśaprasakteḥ kasmānnaiṣa sphurati caṭakālopavṛttaṃ kimetat ||
ityantaraślokaḥ | kṣaṇikatve tu, svakāraṇādeva yathānyarūpavicchinnarūpaḥ samudeti bhāvaḥ | vicchinnabhinnakṣaṇavṛttirevaṃ svakāraṇādeva na jāyate kim ||
ityuktam | abhāvato'rthāntararūpabādhetatrāpyabhāvāntaramīkṣaṇīyam |
tatra yadayamāha, pradīpaprakāśavannānavasthetyeke iti | tatrocyate,
[140,1]
pradīpadṛṣṭāntamataṃ na kāntaṃsvarūpasandarśanaviprayogāt ||
[140,2]
dṛṣṭo hi pradīpaḥ paraprakāśanaśaktiyuktaḥ kathamapahnotuṃ śakyaḥ ? abhāvasya punaḥ svarūpavedanaṃ svapne'pi durlabham | tatra ka evaṃ dhṛṣṭa ākāśacitramācaratu etadbhāve'yamasya bhedaḥ, tadabhāve cātra nāsti, svayaṃ cānena rūpeṇa bhidyamāno nānyamapekṣata iti ? tat kathaṃ pradīpena sāmyam ? kiṃ ca,
[140,3]
pradīpavaccedayamapyabhāvo bhinatti bhāvaṃ ca vibhidyate ca | sa eva bhāvo'pyuditaḥ svahetorbhinattu bhāvaṃ ca vibhidyatāṃ ca ||
[140,4]
na hyevamabhidhīyamānaṃ vadanaṃ vakrayati | adarśanādanyapauruṣābhāvasya | na ca dṛṣṭāntamātrāt sādhyasiddhiḥ, hetustadbhāvasādhanāyābhāve upādīyamānaḥ ko'sāvasti yo nāśrayāsiddha iti ?
[141,1]
yat punarāha, vayaṃ tu paśyāmaḥ | tatrānavasthā nābhyupagamyate yatrānavasthāyāṃ kiñcid dṛṣṭaṃ virudhyeta, na cātra dṛṣṭaṃ kiñcid virudhyate | yā tāvad ghaṭasya paṭādibhyo vyāvṛttiḥ, tayaiva ghaṭādibhyo vyāvṛttaḥ siddhaḥ | tatra vyāvṛttyantarānavasthāyāṃ na kiñcid vighaṭitam | vyāvṛttivyāvṛttiparamparāgrahaṇopakṣīṇaśaktitvād vastu vyāvṛttaṃ na sidhyatīti cet — na, viśeṣaṇaviparyastānāmapi grahaṇānabhyupagamāditi | tatrāpyucyate,
[141,2]
sa hyastu nābhyupagamo'tra paramparāyā bhāvasya tadgrahaparamparayāstamāpteḥ | neṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇavedanaṃ cet nyāyaḥ samāna iti naiṣa tato vibhāgaḥ ||
[141,3]
agṛhītamapi kila vilocanaṃ grāhayati rūpamiti tadviśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇamagṛhītamapi viśeṣaṇaṃ grāhayatīti manyamānasya prathamamapi viśeṣaṇamagṛhītameva grāhayiṣyati viśeṣyamiti kṛtaṃ tadgrahaṇenāpi | na cāyaṃ viśeṣaṇakramaḥ | tato yathā prathamameva viśeṣaṇagrahaṇamanapekṣya lakṣayituṃ viśeṣyamaśaktaṃ tathā dvitīyādyapīti kathamayaṃ vibhāgaḥ śobhāmabhyeti ? yathā hyabhāvopādhigrahaṇamantareṇa saṅkīrṇagrahaṇabhītiḥ, tathā so'pyupādhirasaṅkīrṇo'gṛhyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ parabhedako nāma, svayaṃ viṣṭambhidravyavat ? evaṃ paramparāpekṣāyāṃ vyāvṛttavastunaḥ kalpairapi grahaṇābhāvādastamayo durvāraḥ |
[141,4]
yadi ca viśeṣaṇamabhāvaḥ tadā svahetoreva bhinnabhāvasaṃbhave bhinnadarśanavikalpanayorarthāpattyā siddheḥ kimabhāvena ? na hi bhinnamabhinnamanubhavitavyamabhrāntapratyayena | nāpi bhinnamanubhūtaṃ bhinnasaṅkalpavirodhi | athābhāvamantareṇa na bhinnaṃ nābhinnaṃ, kva tarhi kārakavyāpāra ityabhāvaḥ kāraka eva svīkṛto bhavati | tathāpi svahetoreva bhinnotpattau sarvamaviruddhamiti nopādhivādaḥ saṃvādaviṣayaḥ |
[141,5]
yaccāha — athavā nirvikalpakajñānena vyāvṛttivyāvṛttyānantyamapi gṛhītamiti, tatrāpi,
[142,1]
nirbhāsamāha yadayaṃ hṛdi nirvikalpe tat kauṣikāvaraṇamapyajahādalajjaḥ | yatraikamapyanupalabhyamabhāvanāmnā svavyāpinī sphurati tatra parampareti ||
[142,2]
mṛṣāvādaścedārabdhaḥ kimatra naibhṛtyenetyanurūpameva nyāyabhūṣaṇasya, yadapyayaṃ likhati, nanu svarūpeṇa buddhaṃ vyāvṛttamavyāvṛttaṃ vā ? yadi vyāvṛttaṃ, tadā'narthikā vyāvṛttiḥ | na ced vyāvṛttaṃ, vastusaṅkaraprasaṅgaḥ |
[142,3]
svarūpeṇeti ko'rthaḥ ? kiṃ vyāvṛttiṃ vinā, kiṃ vā vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa ?
vyāvṛttiṃ vineti na yuktam, vyāvṛtternityadharmatvāt | yo hi dharmaḥ kadācid bhavati tena dharmeṇa vinā'pi dharmī vyapadiśyate, yathā kuṇḍalena vinā puruṣo'kuṇḍalī, nāśāt prāganaṣṭa iti | na ca vastvantarād vyāvṛttivihīnaṃ vastu kadācit, yathā na gotvavihīno'sti gauḥ, nauṣṇyavihīno'gniḥ |
[142,4]
atha vyāvṛttivyatiriktena rūpeṇa vyāvṛttamityabhipretam ? tadiṣṭamevāsmākam, bhedābhyupagamāt | na caivaṃ vyāvṛttiranarthikā | yadi vyatiriktena dhanena dhanī puruṣaḥ, kimetāvatā dhanaṃ vyarthaṃ bhavet ? tasmāditaretarābhāvo'pi bhāvādarthāntarameveti, tadapi vidhūtam | yasmāt na khalu vastusatīṃ vyāvṛttimanumatyānyadarthaṃ codyametat | kiṃ tu vyāvṛttapratyaye'sāmarthyavaiyarthyābhyāmanupayogānna taddhanena vyāvṛttisiddhiriti codyārthaḥ |
tatra prathamapakṣe vaiyarthyamuktam | dvitīye tvasāmarthyamabhipretam |
[142,5]
athaṃ cārthaḥ, yadi vyāvṛttasvabhāvo bhāvaḥ svahetorudayavān, tadā tadupajanitayā pratīttyā vyāvṛtta eva pratyetavyaḥ | vyāvṛttilakṣaṇamarthāntaraṃ vināpi na hi vyasanamevaitadarthasya pramāṇena vā kenacidavadhāritam, yat mayā pratyayāntarasākalpe'pi tāmantareṇa na svajñānamutpādanīyamiti | nāpi jñānasya tadutpāditasya tayā vinā tadagrahaṇagraho nāma tadiyamanarthikā vyāvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttapratyayasyānyathāpi saṃbhavānna kalpanīyā |
[143,1]
atha na svahetorvyāvṛtta utpanno bhāva utpannaśca | tataḥ saṅkīrṇasvabhāvasyotpannasya vyāvṛttirevāsatī kathaṃ vyāvṛttapratyayamutpādayedityasamarthā | evaṃ ca codyaprakrame siddhāmeva vyāvṛttimavasthāpya vyāvṛtternityadharmatvādi kutropayogi ? na hyanena prathamapakṣoktavaiyarthyaparihāravārtā | tathā hi vyāvṛttapratyayasāmarthyād vyāvṛttirnāma kalpyate, sa ca vyāvṛttapratyayo'nyathāsiddha iti kimasyāḥ kalpanayeti codye vyāvṛttiḥ nityo dharmaḥ, atastena vineti na śakyamityuttaravādinaḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ? yāvatā vyāvṛttivyatireke sthityaiva vyāvṛttapratyayasyānyathānupapattivādasyāyaṃ nāvasaraḥ, tadvidhūya siddhāntamātrakathayā kimatra ?
[143,2]
na ca vināśāt prāganaṣṭa ityudāhartuṃ yuktam, vināśasya bhedāsiddheḥ | na vyāvṛttivihīnaṃ vastvityapi vyāvṛttestāttvikābhede siddhasādhanam, bhedāsiddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte'pi atadvyāvṛttirūpayorgotvauṣṇatvayorgavāgnibhedena darśayitumaśakyatvāt |
[143,3]
yaccātraiva pakṣe dvitīyaṃ vikalpitamanena, kiṃ vā vyāvṛttiriti vyatiriktena vyāpāreṇeti, tadanabhyupagamenaiva gatam, svarūpeṇa vyāvṛttaṃ buddhamiti viśvasmād vyāvṛttarūpaṃ buddhamityetasyārthasya vivakṣitatvāt | na cādyavaiphalyaparihāra ityuktam | nāpi dhanidṛṣṭāntena bhinnavyāvṛttisiddhirniyamahetorabhāvāt dhanavadvā saṃyogasamavāyānapekṣo, viśeṣaṇāntarasya daṇḍapāṇḍaratvāderapi saṃbandhavyavahāraḥ syāt | tasmānnetaretarābhāvo nāma kaścit, svahetoreva parasparavyavacchinnasyotpatteḥ |
[143,4]
evaṃ kālāntaravyavacchinnasyāpīti | na vināśahetunā kiñcit | tadayam, apekṣeta paraḥ kāryaṃ yadi vidyeta kiñcana | (pra. vā. 3. 579)
iti siddho nyāyaḥ | kimatra piṣṭapeṣaṇena ?
[143,5]
nāśo'dya, jāta iti nānyapadārthabhāvo bhāvaḥ svakālaniyatastu sa nānyadā'sti | nāstyanyadetyapi parodaya eva yasya tasya prasajyaviṣayāstamaye prasaṅgaḥ ||
[144,1]
yatpunarayaṃ prasajyaparyudāsayorbhedasādhanārthamabhāvabhāvavyavahāraviṣayatvena vibhāgaṃ pratyapīpadat, tad bhavato bhāṣaiva bhāvānyatetyatrāntare tiraskṛtam | na hi nyāyasiddhasya samayamātreṇa bādhanaṃ sādhu | tathā hi,
[144,2]
yajjāyamānamupalakṣitamarthakāri bhāvātmanā vyavaharanti tadeva santaḥ | so'yaṃ na yaḥ samayato yadi bhaṅgabhāgī bhāvānavasthitiriyaṃ na ca paryudāsaḥ ||
[144,3]
yadā hi mūrtāmūrtasapratighāpratighasanidarśanānidarśanadūrāsannasthūlasūkṣmādiprakāreṣu kaścid bhāvamabhāvaṃ vā kaścit svecchāvaśādabhidadhīta | vindhyavandhyāsutādikam abhāvabhāvaṃ vā, tadāyātamavyavasthānaṃ bhāvasya | na caivaṃ kṣatiḥ | svasamayānurodhāt abhidhānabhedasaṃbhavāt | kevalaṃ kimidānīṃ paryudastaṃ vastu vyavahriyatām ?
tasmāt samayānurodhādabhāvaśabdāpravṛttāvapi ekasya kāraṇāpekṣasaṃbhavasyopālambhabhājo vā, anyastādṛgeva padārthaḥ paryudasto vaktavyaḥ | tatkathamabhāvaśabdasaṅketamātreṇa paryudāsavyudāsaḥ ? yadi punarupalambhasaṃbhavāvapyabhāvābhimatasya samayamātratantrāvityucyate, tadā vāstavaḥ prasajyapratiṣedha evāyaṃ na paryudāsa iti na doṣaḥ | anena tu nyāyavinmāninā nyāyāgataṃ tameva prakāramullaṅghya saṃbhavopalambhārthakriyāśaktayaścābhāvasya bhāvikyaḥ abhyupagantavyāḥ | paryudāsapratyanīkaprasajyapratiṣedhatā ceti kimato'pi vyasanamanavasānamanyat ?
[144,4]
yaccāyamāha, na hyutpattirbhāvasya lakṣaṇaṃ yena nivṛttirbhavantī bhāvaḥ syādanutpattimatāmapyākāśādīnāṃ bhāvatvāditi | tatrāpi,
[144,5]
pāṇinerna nadī gaṅgā yamunā ca sthalī nadī | abhavannapi bhāvo'sya na bhāvo'sya bhavannapi ||
[145,1]
naraḥ svātantryamāpanno yadicchati karoti tat | ubhayatra samāno'yaṃ nyāyo nyāyavidāṃ mataḥ ||
[145,2]
nadīsaṃjñāniṣedhe'pi nāvagāhasya bādhanam | bhāvasaṃjñāniṣedhe'pi paryudāso na bādhyate ||
[145,3]
upalambhārthaśaktasya kāraṇāpekṣajanmanaḥ | sarvasya paryudastatvaṃ vastvantaramapekṣya hi ||
[145,4]
abhāvasaṃjñāvirahe paryudāsavyavasthitiḥ | na kvāpi sidhyet sarvatra saṃjñāyāḥ sulabhatvataḥ ||
[145,5]
yaccedaṃ svarūpanivṛttilakṣaṇā cotpattiḥ pradhvaṃsasyeṣyate, na tu prāgasataḥ sattāsaṃbandhalakṣaṇā kāraṇasamavāyalakṣaṇā veti, tatrāpi,
[145,6]
svarūpasyaiva nirvṛttiḥ sarvatrotpattirucyate | prakṣipya samavāyaṃ tu vimūḍhaiḥ sāpi hāritā ||
[145,7]
samavāyasyaivābhāvāt kva sattāsaṃbandhādiḥ | astu vā so'pi tathāpyapūrvātmalābha evotpattiḥ dharmādharmāntarāṇāṃ tu bhāvābhāvau na sādhakabādhakau | kiṃ ca kāryasyāpyabhāvasya na prāgasataḥ sattāsaṃbandha iti ko'rthaḥ ? kiṃ prāgasanneva na bhavati ? atha paścādapi na sattvamasya ? ubhayathāpi kutaḥ kāryatvamākāśākāśakuśeśayavat ? prāgasataḥ sattvamastu paścānna tu sattāyogaḥ |
[145,8]
nanu sattvaṃ sattetyanarthāntarametat | yogaśca sambandhaḥ | tatra sattvayogo'sti na sattāyoga iti ko'pyayaṃ nyāyaḥ ? atha sattā mahāsāmānyamucyate, tadabhāve'pi svarūpasattvamātreṇa paścāt sannityucyata iti cet ? tattarhi svarūpasattvaṃ yadi tāttvikam, tāvataiva kāryatvaṃ kimapareṇa kartavyamanyasyāpi kāryasya ? athaupacārikam, tadā nāśasyāpi kutaḥ kāryatā ? na hi bandhyātanayasya paścādbhāvopacāre kāryatā vāstavī nāma |
[146,1]
yaccedaṃ nivṛtterapyādimattvamityucyata iti, tadāpi nādhikaṃ kiñcit | sā ca nivṛttirabhāvarūpeṇaiva ādimatīti punarna sahāmahe, kāryāntarasādhāraṇatāyāḥ pratipādanāt | ādeśamātrametat bhūbhujāmeva śobhate | bhāvopalambhakāle tadrūpānupalambhādityapi paścādrūpopalambhe śobhāmābhajati | sa ca nāsti, kumbhāsaṃbhavavikalpamātraṃ tu saṅketānurodheneti darśitam | arthī paṭārthakriyayā ghaṭasyānupalambhane | na prāvartata ityasti nānyadṛk pratiyoginaḥ ||
tadalamasya prakriyāmātramavakaraṃ nirūpya, svayamūhyadoṣatvāt |
[146,2]
yaccāha, nāpyarthakriyāhetutvamātreṇa bhāvatvaprasaktiḥ, tvaduktabhāvalakṣaṇānabhyupagamāditi, tatrāpi paryudāsatvānatikramādityuktam | tasmānna bhāvādarthāntaramabhāvaḥ |
[146,3]
yatpunarāha, tvayāpi bhāvābhāvayorlakṣaṇabhedo'bhihitaḥ | tat kathamekatvam ?
sarvārthānāṃ lakṣaṇabhedādeva bhedavyavasthā, tato'pi cenna bhedavyavasthitirna kasyacit kutaścid bhedasiddhirityadvaitaprasaṅga iti | tadapyaparyālocanaphalam | yo hi naśvarasvabhāva eva nāśo nāśyatīti bahulādhikārāt kartari ghañ, taddharmatākalpanayā vā tadvācakenābhidhānāt | tannāśaṃ bhāvasvabhāvamicchāmaḥ, tamevāśritya, sattāmātrānubandhitvānnāśasyānityatādhvaneḥ (pra. vā. 3. 565)
ityuktam |
[146,4]
tathā cānenaivotthāpitam bhāva eva kṣaṇasthitidharmā nāśa iti tasyābhedameva brūmaḥ | naśanaṃ nāśa iti prasajyātmā dvidhā vyākartavyaḥ, tattvatastāvad vastutvavirahāt tattvānyatvaśūnya evāsau bhāvo na bhavatīti tadbhāvaniṣedhamātrapātraṃ tu kharaśṛṅgādivat | saṃvṛttau tu yathā kālabhedena vikalpyamānaḥ kādācitka iti pratibhāti, tathā sarvopākhyāviraharūpatayā bhāvādbhinna iva pratibhātīti nāvastutvepi lakṣaṇabhedākhyānavirodhaḥ | evaṃ ca sati saṃvṛttyā lakṣaṇabhede bhāvābhāvayorbhedasyeṣṭatvāt |
tattvena ca lakṣaṇaikatāvirahe bhāvasya tenaikyaniṣedhāt kathamadvaitaprasaṅgopālambhaḥ ? naśyatīti tu nāśo naśvarasvabhāvaḥ kathaṃ bhāvātmatāṃ pariharet ? sa ca sahetuko bhāvahetunaiva, na tu parastasya heturbhāvasvabhāvatvāt | tadayaṃ yat, bhāve hyeṣa vikalpaḥ syād vidhervastvanurodhataḥ | (pra. vā. 3. 574)
ityata āha, tadapi svavacanavirodhādayuktam | tvayā hi bhāvābhāvayostādātmyamuktam, tacca tattvānabhyupagame virudhyate | tattvābhyupagame'pi lakṣaṇabhedo virudhyate | yasya hi lakṣaṇabhedena bheda ucyate tasya kathaṃ tattvātattvanirvacanīyatvamiti ? tatsukhaidhitaḥ krīḍanaśīlatayā kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ punaḥ kārayati | na khalu bhāvapracyutisvabhāvenābhāvena bhāvasya tādātmyaṃ brūmaḥ | yastu na bhavatītyabhāva uttarakṣaṇāpekṣayā tena kastādātmyavirodha iti nāśavimarśena gatametat | evamanyadapyanadhikamavadhīritamasya veditavyam |
[147,1]
yadapyāha, nanvabhāvasya sarvadharmavivekalakṣaṇatvādutpattirna yuktā | sā hi bhāvadharma eveti — na, jñeyatvāderbhāvadharmasyābhāve'pi sadbhāvādityādi, tadapyasāram | na hi sādhāraṇadharmayogamātreṇa virodhapratiniyatānāmapi dharmāṇāmavakāśaḥ, hutāśanasyāpi śaityaprasaṅgāt, abhāvasyaiva vā sarvatra sadbhāvaprasaṅgāt jñeyatvādīnāmapi niṣedhāt | utpattiścābhūtvā bhavanarūpatayā bhāvadharma evetyāpāditameva |
[147,2]
yattu svayaṃ na bhavatīti, ko'rthaḥ ? kiṃ svayamevāyamabhāvaḥ ? kiṃ vā svayamabhavanaṃ karoti ? uta bhavanaṃ na karoti ? atha kiñcinna karoti ? svayaṃ vā na kiñcit ? kiṃ vā svayamabhāvībhavatīti vikalpya dūṣaṇamārabdham, tadapi marmacchedikājanitārtaravaprāyam |
[147,3]
tatra hi svayamiti hetvantaramanapekṣya svahetunā kṣaṇaniyatasthitirjanita iti kṣaṇāntareṇa na kiñciditi prakaṭita evārthaḥ | tato'tatsvabhāvaḥ paścādasau kuto jātaḥ ? svahetorhi tatsvabhāvo'tatsvabhāvād vyāvṛtta utpannaḥ | sa kathaṃ paścādapyatatsvabhāvaḥ syāt ? na hi laghusvabhāvād vyāvṛttaḥ pāṣāṇaḥ kadācillaghu syāditi | tadapi plavata eva | yathā hi deśāntarasthitivyāvṛtta utpannaḥ, tathā kṣaṇāntarasthitivyāvṛtto'pi kathaṃ kṣaṇāntarasthiteravakāśa ityuktaprāyam |
[148,1]
nanvasaditi na tadeva vastvabhidhīyate, vidhiviṣayatvāt | anyaccābhāvaśabdābhidheyaṃ pratītigocarāpannaṃ tvayā neṣṭam, tato nirviṣayaḥ pratiṣedho visaṃvādītyapratiṣiddhaṃ vastu syāt | naivam, pracyuterapi pratipādyatvāt kuto nirviṣayatvam ? nāpi visaṃvādaḥ, bhāvasthitau hi pratiṣedhasya visaṃvādaḥ syāt | sa ca nāsti, pracyuteḥ pratipāditatvāt |
na cāvastunaḥ saṅkalpaviṣayatāyā apyanupapattirityuktameva |
[148,2]
yatpunararthāntaraviṣayo'pi pratiṣedhaḥ kathaṃ vastupratiṣedhaka iti cet ? tadabhāvābhidhāyī kathaṃ na pratiṣedhaka ityuktam, tadapi pratyuktaprāyam | tadabhāvo hi na prasajyātmako'rthāntarasvīkārāt, paryudāsamātratve tu nārthāntaranivṛttiravaśyamarthāntarabhāvena vibhāvitā bhavati | virodhastu nāstīti pratipāditam | satyapi vā virodhe kiṃ viruddhadvārāśrayaṇena ?
sākṣādevābhāvapratipādanamastu |
[148,3]
syādetat, vacasābhāvapratipādane kṛte saṃśayāvakāśaḥ, viruddhadvāreṇa tu niścaya ityasat | viruddhapratipādanamapi hi vacasaiva vartate | tad yathā vacanamātrapratipādye hutabhuji neha śītamityeva sādhu, na tu nātra śītaṃ vahneriti tadvadetadapi ||
[148,4]
athānyaccintyate,
[148,5]
nālaṃ niṣedhavidhaye yadi paryudastamanyopalabdhiritarasya kathaṃ niṣeddhrī | naṣṭo ghaṭaḥ sa iti vā bhavato vikalpākāraḥ kathaṃ ghaṭaniṣedhanamādadhāti ||
[148,6]
atrottaraṃ,
[148,7]
nehāstyasāviti vikalpamabhiprasūteranyo niṣedhavidhiranyadhiyo na tāvat | nābhāvakalpanadhiyo'pyaviśaṅkitāyā mānāṅgabhāvamavadhūya niṣedhakatvam ||
[149,1]
sato vināśanaṃ nāma nopapannamitīritam | nāsataḥ karaṇe śaktiraniṣṭā vastunaḥ sataḥ ||
[149,2]
tataḥ pratiyogyanubhavaḥ pratiyogyantaravirahavikalpamutpādayediti nehānupapattiḥ |
na ca tanmātrādanyo'pyanubhavasya pariniṣedhanavyāpāraḥ | yasyāpi vikalpasya naṣṭo ghaṭa ityevamākārasya vā niḥśaṅkagamanādau tadarthakriyānvitatayā pravṛttivyāvṛttyavasthāyāṃ vā nimittabhāvānnānyaniṣedhakāritvam | evaṃ vacanasyāpi tadvikalpotpādanadvārakameva niṣedhasādhanatvaṃ draṣṭavyam |
[149,3]
etena atha nāstīti jñānamevānupalambhaḥ, tadapi vastusat kathaṃ vastvantarapratiṣedhasya viṣayaḥ syādityādyavakaraparihāraḥ siddhaḥ |
[149,4]
na ca nāstīti jñānamanupalambho'smākaṃ, kiṃ tu pratiyogyupalambho nirvikalpa eva, nāstīti jñānaṃ tu manovyavahārarūpaṃ tat phalameva | kiṃ caivaṃvidhanirbandhena vastucintāyāmanupayogāt ? yadapyasya nāstīti jñānaviṣayanirūpaṇam, tadapyasaditi nirūpaṇena gatārtham | yattu tadviviktabhūtalāderviṣayatvamāśaṅkyoktam, na bhūtalādervastvantaratvāt, na ca vastvantare pratipādite pratīte vādyaghaṭādivastvantaramabhūtamiti pratipāditaṃ pratītaṃ vā bhavati | evaṃ hi vastvantaraṃ hi nāśa ityetasmin mate yaddūṣaṇamuktaṃ tattu svayameva parihṛtaṃ syāditi | tadapyasaṃbaddham, kevalaṃ hi bhūtalamasya viṣaya iti kathaṃ na ghaṭāderabhūtatvabodhaḥ, yaiva hi ghaṭādyapekṣayā kaivalyāvasthā pradeśasya sa eva ghaṭavirahaḥ | vacanādināpyevaṃ kevalaṃ pradeśapratipādane kathamiva na prakṛtaghaṭādyapekṣya bhāvapratipādanam ? evaṃ yadi karparādivat kevalasya nāśasyāpyupalambhaḥ syāt, bhavatu ghaṭo niṣedhapratītiḥ ghaṭaniṣedhastu kena kṛtaḥ ? pūrvaṃ sanneva hi ghaṭābhāvaḥ taddvāreṇa pratipattavyaḥ, na hi pradeśena ghaṭābhāvo janyante, kiṃ tu sanneva ghaṭābhāvaḥ taddvāreṇa niścetavyaḥ yadi hi ghaṭo'pi na syānna pradeśaikarūpaniyatā pratītiriti | evaṃ yathā yadi ghaṭo'dyāpi syānna karparaikarūpaniyatā pratipattistathā na nāśaikarūpaniyatā pratipattiriti balād ghaṭābhāvaniścayo bhavatu yadi pūrvaṃ ghaṭābhāvaḥ syāt, sa ca nāsti |
tadbhāve'pi kiṃ nāśena, kapālenaiva pratiyoginā gatārthatvāt ? na ca nāśapratītirapyastītyuktam, tasmāt sataḥ pradhvaṃsane sadrūpeṇāsadrūpeṇa vā dūṣaṇamuktaṃ kathaṃ sadrūpeṇa sato'sato vā niścaye kartavye syāditi na samānaḥ parihāraḥ |
[150,1]
yattvāha, na ca tadvivekāpratītau tadviviktagrahaṇaṃ bhavati | tadvivekaśca na bhūtalādisvarūpameva, viśeṣaṇatvāditi, tat nyāyabahiṣkṛtam | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo'pi saṅkalpārūḍhe rūpe | sa ca, bhinnaṃ bhāvamabhinnamākalayati vyaktaṃ tadanyātmanā jiṣṇu sphārakadambaḍambaramiva svāṃśairanaṃśaṃ jagat | kiṃ ca svākṛtimātra eva viṣayavyāmohadohakṣamaḥ saṅkalpaḥ paramaindrajālika iva vyādhūtabhūtasthitiḥ ||
yathā hi bhinnaṃ bhāvamekīkurvannutpadyate, tathābhinnaṃ bhāvaṃ bhinnamākalayatītyapyarthaḥ, yathā śilāputrakasya śarīram, śarīre karacaraṇādayaḥ lambakarṇo devadatta ityādi | tasmāt kalpanādhīno viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhāvo'bhinno'pi bhāve bhedavivakṣāpekṣavyavahāraḥ kathaṃ bhedaniyatamātmānamātanoti ? skhaladgatirayaṃ rāhoḥ śira ityādinirdeśa iti cet ?
yadi satyametattadā bhinnasya sākṣādanupalambhādeva | iyaṃ ca gatirghaṭavivekākhyapadārthāntarāpekṣayāpyasti, tathāpi neti koṣapānaṃ pramāṇam | tasmāt sa ghaṭābhapradeśa eva ayamanyo ghaṭavivikto na tu ghaṭavivekena bhinnena viśeṣita iti |
[150,2]
tasmād yadyapi kiñcid viśeṣaṇaṃ bhinnameva dṛṣṭaṃ vāhādi, tathāpi nāyaṃ niyamaḥ, viparyayasyāpi darśanāt, saṃbhāvanācca bādhakādarśanāt | vivakṣāparatantratā tu dṛṣṭāntasaṃbhāvanābījam | tadevaṃ na vācyaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyādarthāntaratvād vāhādivaditi |
kiṃ ca, vyāptaṃ bhidā yadi viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ bhedātyayānnanu tadā tadabhāva eva | deśo viśiṣṭa iti nāsti yathā tathedamapyasti dṛśyamatabhedadṛgasti neti ||
na ca dṛśyānupalabdheḥ pramāṇātmano viśiṣṭavyavahāramātreṇa sa ghaṭādanya ityarthaniṣṭhena bādhaḥ, kiṃ tu tathaivāsyeti |
[151,1]
yaccāha, abhede'pi na pramāṇaṃ kiñcidastīti, tadanunmīlitākṣasyaiva sāmpratam, anyathā pratyakṣodayasya nivārayitumaśakyatvāt |
[151,2]
yaccedam yadi ca ghaṭo nāstītyasya saṃjñānasyābhidhānasya ca bhūtalameva viṣayo na ca tato'nyo ghaṭābhāvaḥ, tadātra ghaṭo'stītyasyāpi bhūtalameva viṣayaḥ syāt | ghaṭo'pi na tato'nyaḥ kalpanīyaḥ, tathotpādena viśiṣṭaṃ bhūtalamevobhayatrāpyastu | na caitadyuktam |
yasmād ghaṭasadbhāvavadghaṭāsadbhāve'pi bhūtalato'nyaḥ pratibhāti, evaṃ hi vidhipratiṣedhayoḥ prayogo'pyarthavāneva bhavediti tadvaraṃ januṣāndho, na punarayaṃ durnītidagdhabuddhiḥ | abhāvavat kila kalaso'pi kalpanāmātraviṣayo na locanagocara iti kimatra brūmaḥ ? sakumbhamudbhutaṃ bhūtalam ityapi sahitotpattirāpadyate, na rūpasaṅkaraḥ, bhedopalambhasya bhinnārthakriyāniyogasya ca durapahnavatvāt | tadvannābhāvo'pi bhūtalakapālādibhyo bhinnaḥ pratibhātīti cintitameva | kiṃ ca,
[151,3]
kimiha kalasadhvaṃso dṛśyo na vetyudito jano vadatu samayasmṛtyā dṛṣṭiṃ vimarśaparāṅmukhaḥ | kalayasi punaḥ kāṃskānarthāniheti paraṃ yadi pradiśati dharādibhyaḥ sabhyastvameva vayaṃ na tu ||
[151,4]
tato vidhipratiṣedhaprayogayorapi kānupapattiḥ, avasthādvayapratipādanāt ? tathā ca jālāntareṇa praviṣṭālokasyābhāvo bhinnadeśo bhāsamānaḥ kimapahnotuṃ śakyaḥ ? kevalam,
[151,5]
vicchinnaḥ sphuṭanīlakāntikalitaḥ tāvatpradeśasthiti— rbhinnārthatvaviniścayāttu sa iti prakhyātināmāntaraḥ | ālokasya yathā tathānyaviraho'pyātmasvarūpasphuṭīkāre kiṃ kalasaḥ kimātapabhidādhyakṣeti citraṃ mahat ||
[152,1]
na hi sūkṣmamīkṣamāṇe'pyatyantavicitrasya bhāvarāśerabhāvānāṃ saṃbandhibhedādbhedopacāramantareṇa sūkṣmo'pi svabhāvabhedastama ivopalambhagocaraḥ | tadvaramālokaviveko'pi sakalānyavivekavadanālokya evāstu, tamastu vastveveti gṛhāṇa | kimaṅga kaṣṭasaṃkaṭe sukhinamātmānamāveśayasi ?
[152,2]
nanu nimīlitākṣasyāpi tādṛṅnīlapratibhāsaḥ saṃbhavī, na ca nīlamarthamupasthāpayatīti | tadayuktam, kṛṣṇavarṇāntarasya sarvasyāpyabhāvaprasaṅgāt | anyādṛśametat kṛṣṇāntaraṃ kalayāpi nimīlitākṣapratibhāsāditi cet ? andhakāro'pi tarhi punaḥ parimitadeśo vicitrasaṃsthānaḥ pratibhāsamānaḥ sphuṭataraṃ nimīlitākṣapratibhāsādbhinnarūpa evānubhūyate, ekarasaśca nimīlitākṣapratibhāsaḥ, andhakārastu kadācit kiraṇaparamāṇunikarasaṅkarakāle viralarūpaḥ, anyadā ghano dhanataro veti kathaṃ sāmyam ? kṛṣṇatāmātraṃ punaranyatrāpi sādhāraṇam |
[152,3]
anyatra nīlavarṇe vastuni sparśāntarasahacāraḥ avaśyambhāvīti cet— na, indranīlādimaṇikiraṇajālake tadabhāvāt | anupalakṣyastatra sparśa iti kalpanaṃ nāndhakārādvibheti | tasmādrūpamātramubhayamastu | na hi dṛṣṭe'nupapannaṃ nāma | yadi cāśrayo'vaśyamṛgyaḥ maṇikuḍyādikamastyeva | na ca vastuvyavasthāyāṃ pratyakṣapratibhāsamāśrayataḥ pratibhāsaviplavena vyabhicārābhidhānaṃ dhīmato dhinoti | anyathā vātapittakṣobhādinā jvalitastambhādisaṃdarśanāt satyamapi jvalitastambhādikamasatyaṃ syāt |
prakṛtipratyāpattau tu yathā tatpratibhāsābhāvaḥ, tathā nayanonmīlanakāle nīlābhāvaviplavasyāpi | andhakārādarśanaṃ tu svasthāvasthāpekṣameva yathopavarṇitaviśeṣam | tatpratibhāsasya ca pratyakṣasaṃbhavasāmagrīvighaṭane vighaṭanaṃ guṇa eva nāparādhaḥ pratyakṣasvabhāvatāyā iṣṭatvāt |
[153,1]
yatpunaruktam, kṛṣṇarūpasyālokena vinā grahītumaśakyatvāditi | nanu pītāvadātādayo'pi nālokanirapekṣavīkṣaṇā iti pradīpacandrātapādayo'pi prakāśāntaramapekṣeran | vicitrāstu bhāvaprakṛtayaḥ pramāṇasamadhigatā na paryanuyogamarhanti |
[153,2]
yaccālokavat, tadabhāvasyāpi grahaṇe cakṣurālokāntaranirapekṣamācakṣāte śaṅkaranyāyabhūṣaṇau, tadapi na kiñcit | niścāyakaṃ hi cakṣurvijñānamabhāvasya na grāhakamavastutvāt, ālokāntarānapekṣamiti tu siddhameva | na caitat vācyam | yo hi bhāvo yāvatyā sāmagryā gṛhyate tadabhāvo'pi tāvatyaivetyālokagrahaṇasāmagryā gṛhyamāṇaṃ tamastadabhāva eveti, tamograhaṇasāmagryā gṛhyamāṇasyālokasyaiva tadabhāvatāprasaṅgenānaikāntikatvāt | ghaṭapaṭayorvā samānagrahaṇasāmagrīkatayā paramparābhāvatvaprasaṅgaḥ |
[153,3]
tasmāt padārthāntare rūpavivekena pratibhāsamānamadhyakṣe andhakāramālokavirodhi vastveva | virodhitve tarhi kadācidālokamapyandhakāraḥ paribhavediti na codyam, adyāpi prakṛtivādasyopasthāpanāt, tūlānalādivat |
[153,4]
etena tamasa eva pratiyogivastuna upalabdhirabhāvaṃ sahasā vyavahārayituṃ prabhavati |
tamasyālokanivṛttāvapīti siddhe yathehālokasyābhāvopalabdhistathā sarvatreti śaṅkarādīnāṃ pratyāśāpratyādeśo veditavyaḥ | anupalabdhiniṣṭhāyāṃ tu jñānākāre'pi pratiyoginyabhāvasiddhirdarśitā | na ca kaścid doṣa ityāstāṃ tāvat | tasmānnābhāvo nāma kiñcid yatra kāraṇavyāpāra iti sthitam |
[153,5]
etena trilocano'pi nirastaḥ, yadāha — bhāvasya vyatiriktāṃ nivṛttimanicchadbhiraśakyā svarūpanivṛttiravasthāpayitum, yā hi tasya prāktanī kācidavasthā bhavadbhirarthakriyānirvartanayogyā dṛṣṭā saiva yadyuttarakālamapyanuvarteta tarhi svarūpeṇaiva nivṛttau bhāvaḥ kathamavasthāpyeta ? tadānīmayaṃ naṣṭo bhāvo, na sapadi svahetupratilabdhasvarūpātirekiṇī tasya kācidavasthotpadyeta ||
[154,1]
utpattau saiva tasyātmāntaraṃ jātamityatādavasthyam | atādavasthyamevāsya vināśaṃ brūmaḥ | tādavasthye tādātmyameva svarūpeṇa nivṛtto bhāva ityasya śabdasya satyamarthaṃ na vidmaḥ | svarūpanivṛttiḥ khalviyaṃ bhavantī bhāva eva syāt, bhāvādanyā vā ? tattve svakāraṇebhyo niṣpannasyānyathānutpattāvuttpatterārabhya sattvānnityatvaṃ prasajyate, anyathātve ca tadeva nivṛtteranyatvamiti priyamanuṣṭhitaṃ priyeṇa | tasmādutsṛjya vibhramaṃ nāśotpattireva naṣṭatvamabhyupagantavyam |
[154,2]
tat kimucyate naṣṭasyādarśanam, na ca tasya kiñcid bhavatīti ? adarśanaṃ naṣṭasya punarabhāvadarśanameva | ātmahānamabhāvotpattimeva vayamaṅgīkurma iti sarvamanavadyam |
[154,3]
akṣaṇikāḥ santaḥ, kāraṇavattvāt | yatkāraṇavattadakṣaṇikam, yathā bhāvavināśaḥ | kāraṇavantaśceme santaḥ | tasmādakṣaṇikā iti | kāraṇavattvasya sādhyaviparyaye vṛttiśaṅkā vināśahetumattvameva nivartayatīti prasiddhavyāptikātkāraṇavattvādakṣaṇikatvasiddhiriti, vyatiriktanivṛttimantareṇāpi svarūpanivṛtterupapāditattvāt |
tataśca kṣaṇādūrdhvaṃ kutaḥ prāktanaśaktāvasthāsthitiḥ ? vyatiriktotpāde'pi kathaṃ naṣṭo nāma ?
atādavasthyamatādātmyaṃ ca jātamityasyātyakṣarasya svahetorevāvasthāsvabhāvāntaravirahito'yaṃ jāta ityevārtha uktaḥ | tanmūlakaḥ atādavasthyādivyavahāra eva paścādbhāvī na tadvikalpapratibhāsi bhāvāntaramiti na tattvānyatvavikalpāvakāśaḥ | tasmādutsṛjya vibhramaṃ naṣṭavyavahāro'stu, na tu tasyānyat kiñcit jāyata iti | adarśanaṃ cābhāvadarśanameveti saṃpratyeva pratyākhyātamiti sarvamanavadyam |
[154,4]
tasmāt prasajyātmano'bhāvasya nāśākhyasya hetureva, na kaścit | vinaśvarasvabhāve tu hetvantaraśaktimapākṛtya svahetoreva sāmarthyasamarthanād jātamātrameva vinaśyatīti na kṣaṇāntaramanvetīti siddheḥ | kāraṇavattvasyākṣaṇikatvena vyāptyasiddheranekāntaḥ |
kṛtakānāmavaśyamante'pi nāśābhyupagame ca virodhaḥ | pramāṇagocarasya pakṣīkaraṇe pratijñāyā anumānabādhā | agocare cāśrayasvarūpayorasiddhiriti sthitam |
[154,5]
yat punarayaṃ bhagavato bhāṣyakārasya pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhimanavagāhamānaḥ anurūpavikalpābhāvodbhāvanamātrasāreṇa vistareṇa dūṣaṇamabhilaṣannapabhāṣaṇapramādamācarati, tadasya caṭulavaṭubhāvasulabhamanātmajñatāviṣkaraṇamātramiti mantavyam | tathā hi pratyakṣasiddhaṃ kṣaṇikatvamiti na pratyakṣavyavahṛtam, anurūpavikalpānudayāt | kiṃ tu pratyakṣagṛhītam, vyavahāratvānumānāt | taccānumānaṃ yadi svayaṃ kutaścilliṅgāt prasādhya pratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgagrahaṇavyavahāramādadhīta sāmarthyāt, tadā na viśeṣaḥ sattvādyanumānavat | arthato hi tadā pratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇabhaṅgagrahaṇamavasthāpyamānaṃ svapauruṣasparśābhāvāt na pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiprasiddhiṃ puṣṇāti | yadā tu pramāṇāntarasiddhamadhyakṣasya kṣaṇamātrasthitigrahaṇamāśritya vyavahāramātrasādhanamanumānaṃ pṛṣṭhajavikalpanirviśeṣaṃ tatpauruṣameva dīpayadutpadyate, tadā pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgasiddhiriti mukhyamākhyāyate | tadayamarthaḥ,
[155,1]
kṣaṇitvamadhyakṣadhiyādhipātaṃ pātaṃ punarna vyavahārametat | ataḥ samakṣagrahasādhanena prasādhyate tadvyavahāra eva ||
[155,2]
kṣaṇabhaṅge'nyadāsiddhe pratyakṣeṇa grahasthitiḥ | pratyakṣeṇa grahādasya kṣaṇabhaṅgavyavasthitiḥ ||
[155,3]
tathā hi,
[155,4]
yannirbhāti yathā tathā tadakhilaṃ gaṅgāmbu gauraṃ yathā nocenna prativastu śaktiniyamaḥ saṅkīrṇabhāve bhavet | saṃskārāḥ pratibhānti cendriyamatiṣvekakṣaṇasthāyinaḥ syādekakṣaṇavīkṣaṇāditarathā dṛṣṭastrikālī kalaḥ ||
[155,5]
liṅgarūpopapattivyavakīrṇo'yaṃ svabhāvahetuprayogaḥ | atra ca sapakṣe sadbhāvānna virodhadoṣaḥ | dvitīyapādena cānekāntaparihāraḥ | tathā hi, nirbhānaṃ pratyakṣe pratibhānamuktam, tato yāvatā viśeṣeṇa padārthaḥ pratyakṣe pratibhāsamāsādayati tanniyamaparihāreṇa yadi svarūpasthitimābhajeta tadā sarvasaṅkīrṇamasya rūpamiti sarvatra sarvopayogādiprasaṅgaḥ | ataḥ svarūpaniyame pramāṇāpekṣāyāṃ pravṛttinivṛttikāmasya yad yathā pratyakṣe pratibhātaṃ tattathaiva san, nānyayeti | tadanena avaitathyavyāpto hi pratyakṣapratibhāso'rthasyānyathāvasthāne vipakṣe vyāpakābhāvādabhavaṃstathāvasthānena vyāpyata iti darśitam |
tṛtīyapādena pakṣadharmopasaṃhāraḥ | tadasiddhiparihāraścaturthena | pūrvāparakālayorekatve hi padārthasya dṛṣṭādrūpādrūpāntaravirahāt sakalakālakalākalitasya deśāntarayuṣo'pi rūpasyāvaśyaṃ pratibhāsa iti na deśakālāntarāvasthāpratipattaye pramāṇāntaraparyeṣaṇāvakāśaḥ |
asti ca paryeṣaṇā idānīmanyadeśe kāle vā tadvastu kathamasti kiṃsvinnopanipātinā rāgarasena siktamiti tadupanipātasaṃbhavinyavasare vimarśadarśanāt | na ca darśanaviṣayīkṛte tathā saṃbhavaḥ | na ca dṛṣṭe'pyanavasāyaḥ śakyo'bhidhātum, tādṛśi jijñāsite raktādau rūpe kṣaṇikatāvadanabhyāsābhāvāt | anyathā paścād darśane'pi nāvasāyodayaḥ syāt | tasmāttadanavasāyastu tadapratibhāsādeva |
[156,1]
nanu vastunastrekālyavyāptipratibhāse'pi svasaṃbandhiviśeṣāṇāṃ kāladeśadaśāntarāṇāmapratibhāso na bādhakaḥ, kṣaṇikagrahaṇe'pi tatsaṃbandhihetuphalasaṃyogyādivastvantarāṇāmapratibhāsasya samānatvāt, ataḥ saṃbandhyantarāpekṣayā pramāṇāntaraparyeṣaṇamapi yuktameveti cet ? naivam, deśakālakriyāguṇādīnāṃ bhāvād bhedāsiddheḥ |
bhinnasya tu saṃbandhino'pi pratibhāsastatpratibhāse mābhūt | tasmāt kṣaṇāntaradaśāḥ sarvā nirvāsya kṣaṇaparigatenaiva rūpeṇa pratibhāsanaṃ samastavastunaḥ siddham |
[156,2]
yāvattarhi raktādirūpā visadṛśī daśā na sannidhīyate, tāvatkālamekīkṛtau ca grahaṇamastu | tadapi nāsti, darśanalakṣaṇānantaraṃ jhaṭiti vicalane vilocanasya sadṛśeṣvapi tattvataḥ kṣaṇāntareṣu viparyayaśaṅkāvatārāt, sākṣātkṛteṣu ca tadayogāt |
yadanantaraṃ tarhi locanacalanaṃ taddarśanaṃ naikakṣaṇikamavasāyaviparyayaśaṅke pṛthagjanasya saṃbandhamutthāpayitum, avaśyaṃ hi dvitrānapi kṣaṇānudīyamānameva taddarśanaṃ tadupayogi |
tato dvitrikṣaṇasthāyino rūpasya kathaṃ prathamakṣaṇe pratibhāsabhraṃśaḥ, yena dvitīyādikṣaṇasya bhedasiddhiriti cet ? yasya tāvatprathamakṣaṇa vīkṣaṇakṣaṇāntarameva calati cakṣuṣi viṣayavikalpodayaḥ, tasya durvāraḥ sarvāparakṣaṇaviparyayavimarśāvakāśaḥ |
[157,1]
naivaṃ kasyacit saṃbhavatīti cet ? kimatra bādhakam ? sādhakamapi kimatreti cait ? ucyate, yadi tāvadīkṣaṇakṣaṇamātrānantaramavasāyodaye sādhakānveṣaṇam, tadā dvividhaḥ pratyakṣapṛṣṭhajo vikalpaḥ, dṛṣṭamātravikalpaśca | dṛṣṭamidaṃ vastraṃ vetyevasvarūpaviśeṣavikalpaśca kṛtrimetaramaṇimuktādau | tatrāsya viṣaye sādṛśyāpahāryamandadhiyaḥ pṛthagjanasya bhrāntirutsargasiddhābhyāsaprakarṣasaṃbhavināpohyate | ataḥ prakarṣatāratamyenodayasya kālasya lāghavatāratamyaniṣṭhāyāṃ darśanakṣaṇānantaramapyayamudayamāsādayannaśakyasaṃbhāvananiṣedhaḥ | dṛṣṭamātrasya vikalpasya tu darśanānantarameva janmotsavasiddhaṃ sāmagrībhedenāpohyate | tathā hi, prakṛtyā anādisaṃsārasantatisātmībhūtavikalpāstvanubhūtapratyakṣe'pi ca vastuni vikalpāpekṣapravṛttinivṛttayo viśeṣataḥ sukhaduḥkhaprāptiparihārārthinaḥ sarve sarvadā tatsādhanavimarśābhyāsavāsitasantatayaḥ kathaṃ tadviṣayānubhave'pi samathahetau samupasthite vilambitavikalpabhāvānanubhavitumarhanti ? kevalaṃ kadācit saṃhatāḥ, yatā na vikalpasaṃhārābhyāsaḥ, kadācidanyāsaktiḥ, kadācidātyantikamāhādāmukhībhāva ityevaṃprakārasāmagryā vilambasaṃvāhitavikalpajanmāno bhaveyuḥ |
tadabhāve tu siddha eva pratyakṣakṣaṇānantaramudayo vikalpasya | tatastaddarśanavinākṛteṣu sarveṣveva viṣayakṣaṇeṣu raktatādisandehadolāndālanaṃ manaso viprakṛṣṭakṣaṇaparamparāsviva dvitīyakṣaṇe'pi vimarśaviṣayīkṛte kathamanavakāśaḥ ? na ca pratyakṣapratibhāse'pyevam |
tasmāt kṣaṇaparigateneva padārtharāśiradhyakṣapratibhāsamāviśati |
[157,2]
syādetat | pratyakṣasya kṣaṇikatve satyupapannametat, yāvatā pratyakṣamanekakṣaṇavyāpi |
tato'nekṣaṇavyāpini pratibhāsite vikalpāvasāyaḥ | tat kathamekakṣaṇagrahaṇasiddhiḥ ? ucyate, kiṃ tāvat svarūpaniṣpattāvupayogādanekakṣaṇasya vyāpakamadhyakṣam, atha kṣaṇaniṣpannasyaiva sthairyāt ? tatrādyakalpastāvadasaṃbhavī, jñārnasyāvayavirūpatāviyogena khaṇḍaśa utpattarayogāt | kṣaṇabhedinaśca te'vayavāḥ pratyakṣasya yadi paricchittisvabhāvāḥ, tadā tāvantyeva pratyakṣāṇoti prathamapratyakṣāpekṣayā saiva cintā |
aparicchittisvabhāve tu samuditamapi na pratyakṣam | akhaṇḍaśaḥ paricchittiḥ samudāyena sakalātmavastuparicchedaḥ | tadāpyādyakṣaṇaparicchinnaḥ khaṇḍa eva sakalātmavastu, tadapraviṣṭasya tato bhinnatvāt | anyathā krameṇa pratīyamānaṃ viśvamekameva vastu syāt, sakalaṃ ca pratyakṣamekameva pratyakṣamiti |
[158,1]
dvitīye pakṣe'pi niṣpannavyāpārasya vā ? kṣaṇāntaravyāptiniṣpannavyāpārasyaiva vā ? prathamapakṣe viṣayagrahaṇamevāsya vyāpāra iti tāvataiva vikalpajanmāvakāśaḥ, svayaṃ kṣaṇāntaramastu mā vā ? tathā ca sati calati cakṣuṣi viṣaye vā tadviṣayagrahaṇapravaṇamadhyakṣamavatiṣṭhata iti apūrvo'yaṃ nayaḥ | agrahaṇāvakṣaṇāvasthāne tu na tāvataiva vikalpajanmāvakāśānmuktiḥ | na ca pūrvagrāhiṇaḥ paścādagrahaṇe sthairyapakṣasthitiriti indriyaviṣayavidhāne bāgṛhṇato'pi tasya sthitiriti śraddhāvadheyameva |
evamaniṣpannavyāpārasthitirityapi duḥśraddhānam | na hi kāryāntaravajjanmātirekeṇa jñānasyāpi vyāpāraḥ | astu caivam, tathāpīndriyaviṣayopanidhau labdhodayamadhyakṣamanadhigatagocaramubhayavicālakāle kalayat kilāstīti subhāṣitaṃ pūrvavat |
[158,2]
tadalamatipratiṣṭhairmithyāvikalpairiti caturthapādena prāk paścād vā citraraktādirūpasya tadaiva nirbhāse sūcitapramāṇāntarāvṛttiviparyayeṇa | yad yad rūpaṃ vyavasitisahaṃ kvāpi nirbhāsamāne mānaṃ bhinnaṃ spṛhayati na tat tatra nirbhāsayogi | rūpābhāse rasa iva tathā tatkṣaṇe bhāsamāne pūrvāvasthā vyavasitisahāpekṣyate mānamanyat ||
iti viruddhavyāptopalabdheḥ sthitametat ekakṣaṇasthāyinamevabhāvasvabhāvamāmukhayati pratyakṣapratibhāsa iti | na ca tatpratibhāsabahirbhūto'pi svabhāvastasyeti niveditaprāyaṃ vyāptisamarthanaprastāve |
[158,3]
tasmāt siddhamadhyakṣeṇa bhaṅguratvam, vyavahṛtaṃ cānumānena mānāntaropapāditaṃ tatsiddhisiddheneti |
[158,4]
pratyakṣeṇa kṣaṇikakalane nyāyadiksūcanātaḥsāmarthyāptavyavahṛtividhau dhīmato na prabandhaḥ |
[158,5]
so'pyācāryapravararaviṇākāri kiṃ tvalpamedhā — stattvābodhāt prakṛtimukharo'satyamabhyujjagāra ||
[159,1]
no mārgamācāryaraverapekṣya cakṣaṇigrahe'smākamatha kramo yataḥ |
[159,2]
yathā ca bhāṣyoktisamanvayastathāna gītamaprastutavistarād bhiyā ||
[159,3]
tadalamānuṣaṅgikakathānirbandhena | sthitametanna vināśo nāma parighādibhyo bhinnaḥ kaścinmudgarādisādhyo yastadanupanipātadaśāyāmabhavan bhāvasya sthairyasiddhimanorathaṃ paripūrayediti |
[159,4]
durnītāśramavedikādṛḍhatarastambhānamūn śaṅkaranyāyālaṅkaraṇatrilocanavacaspatyāhvayān helayā | unmūlya kṣaṇabhaṅga eṣa vihito yatpuṇyamāptaṃ mayā tena syāt parapāragastribhuvane jñānaśriyo'yaṃ janaḥ ||
[159,5]
ahetukavināśādhikāro nāma caturthaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ ||
{2}
<vyāpticarcā>
[161,1]
namo bhagavate vītarāgāya |
[161,2]
iha dahanādinā dhūmādervyāptiradhyakṣānupalabdhisādhanatadutpattilakṣaṇeti vyutpādyate |
pare hi purastanāstāvadagnimati dhūmasya darśanamadarśanaṃ ca tadvirahiṇītyevānvayavyatirekitvaṃ kalpayāmbabhūvuḥ | tatra darśanādarśanaṃ yādṛcchikamapi sakṛd bhavediti ca bhūyaḥ pravṛttimapekṣate | nanu bhūyasāpi pravṛtte darśanādarśane ghaṭakulaṭādāvupalabdho vyabhicāra iti cet ? kimetāvatā, tatrāpyanumānamastvityucyate, atha tadvad dhūmādāvapi mā bhūditi ?
prathamapakṣastāvad vyabhicārādeva nirastaḥ | dvitīyo'pyavyabhicārādeva | na hyanyasya vyabhicāre dhūmasya kiñcit | na khalu viṣānnamaniṣṭamiti bhakṣyāntaramapi heyamastu |
tāvatā ca sarvā nivṛttirlabdheti kimutpattiprārthanayā, tanniścayopayoginā vā pratyakṣānupalambhena ? tadutpattirapi yadi darśanādarśanādeva gṛhyeta kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? anumānameva ca vibhāgena bhavatviti tadanveṣaṇam | sa ca vibhāgo vyabhicārāvyabhicāradvāreṇa siddhaḥ | asati ca vyabhicāre tāvataiva gamakatvam, anarthikā tadutpattiḥ | vyabhicāre ca śatamapi tadutpattayo na samarthāḥ | tasmāt sannikarṣeṇa paryeṣaṇaṃ saṃyogenaiva kṛtārtham | ataeva saṃyogī heturucyate vahnerdhūmo na kāryamiti |
[161,3]
trilocanastvāha, pratyakṣānupalambhayorviśeṣaviṣayatvāt kathaṃ tābhyāṃ sāmānyayoḥ sambandhapratītiḥ ? athānagnivyāvṛttenādhūmavyāvṛttasya sambandhaḥ pratīyata eveti, nanu so'pi kasya pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ ? na tāvat pratyakṣasya, tasya svalakṣaṇaviṣayatvāt |
nāpyanumānasya, tasyāpi tatpūrvakatvāt | na ca vyāvṛttaḥ kaścit sambandhaḥ | atha pratyakṣapṛṣṭhabhāvī vikalpo dṛṣṭe bhede'bhedamadhyavasyati, tadeva sāmānyam | evamapi vikalpānāṃ na vastveva viṣayaḥ, api tu grāhyākāraḥ | sa ca na vastu | vastu tu teṣāṃ parokṣameveti kathaṃ tenāpi sambandhagrahaḥ ? asmākaṃ tu bhūyodarśanasahāyena manasā tajjātīyānāṃ sambandho gṛhīto bhavati, ato dhūmo nāgniṃ vyabhicarati | tadvyabhicāre dhūma upādhirahitaṃ sambandhamatikrāmediti hetorvipakṣaśaṅkānivartakaṃ pramāṇamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptopādhivirahaheturanupalambhākhyaṃ pratyakṣameva | tataḥ siddhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ |
[162,1]
vācaspatestu prapañcaḥ, tathā hi dhūmādīnāṃ vahnyādibhiḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ, na tu vahnyādīnāṃ dhūmādibhiḥ | te hi vināpi dhūmādibhirupalabhyante | yadā tu ārdrendhanasambandhamanubhavanti tadā dhūmādibhiḥ sambadhyante | tasmād vahnyādīnāmārdrendhanādyupādhikṛtaḥ sambandhaḥ, na tu svābhāvikaḥ | tato na niyataḥ | svābhāvikastu dhūmādīnāṃ vahnyādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ, tadupādheranupalabhyamānatvāt | kvacid vyabhicārasyādarśanāt | anupalabhyamānasyāpi kalpanānupapatteḥ | na cādṛśyamāno'pi darśanānarhatayā sādhakabādhakapramāṇābhāvena sandihyamāna upādhiḥ sambandhasya svābhāvikatvaṃ pratibadhnātīti yuktam,
[162,2]
avaśyaṃ śaṅkayā bhāvyaṃ niyāmakamapaśyatām (pra. vā., 3. 324)
[162,3]
iti ca dattāvakāśā laukikapramāṇamaryādātikrameṇa saṃśayapiśācī labdhaprasarā na kvacinnāstīti nāyaṃ kvacit pravarteta, sarvatraiva kasyacidanarthasya kathañcit śaṅkāspadatvāt |
anarthaśaṅkāyāśca prekṣāvatāṃ nivṛttyaṅgatvāt | antataḥ snigdhānnapānopayoge'pi maraṇadarśanāt | tasmāt prāmāṇikalokayātrāmanupālayatā yathādarśanamāśaṅkanīyam, na tu adṛṣṭapūrvamapi | viśeṣasmṛtyapekṣa eva hi saṃśayo nāsmṛterbhavati | na ca smṛtirananubhūtacare bhavitumarhati | taduktaṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārtikakṛtā, nāśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā (ślo. vā., sū. 2. 60)
iti | tathā tenaiva bṛhaṭṭīkāyām, utprekṣeta hi yo mohādajātamapi bādhakam | sa sarvavyavahāreṣu saṃśayātmā kṣayaṃ vrajet ||
iti | tasmādupādhiṃ prayatnenānviṣyanto'nupalabhamānā nāstītyavagamya svābhāvikatvaṃ sambandhasya niścinumaḥ |
[162,4]
syādetadanyasyānyena sahākāraṇena cet svābhāvikaḥ sambandho bhavet, sarvaṃ sarveṇa svabhāvataḥ sambadhyeta, sarvaṃ sarvasmād gamyeta | athānyasya cedanyat kāryam, kasmāt sarvaṃ sarvasmānna bhavati, anyatvāviśeṣāt ? tataśca sa evātiprasaṅgaḥ | yadyucyeta na bhāvasvabhāvāḥ paryanuyojyāḥ, tasmādanyatvāviśeṣe'pi kiñcideva kāraṇaṃ kiñcicca kāryamiti, nanveṣa svabhāvānanuyogo'kāryakāraṇabhūtānāmapi svabhāvapratibandhe tulya eva | tasmāt yatkiñcidetadapi |
[163,1]
kena punaḥ pramāṇenaiṣa svābhāvikaḥ sambandho gṛhyate ? pratyakṣasambandheṣu pratyakṣeṇa | tathā hi yadā tāvat prathamaṃ vahnidhūmayoḥ sahārdrendhanayoḥ sambandhaṃ paśyati, tadā kiṃ dvayorapi svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ aupādhiko vā; atha dhūmasyaupādhikaḥ, vahneḥ svābhāvikaḥ, vahneraupādhiko dhūmasya svābhāvika iti ca na śakyaṃ nirdhārayitum |
tatra vahneranārdrendhanasya vinā dhūmamayogolakādau darśanādārdrendhanopādhirasya dhūmena sambandho, na tu svābhāvika iti niścīyate | dhūmaviśeṣasya tu vinā vahnimanupalambhādupādhibhedasya cānupalabhyamānasya kalpanāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāt viśeṣasmṛtyapekṣasya saṃśayasyānupalabdhapūrve'nutpādāt | utpāde vātiprasaṅgāt | prekṣāvatāṃ pravṛttyucchedāt svābhāvikaḥ sambandho'vadhāryate |
[163,2]
tadidamavadhāraṇaṃ na mānasam, anapekṣasya manaso bāhyeṣu pravṛttābandhavadhirābhāvaprasaṅgāt | bhūyodarśanasāpekṣasya ca pravṛttau pramāṇāntarāpātāt | na hi mano nimittamityeva mānasam | tathā sati na kiñcinna mānasam, pratyayamātrasya manonimittatvāt | tattadasādhāraṇakāraṇāpekṣayā ca tattatpramāṇavyapadeśe'trāpi bhūyodarśanam asādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇamastīti pramāṇāntaraṃ jātam | tasmādabhijātamaṇibhedatattvavad bhūyodarśanajanitasaṃskārasahāyamindriyameva dhūmādīnāṃ vahnyādibhiḥ svābhāvikasambandhagrāhīti yuktam |
[163,3]
evaṃ mānāntaraviditasambandheṣu mānāntarāṇyeva yathāsvaṃ bhūyodarśanasahāyāni svābhāvikasambandhagrahaṇe pramāṇamunnetavyāni | svabhāvataśca pratibaddhā hetavaḥ svasādhyena yadi sādhyamantareṇa bhaveyuḥ, svabhāvādeva pracyaveranniti tarkasahāyā nirastasādhyavyatirekasandehā yatra dṛṣṭāstatra svasādhyamupasthāpayantyeva | na ca śyāmatādiṣu maitratanayatvādīnāṃ svābhāvikapratibandhasaṃbhavaḥ, annapānapariṇatibhedasyopādheḥ śyāmatāyā maitratanayatvasambandhaṃ prati vidyamānatvena maitratanayatvasyāgamakatvāt | etena pakvānyasya vṛkṣasyāgravartīni phalāni, etadvṛkṣaprabhavatvāt, āsvāditaphalavadityādayo'pyaupādhikasambandhā vyākhyātāḥ | tasmād yasya svābhāvikaḥ sambandho niyataḥ so'numānāṅgam, yathā dhūmakṛtakatvādiḥ | yasya tvaupādhikaḥ, so'numānāṅgaṃ na bhavati, yathā tatputratvādiriti sthitam |
[164,1]
atrocyate, vyāptirnāma vyāpakasya tatra bhāva eva, vyāpyasya vā tatraiva bhāva ityevaṃ kartṛkarmadharmatayā pratīteranvayavyatirekarūpatayā dvidhānumānasamīhayā samīhitā, anyathānumāne'nupayogāt | yadi hi sādhane satyavaśyaṃ sādhyaṃ bhavatyeveti sāmānyena siddhaṃ bhavati, sādhyābhāve vā sādhanamavaśyaṃ na bhavatīti, tadā viśeṣoddeśena sādhanavati sādhyapratyāśā bhavati, sādhyābhāve tadabhāvasya | yadā tu na yathoktaniyamaḥ, tadā sādhanaṃ ca bhavati na ca sādhyamityāśaṅkāyāṃ kathamanumānāvakāśaḥ ? tasmādanumānamicchatā niyataṃ yathoktaiva vyāptirapekṣitavyā | na ca bhūyodarśanamātreṇa tasyāḥ siddhiḥ |
yathā hi yadṛcchayāpi sakṛt saṃvādasaṃbhāvanā, tathā katipayavārānapi yadṛcchayaiva bhavataḥ saṃvādasya niṣedhaḥ, yathā ca sakṛt sahacāradarśane vyabhicāra upalabdha iti na sarvatra sarvadā ca tatsahacāraniyama iti śaṅkā, tathā bhūyodarśane'pi vyabhicāradarśanādeva bhavantī na śakyaniṣedhā |
[164,2]
yat tu vyabhicāradarśanādananumānamuktam, tanna yuktam | tathā hi kasya punariha vyabhicāradarśanamanumānavidhnāya prayojakam | kiṃ pratipattureva, atha śāstrakārasya, yasya kasyacid vā ? antyapakṣe pratipattuḥ kimāyātam, yato nānumānamayaṃ kuryāt ?
anyathānyasya tattadviṣayapratyakṣīkāreṇaiva so'pi kṛtārtha iti kimanumānamavaśyamanveṣate ? śāstrakāraṃ ca pṛṣṭvā adṛṣṭasambandho'pi dhūmādagnimanumāsyate ityalaukikam | pratipattustu nāvaśyaṃ sannapi vyabhicāro gocarībhavati | na hi yatra vyabhicārastatraiva tāvati kāle deśe vāvaśyaṃ pratītimavatarati | apratīyamānaśca nāstyeveti na śakyamavasātum, ātyantikakālavyavadhāne'pi vā darśanāt, anupajātabādhabuddhīnāmapi nidhanasannidheravarodhācca | tataśca satyapi vyabhicāre pratipatturdarśanaṃ saṃbhāvyate | bhavati cāvyabhicāre'numānamanyathā netyupadiṣṭasya smaran kimasāvavyabhicāraniścayādanumāne pravartatām, nivartatāṃ vā'darśanamātreṇa niścayāyogādavyabhicārāsiddheḥ sandigdhāsiddhahetuvat | tatrādyapakṣe karabhādapyanumānaṃ kuryāt | dvitīye tu na dhūmādapi | na hi vidyamānasyāvidyamānasya vā vyabhicārasyānavalokanakāle kaścid viśeṣaḥ | tato yadi bhūyāṃsamapi sahopalambhaṃ karabhagardabhayoryādṛcchikamāśaṅkate, tathā dhūmadahanayorapi kasmānneti samānam | atha pratyāsannayorapi karabhagardabhayoḥ svātantryeṇopalakṣyamāṇayoḥ paśyāmi tāvat kimekamapasāryamāṇamanyo'nudhāvati dhenumiva vatsa iti jijñāsayā tathānutiṣṭhanna tathā pratipadyate | vahnau tvapasārite dhūmāpagamameva pratyeti, vahnisannidhāne vā dhūmasaṃbhavam |
[165,1]
ataḥ saṃbhāvyate vyabhicāraḥ karabhasyānyadāpi na dhūmasyeti cet ? viśiṣṭameva tarhi darśanādarśanaṃ dhūme utpattigrāhakaṃ ca yādṛśaṃ tādṛśaṃ na karabhe | tathāhi yadāgnyabhāve dhūmābhāvaṃ pratyeti, tadā sahopalambhapūrvakamagnimātrābhāve dhūmādarśanamupayuktaṃ pratibandhasiddhau | anyathā sahadarśanābhāve tāvadaṅgārāviśeṣacitrabhānumātrāpasāraṇaṃ ca dhūmaśca nāstyeva, karabhavad gardabhābhāva iti kva sambandhabodhaḥ ? sahadarśane'pi yadi vastvantarasahitahutāśāpasāraḥ, tadā pūrvamasya sattā kiṃ hutāśasya vastvantarasya vā sattayā prayukteti na niścayaḥ, hutāśamātrābhāve tu tadbhāvaprayukta eva prāgasya bhāva iti sulabham | yadāpi pāvakamātrasannidhau dhūmasattā, tadāpi pūrvamubhayādarśanapūrvakamagnimātropadarśane darśanaṃ dhūmasyopayuktam, anyathāgnimātramānītaṃ dhūmaścāstyeveti karabhavat kutra pratibandhasiddhiḥ vastvantarasahitahutāśanānayane'pi kasyābhāvena prayuktaḥ prāgabhāvo dhūmasyeti na niścayaḥ |
hutāśamātropalambhe tu tadabhāvaprayukto yuktaḥ |
[165,2]
tadevaṃ pūrvadarśanāpekṣaniyataikādarśanapūrvaṃ cānyādarśanaṃ viśiṣṭamucyate | tadapi prācīnadarśanamautarakālikayathoktādarśanadvayāpekṣayā viśiṣṭam | evamadarśanapūrvake'pi darśane viśeṣa ūhitavyaḥ, yadabhāvāt karabhādau nāśvāsaḥ | tameva darśanādarśanayorviśeṣamāśritya pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāravyavahāraḥ tadviṣayaśca bhāvadvayasvabhāvaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāva ityucyate |
[165,3]
yaccāyattamanāyatte paratra tat tatra tadutpattyā pratibaddhamityapi | tathā hi tanmātrāpanayane dvitīyasāhityasyāpi niṣedhād vyaktaṃ tadāyattaṃ tat | evaṃ tanmātrāpasāraṇe'pi bīddhavyam, anyathā dvitīyāpasāraṇāpekṣaṇāt kutastannātrāpasāraṇamiti tadutpattyaiva pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanayā vyāptiruktā bhavati, na tadviśeṣavirahiṇā darśanādarśanamātreṇa ?
tadviśeṣāpekṣaṇe ca sakṛdeva pravṛttau nirvṛttilābhānna bhūyaḥ pravṛttyapekṣā | yathā hi sakṛd darśanādarśanena pratītasahacāramātrādanāśvāsakarānnāparamapareṇa pratyayam, tathā sakṛt pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ pratītaviśiṣṭajātidvayahetuphalabhāvasambandhānnāparamparābhyāṃ pratyeyamiti tāvataiva nirvṛttiḥ | yadi na sādṛśyādinā jātyantare tadadhyavasāyaḥ puruṣasyeti nipuṇena pratipattrā bhavitavyam | sahacāramātre tu tajjātāveva saṃśayaḥ | anyatra sahacāramātre vyabhicāradarśanaṃ ca puṣṭaṃ bījamasya | na cātra viṣānnadṛṣṭāntaḥ śāntaye, viṣānnād bhojyāntarasya bhinnajātīyatvāt | atra tu yaḥ prayojako bhāgo bhūyaḥ sahacāralakṣaṇastenaikajātīyatvameva dhūmasya, na tu viṣadigdhatvaṃ dadhibhaktādeḥ sādhāraṇamiti vaiṣamyam | tadutpattimantareṇa cāvyabhicārasyaivābhāvād bhede avyabhicārasyaiva tadutpattirūpatvāt | avyabhicārāpekṣayā kṣepastadutpatterayukta eva | tasmāt kāryameva heturdhūmo dhūmadhvajasya, tadutpattyāvyabhicārākṣepāt; na saṃyogī, sahacāramātrollekhāt |
kathaṃ tarhi karabhagardabhodāharaṇamasaṃyogāt ? dāsīkalasasaṃyogadarśanabhūmnā santoṣo'stu |
karabhagardabhayorapi vā jalabalākayoriva tāvati kāle deśe'vasthitiniyamastathā darśanādastviti na kiñcidetat | tasmādarthāntare gamye kāryahetuḥ, tadbhāvasiddhiśca pratyakṣānupalambhāditi sthitam |
[166,1]
trilocanacodye tu brūmaḥ, viśeṣaviṣayaṃ pratyakṣamiti kiṃ viśeṣo'pi viṣayo'sya, atha viśeṣa eva ? ayogavyavacchedapakṣe na sāmānyaviṣayatāpratihatiriti kathaṃ na pratyakṣānupalambhāvakāśaḥ sāmānyadvaye ? anyayogavyavacchedastu kimasmatsiddhāntāśrayeṇa ucyate, vastuvṛttyā vā ? asmākaṃ tāvadubhayamubhayamapi pramāṇamubhayaviṣayam, grāhyādhyavasāyabhedena | yaddhi yatra jñāne pratibhāsate tad grāhyam, yatra tu tatpravartate tadadhyavaseyam |
tatra pratyakṣasya svalakṣaṇaṃ grāhyamadhyavaseyaṃ ca sāmānyam | anumānasya tu viparyayaḥ | tatra sādhanapratyakṣaṃ tadaivārthakriyārthinaḥ kṣaṇavokṣaṇe'pi santānāpekṣayā sāmānyaviṣayam |
vyāptigrahaṇaprakaraṇe punarekavyaktidarśane'pi sarvasajātīyavyaktiviṣayatvena sāmānyaviṣayam | pratyakṣeṇa mayā agnijanmā dhūmaḥ paricchinna iti sakalatadanyāpoḍhavyaktijātamantarbhāvyaiva tadbalotpannasyādhyavasāyasya saṃvedanāt | yathā rūpamātradarśane rūparasagandhasparśasamudāyaviśeṣātmani ghaṭe dṛṣṭādhyavasāyāt tadviṣayatvaṃ pratyakṣasya |
[166,2]
na ca sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñcidanyadeva, kiṃtu svalakṣaṇānyeva parasparamavivecitabhedāni sāmānyamucyante | bhedavivecane tu pratyekaṃ svalakṣaṇamiti svaśabdenaiva vyavahāraḥ | tato yadyapi paravilakṣaṇāśeṣasvalakṣaṇānāmapratibhāsānna grāhyatvena viṣayatvam, tathāpyadhyavaseyatvena durnivāramiti kathamanyayogavyavacchedaḥ ? vikalpānāmavastveva viṣaya ityapi parakṛtāntānabhijñatayaivocyate, anusandhānānumānayoradhyavasāyāpekṣayāvastuviṣayatvāt |
śeṣaṃ siddhasādhanam | atha vastuvṛttyeti pakṣaḥ ? so'pyayuktaḥ, sarvajñānānāṃ grāhyādhyavaseyabhedena viṣayadvaividhyasya duratikramāt | pramāṇasya hi prāmāṇyamevātiricyate, viṣayadvaitaṃ tu sarvatra siddham | tatrānumāne tāvadvastuno'pratibhāsādadhyavaseyameva svalakṣaṇam, grāhyastu svākāraḥ | evaṃvidhaṃ nirloṭhitamasmābhirapohaprakaraṇe iti na prastūyate | yadyapi ca buddherākāro neṣṭastathāpi vastubalādāyātaḥ kathamapohituṃ śakyaḥ ?
na hyapratibhāse jñānaṃ nāma, pratibhāsi cānumāyāṃ na vastviti sthite niyataṃ svākāraḥ |
alīkamastviti cet ? tathāpi tatpratibhāse grāhyamavaseyaṃ ca bāhyamiti viṣayadvaitasiddhau kiṃ nirbandhena ? evaṃ pratyakṣe'pi kācideva vyaktiḥ pratibhāsinī grāhyā | sarvā tu sajātīyādhyavaseyā pratibandhabodhakāle, asphuraṇe hi yadyavasāyo'pi syāt pratyakṣeṇa sambandhabodhaprasiddhigandho'pi nirdhūtaḥ syāt |
[167,1]
yattu mānasena bhūyodarśanajanitasaṃskārasahāyenendriyeṇa vā grahaṇamuktam, tatredaṃ vicāryate | asti tāvadagnidhūmavyaktyoḥ punaḥ punarupalabdhiraindriyī | asti ca tatkṛtasaṃskārajanmā vimarśaḥ ayametatsahita evopalabhyate, tat kimanayoḥ sadātano'yaṃ sahacāraḥ, atha suhṛddvayasyeva sātyaya iti ? parāmarśadurbalasya hetunāntarīyakapratītirapi bhavati | tadanurūpaṃ cānuṣṭhānam | na punaratrāparo jñānavivartaḥ saṃvedyate | tato bhūyodarśanaṃ tāvat saṃskāradvāreṇa sahāyameva kṛtam, na tatprastutamabhidhātuṃ śakyam, tadantimamekajātikāśeṣavyaktiviṣayaka ityapi manorathamātram, tadvyaktīnāṃ nirbhāsābhāvāt | saṃśayo'pi tadanantaraḥ saṃśayatvādeva na niścāyakaḥ sambandhasya | paścimaśca niścayākāratve'pi parāmarśaśūnyasyaiveti pratyakṣābhikhyayāpi tadupasthāpite prameye ka āśvāsaḥ ? aliṅgajasya hi vikalpasya pūrvapravṛttadarśanavyāpāranusārādevārthatathābhāvasambhavo, na svātantryāt, atiprasaṅgāt, pūrvapravṛttāni ca darśanāni sahacāramātrasākṣīṇi vātātapādisahacāravat kañcid viśeṣamanāviśanti kathamasya yathārthatāṃ samarthayitumīśate ? tathābhāve'pi tānyeva tatra pramāṇam, idaṃ tu smaraṇaṃ pramāṇatvena nirdiśyata iti sādhu | vātātapayoḥ paścāt sahacāravighaṭanāsti viśeṣa iti na vācyam, vyabhicārādarśanakālāpekṣayābhedasya vivakṣitatvāt, atrāpi avighaṭananiścayānupapatteścoktatvāt | yāvadeva vahnivyāpārāt pūrvaṃ dhūmānudayo hṛdayasaṃvāsī, tāvadeva hi sahacārāntarād bhedavimarśaḥ, tata eva tadvyabhicāre dhūma upādhirahitaṃ sambandhamatikrāmediti śobhate | anyathā pūrvaṃ sahacāramātropalabdhau yathā dhūmamantareṇānalavilokane analasya dhūmena sambandhe upādhikalpanaṃ sāmānyena, tathā dhūmasyāpi vahnimantareṇa bhāvasaṃbhāvanāyāmupādhyantarakalpanaṃ bhaviṣyati, ataḥ kasya kenaupādhikaḥ svābhāviko vā sambandhaḥ syāt ? na hi suhṛdorekavyatirekeṇānyadarśane'vyatirekeṇāpi taddarśanasaṃbhāvanā na bhavati | kevalaṃ caitramantareṇāpi maitrasya bhāvāvirodhād bhūdharavivarapraviṣṭasyāpi na darśanayogyatā vigalati, dhūmasya tu niyataṃ vinā vahnimudaya eva nāstīti na saṃbhāvanā, tāvatā ca tadutpattireva śaraṇīkṛtā bhavati | sā ca na bhūyodarśanādityuktameva |
[168,1]
ata eva gogotvayorapi na svābhāvikaḥ sambandho'bhidhātuṃ śakyaḥ, tadutpattipratītivirahe'nyasmāt sahacāriṇo viśeṣābhāvāt | na ca sahacāradarśanamapyasti, pratyakṣeṇobhayabhāgānullekhāt | tat kimatra svābhāvikaupādhikavādaprakṣepeṇa vibhāgena ? gamakatvaṃ ca sāmagryāḥ kāraṇatvādekaṃ kāraṇamanyāpekṣameva janakamityaniyamaḥ |
kāryaṃ tu sāmagrīniyatatvena pratyekaṃ niyatamiti tadeva liṅgaṃ na kāraṇamiti siddham |
athāgnerindhanasannidhau dhūmadarśanād viśeṣoddeśenaiva siddha upādhirindhanam | dhūmasya punaragninā sambandhe tadupādhirbhavan dṛśya eva bhavet, anupalabdhastu nāstītyucyate |
tat kimindhanameva paramupādhiryena dṛśyatāniyamaḥ sambandhe hi vivakṣyate, apekṣaṇīyamarthāntaraṃ svabhāvaviśeṣa eva copādhirabhidheyaḥ | na cārthāntaraṃ dṛśyatāniyatam | tataśca dhūmasyāpi hutāśena saha sambandhe syādupādhiḥ, na copalakṣyata iti kathamadarśanānnāstyeva, yataḥ svābhāvikasambandhasiddhiḥ ?
[168,2]
atha yadyapekṣaṇīyamarthāntaraṃ syāt, kathaṃ dhūma ityeva pāvakasya sattāniyama iti cet ? nanvidameva cintyate, kiṃ dhūme sati avaśyamagniḥ sambhavī, na veti ?
kadācidarthāntaramupādhimapekṣya dhūmo'pi syāt, nāgniriti kimatra niṣṭaṅkakāraṇam ?
tasmāt pāvakaparādhīnodayo dhūmaḥ pariniṣṭhataḥ kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi bhāvaṃ svīkuryādityeva sādhu | asiddhā ceyamupādhyanupalabdhiḥ | yathā hi dahano nendhanena vinā dhūmena saṃbadhyate, tathā dhūmo'pi na tena vinā'gni saṃbadhyata iti samānamupādhitvamindhanasyobhayatra | atha siddhasyāgnerindhanasāhityena dhūmalābha ityupādhivyavasthā, asiddhasya tu dhūmasya tannimittātmalābhatayā tadavyabhicārāt svābhāvikaḥ sthāpyata iti cet ? evamapi saiva tadutpattirāyātā, saiva ca svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ | na ca yathoktamānasādigrāhyaḥ | na copādhirdṛśyānupalabdhibādhya ityaupādhikaśaṅkāyāṃ na vipakṣānnivṛttirdhūmasyeti sthitam ||
[169,1]
vācaspatye tu prabandhe'gnerdhūmena saṃbandhe indhanamupādhirdṛśya ukta eva | dhūmasya tu vahninā sambandhe svābhāvikatvamupādheranupalabdhimātreṇa ca bādhaḥ | tatra ca kvacid vyabhicārasyādarśanāditi hetuḥ | tatredamālocyate, kimayaṃ heturupādhyanupalabdhisādhakaḥ, atha saivāsya sādhikāyaṃ svābhāvikatvasya bhūtānupalabdheradārḍhyaṃśaṅkayopādhereva bādhakaḥ ?
prathame nirupayogaḥ, na hi buddherbhāvābhāvau hetvantarasādhyau, svasaṃvedyavedanāntarasvabhāvatvāt | nāsti copādherupalabdhiriti siddhaivānupalabdhiḥ | evaṃ vyabhicārādarśane'pi hetvanupayogo vācyaḥ | vyavahārasādhanamupayoga iti cet — na, vimaterabhāvāt, apratītimātrasya siddhatvāt | tṛtīyo'pi na yuktaḥ | ekasyā dṛśyaviśeṣaṇarahitāyā niṣedhasādhanāśaktau dvitīyasyāḥ kīdṛśī śaktiḥ ? vyabhicāro dṛśya eva vivakṣita iti cet ? tarhi na sarvatra sarvadā vā | tataśca na kvacid vyabhicāra ityataḥ svābhāvikatvamayuktam | kvacit tu na dṛṣṭo vyabhicāra ityevaṃ tatkalpanamanalasyāpi dhūmena prasajyeta |
caitramaitrādīnāṃ vā parasparam | sati caivaṃ svābhāvikasambandhe'pyanāśvāsa ityāyātam |
[169,2]
tasmāt sarvatraivāvyabhicāraḥ paryeṣaṇīyaḥ | tato'numānaviṣaye'pi yāvanna sādhyaṃ pratyakṣeṇopasthāpayati, tāvannāvyabhicāraṃ pratīyāditi kṛtamanumānena | kiṃ ca tadutpattivāderṣyayā dhūmasyānekāntaparihārāya svābhāvikavāda āśritaḥ, anekāntaśca vyabhicārāśaṅkayā | tataḥ svābhāvikatvādavyabhicāraḥ sarvatra | sarvatrāvyabhicārācca svābhāvikatvamitītaretarāśrayaḥ | yasya tu sakṛdekajāteranyajātyadhīnotpattipratītireva sarvatrāvyabhicārapratītiḥ, tasya nāyaṃ prasaṅgaḥ, bhūyodarśanāpekṣāyāmeva tadavatārasya nyāyaprāptatvāt | yathā hyekadā darśane śaṅkāyāmanyāpekṣā, tathānyadāpi śaṅkāpekṣā | parasparākṛṣṭa eva sarvatra darśanākṣepaḥ | yadi tu tatrāpi vārasaṃkhyāniyamaṃ darśayet, yathāsmākam — prāgadṛṣṭau kramāt paśyan vetti hetuphalasthitim | dṛṣṭau vā kramaśo'paśyannanyathātvena ca sthitiḥ ||
iti pratyakṣānupalambhayorvāratrayaniyamo'vayave, samudāye tvekavārasya, tadā tāvataiva sustho bhavet | bhūya iti tvapariniṣṭhitasaṃkhyaḥ kiyatā nirvṛttimāsādayet lakṣyānusārī ?
tadaśakyatve ca na kvacidanumānamayaṃ kuryāditi lakṣaṇaśāstramanarthakam | smaraṇe tu cittapāṭavādhānāya kiyadapi darśanaṃ pravartsyati | na tatra parimāṇaniyamamantareṇa kiñcit kṣīyate, bīje'ṅkurajananāya kālaparimāṇaniyamavat | evamabhijātamaṇitattvasphuṭībhāve'pi na darśanānāṃ parimāṇaniyamaḥ | sūkṣmarūpabhedodbhedamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt, prabhāsvarādivāvarakapraviṣṭasya | yamalakavad vā | dhūmādau tu na rūpasya bhedo vivakṣitaḥ, kiṃ tu svarūpasya | yathā hi nīletararūpayoḥ prāk paṭīyaso'pi koṭirapi darśanāni na bhedāvadhāraṇapaṭūni, tathā vyabhicāradarśanāt prāk vyabhicārāvyabhicāravatorarthāntare sannidhīyamānayorna kiñcid rūpabhedāvadhāraṇam | dhūme tu na rūpādviśeṣollekhi hṛdayamapi tu pāvakādhīnasaṃbhavatayetyuktam | ata eva ca sakṛtpravṛttapratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ nirvṛttiḥ |
rūpāpekṣayā tu dhūme'pi yādṛgeva darśanamādyaṃ tādṛgeva koṭitamamapi na maṇivadviśeṣabhāk |
tādṛgeva darśane yadi vyabhicāraśaṅkārahitaḥ pratipattā, tadā na dvitīyasyāpi darśanasya apekṣā | śaṅkamānastu śatenāpi darśanairapratyaya eveti bhūya iti bhavadīyamantrākṣarajāpinaḥ kā gatiḥ ? ataśca śatadhāpyavyabhicāradarśī purastāt sandehavāneva |
[170,1]
yat tvanupalabhyamānasyāpi kalpanānupapatteriti supteneva vilapitam, tad bālasyāpyasāmpratam | anupalabhyamānasyaiva hi kalpanā bhavati prakṛtīśvarādivat |
kalpitaṃ tu kiñcit pramāṇamanveti kiñcinneti viśeṣaḥ | na hi dṛśyamāno ghaṭaḥ kalpita ucyate | tasmādanupalabhyamāneṣveva kalpanāvyavahāraḥ, kevalaṃ kvacidāptavacanādinā bādhakādarśanād dṛḍhaḥ sattāvasāyaḥ, vimarśakasya tu pākṣikaḥ | tato dhūmasyāpi yadi vyabhicāro dṛṣṭo, dṛṣṭa eva | kastatra saṃśayaḥ ? yadā tu na dṛṣṭastadā sattaikāṃśāvasāyo mā bhūt prāmāṇikādhikārāt, pākṣikastu sattollekhaḥ kathaṃ vāryaḥ ? athaivamabhiprāyaḥ, na tatraivānupalabdhirvivakṣitā, kiṃ tvanyatrāpi yannopalabhyaṃ tasya na śaṅketi cet ? nanvagnivyabhicāraścāmīkarādau dṛṣṭa evetyastu santoṣaḥ | atha dhūme na dṛṣṭaḥ, tat kiṃ sthāṇau puruṣatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yena sthāṇau śaṅkyate ? ūrdhvatāliṅgite dṛṣṭamiti cet ? ihāpi bhūyaḥ sahacāriṇi dṛṣṭa evānyatra | ata eva na cādṛśyamāno'pītyādi viplatam | yatraiva tu yat saṃśayyate, tatraiva tasya darśanamapekṣyata ityalaukikam | ato dhūmajātāvadṛśyamāno'pi vyabhicāra upādhirvā darśanāyogyatayā niṣeddhumaśakyaḥ | sa idānīṃ saṃśayaḥ svābhāvikatvasaṃśayasvabhāvaḥ svābhāvikatvaniścayaṃ tāvadavaśyaṃ pratibadhnāti | svābhāvikasaṃbandhabalena ca dhūmo gamakaḥ kathaṃ tadaniścaye gamakatvena gṛhyeta ? na hi dharmiṇi sattvena heturgamakaḥ sattvasandehe'pi gamako bhavitumarhati | yaśca yatsandehe pravartate sa tadasambhave'pi pravartata eveti svābhāvikasaṃbandhaṃ vidhūyāpi dhūmasyevānyasyāpi gamakatvaprasaṅgaḥ | tasmānniścayapratibandhaḥ svābhāvikatvapratibandha evārthataḥ, niścayamantareṇa gamakāṅgasya svayamakiñcitkaratvāt | tasmānniragnau dhūmasya, avaśyaṃ śaṅkayā bhāvyaṃ niyāmakamapaśyatām (pra. vā., 3. 324)
iti durlaṅghyametattadutpattyanāśrayaṇe | na caivaṃ prāmāṇikalokamaryādātikramopālambhaḥ | na hi pramāṇagocare kaścidaniścayamācaṣṭe, pramāṇābhāve vā niścayam, yathā bhavānupādherbādhakapramāṇābhāve'pyabhāvaniścayam | ata eva na saṃśayapiśācasya sarvatrāvakāśaḥ pramāṇābhāva evānumatatvāt | pramāṇaviṣaye'pi kiñcidvaktuṃ śakyata iti cet ? yadi mukhamastīti vaktavyamucyatām | kevalaṃ yadi svīkṛtapramāṇadharmo vakti tadā sudānamuttaram | athetaraḥ, tadetareṇaiva vaktavyam, nāsmākamavasaraḥ | svīkṛtapramāṇasya hi niścayaphalatvāt pramāṇasyāvipratipannapramāṇaviṣaye niścayasvīkāranāntarīyaka eva tatsvīkāraḥ kathaṃ sarvatra śaṅkāpiśācī labdhāvakāśā bhavet ? kevalaṃ tvatpraṇītalakṣaṇaṃ na pramāṇamiti brūhi |
tacca vicāryamāṇameva vartate | athādṛśyamāno'pyupādhirdhūme śaṅkyata iti prāmāṇikalokayātrātikrama iti cet — na, prāmāṇikairevāyogyānupalabdherbādhādhikārapratiṣedhāt |
anyatheśvarasvargasādhanāderdatto jalāñjaliḥ | anumānāgamapramāṇasiddhernāyaṃ doṣa iti cet — na, pūrvamanupalabdhyā bādhite'numānādeḥ sādhakasyāpravṛtteḥ sarvajñasiddhau prasādhitatvāt |
[171,1]
tasmāt pūrvāparaparāmarśavivekaphalametadanupalabdhimātraṃ niścayasādhanamiti |
tataḥ pramāṇaviṣaye saṃśayānavakāśānnāyaṃ kvacitpravartetetyasaṃbaddham | na ca śaṅketyeva na pravṛttiḥ, arthasaṃśayena pravṛtteranivāryatvāt, snigdhānnapānavat | etat tvanarthakasaṃśayenodāharato'rthānarthasaṃśayaviṣayo'pyajñāta iti kimataḥ paraṃ vācyam ? na caitat prakṛtam, pramāṇavṛttau saṃśayo'stu na vetyasya prakṛtatvāt, tatra coktameva | athedamākūtamanekadhā dhūmasya dhāmanyavyabhicāradarśanāt kadācit tadantareṇa dhūmo bhaveditīyamanarthaśaṅkā |
