evaṃ tarhi tṛṇavahnirindhanavikārakriyānāntarīyakadhūmotpādanasamartho dṛṣṭa iti khādirastathā na syāt | sāmānyena tu vyāptirubhayatrāpīti na viśeṣaḥ | tato yadi khādire vikāravirahastadā nāsau dhūmo'pi tu vātyāsaṃvalitadhūlinivahaḥ | na vā tatra dhūmadhvajaḥ, kiṃ tu kāntimatpadmarāgaratnarāśiraśmisaṃhatirucchrāyavatī | yadi punarasau dhūmaḥ sa ca dhūmadhvajaḥ khādire vāvaśyaṃ vikāra iti, tathā yadyasau dharmibodhastatsādhanaśca śabdo, niyataṃ tadāśrayadharmabodhadoṣaḥ | na cet tadāśrayadharmabodhaḥ, tadā nāsau dharmibodho nāpi dharmibodhanaḥ śabdaḥ | yat kvacit jñānasādhanaṃ tat tadīyadharmāṇāṃ pratītisādhananiyataṃ yathendriyam | tathā ca liṅgaśabdau parokṣābhimatasya pratītisādhanāviṣṭau taveti svabhāvaḥ prasaṅgahetuḥ | na caivaṃ, śabdaliṅgāntarāpekṣaṇāt | yanna yatsamavetadharmabodhasādhanaṃ na tat tasya svarūpajñānajanakam, yathā gośabdasturage, turago vā gardabhe, na bodhayataśca godhulidhūmau svaviṣayābhimatasamavetadharmāntaramiti viparyaye vyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | jātiguṇakriyādirahitasya svapne'pi darśanaśaṅkāvirahād vastudarśanaṃ tatsattāmātrabhāvinā dharmāntarajñānena vyāpyata ityubhayorapi prayogayornānekāntaḥ | bhede eva hi jātyādīnāṃ vivādaḥ |
samavetaśabdastvabhedapakṣe'pi kalpanābuddhau bhinnavadābhāsamānānāmapṛthakprathanaparaḥ | tad varamabheda eva dharmāṇāmastu, sarvathā vastupratītisvīkāre dharmāṇāṃ pratīticodyasya duṣpariharatvāt, kimanubhavabhraṣṭabhedābhyupagamena ? svabhāvā eva bhāvasya jātyādayaḥ |
[214,2]
yattu bhāṣaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇasya, na ca yatsvabhāvasaṃbandhi sa svabhāvaḥ, tathā satyasaṃbandhitvameva, na hi tadeva tena sādhyata iti | tadasat | svabhāvasaṃbandhītyatraiva svabhāvaḥ kasyacidvastuno vivakṣitaḥ, na ca tayorbhedaḥ | bhede hi svabhāvatvamityalaukikametat |
tat kathaṃ tadeva tena saṃbaddhamiti parihṛtam, anyathāsya svabhāva iti ṣaṣṭhīnirdeśānupapatteḥ | atha svabhāva iti jātyādirevocyata iti na doṣa eva, yadā jātyādikaṃ vivicya vastumātrasvabhāvaparāmarśaḥ | na hyasau vastunaḥ kevalasya svabhāvo na vaktavyaḥ |
sa eva ca yatsvabhāvasaṃbandhītyatra vivakṣitaḥ, saṃbandhiśabdena jātyādervivakṣitatvāt |
tasmād yato yadabhinnamapi kalpanayā bhinnameva darśitam, tat tasya saṃbandhīti vyavahāro duṣpariharaḥ ||
[215,1]
yacca vācaspatiḥ, na caikopādhinā sattvena viśiṣṭe'smin gṛhīte upādhyantaraviśiṣṭatadgrahaḥ, svabhāvo hi dravyasyopādhirviśiṣyate, na tūpādhayo viśeṣyatvaṃ vā tasya svabhāva iti | tadapi plavata eva | na hyabhedādupādhyantaragrahaṇamāsañjitam, ākare'pyupakāryopakāradvāreṇa bhedaṃ puraskṛtyaiva sarvākāragrahaṇaprasañjanāt | śaktīnāṃ tu śaktimatoḥ abheda uktaḥ | tadanenāpi na spṛṣṭam |
[215,2]
yatpunastatra dūṣaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇena, sūryādigrahaṇe tadupakāryāśeṣavasturāśigrahaṇaprasañjanamuktam, tadabhiprāyānavagāhanaphalam, tathā hīdamākūtam | svayaṃ vakṣyamāṇasamavāyaniṣedhaṃ sthirīkṛtya bhavatā naiyāyikapravareṇa pratyakṣakāle'kṣasaṃbandhamanubhavitari dharmiṇi dharmāṇāṃ jātyādīnāṃ bhedābhyupagamādupakāryatayaiva tadupakārakaśaktyabhedāt pratipattireṣitavyā | na hyanupakāre kvacit kasyacit pratibandho bhedavata iti śaktyabhedāpādanamukhenāha, dharmopakāraśaktīnāṃ bhede tāstasya kiṃ yadi | nopakārastatastāsāṃ tathā syādanavasthitiḥ || (pra. vā. 3. 53)
iti | yattu śaktirnāma sahajā jātiraupādhikī ca sahakārisākalyamato bhinnaivetyālambanam, taddūṣayitvā kṣaṇābhaṅgādhyāye kāryakriyāpravṛtta eva svabhāvaḥ śaktirityeva nirvāhitam | upakāraśca samānakāryārjanasvabhāvo'kāryasyāpi saṃbhavatītyapi tatraiva dhvastam | kāryopakāryayorapi tattvato nāstyeva bhedaḥ, vyavahāre punarapūrvotpattau sohāpohāt kāryatā | pūrvasthitābhimānaviṣaye tu viśeṣānubhavādupakāryatocyate | tattvatastu pūrvasthitaścādhunā viśiṣṭaśceti viruddhameva | tadiha sthirābhimatajātipuraskāreṇa cintāyāṃ kāryatāniṣṭha evopakāryavyavahāraḥ, tattvata ekārthatayā veti na doṣaḥ | tadevam avaśyābhyupagantavyāyāmupakāralakṣaṇāyāṃ pratyāsattau sūryopakāryādibhiranubhavavyabhicāraḥ prasajyāyātaḥ sādhāraṇa evāvayoḥ |
[216,1]
yattu vācaspatiḥ, svābhāvikaśca saṃbandho vyakterjātyā saha nopakāramapekṣata iti |
tatra na svābhāviko nāma yathā prasiddhādanya eva kaścit saṃbandhaḥ, kiṃ tu saṃyogādisattāyāmeva saṃbandhinorvyabhicārāvyabhicāreṇa vṛttibhedādaupādhikaḥ, svābhāvikaśca sambandha iti vyavasthāmātram | etadvicāraśca vyāpticarcāyāmapekṣitavyaḥ | yathā ca jātthā saha vyaktestadavyabhicārāt svābhāvikaḥ saṃbandhastathā jāterapi vyaktyā sahāvyabhicārādeva, nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavet śaśaviṣāṇavat iti nyāyāt | tadanayoḥ pratyāsattyantarābhāvāt samavāyasya ca kalpanāmātratvād yadyupakāryopakārakabhāvo'pi parasparamasannavanibījādivat, avyabhicāraniyama eva bhedābhyupagamavyasanināmatiprasaṅgādanupapannaḥ | upakāre hi svabhāvastadviśeṣo vā tannāntarīyaka ityevāvyabhicārārtho nānyatreti nātiprasaṅgaḥ |
[216,2]
tadabhāve tu dvidhā tatparihāraḥ svabhāvavādaṃ samavāyabalaṃ vāvalambya | nādyaḥ pakṣaḥ, sarvasya yatra kvacana dṛṣṭaśakterviparyāsanaprasaṅgāt | dṛṣṭaścopakāro vahniśilpijalādau dhūmakumbhabalākāderavyabhicārahetuḥ | kevalaṃ kāladeśādyapekṣayeti viśeṣaḥ | tato bhede'pi svabhāvādevāvyabhicāro nopakāra iti bruvatā niyamena sāmarthyamapohitam | dvitīyapakṣaścāsambhavī, samavāyasyaivābhāvāt | ihedamiti buddhisādhano hi samavāyo'bhyupagataḥ, sā ca buddhirna samānasaṅketagrahatimiranikurambakarambitadṛśāmupādeyā, sarvasya sarvārthasiddhiprasaṅgāt | icchāmātraparatantrodayatvād vikalpānām | anyasya ca lokasya nāstyeva vivādapade sarvatra sā buddhiḥ, kāraṇābhāvāt | paraspararūpāsaṅkīrṇavastudvayapratibhāso hi kāraṇamihedamiti saptamīprathamārthavibhāgamutkalayato vikalpasya, kumbhe'mbhaḥsaṃbhave'pi kumbhamātropalambhinaḥ sakalānyakāraṇakalāpavatastadabhāvāt |
tādṛgavasthasya ca paścād dvitīyopalambhamātre bhāvāt | na cāsau dvayapratibhāsaḥ kvacidapi samavāyaviṣaye'stīti saṃyogakalpanāviṣaya eva tadvikalpaviṣayaḥ | yatrānātmarūpaparihāreṇa nobhayopalambho na tatredamiheti pratītiranunmattasya, yathā pātravadarayorekānupalambhe | nāsti cātmātmīyarūpapratibhāsabhedena jātitadvatoranubhava iti kāraṇānupalabdhiḥ | dhūmāgnivat kāryakāraṇabhāvasya vivakṣitayoḥ sādhanānnānekāntaḥ | tadamī svayaṃkṛtaśabdenārthāntaramupakalpayantasturagatulāmanupatantītyetadeva vakṣyati, paṭastantuṣvihetyādiśabdāśceme svayaṃ kṛtāḥ | (pra. vā. 2. 149)
iti | nanu nirvikalpakabodhena dvyātmakasyāpi vastuno grahaṇamityuktam, tat kathaṃ na svarūpadvayapratibhāsa ityasiddhā kāraṇānupalabdhiḥ ? tadetat pāpīyaḥ | na hi pratyakṣagamye'rthe paropadeśo garīyān | pratibhāso'pi tatheti cet ? tadetadāyātam, etāsu pañcasvavabhāsinīṣu pratyakṣabodhe sphuṭamaṅgulīṣu | sādhāraṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhamihekṣate yaḥ śṛṅgaṃ śirasyātmana īkṣate saḥ ||
iti | vayaṃ hi tāvaccarmacakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuṣī sudūramunmīlya śatakṛtvo nirūpayanto'pi nāparam upalabhāmahe, bhavatastvadṛṣṭadevatāprasādāt tathā pratibhāse'pi netarasya tathā bodhasiddhiḥ |
[217,1]
tena pratyakṣameva draṣṭavyaṃ yadekamanekasādhāraṇaṃ draṭraṣṇāṃ darśayatītyācakṣāṇaḥ trilocano'pyanyalocaneneva vīkṣata iti lakṣyate | yaccāha dṛśyamānāpi jātirapṛthagdeśavartitvād vyaktito bhedena vyaktyantaravanna dṛśyata iti | tatrāpi dṛśyate jātirna tu bhedeneti bruvatā niyamādabhedena pratyakṣagocara ityuktaṃ bhavati | yathā ca pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītaṃ tavaiva samastaṃ vastu, na khalu tatra bādhakasādhakayoryogaḥ | tataśca pratyayānuvṛttistu vyaktitaḥ sāmānyaṃ bhetsyatītyupapattivarṇanamanavakāśam | yathā spārśanaḥ pratyayo gandhādibhyaḥ sparśaṃ bhinattītyapi na yuktamuktam | na hi gandhasparśayorapyabhedagrāhi pratyakṣam |
[217,2]
evaṃ tarhi bhedena na dṛśyata iti bhedena na vyavasīyata iti vyākhyāyatām, tadāpi dṛśyamānāpi jātiriti kiṃ bhedenābhedena veti vivakṣitam ? yadyabhedena, tadā vyavasāyo bhedenābhedena vāstu, kimasya cintayā, pratyakṣeṇābhedasya siddhatvāt ? atha bhedena dṛśyamāneti vivakṣitam ? tat punaraśakyam, pratibhāsabhedābhāvasyoktatvāt | yuktyā sādhyate pratibhāsabheda iti cet ? tadetat lajjākaram | yataḥ, kasyacit pratibhāsena sādhyate'pratibhāsi yat | pratibhāso'sya nāsyeti nopapattestu gocaraḥ || (kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāye pṛḥ 111)
iti vivecitamasmābhirahetukābhāvaprastāve |
[218,1]
kiṃ ca yadyekākārapratibhāse'pi pratibhāsāntaraṃ yuktisādhyamabhyupeyate, tadā'nuṣṇo vahniriti na pratyakṣabādhyamabhidheyam, anuṣṇapratibhāsasyāpi tatra saṃbhavāt, vyaktau jātipratibhāsavat |
[218,2]
anuṣṇapratibhāsasya citrabhānau sādhanābhāvānna sāmyamiti cet ? tathāpi saṃśayo'stviti kathamanuṣṇasya bādhakamadhyakṣam, kathaṃ ca sādhanābhāvaḥ, prameyatvasya vidyamānatvāt ? avyabhicārī heturiti cet ? vyabhicāro'pi sākṣāt paramparayā vā pratyakṣādeva | tatra ca viparītapratibhāso niṣeddhumaśakya ityuktam | yadi cānaikāntikatayā prameyatvānna siddhiranuṣṇatāyā hetudoṣāt tarhi dṛṣṭamanuṣṇo'gniriti nāyaṃ pakṣadoṣaḥ, tato'nuṣṇatvābādhanāt | sādhanamapi nādhyakṣam | uṣṇameva hi uṣṇam |
na punaruṣṇānuṣṇam | tasmānniyatapratibhāsasaṃvedanamanyapratibhāsasya niyamena bādhakam abhyupagantavyamakāmakenāpi, anyathā pravṛttisaṅkaraprāpteḥ | tathā ca,
[218,3]
na hyayamanalaṃ paśyannityādi |
[218,4]
tato yadodhapatitairudghuṣyate, jātimatīṣu vyaktiṣu saṅkete kṛte yatra yatra jātidarśanaṃ tatra tatra tacchabdavācyatāpratītiriti, tadasūtramambaraṃ viḍambayati, svalakṣaṇavilakṣaṇasya svapne'pyanupalakṣaṇāt | ataeva svarūpamātreṇa gṛhītāvupādhitadvantau yojayato vikalpasya prāmāṇyamiṣṭaṃ yat tatpratyādiṣṭam, pūrvaṃ dvayadarśanasyaivābhāvāt | tasmānna kāraṇānupalabdherasiddhiḥ | asiddhiḥ punariheti pratyayasyeti kva samavāyavārtā ? vārtaṃ caitad vyakterjātyā saha svābhāvikaḥ saṃbandha iti ? tataśca yadyapyupādhitadvatāṃ bhedavādo duṣpariharaḥ, tadā upakāralakṣaṇāyāmapi pratyāsattau samānadeśasyaiva grahaṇe vastugrāhiṇaḥ śaktiṃriti samānaḥ sūkṣmopakāryavyabhicāraparihāraḥ |
[218,5]
tasmādekadharmadvāreṇāpi vastusvarūpapratītau sarvātmapratīteḥ kva śabdāntareṇa vidhiniṣedhāvakāśa iti kimadyāpi kevalavṛkṣapadena ? tataśca kva sāmānyasāmānādhikaraṇyaviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvavyavasthā ? yadā tu, ekārthaśleṣavicchede eko vyāpriyate dhvaniḥ | liṅgaṃ vā tava vicchinnaṃ vācyaṃ vastu na kiñcana || yasyābhidhānato vastusāmarthyādakhile gatiḥ | bhavennānāphalaḥ śabda ekādhāro bhavatyataḥ || (pra0 vā0 3, 128 — 30)
vastuni hi vācye sarvātmanā pratipattervidhiniṣedhayorayogaḥ | yadā punaranādivitathavikalpābhyāsavāsanāvaśādekavyāvṛttyākāraśekharā buddhireva kutaścid vāsanāprabodhād udayamāsādayati, tadā vastugrahaṇasāmarthyabhāvināmuktadoṣāṇāṃ kvāvakāśaḥ ? tathā hi vṛkṣa ityukte dhavakhadirādisādhāraṇarūpapratibhāsavaśāt sāmānyamavṛkṣāpohaparamārtham avasthāpyate | tacca rūpamapratikṣiptānupāttasattāsādvalatvādibhedatayā padāntaraprayogasāpekṣam ityekatra dharmiṇi dharmyantaranibandhanairiva sannīlacalādipadaiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca, tadā buddhyanurodhataḥ ekabhedacodanāpekṣāyāṃ vṛkṣasya sattvamiti bhedanirdeśaśceti dvividho'pi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ | evaṃ ca sati yathā pṛthvīruhe pātho'gnisaṅgamādupacayāpacayau dṛṣṭau, ekatvāropācca sa evāyaṃ pādapa īdṛśo jāta iti pratītiḥ, sa ca dharmāṇāṃ tatsaṃbandhayogyānāmanudaye'pi tadyogya iva vyavasīyate, tathā vikalpe'pi vṛkṣākāro dharmāntarāpratibhāse'pi tadyogya iti nīlo na phalina ityādiprayoge copacayāpacayabhāgiva bhāsate sa eveti cāvasīyate, na tathā bāhyo jalādisamparkavacchabdoccāraṇakāle'pyupacayāpacayavān | etacca na bāhyaviṣayatve yuktam, yathāpratibhāsam atattvāt, yathātattvaṃ cāpratibhāsanāt | ataeva caitrasya gaurgomān maitro nāśvavāniti bhinnaviśeṣaṇāpekṣayāpi na padāntaraprayogayogaḥ, tatkṛtopacayāpacayapratibhāsasya bahirabhāvāt |
[219,1]
tasmād buddhivilāsa evaiṣaḥ | yatra cāyaṃ viplavaḥ paramparayā parāpoḍhavastunāntarīyakaḥ tatrābhimatārthakriyākṛtārtho janastādṛśaṃ viśeṣamūhituṃ na prayatnavān, nāpi kṣama ityanavacchinno vyavahāraḥ visaṃvāde'pi mṛṣedamiti na vyavasthāpayati | na punaranyadāpi bāhyenābiṣayatvamiti śāstrakārāṇāmapyabhyūhasaṃbhavāt kā parasya kathā ? tasmānna svalakṣaṇasya śabdādigocaratvamiti sthitam || ekaṃ dharmiṇamākalayya vividhavyāvṛttidharmāśrayaṃ tatraikaikavidhānabādhanavidhāvāyavyayābhāsinam | mukhyā buddhiriyaṃ yathā bhramayati bhrāmyaṃstathāyaṃ janastattvāṃśena kṛtārthatāmupagato nopaplavaṃ manyate ||
iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ ||
[220,1]
nāpi sāmānyalakṣaṇasya | tathāhi uttaratīre saritaścaranti gāva iti vākye gavādiśabdāt sāsnāśṛṅgalāṅgūlādayo'kṣarākāraparikarāḥ sajātīyabhedāparāmarśāt saṃpiṇḍitaprāyāḥ pratibhāsante, na ca tadeva sāmānyam, varṇākṛtyakṣarākāraśūnyaṃ gotvaṃ hi kathyate | (pra. vā. 2. 147)
na cāparamākāśavat kiñcit pratibhāti | anyathā gotvāśvatvavikalpayoraviśeṣaprasaṅgāt | tadeva hi jvaladbhāsurākāramātramakhilavyaktāvatyantavilakṣaṇamapi svalakṣaṇena ekīkriyamāṇaṃ sāmānyamityucyate | na tu tatsāmānyameva tāsām, buddhyākāratvenānyatrānugamāt | śāstraṃ hi, buddheravyatiriktaṃ ca kathamarthāntaraṃ vrajet |
na cālocanānantarajanmanīndriyārthajanyatayābhimate so'yaṃ, tādṛśo'yaṃ, gaurayamiti vā vikalpe'rthāntarapratibhāsaḥ | yathā tu saṃpiṇḍitākāramalaukikamātmani pratibhāsamānaṃ puraḥ pratibhāsini piṇḍe yojayati, tathā tasya bāhyasyābhāvād bhrāntirevāsau, keśaprakāśavat |
[220,2]
bādhakādevamiti cet ? nanu prayatnapraṇihitapāṇipratighātādyabhāvāt keśapāśe visaṃvādaḥ, prastute tu yadi paribhāvako bhavati sa eva vyaktavyaktyanubhavo bādhakaḥ kim apareṇa ? janasya tu vivecanāsāmarthyamityuktameva | kathaṃ vā karapratighātādiviraho'dyāpi na bādhakaḥ ? ta eva hi śṛṅgādayo yathāsthānaniveśino'spaṣṭarūpā apratiṣṭhitadeśadaśāviśeṣā deśakālādibhedādanantamūrtayaḥ saṅkīryamāṇā ivādyāpi bhāsante, teṣāṃ pratidhātādiniyatatvāt kīdṛśaḥ keśādibhyo bhedaḥ, yato nātra bādhakamiti syāt ?
[220,3]
tasmād vāsanāvaśād buddhereva tadātmanā vivarto'yamastu, asadeva vā tadrūpaṃ khyātu, vyaktaya eva vā sajātīyabhedatiraṣkāreṇānyathā bhāsantām, anubhavavyavadhānāt smṛtipramoṣo vābhidhīyatām, sarvathā bhrāntireveyaṃ bahirapekṣayā sāmānyavārtā, idantayā ca purovartivastvanubhavaprabhavatayā bhavituṃ yuktaiva | nanu bhrāntihetavastimirāśubhramaṇādaya indriyavikārakāriṇaḥ parigaṇitā eva | na ca tatraikasyāpi sannidhiriti kathamiyamākasmikī bhrāntiḥ ? atha nirvikalpakabhrāntereva hetavaste, iyaṃ ca mānasī bhrāntiriti manyase ? sāpyāropyāropaviṣayayoḥ sādṛśyadarśananibandhanaiveti tādṛgavibhāgābhāvāt kathaṃ mānasyapi bhrāntiḥ ? sarvā ca bhrāntiḥ sādṛśyanibandhanaiva, na khalu janmāntare'pi sadṛśadarśanamantareṇa bhavitumarhati | na ca saṃbhinnākāraṃ kiñcij janmāntare'pi dṛṣṭamiti kathaṃ tadāropaḥ ? aho mahat pauruṣam ! tathā hi nirviṣayatvaṃ tāvaduktena krameṇa na cetparihartuṃ śakyate, bhrāntivyavahāraṃ kuryāt mā vā, tāvataiva prakṛtasiddheḥ kimatra nirbandhena ?
[221,1]
yat punarākasmikatvamuktaṃ tadayuktam, janakasāmagrībhedasya bhavatāpyavaśyasvīkaraṇīyatvāt | kathamanyathā indriyārthau nirvikalpakajñānajanananiyatau dṛṣṭau vikalpam utpādayataḥ ? tasmāt pūrvapiṇḍadarśanasmaraṇasahakāriṇātiricyamānasāmarthyeyaṃ sāmagrī vikalpamutpādayatīti nirviṣayaṃ jñānamutpādayatyevārthaḥ, nirviṣayatāniṣṭhatvād vikalpatāyāstadaṃśena | tad varaṃ vijātīyavikalpavad vispaṣṭapratibhāsādanubhavād bhinna eva sajātīyavikalpo'potyeva sādhu, tasmānna jātisiddhiradhyakṣāt |
[221,2]
nāpyanumānāt, adhyakṣagocaratayaiva kenacidagnidhūmavat kāryakāraṇabhāvasya grahītumaśakyatvāt | sāmānyena tu jñānajanmani yathā paridṛṣṭakāraṇebhyaḥ kāraṇāntaram apekṣaṇīyamindriyavat kadācit sidhyet yadi sakalānyakāraṇasannidhau kadācidabhimatajñānakāryābhāvaṃ vibhāvayet | na caivaṃ prastute śakyam | yadā hi piṇḍāntare'ntarāle vā gobuddherabhāvaṃ darśayet, tadā gopiṇḍasyaivābhāvāt abhāvo gobuddherupapadyamānaḥ kathamarthāntarāpekṣāmākṣipet, yatastadeva gotvamiti pratyāśā syāt ? nanu gopiṇḍa iti gotvādeva sāmānyādanyathā turagapiṇḍo'pi gopiṇḍaḥ syāt | yadyevaṃ gotvamapi sāmānyaṃ gopiṇḍādeva, anyathā turagatvamapi gotvaṃ syāditi samānam | na cādṛśyasya sāmānyasya bhāvābhāvau kvacit niścetuṃ śakyau piṇḍavaditi na kiñcidetat |
athāpi syād yadi bāhuleyapiṇḍābhāvāt turage na gobuddhiḥ, śābaleye'pi mā bhūt, svalakṣaṇasya kvacidananvayāt | satyamananvayi svalakṣaṇam, yathā tu svajātīyapiṇḍāntaradarśanasmaraṇavati prattipattari tadākārapratyavamarśajananasāmarthyaṃ bāhuleyasya tathā śābaleyasyāpi | tato naika eva gopiṇḍo'pi tu tādṛg vikalpārohiṇaḥ sarva eva piṇḍāḥ | atasturage na gopratyayaḥ |
[222,1]
nanu sāmarthyaṃ śaktiriti jātirevocyate | sā hi śaktirbhinnā vā syādabhinnā vā ? yadyabhinnā, tadā svalakṣaṇavadananugāminīti netaraḥ śaktaḥ | atha bhinnā, anyasādhāraṇī ca, tadā jātirevāsāviti nāmni vivādaḥ | atrocyate | abhinnaiva sā prativastu, yathā tvekaḥ śaktasvabhāvo bhāvastathā'nyo'pi bhavan kīdṛśaṃ doṣam āvahati ? yathā hi bhavatāṃ jātirekāpi samānadhīdhvaniprasavaheturanyāpi svarūpeṇaiva jātyantaravirahāt, tathā'smākaṃ vyaktirapi nirapekṣā svarūpeṇaiva bhinnāpi hetuḥ | tat tu svarūpaṃ vyakteḥ kāraṇaparamparāpratibaddham |
[222,2]
yattu trilocanaḥ, aśvatvagotvādīnāṃ sāmānyaviśeṣāṇāṃ svāśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ sāmānyamityabhidhānapratyayayornimittamiti | tat samavāyanirākaraṇenaivāpahastitam |
samavāya eva vā svarūpeṇaiva nimittamiti na dṛṣṭāntakṣatiḥ | na ca jātisamavāyayoḥ sahakriyākalpanenānyonyaśaktitvam, tadā hi svarūpeṇaikasyāpi janakatvamiti sāmānyābhidhānadhiyordatto jalāñjaliḥ | svarūpeṇa janakānāmeva hi bījādīnāṃ sahakārisākalyamaupādhikī śaktiriti svarūpeṇa janakatvamavaśyavācyamiti samavāyāvalambanaṃ viḍambaḥ | na ca tadvyāpāravirahe tadākāravedanodayaḥ kāraṇāntaramātrāt, anyathānuvṛttākārasyāpi pratyayasya janmani svalakṣaṇaireva kiṃ na nirvṛttiriti cintāpi jāteḥ samūlakāṣaṃ kaṣitā syāt | ākasmikatve'pi sa eva doṣa iti gale pādikayā jātisvīkāriṇo'nuvṛttapratyaye svarūpeṇaiva jātivyāpāramanavasthābhayāt svayamevānāropitajātyantarāḥ svīkārayitavyā iti kathaṃ samavāyena parihāraḥ ? sa punaradhikaḥ sahakārī bhavatu mā vā bhūt, jātistu jātinirapekṣā svarūpeṇa śaktimatī anuvṛttapratyayaṃ janayati, svabhāvasyāparyanuyojyatvānna vyaktiriti na rājñāmājñāmantareṇa śakyamabhidhātum |
[222,3]
etena seyaṃ pratyayānuvṛttiranuvṛttavastvanuyāyinī kathamatyantabhedinīṣu vyaktiṣu vyāvṛttapratyayaviṣayabhāvānupātinīṣu bhavitumarhatītyapyūhapravartanamasya pratyākhyātam, jātiṣveva parasparavyāvṛttatayā vyaktīyamānāsvanuvṛttapratyayena vyabhicārāt | atha jātīnāmadarśanāt kvānuvṛttapratyayo yato vyabhicāra iti cet — na, abhyupagamavirodhasya anena krameṇa pratipādanāt | tathā hi pratyayānuvṛttiranuvṛttavastusādhanāyopanīyate, sā cānuvṛttavastvabhāvanāntarīyikā yadyanuvṛttavastusiddhiriti ka imaṃ vyāghātamudvoḍhuṃ śakto'nyatra jāḍyāt ? kiṃ ca kalpitāsvapi jātiṣu vyabhicārastadavastha eva kimatra darśanena ?
[223,1]
atha dṛśyamāneṣvartheṣu niyama ucyate — na, tatrāpi viparyayabādhakābhāvāt pratibandhānupapatteḥ | sāmānyena ca vyabhicāradarśanādanyatrāpi śaṅkābījam | yadi ca dṛśyaviśeṣāpekṣayā sāmānyavyabhicāraparihāraḥ, tadā na vaktavyaṃ yā bhinneṣvabhidhānapratyayānuvṛttirasāvanuvṛttavastunimittā, yathā kusumeṣu sūtramityabhidhānapratyayānuvṛttistathā ca goṣu bhinneṣu gaurityabhidhānapratyayānuvṛttiriti | dṛśyamānanimittatāyāmevābhidhānapratyayānuvṛtteranuvṛttavastunimittatayā vyāpterviśrāmaniyamāt | yuktaṃ caitat | na khalu sūtre'pi darśanāviṣayīkṛteṣu sūtrapratyayānuvṛttiḥ | savastuko hi vikalpo'numānaṃ vinā vastudarśanakāryaḥ siddha iti viparyayāt kāraṇānupalabdhyā nivartamānānuvṛttavastunā pratyayānuvṛttivyāptirdṛśyanimittatāyāmeva viśrāmyati, sati vastuviṣayatve |
vastuviṣayatvavivāde tu nāyaṃ niyamaḥ |
[223,2]
yat punaranena viparyayabādhakamuktam, abhidhānapratyayānuvṛttiḥ kutaścinnivṛttya kvacideva bhavantī nimittavatī | na cānyannimittamityādi | tanna samyak | anuvṛttamantareṇāpyabhidhānapratyayānuvṛtteḥ atadrūpaparāvṛttasvarūpaviśeṣādavaśyaṃ svīkārasya sādhitatvāt | tasmāt yathā svalakṣaṇānnivṛttya gotvāśvatvādāveva sāmānyaṃ sāmānyamityabhidhānapratyayānuvṛttiḥ kayācit pratyāsattyā bhavati, tathā vyaktiṣvapi bhavatu, etenānunṛttavastuni sādhye'bhidhānapratyayānuvṛttiḥ, tenāsyā vyāptau ca viparyayabādhikā vyāpakānupalabdhirityubhayamanaikāntikamiti veditavyam | pratyāsattirityapi nāstyanyavyāvṛtteranyā | yathāhi gotvamaśvasāmānyādvyāvṛttaṃ tathāśvatvadravyatvādikamapi, evaṃ yathaikā govyaktiragotaḥ parāvṛttā tathā'nyāpi | asyā api bhedābhedacintāmaukharye śaktivadevottaram | tataśca ye'rthā atadrūpaparāvṛttyā parasparaṃ pratyāsannāste teṣvekadarśanānantaramaparadṛṣṭau anuvṛttapratyayamutpādayanti nānye | saiva ca śaktiḥ, na jātyātmā | anyathā,
[223,3]
ātmaikatrāpi so'stīti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ (pra. vā. 3. 164)
[224,1]
etacca kṣaṇabhaṅge sahakārivādādavadhāryam | sā ca pratyāsattiḥ kāraṇaparamparāyātetyanantaramuktameva | avaśyaṃ ca hetukṛtaḥ pratyāsattiviśeṣa eṣitavyaḥ, yataḥ kāścideva vyaktayo jātyadhiṣṭhānabhājanībhavanti netarāḥ | anyathātve tu sāmagrīniyamācca niyatajātimat kārya bhavatīti uktamaparitrāṇaṃ bhūṣaṇasya syāt |
tathā ca sati, tulye bhede yathā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati | kvacinnānyatra saivāstu śabdajñānanibandhanam || (pra. vā. 3. 161 — 2)
kimatra jātyā ?
[224,2]
yat punaratra tenoktamaparamapi kuvodyam, na hyevaṃ bhavati, yathā pratyāsattyā daṇḍasūtrādikaṃ prasarpati kvacinnānyatra, saiva pratyāsattiḥ puruṣasphaṭikādiṣu daṇḍisūtritvādivyavahāranibandhanamastu kiṃ daṇḍasūtrādineti ? etat kadā śobhate ? yadi pramāṇasiddhaṃ sāmarthyaṃ kiñcit kvacidapalapyeta | yathā hi, upasarpaṇapratyayādyāśrayā pratyāsattirdaṇḍasūtrayoḥ puṃsi sphaṭike ca prasarpaṇahetuḥ pratyakṣādipramāṇasiddhā, tatsaṃpṛktapuruṣasphaṭikānubhavaśca daṇḍisūtribuddhernibandhanaṃ siddhaṃ samayasmaraṇavataḥ pratipattuḥ, tathā na gotvabhāvābhāvāvanuvidhīyamāneyaṃ gobuddhirupalabdhā, kiṃ tvandhakāre karāmarṣamātrametadīdṛśā kenacid bhavitavyaṃ gobuddhinibandhaneneti | tatra yadyavaśyābhyupagantavyena prakārāntareṇa tatsiddhau na bādhastat kiṃ gurvitarayā parikalpanayetyucyate ? anyathā tadapi kalpayitvānarthakārthaśatakalpanamanivāryam | yadi tu yathopasarpaṇapratyayādeḥ puruṣādau daṇḍādisannidhirbhāvābhāvamanuvidadhāno dṛṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭaśca puruṣādau daṇḍādisannidhānānubhavabhāvābhāvānuvidhāyī daṇḍyādipratyayastathā kāraṇakalāpasya niyatajātikatāyāmeva paraṃ vyāpāro naikāmarśe | ekāmarśe punariyamasau jātireva saṃprati vyāpāravatītyanubhūyeta, syāt tadapavadituraparādhaḥ, yāvatā samayamātrametat, jāteranubhavātikrāntipratipādanāt iti kutastadvaiyarthyacodanaṃ daṇḍādikamapi viṣayīkuryāt ? evamanyatrāpīdṛśi pratividhau bādhanamūhyam |
[225,1]
athaivamanumānam, yadviśiṣṭajñānaṃ tadviśeṣaṇagrahaṇanāntarīyakam, yathā daṇḍijñānam |
viśiṣṭajñānaṃ cedaṃ gaurayamiti pratyaya ityarthataḥ kāryahetuḥ | viśeṣaṇānubhavakāryaṃ hi dṛṣṭānte viśiṣṭabuddhiḥ siddheti | atrānuyogaḥ, viśiṣṭabuddherbhinnaviśeṣaṇagrahaṇanāntarīyakatvaṃ vā sādhyam, viśeṣaṇamātrānubhavanāntarīyakatvaṃ vā ? prathamapakṣe pakṣasya pratyakṣabādhā sādhanāvadhānamanavakāśayati, vastugrāhiṇaḥ pratyakṣasyobhayapratibhāsābhāvāt | viśiṣṭajñānatvaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ heturanaikāntikaḥ, bhinnaviśeṣaṇagrahaṇamantareṇāpi darśanāt | yathā svarūpavān ghaṭaḥ, gotvaṃ sāmānyamiti vā | dvitīyapakṣe tu siddhasādhanam, svarūpavān ghaṭa ityādivat gotvajātimān piṇḍa iti kalpitaṃ bhedamupādāya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasyeṣṭatvādagovyāvṛttānubhavabhāvitvād gaurayamiti vyavahārasyeti | tadevaṃ śābdādibuddhau na bāhyasya svalakṣaṇasya sāmānyalakṣaṇasya vā pratibhāsaḥ | na ca sāmānyaṃ pramāṇasiddhamiti pratipāditam |
tadvadupādhyantarāṇi cintyāni ||
[225,2]
yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tarhi, śabdaistāvanmukhyamākhyāyate'rthaḥ |
iti śāstraṃ saṅgatiyuktam ? na hi tacca tena pratipādyate, na ca tajjñāne tatprakāśa iti saṅgatiḥ kācidityāha, adhyāsata iti |
dvidhā viṣayavyavahāraḥ pratibhāsādadhyavasāyācca | tadiha pratibhāsābhāve'pi parāpoḍhasvalakṣaṇasyādhyavasāyamātreṇa viṣayatvamuktam | tathā ca tato'pi vikalpāt tadadhyavasāyena vastunyeva pravṛtteriti | atha ko'yamadhyavasāyo nāma vikalpādanyaḥ, vikalpitamadhyavasitamityanarthāntaratvāt ? tat kathaṃ vikalpādadhyavasāyeneti bhedanirdeśaḥ ? anyāpoḍhaṃ ca svalakṣaṇaṃ na vikalpe parisphurati | adhyavasite vikalpita iti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ, yato'dhyavasāyāpekṣatayā tadapi vikalpasya viṣaya iti vyavasthāpyate ? kiṃ ca vikalpasyāviṣayaśca bāhyam, grahaṇaṃ cāsya śabdena saṃyojyeti duryojam | ātmani ca tannāstīti vikalpo nāma nāstyeva, tat kasya viṣayacintā ? agṛhīte ca svalakṣaṇe śabdāt pravṛttiriti sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa prasajyeta, sarvasyāgṛhītatvena viśeṣābhāvāt | tataḥ prāptirapi nābhimatasya niyamenetyanumānasyāpi viplava iti |
[226,1]
atrocyate, satyamekārthau vikalpādhyavasāyau kevalaṃ vikalpaśabdaḥ śabdādiyojanānimittakaḥ | adhyavasāyastvagṛhīte'pi pravartanayogyatānimittaḥ | yadyapi ca viśvamagṛhītam, tathāpi niyataviṣayā pravṛttirniyatākāratvād vikalpasya | niyataśaktayo hi bhāvāḥ pramāṇapariniṣṭhitasvabhāvā na śaktisāṅkaryaparyanuyogabhājaḥ, asadutpattivat | sarvasya tatrāsattve'pi hi bījādaṅkurasyaivotpattiḥ, tatraiva tasya śakteḥ pramāṇena nirūpaṇāt | tathehāpi hutavahākārasya vikalpasya hutavahārthakriyārthinaḥ, tatsmaraṇavato hutavahaviṣayāyāmeva pravṛttau sāmarthya pramāṇapratītaṃ kathamatiprasaṅgabhāgi ?
pratyāsatticintayā ca tāttvikasyāpi vahnerjvaladbhāsurākāratvaṃ vikalpollekhasyāpīti, tāvatā tatraiva pravartanaśaktirjvalanavikalpasya na jalādau | na ca sādṛśyāropeṇa pravṛttiṃ brūmaḥ, yenākāre bāhyasya bāhye vākārasyāropadvāradūṣaṇāvakāśaḥ | kiṃ tarhi ? svavāsanāparipākavaśādupajāyamānaiva sā buddhirapaśyantyapi bāhyaṃ bāhye pravṛttimātanotīti viplutaiva |
[226,2]
yacchāstram, deśabhrāntiśca na jñāne tulyamutpattito dhiyaḥ | tathāvidhāyā anyatra tatrānupagamād dhiyaḥ ||  (pra. vā., 2. 13)
iti | tasmānna rūpyādivadāropadvāreṇa pravṛttirapi tu tathāvidhākārotpattipratibaddhaśaktiniyamāt, yathā śālitvena śālibījamupādānaṃ niranvayodaye'piṃ śālyaṅkura upādeye, śalitvādisthiteḥ sthairyadūṣaṇena nirastatvāt | na ca vicārakasya vastvadarśanaṃ niścinvataḥ apravṛttiprasaṅgaḥ saṅgacchate, darśane'pi hi pravṛttirarthakriyayānvitayā, arthakriyāprāptiśca vastusattāniyame | sa ca niyamo yathā darśanād vastupratibandhakṛtastathā vikalpaviśeṣād api pāramparyeṇeti, nānumānamanavasthitam | śabdāt tu kvacidarthasaṃśayeneti prāpterapi tatrāniyamaḥ | tasmādadhyavasitamityapratibhāse'pi pravṛttiviṣayīkṛtamityarthaḥ |
[226,3]
tato vikalpabuddhāvapratibhāse'pyadhyavasitatvaṃ na bāhyasya bādhyate | ayameva cārtho dṛśyavikalpayorekīkaraṇasyābhedapratipattyādeśca | tataśca tacca na pratīyate tena cābhedabhāsanamityupālambho'saṃbhavoti darśitam, tadarthaniṣṭhāyāḥ kṛtatvāt | sa cāgniratreti vyavasāyo yathā kāyikīṃ pravṛttiṃ prasūte, tathāgnirmayā pratīta iti vācikīmapi prasūte | etadākārānuvyavasāyarūpāṃ mānasīmapi prasavati | evaṃ sati yathā vikalpena ayamartho gṛhīta iti niścayastathā śabdena saṃyojyetyapi, arthākāraleśavacchabdākārasyāpi sphuraṇāt | tasmād yāvadarthagrahaṇābhimānavān mānavaḥ tāvadabhidhānasaṃyuktagrahaṇābhimānavānapītyavasāyānurodhādeva vikalpavyavasthā na tattvataḥ |
[227,1]
āha ca,
[227,2]
na śabdeḥ saṃsargaḥ kvacidapi bahirvā manasi vākṣarākārākīrṇaḥ sphurati punararthākṛtilavaḥ | ubhāvapyātmānau yadapi dhiya evādhyavasitirnidhatte tau bāhye vacasi ca vikalpasthitirataḥ ||
[227,3]
ataeva ca tadabhimānamlānamānasaṃ vyāvahārikaṃ prati pratyakṣalakṣaṇe kalpanāpoḍhaviśeṣaṇamupādīyate, sūtrato'pi vikalpādadhyavasāyeneti bhedanirdeśaḥ | tatrāpi nāyam adhyavasāyadhvanirdharmiṇa eva vikalpasyābhidhāyakaḥ prayuktaḥ, kiṃ tu tadgatasyādhyavasānalakṣaṇasya dharmasya | tadayamarthaḥ, adṛṣṭe'pi pravartanayogyatā nāma yo dharmastayā vikalpāt pravṛttiriti | jñātaścedartho vyavasthāpito'dhyavasāyāt saṃvṛttyā, tato viṣayavyavahāro'pi labdha ityavasāyamātreṇa viṣayatvamiti yuktam |
[227,4]
ata uktam,
[227,5]
arthaścaiko'dhyāsato vācya iti |
[227,6]
yadāha bhāṣyakāraḥ,
[227,7]
kathaṃ tadviṣayatvaṃ tatra pravartanāditi |
[227,8]
yastu kathamadṛṣṭe pravartanamityāśaṅkyādṛṣṭa eva sarvatra pravartanamityādisiṃhanādaḥ, sa na vipañcito'smābhirgranthagauravabhayāt |
[227,9]
evaṃ svapratibhāse'narthādhyavasāyena pravṛtterityatrāpyanarthe svapratibhāse sati adhyavasāyaḥ pūrvavat, arthastvarthakriyāsamartho bāhya uktaḥ | tatparyudāsenānartho buddhyākāraḥ | evaṃ sa vastviti asanniti ca draṣṭavyam | etacca vārttikavācaiva sphuṭīkṛtaṃ sākārasiddhau | arthādhyavasāyena pravṛttiranumānasyetyapi hi arthādhyavasāyānumānamityarthaḥ |
ṭīkākārasya tu yathā'tra vyākhyānaṃ svāpohasiddhau taddheyameva, vistaraprasaṅgabhītyā nodbhāvitamasmābhiḥ |
[228,1]
yadi tarhi bāhyasyādhyavasāyena vācyatā, kathaṃ buddhyākārasya ? yacchāstram, anādivāsanodbhatavikalpapariniṣṭhitaḥ | śabdārthaḥ trividho dharmī bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayaḥ ||  (pra. vā. 3. 204 — 5)
ityādi | vikalpapratibimbeṣu tanniṣṭheṣu nibadhyate | (tato'nyāpohaniṣṭhatvāduktānyāpohakṛcchratiḥ || ) vyatirekīva yajjñāne bhātyarthapratibimbakam | śabdāt tadapi nārthātmā bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanodbhavā ||  (pra. vā. 2. 164 — 5)
iti | na hi buddhyākāre'pyadhyavasāyaḥ śakyo'bhidhātum, pravṛttiviṣaye tasya vyavasthāpanāt | sa cārthakriyārthino bāhya evetyāha, bhāsate'nyo'rtho vācya iti |
bāhyādanyo buddhyākāra ityarthaḥ | śabdādijanyāyāṃ buddhāvākāramātrasya pratibhāsanāt sa eva viṣaya ucyate, cakṣuṣa iva rūpaṃ viṣayaḥ, na punaradhyavasāyāditi bhāvaḥ | uktaṃ ca, yathāpratīti kathitaḥ śabdārtho'sāvasannapi (pra. vā. 3. 83)
iti | asanniti tu yathāpratibhāsaṃ bahirabhāvāt, bahirmukhāpekṣayā ca cintāyāḥ prakramāt | ayamevārtho yathādhyavasāyamatattvāt, yathātattvaṃ cānadhyavasāyāditi |
adhyavasāyasya vikalpaparyāyatvād yathāvikalpasphuraṇamityarthaniṣṭhānāt | asadarthaprakāśanāderapi yathāpratīti bahirasattvamevārthaḥ | bhrāntitvamapi bahirapekṣayaiveti sarvam anākulam | na tu svasaṃvedanagocarasya jñānarūpatayārthatvāt keśādyākārasyevāsattābhidhānaṃ sādhu | ataeva vācyatve'pi,
[229,1]
nākārasya na bāhyasya tattvato vidhisādhanam | bahireva hi saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛtyāpi tu nākṛteḥ ||
[229,2]
na hyasandehasya viṣayasya svasaṃvedyasyākārasya śabdādinā vidhiniṣedhayogaḥ vaiyarthyādasāmarthyācca | nāpi vikalpāpratibhāsino bāhyasya | viṣayāpratipatterhi kasya vidhirniṣedho vā syāt ? tasmād yathā vṛkṣaśabdena bāhyo vṛkṣo'dhyavasāyādabhidheyo vyavasthāpitaḥ, tathādhyavasāyādeva bāhyasya vidhirniṣedho vā vyavahriyate | yadāpi kutaścit prakaraṇād buddhyākāraṃ kañcid vikalpāntareṇādāya parīkṣā, tadāpi tadvikalpād bāhya eva vidhiniṣedhau | taṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan | (pra. vā. 2. 220)
iti hi śāstram | tasmāt tattvato nobhayorapi vidhiniṣedhau, saṃvṛttyā hi bāhyasyaiva duṣpariharau ca | anyathā saṃvyavahārahāniprasaṅgāt |
[229,3]
etena yaṭṭīkākāraḥ āropitasya bāhyatvaviṣayau vidhiniṣedhāvityalaukikamanāgamamatārkikīyaṃ kathayati, tadapahastitam | na hi saṃvṛtiparamārthasatyadvayamanāśritya kācid vyavasthā | tatra na tāvadiyaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, lokābhimānarūpatvāt tasyāḥ, lokasya ca bāhya eva padasyārtho vihitaḥ pratiṣiddho vetyavigānena vyāpī pravṛttinivṛttyāśrayaḥ abhimānaḥ, nāropitasya bāhyatvādikaṃ spṛśati lokaḥ | nāpyeṣa paramārthaḥ | na hyavācyasya vidhiniṣedhau | na ca vācyaṃ kiñcit tattvata ityāgamaḥ | tarkasyāpi nānyā dik |
kiṃ ca nānadhyavaseyasya vidhiniṣedhau, na ca śabdādadhyavasāyaḥ svalakṣaṇādanyatreti svayamapyudghuṣyate | ataḥ kimāyātamāropitabāhyatvavidhiniṣedhayoḥ ? pratibhāsādhyavasāyadvārā ca sarvā vyavasthitistattvamaspṛśatī | tatrāropitamāropitabāhyatvaṃ vā na pratibhāsasya viṣayo, nāpyadhyavasāyasya | tatrāropitaṃ tāvanna pratibhāsasparśi, yat svayam evāha, ullekhānubhavasamānakālaṃ samāropaṇamapratibhāsarūpamevāvastu vikalpaviṣaya iti | ataeva tadvāhyatvamapi na pratibhāsi, taddharmatvāt | adhyavasāyavastu bāhyasvalakṣaṇaniyamādeva nainayorityalamenāmutthāpya |
[230,1]
āropitamityapi kalpitamebocyate, kalpanākarma ca pratibhāsamavasitaṃ ceti dvayam | tat kutastyo'yamāropitākhyo rāśiraparaḥ ? tasmād buddhyākārabāhyāśrayaiva saṃvṛtiparamārthābhyāṃ cintociteti | tathāvidhārthakriyāvivakṣāyāṃ ca kiṃ vakradurgamārgāśrayeṇetyalamatinirbandhena | sthitametadadhyavasāyena bāhyasya buddhyākārasya tu pratibhāsena śabdavācyatvamucyate iti | nanvevaṃvyācakṣāṇena bhavatobhayārtharāśeraśeṣasya vācyatā svīkṛteti kathaṃ sarvadharmānabhilāpyatāsamarthanārthamidamavatāritamityāha, sthāpyata iti prayojanāntaramuddiśya vyavasthāmātrametat kriyate, adhyavasāyamātreṇa pratibhāsamātreṇa vā vācyatvamiti | tathā ca bahirviṣayīkaraṇaṃ tattvavyavasthānamātraṃ gṛhṇataḥ tāvadanyāpoḍhaṃ svalakṣaṇameva viṣaya ityucyate upādhirāśiniraśanaparaṃ, evamanyāpoḍhākāro vikalpasyātmā viṣaya iti samastabāhyanirasanaparam, na tu svasmin viṣayatvasya viśrāmāyeti na virodhaḥ |
[230,2]
kutaḥ punaretat ? tatra tatra viṣayatāpratipādane'pi na viśrāmo vivakṣitaḥ, kiṃ tvanyanirasane tātparyamityāha, vācyastattvato naiva kaścidarthaḥ |
iti | adhyavasāyasahāpohipratibhāsaḥ sāṃvyavahārikāpekṣayā tattvato jñeyasya jñānaviṣayatāmupanayati pratyakṣavat | na hi pratibhāsamātramavasāyaśūnyamanyāvasāyākrāntavyāpāraṃ vā pravṛttikāmasya viṣayavyavasthāmarthe kṣamate, gacchattṛṇasparśavat, marīcāvudakāropavat | nāpyavasāyamātramapetapratibhāsam, udakāropavadeva | tasmāt pravṛttiyogyatayā vyāptaṃ viṣayavyavasthānamubhayābhāvo vyāpakābhāvena paribhūyamānamubhayasaṃbhavapratibaddhamekaviveke svīkriyamāṇaṃ sāṃvṛtameva | yatra jñāne yanna pratibhāsate yena vā yannāvasīyate sa na tasya viṣayo yathā gojñānasyāśvaḥ | na pratibhāsate ca śābdajñāne svalakṣaṇaṃ, nāvasīyate cānena buddhyākāra iti vyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | pratibandhasādhanāt nānekāntaḥ | yadyapi cātyantābhyāse pratibhāsamātreṇāpi pravṛttirviṣayatvaṃ ca dṛṣṭam, tathāpi sa evābhyāso nāvasāyād vinetyavasāyasyaiva tat pauruṣam, tato yena yannāvasīyate'satyabhyāsa iti viśeṣaṇamapekṣyam |
[231,1]
nanu pratyakṣe'pi na gṛhītakṣaṇasyāvasāyaḥ, kiṃ tu santateḥ, na cāsyāḥ pratibhāsa iti kenāsyāpi saviṣayatvaṃ, kṣaṇe santatau cobhayābhāvāt | anumāne tu parīkṣaiva vartate | na cānyat pramāṇamasti, yasyobhayasaṃbhavena viṣayaḥ kaścidityasaṃbhavametat |
tadekaikena vidheyatve sthitaviṣayakasthitirakhilasya bāhyasyāntarasya vā vācyatvamiti |
[231,2]
atrocyate | tattvavyavasthāmāha, ubhayasaṃbhavenaiva viṣayatvaṃ, kevalaṃ sāṃvyavahārikāpekṣayā saṃvṛterevādharasaṃvṛtimapekṣya tattvamiti vyavahriyate, kṣaṇabhedāvatāre saṃvyavahāravilopāt vyāvahārikaṃ prati pratikṣaṇakṣīṇatāyā abhāvāt, tattvataḥ pratyakṣeṇobhayasaṃbhavābhāvaḥ, iti na doṣaḥ | atha pṛthagjanasya dṛśyavikalpyayorapyabhedagraho niyata evetyavasito vahniḥ pratibhāsita eveti cet — na, pratibhāsāntarasmaraṇena tatpratibhāsabhramabhraṃśasya kṛtatvāt | yathā ca vikalpapratibhāsādanya eva vastupratibhāso darśayitum adhyakṣe śakyaḥ, tathā nādhyakṣapratibhāsādanyo'stīti tatraiva vastupratibhāsaviśrāmāt tadvijātīyasya vastupratibhāsatāvyudāsaḥ śreyān | tasmād yuktamuktam, sthāpyo vācyastattvato naiva kaścit |
iti | athavā vastvantarāvācyatve'pi tatrāpohastadviśeṣaṇatvena gamya iti apohasya vācyatā svīkṛtaiva | tathāpi kathaṃ sarvadharmānabhilapyatvamityāha,
[231,3]
vācyastattvato naiva kaścidartha iti |
[231,4]
ayamabhiprāyaḥ | paryudāsapakṣe tāvad vasturūpavat tasyāpyadhyavasāyamātrakṛtaṃ vācyatvam, na pratibhāsādadhyakṣavat | prasajyapakṣe punaranyanivṛttimātrasyānyadāpi na viśeṣaḥ, tathāpyasau nārtha iti noktadoṣaḥ | yada vā yaḥ śāstre, tasmāt siddhametat sarvaśabdāvivekaviṣayā vikalpāścetyupasaṃhāraḥ, tasyārthaniṣṭhāmupasaṃhāreṇaiva darśayati — vācyastattvato naiva kaścidartha iti |
saṃvṛtau pratibhāsādhyavasāyamātreṇa vācyatāyā darśitatvāt, tattvata ityāha |
tadayamarthaḥ | yadetacchāstre viveka eva vācya ityupasaṃhṛtaṃ tasya na kiñcid vācyamevārthaḥ, yathā abhāvo bhavatīti bhāvo na bhavatītyevārthaḥ, tathā apohasya vācyateti vācyatāyā evāpoha ityarthaḥ | etacca hetutrayavibhāgakaraṇādinā svayameva śāstreṇa sphuṭīkṛtamityupapāditam |
[232,1]
tadevaṃ kathamapohaḥ śabdavācya iti praśne tadguṇatvena yathoktārthenetyuttaram | atha buddhyākāraḥ svalakṣaṇamupādhayo vā kasmānna vācyā iti praśnaḥ, tadadhyavasāyasya pratibhāsasya ubhayasya cābhāvāditi krameṇa visarjanāni | yadā tu śabdaiḥ kiṃ vācyamityanuyogaḥ, tadā pratibhāsādarthādhyavasāyāt, yad vā tattvata iti vikalpya vikalpasthe'nyāpoḍhākāraḥ, anyāpoḍhasvalakṣaṇaṃ na kiñciditi prativacanāni krameṇaivetyuktaṃ bhavati |
tasmāt śabdaliṅgayorapohaviṣayatāsthitiprasādhanaṃ sarvadharmāvācyatvapratipādanaparamiti prathamaślokārthopasaṃhāraḥ ||
[232,2]
bhavatvapohe kṛtināṃ prapañco vastusvarūpāsphuraṇaṃ tu marma | tatrādṛḍhe sarvamayatnaśīrṇaṃ dṛḍhe tu sausthyaṃ nanu tāvataiva ||
[232,3]
samarthanaitasya diśaḥ prakāśaḥ kṛto'yamasmābhiravistareṇa | tadvistarastvākara eva cintyaḥ paroditaṃ tūlamiva kṣipadbhiḥ ||
<īśvaravādaḥ>
{7.1}
<pūrvapakṣasaṃkṣepaḥ>
[233,1]
karmanirmitavaicitryamanīśaṃ yo jagajjagau | praṇamāmi pramāṇena tamavyāhataśāsanam ||
[233,2]
iha pratyavasthānamanyeṣām, vivādāspadībhūtaṃ bhūdharādi buddhimatkartṛpūrvakam, kāryatvāt | yadyat kāryaṃ tad buddhimatkartṛpūrvakaṃ dṛṣṭam, yathā ghaṭaḥ | kāryaṃ cedaṃ bhūdharādi |
tasmād buddhimatpūrvakamiti | na cedamasiddham, bauddhasyāpi vindhyagandhamādanādīnāṃ kāryatve vivādābhāvāt | nāpi viruddham, sapakṣe bhāvāt | na cānaikāntikam, kvacidapi kārye buddhimadadhiṣṭhānavyabhicārasya darśayitumaśakyatvāt | pratyakṣāgamābhyām abādhanācca na kālātyayāpadiṣṭam | pratihetorabhāvācca na prakaraṇasamam | tadanena yat siddham, tadupādeyaṃ viduṣām, sādhanāntarasiddhavat | na ca sarvatrānvayavyatireke hetuvallabhatayā buddhimati kāryasya tadubhayāsiddherasādhanatvamabhidheyam, sapakṣe sato'sya vipakṣarāśerākāśaderatyantaṃ vyāvṛtteḥ |
[233,3]
trayo hi bhāvarāśayaḥ | buddhimatkartṛkāśca ghaṭādayaḥ, akartṛkāścākāśādayaḥ, sandigdhakartṛkāśca bhūdharādayaḥ | tatra ghaṭādiṣu sapakṣeṣu vidyamānam, avidyamānamambarādiṣu vipakṣeṣu ityanvayavyatireki kāryatvaṃ śeṣeṣu vartamānamavaśyaṃ sādhyamupasthāpayati | yadyapi ca digambarādayo'santastanmate paramāṇavastu kāryameva, tathāpyasato'pi vyāvṛttiḥ svīkṛtaiva | tathā ca, nivṛttiyaṃdi tasminna hetorvṛttiḥ kimiṣyate | (pra. vā. 4. 224)
iti hi śāstram | na ca vipakṣatākṣatiḥ, sādhyānadhikaraṇalakṣaṇatvād vipakṣasyeti kimeṣāṃ sattāsādhanaprayāsena ? tasmānnānvayavyatirekārekaḥ kartari yathoke kāryatvasya |
evamutpattimattvācetanopādānatvasthityā pravṛttyādiṣu yojyam ||
[234,1]
atra bauddhamutthāpayan śaṅkaraḥ prāha, notpattimātreṇa yathoktabuddhimatpūrvakatvasya siddhiḥ | api tu yādṛśaṃ prāsādādiṣu dṛṣṭam, yaddṛṣṭerakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirutpadyate, yadi tādṛgeva kṣityādiṣu bhavet syādatrāpi buddhimato'numānam | na kāryatvaśabdasāmyena, tatra vyabhicārasyāpi saṃbhāvyamānatvāt | na hyarthāntarāt, śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ (pra. vā. 1. 14)
pāṇḍutvādagneranumānaṃ nyāyyam | acetanopādānatvād ghaṭādivat kṣityāderapi kartuḥ anumānamiti cet ? evaṃ tarhi ghaṭādermudvikārasya kumbhakārapūrvakatvād valmīkasyāpi tatpūrvakatvānumānaprasaṅgaḥ | taduktam, siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi (pra. vā. 1. 12)
vārtikatrayam | tadidamanirūpitaparābhiprāyasya vyāhṛtam | tathā hi buddhimatkāraṇasya sadbhāve bhāvo ghaṭādābutpattyāderabhāve cābhāvo gaganādiṣu | sa ca tathā prasiddhāvinābhāvo yatraiva kṣityādāvupalabhyate tatraiva tadvinirmāṇasamarthakartṛbuddhiṃ tadvido janayati | na caivaṃ pāṇḍutvādayaḥ, teṣāṃ jātyantarasamavāyināmagnivyabhicāropalabdheriti | tathā na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāṃ prayatnavatā karaṇakarmaṇāṃ kriyāsu svātantryamupalabdhapūrvam, sarvatra buddhimadadhiṣṭhitebhya eva prāsādādiprasavopalabdheriti ||
[234,2]
vācaspatistu svābhāvikasambandhaṃ prastutyāha, ihāpi kāryatvasyopādānādyabhijñena kartrā svābhāvikaḥ sambandho'styeva, upādheranupalambhena vyabhicārāsiddheḥ | tṛṇādayaśca pakṣīkṛtā ityuktam | utprekṣaṇamātraṃ tu na kartavyamityapi pratipāditameva | tataḥ svabhāvataḥ pratibaddhaṃ svasādhyena yadi sādhyamantareṇa bhavet, svabhāvādeva pracyaveteti tarkasahāyaṃ nirastasādhyavyatirekavṛttisandehaṃ bhūdharādiṣu dṛṣṭaṃ svasādhyamupasthāpayituṃ śaktaṃ kim arucibhiḥ ? ye tu pāṇḍutvamṛdvikāragotvādayasteṣāṃ jātyantarasamavāyitvena pratyakṣa eva vyabhicāropalabdherna te hetavaḥ, jātyantarasamavāyino himādigatapāṇḍutvasyāgnivyabhicārāt | tathā mṛdvikārasya sthapatyādipūrvakatvena kulālavyabhicārāt |
evamanyatrāpi boddhavyam | tataścāyaṃ tatra vibhāgaḥ | yadeva viśiṣṭaṃ pāṇḍudravyadhūmarūpam, tadevāgnerhetuḥ, tatra tasyāvyabhicāradarśanāt | yat punaragnivilakṣaṇakāraṇajanmapāṇḍudravyamātramarthato bhinnaṃ śabdasāmyādabhedi, na tato'gneranumānam, tatra tasya vyabhicāropalabdheḥ | evaṃ mṛdvikārādiṣvapi yojyam | kāryatvasāmānyasya tvabhūtvābhāvalakṣaṇasya parvatādiṣu bhāvaḥ parairiṣṭa eva | kiṃ tu pratibandhāsiddheranaikāntikamiti bruvate | sa ca dhūmāderiva pratipādita iti yuktaṃ tatastadanumānamiti ||
[235,1]
vittokastvāha, syādetat | na sapakṣavipakṣayordarśanamātreṇāvyabhicāraniścayo'tadātmano'tadutpatteścāvyabhicāraniyamāyogāt | tadidaṃ kāryatvaṃ sandigdhavyatirekatvādasādhanam ||
[235,2]
atrocyate | nāsti vipakṣavyāvṛttisandeho dhūmānalayoriva kāryabuddhimatorupalambhānupalambhasādhanasya kāryakāraṇabhāvasya siddhatvāt | kāryaviśeṣasyaiva tadutpattisiddhirna kāryasāmānyasya, yathā dhūmādivartivastutvādernānalādijanyatvaniścaya iti cet — na, viśeṣahetvabhāvāt | upalambhānupalambhayostadutpattisādhanatveneṣṭayoḥ sādhyasādhanasāmānyayoraviśeṣāt kāryaviśeṣasyeva kāryamātrasyāpi prabodhāśrayāyattatāsiddheḥ |
na caivaṃ vastutvasyāpi vahnikāryatvam, tadantareṇāpi sahasraśa upalambhāt | tato yathā kāryaṃ vastrādi upādānavad dṛṣṭamiti kāryāntaramapi tathā vyavasthāpyate, tathā tadeva vastrādikāryaṃ buddhimaddhetukaṃ dṛṣṭamityadṛṣṭakartṛkamapi kārya kartṛpūrvakaṃ vyavasthāpyate, upādānasyeva karturapi kāryeṇānukṛtānvayavyatirekatvāt | tena yathā kāryaṃ ca nirupādānaṃ ceti na śakyamāśaṅkitum, tathā kāryaṃ ca bhavedakartṛkaṃ ceti nāśaṅkanīyam, kāryamātrasya kartṛmātrādupādānādivātpādasiddheraviśeṣāditi ||
[235,3]
yat tūcyate, anyādṛśameva kāryaṃ buddhimatā vyāptam, yaddṛṣṭerakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhiḥ, taccāsiddhaṃ sindhubhūdharādāviti | nanu keyaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ ? kiṃ sādhanabuddhiratha sādhyabuddhiḥ ? sādhanabuddhistāvad bhavatāṃ siddhaiva, karmajaṃ lokavaicitryamityabhyupagamāt |
athottaraḥ pakṣaḥ, tenāyamartho bhavati, nedaṃ kṣityādiṣūpalabhyamānaṃ sādhyānumānasamarthaṃ kāryatvaṃ kiṃ tvanyadeva sādhyabuddhijananāt | na caitad yuktam, sarvānumānocchedaprasaṅgāt | dhūmādiṣvapi hi śakyamevaṃ vaktum — nāyaṃ vahnyanumitisamartho dhūmaḥ, kiṃ tvanya eva sādhyadarśinaḥ sādhyabuddhyajananāt | tathā ca tāvanna sādhanaṃ sidhyati, yāvanna sādhyabuddhiḥ sidhyati | tāvanna sādhyabuddhiḥ sidhyati, yāvanna sādhanaṃ sidhyatīti sphuṭataramitaretarāśrayatvamiti ||
[236,1]
śaṅkaro'pyāha, na ca vyāmohāt kasyacit sādhyabuddhyabhāve hetorasiddhiḥ, sarvānumāneṣu tadbhāvaprasaṅgāditi ||
[236,2]
bhūṣaṇakārastvāha, kṛtakatvena pratītau kathaṃ na kṛtabuddhiḥ ? sarveṣāṃ prāsādādiṣvapi kṛtabuddhirna bhavati, yathā cirantaneṣu prāsādādiṣu vyāptyabhijñasyaiva kṛtabuddhiḥ bhavati, vyāptivimūḍhānāmakṛtabuddhireva, tathā kṣityādiṣvapīti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ | puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ prāsādādiṣviva kṣityādiṣu na bhavatīti cet ? kiṃ prasiddhāvinābhāvānāmuta aprasiddhāvinābhāvānām ? prasiddhāvinābhāvānāmapi kiṃ vyāptigrahaṇasmṛtivikalānām, athānyeṣām ? abhraṣṭasmaraṇānāṃ tāvadbhavatyeva puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ, loke'pi vicitraṃ jagat kenacid dhātrā nirmitamityasti pratītiḥ | vyāptigrahasmṛtivimūḍhānāṃ tu prāsādādiṣvapi keṣucinna puruṣakṛtabuddhirbhavatīti naitāvatā teṣāmapuruṣakṛtatvam |
[236,3]
api ceyaṃ vedeṣvapi puruṣakṛtabuddhirmīmāṃsakānāṃ nāstītyataśca tatrāpi puruṣakṛtisādhanāyoktā vākyatvādayo'siddhāḥ syuḥ | kiṃ cānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ yat kṛtakatvaṃ sādhanamuktam, tadapyasiddhaṃ syāt | na hi yādṛśaṃ kṛtakatvādi ghaṭādiṣu dṛṣṭaṃ śrotrāgrāhyarūpam, tādṛśaṃ śabde'stīti | tasmāt dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikavaidharmyametat sarvānumāneṣu samānaṃ neśvarānumānasyaiva bādhakamiti ||
[236,4]
mañjaryāṃ trilocanaḥ punarāha, buddhimatpūrvakatvena vyāptaṃ janma dhaṭādiṣvevāstīti kutaḥ pratipadyase ? kṛtabuddhihetutvāditi cet ? evaṃ tarhi ghaṭādīnāṃ sa viśeṣo vācyo yena mahābhūtāsaṃbhāvinā viśeṣeṇa ghaṭādaya eva kṛtabuddhimutpādayanti na mahābhūtāni |
na tāvat kartṛkriyopalabdhirviśeṣaḥ, akriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhihetutvābhyupagamāt |
mahattvaparimāṇaṃ viśeṣa iti cet ? tasyāpi kāraṇabahutvamahattvapracayaviśeṣebhyo mahābhūteṣvapi dṛṣṭatvāt | kṛtakatvameva viśeṣa iti na vācyam, kāraṇasamavāyalakṣaṇasyābhūtaprādurbhāvasya pṛthivyādiṣvapyaviśiṣṭatvāt | na caitebhyo'nyaḥ śakyo viśeṣaḥ śakreṇāpi nirūpayitum, yasya bhāvād ghaṭādaya eva kṛtabuddhihetavo na pṛthivyādaya iti ||
[236,5]
vācaspatistvāha, idamatra nipuṇataraṃ nirūpayatu bhavān, kiṃ buddhimadanvayavyatirekānuvidhānaṃ viśeṣaḥ ? utāho taddarśanam, yat parvatādiṣu nāstītyabhidhīyate ? yadi pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ, sa buddhimaddhetukatvaṃ tanubhuvanāderātiṣṭhamānairabhyupeyata eva | na hi kāraṇaṃ kāryānanuvihitabhāvābhāvamanyo vaktumarhatyahrīkāt | atha darśanamiti caramaḥ kalpaḥ ?
na tarhi akriyādarśinaḥ kṛtabuddhisaṃbhavaḥ | ya eva ghaṭo'nena buddhimadanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyī dṛṣṭaḥ, sa eva tatkāryo, na tu vipaṇivartī | tajjātīyasya tadanvayavyatirekānuvidhānadarśanādadṛṣṭānvayavyatirekānuvidhānamapi tajjātīyaṃ tatheti cet ? hantotpattimaddhaṭādi buddhimadanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyītyanyadapi tanubhuvanādi tathā bhavanna daṇḍena parāṇudyate | ghaṭajātīyamutpattimadbuddhipūrvakamiti cet ? nanu prāsādādi taddhetukaṃ na bhavedaghaṭajātīyatvāt | atha yajjātīyaṃ buddhimadanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyi dṛṣṭam, tajjātīyamevādṛṣṭānvayavyatirekamapi buddhimaddhetukam | tat kimidānīṃ kāryajātīyaprāsādādi buddhimaddhetukaṃ na dṛṣṭam, yenotpattimat tanubhuvanādi tathā na syāt | na khalu tajjātīyatvena kaścid viśeṣaḥ ||
[237,1]
vittoko'pi, bhavatu vā kaścidanirūpitarūpo viśeṣaḥ, kiṃ punaranena viśeṣaṃ pratipādayatābhipretam ? kiṃ kāryatvasāmānyasyāsiddhatvam, atha kāryaviśeṣasya, atha kāryamātrasya buddhimatkartṛvyabhicāraḥ, atha sādhyadṛṣṭāntayorvaidharmyamātram ? kiṃ cātaḥ ?
yadi tāvat kāryamātrasyāsiddhatvam, tannāsti, viśvambharādiṣu ghaṭādiṣviva kāraṇavyāpārajanmatayobhayasiddhatvāt | atha kāryaviśeṣasya kumbhādivartinaḥ pakṣe'siddhiḥ abhidhoyate, tadā na kācidatra kṣatiḥ, viśeṣasya hetutvenānupādānāt | yadi tu kāryasāmānyasya kartṛvyabhicāraḥ pratipādayitumiṣṭaḥ, sa na śakyo vipakṣe'darśanāt, tṛṇādeśca pakṣīkṛtatvāt | atha sādhyadṛṣṭāntayorvaidharmyodbhāvanam, tanna, sarvatra tasya sulabhatvāt ||
[237,2]
aparastu evaṃ tāvad dhūmāderiva kāryatvasya svābhāvikaḥ pratibandhaḥ pratipāditaḥ |
idānīṃ saugatamano'nurañjanārthaṃ bādhakānyapi pramāṇānyabhidhīyante | na khalvasmākaṃ bādhakapramāṇadāridryam | kiṃ tu nāyaṃ nyāya iti brūmahe | tatra tāvadidameva bādhakaṃ pramāṇam, sakṛdapi puruṣādanutpādo nāma | yathā saugatānāṃ citrabhānoranumāne yadi citrabhānumantareṇa kāraṇāntarādapi dhūmo deśāntare kālāntare vā jāyeta, dṛṣṭayorapi deśakālayorna citrabhānoḥ sakṛdapyātmasattāṃ labheta, yasmānna tadabhāve bhavatastatkāryaniyamo yuktaḥ, atiprasaṅgāt | tataśca tādṛśasya sarvasyaivātaddhetutvānna tataḥ sakṛdapi jāyeta | bhavati ca tasmānnātajjanyaṃ tādṛśamiti viparyaye bādhakapramāṇavṛttyā pratibandhasiddhiḥ, tathā'smākamapi yadi kiñcid buddhimadadhiṣṭhānamantareṇānyato'pi kāryamupajāyeta, hanta na tarhi sakṛdapi buddhimataḥ kumbhakārāderutpadyeta | bhavati ca tatastajjanyam ityekaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
[238,1]
yathā vā saugatānāmapi na dhūmo'nyasmād bhavatīti śaṅkanīyam, aniyatahetukatvena nirhetukatvaprasaṅgāt | nirhetukasya ca, nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vā'hetoranyānapekṣaṇāt | apekṣāto hi bhāvānāṃ kādācitkatvasambhavaḥ || (pra. vā. 3. 34)
tathāsmākamapīti dvitīyaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
[238,2]
evaṃ ca sati yathā bhavatāmayaṃ niyamaḥ sidhyati, sa dhūmo'gnyanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyī padārthaviśeṣaḥ, sa cāgniryastasya janakaḥ | tad yadyasau śaṅkyamāno dhūmastadāgnikārya eveti, tathāsmākamapi tatkāryaṃ yad buddhimatpūrvakam | sa puruṣo yastatkāroti |
tathā yadi cetanāvantamadhiṣṭhātāramantareṇa kvacidapi kārye niścetanānāṃ pravṛttinivṛttī syātāṃ tadānīṃ kāryakriyāyā avirāmaprasaṅgaḥ | tathā hi yadyacetanānāṃ svarasataḥ pravṛttistadā nirabhiprāyavyāpāratayā sarvadā pravṛttiḥ syāt | na hyakasmāt pravṛttināśo yuktaḥ | tataśca kāryasyāvirāmaḥ | athaudāsīnyam, tadā kadācidapi pravṛttirna syāt, viśeṣābhāvāt | adhiṣṭhāyakena tu prayatnavatā kadācit pravatyanta iti yuktaṃ paśyāmaḥ, nācetanena | tasyecchāyattapravṛttinivṛttyorayogāditi tṛtīya bādhaka pramāṇam |
[238,3]
iha khalu kāryatvaṃ kādācitkakāraṇasannidhimattayā vyāptam, kādācitkakāraṇasannidhiścānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ kartṛvyāpārādhīnaḥ, yathā turovemādīnāṃ sannidhiḥ |
vipakṣe ca kādācitkakāraṇasannidhisattā nāsti | na hyacetanaḥ kāraṇāni sannidhāpayituṃ śaknoti, śaktau vā ghaṭādāvapi kartṛvyāpāranivṛttiprasaṅgāt | tataśca vyāpakānupalabdhyā vipakṣānnivartamānaṃ kāryatvaṃ buddhimatpūrvakatvena vyāpyata iti pratibandhasiddhiriti caturthaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇam |
[238,4]
tathā deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgo bādhakaḥ | tathā hi kāryatvaṃ deśakālaprakṛtiniyamena vyāptaṃ yadi prayatnavantamantareṇa bhavet, na deśādiniyamena bhavet | karturicchayā hi kvacid deśādāvanyadeśādivyavacchedena jāyeta | tadabhāve sarvatra deśādau bhavediti vipakṣād vyāpakānupalabdhyā nivartamānaṃ kāryatvaṃ prayatnavannāntarīyakatvena vyāpyata iti pratibandhasiddhiḥ pañcamaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇamiti ||
[239,1]
yat śaṅkaraḥ, nirabhiprāyavyāpārebhyaḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ deśādiniyamo na syāditi |
tathā nāpi kaścid viśeṣaḥ kṣityādihetūnāṃ prāsādādihetubhyo yenāmī nirabhiprāyavyāpārāḥ santaḥ prayatnavannirapekṣāḥ pratiniyamavatā ca vyāpāreṇa tadvantaḥ syuriti ||
[239,2]
vācaspatistu kaṇikāyāmīśvaravādamutthāpayannāha, yadi punaracetanāni cetanānadhiṣṭhitāni kāryaṃ kuryuḥ, tato yatra kvacanāvasthitāni janayeyuriti na deśakālapratiniyataprasavaṃ kāryamupalabhyeta | hetusamavadhānādhīnajanmatayā kāryaṃ na pratyekaṃ kāraṇairjanyata iti cet ? satyam, samavadhānameva tu kāraṇānāṃ kutaḥ ? kādācitkaparipākād adṛṣṭaviśeṣāditi cet ? nanvayamapyacetanaḥ kathaṃ yathāvatkāraṇāni sannidhāpayet ?
no khalu yatra kvacanāvasthitāni daṇḍādīni vinā kumbhakāraprayatnamadṛṣṭaviśeṣavaśādeva parasparaṃ sannidhīyante, sannihitāni vā kāryasyeśate | tasmāt kāraṇasamavadhānavyāptatvāt kāryotpādasya, tasya copalabdhimatpūrvakatvābhāve'nupapattervyāpakanivṛttyā vipakṣāt kāryotpādo nivartamāna upalabdhimatpūrvakatvena vyāpyata iti pratibandhasiddhiriti ||
[239,3]
evaṃ sati bhavatu kartṛmātrasiddhiḥ, sarvajñatā tu kathamasya, dṛṣṭānte tadanvayasyābhāvāditi cet ?
[239,4]
atra trilocanaḥ, naitadasti | yato nāsmābhirupāttabhedaḥ kartā sādhayitumiṣṭaḥ, kiṃ tarhi ? sādhyasāmānyam | tasya ca yena viśeṣeṇa saha vāstavaḥ pratibandho'sti so'pyupādānādisākṣātkāraṇalakṣaṇo viśeṣaḥ sādhyasāmānye niścetavye'vaśyaniścetavyaḥ, tattyāge sādhyasāmānyatyāgaprasaṅgāt | na ca śakyaṃ tyaktum, sādhyasāmānyasya kṣityādidharmivyāpakatvāt | tatpunaḥ kṣityādyupādānaṃ paramāṇucatuṣṭayam sarvakṣetrajñasamavetasiddhirūpāṇi karmāṇi | dikkālau copakaraṇam | sarvakṣetrajñalakṣaṇaṃ ca sampradānam |
kṣetrajñopabhogalakṣaṇaṃ ca prayojanam | etat sarvaṃ pratyakṣataḥ pratipadyamānaḥ kartā pratyakṣīkṛtasakalaviśvavibhāgaḥ sarvajñaḥ | na cāsyopanyāsapūrvako'nvayo dṛṣṭānte pradarśyate, yenānanvayādidoṣagaṇasyāpattiḥ syāt ||
[240,1]
syādetat | mahābhūtotpatterdvyaṇukādikramasya ghaṭaniṣpatterapi dvyaṇukādikramaviśeṣānupalabdherayaṃ ghaṭaṃ kurvan kumbhakāro dvyaṇukamapi karoti | na ca tasyopādānam upakaraṇaṃ vā kulālaḥ pratyakṣataḥ pratipadyate | tasmādayamanekāntaḥ, yo yasya kartā sa tasyopādānādi jānātīti ||
[240,2]
atrocyate | bhavedanekānto yadi kulālo dvyaṇukasya kartā bhavet | na hi yāvadantyāvayaviniṣpatteraṅgaṃ tat sarvaṃ kulālaḥ karoti, dṛṣṭasāmarthyakāraṇaprayoktṛlakṣaṇatvāt kartṛkatvasya | tasmād dvyaṇukamapi mahābhūtavat sandigdhakartṛkatvāt sādhyameva |
tadevaṃ yat sādhyavādinā sādhayitumiṣṭamanumeyasāmānyaṃ tad dūṣaṇavādinā pratibandhuṃ na śakyate | yastu dūṣaṇavādinā pratibandhumiṣṭo viśeṣaḥ, nāsau sādhyasāmānyavādinā sādhayitumiṣṭaḥ | kiṃ tarhi ? sādhyasāmānye niścetavye tena vāstavapratibandhasya viśeṣasya siddhirbalād bhavantī nopekṣyate | evaṃ sādhanāyattāṃ viśeṣasiddhimācāryo manyamāno yad dūṣaṇamavādīt — yāvatīmarthagatiṃ sādhanaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatīṃ dūṣaṇamapi | yadyasau viśeṣo na sādhanena viṣayīkṛtaḥ, kathamatastatsiddhiḥ ? sidhyan vā kathamaviṣayaḥ ?
viṣayaścet, kathaṃ svāśrayāṃ doṣagatiṃ na spṛśediti, tannirastam | yataḥ sādhanavādī sādhanādhīnāṃ yadi viśeṣasiddhimabhyupagacchet tadaitat syāt | na ca naiyāyikaḥ sādhanāyattāṃ viśeṣasiddhimupajīvati | kiṃ tarhi ? sādhyasāmānyapratibandhākṛṣṭasya viśeṣasya siddhim, yathā bauddhaḥ kṣaṇikatvasiddhau tena vāstavapratibandhānnairātmyasiddhimupajīvati |
na hyātmani nitye vibhau ca sati sarvavastuviṣayaṃ kṣaṇikatvamanumātumīśaḥ ||
[240,3]
mīmāṃsako'pi darśanasparśanābhyāmekamavayavinaṃ niścinvan niścetavyānuṣaṅgiṇa indriyasya nānātvaṃ niyataviṣayatvamindriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayagrahaṇaliṅgatvaṃ jñāturjñānasādhanatvaṃ gandhādiguṇavyatiriktaṃ ca guṇādhikaraṇamaniyataviṣayaścetana ityetāvato'rthānupajīvati | tathā sādhyaviśeṣo'pi naiyāyikairupajīvyata iti sarvaṃ samānam anyatrābhiniveśāt | tasmāt siddhaṃ sarvajñatvamiti ||
[240,4]
vācaspatistu, syādetat | utpattimattvamupādānādyabhijñakartṛmātravyāptaṃ ghaṭādiṣu dṛṣṭaṃ tanmātrameva pṛthivyādīnāṃ gamayet | nityasarvaviṣayajñānavatkartṛpūrvakatvaṃ tu kutastyam ? na caitad ghaṭādau dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇi dṛṣṭam ||
[241,1]
nanvevaṃ rūpādyupalabdheḥ kriyātvena cakṣurādisādhanānumānamapi katham ? na hi cchidādayaḥ kriyā indriyasādhanā dṛṣṭāḥ, tāsāṃ kuṭhārādisādhanatvāt | atha dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇyadṛṣṭamapi indriyasādhanatvaṃ pakṣadharmatābalāt sidhyati, rūpādyupalabdhigataṃ hi kriyātvaṃ tadeva karaṇaṃ gamayet, yat tadupalabdhinirvartanasamartham, na ca kuṭhārādayaḥ samarthā iti pakṣadharmatābalāt kuṭhārādivilakṣaṇamadṛṣṭacaramapi cakṣurādi upasthāpayatīti |
tadatrāpi samānam | na hyaparimeyāniyatadigdeśaindriyakātīndriyakatrasasthāvarādilakṣaṇakāryotpādayaugapadyamasati sarvaviṣaye jñāne nitye vā seddhumarhati | no khalvīdṛśaṃ pārameśvaraṃ jñānaṃ kāryaśarīrendriyādikāryaṃ saṃbhavati, śarīrādyutpatteḥ prāgasyācaitanyena tatprākkālakāryotpādāya parameśvarāntarakalpanāprasaṅgāt | evaṃ ca tataḥ prāk tataḥ prāgiti anekālaukikakalpanāyāṃ varamekamevālaukikaṃ buddhinityatvaṃ kalpitam | etenaiva śarīrendriyanityatvakalpanā prativyūḍhā | etena yadeke bruvate, sanniveśādimatsarva buddhimaddhetu yadyapi | prasiddhyet sanniveśāderekakartṛkatā kutaḥ || (vidhibiveke pṛ. 219)
iti, tadapi parākṛtam | teṣāṃ sidhyet sarvajñanirākriyāmanoratho yadi piśitacakṣuṣaḥ paramāṇūn kṣetrajñān tatsamavetān vā karmāśayān draṣṭumīśate | na caitadasti | tasmāt atīndriyārthadarśino'smadādivilakṣaṇā bahavaḥ kalpanīyāḥ | tad varamastveka eva tādṛśaḥ kalpanālādhavāyeti | tadevaṃ kāryatvādeva pakṣadharmatāsahāyādevambhūteśvarasiddhiriti sthitam ||
[241,2]
bhavatu vāsmādupādānādyabhijñakartṛmātrasiddhiḥ | pāriśeṣyānumānāt tu vyatirekidvitīyanāmno viśeṣasiddhiḥ | tathā hi tanubhuvanādyabhijñaḥ kartā nānityāsarvaviṣayabuddhimān, tatkartustadupādānādyanabhijñatvaprasaṅgāt | na hyevaṃvidhastadupādānādyabhijño dṛṣṭo yathāsmadādiḥ | tadupādānādyabhijñaścāyam | tasmāt tatheti | no khalu paramāṇubhedān pratikṣetrajñasamavāyinaśca karmāśayabhedānaparimeyānanyaḥ śakto jñātumṛte tādṛśādīśvarāditi ||
[242,1]
vittokastu, yathā dhūmadarśanena pakṣadharmatābalāt nikuñjavartitvaṃ vahnerviśeṣo'vyāpako'pi pratīyate tathā karturapītyadoṣa iti tādṛgeva puruṣaviśeṣa īśvaraḥ pramāṇasiddha iti kathamanīśajagadvādino bhagavataḥ pramāṇenāvyāhataśāsanatvamiti ||
{7.2}
<īśvaravādādhikāre saṃkṣepadūṣaṇam>
[243,1]
vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyāpekṣaprabandhabhīrūṇām | īśvaravāde dūṣaṇamātrakatheyaṃ samāsena ||
[243,2]
iha yadyapi bahulaṃ sahacāramātraṃ kāryasya prayatnavatā darśitam, darśitaśca tadabhāve kvacidabhāvaḥ, tathāpi pratibandhāsiddheḥ kāryamapi syāt, na ca buddhimatkartṛpūrvakamityāśaṅkā bādhavaidhuryāt kāryaṃ buddhimati sādhye sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttiko hetvābhāsaḥ | na ca sapakṣavipakṣayordarśanādarśanamātreṇa sādhanasya bhāve sādhyasyāvaśyambhāvaḥ, sādhyābhāve vā tadabhāva ityevaṃ rūpāyā vyāpteḥ pratibandhaśabdavācyāyāḥ sādhanaṃ bhavitumarhati, bhāvivyabhicāradarśaneṣvapi tathopalabdheḥ | kimidamidānīmadarśanamabhāvādeva vyabhicārasya, atha darśanasāmagrīsamavadhānavirahāditi nirṇetumaśakyameva sahacāramātradarśino vimarśaśīlasya |
[243,3]
ata eva vācaspateḥ svābhāvikasambandhadhoṣaṇamapi śabdapuṣṭimātram, tadatiriktārthāpoṣaṇāt | bhūyodarśane hi vyabhicārādarśane svābhāvikavyavasthā | vyabhicārādarśanaṃ ca vipakṣe'darśanamātramuktaṃ bhavati | yat punaretadupādheranupalambhena vyabhicārāsiddhiriti, tatra nopādhirnāma dṛśyacihnasthānīyaṃ kiñcidasti, yadanupalambho'vyabhicāraṃ vyavahārayet | kiṃ tu vyabhicāradarśanamātreṇaiva tatparikalpaḥ | tadadarśanāt ca svābhāvikatvamiti viśeṣābhāvāt na svābhāvikavādena kiñcit, sādhyena saha bhūyo dṛṣṭo heturvyabhicāre ca na heturitīyataiva paryāptatvāt | etacca sarvaṃ vyāpticarcāyāṃ vivicya kvacidarthāntarasya pratibandho nāma tadutpattimantareṇa, sā ca pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanaiveti vyavasthāpitamiti tata evāvadhāryam |
etena śaṅkaravācaspatimatāvalambinaḥ pratyuktāḥ |
[243,4]
astu tarhi prayatnavatāpi kāryasya tadutpattilakṣaṇa eva pratibandho dhūmasyeva vahninā | yathoktaṃ vittokena | tathā hi kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk mṛtpiṇḍadaṇḍacakrādiṣu satsvapi kāryaṃ kumbhākhyamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhaṃ tadvyāpārānantaram upalabhyata iti hetuphalabhāvasiddhau kuto vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ ? satyamatra pakṣavipakṣavṛttireva na sandehaḥ, atra hi pratyakṣānupalambhayogyasvarūpasvīkārādabhivyakto'nupalabdhapuruṣavyāpārairvṛkṣavīraṇādibhirvyabhicāraḥ | pakṣīkṛtāstṛṇādayaḥ, na ca pakṣīkṛtenaiva vyabhicāra iti cet — na, pratikṣiptasya pakṣīkaraṇe nyāyābhāvāt | anyathā anuṣṇo'gniḥ prameyatvādityādāvapi pakṣīkaraṇameva śaraṇaṃ syāt | tathā hi, sandigdhe hetuvacanād vyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ | (pra. vā. 4. 91)
iti nyāyaḥ | adhyakṣameva pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogyantarāpekṣayānupalabdhirucyate |
tato'nupalabdhibādhitamapi pratyakṣabādhitameva | vyavahārasādhanāpekṣayā tu sānumānam |
na cānumānabādhite'pyanyāvakāśaḥ | sā tarhi dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpannasyaivābhāvaṃ vyavahārayati, dṛśyādṛśyaśarīretarasādhāraṇaṃ ca buddhimattvamiti dṛśyatāniyamānupapatterbuddhimataḥ katham anupalabdhimātreṇa tṛṇādijanmani niṣedhaḥ ? tataḥ sandehāt pakṣīkaraṇaṃ nyāyyamiti cet ? tadetad vikrotagavīrakṣaṇam | vyāptisādhanāyādhyakṣānupalabdhyoravakāśadānādeva dṛśyaviṣayatāsvīkārasya prasahyāyātatvāt | na hyadṛśye pratyakṣamanvayasādhanamanupalabdhirvā vyatirekasādhanī bhavitumarhati | tadayaṃ bhede satyanvayavyatirekarūpamadhyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ hetuphalabhāvamavataranna dṛśyatāmativartituṃ sādhyasya śaktaḥ | dṛśyatve ca niyatatṛṇādinā vyabhicāra iti sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ ||
[244,1]
atha vyabhicāracamatkārādadhyakṣāgocareṇa prayatnavatā vyāptiṃ gṛhṇīyāt ?
gṛhṇātu, na tu pratyakṣānupalambhāśrayaḥ śreyānasya | nanu dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇamanapekṣya prekṣāvanmātreṇa vyāptigrahaḥ ? naivam, tāvatāpi hi pratyakṣakṛtāyā vyāpteranavakāśa eva |
dṛśyaikasvabhāvaniyatā hi sā kathaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviṣayā bhavet ? taddhi dṛśyamadṛśyaṃ ca rūpamekabuddhimattvādidharmānuvṛttāvapi svabhāvaviprakarṣetarābhyāmatyantaṃ bhinnajātiḥ | tataḥ pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyaikajātisvīkāreṇa pravṛttamitaravārtānabhijñaṃ tadviśiṣṭameva sādhāraṇamapi dharmaṃ vyāpakamādarśayati |
[244,2]
yadyapi deśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi na dṛśyam, tathāpi tadadarśanayogyatayaikajātyeveti svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭasyaiva pratyakṣeṇa parihāraḥ | sarvānyavarjane hi svalakṣaṇaikaparyavasānād vyāptireva na syāt, dhūmāgnivat, kampamārutavacca | yathā hi svapravṛttiyogyajvaladbhāsurākārapuraskāreṇa pravartamānādhyakṣakṛtā vyāptiḥ saptārciṣi na jaṭharānalasādhāraṇarūpaparyavasāyinī, anyathā tārṇādibhedavadabhimate'pi rūpe sandihāno na tatsādhyārthakriyālābhaikāgrabuddhiḥ pravarteta | pratibandhavaikalyavad vāsati jaṭharyatva ityāmṛśataḥ pravṛttiḥ syāt | yathā vā pallavollāsane samīraṇena vyāptiradhyakṣajakṛtāspṛśyarūpapuraskārānnastimitamārutasādhāraṇarūpaparyavasāyinī, anyathādyāpi kisalayakampena mātariśvānamanumāpayan spṛśyaprabhañjanānurūpapravṛttinivṛttī niścayenācaret, tathā puruṣe'pi pratyakṣakṛtā vyāpitāgṛhītiradṛśyarūpaparihāreṇaiva | tasmāt pratyakṣāvyājena yadi paramiṣṭamātrameva sādhanaṃ nādhyakṣaṃ dṛśyādṛśyasāmānye'pīti vyāpterabhāvāt sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva |
[245,1]
prayogaḥ, yo yaḥ pratyakṣakṛtaḥ kāraṇatvaniścayaḥ, nāsau dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyī, yathāgnau jaṭharajātajātavedaḥsādhāraṇarūpaṃ pariharan | pratyakṣakṛtaścāsau buddhimatīti vyāpakaviruddhavyāptopalabdhiḥ | pratyakṣakṛtatvaṃ hi dṛśyaviṣayatvena vyāptamadṛśye tasyāpravṛtteḥ, tadviruddhaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviṣayatvam, tadvyāptaṃ dṛśyādṛśyarūpaparyavasāyitvam |
kiṃ ca yadi dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇamavadhūya dhīmanmātreṇa vyāptirvivakṣitā, evaṃ sati yadā buddhimadabhāve kumbhakāryasyābhāvamupadarśayed vyatirekapratipādanāya, tadā dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣaṇarahitacetanamātrasyābhāvaḥ kena pramāṇena siddhaḥ, dṛśyānupalabdherdṛśyasyaiva pratiṣedhe'dhikārāt ? anyathā tṛṇādinā vyabhicārasyāśakyaparihāratvācca ?
[245,2]
na ca dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhirbuddhimanmātrasya vyatirekabodhasādhanībhavitum arhati, ātyantikaviṣayabhedasya vyaktatvāt | anyathā tṛṇādijanmanyapi dṛśyapuruṣaviṣayaivānupalabdhistadvyabhicārasthirīkaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt | na hi lābhe praveśaśchede niḥsaraṇamiti nyāyyam | tasmād dṛśyaviśeṣaṇāpoḍhapakṣe vyāptigrahaṇakāle vyatirekagrahaṇopāyābhāvād avyāpteḥ punarapi vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehaḥ | na ca nabhasyubhayābhāvavibhāvanamupāyo vyatirekagrahaṇasya, kāryābhāvasya buddhimadvyāpārābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayānupapatteḥ | tadaparakāraṇasākalye hi tanmātrābhāve'bhāvaḥ kāryasya tadabhāvaprayuktaḥ pratyetuṃ śakyaḥ | yathā trikapañcakacintāyāṃ cintitam | dvayostu kvacinnivṛttimātram akāryakāraṇabhūtayorapi sulabham |
[245,3]
kiṃ ca buddhimatkāraṇavyāpāravirahāt vihāyasi kāryatvābhāva uta kāraṇamātraviprayogāditi ko niṣṭaṅkaḥ ? tathā ca sati viphalaḥ sakalo yatnaḥ | anvayo'pi hi kāraṇamātreṇa kāryamātrasya gṛhyatāmutasvit puruṣaviśeṣaṇena kāraṇeneti sandeha eva |
atha dṛṣṭa evāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathaṃ parihartu śakyaḥ, dhūme dahanātmavat | yadyevaṃ dṛśyaśarīrarūpo'pi viśeṣaḥ pratīta eva, kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ, citrabhānorbhāsurākāravat ? sa tarhi viśeṣaḥ kāryeṇa vyabhicaryata iti cet ? vyabhicaryatām | kārye'pi kāraṇavad yathā paridṛṣṭaviśeṣaniṣṭha evānvayo bhavatu ghaṭavat saudhādāvapi dṛṣṭatvāditi kiṃ naśchinnam ?
etaccānvayamātraṃ gajanimolitena dūṣaṇamavadhīryābhidhoyate | vastutastu pratyakṣānupalambhayorekasyāpi vyāpārāyogānnānvayo na vyatirekaḥ | asti ca kāryatvamurvīdharādau, na ca darśanātikrānte kartaryanvayavyatirekau spṛśati | tādṛkcetanakṛtetaratvābhyāṃ ca rāśyantarābhāvād gandhādivadasādhāraṇānekānta eva | tasmānna pratyakṣeṇa kāryamātrasya vyāptigrahaṇamiti siddham |
[246,1]
yātāścaivaṃ yadamī pratyakṣānupalambhāviśiṣṭakāryajātyullekhenaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇapravṛttayo na kāryamātrollekhena | tathā hi pratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttisamanantaramīdṛśāt jvaladbhāsurasvarūpavastuviśeṣādīdṛśaṃ dhavalimaliptakaṇṭhāmbakavikārakāri vastu jāyata ityanenākāreṇa hetuphalabhāvavyavahāraḥ sarvāparakāryakāraṇajātivyudāsena viśiṣṭameva jātiyugmamullikhan pravartate | iyameva gatiḥ sarvatra hetuphalabhāvavyavahṛtau, īśvarānurodhāt tu prasiddhanyāyollaṅghanametat iti paśyāmaḥ ||
[246,2]
kaḥ punaratrāparādho yadi tārṇādibhedamudasya vahninā dhūmamātrasyeva bhūdharādibhedamapyudasya kāryamātrasya buddhimatā vyāptiṃ pratīyāt pratyakṣam ? yathaiva tarhi varhiṣā kāryajātiviśeṣasya dhūmasyāvāntarasūkṣmajātimātramantarbhāvya vyāptigraho na tu tadvijātīyasparśaḥ, tathā buddhimatāpyastu vastrādeḥ | yathā vātyantavisadṛśorapi kāryajātīḥ antarbhāvya bhūtimanmātrasya cetanena vyāptiṃ jighṛkṣasi, tathā vahnināpi gṛhṇīyāḥ |
indriyapratyakṣasyaiva hi vyāpāra ubhayatra kathaṃ bhinnāṃ vṛttimāśrayeta ? vyabhicāradarśanādarśanakṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet ? tattarhi darśanādarśanaṃ saṅkalpamanārūḍhaṃ gacchattṛṇasparśavadakiñcitkaramiti tadanurūpavimarśenāvaśyabhāvyam | na cāsti |
[246,3]
na hi kaścidagnidhūmādiṣvanvayavyatirekagrāhipratyakṣānupalambhapravṛttau kāryajātiḥ akhilānalādutpadyata iti saṅkalpamanubhūya bhūyo vyabhicāradarśanāt yato vā kāryāntarāṇi vahnimantareṇāpyupalabdhānyupalabhyante vā tato dhūma evānena janyata iti niścayaṃ paricinoti, kiṃ tu jhagityeva pratyakṣānupalambhāntaramasmādagnyāderidaṃ dhūmādīti jātiviśeṣadvayaṃ hetuphalabhāvavyavahārabhājanīkurvannanubhūyate'nusandhānapratyayaḥ | pratyakṣagocare anvayavyatirekayorna kaścid viśeṣaḥ | yadā ca vikalpāntarasthitasya jhagiti kaṇṭakād vyathetyanupalambhapūrvikādhyakṣavihitā hetuphalabhāvagrāhiṇī matiḥ, tadābhivyakto vyabhicāradarśanavimarśavirahaḥ, samasamayāsambhavād vikalpānām | tadihāpyasmāt śilpina idaṃ pṛthubudhnodarādyākāraṃ kāryamityavāntarasūkṣmabhedamudasya vyavahāraḥ | yadā tu paṭaśakaṭādikamapi puruṣādutpadyamānaṃ paśyati, tadedamapīdamapi puruṣeṇa janyata iti matiravisaṃvādinī samudeti ||
[247,1]
kiṃ ca vyabhicāro nāma kiṃ siddhāyāmeva vyāptāvanumānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati ?
atha vyāptireva mithyeti vyavasthāpayati ? atrāpi pakṣe svasāmarthyena sphuratyeva vyāptigrāhiṇi pramāṇe | yad vā tasyaiva prāmāṇyakṣayamādadhānaḥ, adyāpi sarvatra viṣaye niyate vā ?
niyate'pi kimiṣṭivaśāt, atha pratyakṣasya tatraiva pravṛtteḥ ? prathamaḥ pakṣastāvanna yukto virodhāt | na hi sādhyāvinābhāvalakṣaṇā ca vyāptirhetoḥ sādhyābhāvasaṃbhavakṛtaścānumānābhāvaḥ saṅgacchate, anyatrāpi vyāptāvanāśvāsācca |
[247,2]
evaṃ vyāptigrāhiṇi pramāṇe prāmāṇyādapracyutibhṛti vyāptimṛṣātvabodhanamapyasambaddhaṃ boddhavyam | sarvatra ca vyāptigrāhiṇaḥ prāmāṇyakṣaye dhūmādagnirapi nānumātavyaḥ, anyasya vyāptigrāhiṇo'bhāvāt | kimidānīṃ śaraṇamīśvarānumānasya bhaviṣyati ?
svecchayā ca niyate viṣaye vyāptivihitau pramāṇaṃ varākamudāsīnamiti na kaścit heturaheturvā tattvataḥ, dhūme'pi svecchayā vyāptikhaṇḍanaprasaṅgāt | niyataviṣayatvaṃ tu vyabhicāragocarasyāpi pratyakṣasya katham, yāvatā yathā niyatajātipravṛttaṃ vyāptigrāhi sarvaviṣayamiṣṭam, tathā vyabhicāragocaramapi sarvaviṣayamevānyūnānatiriktaśaktitvād ubhayoḥ ? tadekaviṣaya eva vyāptigraho vyabhicāravedanaṃ ceti kimadhunā sādhanamasādhanaṃ vā syāt ? bhavatu vā bhavaduparodhād bādhabodhinaḥ pramāṇasya niyataviṣayatvam |
tathāpi na khalu sakṛdeva vyabhicāravatāṃ bādhabodhaḥ, kiṃ tu krameṇa | tadā ca vyabhicāriṇāmapi vyabhicāradarśanamāhatya nāstīti dhūmasya tato viśeṣābhāvāt punarahetutvam, hetutvaṃ vānyasyāpi |
[247,3]
na ca sarvasyānyasya vyabhicāradarśanairdhūme vyāptiviśvāsa iti vācyam | evaṃ hi purastād dhūme vyāptigrahaṇānantarameva parvatanitambe dhūmād dahanānumānaṃ na śārdūlāditi na syāt, vyabhicāradarśanavilambāpekṣaṇāt | aśakyaṃ caitadanyatra vyabhicāradarśanairabhimate vyāptiviśrāma iti | vyabhicāraviṣayāṇāmapyanantatvād deśādiviprakarṣavatāṃ gocarīkaraṇakālāpekṣayā puruṣāyuṣasya kanīyastvāt | tasmād vyabhicāradarśanavanniyataviṣaya eva vyāptigraho nirapavādaḥ, śuddhekādhyavasāyasya vibhāgena pravṛtteḥ | ataeva ca svābhāvikavikalpasyaiva kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇe'dhikāro naupādhikasya |
[248,1]
asti hi śuddhaviṣayajanitālocanājñānamātrāpekṣo bālatiryaksādhāraṇo vikalpaḥ |
sa śuddhaḥ svābhāvika iti cocyate, yadvaśāt paśavo'pi kṣutpipāsāpraśamādisādhanāni tatraiva samarthānyavadhārayantaḥ punastadanvitayā tathaiva tatastatra pravartante, nivartante vānanvitayā |
asti ca saṅketasmaraṇasacivālocanājñānajanito vikalpaḥ, yathā dīpāt kajjalamālokayato nīlamidaṃ rañjanādyupayogītyeva vikalpaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭārthakriyāsmaraṇasahāyānubhavabhāvitastādṛgaupādhika ucyate | na ca tadā nīlavikalpa ityeva pradīpādakhilaṃ nīlamutpadyata iti prekṣaḥ kaścinniścinoti | kiṃ tu yadeva kajjalāvalokanamātrānurūpavikalpapuraskṛtaṃ vastu kajjalaśabdasaṅketayogyaṃ jātiyogāt svarūpaviśeṣād vā tadeva pradīpakāryaṃ vyabhicārālambane coktam |
[248,2]
evaṃ dhūme'pi dhavalamidaṃ vastu vahnerjāyata iti saṅketānusārī vikalpa aupādhika evākṣipati kāryatvena tuhinādikam | śuddhe tu vikalpe dhūmajātireva parisphuratīti tata eva tuhinādervyāptau nirāso na vyabhicārālambanaṃ sādhviti boddhavyam | tadvat kāryavikalpo'pi sarvatra aupādhika eva | apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi svotpattāvandhaḥ | kāryamiti saṅketasmaraṇasahāyādindriyajñānādutpattiriti na hetuphalabhāvavyavahārasyāṅgam |
tato yadyapi puruṣāt ghaṭodayadarśane ghaṭo'yamasmāditi vikalpavat kāryamidamasmādityapi sulabho vikalpaḥ, tathāpi svābhāvikatvābhāvānna tatpuraskṛtasvarūpasya tatkāryatvavyavasthā |
naisargikavikalpaviṣayīkṛtasya tu bhavatu |
[248,3]
nanu śuddhāvasāyagocare'pi vikalpaḥ saṅketasmṛtijanito dṛśyate'yaṃ ghaṭaḥ pauruṣeya iti nāmollekhāt | tataḥ so'pyaupādhikaḥ prāptaḥ | na, tanmātravikalpane smaraṇasya aprayojakatvāt, vācakāṃśollekha eva tasya sāmarthyāt | yadyapi ca vācyavācakākārotkalitākhaṇḍavikalpodayaḥ smaraṇasāhāyakena, tathāpyapoddhāradvāreṇa tanmātre tadvyāpāra ucyate, mṛnmayatvamātre kulālasyeva | jātyantarasamavāyikāryatvadhavalatādidharmakalpanaṃ tu saṅketasambandhagrahaṇādiprācīnavyāpārasmaraṇamantareṇa śuddhādhyavasāyasya tanmātrajātyullekhenaiva kṛtārthatvād bālakādivat, atastanmātraviṣayaiva pratyakṣakṛtā vyāptirityanavadyam | tasmād vyāptigrahaḥ pratyakṣakṛto vyabhicārapratyayo vā bhinnaviṣaya eveti siddham |
[249,1]
evaṃ tarhi vyabhicāradarśanena sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā duḥstheti cet ? evametad yadi buddhipāṭavaniyamaḥ sarveṣām | mandabuddhistu sādṛśyādinā jātiviśeṣapravṛtte'pi pratyakṣe jātyantareṇaikīkṛtya vyāptigrahābhimānādanumānamātiṣṭhamānaḥ paṭunā pareṇa vyabhicāramādarśya vyāptidurgrahamāpādyate | ataḥ sādhāraṇānekāntavyavasthā |
yathā dhūme pravṛtte'pi pratyakṣe vyāptigrāhiṇyucchaladvahalarūpamanalavyāptimanusmaran mārutoddhūtadhūlipaṭalādanalamanumāpayan vāṣpodayena prasiddhoṣarbudhavaidhuryeṇa vyabhicāramādarśya vāryate, tato'pi kāraṇāt jātiviśeṣaviṣayaiva vyāptiḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti siddham |
[249,2]
yadi hi dhūmaikajātipratibaddhapratibandhabodhamadhyakṣam, tadā sādṛśyāpekṣo'nyatra tadrūpāropaḥ, sadṛśāntaravyabhicāreṇa ca vāraṇaṃ yuktam | yadā tu kāryajātau sarvatra vyāptigrahaḥ, tadā kiṃ sādṛśyāpekṣayeti ? yadi tarhi jātiviśeṣapratibaddha evādhyakṣeṇa pratibandhabodhaḥ kathamatyantavijātīyā api ghaṭakuṭakuḍyādayaḥ sādhāraṇarāgayogino haridrādidravyasaṃskāramanumāpayanti ? kathaṃ vā kuṭhārādi cchedakriyāyāṃ dṛṣṭavyāpāraṃ karaṇamatyantavijātīyāpi buddhiḥ kriyātvenānumāpayati ?
[249,3]
evamatyantavijātīyā api kailāsakuliśādayaḥ sādhāraṇakāryatvādidharmakāḥ puruṣamanumāpayiṣyantīti cet ? naivam, vyāpyasya gamakatvāt, tadapekṣayaiva sajātīyavijātīyatāyāścintyatvāt | vyāpyaṃ ca nirvartyavikāryakarmāpekṣayā dvividhaṃ dharmirūpaṃ dharmarūpaṃ ca | tatra sarvathāpūrvotpattau dharmiṇo vyāptirucyate, dhūmādivat | tadā ca dhūmāntarameva sajātīyam, vijātīyamanyad vastu | yadā tu pūrvasthitasyaiva dharmāntarotpattivyavasāyaḥ, tadā dharmavyāptirucyate, payasi auṣṇyādivat, tadā ca auṣṇyāntarameva sajātīyo dharmaḥ, nādhunā dharmijāterapekṣā |
[249,4]
evaṃ rāgo'pi ghaṭakuṭādidravyavaijātyamavamatya svayaṃ svajātīyakāryāpekṣayaiva rāgadravyasaṃskārasya gamakaḥ | ataeva tadviśeṣe kvacit kuṅkumasya samparkaḥ kvacit haridrāderanumīyate | na caivaṃ pūrvasthite bhūdharāmbhodharādau kāryatvādimātranirvartakaḥ puruṣa iṣṭaḥ, kiṃ tu kumbhādivadapūrvakotpādaka eva | tadā ca dhūme dhavalatādivat kāryatādayaḥ santo'pi jātyantarasamavāyino dharmā vyāpterbahirbhāvādakiñcitkarā eva | tasmād dharmivastuvyāptigraho na dharmamātrapratyāsattimanurudhyate | nāpi dharmavyāpterdharmiṇaḥ sajātīyatām | śuddhaikavimarśāpekṣayā ca sajātīyetaravyavasthānamuktam | nāto rāgavaddharmivaijātye'pi kāryatvādīnāṃ gamakatvam | anyathā pāṇḍudravyādapi havyāśanānumānaprasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ, vyabhicārottarasya dūṣitatvāt |
[250,1]
indriye tvevamanumānam | yadanyakāraṇasannidhau kādācitkam, tat kāraṇāntarāpekṣam, yathā pāthaḥpṛthvīsannidhāvaṅkuraḥ, viṣayamanaskārālokasannidhau ca kādācitkī buddhiriti svabhāvahetuḥ | anapekṣatve vipakṣe kādācitkaṃ virodhādanavasthāyīti bādhakāt vyāptisiddhiḥ | yat tadanyadapekṣyaṃ tadindriyamiti vyavasthā, tato na kriyātvena kāraṇānumānaṃ, nāpi pratyakṣaṃ vyāptigrāhi | avaśyaṃ ca svābhāvikavikalpāmukhīkṛtajātibhedapuraskāreṇaiva sāmānyagrahaṇameṣitavyamadhyakṣasya, anyathā yadā pratyakṣeṇa vyāptimekāmupadarśyāyaṃ ghaṭa iti saṅketaḥ kriyate, tadā kimasau kāryatvādidharmayogi viśvamāviśati ? vyabhicāradarśanena ca niyataviṣayatāmupanīyate ? upadeṣṭaiva vā sarvānyajātiṣu niṣedhan viṣayaniyame niṣṭhāpayati ? atha sāmānyaviṣaya eva nāsau samayaḥ ?
[250,2]
evaṃ vācakajātibhede'pi draṣṭavyam | kāryaśabdastu pratyakṣamanapekṣya vikalpamātragocarite parāpekṣodayamātre niveśita iti na viśeṣavṛttiḥ | yadi tu so'pi pratyakṣavartinyayaṃ kārya iti niveśyeta, so'pi tatparyāyāntaravānniyatavṛttireva syāt |
tasmāt kāyajātiviśeṣaviṣayīkaraṇameva nisargaḥ pratyakṣasya | yadi ca kāryajātibhede pravṛttamapi pratyakṣaṃ kāryamātramadhiṣṭhānīkaroti, kāraṇe tarhi pravartamānaṃ kāraṇamātrameva vyāpakamavadhārayatu, kasmādupādānādivedanaviśiṣṭamavalambate ? tato yadi na bhavadabhiprāyānurodho'dhyakṣasyobhayatra sāmānyāvalambinā viśeṣāvalambinā vā bhavitavyamanena, sāmānyālambane kāryāt kāraṇānumānamiti kā vārteśvarasiddheḥ ? viśeṣāvalambane ca kāryamātravyāpterasiddheriti | tasmādanubhavād yuktaśca viśiṣṭāmeva kāryajātiṃ hetuviśeṣavyāptāmupadarśayati pratyakṣamiti |
[250,3]
prayogaḥ | yad yat kāryakāraṇabhāvagrāhi pratyakṣam, tad viśiṣṭajātipratiniyatavyāpāram, yathāgnidhūmayoḥ | tathā cedaṃ buddhimatā kāryasya vyāptisādhanamiti svabhāvahetuḥ | nāsyānyathāvyāpārāśaṅkayānekāntaḥ, kāraṇānupalabdhibādhitatvāt | kāraṇabhedo hi kāryabhedasya kāraṇam, anyathā sarvasyāhetukatvaprasaṅgāt | na cāsya kāraṇabhedo'sti, viṣayendriyālokādilakṣaṇasamānasāmagrīprabhavatvāditi | dṛṣṭānte sādhyaśūnyatāśaṅkāyāṃ ca yad yat pratyakṣam, tat tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva sāmānyāvalambanam, yathā vyabhicāragrāhi pratyakṣam, pratyakṣaṃ ca vyāptigrāhīti svabhāva eva | sa evānekāntaparihāraḥ | buddhimatkāryayorapi vyāptigrāhiṇi dharmiṇyayameva vā prayogaḥ | athavobhayatrāpi yad yat sambandhagrāhi pratyakṣaṃ tad viśiṣṭajātyaiva, yathā vācyavācakayoḥ, sambandhagrāhi ca pratyakṣaṃ kāryakāraṇayorapi pūrvavat | tadayaṃ yadi tattvataḥ kṛtsno'pi kāryagrāmaḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaḥ, tathāpi kāryajātīnāmatyantavilakṣaṇānāmānantyāt, pratijātibhedaṃ ca vyāptigrahaṇāpekṣaṇāt, yāvajjātikaṃ kāryaṃ puruṣapūrvakaṃ paricchinnam, tāvata eva tadanumānamāñjasamiti yuktamuktam,
[251,1]
siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi |
[251,2]
tathā ca vahnereva dhūmabhasmāṅgārapākapāradotsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛtiṣu kāryeṣu yatra yatraiva pratibandhasādhakamadhyakṣaṃ pravṛttam, tata eva tadanumānam, nānyasmāt | evaṃ devakulakalasaprāsādasyandanadukūlādiṣu vastuvṛttyā pauruṣeyeṣvapi yajjātīyeṣveva puruṣakriyopalabdhirāsīt, tajjātikādeva kāryāt tadanumānamanumanyāmahe | dhārādharadharādharādijātau punastadvyāpārānavadhāraṇāt kānumānavārtā, jātivaijātyasyātyantikasya sambhavena vyāpteragrahāt ? gṛhītavyāpteśca kāryasyādarśanāt || krīḍāparvatakādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumā nāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam | kiṃ cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyanti cedīśinaḥ kā vārtā phalasāmyasaṃvidi kuto hetorviśeṣasthitiḥ || iti hyantaraślokaḥ ||
[251,3]
kīdṛśī punaḥ kāryajātiḥ prayatnavatā vyāptetyāśaṅkya tasyā apyānantyāt saṃkṣepārthamucyate, yaddṛṣṭerarthakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavatīti | tatra ca kṛtabuddhiriti na sādhanabuddhiḥ, nāpyupādānādyabhijñalakṣaṇaprakṛtasādhyabuddhiḥ, kiṃ tu kuvindādisvabhāvasādhyabuddhiḥ | tadabhāvācca na sākṣādbhavadīyahetvasiddhiḥ prakṛtasādhyasiddhirvā vivakṣitā, kiṃ tu ātyantikavaijātyapradarśanametat | taddvāreṇa ca hetorasiddhiravyāptirvābhimataiva |
[252,1]
tathā hi śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādau kulālādisamaśilpibuddhirāvirasti, na malayamakarālayādau | tasyāḥ śilpibuddherbhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamātyantikamantareṇa ityabhiprāyaḥ | vyāpteragrahaṇe smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśe vā devakulādāvapi na syādiyaṃ samānaṃ śilpibuddhiḥ | tato yathā dhūmādagnibuddhirbhavantī gardabhādabhavantī dhūmād gardabhasya niyataṃ jātibhedamāpādayati, tatheyamapi pariniścitapauruṣeyabhāvebhyo bhāvebhyaḥ kailāsakuliśādīnām |
[252,2]
kathaṃ punaranumānābhāva eva pratyetavya iti cet, kumbhakārādambhodadambholiprabhṛtisambhava iti svapne'pi śaṅkāvirahāt | anyathā kuvindapādamardanādanāvṛṣṭikaṣṭam āviśet na lokaḥ, paracakrākrāntikātaro vā kṣitidharajaladhivyavadhimabhilaṣaṃstata eva nirvṛttimāsādayet | kuvindasthānīyastatrāparo'pekṣyata eveti cet — na, samāne kāryajanmani vijātīyakāraṇagaveṣaṇānupapatteḥ, kuvindenaiva sādhyasiddheḥ | na hi paṭāntare api kuvindādaparasyāpekṣā |
[252,3]
asti ca vastraviśeṣe viśiṣṭaśilpino'pekṣeti cet ? asti, yāvadeva tu vastrāntareṇaikajātiparāmarśo dṛḍhaḥ, ata eva kuvindasyaiva śilpinaḥ kalpanam | tadvimarśābhāve pauruṣeyatāyā eva sandehaḥ | merumandarādayastu na kenacit pauruṣeyeṇaikapratyavamarśabhājaḥ | tadeṣāmadhyakṣasiddhamatyantavaijātyaṃ śāṭhyādapahnavānaḥ samānaśilpyanumānaviraheṇa svīkāryate | siddhe ca jātibhede yādṛk kāryaṃ kumbhādi puruṣapratibaddhaṃ siddham, na tādṛggarbhārbhakādi | yādṛk cedaṃ na tādṛk puruṣavyāptamiti siddhā asiddhiḥ avyāptiśca dvayoḥ | evaṃ ca sthite prakṛtasādhyabuddhyajananadvārāṇi dūṣaṇāni dūram apāstāni ||
[252,4]
na hi vayaṃ prakṛtasādhyabuddherabhāvāt kāryatvādihetorasiddhiṃ brūmaḥ | kiṃ tarhi ?
mandarādau kuvindasamaśilpibuddherabhāvādambarādisajātīyakāryatvāsiddhim | tataśca prakṛtasādhyabuddhivaidhuryamiti na kaścid doṣaḥ | kuvindasādhyāpekṣayā ca vyāptigrahaṇasmaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśa eveṣṭa iti na bhūṣaṇavikalpāvakāśaḥ | kṛtakatvamātrapratītistu na vivakṣitaiva | abhraṣṭasmaraṇānāṃ tāvad bhavatyeva puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ kṣityādiṣviti tu dūramapakṛṣṭam |
[252,5]
bauddhakṛtasya hi kṛtabuddhiniṣedhasyāsiddhiḥ prastutā abhidhātum | na ca sā śakyā, kṛtabuddhiśabdena śilpibuddherasya vivakṣitatvāt | puruṣakṛtabuddhibhāvavibhāvanaṃ punaranupayogi | pratīta eva tasmin dūṣaṇacinteyam | tatrāpyabhraṣṭasmaraṇānāmityasaṅgatam, atyantavaijātyasiddheḥ sindhvāderanyato na vyāptipratīteḥ, smaraṇasaṃskārabhraṃśasya parihartumaśakyatvāt | ata eva jagat kenacit sṛṣṭamiti pralāpamātre ka āśvāsaḥ ?
prakṛtasādhyabuddhyāsiddhicodanaparihārādeva ca vedeṣvapītyādi pratyādiṣṭam |
[253,1]
yadi tu pauruṣeyavākyāderatyantaṃ vedasya vaijātyamupadarśayet mīmāṃsakaḥ, tat kiṃ samayamātreṇa parājetavyaḥ ? na tu tayoḥ svarūpadvārakaḥ śaktidvārako vā kaścid viśeṣo'sti | tathā ca tat dvayamagṛhītasaṃketasya puraḥ paṭhitvā pratīhi kasya kīdṛśaṃ viśeṣaṃ vyākurvīta śrotā, kiṃ na vā paśyasi garuḍādimantrakṛtaṃ viṣāpākaraṇādi ?
tadetadāyātam, ekaḥ kāryaviśeṣameva kalayan hetorviśiṣṭaṃ nijaṃ lakṣyāgneriva kāryamātramamunā vyāptaṃ samutpaśyati | tajjātīyakameva kāryamaparo nāvaiti taddhetukaṃ hanta dhvāntaviśeṣa eṣa viduṣāmadhyakṣavastunyapi ||
tasmāt,
[253,2]
yad vācaḥ puruṣānvayavyatiricostadbhāvabhājaḥ sthitā nānyasmād vacasaśca vadikagirāṃ bhedo'sti śakyātmanoḥ | tulyātīndriyasūcanā ca niyataṃ naikatra cāśvāsanaṃ vedastena na pauruṣeyapadavīmaprāpya viśrāmyati ||
[253,3]
yadi tat, kā kathā vicāragocarātītātyantikajātibhedeṣu kumbhādambhodadambholiprabhṛtiṣu tajjātiniyatapratīteḥ pauruṣeyatāyāḥ ? yadapyanityatāsādhanāyopālabdham, tadapi nyāyabāhyam | pratyakṣeṇa pratibandhabodhādhikāre hi tādṛśī sajātīyetaratvamīmāṃsā | anityatve kṛtakatvamātrasya viparyayabādhakapramāṇādanumānasvabhāvāt pratibandhasiddhiriti na tatra jātiviśeṣānurodhaḥ | jātiviśeṣānavacchinne tu kṛtakamātre vyāptisādhanasamarthamasamarthaṃ vā tat pramāṇamiti cintanīyam | śaktau na doṣasparśaḥ |
ata eva tatra ghaṭaśabdabhedena bhedodbhāvanaṃ dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikavaidharmyābhidhānamiti na yuktam | yato dharmirūpādākṛṣṭadharmadvayasya vyāptivyavasthāpanād dharmavastveva dharmīti tadbhedābhidhānasya dharmimātrabheda evārthaḥ |
[254,1]
ihāpi tarhi kāryeṣu dharmiṣu pauruṣeyatvaṃ sādhyaṃ kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti na viśeṣaḥ kaściditi cet ? ucyate, kāryatvamātraṃ heturiti ko'sya bhāṣitasyārthaḥ ? kiṃ tāvanmukhyatayā dharmamātre kāraṇasya kuṅkumādereva rāge vyāpārādevamucyate ? utasvit kārtsnyena kārye vyāptisiddheḥ, dhūmatvamātraṃ heturitivat ? yathā kṛtsno dhūmaḥ sādhyavyāptaḥ, tathā yāvat kāryaṃ tat kṛtsnaṃ puruṣavyāpārajanmakamiti niścayāt | tadetadubhayamapi nirastam |
kṛtakatvamātramanityatvavyāptamiti tu kārtsnyapara eva bhāvanirdeśaḥ, yāvat kṛtakaṃ tat sarvamanityamityayamevārthaḥ | atrārthe pramāṇabale milite siddhe ca dhvaneḥ kṛtakatve ghaṭa eva kṛtako'nityo dṛṣṭaḥ kathaṃ śabdaḥ syāditi niravakāśamevetyayamevārtho dharmimātrabhedo'yamityanayā rītyā prakāśyate |
[254,2]
yathā hi svabhāvahetvadhikāraprastāvāt sādhyasādhanadharmau vikalpārūḍharūpāpekṣayā bhinnau vyavasthāpitau tathā dharmyapi śabdādiḥ, anyasya taddharmaṇo'bhāvāt | na cānyatra dharmiṇi kṛtakavastunā anityavastusādhane dhvaneranityatāsiddhiḥ | tasya ca dharmiṇo ghaṭaśabdabhāvena bhedamāpādayan dūṣaṇamabhidhāya nigṛhyate dharmimātrabhedadvāreṇa | prastute tu kāryahetvabhimānād dhūmasthānīyaḥ kāryarāśiḥ sādhyaśca bhinno'gnivat puruṣaḥ | kevalaṃ nāgnivat taddeśakāla eva | kiṃ tu janmadeśakāle sannihito niśceyaḥ, bhasmakumbhābhyām ivānalakulālau | tato yathā kulālapūrvo'yaṃ ghaṭo ghaṭatvādityupanyāse'pyutpattikāladeśasannihitavyāpāraḥ kulālo niścīyate, ghaṭaśca heturvastutaḥ, tathā puruṣe'pi sādhye vastveva heturna kāryatvadharmaḥ, tathā sati puruṣavyāptāt kāryād vilakṣaṇaṃ kṣīṇīdharādikāryāmati vadatā sādhanavaisadṛśyamudbhāvitam, na dharmivesadṛśyam | tadā hi tadudayadeśakālameva dharmi, na ca kalasādikāladeśāt kailāsādikāladeśavaisadṛśyaṃ kaścid vaktumupakrānto yena dharmivaisadṛśyodbhāvanaṃ bhavet |
[254,3]
tasmād dahanarūpamātrād dahanānumānavat sādhanavaisadṛśyodbhāvanametadasiddhim avyāptiṃ vā darśayituṃ dharmiṇa iti tu viplavaḥ pareṣām | ayamevārtho yādṛk kāryatvaṃ devakulādau puruṣavyāptaṃ pratītam, na tādṛg yugandharādāvityanayā diśopadiśyate |
yajjātīyaṃ devakulādi puruṣavyāptaṃ na tajjātīyaṃ yugandharādītyarthaḥ | atyantavejātyācca kāryaśabdamātrasāmyamucyate na punarakāryavyāvṛtteḥ kvacit nyūnabhāvaḥ | vyāptau tu kāryatvāderanantarbhāvaṃ brūmaḥ | ataeva tanmātreṇa sāmyaṃ nopayogi, mūrtatvādineva dahanānumāne |
[255,1]
