mañjaryāstu paryanuyogo'sthānapatitaḥ | ghaṭādijātireva puruṣavyāptā siddheti vadatānyatra saṃśayamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt | kulālādimanuṣyakṛtabuddhiśca kṛtabuddhiruktā |
tadabhāvaśca jātibhede uttarīkṛtaḥ | sa cobhayasiddhatayā na visarjanānyavakāśayati |
na cātyantikajātibhedamantareṇopapadyata iti niveditam |
[255,2]
evaṃ vācaspaterapi viśeṣagaveṣaṇaṃ kṛtabuddhivaidhuryasyābhidheyaprayojanayoraparijñānaprayuktamiti veditavyam | yadi hi kṛtabuddhirnāstīti prakṛtasādhyabuddhirnāstīti vivakṣitam, tadā pratītikalahe'muṣmin kuto viśeṣādanyatra sā bhavati parvatādau tadabhāvānneti cintyate | yadā tu kṛtabuddhirnāstīti samānaśilpikṛtabuddhirnāstītyabhidheyam, tatra ca na vivādaḥ | prayojanaṃ ca kumbhādibhyo'mbhodharāderatyantavaijātyakhyāpanam |
tadapyaśakyaparihāram | tato gṛhītavyāptikebhyo'tyantavilakṣaṇāt kathaṃ prakṛtasādhyabuddhirityabhipretam ? tadā plavata eva sakalamevaṃvidham | utpattimanmātre ca vyāptinirasatāt hantotpattimadityādyuttaraṃ kāladaṇḍakhaṇḍitameva | tena ghaṭe dṛṣṭavyāptikasya ghaṭasajātīyameva buddhimatpūrvakam | yadā tu prāsādādāvapi vyāptigrahastadā tajjāterapi tatpūrvakatvasiddhirityapyuktam |
[255,3]
yaccātha yajjātīyamityāśaṅkya, kiṃ kāryajātīyam ? tathā na dṛṣṭamityuttaram, tadapi svābhāvikavikalpāvabhāsinaḥ sāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa vyāptigrahaṇayogyatāsamarthanāt kadarthitam | tasmād yadapi aupādhikavikalpapratibhāsināpi rūpeṇa tajjātīyavyavahāro duṣpariharaḥ, vyāptigrahaṇe tu pratikṣiptatvānmahān viśeṣa iti |
[255,4]
ata eva vittokavikalpā api na kiñcit | tathā hi, yadyasmadabhiprāyapraśnaḥ, tadā viśiṣṭaiva kāryajātirdevakulakalasādilakṣaṇā buddhimadvyāptā yaddṛṣṭerhi parokṣakriyasyāpyanubhūtasajātīyaśilpyanumānam, sā na siddhā sindhubhūdharādau | kāryatvamātraṃ tu na vyāptamityuccaistarāṃ tanvanta evāsmahe | tatra kimebhirvikalpairiti cintaya | yadviśeṣād viśiṣṭā kāryajātiḥ sa viśeṣaḥ kimanirūpitarūpa evetyapi pāpīyaḥ, pratyakṣasiddhānāṃ kāryajātīnāṃ parasparavaisadṛśyasyāpahnotumaśakyatvāt | vyāptistu viśiṣṭāyāṃ jātau bhavatu kāryamātre vetyatra paramāpātato vimantumarhati | kathamanyathā svayamapi vastutvasyāgnikāryatvāsaṃjananaṃ vyabhicāramālambya parihṛtam ? vyabhicārabuddhīnāṃ niyatajātiviṣayatve vivādābhāvādityāvirbhāvitameva | tasmādākārārthakriyāsāmarthyādivedanāt citrākāre jagati niyatamīśvaraprasādādevālaukikamekākāramālokitamasyetyupekṣaiva jyāyasī |
[256,1]
yadapi prācīnamupādānodāharaṇamasya kāryamātre vyāptisamīhayā, tadapi naupayikam, tatrāpi pratyakṣavyāpārasyāśakyasādhanatvāt, naisargikavikalpaviṣayatvāt, upādānasya dṛśyādṛśyasvabhāvatvācca | tat kimidānīmupādānena kāryarāśervyāptireva nāsti ? āhosvit pramāṇāntaragamyā bhavatviti cet ? ubhayatra saṃśayaḥ, sato'pi vyabhicārasya viparyayabādhakānumānasya vānullekhasaṃbhavādidānīmekāntahetorabhāvāt |
tadayaṃ sopādānaṃ sarvotpattiriti sarvatantrasiddhānto'virodhādanuvṛttaḥ, yāvacca kāryam ālokayāmastāvadupādānavadevetyavigānena vyavahāro'pi | na ca kāryaparyantabodhaḥ pṛthagjanasyeti tanīyasāpi viparītāṃśena saṃśayo durvāraḥ | buddheśca buddhirupādānaṃ niścitā iti vijñānasya vijñānānyānupādānācca sidhyatīti na virudhyate, tato yadi siddhāntādapi tadvyāptivyavasāyo na kācit kṣatiḥ | pratyakṣāt tu mā bhūt, kevalamatra pakṣe'cetanopādānatvaheturekadeśasiddhaḥ śaṅkyeteti vyavasthā | sā cāyātaiva, kiṃ kriyatām ? viparyayabādhakapramāṇalābhe tu sāpi na syāt | kevalaṃ pratyakṣeṇa kṛtsnakāryavyāptivāde'nudāharaṇamevedam | ataḥ pratyakṣasya jātiviśeṣe vyāpāraniyamaprasādhanād viśeṣahetvabhāvādityādyapi dhvastam ?
[256,2]
yatpunaraparasya viparyayabādhakapramāṇopanyāsapauruṣam, tatrāpi prathamadvitayaṃ tāvad bādhakaṃ dhūmasyeva siddhāyāmeva tadutpattau tatsādhakapratyakṣānupalambhasya viśiṣṭajātyadhikāreṇa pravṛttisādhanād viśiṣṭameva ghaṭādikāryaṃ prati śakyam | evaṃ ca yadi buddhimantamantareṇa jāyeta sakṛdapi tato na bhavet, aniyatahetutve vāhetutvamiti na kāryamātraṃ prati, tasya puruṣādutpattiprasādhanābhāvāt | tataśca tat kāryaṃ yat puruṣapūrvam ityapi niravakāśam ||
[256,3]
nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ, svakāraṇāyattasannidheradṛṣṭapariṇāmasahakāriṇaḥ kāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasya satatamabhāve'pi kāryāṇāṃ kādācitkatopapatteḥ, yadapekṣayā nityaśakterapi īśvarasya śaśvanna karaṇatvam | ekāvasthāniyame hi kāraṇāntarāṇāṃ pravṛttinivṛttisādhanīcchā prārthyeta | sa ca nāsti, bījasyocchūnataratamādibhāvavat pariṇāmaparamparāparicayasya teṣāmapahnotumaśakyatvāt | astu vā ekāvasthāniyama īśvarasya icchāyā api nityatvāt tadavasthaḥ kāryāvirāmaḥ, anitye tu yadapekṣo'syāḥ kadācid bhāvaḥ, tadapekṣayā kāryagrāmasya yadi syāt kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? kumbhādikāryakrame'pi tarhi kiṃ puruṣecchayā, yadapekṣo'syāḥ kramaḥ, tadapekṣa eva kumbhāderapyastīti vaktuṃ śakteḥ ?
tadayuktam, pramāṇena dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya hetorapohitumaśakyatvāt | prastute tu pramāṇābhāvāt kāryakādācitkatāmātramāśritaṃ tadanyathāpyupapatsyata iti kutaḥ puruṣāpattiniyamaḥ kāryasya ?
[257,1]
atha kumbhādeḥ kadācidbhāvaḥ puruṣādhīno dṛṣṭa iti kāryāntarasyāpi tatheti cet ? evaṃ tarhi tadeva darśanādarśanamātraṃ vyāptisādhanamāyātam, kimatra viparyayabādhakopanyāsaśauṭīryeṇeti tṛtīyamapi nirastam ||
[257,2]
yaccocyate, kāraṇasannidherdhīdhanādhīno niścita iti, tatrāpi tathā darśanamātrāśraye etadeva vācyam | viparyayabādhakaṃ ca na kiñciduktam | pratyakṣānupalambhaśaraṇīkaraṇe ca vātopaghātādimilajjambālabījādisāmagryā anaikāntikatvādi sarvamākṣepaparihārasametaṃ kāryabadavagantavyaṃ sāmagrīviśeṣa eva vyāptiyogya ityetatparyantam | tanna kāraṇasāmagryāḥ puruṣeṇa vyāptisiddhiḥ, yato vipakṣe vyāpakānupalambhādasambhava iti caturthamapi kadarthitam ||
[257,3]
tāvataiva vācaspaterapi hṛdayaśūnyaḥ pralāpo'pahastitaḥ | yathā hi vitatānāṃ tāvadajananabījamuktamavasthāviśeṣābhāvo nāma | yadyapi daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ puruṣādeva milanamupalabdhaṃ tatprayatnasacivānāṃ ca kāryārambhaḥ, tathāpi sarvatra sarvadā vā tathaiveti niyamayituḥ pramāṇasyābhāvāt kāryotpādavyāpakasyāpi kāraṇasamavadhānasya buddhimadadhīnatvena vyāptyasiddhestadavastho doṣaḥ | yathā ca kāraṇāntaradaśāviśeṣāśrayeṇaiva kāryāṇāṃ kadācid bhāvastathā prakṛtaviśeṣo'pīti pañcamaṃ ca pañcatāmañcitam ||
[257,4]
kāraṇamātrāpattisādhanaṃ punaretaditi darśitaṃ śāstre ||
[257,5]
etenaiva śaṅkaroktamapi nāpi kaścid viśeṣa ityādi kāvyaracanāmātramāpāditam, pratibandhasādhakapramāṇaparyādānāt | yadyapi ca nirabhiprāyavyāpāratvena prāsādādihetubhyo bhūbhūdharādihetūnāṃ na viśeṣastathāpi prayatnavadapekṣānapekṣābhyāṃ yadi syāt ko doṣaḥ ? yathā pārthivatvāviśeṣe'pi lohalekhyatvālohalekhyatve | avaśyaṃ ca nirabhiprāyatvāviśeṣe'pi viśeṣa eṣāmeṣitavyaḥ śakteḥ, kathamanyathā kāryavaijātyamātyantikam ?
tadasau śaktiḥ prayatnavadapekṣāvaimukhyamapi yadi kṣameta kā kṣatiḥ ? kiṃ ca karturapi karādivyāpāramantareṇa samīhāmātrāt na mūrtakāryasiddhirupalabdhā, tamativartamānānāṃ bhūdharādīnāṃ kā gaṇanā samīhāmātre ?
[258,1]
karādayo'pi samīhayā pravartthanta iti cet ? samīhāpi sanniveśini śayādivyāpāravirahe na kiñcitkarītyuktam | tato yayā śaktyā karādivyāpārapāravaśyamapāsya mahīdharādihetavo nirabhiprāyatve satyapi na kāryakarmaṇi pratihanyante, tayā samīhāmapi nātikrameyuriti ka evaṃ śraddadhīta ? na hi dhūmodayakāle ucchaladbahalarūpaṃ vastu vahnīndhanajanyatayā sambhāvitamekābhāvaniścaye niścīyamānamanyābhāve'pi na bhāvaśaṅkāyāṃ niveśayati, tādṛgetadapi ||
[258,2]
śarīrasvīkāre tu prādeśikakāryānityānekāsarvajñatvāt sādhu sādhitaḥ sudhībhirīśvaraḥ | etenaiva vā vyabhicāraḥ kāryatvādeḥ | na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāmityādivacanād darśanādarśanamātrādanyamupāyamasya vyāptisādhanāya spṛśati, tacca kṛtottaram | yadi ca darśanādarśanameva śaraṇam, tadā yathā samīhāvataḥ kāryakriyā dṛṣṭeti kārye sati samīhāvato'numānamiṣṭam, tathā karādimata eva mūrtakriyā dṛṣṭeti karādivyāpārānupapattau puruṣasyākriyaiva kasmāt na niścīyate ? na khalu kāryahetuvyāpakānupalambhayoḥ prāmāṇye kaścid viśeṣaḥ | yadi tu darśanādarśanamātramanāsthāya pramāṇāntaramekaniyataṃ syāt, syādekasādhyabuddhiḥ, tadabhāve tu pratibandha eva tayoḥ parasparam, na bādhā tulyakakṣatvāditi prakaraṇasamaḥ parābhiprāyāt |
[258,3]
prayogaḥ, yo na svāṅgavyāpāravān nāsau mūrtanirvartanasamartho dṛṣṭaḥ, yathā kulāla eva saṃhṛtakarādivyāpāradaśāyām | nāsti ca svāṅgavyāpāraḥ prakṛte puṃsīti vyāpakānupalabdhiḥ | nāśrayāsiddhiḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgādhyāyanyāyeneti vastutastarhi dūṣaṇāntarameva yuktaṃ, kaḥ pratihetoravakāśa iti cet — na, bhūyodarśanasya vyāptisiddhāvanaṅgatvapratipādanārthamasyopanyāsāt | yadi bhūyodarśanamupāyaḥ tadaivamapi syādityukteriti vyāptigrahaprakārāṇām ayogādanekānta iti sthitam |
[258,4]
astu vā vyāptigrahaḥ kathañcit, tathāpi neśvarasiddhipratyāśā phalavatī, buddhimataḥ sādhyasyaikatvaniyamaniścayābhāvāt | ekatve hi tasya siddhe nityavibhusarvajñatvasiddhirīśvaravyavahāramāropayet | yadā tu bhinnadeśakālakalitaṃ kāryajātamanekena saṃkhyātikrāntena kartrā kṛtaṃ sambhāvyeta, na tadā vibhutvanityatve, svasvaviṣayopādānādimātravedanasiddhau ca kva sarvajñatvam ?
[259,1]
atha bahūnāṃ vyāhatamanasāṃ vyāpāre kāryasyānutpattirupanyasya vilopādiprasaṅgaśca syāditi cet ? pratyekaṃ vaibhavādiguṇayogādīśvarāṇāṃ vyāpāre syādapīyamāśaṅkā, adya punareko'pi tādṛṅ na sidhyatītyucyate | arvācīnaśaktayaśca bhūyāṃsa ekamanekaṃ ca kāryam ārabhya niṣpādayanto dṛśyanta eva | nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenaikena bhāvyam, balīyasā vā, sūtradhāravat, senānīvad vā | atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvṛttitvāditi cet — na, tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt, svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcidekasattvādidhaṭanādarśanāt | tatrāpi kaścideva prathamaḥ prayojaka ityapi nāsti, anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyā anivāraṇāt, nīcasyāpi prayojakatvasambhavāt |
[259,2]
tasmād bhramaramadhumakṣikāvalmīkajantuvat kṣudraprāṇibhirapyekaikamainākādikaraṇasambhāvanāyāṃ kā vārtā viśvasyaikena kriyāyāḥ ? tatrādṛṣṭajanmānastāvat tāvataiva kṛtārthīkṛtacetanānumitayaḥ kṣitidharādayaḥ | te ca kṣudrajantava upādānamatikṣudraṃ pṛthivyādidravyamupakaraṇaṃ sukhādisampradānamātmānaṃ sthitisukhādi ca prayojanaṃ jānanta eva valmīkajantuvat pravarteran | siddhe ca nāvaśyamadhiṣṭhāyakā dṛśyeran, vicitraśaktikarmākṣepāt svabhāvaviprakarṣād vā | ye'pi dṛṣṭajanmāno vṛkṣādayaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ, tatra cintaiva nāsti | adṛṣṭapuruṣavyāpārāstu ye bindhyayugandharādiparisaradbhāvāste'pi piśācādiprakārairadhiṣṭhātṛbhirasaṃkhyaiḥ kartṛmanta iti kaḥ sarvavedī bhavatu ? deśakālayośca bhinnā evepri kva vibhutvanityatve ? na caivaṃ śaṅkāyā bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti vastubalapravṛttamanumānam |
[259,3]
nanu caivaṃ tāvad bhavadbhirapi na svīkṛtameva | etāvaccātikaṣṭataraṃ kalpayato varam īśvarakalpanaiva lāghavāditi cet ? satyam, yadi kalpanāmātretaranyāsaḥ, tadā bhavadupanyāsameva puraskariṣyāmaḥ | yāvat punaranumānavyājaṃ na varjayasi, tāvadavaśyamasmākaṃ dṛḍhanirūpaṇābhiyogaḥ | atha kṣudrairasaṃkhyairnirmitā narmadādaya iti dunoti cetaścet ?
ekenāśarīreṇa nirmitā iti suṣṭhutarām | tasmāt pramāṇameva sarvato balavad yathā sthāpayati tathārthasthitiḥ | ataeva tad dṛḍhaṃ nirūpyate | na ca kṣudreṣvanurodhaḥ kaścit |
kṣudrairakṣudrairadṛśyaiḥ samānaśaktibhiradhikaśaktibhiḥ svatantraiḥ pradhānasammataikaikajantusanāthāparimitayūthairvā sthūlāṇukaikānekasvakāryabhāgopādānādimātravedibhiḥ ṣaḍgatiparyāpannaiḥ kṛto bhavatu bhuvanasanniveśaḥ, eka eva tu kartā'sya mā bhūt |
[260,1]
nāpi bauddhaistathānupagamāt tato hetuvyāvṛttiḥ, ekato'pi vyāvṛttiprasaṅgāt |
na ca vastubalapravṛtte'numāne paropagamāpekṣā | upagamamātrasya tyāgenāvirodhāt | tadevaṃ buddhimanmātre sādhye upādānādyabhijñatālakṣaṇaviśeṣanāntarīyakatayā sākṣādupādānādyabhijñakartṛsādhanād vābhimatasiddhirnaikāntikī, sarvakāryakriyāyā ekakartṛtvāsiddheḥ |
upādānādyabhijñamātrasādhane ca vaiphalyam, bhāratādikathāvat | tataḥ sādhanāntarābhāvādasmādeva sarvajñādiguṇavataḥ siddhiriṣṭeti tadapekṣayaiva dūṣaṇamabhidhānīyamanekāntalakṣaṇamiti sthitam |
[260,2]
ato yāvatīmarthagatimityādi durlaṅghyam | sādhyasāmānyapratibandhākṛṣṭatve'pi viśeṣasya siddhiḥ sādhanādhīnaiva, tadekaparatayā sādhanopanyāsādanyasādhanābhāvācca |
bauddhasyāpi hi nairātmyasiddhiḥ sādhanādhīnaiva | yadi hi nairātmyatyāge'pi kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ caritārthaṃ bhavet, tadā kiṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhane nairātmyasiddhiḥ syāt ? bhavatastu sārvajñyādisiddhimuddhūyānyathāpyupādānādyabhijñānalakṣaṇo viśeṣa upapāditaḥ | ataeva nātmopanyāsapūrvako'nvayo dṛṣṭānte pradarśyata iti anupayuktam | sākṣāt tadanvayadarśane api tannāntarīyakatvaṃ sādhyasāmānyasya darśayitavyameva | taccaikatvena sakalakriyādhārasya vyāpterabhāvādaśakyam |
[260,3]
etenaiva vācaspatyo'pi sārvajñyasādhanābhinayaḥ prativyūḍhaḥ | siddhe tu sarvajñe kartari karturekatvanirūpaṇaśramo'smākamanupayogītyuparamyate | yadapyayaṃ vyatirekiprayogamāha, tadapyekatvāniścayādeva dūṣitam, anityāsarvaviṣayabuddhitve'pyupādānādivedanasambhavasyopapāditatvāt |
[260,4]
vittokasamādhāne tu dhūmāddharādharāyogavyavacchedavat agneḥ pañcavarṇaśikhākalāpatāyā apyanumānaprasaṅgaḥ | nātra sāmarthyamiti cet ? tatrāpi pakṣāyogavyavaccheda eva sāmarthyāt | pṛthvībhṛti prayatnavataḥ siddhāvapyekatvāniścayāt kva sarvavedanasiddhiḥ ?
[260,5]
nanu dvyaṇukasyāpi kāryatvāt kartā tadupādānaparamāṇudarśī niyamena eṣitavyaḥ | na ca māṃsacakṣuṣastathā bhavitumarhanti | anyathā kimasmadābhiraparāddhaṃ yena tathā na bhavāmaḥ ? tadavaśyaṃ kartātīndriyadarśī svīkriyamāṇo neśvarādanyo yuktaḥ | tadapi yatkiñcit | na hi māṃsacakṣuṣṭve'pi sarvasādhāraṇaṃ karaṇasāmarthyam, asmadatyantamapakṛṣṭānāmapi gṛdhrādīnāmindriyapāṭavātiśayadarśanāt | kṣodiṣṭhānāmeva ca keṣāñcit paramāṇudarśanamapi syāt karmaśaktiviśeṣāt, yathā pipīlikānāmasmadagocaragandhāṇugrahaṇam | na ca tanmātrasūkṣmamīkṣamāṇairdeśakālaviprakṛṣṭasyāpi sūkṣmāntarasya grahaṇam, sakalasthūlasya vā ?
tanna tāvataiveśvarasiddhipratyāśā |
[261,1]
evaṃ tarhi bhavatu paramāṇordarśanasambhāvanā sakalakṣetrajñatatsamavetadharmādharmāśayaviśeṣāṇāṃ tu katham ? na kathañcit | na hi kāryakriyā kṣetrajñasvarūpādiparijñānenāpi vyāptā kulāladṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭā, kiṃ tu sampradānopakaraṇavedanadvāreṇa tadākṛṣṭiriṣyate | sā cāśakyā, sāmarthyānupapatteḥ, uktakrameṇāpi tanmātravedanasya caritārthatvāt | karmaṇi svasyābhipreyamāṇatvena sampradānatāyā durvāratvāt; yathā svasmai mandiraṃ karotīti | anyathā tenaiva vyabhicāraprasaṅgaḥ sampradānajñānāpekṣāyāḥ |
[261,2]
anumīyamānastatrāparaḥ sampradānavedī bhaviṣyatīti cet — na, vyabhicāradarśanena kartuḥ sampradānajñānanāntarīyakatvāsiddheranumānavārtāvirahāt | na cānumīyamānāpekṣayā tasyākartṛtvam | evaṃ hi kulālasyāpyakartṛtvaprasaṅge vyāptigrahavirahāt tadavastho'numānānudayaḥ | tasmād yad yadavaśyaṃ sampradānajñānāpekṣaṃ kartṛtve, svātmāpi sampradānameṣitavyaḥ |
na ca paramapi sampradānaṃ vyavahāraprasiddhamuddhūya kṣetrajñarūpamasau jñātumīśaḥ karmāśayabhedārthopakaraṇaśabdasaṃgṛhītānapi | tato yathā kulālastānavidvān daṇḍacakrādivedanenaivopakaraṇajñaḥ, tathānumīyamānā api jantavaḥ svakīyakaramukhādijñānenāpyante bhaviṣyanti |
[261,3]
tat kutastyametat kṣetrajñarūpatadīyadharmādharmāśayabhedaparijñānam ? athāśarīrasya kva svāṅgavyāpārasaṅgatiḥ ? aśarīrasya siddhisaṅgatirapi kīdṛśī ? ekatve hi siddhe śarīrī prādeśiko na sarvakarmaṇi samartha iti sāmarthyādaśarīrisiddhipratyāśā, ekatvaṃ ca duḥsādhamityuktam | na cāśarīratve'pi daṇḍacakrakaramukhādyupakaraṇānupapatteḥ pāriśeṣyāt karmāśayabhedajñānenaivopakaraṇajñānaniṣṭheti sauṣṭhavāya | dikkālasamavāyāderapyupakaraṇasaṃgṛhītasya jñānena tajjñatāmātrasya kṛtārthatvāt |
[261,4]
kaḥ punarasau viśeṣo yatastadavasthasya digādijñānenaivopakaraṇajñatā ? na dharmādharmādijñāneneti | ubhayajñānenaiva bhavatviti cet ? tadayuktam | nahi yāvadupakaraṇaṃ tāvat kartrāvaśyaṃ jñeyamiti dṛṣṭam | na ca digādijñānenaivopakaraṇavittistadavasthasyeti niścayaṃ brūmo yato viśeṣaparyanuyogaḥ, kiṃ tūpakaraṇāntarasambhavānna pāriśeṣyaviśrāntiḥ atretyucyate | tato yathā parāparakartṛṣu daṇḍacakrāditurīvemādyupakaraṇavirahaparamparāyām anyānyairupakaraṇairdharmādibāhyairupakaraṇajñatāsthitirupalabdhā, tathā kimadyāpyastu ? uta dharmādīnādāyaiveti sandeha eva | yadi punaranyadupakaraṇaṃ na syāt pāriśeṣyavyākhyānaṃ śobheta | abhyudayaniḥśreyasamārgādisandehe ca kiṃ tādṛśā tena kartavyamīśvarābhidhānena dhanavirahiṇeva ?
[262,1]
tasmādaśarīritve'pi na dharmādijñānākṛṣṭiḥ, kiṃ punastadasiddhau ? mā bhūdupakaraṇatayā dharmādervedayitā niyamena kāryatayā bhaviṣyati, yataḥ kartā kāryarūpādivedakaḥ sa ceśvara ityapi niḥsāram | dānahiṃsādikaṃ hi kurvantastad vedayanta eva svarūpamātreṇa, na tāvatā ta eveśvarāḥ | na cānyaḥ kārtsnyena tadvedī siddhaḥ | dharmādharmatvena tu niścayaḥ tatkāriṇo'pi nāvaśmbhāvī kumbhakāravat | tatkāriṇāṃ tarhi tattvena niścayābhāvāt tattvaniścayaḥ kāryatvāt kartāramīśvarameva sannidhāpayedityapi nāsti | dharmādharmatvaniścayo'pi hi samīcīnaḥ sandigdhasattāka eva vartate | kathaṃ tataḥ pratyāśā ? anirastaviparyayāśaṅkasaṅkalpasvabhāvastu bhūyasāmāgamadvāreṇa | devajātismarādisvīkārācca teṣām apyasti leśena samyakkarmaphalasambandhabodhaḥ | na ca tāvataivaiśvaryaparyāptiriti |
[262,2]
tadevamīśvarāsiddheḥ sakalajanmināṃ śubhāśubhakarmāṇi nopakaraṇam, kiṃ tu kāraṇānyeva lokavaicitryasyeti dhīmatāmupādeyaḥ prathamaślokārtha iti ||
{7.3}
<vārtikasaptaślokī>
[263,1]
sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu | iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā || 12 ||
[263,2]
siddhaṃ yādṛgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat | sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate || 13 ||
[263,3]
vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ | na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśane || 14 ||
[263,4]
anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit | ghaṭādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ || 15 ||
[263,5]
sādhyenānugamāt kārye sāmānyenāpi sādhane | sambandhibhedād bhedoktidoṣaḥ kāryasamo mataḥ || 16 ||
[263,6]
jātyantare prasiddhasya śabdasāmānyadarśanāt | na yuktaṃ sādhanaṃ gotvād vāgādīnāṃ viṣāṇavat || 17 ||
[263,7]
vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā | tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarvaṃ sarvasya sidhyati || 18 ||
<īśvaravādādhikāre vārtikasaptaślokīvyākhyānam>
{7.4.1}
<prathamaḥ khaṇḍaḥ>
[265,1]
karmanirmitavaicitryamanīśaṃ yo jagajjagau | praṇamāmi pramāṇena tamavyāhataśāsanam ||
[265,2]
nityapramāṇapratiṣedhasiddhau yadapramāṇatvamanityabhāve | vibhāvayannāha kṛtī tadaṃśe vimohadaṃśāpaha eṣa mārgaḥ ||
[265,3]
svayaṃ nirasyāpi parasya sādhanānyasaṅgatau vārtikakārakīrtane | na nirvṛtiścet punarasya varṇanād varaṃ hi tadvarṇanayaiva vikramaḥ ||
[265,4]
yad yat kāryaṃ tat tad buddhimatpūrvakam, yathā ghaṭaḥ | kāryaṃ ca mahīmahīdharādi |
yad vā, yad yat na buddhimatpūrvakaṃ tat tanna kāryam, yathā ākāśam | kāryaṃ ca tarugirisāgarādītyarthataḥ kāryahetuḥ | evamacetanopādānatvam, arthakriyākāritvam, svārambhakāvayavasanniveśanāviśeṣavattvam, sthitvā sthitvā kāryakarmāṇi, pravṛttidharmakatvaṃ ca prayojyamiti kathamucyate,
[265,5]
anitye'pyapramāṇateti ?
[265,6]
etacca nityānityayoḥ sādhāraṇameva sādhanam | anityatāprakramaṇe tu parasya pramāṇaparyeṣaṇā pravarteta | tadupanyāsanidānatvamātreṇānityaśabdānuvādaḥ | na punaḥ asāvanitya eva bhagavān asmābhiriṣyate | tathā hi —
[265,7]
eko vibhuḥ sarvavidekabuddhisamāśrayaḥ śāśvata īśvarākhyaḥ | pramāṇamiṣṭo jagato vidhātā svargāpavargārthibhirarthanīyaḥ ||
[265,8]
atrocyate | kimebhireva hetubhirupadiṣṭaguṇagaṇāgārapuruṣātiśayasādhanamanoratho'tha hetvantarabalāt ? tatra na tāvadādyaḥ pakṣaḥ | tathā hi yat sādhanaṃ yāvatīmarthagatiṃ vyāpnoti tatastāvatyeva sidhyati nārthāntaram | na hi yāvānicchayā vyāpto'rthaḥ, tāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam | api tu yāvati pramāṇasya sāmarthyam, tāvato'rthasya tannimittā siddhiḥ | na ca kāryatvādi cetanapūrvakatvena vyāpyamānamapi tadekatvādiniyatāṃ matimutpādayituṃ śaktam, tadviśeṣaṇe vyāpterevāpratīteḥ, anyathā viparītarūpaniścayasyāpi prasaṅgāt | na hi dahanasāmānyena vyāptaṃ dhūmamupalabhya kaścid visphuratpañcavarṇaśikhākalāpakamanīyamanalamanumātumīśaḥ |
[266,1]
nanu tathāpi deśakālaviśeṣaviśeṣaṇamanumimīta eva pakṣadharmatābalāt, evaṃ bhūdharādāvapi buddhimadadhiṣṭhānādhīnaṃ kāryatvamupalabdhavato'bhimatasiddhiradhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyena bhaviṣyatīti cet — na, sāmarthyānupapatteḥ | yathā hyetaddeśakālena vahninā janyamānasya na taddeśakālatvamiti dhūmādyanumāne sāmarthyam, na tathā cetayiturekatvasarvajñatvādikamantareṇa tarūṇāṃ vāsaniveśādyanupapattimākalayāmaḥ | tataḥ pakṣadharmatābalāt kulālādau tadutpādanasamarthatvasiddhirapi bhavantī nābhimataṃ viśeṣamavalambitum alam |
[266,2]
nanu yadi bhūdharādinirmāṇasamarthaḥ siddhaḥ, kimaparaṃ prārthyate ? tat kimidānīm apariniṣṭhitavācyarūpeṇa vācakamātreṇa parituṣṭiḥ ? na hyevamabhimataprastutavastusiddhiḥ |
utpādanavyāpāro hi notpitsukāryaṃ prati niyataprāgbhāvitvamātrādatiriktaḥ | sa cācetanasādhāraṇo buddherapi naikasarvagatvādiviśeṣapratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ | tato vivakṣitasādhyāpekṣayā vacanamātrasiddhyā na kiñcit |
[266,3]
kaḥ punarevaṃ pratijānāti sarvajñapūrvakāḥ parvatādaya iti ? api tu buddhimaddhetukā ityāśaṅkya sādhanenāntarupahasannāha,
[266,4]
sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu | iṣṭasiddhiriti |
[266,5]
sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇakarmanirmito hi samasto vasturāśiriṣyate | karma cācetanasvabhāvamiti sakalajñānahetavo'sidhyantaḥ sindhubhūdharādayaḥ kimaniṣṭamasmākamāvahantīti bhāvaḥ | tanmātrasādhyābhiprāye ca virodhāsiddheḥ sādhanopanyāsavaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ | tasmāt upāttaviśeṣa evānena sādhyaḥ | na ca tatra sādhanasāmarthyamityuktam | astu tarhi sādhanāntarādeva tathā siddhiriti dvitīyapakṣāpekṣayā niścayābhāvamudbhāvayannāha,
[266,6]
asiddhirveti |
[266,7]
na pramāṇāntaraṃ na vā hetvantaramasti yato'yaṃ niścayaḥ syādityarthaḥ | athavā, atīndriyatvenādhyakṣāsaṃbhavādanumānamabhyarthanīyam, tadarthaṃ ca sarvaṃ hetumadhikṛtyāha, asiddhirveti |
uktānumānato hi prativādisādhāraṇasarvakṛccetanamātre siddhe'pi viśeṣaśaṃsī na kaściddheturyo na svarūpāsiddho'nyatra sattāyāḥ, tanmātrasattātirekiṇi dharme'numānasyānavasarāt | sattā tu kṣaṇabhaṅgaśaṃsinīti nityaikatvāpekṣayā āha,
[267,1]
asiddhirbeti |
[267,2]
viparītasiddhirityarthaḥ | adharmādivat paryudāsena nitye'pi hi parasādhanavad dūṣaṇasyābhimatatvāt, prastāvamātraphalatvādanityokteḥ | vyāpitvāpekṣayā anekāntamapyāha,
[267,3]
asiddhirvā dṛṣṭānta iti |
[267,4]
vyāptitvasya paramārthato'bhāvādeva dṛṣṭānte darśanābhāvānna tena kasyacid dharmasya vyāptiḥ sidhyatītyuktaṃ bhavati | sarvabodhasya tu bhāve'pi na vyāpakatvapratītiḥ |
kuta ityāha, dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā iti, arvāgdarśanena viśeṣaniṣṭhatayā vastuto niścetumaśakyatvāt | tasmādupagītaguṇasya yathoktasādhanebhyo na sākṣānnādhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyena, nāpi sādhanāntarāt siddhiḥ iti siddhaḥ sādhakapramāṇavirahaḥ | tadviśeṣavirahiṇi tviṣṭasiddhiriti ||
[267,5]
athavā kāryatvādihetuṣūpanyasteṣu sādhyasāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena vikalpa iti siddhirasiddhirvetyāha | tatra karmavāditāprasiddhyā siddhasādhanaṃ vyaktamityasiddhinibandhanaṃ viśeṣe'nugamābhāvamādarśayannāha, asiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā iti, sādhyasyeti prakṛtam | tatra vibhutvādipratyanīkadharmaṇaḥ kulālāderavivādena siddheḥ asiddhiriṣṭasya dṛṣṭānte | atha dehātiriktabhāgasyānisargadurvibhāvasya vaibhavādikamiṣṭam iti matistathāpi saṃśayo'stu, kimidānīmatra nirbandheneti bhāvaḥ |
[267,6]
sāmānye siddhasādhyateti,
[268,1]
tasmāt sādhyavikalpātsandigdhasādhyadharmatvād vā na dṛṣṭānte sādhyena kāryatvādervyāptiriti viśeṣasyāsiddhereva, anekāntastu hetudoṣaḥ |
[268,2]
nanu dhūmānugame'pi, viśeṣe'nugamābhāvaḥ sāmānye siddhasādhyatā |
iti samāno nyāyaḥ, tadanayornaikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamanyad veti | niyataṃ cet ? na samīcīnamālocitam | tathā hi na tāvadviśeṣasiddhimabadhūya prāmāṇyamanumānamanubhavatīti siddham | sa tu viśeṣaḥ pakṣāyogavyavacchedamātralakṣaṇastadatiriktaśca saṃbhavati, yathā agniratra dhūmāt, evaṃrūpo vā ? tatra prathamāpahnave syādanumānasyāpalāpaḥ, tanmūlatvād atiriktasiddherapi | na cāsau tathānvayānusaraṇamantareṇāpi nirasituṃ śakyaḥ | pakṣadharmo hi yatpratibaddhaḥ siddhaḥ sa tena dharmiṇamaviyuktamanādarśayan svarūpasattayaiva viyujyeta, yadi paraṃ kāryahetvadhikāreṇa kālādyapekṣātiricyate | dvitīyasiddhistu tanmātrasādhyeti tajjanyaviśeṣagrahaṇanāntarīyakatayānvayānusaraṇamantareṇābhavantyapi nānumānāpalāpāya prabhavati, tadviśeṣavirahiṇā dharmeṇāyogavyavacchedasiddhyāpi tasyāścaritārthatvāt | anumānaviśeṣāpalāpastu syāt, yathā kaścit pañcavarṇaśikhaṃ śikhinamanumātumabhipretya vahniratra dhūmāditi sādhane pareṇa siddhasādhanānanugamābhyām abhiyujyamānastarhi dhūmamātrocchedeneha cānumānamapi na syāditi bruvāṇaḥ śobheta |
na tvanumānoccheda eva syāt, tadaiva dahanasāmānyānumānasya tena pramāṇīkriyamāṇatvāt | tasmāt,
[268,3]
pakṣāyogavyavacchedamātrabhedena dūṣaṇam | iṣṭasiddhyanvayābhāvāvatirikteṣu dūṣaṇam ||
[268,4]
naitau dūṣaṇatve'dūṣaṇatve vā niyatau, viṣayabhedena tu dvayī sthitiriti matam |
tadvadihāpi jaladhibhūdharādau buddhimadadhiṣṭhānāyogavyavacchedamaṅgīkṛtya vivakṣitaviśeṣāntarāpekṣayā tau dūṣaṇamudbhāvayataścitrakāntiśikhānumānoccheda eva prasañjayitumāñjasaḥ nānumānocchedaḥ | tato'numānaviśeṣāpekṣayā naikaniyataṃ prāmāṇyamaprāmāṇyaṃ veti yuktaṃ na sāmānyena |
[269,1]
nanu cādyāpi bhedo'nvayamanapekṣyaiva siddha iti bhedāntare kaḥ pratirodhaḥ ? na vai niranvayā kāpi siddhirasti | sāmānyānvaya eva tu taṃ viśeṣamanākṛṣya nāvasthātuṃ śaktaḥ | na caivaṃ viśeṣāntare'pi tasyāvaśyaṃ śaktiriti śakyam, yathopavarṇitaṃ prāk, anyathā pañcavarṇaśikhādyanumānasya durnivāratvāt | atrāsaṃbhavādikṣeyaṇamekacittatvādimati puruṣe'pi samānam | tādṛganumānodgārastatrāpi samānaḥ | tasmādatirekaviśeṣaśaṃsināvaśyamanenānvayaḥ pradarśanīya iti tadabhāvādanekānta eva | buddhimanmātrasādhane ca siddhasādhanamiti sthitam ||
[269,2]
syādetat | buddhimāniti na caitanyamātravān, api tūpādānādyabhijñaḥ prayatnavān vābhimataḥ, tena cānvayo ghaṭādikārye siddha iti bhūdharādāvapi kāryatvamupalabhyamānaṃ tādṛśameva kartāramupasthāpayatīti noktobhayadoṣaḥ | tathā hi tadupādānādyabhijña ityeva sarvajñaḥ, deśakālaniyataśca, na tadbheda upādīyamānakāryagrāmanivaṃrtanasamarthaḥ syāt iti nityatvavibhutvādayo'pi taddharmāḥ siddhā iti cet ? seyaṃ chinnamūlaviṭapasya phalabhogapratyāśā | ekatve hi siddhe siddhireṣāṃ guṇānām, anyathā bhinnadeśakālasya kāryasyānekakṛtau saṃbhāvyamānāyāṃ kasya vaibhavādayaḥ, svasvavyāpāraviṣayamātravedanācca kasya sārvajñamiti ?
[269,3]
ekatve siddhe sādhyamaśeṣamākṛṣyeta, na ca tanniścaye kiñcinnibandhanam asti | na ca kṣityādinirmāṇasamarthaḥ siddha ityekavacanaprayogapatanāt tatsiddhiḥ, pratibandhābhāvāt | pratibandhe vā siddhaikatvaḥ paraḥ kathamenamupekṣeta ? jātyapekṣayā tu syādapīti na nirbandhaḥ, aparāparadhūmapramitasyeva vahneḥ | na ca vicitre'pi citrakarmaṇi sajātīyarekhādyanugamādekakartṛsiddhivat kāryabhedeṣu guṇaviśeṣānugamāt tadekatvasiddhiḥ, tathāvidhasya kasyacidanugatasyaivānupalabdheḥ | upālabhyamānaṃ ca kāryatvavastutvādi naikatvasādhanaṃ citravadeva | guṇāntarasaṃbhave'pi hi sadṛśa eko vā karteti sandeha eva kiṃ punastadabhāve'pyekaniścayaḥ ? niyatamidamabhitticitrakarmaiva, yadabhedāniścaye sarvajñatvādi vyavasīyata iti |
[269,4]
itarastvāha eva tvamapi kāryotpattyaivāvagantavyam | katham ? bahūnāṃ vyāhatamanasāṃ svātantryeṇa parasparavirodhena mithaḥ svānukūlābhiprāyānavabodhena yugapat kāryānutpattiḥ, utpannasya vilopanādiprasaṅgaśca syāditi |
[270,1]
atra cintyate bahubhiḥ karaṇe yugapat kāryānutpattiriti bhinnakālānāṃ bhinnadeśānāṃ kāryānutpattirvivakṣitā, ekasyaiva vā mahāvayavinaḥ kṣitidharādirūpasyeti pakṣaḥ |
tatra naikatrāpyanekena karaṇe utpattivirodhaṃ paśyāmaḥ | yathā hyekasya pravṛttistathānyeṣāmapi syād valmīkavat | kiṃ prayojanamabhisandhāya teṣāṃ pravṛttiriti cet — na, vicitravṛttitvānmanasāṃ pravṛttinibandhasya viśeṣaniścāyanāśakteḥ | anyatheśvarasyaiva kimabhipretyeti cintānirbandho nirvoḍhuṃ na śakyaḥ | śakyo vā anyeṣāmabhipretādibādhyatāvadhāraṇapaṭīyasām, na mṛduprakṛterīśvarasya |
[270,2]
nāpi bahūnāṃ parasparavyāhatiniyama upapādayituṃ śakyaḥ, valmīkaukasāmekārambhadarśanāt | puruṣāṇāmahamahamikayā saṃbhāvyata eva taditi cet ? sadvivekino hyekakāryārambhiṇaḥ santyapīti tathāvidhairaparairapyatipracuratarairekasya krameṇa sthavīyasaḥ karaṇe saṃbhavini ko'smākaṃ nareṣvanurodhaḥ ? nāpi yugandharāderyugapanniṣpattiḥ kenacidupalabdhā, yata ekasyaiva kasyacicchaktiḥ saṃbhāvyate | na cāhamahamikayā puruṣeṣvapi vyādhātaniyamaḥ śakyanirvāhaḥ, parasparāvyāghātena puruṣasya virodhadvayasyānupapatteḥ | tasmāt saṃbhāvanāmātrametat, na pramāṇavartma ityupanyāsamarhati, nānekenaikamainākādeḥ karaṇamiti samayamātrānusmṛtirvā |
[270,3]
nanvanekatrāpi pradhānabhūtenekena bhāvyaṃ balīyasā sūtradhāravat, senānīvad vā, atastasyaiva kartṛtvamitareṣāṃ tadanuvartitvāditi cet— na, tatrāpi niyamābhāvāt, svasvaprayojanānurodhena svatantrāṇāmapi keṣāñcidekasetvādighaṭanādarśanāt |
tatrāpi kaścideva pradhānaḥ prayojaka ityapi nāsti, anekasya tathā hṛdayotkalikāyā nivārakābhāvāt, apradhānasyāpi vā prayojakatvasaṃbhavāt | na tāvataiva prādhānyaṃ, lokavirodhāt | kiṃ ca sūtradhārasthānīyāparimitaikaikajanasanāthaiḥ sārthairaparimitaireva khaṇḍaśaḥ sthūlārambhasaṃbhave'pi kā nāma kāmasiddhiḥ ? etena valmīkajantuṣu mukhyopanyāsaḥ pratyuktaḥ |
[270,4]
api ca yathaikahṛdayānuvartibhiranekairabhinirmīyamānasya prāsādasya sukhopadhānāvayavasanniveśaviśeṣa upalabhyate, na tathā visaṃsthūlasthūlaśilājālakaliteṣu kulagiriṣvapi, yena tathaivaikapradhānabhūtapuruṣapūrvakatvameṣāmapi syāt | tasmādekaikakailāsādisampādane bādhitumaśakyo'nekavyāpāraḥ kathamaparadūrāntarānekadeśakālakaliteṣu bhāveṣu bādhyaḥ ?
[271,1]
āgamādekatvasiddhistarhi iti cet ? so'yaṃ sannipātāpannasya sarṣapai rakṣābandhavidhirabādhaka eva bauddhānadhikṛtyāgamavicāraikacaturacetasaḥ | yadi hi parīkṣāgamagrahaḥ tadāyameva parīkṣākāla iti kastadanurodho'dhunaiva ? atha parīkṣānapekṣaḥ, tadāpi tata evābhimatasamastavastusiddhirastu, kimanumānopanyāsavyasanena prayāsaikasāreṇa ? kaṣṭo hi hetuśodhanavyavasāyaḥ sūkṣmaprativedhavidhurabuddhīnām, sukarastu śāstraikadeśapāṭhenābhimatalābhaḥ |
[271,2]
yadapyayameva vādī prāmāṇyamāgamānāṃ samarthayan na hyapramāṇatve samastāśramiṇāṃ saṃvādo nāma, tasyāpramāṇatve kasyacidaprāmāṇyabodhena visaṃvādasyāpi saṃbhāvyatvāt, saṃvādaniyamasya ca pramāṇeṣveva pratyakṣādiṣūpapatteriti nāpramāṇāni ṛgyajuḥsāmāni, samastāśramiṇāṃ saṃvādijñānasādhanatvāt pratyakṣādivadityādi pañcālakaṃ paṭhati, tadapi śiṣyasamitāvevopayujyate | tathā hi saṃvādo nāma pramāṇāntarasaṅgatirarthakriyā vā syāt, na ca tadubhayamapi, sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ (ṛ. ve. 10. 90. 1) sa vetti viśvaṃ na ca tasya vettā(tula0 śvetā0 upa0 3. 19)dyāvābhūmiṃ janayan deva eka āsīt (tula0 saiva 3. 3)
ityādivākyārtheṣu svargasādhanāgniṣṭomādau vā kasyacit saṃbhavati |
[271,3]
āśramiṇastāvad yathaikasya eko vibhuḥ śāśvataḥ sraṣṭā jagato'stīti matiḥ, tathānyasyāpi | tadanurūpānuṣṭhānaṃ ceti cet ? sā punareṣāṃ matistadekāgamaprabhavā, tādṛganyaprabhavā vā, ākasmikavikalpamātrarūpā vā syāt, na tu pratyakṣānumānarūpā, anāśramiṇāmapyavakāśaprasaṅgāt, pratyakṣādeḥ puruṣāntaraiḥ anaparādhāt | āgamāśrayaṃ tu jñānamaśrutavato'nādṛtavato na syāt, bhavāntarābhyāsavāsanāvaśād vā saṃbhavet nānyasyeti yuktam | tatredaṃ svatantratayā na pramāṇam, satyasati vā vastuni saṃbhavinaḥ abhyāsāt prasūteḥ | tadāgamaprabhavatvena pramāṇāntarasaṅgatiruktā bhavati, tādṛkprabhavatvāt, tasyāpyaprāmāṇyāt | tadasiddhaṃ yadasiddhena sādhyata iti nyāyaḥ | tasmāt tādṛksamayānusmaraṇamātrametadevambhūtaḥ kaścidastīti | kiṃ ca, āśrama ityapi darśanamātraṃ vidmaḥ, tataśca samastāśramiṇāmiti viśeṣaṇāsiddhiḥ, bauddhadigambarādeḥ saṃvādāsiddheḥ |
katipayasaṃvādaśca viparītamate'pyastīti nopanyāsaḥ saphalaḥ | ataeva visaṃvādasyātyantanivṛttirasiddhā, yataḥ prāmāṇyamavatiṣṭheta | abhimatamāśramiṇāṃ tvanādikālapravṛttasamānasaṃmohasāmarthyādapi syāditi yatkiñcidetat |
[272,1]
tasmādekatrāpi mandarādāvaparimitapuruṣavyāpāraviṣayabhāgopādānādivedināṃ prayatnavatāṃ katamaḥ sarvavedī ? bhinnadeśakālaiśca tādṛśāṃ karaṇe kuto nityavibhutvādayaḥ ?
na cādṛṣṭabhāgajñānāvakāśaḥ, tadantareṇāpi kumbhakāreṇa svavyāpāraviṣayasya niṣpādanopalabdheḥ | na ca bahubhirutpāditasyāvaśyaṃ vilopanādiprasaṅge saṅgatiḥ kāciditi ekatvāpāye'numṛtatvamanivāryaṃ sarvajñatvādīnāmanumatamiti | evaṃ ca sati, etadapyanibandhanameva, yadāha — teṣāṃ bahutve sarvajñatve sati sarvakartṛkatvāt taddeśakālapratiniyateṣu kāryeṣu pravṛttau yaugapadyapramāṇābhāvāditi, sarvajñānakriyayorekādhārāsiddheḥ | ataevaikanirākaraṇe bahutarādyapagamaprasaṅgo'pi na bādhakaḥ | yadi hi sarvajñāḥ sarvakartāraśca bahavaḥ siddheyurekanirākaraṇamevānupayogi syāt, bahutaraprayāsaścābhyupagato bhavati | yadā punaranekamekaikajanakaṃ valmīkajantuvajjantujātamāsajyate prakṛtaguṇāsaṃsparśi, tadā kā nāma hāniḥ ? na hi tadā ta eva, svargāpavargārthibhirarthanīyāḥ bhaveyuriti,
[272,2]
etena yo'pi manyate, bhavadīyasarvajñavadīśvaro'pyaneka eva bhaviṣyatīti, tadapi anavakāśam, sarvakriyādhikaraṇasyaikasyāpyasiddheḥ | asmākaṃ tu na sarvakriyayā sarvabodhasiddhiḥ, kiṃ tvabhyāsāt | sa ca sakalasākṣātkartavyākāravikalpasaṃbhavāt saṃbhavānumānamanvetīti tādṛksārvajñyasiddhiryathaikasya tathānyasyāpi syādiṣyate vā ityadoṣaḥ |
[272,3]
abhyāsādeva tarhi sarvanirmāṇamapi bhaviṣyatīti cet — na, aśakyatvāt | tathā hi, sthāvarajīvajananaṃ jaṅgamāpattirvā nābhyāsaphalam | pariśiṣṭapratikṛtinirmāṇakalpanāyāmapi kaścidevamapi syāditi syāt | na tu idameva paridṛśyamānaṃ bhavatu vanādikaṃ na tatheti niścayaḥ, viśeṣoddeśena saṃbhavānumānasyāpravṛtteḥ | tatrāpi durlabhabāhyopakaraṇasaṃbhavātiśayaparādhīno na cittamātraparāvṛttivat sukarastadabhyāsa iti adhyavasāyaḥ |
[273,1]
prabhāvātiśayasahāyāpekṣāyāṃ kiṃ śilpena ? na tadantareṇa tasya śaktiriti apramāṇakam, tathaivānyatra darśanāditi cet — na, dṛṣṭakrameṇa garbhasthaśarīrādinirmāṇaprāpteḥ | tadavaśyaṃ prabhāvetaraḥ | na ca tādṛkprabhāvādhigataye mārgasya kaścinniścayaḥ | astu vā vyāpiśilpasiddhirādiśabdasaṃgrāhyaścābhyāsaḥ | tathāpyāha, sanniveśādiṣu hetuṣu iṣṭasyākartṛtvasya siddhirasiddhirvā, asiddhireva, upayogābhāvāt |
[273,2]
na hi narakādinā tāvat kaścidupayogaḥ saṃvittyānuṣṭhātuḥ sukhopakaraṇamātrasṛṣṭāvapi nārthaḥ | śrameṇa svaśreyasaḥ saṃbhave hi tānyanyathā bhavanti, bhūtāni vā sukham ādhāsyanti | yadi paraṃ tanmārgamaviduṣāṃ tadupadeśa evānugrahakaraḥ, atastadarthaṃ mārgasākṣātkaraṇābhyāsa eva śreyāniti vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyābhyāṃ nābhyāsaḥ | tarhi pratiparamāṇu jñānābhyāse'pi kathaṃ tadvad vā sarvakaraṇe'pi na kṣatirityāha sarvasarvavidi, dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā iti, upayuktasarvajñapakṣasya mukhyatayā vakṣyamāṇatvāt | athavā vaiyarthyānadhyavasāyayostatra saṃśayo nābhāvaniścaya ityarthaḥ | uddeśaścānyatropadarśanamiti na pareṇa saha sāmyam |
tataḥ prakṛtahetubhyaḥ prayatnavatāṃ siddhāvapi na kṣatiriti |
[273,3]
nanu prayatnavatā jantujātena janitā gandhamādanādaya iti bhavatāmaniṣṭameva, tataḥ prakārāntarābhāvenānekato nivartamānaḥ prayatnavāneka eva sakalakāryakartā sidhyan sarvajñatvādikamapi pratyujjīvayatīti cet ? naitadasti, vastupratibandhānupapattericchāyāḥ, tatkṛtāyā anekato nivṛtterasādhanatvāt | yadi ca kathañcidasau na svīkurute, svīkārayituṃ tarhi caraṇamardanādinārādhanīyaḥ prativādīti, nāyaṃ nyāyaḥ svatantrasya prasaṅgo'pi na saṅgataḥ | prasahyaikyamapāye'sya na hyanekatvamīhitam ||
viparyayaparyavasāyivyāpāratvāt tasyeti |
[273,4]
nanūbhayathāpi tāvat parasyāniṣṭameva, na hi sattvalokaḥ sakalo'pi prayatnadvāreṇa kāraṇamiṣyate, api tu cetanālakṣaṇakarmādhipatyamātreṇa, tataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakaṃ kāryatvamekamanekaṃ vā prayatnavantamantike dadhānaṃ sādhanamaniṣṭasyaiveti cet ? tat kimidānīṃ parāniṣṭamātrasiddhaye sādhanamupanyastam, kiṃ nu svasādhyasiddhaye ? tatra ca pareṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvātmana iti na kiñcit sādhanopanyāsaphalamiti vaktumāha, sthityā pravṛttyādiṣu, iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā iti | samānamidamubhayasādhanāṅgavacanatvanibandhanamānarthakyāditi bhāvaḥ | na ca para eva sādhanavādī, yato'sya dvidhāniṣṭamāpādyamānaṃ śobheta | aniṣṭamapyasya prakaraṇāpannaṃ nityaikasarvajñatve tattvameva viśvasyāpādayitumārabdhaṃ na yatkiñciditi | evaṃ tarhi sādhanopanyāse'pi kimasiddhinibandhanamiti vaktavyam |
[274,1]
yatpunaruktam, viśeṣe'nugamābhāvaḥ iti, tatra yadyapi sarvagasarvajñatvādibhiranvaye'siddhisaṃśayau yathāyogam, tathāpyekatvena mā bhūtām, tadekaprayatnavat kartṛsiddhau siddhamaśeṣaṃ sādhyam | dṛṣṭaśca kulāla eko'nekaghaṭapiṭharādikāraka ityāśaṅkya ekatve'pyanvayamāpādayannāha, dṛṣṭānte iti | asiddhiriti vartate | ayamabhiprāyaḥ | na prakṛtameva ghaṭapiṭharādikāryamekena kṛtamiti sarvasya tathābhāvaḥ | tatrānekakulālādivyāpāraḥ sphuṭamavadhāryate | tat kuta ekena yatnavatā dṛṣṭakāryāṇāmanvaya iti ? athavā kulālo nāmaikaḥ kaścidasti bhūtabhautikasaṃvittirāśirayaṃ kumbhakārādiprajñaptiviṣayaḥ, karacaraṇasamudāyo veti | vastutaḥ kenaikena karaṇaṃ kumbhāderupalambhagocara ityarthaḥ |
[274,2]
atha kimanena nirbandhena ? yādṛśa eva kaścidekavyahāragocaro dṛṣṭaḥ, tādṛśaḥ saṃhatasvabhāva evaikaḥ kartā sarvasyopādānādyabhijñaḥ sidhyan sarvajña eva sidhyati | tato guṇāntaratiraskāre'pi tāvataivopādeyatvamubhayapuruṣārthaśaṃsitirasyopapadyata iti na kācit kṣatiriti, atrāpi pakṣe tenaiva sarve'mī kāryatvādihetavo vyabhicāriṇa iti vyaktamanaikāntikatvamabhipretyāha, saṃśayo'thavā iti | sādhyasyeti śeṣaḥ | kulālavat saṃdhātamātratayā kāryatvasanniveśādibhāve'pi prayatnavatkartṛpūrvakatvasyābhāvāt, etadabhāve'pi vā tasya bhāvāt | tatrāpyanyatkārakeṣṭau vā anavasthānādapratipattiḥ |
[275,1]
nanu cācetanasvabhāvaḥ svayamutpattau paraṃ cotpādayituṃ prayatnavantamapekṣate | sa tu svayameva tathāvidhabuddhyādhāra iti kimapareṇa ? na hi jaḍā ghaṭādayaḥ prakāśamapekṣanta iti prakāśenāpyaparaḥ prakāśo'pekṣitavya ityasti niyamaḥ | tataḥ keyamanavastheti ?
[275,2]
evaṃ tarhi kulālasaṃjñita eva prayatnabān buddhīndriyādikalāpaḥ kathamaparamapekṣate ?
tasmāccetano'cetano vā kalāpaḥ svabhāvenaivāparacetanamapekṣya jāyate janayati vetyupagantavyamityanavasthaiva | atha cetanavargaścetanāntaranirapekṣa eveṣyate, tadā ghaṭādivartinaḥ kāryatvādayo'bhimatakārakādhiṣṭhāyakaviparītanāntarīyakāḥ sidhyanto na virodhadūṣaṇaparihāreṇa sthitimanubhaveyuḥ | tathāvidhādhiṣṭhānasvīkāre tu svabhāvaviprakarṣādanupalabdhāvapi tadvyāpārasaṃbhāvanāyāṃ na tadviparītadṛṣṭaikanāntarīyakatvameṣāmiti viparyayavyāpterabhāvādabhāvo viruddhavyavahārasya syāt | tadāpi yadi kāryakāraṇavyavasthānāya vyatirekacintācaturaḥ kaścinna pratyavasthānamādriyate, na cedānīṃ tadārabdhamityāstāṃ tāvat,
[275,3]
tat kimanena nirbandhena ? nirbandhe vā virodhyadhyakṣasthūladoṣāvatāraprasaṅgāt tathāpyasiddhirveti viparītasiddhiryojayiṣyata iti sāntargarvo gajanimīlitenaiva vā'vadhīrya yathaivānena sarvakāryotpattau nimittakāraṇamīśvaro gṛhītaḥ, tathainaṃ saṃbhāvya cetanasyāpi cetanāntarāpekṣāyāmanavasthānabhīrostenaivāvyabhicārānāśritya saṃśayamāha — atha prayatnavānapi kulālo na svaśarīre kiṃ tu kumbhādau, tataḥ svaśarīrasiddhaye kiṃ na paramapekṣeta ? tarhīśvarābhimato'pi parakaraṇaprayatnavān na svaśarīra eva, svātmani kāritravirodhāditi kiṃ na paramapekṣeta ? na cāpekṣate | tato yadarthakāri kāryādi vā tatpratiyatnavadadhiṣṭhitamiti tattenaiva vyabhicārīti saṃśayasiddhiḥ |
[275,4]
nanu tasya śarīrameva nāstīti kuto'nekānta eṣaḥ ? tadetat prakaraṇavismaraṇaphalam | tathā hyanvayopadarśanasamīhayā kulāle sāṃvṛtamekatvamaṅgīkṛtya tādṛksāṃvṛtaikapuruṣanirmeyatvaṃ jagato bhavataiva svīkṛtamityayamasmākamavakāśaḥ | yadi tu vāstavameva ekatvaṃ śarīrasahacāraviruddhamanurudhyate, na tarhi sāṃvṛtamekatvamupanetavyaṃ dṛṣṭānte vyāpakatvena kāryādeḥ | nāpi nāmamātrapareṇa tena vyāptā tattvatastathāsiddhipratyāśā phalavatī | na khalu dahanopacaritamāṇavakapratibaddhavacanaviśeṣādikāryamupalabhya pāramārthikaṃ kaścid dahanamanumīyate |
[276,1]
askhalantī ekapratītiḥ puruṣāvayavinīti cet ? kaḥ punariha sākṣādupacāratvam āha ? atasmistadvyavahārastu dvayoḥ samāna ityucyate | śarīratve'vayavibādhakāt ekādhyavasāyasya bhramatvamavasātavyam, sattve'pi vāvayavinaḥ śarīrāvayavī karādyavayavā buddhirityeṣa kalāpa ekaśabdābhidheyaḥ, bhūtādikalāpo vetyapāramārthikatvaṃ siddham adhiṣṭhātuḥ |
[276,2]
syādetat | puruṣa eva tatrādhiṣṭhātā, kartā vā, sa ca śarīrādibhyo labdhavyatireka eka eveti cet ?
[276,3]
saṃdṛṣṭakāraṇakalāpakṛte'pi kāryajanmanyadṛṣṭamaparaṃ parikalpyate yat | tatrāpi dṛṣṭamavadhūya tadeva tacca nānekamityanavadhirvividho vimohaḥ ||
[276,4]
adṛṣṭasya tāvad bhāva eva duravadhāraḥ sahajavaiṣamyādatrānumānasyetyuktam |
tasyāpi dṛṣṭānupalambhasacivapratyakṣasādhyaḥ kāraṇabhāvaḥ | sa ca dṛṣṭavyavacchedena tasyaiva |
anyathā karacaraṇāderapi vyāpārasaṃbhave tasyāpyanumānaprasaṅge punaḥ sa eva vyabhicāraḥ |
anyathā puruṣasyāpyanumānamanibandhanaṃ syāt | etena caitanyasantānasyaikapuruṣatvaparikalpanaṃ pratyuktam, asyāpi karacaraṇādisahakṛtasyaiva śaktipratīteḥ, kāryāt tattvata evānumānaprasaṅgo dhūmādiva sendhanaśikhinaḥ |
[276,5]
caitanyamātreṇa vyāptirgṛhyate nāpareṇāpīti cet — na, samānanyāyatayā vibhāgasya kartumaśakyatvāditi | tadayaṃ buddhiśarīrāvyatirekiṇaḥ kāraṇatāmanyayogavyavacchedenaiva vaktumarhati, yatastanmātramanumātumapratibandhena śaktuyāt, pāramārthikaikatvena ca vyāptiṃ grahītum | tathā ca sati dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭānvayavyatirekaṃ kārakasamudāyamapahāyānyadeva kāraṇaṃ kalpitamityayamaparo dhikkāraḥ | tadapi yadi kathañcidanekaṃ syād viphalaḥ sakalo yatna ityekameva parikalpanoyamityākāśakamalaparimalākṛṣṭamadhukarakolāhalaprāyamidam akhilamākalayāmaḥ |
[277,1]
tadalaṃ dehādivyatiriktopakṣepeṇa | tasmāt prayatnavataḥ karturekatvena vyāptirna mukhyā, kartṛvācyasya kulālādestattvata ekatvānupapatteḥ | sāṃvṛtāśraye ca tādṛśasyaivānumānaprasaṅgena teneva vyabhicāraḥ kāryatvāderiti saṃśayaḥ sādhyasyetyuktam |
[277,2]
nanu tathāpi tādṛśaḥ sādhyasyāsiddhau kena vyabhicāraḥ, siddhau ca vyabhicāraḥ kiṃ kariṣyati ? vyabhicārādasiddhireveti cet ? asiddhau tarhi vyabhicāro'pi nāstīti kuto'siddhiriti siddhiriti vā vyavatiṣṭhate ? kāryatvādeśca vastudharmasya vastusanneva dharmī bhavitumarhatīti na codyam, abhyupagamavirodhasyānena krameṇa pratipādayitumārabdhatvāt tattvataḥ | asti cāsau sādhyasya sādhanatrairūpyeṇa trirūpasādhanasya ca yathābhimatasādhyena, tatra sādhyasattve vipakṣavyatirekasyāsattvāt, svābhyupagamasiddhatayā pramāṇasiddhamiti sādhāraṇānaikāntikamucyate, tatrābhyupāyaḥ kāryāṅgam iti vacanāt | parābhyupagamaḥ khalu na pramāṇamiti yuktam, tadbādhanāyaiva pravṛtteḥ |
ataeva na svatantrahetāvasyāśrayaḥ | prasaṅgasya ca viparyaya eva phalam | svopagamasya tvapramāṇatve vacanoccāraṇameva na syāt | svadṛṣṭārthaprakāśanaṃ ca vacanaṃ parārthānumānāt |
na caivaṃ svadṛṣṭarūpatrayaprakāśanamanena kṛtaṃ bhavatīti tadvādino'sādhanāṅgavacanaṃ nigrahasthānamucitam | parasya tu doṣodbhāvanameveti sthitam | athavā anvayaghaṭanārthamevaikena karaṇamupanītamāśaṅkyāha, dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā (pra. vā. 1. 12)
iti | dṛṣṭānte'siddhireva tāvadekena karaṇasya | siddhāvapi vā sandeha eva kasya, yadartham upanīyate dṛṣṭāntaḥ ? sarvopasaṃhāravatyā vyāpteriti yāvat | tathā hi na dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭam ityeva yasya kasyacid vastuno vyāpyavyāpakabhāvapratītiḥ, atiprasaṅgāt, api tu pratibandhasiddheḥ | na ceha kiñcinnibandhanamastīti sādhyadharmiṇi sidhyanto'pi kartṛtvādayo naikatvaniyatamātmānamātanvantīti viparyaye bādhakapramāṇābhāvāt prayatnavatkartṛniyatā api kāryatvādaya ekakartṛkatve sādhye sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatayā saṃśayahetava eveti |
[278,1]
tathā ca śaṃkara evāha, na karturekatvenācetanopādānatvasyāvyabhicāra ityādi |
yat punarāha, na caivamacetanopādānatvasya prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānamātreṇa vyabhicāra iti, na tanmātreṇa prastute kaścidupayogaḥ | vivādādhāradharmasiddhestatsiddhau pratibaddhatvasya pūrvaṃ pratipādanāditi |
{7.4.2}
<dvitīyaḥ khaṇḍaḥ>
[279,1]
tadevaṃ sādhyaviśeṣāpekṣayā vyāptidūṣaṇamabhidhāya prayatnavanmātre'pyabhidhātuṃ vitarkayannāha, sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu | iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayo'thavā ||
iti | dṛṣṭo'nto dṛṣṭāntaḥ siddhānta iti yo'rthaḥ, prayatnavanmātreṇa vyāpteḥ siddhatvāt, ekānekarūpānatikramācca vastunaḥ | sthitvā pravṛttyādiṣūpanyasteṣu vādina iṣṭasiddhiḥ kimastu ekatvapakṣe, asiddhimātraṃ vānekatve, atha vyāptireva nāstīti siddhānte saṃśaya eva ubhayatrāpīti praśnārthaḥ |
[279,2]
atra cānantaramabhedasādhanādhikāreṇa sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvodbhāvanena dattamevottaram | atastṛtīya eva pakṣaḥ | na hi prayatnopayogamantareṇāpi kāryajanmani saṃbhāvyamāne bādhakaṃ kiñcidālocayāmaḥ | tat kutastatra niyamaḥ kāryādeḥ ? atha kāladeśādyaniyamaprasaṅgo bādhakaḥ ? tadayuktam, yataḥ pratiniyataśakterasarvakālabhāvinaḥ svakāraṇāyattasannidheḥ kāraṇadaśāviśeṣasya vyatireke'pi vyatirekaḥ kāryasya saṃbhavanna prayatnavannāntarīyakatvamupakalpayituṃ kalpate | sarvathā hetvanapekṣāyāṃ tadvādhakamupapadyamānaṃ kāryasya hetumātreṇa vyāptiṃ sādhayet | na tu hetuviśeṣeṇa prayatnavatā |
[279,3]
nanu kāraṇaṃ nāma sarvatra kalāpa eva, sa ca na vyagrāvasthāyām | tatsaṃhatiśca prayatnavantamantareṇa yadi syāt, nityameva syāt | evaṃ deśe'pi vācyam | tataśca sa eva deśakālaniyamaprasaṅga iti, caitanyanirapekṣatvena kalāpakāryatvasya vyāpakasyābhāvena kāryatvādayo'saṃbhavantaḥ prayatnavadapekṣatvena vyāpyanta iti cet ? evaṃ tarhi so'pi prayatnavān yadi kṣaṇikaḥ prādeśikaśca tatkṣaṇaikadeśatvameva sarvakāryagrāmasya syāditi sanātana evāṅgīkartavyo vyāpī ca | tataśca sa eva deśakālāniyamo'dyāpi prasakta iti kimasyopagamena ? atha so'dṛṣṭamapekṣya janayanniyataṃ janayet ? jaḍānāṃ tu nādṛṣṭaṃ locanamiti |
[279,4]
evaṃ tarhi tadadṛṣṭaparipākasahāyā eva pratyayā niyatamutpādayiṣyanti nirālocā apīti kiṃ caitanyeneti cet ? evaṃ bruvataḥ kulālāderapi vaiyarthyaprasaṅgaḥ, na hi tatrāpi nādṛṣṭamasti sahakāri | na caivam | tasmād viparyayaḥ | yā yā sāmagrī sā nādṛṣṭāpekṣayā puruṣaprayatnaṃ viphalayati | yathā sūtrapiṇḍadaṇḍacakrādiḥ | sāmagrī ca girisāgarādijaniketi virudvavyāptopalabdhiḥ | prayatnaviphalīkaraṇaṃ hi tadanapekṣatvam ambarādau siddhaṃ niṣedhyam | tena yad viruddhaṃ prayatnāpekṣatvaṃ tadvyāptaṃ sāmagrītvam, tasyā yatnakāryatvāt |
[280,1]
atrocyate | yadi prayatnakāryaṃ sāmagrī sarvopasaṃhāreṇa sidhyed, yuktametat | na caivam, na hi tatrāpi viparyaye bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti | yathā hi kāryaṃ svakāraṇāyattasannidheḥ kāraṇāvasthāviśeṣasyāpekṣayā asarvakālabhāvi saṃbhāvyate, tathā sāmagryapi kiṃ na syāt, yato nityaṃ bhāvaprasaṅgaścodyeta ? tataścānivartitavipakṣavṛttiśaṅkā sāmagrī yadi prayatnāpekṣāṃ niyacchet, vsākṣātkāryatvādibhireva kīdṛśo'parādhaḥ kṛtaḥ, yena tadupanyāse saṃśayitasya sāmagrī śaraṇamupakṣipyate ?
[280,2]
mṛdādayaḥ puruṣādeva milanto dṛṣṭā iti cet ? kāryamapi prayatnavata eva jāyamānamupalabdhamiti kiṃ nocyate ? yathā ca yadyapi kimapi kāryaṃ prayatnavato dṛṣṭam, tathāpi kāryāntaraṃ tiraskṛtyāpi buddhimantaṃ bhaviṣyatīti śaṅkā, tathā sāmagryapi saṃbhāvyamānā kamarthaṃ puṣṇāti ? tato'nuktasamametat | tasmāt sāmagrīmapi madhye prakṣipya kumbhādiṣu sāmagryāstathā darśanameva pramāṇayitavyam | tathā ca sati kāryameva pratyakṣānupalambhaiḥ pratyatnavannāntarīyakaṃ siddhamityeva sādhu | kimatra vyāptisiddhaye bādhakapramāṇopanyāsaśauṭīryeṇa ? atha vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa pratyakṣānupalambhā jātiviśeṣameva viṣayīkartuṃ śaknuyuriti na kāryamātraṃ prayatnavatā vyāptaṃ sidhyet ? tadarthaṃ viparyayabādhāśrayaṇam, evaṃ tarhi sāmagryā api prayatnavatkāryatve ta eva pratyakṣānupalambhāḥ śaraṇamiti evaṃvidhā saṃhatiḥ prayatnavatā kriyata iti yuktaḥ sarvopasaṃhāraḥ | tathā ca, na vyagrādudayaḥ kvacinna ca cayaścaitanyaśūnyād bhaved bhāve kiṃ na sadā sadātanatanorapyeṣa doṣaḥ samaḥ | tasyādṛṣṭamapekṣya kālaniyame kiṃ cetasā cet tadā kumbhādāvapi śilpino viphalatā naitacca tadvyatyayaḥ || kumbhādau yadi darśanādabhividhiḥ kiṃ vyatyaye bādhayā pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ kimu matā na vyāptirevaṃ sati | teṣāṃ jātiviśeṣa eva viṣayo yadyevamevaṃvidho vyūhaścetanato bhavediti bhavedanyatra ko niścayaḥ ||
iti saṃgrahaślokau ||
[281,1]
na ca sāmagryantarasyātatpūrvakatve asyā api mā bhūditi yuktam, asarvavyāpināmapi dharmāṇāṃ pradeśavṛtterdarśanāt lohalekhanasyeva pārthive, asiddhaśarīrapūrvakatvasyeva vā kārye | tatra bādhakānna sarvavyāpitvamiti cet ? tadasphuraṇe tarhi saṃśayaḥ kena nivāryate | yathā hi na parasya bādhakaṃ kalāpāntare'pi kāryāntarādau vā cetanāpekṣāyāḥ, tathā bhavato'pi sarvajātau tayāvaśyaṃbhāvyamiti na sādhakamasti |
yathā ca tava kvacidbuddhimadapekṣādarśanamasti, tathā parasyāpyekatra dṛṣṭasya dharmasya bhinnajātīyāvyāptidarśanamasti | tato lohalekhanasya śarīravyāpārasya ca kvacid bādhakādarśanaṃ sandehasādhanamupayuktameva parasya, anyathā saṃśayasyaiva nirbījatāprasakteḥ |
[281,2]
na ca sādhāraṇānaikāntaḥ prārabdho'dhunābhidhātum, yatastadvadatra bādhakānupadarśanaṃ bādhakaṃ syāt prativadituḥ, api tu sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvameva | tacca siddhaṃ, dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭimātreṇa vyāpterasiddheḥ, nibandhanāntarasyābhāvāt | etena kṣityādihetūnām acetanatve sati niyatapravṛttitvena prāsādādihetuvat prayatnavadadhiṣṭhānāsiddhirityapi pratyuktam | acetaso'pi kālādiniyatāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ prayatnavannāntarīyakatvasādhakapramāṇasya tadvadevābhāvāditi |
[281,3]
nāpi kāryāvirāmaprasaṅgaḥ saṅgatimāvahati, aparāparapratyayayogajanyasvabhāvabhedasaṃbhavena bhāveṣvekaśaktinirvāhasya dūrīkṛtatvāt | tataśca karturekatve sandehodbhāvanena samānanyāyatayā āgatameva buddhipratibandhaṃ paraparitoṣāya sādhāraṇānaikāntikatvena dūṣayitumāha, sthitvā pravṛttisaṃsthānaviśeṣārthakriyādiṣu | iṣṭasiddhirasiddhirvā dṛṣṭānte iti | vāśabdaḥ samuccaye | eṣu satsu yadiṣṭaṃ caitanyaṃ tasya dṛṣṭānte sādhanavati dharmiṇi siddhirasiddhiśca ghaṭādau viṭapādau ca yathākramam | tato vyaktaṃ vipakṣaikadeśe vṛttireṣāmiti bhāvaḥ | etena yadi kṛtakādivad viparyayabādhābhidhānamaśakyam, dhūmādivat pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekapratītiḥ prayatnena saha kāryādīnāṃ bhaviṣyatīti gatyantaram apāstam, tamantareṇāpi kāryasyodayād vyatirekasyaivābhāvādityuktam |
[281,4]
nanu buddhimattvaṃ nāma dṛśyādṛśyaśarīretarasādhāraṇo dharmaḥ kṣmāruhādijanmani vyāpriyamāṇaṃ nāstīti kathamavagantavyam, anupalabdhimātrādabhāvāsiddheḥ ? yuktametat, yadi dṛśyaśarīropādhividhureṇa buddhimātreṇa vyāptirabhimatā syāt | bāḍhameveti cet ?
evaṃ tarhi dhūmavadvyattirekamevādhikṛtyāha, saṃśayo'tha vā iti | yadā kumbhakāravyāpārāt prāk kalasasya vyatirekaḥ pratyetavyaḥ, tadā na sādhyābhāvakṛto ghaṭa vyatirekaḥ pratītaḥ syāt, sādhyābhāvasya sandehāt | na hi tathāvidhaśarīropādhikena cetasā vyāptirjijñāsitā, yato'nupalabdhiviśeṣeṇa niṣedhaḥ sidhyet, kiṃ tu prayatnavanmātreṇa | tasya ca yathā vṛkṣādijanmasamaye saṃbhāvanā niṣedhasyāśakyatvāt, tathādyāpīti, tatsaṃbhave'pi saṃbhāvyamānaḥ kumbhābhāvastadabhāvaprayuktatvamātmano bodhayituṃ na śaknotīti sandigdhavyatirekaḥ |
[282,1]
nanu sādhyābhāve sādhanasya bhāvasaṃśaye sandigdho vyatireka iti yuktam, na tu kulālavyāpārāt prāk kumbhabhāvaḥ sandihyata iti cet ? tadayuktam, sādhyavyatirekaprayukto vyatirekaḥ sādhanasya vyāptivādinā darśayitavyaḥ | sa ca sādhyābhāvasandehād vā svayamato'pi na darśitaḥ | sādhyābhāve'pi vā svabhāvasandehāditi na kaścid viśeṣaḥ, ubhayathāpi tasya saviśeṣaṇasya sandigdhatvāditi | ataeva sandigdhasādhyasādhanadharmitvaṃ dṛṣṭāntayordoṣa ucyate |
[282,2]
yadi tu sādhanābhāvamātramabhidhīyeta sādhyābhāvamanapekṣya, tadā yuktametat |
na ca tāvatā vyāptigrahaḥ | anyathā pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptiṃ pratipadya pavanopaghātasādhanopanīyamānaḥ kampo yadā mardanādisaṃbhavena kampena sādhāraṇaṃ kriyate, tadā stimitamārutamasparśayogyatayā niṣeddhumaśakyaṃ saṃbhāvya pariharannanivāryaḥ syāt |
[282,3]
tatra viśeṣasādhanād vyabhicāra eveti cet ? kutaḥ punaretadviśeṣastena sādhyata iti ? upahatiśabdastvaśarīravyāpāravat tadanurūpaviṣayo bhaviṣyati, pratyakṣānupalambhena vyāptivarṇanāditi cet ? tadapi bhavataḥ samānam, yathā cāsya tādṛgmarunmātrāpekṣayā adṛśyatvena vyabhicāraparihāre vyāptigrahaṇakāle'dṛśyatvenaiva vyatirekāsiddhistathā bhavato'pi śarīravirahiṇi caitanyamātre | tato yadā tadabhāvasaṃśaye'pi kāryābhāvamātreṇa vyāptigrahaṇābhimānastathā aspṛśyaprabhañjanābhāvasaṃśaye'pi kampābhāvaḥ siddha iti syād vyāptiḥ |
[283,1]
atha na kaścit dehavateva dehavirahiṇāpi vyāptiṃ karoti, kiṃ tu caitanyamātreṇa, tacca kāyavatkāle'pyasti viśeṣasaṃbhave sāmānyasyāvaśyaṃbhāvāditi tadapekṣayā vyāptigrahaḥ sāmānyaviṣaya evāvatiṣṭhate, vahnāviva vahnyantarasvarūpānupraveśāditi | etadapi samānaṃ samīrānumāne | na ca kaścit cetanāvān vepathumātreṇa mārutamanumimīte, sarvagatvādhyavasāye'pi kampamātrasya sādhanasāmarthyāpratīteḥ | na hi rājyamiṣṭamiti tannāmakaraṇānantaramupajāyamānamapi tadupāyavādinaṃ pramāṇīkaroti, sādhanamapi vā kṛtakatvaṃ vastutaḥ asādhanāṅgo vyāpakatvenopanīyamānamanityatāsiddhau |
[283,2]
tasmāt na koṣṭhaśuddhyā prameyatathābhāvena paritoṣaḥ, pramāṇaguṇastu nirūpyate |
na ca kampasya marunmātreṇa vyāptisiddhau kiñcid viparyaye bādhakamasti, pratyakṣānupalambhāstu svagocarībhāvayogyameva svabhāvadeśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi tadā tvasannihite'ntarbhāvayituṃ śaknuvantītyavaśyameṣitavyam, nānyam | anyathā vyāptigrahaṇavadvyabhicāro'pi tanniṣṭha eva prasajyeta | tato yathā viśeṣaviṣayāvanvayavyatirekau pratyakṣādyagocaracaitanyamarunmātraviṣayau vyavasthitau, tathāpi viśeṣaviṣayo vyabhicāro'pi tanmātraviṣayaḥ kiṃ na vyavasthāpyate ? na hi lābhe praveśaḥ, chede niḥsaraṇamiti labhyam |
[283,3]
vahnistu deśakālaviprakṛṣṭo'pi tadātmā sannihita iva svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭapratyakṣādiyogyatayā tadanupraveśamāsādayatīti yuktam, yatastadekādhyavasāyāt sarva eva dhūmavyāpakatayāvadhāryamāṇo na duṣyati, jāṭharaṃ tadayogyatayā tathā niścāyi | ata eva dhūmādabhimate śikhini pravṛttirasaṃśayānasya yujyate | itarathā pratyakṣāyogyenāpi vyāptiḥ āśrayabhujā gṛhyamāṇā dhūmasya tadyogyāyogyadahanasāmānyaviṣayaiva vyavatiṣṭhata iti tārṇādibheda ivābhimate'pi rūpe sandihāno na tatsādhyārthakriyālābhaikāgrabuddhiḥ pravarteta |
pratibandhavaikalyavad vā asati jāṭharatva ityāmṛṣataḥ pravṛttiḥ syāt | na caivam, tasmānna svarūpaviśeṣaniṣṭhaṃ pramāṇaṃ sāmānyena vyāptiṃ prapadyate |
[283,4]
anityatvena tu kṛtakatvasya vyāptiṃ viparyayabādhakapramāṇamadhigacchad bhūtvābhavanamātreṇa viśeṣānavacchinnena pravṛttamiti sāmānyenaivādhigacchati | nāpi kṛtakāt pravartamāno'bhimatānityaikāgrabuddhiḥ kaścit pravṛttimarhati | ataśca sāmānyaparyavasitamapi pramāṇaṃ na viśeṣeṇa vyāptiṃ gṛhṇātīti siddham | uktaṃ ca nyāyānusāriṇā śaṃkareṇa, yat pramāṇaṃ yāvatīmarthagatiṃ vyāpnotītyādi | yat pramāṇaṃ yatsvabhāvasāpekṣapravṛttikaṃ tannaiva taditarasvabhāvena kasyacid vyāptiṃ pratipadyate, yathā viparyayabādhakaṃ bhūtvābhavanamātrāpekṣamanityaviśeṣeṇa kṛtakatvasya | yathā vābhimatasvarūpaviśeṣāpekṣamadhyakṣānupalambham agnerjāṭharasādhāraṇena rūpeṇa dhūmasya | svarūpaviśeṣāpekṣapravṛttayaśca pratyakṣānupalambhāḥ prabhañjanena kampasya vyāptigrahaṇa iti vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhiḥ, mātariśvalaghutvavat pratyakṣapravṛtterabhāvāt |
[284,1]
nāpyanekāntaḥ | vivakṣitasvabhāvena hi kasyacit vyāptigrahaṇaṃ pramāṇasya tatsvarūpāpekṣapravṛttikatvena vyāptam, anyathātiprasaṅgaḥ pravṛttisaṃkaraśca doṣaḥ | tadviruddhā ca taditarasvabhāvāpekṣā pravṛttiḥ, tasmāt svarūpaviśeṣāpekṣaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ nānilamātreṇa stimitetarasādhāraṇena kampasya vyāptiṃ pratipadyata iti pramāṇārthaḥ | tato na paramārthataḥ kampena pavanānumānamasti |
[284,2]
atha ca na kācid bhavadīyasamayasamādhānakalpanā, yā nainamanudhāvati, na caitadīyamaprāmāṇyanibandhanaṃ kimapi, yanna bhāvatkamanumānamupanīyate, tataśca vahnidhūmavat prayatnavatkāryayoryadi vyāptisiddhaye'dhyakṣānupalambhaṃ śaraṇamāśriyate, tadā tatpravṛttiyogyasvarūpāpekṣayā prayatnavato niyato vyabhicāraḥ kāryamātreṇa tṛṇādinā |
[284,3]
atha vyabhicāracamatkārāgocareṇa cetanāvatā vyāptiriṣyate, tadā mahīruhādijanmanīva śilpivyāpārādapi prāk niṣeddhumaśakye prayatnavanmātravyāpāre vyatiricyamāno ghaṭādiḥ kasyābhāvaprayuktābhāvo'vadhāryatām, yatastena vyāptaḥ sidhyediti sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatayā punaranekāntaḥ pūrvaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaviśeṣamanapekṣya viparyaye bādhakābhāvaṃ svayamupadarśya kṛtaḥ, idānīṃ vādina evābhyupagamena tadiṣṭapramāṇāpekṣayā vyatirekāsiddheriti bhedaḥ | vipakṣabādhakaṃ tu hetumātreṇa vyāptiṃ pratīyāt na tadviśeṣaṇabuddhimatetyuktam |
[284,4]
nanu vṛkṣādayaḥ pakṣīkṛtā iti kathaṃ tairvyabhicāraḥ ? trividho hi bhāvarāśiḥ, sandigdhakartṛko buddhimatkartṛko'kartṛkaśceti | tatra buddhimatkartṛke ghaṭādau pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptimādāya sandehapade bhūdharādau kāryatvamupasaṃhṛtya prayatnavān sādhyate |
na punarasau vyabhicāraviṣayo bhavitumarhati |
[284,5]
yadāha, na ca sādhyenaiva vyabhicāra iti, tadayuktam | na hi vyabhicāraviṣaya eva pakṣo bhavitumarhati, sandigdhe hetuvacanād vyasto heturanāśrayaḥ | (pra. vā. 4. 91)
iti nyāyāt | tataśca kṣmādharādireva sandigdhakartṛkaḥ pakṣīkartumucitaḥ | kṣmāruhādiḥ tvacetanakartṛka iti caturtho rāśireṣitavyaḥ | vyāptisamīhayā pratyakṣayogyābhimatasya vṛkṣādijanmanyanupalabdheriti kathaṃ pakṣīkaraṇam ? mā bhūdaśeṣasādhāraṇānaikāntikocchedaḥ | kāryatvasya vipakṣavṛttihataye saṃbhāvyate'tīndriyaḥ kartā ced vyatirekasiddhividhurā vyāptiḥ kathaṃ sidhyati | bādhā tvāhitahetumātraniyatirbhedena na vyāptaye nāpyardho vyabhicāragocaracaraḥ pakṣīkriyāyāṃ kṣamaḥ ||
iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ ||
[285,1]
nanu tathāpi kathamavyāptirākāśasya vyatirekagrahaṇādhikaraṇasya saṃbhavāt ?
yadāha, buddhimatkāraṇasadbhāve bhāvo ghaṭādāvutpattyādeḥ, abhāve cābhāvo gaganādiṣu, sa ca tathāprasiddhāvinābhāvo yatraiva kṣityādāvupalabhyate, tatraiva tadvinirmāṇasamarthakartṛbuddhiṃ tadvido janayatīti | utpattyāderiti kāryatvāderityarthaḥ | atrābhidhīyate | na sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa vā dṛṣṭāntamātramastīti sādhyasiddhiḥ, yadṛcchopanatāvapi tathā saṃbhavāt | tasmānnidarśanaṃ nāma gṛhītavismṛtapratibandhasādhakapramāṇasmaraṇadvāreṇaiva hetāvupayogi, na svasannidhimātreṇa |
[285,2]
sa ca pratibandho dvārāntareṇa vā gṛhīto vihāyasā smaryeta, svādhikaraṇapramāṇaprasiddho vā ? tatra tāvat prathamakalpanamapāstaṃ, prāgeva dṛśyaśarīropādhinā dhīmātreṇa vā kāryatvāderghaṭāvapi pratibandhagrahaṇopāyāpāyāt | caramaṃ cāsaṃbhavi | tathā hi, yadi nāma vyomni dvayanivṛttirupalabdhā, tathāpyekābhāvaprayuktatvaniścayāyogādanyābhāve viśvarūpasya ca tatrāvṛtteḥ kasya kena saṃbandhabodhaḥ syāt ? karabhagardabhāderapi kāryakāraṇabhāvagrahaṇaprasaṅgācca | anyatrānvayadarśanasahāyasya tathā pratītiriti cet ?
nanu sahadarśanamevānvayārthaḥ, tacca kadācit karabhāderapyastīti sādhvī vyavasthā |
[285,3]
na sahadarśanamanvayasyārthaḥ, kiṃ tvekasaṃbhavaprayukto'nyabhāvaḥ | sa ca buddhimatkāryatvayorasti nānyatreti cet — na, tadbhāvaprayuktatvaṃ nāmāparabhāvasya na tadvyāpārāt prāgabhāvinaḥ sattālābhādanyaḥ prāgabhāvaśca nānupalabdhivyāpāramantareṇeti pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekayorniścaye saṃśayo nāma kīdṛk hetuphalasthitāviti tatpratītipratibandhasmaraṇameva vihāyasā vidhīyata iti prathamapakṣa evāyam |
[286,1]
kiṃ ca kimidamīśvare'nujovivṛttāvivṛttāviṣkaraṇamātramatrabhavataḥ, uta prativandīkṛte ? dhūmānumāne'pi saiva gatiḥ, ekatrobhayasaṃbhavamupalakṣyāntarīkṣe ekavyāpāranivṛttau anyanivṛtterupalakṣaṇād vyāptigraha iti | yadyeṣa eva nyāyaḥ, tadā tadicchatāmanibandhanaḥ prakṛtapradveṣaḥ, kevalamevaṃ vilapatā dahanānumānamapi hāritaṃ, dūratarā tu prakṛtasiddhiḥ, uktakrameṇa gardabhenāpi tasya prasaṅge vahnāvapi hastakatyāgāt | yadā tu gatyantara mapi tatra prakṛtāsaṃbhavi saṃbhavi, tadā kuto vandīkaraṇaṃ śaraṇam ?
[286,2]
evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāraḥ tadatiprasaṅgabhayādevāśrīyate, na tu sa eva samaya iti cet ? evaṃ sati bhavataiva kimayamatiprasaṅge bharo datto neti kośapānaṃ kartavyam, yo hi pratyakṣānupalabdhī vihāya vihāyasi vahnivyāpāranivṛttyā dhūmanivṛttim ādāya vyāptimabhidhatte, taṃ prati yathā vastumātrasyāpi tatra vyāpāroparamāttenāpi vyāptisiddhiḥ syādityatiprasaṅgaḥ, tathā yo'pi pratyakṣānupalabdhīruddhūya tadyogyapuruṣaviśeṣavyāpāraviraheṇa vyomani ghaṭādikāryatvanivṛttiṃ darśayitvā tena vyāptimasya manyate, taṃ prati puruṣamātrasyāpi tatra nivṛttyā tenāpi vyāptiḥ, tathā kāryāntaratvasyāpi nivṛttyā tasyāpi syāditi vyaktamatiprasaṅgamātrametat, na nyāya iti paśyāmaḥ |
[286,3]
dhūme gardabhādivyabhicāradarśanānna vastumātreṇa vyāptiriti yuktam, puruṣamātrasya tu vyabhicārānupalabdhernedamatiprasaṅgamātrodbhāvanaṃ bhaviṣyati | naivaṃ, samānanyāyānām ekatra bādhakadarśanamanyatrāpi śaṅkāmutpādayati | yadi hi vihāyasi ubhayanivṛttidarśanaṃ pratibandhasādhakaṃ bhavet, vastudhūmayorapi na bādhyeta, tatra tu bādhyamānamanyatrāpi katham ekāntāvasāyasādhanaṃ syāt ? na ca pakṣīkṛte naiva vyabhicāra ityapi, na pakṣīkaraṇaṃ mantraprabhāvaḥ, kiṃ tu vyāptigrāhakadārḍhyam | tacca yadi nabhasi ubhayābhāvamātram, tadā tatra bādhakādhigaterastaṃ dārḍhyamiti satyapi pakṣīkaraṇavyabhicārāśaṅkā na nivartata iti | vyomāsti vyatirekabhūmiriti ced dhūmasya dhūmadhvajād utpattāvapi kiṃ sa eva samayo nātiprasaṅgodayāt | yadyevaṃ bhavataiva kiṃ vinihito nātiprasaṅgetarastasmin bādhavilokanaṃ punarihāpyārekamākarṣati ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ ||
[287,1]
tasmāt nākāśe dvayanivṛttyā vyāptisiddhiḥ, siddhavyāptikayostvabhāvadarśanaṃ gṛhītavyāptismaraṇakāraṇaṃ syāt | na ca vyāptigrāhakaṃ kiñcidupapadyata ityuktam | tasmāt anvayamātrabhāve'pi vyatirekābhāvādanekānta eveti sthitam | vastutastu vyatirekavadanvayo'pyasya durlabha eva | yasya hi pratyakṣāgocaratayā abhāvaprayuktaḥ kāryābhāva iti pratyetumaśakyaṃ tasyānvayo dūrotsārita eva, pratyakṣagrāhyatvāt tasya | pratyakṣaṃ hi paridṛśyamāne vastuni deśakālaviprakṛṣṭamapi svapravṛttiyogyamevāntarbhāvya vyāptimavakalpayet, na svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭamapīti uktaprāyam | tataścānvayamātraṃ gajanimīlitenāvadhīrya vyatirekābhāvenaiva dṣaṇamuktam | vastutastu nānvayo na vyatireka iti prayatnavanmātre sādhye kāryatvamasādhāraṇameveti vā darśayitumāha, saṃśayo'thavā iti | pratyakṣādiyogyāpekṣayā sādhāraṇānaikāntikam, caitanyamātrāpekṣayā asādhāraṇam ityarthaḥ | nanu śarīropādhibuddhikṛtaṃ kāryaṃ sidhyat buddhimātrakṛtaṃ sidhyatyeva, śiṃśapākṛtamiva bṛkṣakṛtam, viśeṣe sāmānyānapahnavāditi kathamucyate'nvayābhāvaḥ ? evaṃ sati vyatireko'pi tadapekṣayā syāditi cet ? kā no hāniḥ, buddhimati kāryahetoranvayavyatirekavattvābhyupagamāditi ? uktamatra, evamanvayavyatirekakalpane jāṭharacitrakādigatenāpi rūpeṇa dhūmādanumitamagniṃ saṃśayāno nābhimataikāgracittaḥ pravarttetetyādi |
[287,2]
api ca na tatra saṃbhavītyeva pratyakṣeṇa yatkiñcidvastuno rūpaṃ kāryasya vyāpakam avadhāryate, api tvadhyavasāyāpekṣayā | adhyavasāyaśca puruṣeṇa kṛta eva iti buddhimatā veti viśiṣṭaviṣaya eva pravartate, tādṛśyeva puruṣādiśabdasya rūḍheḥ | na tu karādivyāpāranirapekṣeṇa caitanyamātreṇeti, caitanyamātraṃ sadapyudāsīnamanvayagrahaṇakāle'dhyavasāyasya viśeṣonmukhenaiva pravṛtteḥ, sāmānyaśabdatve'pi vā prakṛtaviśeṣamākṣipyaivāgnivyāptivat | sa cādhyavasāyaḥ pratyakṣavyāpārānusārī tadyogyameva rūpaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt, na tu tadayogyamapi, jāṭharādivat, tārṇādivacca | evaṃ puruṣeṇāpi vyāptau kasyacit śarīropādhividhurasya buddhimātrasya tadayogyasya pratikṣepaḥ syādeva | apratikṣepastu kharvādibhedasyaiya | ayameva nyāyaḥ sarvatra pratyakṣeṇānvayagrahaṇe |
[288,1]
athāṅgārasaṅgādagurukhaṇḍajanitaṃ dhūmamupalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣayogyatayā indhanādyantareṇāpi tadanvayaprasaṅga iti cet ? tatkimidānīṃ pramāṇaviṣayapratiniyamam anādṛtya yatra kvacit pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ yena kenacidanvayaṃ pratyetviti vivakṣitam ? evaṃ sati hetumadābhāsavyavasthāvilopāt sarvasya sarvasiddhiriti pratiniyatasādhanānveṣo viphalaḥ |
[288,2]
atha pratyakṣeṇa svayogyamullaṃdhyāpi vyāptirgṛhītetyucyate ? tadasiddham | yadāpi pratyakṣaṃ svapravṛttiyogye'pi vastunyavāntarabhedāpekṣayā sāmānyamudāsayadanvayaṃ pratipadyate, tadā kaiva kathā svapravṛttyayogyasyātyantaṃ vijātīyasya ? na cāsmākaṃ pakṣaḥ pratyakṣayogyeṇa sarveṇa vyāptiriti, kiṃ tu pratyakṣayogyeṇaiva tatkṛtā vyāptiriti | anyathā gardabhādibhirapi dhūmakumbhāderevānvayaprasaṅgaḥ | kimataḥ param ? kathaṃ punaratrāvāntarabhedāpekṣa eva vyāptigraho na darśanayogyatāmātrāpekṣaḥ ? vikalpastu vāsanāprabodhamātrārthamapekṣitapratyakṣādisannidhiraniyatodayākāratayā na pratiniyataṃ viśeṣamāveśayitumarhatīti |
[288,3]
satyam, ataeva vyatirekasādhanyā anupalabdheravatāraḥ | tatra yathā vahnipuruṣābhyāṃ dhūmakumbhayoranvayādhyavasāye sahāyatāmanupalabdhiḥ pratipadyate, pūrvasthitiranyata utpattiranyata āgamanamiti tridhā bhinnasaṃbhavavyatirekaṃ sādhayantītarathānupayogāt, tathā yadi gardabhānvaye vedanamātrānvaye vā pratipadyeta, syādeva tābhyāmapi vyāptiḥ, nānyathā, yato na pratyakṣamātraṃ vyāptiṃ pratipadyate, nāpyanupalambhamātraṃ, kiṃ tu pratyakṣānupalambhāvanyonyasahāyāviti nirṇītaṃ śāstre bahuśaḥ | asmābhirapi trikapañcakacintāyāṃ kiñciditi |
[288,4]
na ca gardabhādyanvaye tasyāḥ sāhāyakamasti | etena dhūmaviśeṣāpekṣayānupalambhavyāpārābhāvo vyākhyāta iti naivaṃvādini kaścit paryanuyogaḥ | yastu pratyakṣagocare'pi tatkṛtāṃ vyāptimupavarṇayati tasya tadviṣaya eva vyāptigrahaviraha iti duḥsthā vyavasthā |
tataśca tasyaivāsau paryanuyogaḥ | tasyāpyanupalabdhivyāpārābhāvānneti cet — na, yataḥ pratyakṣayogye'pi tatkṛtavyāptivādino'nupalambhavyāpāravirahe'pi tatkṛtavyāptimicchataḥ kaḥ pratiroddhā ? yadi hyasya vrīḍā syādapratyakṣayogya eva tadvyāpāraṃ kathaṃ varṇayet ?
athopādānādividā prayatnavatā kāraṇadarśanādeva gardabhasya nirāsaḥ, kimatrānupalabdhyā ?
[289,1]
evaṃ tarhi dṛśyamānenaiva vyāptimupavarṇayan na ca darśanapathātikrāntena, na ca śarīropādhiṃ vyavadhūya caitanyamātramupalabdhaṃ kvacit | yadi ca darśanabalādeva vyavasthā caitanyamātrādhiṣṭhitaṃ śarīraṃ kumbhādi janayat dṛṣṭameveti na gardabhenānvayavirodhaḥ, tat kathamanupalabdhipratikṣepaḥ ? vyāpakagatāḥ sāmānyadharmā eva vyāptau sādhakāḥ itareṣāṃ vyabhicāradarśanenānyatra śaṃkāvakāśādeva na gardabhenānvaya iti cet ? nanu vyabhicāradarśanamiti tadabhāve'pi bhāvadarśanamityanupalabdhivyāpārābhāve'sādhanatvam upanīyamānamanupalabdhereva sādhanāṅganiścaye vyāpāraṃ paridīpayati |
[289,2]
yadi ca viśeṣe vyāpāraśaṃkākulaḥ sāmānyamanusarati bhavān, upādānādyabhijñamapi viśeṣamapahāya caitanyamātreṇa gardabhasādhāraṇena siddhasādhanayogyena tato'pi vā sāmānyena kāraṇamātreṇa vyāptimabhidhattām | evaṃ hi sati sarvathā dūrīkṛtaḥ śaṃkāvakāśaḥ syāditi | etāvattu sāmānyamavamanya upādānādyabhijñaviśeṣe sthitirna tu tadapyavajñāya yathādṛṣṭa iti kimatra sāmarthyamanyatra jāḍyāt ? pratyakṣānupalambhavādinastu yāvati yādṛśi sāmānye pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpāro na tatra śaṃkā, śaṃkāvakāśini ca na vyāpāra iti nāsau kvacana svayamicchayā vyāptimupanayatyapanayati vā pramāṇenaiva samarpaṇāditi na doṣaḥ |
[289,3]
nanu so'pi hetumātrakṛtaṃ vā kāryagrāmaṃ bruvan pratyakṣayogye'pi pratyakṣavyāpāropalambhaṃ kiṃ na paśyati ? paśyatyeva viparyayabādhakādāgamācca tasya tadābhyupagamāt |
pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ tu śarīraviśeṣādhika eva cetasi sa pramāṇayati | icchāyāmapi karādivyāpāroparame kāryābhāvāt taddvāreṇaiva kulālādivyapadeśaviṣayasya samudāyasya pratyakṣatvavyavahārāt | na tviyaṃ gatiḥ prayatnasacivacittamātre | tadāpyanumānādanvayaḥ pratyeṣyate | na ca pratyakṣasyaiva kaścidanurodhaḥ | upalambhānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekaniścayaḥ kartavyaḥ | sa copalambhaḥ pratyakṣarūpo'numānarūpo veti nātra nirbandhaḥ |
[289,4]
atra cintyate | kiṃ tadeva śarīropādhikaṃ cittaṃ prayatnavaccittamātraśabdenābhimatam, utānyat ? tattve kimanumānena, pratyakṣasiddhau vivādābhāvāt | tena cānvayavyatirekau siddhau kāryamātreṇa ca tadvyabhicāro vyaktaḥ | anyatve liṅgābhāvadoṣaḥ, bhāṣaṇādeḥ kāryasya śarīriṇaiva caritārthatvāt | na ca tenānumitenāpi vyāptiḥ svīkriyate, vyatirekāniścayāt pūrvavat | evaṃ tarhi barhiṣāpi dhūmasya vyāptirna deśakālāvasthāniyatena, kiṃ tu vahnimātreṇa | tacca dṛśyamānādanyenaiveti vikalpe vyabhicārādidoṣaḥ sādhāraṇa iti tādugviśeṣavirahiṇā sāmānyena vyāptirvaktavyā |
[290,1]
tathehāpīti cet ? evamapi jāṭharādigatenāpi rūpeṇa vyāptiprasaṅgo dhūmasya |
tasmānna sāmānyamityeva vyāptāvadhikriyate, nāpi viśeṣa ityeva pratikṣipyate, dhūmānumānasyaivocchedāt, abhimate śikhani pravṛttisandehāt | tato yadi na svecchaiva saṃgrahaparicchedasādhanī, tadā pramāṇavyāpāramanviṣya vyavasthāprakrame kiñcit sāmānyaṃ svīkārapravṛttenāpi pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣiptamarthādeṣitavyam, yadviśeṣātikrameṇa nāsyāvatāraḥ |
yathā jvaladbhāsurākāra pātikrame dhūmavyāptigrāhiṇaḥ | kiñcittu pratyakṣasvīkṛtam apyanupalabdhiḥ pratikṣipati, pīṭharādivat sāmarthyāt |
[290,2]
sā hi dahanābhāve kāryābhimatābhāvaṃ sādhayantī dahanabhāvaprayuktatadbhāvavibhāvanādayogavyavacchedena tatkāryatāsādhanapravṛttāpyanyasya hetutāṃ sādhayatyeva, yadabhāve svayaṃ na vartate | anupalambhapūrvake tu pratyakṣe prāgbhāvādibādhanapravṛttayānupalabdhyānekavasturūpasattvābhāve'bhāvasiddhau yadekavastusvabhāvasannidhau sannidhiradhyakṣeṇa pratīyate prāgapi tadabhāvaprayuktābhāvavibhāvanāt taddhetubhāvasādhane yadapravṛttiyogyatayā pratikṣiptam adhyakṣeṇa tatpratikṣiptameva |
[290,3]
tato na jāṭharāderanvayaḥ | nāpi kāladaśābhedabhinnasvabhāvapratikṣepaḥ, sarvasya pratyakṣeṇa svajanmayogyatayā svīkārāt | nāpyanupalabdhyā, sā hyatādṛksvabhāvābhāve'bhavantī tadvijātīyahetutāṃ pratikṣipatīti yuktam, na tu tasyaiva, anyathā tadāśrayaṇavaiyarthyāt | nanu deśādibhinnasvabhāvābhāve'pyayaṃ dhūmo dṛṣṭaḥ, na deśādibhinnasyāpyekākārapratyavamarśapratyayena paridṛśyamānarūpeṇa sahaikīkaraṇāt, darśanāyogyasvabhāvād anyatra | ataeva vahnimātraśabdābhidheyaṃ tadeva paridṛśyamānayogyādbhedākṛṣṭāvapyabhedāvabhāsāt |
[290,4]
nanu deśādiviprakṛṣṭamapyadarśanayogyameva | satyaṃ, kevalaṃ kadācit kvacit | svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭaṃ tu sadetyatyantavijātīyatayā svīkāraparihārayorbhedena vṛttirna virudhyate |
tato yathānumānavādinā sāmānyamanusaraṇīyamavyāptimasaṃbhavaṃ vā parihartu, tathā dṛśyaviśeṣāpekṣayātiriktasāmānyamapi parihartavyamativyāptiparihārāya | evaṃ sati yathā darśanāyogyavahnisāmānyaparihāreṇa tadyogyāvāntarasāmānyena vyāptirekatvavyavasthā ca yuktā, na prayatnavanmātreṇa, pratyakṣapratikṣiptatvāditi |
[291,1]
tatra vyāmohāt pramāṇāntareṇānvayamicchan tattvānyatvābhyāṃ paryanuyujyate |
dahane tu tatpakṣeṇaiva samādhirityuktam | tasmāt pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ vyāptijighṛkṣāyāṃ tadyogyasāmānyāpekṣāyā ghaṭaviṭapādau dṛṣṭānta iṣṭasya siddhirasiddhiśceti sādhāraṇānaikāntikatvaṃ kāryasya | caitanyamātreṇa tu tadayogyenānvayavyatirekayorekasyāpyaniścayāt sandigdhānvayavyatirekatvaṃ vaktuṃ yuktamuktam, saṃśayo'thaveti |
siddhyasiddhyoriti prakaraṇāt | tābhyāṃ ca bhāvābhāvāvuktau | yathāha — upalabdhireva sattā anupalabdhirasatteti | tataḥ kāryatvādisādhanavati dharmiṇi dṛṣṭānte sādhyatveneṣṭasya prayatnavanmātreṇa sattvāsattvasandehāt, tadadhiṣṭhānānadhiṣṭhānābhyāṃ ca sarvasaṃgrahādekatānvayavyatirekānupapatteryuktamasādhāraṇānaikāntikatvam |
[291,2]
nanu tathāpyanekānto'pyastu, anvayamātraṃ kimiti pratikṣipyate, kāryotpattau buddhereva vyāpāradarśanāt ? jāṭharasādhāraṇenāpi rūpeṇa tarhi dhūme'nvayaprasaṅgaḥ, dahanavyāpāradarśanāt | tataśca tadapekṣo vyatireko'pi syāditi prācīnadoṣaḥ | pratyakṣapratikṣepastu sādhāraṇaḥ |
[291,3]
nanu jāṭharādyabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvānna prācīnadoṣaḥ, satyapyanvaya iti cet ? kailāsakaraṇakauśalavikalenāpi kalasasya karaṇaṃ kiṃ na kīrttyate ? atha karaṇakauśalasāmānyenānvayo'tra ? tatrāpi dāhakamātreṇeti na vyaktyupakṣepeṇa kiñcit | jātyapekṣayā tu tadānyadāpīti kathaṃ tadabhāve'pi dhūmabhāvaḥ ? atha dāhakatvamātraṃ paridṛṣṭaviśeṣād bhinnāṃ jātimāsthāya vyabhicāra ucyate, tadā tadapekṣayānvayo'pi kutaḥ, pratyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭāyā eva jāteradhigamāt ? anvaye vā punarvyabhicārānupapatteriti |
[291,4]
yatpunaḥ sajātīyena pratyakṣataḥ pratibandhaniścayamāśaṃkya, na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyate, pratyakṣaśca yasmādasamānajātiḥ, apratyakṣaśca rūpādivyaktibhiranumīyate cakṣurādigrāmaḥ, tathā candramasaḥ pṛthivyāśca parabhāgādhobhāgāvityuktam, tadapi pāpīyaḥ | tathāhi na tāvad vyāptiśūnyamanumānam, vyāptiśca sāmānyena sāmānyasya bhavantī kathamasamānānumānamanusaheta ? tathā ca sā dvidhaiva pratyakṣānupalambhataḥ viparyayabādhakād vā | ubhayathāpi dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭasajātīyasyaivānumānam | anyathānyajātīyena dharmeṇa vyāptimupādāyānyajātīyamanuminotīti mahatī prekṣā |
[292,1]
sāmānyato dṛṣṭānumāne'pi hi yadeva gatisāmānyamanyasthānaprāptinibandhanamupalabdham, tadevādhikaraṇāntare niścīyata iti kathaṃ vijātīyadharmānumānam ? athādhārabhedāpekṣayā sāmarthyasādhyamavāntarabhedamabhipretyocyate, tadanuktasamam | na hi kaścit anumānavādo tanmātreṇa viśeṣamanicchan phalinamanumānaṃ samarthayitumīśaḥ | yadi ceśvarānumāne'pi tādṛśo vyāptiḥ syāt, tanmātraviśeṣasiddhyā ceṣṭasiddhiḥ syāt, kastatra matsaramācaret ?
na ca tanmātraviśeṣāpekṣayā na hi sarvatra samānajātiranumīyata iti vaktuṃ yuktam, kvacidasamānajātyanumāne'pi tathocyate, tanmātraviśeṣaśca sarvatrānumāne'sti | viśeṣato dṛṣṭasya sāmānye'pi tadeva niścīyata iti tadapekṣayā na sarvatra tadevānumīyata iti vaktavyam, bhedādhiṣṭhānatvāt samānajāticintāyāḥ |
[292,2]
tat punaraprakṛtameva | sa tu na sarvaḥ pratyakṣo'numīyata iti | yadi prakṛtamagnivat pratibandhagrahe pramāṇamadhikṛtyocyate, tadā pratyakṣasyaiva sarvatrānumānam anyatrāpadiṣṭapramāṇapravṛtteḥ | atha viparyayabādhakāpekṣayā, tadā na vaktavyaṃ na kaścidviśeṣo'gnisādhanāt īśvarānumānasyeti | anityasādhanāditi tu vaktumucitam | atha kāryahetutāmātreṇaivam ucyate, tadā kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pratyakṣānupalambhasādhana eveti sa eva doṣaḥ | na ca viparyayabādhakaṃ kiñcidastīti carcitameva | deśādyaniyamaprasaṅgaśca hetumātrāpattiṃ sādhayatyapi | tasmāt prakṛtaprameyānavagāhanāt plavata etat na sarvaḥ pratyakṣo'numīyata iti |
[292,3]
anumānakālāpekṣayā tu sarvaḥ parokṣa evānumīyate, na ca tatra kācid vimatiḥ ityanuktasamam | indriyaṃ tu na sākṣād buddheranumātuṃ śakyam, pratibandhāgrahaṇāt | buddhikāryaṃ tu keṣucit satsvabhāvābhāvavattadatiriktakāraṇasāpekṣatāmāvahatīti tādṛśīndriyaghoṣaṇā |
tatrāṅkurādiṣu dṛṣṭajātīyameva sāpekṣatvaṃ yathā sādhyate, tathā parabhāgādhobhāgāvapi ghaṭādikāryeṣu | arvāgaikasāmagrīpratibaddhau sāmānyato dṛṣṭāvevānumīyete iti sādhyaśūnyamudāharaṇamapi ityalaṃ bahunā | athavā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāpyate, kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa tu kāryaviśeṣa eveti nyāyaḥ | adhyavasāyamātrato vā kāraṇasāmānyena kāryaviśeṣa iti pravādaḥ | tatrāyaṃ kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā kāryasāmānyaṃ vyāptamitibruvāṇaḥ pramāṇāvaṣṭambhena nāma prasiddhimullaṅghayet |
[293,1]
tacca pramāṇaṃ vyāptisādhakaṃ dvividhameva pratyakṣānupalambhaṃ vā, viparyayabādhakaṃ vā, anayoḥ pratyakṣānumānasvabhāvatvāt, anyato niścayāyogāt | tatra tāvaduktakrameṇa kāryasāmānyasya,
[293,2]
no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśād vyāptiḥ samastasya ca pratyakṣānupalambhato na tadatajjātīyabhedaspṛśaḥ | prāgbhāvādiniṣedhapūrvakatayā dhūmādivajjanmadhī ranvetīdṛśamīdṛśāditi yataḥ sāmānyabhedadvayam ||
[293,3]
idamupalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptamanupalabdhamasyopalambha upalabhyata ityevaṃ hi pratyakṣānupalambhayorvyāptigrahaṇakramaḥ | tatredamityekajātīyatayā ekapratyavamarśapratibhāsi dhūmādikamanekakāryajātyantaravyudāsenānekakāraṇajātyantaravyudāsena cāsyeti vahnyādeḥ ityarthaḥ | tataḥ kāryakāraṇayoḥ pratyekaṃ tajjātīyetarayoritaretarato bhede parāmarśapūrvikā pravṛttiḥ, anyathā sāmarthyavaiyarthyābhyāmanupayogāt |
[293,4]
tathā hyakāryarāśivyavacchedena vā, kāryāntaravyavacchedena vā idametad bhāvābhāvānuvidhāyītyavadhāryeta ? ādye pakṣe etāni vastuni etanniyatāni ityayamartho naitadvastviti, ekākāravirahādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteḥ | nanu kāryatvādinā sāmānyena idamiti kāryaṃ sanniveśo vetyādi vaktuṃ śakteḥ, asiddhametaditi cet ? ucyate, iha bhāvābhāvavidhānabuddhirdvidhā saṃbhavati, dharmiviṣayā dharmaviṣayā ca, kāryasya nirvarttyavikāryabhedena dvaividhyāt | tatrādyā sarvātmanotpattiniścayamupādāya dharmiṇameva viśiṣṭākārakroḍīkṛtaṃ kāladeśādibhedabhinnamapi svabhāvamantarbhāvyaikapratyavamarśād viṣayīkarotīti tadviṣayetyucyate | sa hi saṃbhavinamapyatadākārabhedavirodhinaṃ dharmamudāsayati, dhūmādiṣu dhavalatādivat |
[293,5]
yatra punaravasthitasyaiva dharmiṇo dharmāntaramudayamāsādayati, tatra dharmamātrasyaiva hetubhiranvayavyatirekāviti dharmaviṣayetyucyate | sā punarākāramevodāsayantī dharmamātram adhiṣṭhānīkaroti rāgādivat | na hyākārakriyādivaijātyamatyantamanubhavantaḥ paṭakūṭādayaḥ sādhāraṇarāgayogino gṛhītasāmarthyarāgadravyāntarayogamanumāpya tṛpyanti | prathamā tvākāraśaraṇaiva sarvātmanotpatteḥ | yathaiva hi viśiṣṭākāroparaktaṃ vastu kutaścidupajāyate tathaiva tadvalotpannenendrijñānenānubhūyānantaraṃ vikalpadvāreṇa vyavahāragocarīkriyata iti kathamākāraparihāraḥ ? ataeva dhūmakumbhādivyaktirekatrānupalabhyaprabhavā upalabhamānasya anyatra tadaiva yadyuktibhedena vyāptisiddhistatraiva tatkāraṇāvasāyo jāyate, nānyatra vyabhicāradarśanādarśanamapekṣyāpi | anantaraṃ tvākāramudāsayet kevalaṃ vyavasthite dharmiṇi dharmamātrodayadarśinaḥ |
[294,1]
na ca vyavasthite kumbhādau kāryatvādidharmamātrotpattirīkṣyate, kṣitidharādau vābhyupeyate, yenākāramanādṛtya rāgavattanmātrameva hetumanumāpayet | sanniveśastarhi sthita eva tadātmani kumbhakārāditi cet — na, drāgapi saṃsthānavinākṛtāyā mṛdo'nupalabdheḥ |
atha tādṛśasyābhāva eva pūrva yaḥ kumbhaprajñaptigocara iti cet ? tadeva saṃsthānaṃ tarhi puruṣāditi na tāvanmātravyāptiḥ,
[294,2]
tathāpi yadi saṃsthānasāmānye puruṣakriyā | haridrādravyayogo'pi varṇamātravidhāyakaḥ ||
[294,3]
nanu tathāpi na pūrvasiddhadarśanamityeva vyaktyantare gṛhyamāṇāyā vyāptervyāghātaḥ, tadvalāttvanumānameva tatretyanantarameva samarthitam | na ca tāvatā varṇamātraṃ kusumbhasaṃbhavasādhanasādhu, vyabhicārālambanaṃ tu durbalamiti kimatra prāptam ?
[294,4]
guṇe'pi dravyavat tasmāt sajātīyaparigrahaḥ | tatpūrvasiddhe'pyanumā na varṇāt kuṅkumasya ca ||
[294,5]
tanniyataviśeṣāparigrahe hi rāgādapi kutaḥ kuṅkumānumā ? davīyasī tu varṇamātrāt | varṇavacca saṃsthānasyāpi vicitrameva vaijātyamanubhavaviṣayaḥ | tadanayorekatra jātiniyamena vyāptivyavasthānamaniyamena vā vyaktau vyabhicāro naikaniyataḥ | tasmād varṇavadanekajātini saṃsthāne'pi tattvaṃ sāmānyamanuvartamānamapi vyāptigrahād bahirbhūtam eva | evamarthakriyāpi pūrvamasati vastuni puruṣāditi vaktumaśakyam | sarvasāmarthyavirahiṇaḥ prāgabhāvaprasaṅgenāpūrvotpattiprāpteriti viśiṣṭe vārthakriyāpi puruṣānvayavyatirekānuvidhāyinīti siddham |
[294,6]
tasmādevaṃvidhā dharmaviṣayāpi vyāptibuddhirna sāmānyamanudhāvati | yadā tu kāryahetvadhikāreṇa dharmiviṣayaiva, tadā yathāparidṛṣṭākārārthakriyāsāmānyaṃ samāśritya yathā kāraṇe pratiniyatasvarūpasāmānyena vyāpakatvāvasāyinī, tathā kārye'pi pratiniyatākārasāmānyapuraskāreṇaiva vyāpyatvāvasāyinī samakṣabuddhiriti na sandehaḥ |
anyathā kāryavat kāraṇe'pi buddhimadādiviśeṣavyudāsena pravṛttimatī matiḥ kimabhimatam upanayet ? tasmāt kāraṇavat kārye'pi tathābhūtākāraviśeṣamevamayamavasātumarhati |
[295,1]
tatredānīṃ tadākārabahirbhūteṣu bhūtalādiṣu sadapi kāryatvamabhidhīyamānamanupayuktameva, dharmaviṣayahetuphalagrāhipratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā dharmamātrasāmyasyākiñcitkaratvāt |
na hi tadevākārārthakriyādirūpaṃ tatsāmyonmīlanaheturvā | tadanena sāmyaṃ na kiñcidartha puṣṇāti agauṇakāryaśabdapravṛtteranyatra | sa hi saṅkalpaniveśinyudayārthamapekṣitaparavyāpāramātre arthe akārādikamudāsya kṛtasamaya iti na tasya vyāghātaḥ | upapattyantareṇa vyāpakatayā yaḥ pratīto dharmaḥ tatraiva nāśavatpratyakṣavyāpāra eva tu svodayasamayaparisphuradākārādisādṛśyamapekṣate, deśādikṛtabhede tu vaisadṛśyāvasāya iti na virodhaḥ |
[295,2]
tasmādekakāraṇavirahāt pratyekaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhāpekṣāyāmetāni vastūni etatkāraṇānugāmīnītyanenaivākāreṇa vyāptiniścayaḥ kāryaḥ | kevalamadyāpi na vyaktikārtsnyenopayoga iti sarvakāryaprakāreṣvekaikaviṣayo'vatiṣṭhate | sa cāśakyaḥ kramayaugapadyābhyāmayogāt | tathā hi na tāvat sakṛdeva teṣāmanvayaḥ, sarvaprakāropanipāte darśanasya draṣṭurevāntardhānaprāpteḥ | vyatireko vā śakyaniścayaḥ; aśakyaparihāratvāt keṣāñcidādhārālokaśarīrādīnām | nāpyekena narāyuṣā kṣamamidaṃ sarvaprakārekṣaṇaṃkāryasyāntaviyogataḥ katipayāpekṣāsu kārtsnyaṃ kutaḥ ?
na khalu bhūyaso'pi bhāgasyābhividhibodhe nirvṛttiḥ, na hi tadapi yadyat kāryaṃ tattadevam iti śakyamabhidhātum, etāvaditi tu syāt |
[295,3]
yatpunarekatra pravṛtto vicāraḥ sarvabhāvāṃstathābhāve vyavasthāpayatītyucyate, tatsādhāraṇākārapravṛttimadhikṛtyākṛtyādivyudāsena pramāṇāntarāvalambanāt | pratyakṣavyāpāra eva hyekajātigrahaniyama uktaḥ | nanu tatrāpyavāntarānekabhedasaṃbhavādayamevam ityabhidhātumaśakteranāśvāsaḥ | atra vā bhedatiraskāreṇa dhūmādijātyantaramavalambya saṃvyavahāre kāryatāmāśritya jātyantareṣvapi kīdṛśo doṣa iti cet ? na vayaṃ svecchayā kañcidbhedaṃ tiraskurmaḥ, puraskurmo vā kāmapi jātim | adhyakṣapūrvakastu saṃkalpo yathā arthānupasthāpayati bhedenābhedena vā, tathā hetuphalabhāvavyavahāramavatarāmaḥ | sa tu prakṛtiviśeṣamāsādya yadi sūkṣmasthūlabhāvena bhedeṣvabhibhūtisāmarthyāsāmarthyābhyāṃ bhinatti vṛttim, kimatra kaiścitkartavyaṃ tadvivartastu cintyaḥ | tatra,
[296,1]
dhūmo'vāntarabhedavatyapi yathā jātyantarāpohitaṃsārūpyaṃ viṣayīkaroti hṛdayaṃ kiṃ kāryamātre tathā ||
[296,2]
ekasaṃsthānādyanugamānanugamayoḥ, pratyātmavedyatvāt nāparamatra prārthyate nirṇayanibandhanam, anyathā ca vyapadeśārthakriyāviniyogādisaṃkaraprasaṅgaḥ | tasmānna kvacit kāraṇe sarvakāryaprakāraṇāṃ krameṇa yaugapadyena vā adhyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhavā vyāptirupapādayituṃ śakyeti kimābhyām ? ata evaṃmukhena sarvakāryavyāptivādinaḥ svābhiprāyanivedanamātrametad, vartmani sthāṇūpadeśaghoṣaṇavat | tathā ca sati icchāmātraṃ sādhanam astviti sphuṭamanayorapārthakatvam | tasmādābhyāmata idamiti matiḥ kāryāntaravyavacchedenaiva bhavantī na kāryamātragocarīkaraṇasaṃvādamāsādayati | tato niścayamupādānādivido'panudannāha —
[296,3]
saṃśayo'thaveti ||
[296,4]
pareṣṭasiddhirna parasya bādhane prasādhane vedanayatnamātrayoḥ | ananvayo'bhīṣṭaviśeṣasādhane vipakṣasandehasahaṃ tu sādhanam ||
[296,5]
sādhye ca dṛśye vyabhicāra eva dṛśyaṃ na cenna vyatirekasiddhiḥ | na cānvayo'pi vyatirekavad vā vyāptirviśeṣeṇa na cetarasya ||
{7.4.3}
<tṛtīyaḥ khaṇḍaḥ>
[297,1]
evaṃ sati satyapi vyāptiraśakyaniścayā saṃbhāvyata iti kimatra sāmpratamiti cet ? paśya,
[297,2]
