kāryaṃ tāvadanekajāti, janakaścaiko jaḍo vīkṣate nānābhedavato na caikaniyamajñāne'nyabhede'pi tat | yadyajjātikamekahetuviditaṃ tattattadaṅgaṃ tato naivaṃ cedatisañjanaṃ na ca mataḥ sādhyopame'yannayaḥ ||
[297,3]
na hi nānāprakārakāryajananaṃ nāma prayatnavatyeva niyatam, vahnyāderapi vividhasāmagrīmadhyamadhyāsīnasya dhūmabhasmāṅgārāṅgatāpapākapāradotsāraṇavīkṣaṇakṣatiprabhṛtivicitrakāryakriyādarśanāt | yadi paraṃ prayatnavato'dhiṣṭhānenetyatra vivādaḥ, na caikasya tatra niyame jñāte kāryāntare'pi niyamajñānamupapadyate, yathoktaṃ prāk | tato yāvantaḥ prakārā ekahetavo niścitāḥ, tāvantastasya hetoścetanasyetarasya vā sādhanaṃ yujyante | anyathā stimitendhanasakhena śikhinā gṛhītadhūmavyāptiraparicitatatkāryabhāvairbhasmādibhirapi dahanamanuminuyāt | na caivaṃ, tasmāttajjātibhedo vyakto vyāptigrahaśca pṛthak pṛthagapekṣyamāṇo yatra kvacittadgrahaṇena yena kenacidanumānamunmūlayati |
[297,4]
kaḥ punarevamāha, yatra kvacidgṛhītavyāptiryena kenacidanumimītāmiti, ekadharmānuvṛttivirahe hetorevābhāvāt ? na hi tadā bhasmasādhanamavyāpteḥ | nāpi dhūmo'siddheḥ |
kuṭakūṭādau kāryatvamevānyadharmānanuvṛttāvapyanumāne vartamānaṃ hetuḥ syāditi cet — na, kāryatvasyāpi prāgavyāptervistareṇa sādhanāt | tatra yathā kulagiriḥ kulālavyāpārakāle svabhāvavaikalyādikalitaniyamaḥ, tathā sadapi kāryatvaṃ prāmāṇyapravṛttyā dhūmajanmanīva rāsabha iti pramāṇena vyāptigrahavirahe na kaścidviśeṣaḥ | tadayaṃ ghaṭādau kāryaviśeṣe gṛhītavyāptiḥ sarvato na kāryatāmātreṇa vā vyāpakamanumātu | na tu vyāptigrahaṇasādhanavyavasthayorbhinnādhikaraṇatāmatikrāmatīti kathamatiprasaṅgopālambhaparihāraḥ ?
[297,5]
tasmānnaikadharmānuvṛttimātreṇopayogaḥ | kena vā dhūmasaṃbhavinaḥ kāryatvavastutvādayo bhasmani bhasmasādeva kṛtāḥ ? santo'pi vyabhicāriṇa iti cet ? nanu savyabhicāro vyāptiviyogādeva, vyāptau tadgandhasyābhāvāt | sa ca vyāptyabhāvaḥ kāryatvenāpi avarjita iti tatrāpi vyabhicāro durnivāraḥ | āhatyādarśanaṃ tu viprakarṣādapi syāt |
na tāvatā tadabhāva eva, tanmūlabhūtāyā avyāptestādavasthyāt | yadi tu vyāptāveva savyabhicāraḥ, tadā nitarāmavyāptāvityalaṃ mithyābhiniveśena | tad yadyapi sādhāraṇadharmā tanmātraṃ vyāptimanādṛtya sādhanamiṣyate, kiṃ na bhinna evaṃ bhūdharādisādhāraṇaṃ dharmam anādṛtyetyatiprasaṅgastadavasthaḥ ?
[298,1]
nāpyayaṃ nayaḥ sādhyasamānīkṛte kalasādāvapyasti, tatrāpi yathāyathā pratisaraśarābodañcanādiṣu kumbhakārakṛtimupalabhāmahe, tathātathaivamapīdamapyanena sṛjyata iti pratiyantaḥ paricitakriyebhya eva prakārebhyastadvyāpāramavadhārayāmaḥ, anyathā taddoṣānativṛttiḥ | tasmād yadi paramārthataḥ prayatnavannāntarīyaka evāyaṃ sakalaprakāraḥ kāryagrāmaḥ, tathāpi svayamakiñcitkara iti pramāṇavṛttyapekṣayā, siddhaṃ yādṛgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat | sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmād yadanumīyate || (pra. vā. 1. 13)
iti || yaddṛṣṭerakriyādarśino'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavati, śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādivat sanniveśādi, tādṛgeva yadīkṣyeta tannagādiṣu dharmiṣu | yuktaṃ tatsādhanādasmādyathābhīṣṭasya sādhanam ||
taccāsiddhamityākūtam |
[298,2]
nanu bhavatyevāsmākaṃ sarvatra pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ, kṛtabuddhiḥ sā, sādhyabuddhirevānumānam iti niyamaḥ, kathañcit kasyacittatrāpyabhāvāt | kiṃ ca kṛtabuddhiriti kāryamātrabuddhirvā, puruṣamātrabuddhirvā ? yadi kṛtamātrabuddhiḥ, sā bauddhasyāpi siddhā sindhubhūdharādiṣu | sāvayavatvācca tadārambhasaṃbhavitvameva kṛtatvam | atha pauruṣeyabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhiḥ ?
sā sādhyabuddhirevānumānamiti cocyate, tatastadabhāvānnānumānamiti kathamucyamānaṃ nopaplavate ?
[298,3]
yadāha, na ca vyāmohāt kasyacit sādhyabuddhyabhāve hetorasiddhatādoṣaḥ, sarvānumāneṣu tadbhāvaprasaṅgāditi | yadapīdamucyate, tādṛkkāryatvādi niṣiddhamacalādiṣviti, tatrāpi na kāryatvādinā kailāsakalasādeḥ kiñcidviśeṣamupalabhāmahe | āha ca, nāpi kaścidviśeṣaḥ kṣityādihetūnāṃ prāsādādihetubhyo yenāmī nirabhiprāyāḥ santaḥ prayatnanirapekṣāḥ pratiniyamavatā ca vyāpāreṇa tadvantaḥ syuḥ, na hyanadhiṣṭhitānāṃ prayatnavatā karaṇadharmāṇāṃ kriyāsu svātantryamupalabdhipūrvam, sarvatra buddhimadadhiṣṭhiteṣveva prāsādādiprasavopalabdheriti ||
[299,1]
atrocyate, neyaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ siddhāntābhiniveśavāsitabuddhīnadhikṛtya kīrtitā, kiṃ tu saṃvyavahārapragalbhapuruṣamātrāpekṣayā | tasya ca pūrvapratītapratibandhasmaraṇavataḥ kāraṇaparāmarśavaimukhyābhāve bhavatyeva devakulādau tādṛśī buddhirna tu malayamakarālayādau |
tadanayorasyā dhiyo bhāvābhāvau na jātibhedamavyavasthāpya sthātuṃ prabhavataḥ, dhūmadvayadarśane'pi tathābhāvaprasaṅgāt | iyaṃ ca kāmaṃ sādhyabuddhireva, kaḥ punarenāmetadvato'numānanibandhanamāha, tadabhāvād vā bhūdharādau tadabhāvam ? kiṃ tu jātibhedamātropalakṣaṇārthamasyā bhāvābhāvopanyāsaḥ samānajanāpekṣayā kasyacid durvidagdhabuddheḥ pratibodhasādhanāya |
jātibhede hi tāvati siddhe naikatra pravṛttamadhyakṣānupalambhamanyatra pratibandhasādhanasamarthamiti vaktuṃ samarthaḥ syāt |
[299,2]
tato nāpratibaddhāt sanniveśādeḥ sādhyasiddhiḥ, pratibaddhaścāsiddha iti kathamanumānamityantato'numānaniṣedhāyopanyāse'pi naikasyaiva tadabhāvāttadabhāva ityuktaṃ bhavati | nanu tathāpyanyasyānumānodayābhāvādanyasyāpi na bhavitavyamityuktaṃ bhavati |
tacca kathaṃ saṅgatimālambeta ? uktaṃ hi, na ca vyāmohādityādi | tadayuktam | samānasādhanasāmagrīsaṃbhave sādhyasyaikapratiniyamānupapatteḥ | yad yena viśiṣṭasāmagrīkaṃ tat tenāviśiṣṭaphalameva, yathā sādhāraṇadhūmasādhanendhanadahanādisamudāyaṃ pradeśadvayam anyonyam, aviśiṣṭānumānasādhanapratibandhagrahaṇādisāmagrīkaśca bhavatā saha sāṃvyavahārikaḥ puruṣa iti svabhāvahetuḥ prasaṅgaḥ | bhavato'pi hi pratyakṣānupalambhameva pramāṇaṃ pratibandhasādhanaṃ devakulasūtradhārādyadhikāreṇa pravṛttam | etacca parasyāpi sādhāraṇam |
asādhāraṇaṃ tu viparyayabādhakapramāṇameva durabhyūhatayā bhavet | tacca bhavato'pi nāstīti prāk prakāśitam |
[299,3]
tad yadi svamatābhiniveśamātramanubhavato nāvṛṇoti cetaḥ, kiṃ tu tadeva sādhanam itarasādhāraṇam, tadā tasyāpi śūnyanagaraparidṛṣṭadevakulādivanmerumandarādāvapi pauruṣeyānumānamanivāryam | na caivam | tato yasya yatpratibandhagrāhakapramāṇavyāpāre yathāvatsmaraṇavato yaddarśanānna tadanumānaṃ na tasya tatra pratibandhaḥ siddho, yathāgnau dhūmapratibandhasyānusmarato gardabhadarśanādagnimananuminvataḥ | na bhavati ca cetanena devakulādipratibandhasmṛtimato malayahimālayādau puruṣānumānamiti kāryānupalabdhiḥ smaraṇakāraṇānusaraṇavaimukhyādipratyayāntarasaṃbhave prācīnapratibandhasādhakapramāṇena viṣayīkaraṇavaikalyaṃ sādhayati | tacca na jātibhedātiśayamantareṇāvāntarabhedavato'pi, dhūmād gardabhavat |
[300,1]
vyāptigrahaṇasmaraṇayoraparādhe tu neyamiṣṭasiddhiḥ | tadarthaṃ yathāvadgrahaṇam | tatra smaraṇāparādhe devakulāntarādapi nānumimīta, grahaṇāparādho'pi pratyakṣāpekṣayā'saṃbhavī, ekapratyavamarśayogyatāyā evābhāvādityukteḥ | anyathā jaladharādyarthino'pi kumbhakārasūtradhārādīnapekṣeran | apekṣata eva tatrāpi sūtradhārasthānīyo'nyo yathā kumbhakārasthānīyaḥ kvacit sūtradhāra iti cet — na, kāryajātivaisadṛśyābhāve kāraṇasāmarthyavaisadṛśyāpekṣānupapatteḥ | anyathā kumbhāntare'pi na kulālamātreṇa toṣamaśnuvota | tadvad vā kṛṣīvalaḥ kulālapauruṣāpaneyānāvṛṣṭikaṣṭaḥ syāditi siddha eva tādṛśo jātibhedaḥ, tasmādekākārapratyavamarśānupapatteradhyakṣasādhyā vyāptirviśiṣṭaviṣayatayā na durgrahadoṣamāvahati, yato'numānābhāve'pi jātibhedātiśayasyāsiddheḥ siddhasādhanadoṣaḥ syāt |
[300,2]
tataśca yathāvad grahaṇasiddheryatra nānumānaṃ tatra vyāpterevāgrahāditi nānekāntaḥ | kathaṃ punaranumānahānameva tādṛśi lokasyāvagantavyamiti cet ? uktādeva jaladharārthino'pi kulālajaṅghāmardanaprasaṅgāt, paracakrākrāntikātarasya vā kulagirijaladhivyavadhimabhilaṣataḥ, cetanamātreṇa vyāptiṃ pratīmo na kumbhakārādyavasthāniyatena tena nāyaṃ prasaṅga iti cet ? tadavasthāniyatenaiva vyāptigrahe kīdṛśo doṣa iti kimatra vaktavyam ? na ca samayāpakṣālakalāṅkitadhiyaṃ bhavantaṃ prati kāciccintā, api tu lokaṃ prati | so'pi vyabhicārānna tena pratipadyate iti cet ? evaṃ tarhi kalasāntarādapi nānumānamayaṃ kuryāt |
[300,3]
anyatraiva vyabhicāradarśanādatra ko doṣa iti cet ? tadetajjātivaisadṛśye'sati na labhyate | tataśca viśiṣṭāyāmeva jātau vyāptigrāhi pratyakṣaṃ pravṛttamato nānyatra tadvyāpārānumānamityevaṃ kiṃ nocyate, kimatra vyabhicāropakṣepeṇa ? avaśyaṃ ca pratyakṣasya pratiniyatajātivyavasāya eṣitavyo'nyathā vyabhicārāgocaramapi pratyakṣaṃ na niyatajātikamiti kalasāntaramapyāskandet | tathā ca sati sa eva doṣaḥ | vyāptigrāhiṇaiva kalasāntarasyādhiṣṭhitatvāditi cet ? nanu tadadhiṣṭhita eva viṣaye vyabhicāracāri cetaḥ pracarat kathaṃ tameva pariharet ?
[301,1]
ubhayorniyataviṣayatve tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ | kevalamidānīmadhyakṣeṇa viśiṣṭaviṣayasvīkārānna vyabhicāropanyāsaḥ saphalaḥ | vyāptigrāhiṇastu pramāṇasya viśiṣṭaviṣayapravṛttismaraṇādhānārthamupayujyate mūḍhaṃ prati | na tu parito visāriṇī vyāptigṛhītirasya niyataviṣayā kriyate vyabhicāreṇa | nāpyanumānakhaṇḍanamātramuktanyāyādeva | tasmād viśiṣṭaviṣayaiva vyāptiḥ kumbhakārādinā gṛhyate vyabhicāradarśanādarśanāpekṣyapratyakṣasyaikajātyapekṣayaiva pravṛtteriti siddham |
[301,2]
evaṃ cetanamātreṇāpi vyāptijighṛkṣāyāṃ vyabhicāro darśanābhāvāt yajjātini vastuni pratyakṣapravṛttistadeva tena vyāptaṃ sidhyatītyapi siddham | tat kathaṃ sāmānyena vyāptimabhidadhānaḥ samayānuvādamātreṇa nopālambhamarhati ? yadi tu puruṣamātreṇa vyāptiṃ jighṛkṣoradhyakṣapratikṣepeṇa pramāṇāntaraṃ śaraṇam, tadā naiṣa doṣaḥ | tattu vicāritam | yadi veśvaraprasādādasya vādino jagataścitrākāraparihāreṇa sarvatraikākāraṃ pratyakṣamudayamāsādayati, taccāsādhāraṇamiti na vyavahārāṅgam | saśarīrāśarīrayoḥ prayatnavatorna kaścidviśeṣaḥ karmadharmāpekṣayā pratyakṣeṇa vyāptigrahaṇe, yato jaladharārthinā kumbhakārānanusaraṇena tatkṛtānumānavirahānumāne prakārāntareṇāpi saṃbhāvanāyāṃ jātibhedaikanibandhanāpratibandhāt siddhasādhanaṃ punarapyāsajyeta | tato jātibhedakṛtastatrānumānābhāvaḥ saṃsidhyan pratiniyatajātipratibaddhamanumānamupapādayati |
[301,3]
viśiṣṭajātipratibaddhapauruṣeyānumānāsiddhau vā anubhavasiddhamapi jātibhedaṃ śāṭhyādapahnuvānaḥ paralokasya jātibhedanāntarīyakeṇa tathā pravṛttyabhāvasiddhena kulālādikṛtatvānumānābhāvena | anyathānumānodayaṃ prasajya jātibhedamāpādyate, yathā sthāṇukākābhyāṃ bhinnaḥ saṃyogo nāma yadi syād dṛśyo loko'pyenaṃ tṛtīyamīkṣeteti ucyate | tathā ca yadi yādṛśaḥ sanniveśo buddhimatpūrvako dṛṣṭastādṛgeva jaladharādāvapi syāt, lokasyāpi puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ syāt, ghaṭāntaravat |
[301,4]
na caivaṃ tajjātibhedakṛto'yaṃ vibhāgo'nyanimittābhāvādityuktaṃ bhavati | tataḥ kīdṛśaṃ punaḥ sanniveśādyadhiṣṭhātṛnāntarīyakaṃ siddhamityapekṣāyāṃ yaddarśanādakriyādarśinaḥ apītyādyucyate, paryāyaparikalitānekaprakāraparigaṇanagauravaparihārārtham, tatra puruṣakṛtabuddhiriti prayatnavadanumānaṃ vā kumbhakārādivyāpārānumānaṃ vetyubhayasyāpi saṅgateḥ prāguktakramāt | kevalaṃ prayatnavanmātraniṣedhasādhanasāmagrīkatayā kulālānumānābhāva eva liṅgam, tadvitsiddho vā vyāptigrahaṇābhāvaḥ | etacca parecchāmanupālya pallavitam |
[302,1]
lokastu yathādarśanānusārī yajjātikaṃ puruṣapūrvakaṃ paśyati, tattattādṛśā tanumataiva kṛtamavabudhyate, na tu śarīraviratisandehamapyullikhatīti samānamānavānumānaparyavasānaiva kṛtabuddhiravatiṣṭhata iti | yadāpi yadi kasyacit siddhivaśādāsurīṃ māyālim ālocayato'cale'pi kaścidullekho jāyate, kenāpi kairapi vā kaccit kṛto'yamapi bhavediti, tadāpi kenāpi karacaraṇāṅgoparakta evātyantaṃ pratibhāti | niścayastu sudūra eva | na caikajātitve tadupapadyate, dhūmakumbhāderivānalakulālādeḥ | na ca karacaraṇādivyāpāravirahiṇa ullekho'pi | na ca tāvatā kṣaṇikādivādino'numānāpalāpaḥ śakyate | adhyakṣapūrvavyāptigrahasahāyaṃ tu jātiviśeṣāpekṣavṛttikamanumānamubhayorapi sādhāraṇatvānna saṃbhavati laukikaparīkṣakayoriti brūmaḥ |
[302,2]
yadyapi ca dvitīyamapi laukikameva, tathāpi kaścidviṣayo'nabhyastatayā tīvratarābhyūhasāpekṣaḥ sūkṣmadhiyaḥ sāṃvyavahārikasyāpi saṃbhavati | tatra pratyakṣākṣamatve'pi vipakṣabādhakenānumānāntareṇa lokapratītimevāśritya gṛhītā vyāptiranumānaṃ prayojayed iti na kṣatiḥ, yathā yatrārthāpattighoṣaṇāviśeṣo lokasya | tasmāt sādhyabuddhirūpā kṛtabuddhirbhāvābhāvābhyāṃ jātibhedaṃ prasādhayatīti yuktameva | yadāpi kṛtamātrabuddhiḥ kṛtabuddhiḥ, tadāpi na doṣaḥ | tathāpi kṛtatvaṃ nāma svajanmanyapekṣitaparavyāpāratvam | tacca na tāvad vṛkṣādivat pratyakṣataḥ kṣitidharādiṣu siddham | parābhyupagamamātrasiddhaṃ tu svatantrasādhanādhikāre'naṅgameva |
[302,3]
tato'numānasiddhamāśrīyamāṇaṃ dṛṣṭasajātīyaṃ yathā kathañcid vāśrīyate ? antyapakṣe yadyanādyupādānaśaktisaṃtanyamānakṣaṇaparamparārūpameva kāryatvaṃ niyatadeśatayā vyavasthāpyamānaṃ sidhyet, tādṛśāt, kīdṛśī puruṣādhiṣṭhānapratyāśā ? dṛṣṭasajātīyaṃ tu tadaṅgamucitam | cetanācetanādhiṣṭhānakṛtaṃ viśeṣamavadhūya vitatānekakāraṇakalāpamilanalabhyodayaṃ hi puruṣavyāpāramākarṣedapi, milanasya tadadhīnādhyavasāyāt | acetanopādānatvamātramapi hi prācīnakrameṇa caritārthaṃ na prakṛtaṃ viśeṣamākarṣet | etadeva tu kāryatvaṃ loke viditam | tacca nācalādau siddhamiti kathamasiddhiparihāraḥ ? kevalaṃ na sākṣādasiddhisādhanamidam, kiṃ tu vijātīyatvasādhanārtham | na ca kāryatvamātramadhikṛtya, kiṃ tu sarvam |
[303,1]
tadayamarthaḥ, kiṃ tadadhiṣṭātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttisanniveśādisiddham, yaddarśanādakriyādarśino'pi lokasya kṛtabuddhirbhavatīti | tato yadi sāvayavā kṛtabuddhirapi bhavato bhavati, tathāpi lokasya nāstīti bhinnajātīyatvaṃ vyavasthāpyate | anyathā kumbhakārādināpi bhūdharādivyāpyaṃ pratīyālloka iti pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ | tato jātibhedādanyadeva pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāṃ puruṣakṛtaṃ pratītamiti siddham |
[303,2]
yattūktaṃ kāryatve na kaścidviśeṣa iti | atra sarvasādhāraṇadharmatve'pi kāryatvasya yadi pratyakṣasādhanā vyāptirabhimatā, tadā sadapi tadudāsīnamevetyuktaprāyam | yadi tu viśeṣamutsujyābhūtvābhāvamātrasya cetanāvyāptirvivakṣitā, tadā pratyakṣavyāpāramapyutsṛjya pramāṇāntaraṃ śaraṇamastvityapi | tadabhāve vā na kiñcit kāryatvena satāpi |
[303,3]
yadapyāha — nāpi kaścidviśeṣaḥ kṣityādihetūnāmityādi, tadapi grāmyajanadhandhīkaraṇamātropayogi na vivakṣitārthagatergatirbhavitumarhati | yathā pārthivatvena vajropalānāṃ lohalekhyatvaṃ sādhayan sandihāne prāha | nāpi kāṣṭhapāṣāṇādibhyo dambholīnāṃ kaścidviśeṣo, yenāmī pārthivāḥ santo lohalekhyatāvirahiṇaḥ syuḥ | na hyalohalekhyānāṃ kadācitpārthivatvamupalabdham | sarvatra lohalekhyatāsvīkṛteṣveva ghaṭaviṭapādiṣu pārthivatvopalabdheriti | tadvat prakṛtamapi vacanaracanāmātramābhāti |
[303,4]
yathā hi nirabhiprāyatvena sāmānyamanuyantaḥ sarve puruṣāpekṣakāryārambhabhājaḥ pratīyante, tathā pārthivatdhena lohalekhyatvasvabhāvabhājaḥ | yathā ca tathā bahudarśanaṃ vihāya nānyā gatistathā atrāpi | yathātra kimetallohalekhyatvaṃ pārthivatvamātrānubandhi, uta pārthivatve'pi kiñcidviśeṣamapekṣyeti śaṅkā bahuladarśane'pi, tathā kim acetanamityeva kāryakriyāsu cetanāpekṣamuta kriyāviṣayāpekṣayaiveti samānam |
[303,5]
kiṃ ca yadi dahanādiṣviva sūkṣmāvāntarabhedatiraskāreṇaikapratyavamarśayogyatāpekṣayā nāpi kaścidviśeṣa iti ucyate, kārye'pyaviśeṣaprasaktyā dhūmādivat saudhasādhanasyāpi kulagirikaraṇaprasaṅgo durvāraḥ | īśvarasvīkāre kadācidanyathāpi syāt, sarvadā viparyaye śālibījasyāpi śālyaṅkurakaraṇanirākaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ, saudhāntarakriyāniṣedho vā syāt | athātyantajātibhede'pi nirabhiprāyatvadharmamātrāpekṣayā ? tadapi biplava evāyam, na hi kvacit sādhāraṇo dharmo durlabha eva | nāpi tāvatā svabhāvaparabhāvo bhāveṣu viṣāmṛtayorekakriyāprasaṅgāt kimaniṣṭamasaṃśitānyeva vā saudhādisādhanāni aśakyaparihāranirabhiprāyatvaṃ sādhāraṇamavajñāya yayā svabhāvabhedādhiṣṭhānayā śaktyā kāryabhedamātyantikamārabhante tatkṛtaprayatnāpekṣāniyamaniṣedho'pi yadi syāt kīdṛśo doṣa ityarthapadametannāsti kaścidviśeṣa ityādi |
[304,1]
tasmādvividhaviśeṣavyāptigrahaṇaprakārasyābhāvāt śaṅkāyā anivṛtteḥ, svahṛdayasyāpi saṃpratyayākṣamatayā saṃbhāvanārakṣāmātramevaṃvidhaḥ pralāpaḥ | tato'vasthitametadadhyakṣasādhyapratibandhāpekṣayā yajjātīyaṃ sanniveśādi prayatnavatā vyāptaṃ siddham, na tad bhūdharādau asti, yādṛśaṃ cāsti na tadvyāptaṃ siddhamityasiddhiranekānto veti |
[304,2]
etena yadāha trilocanaḥ, nanu keyaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ kiṃ sādhanabuddhiratha sādhyabuddhiḥ ?
sādhanabuddhistāvad bhavatāṃ siddhaiva, karmajaṃ lokavaicitryamityabhyupagamāditi | athottaraḥ pakṣaḥ ? tenāyamartho bhavati, nedaṃ kṣityādiṣūpalabhyamānaṃ sādhyānumānasamarthaṃ kāryatvam, kiṃ tvanyadeva sādhyabuddhyajananāt | na caitad yuktam, sarvānumānocchedaprasaṅgāt |
dhūmādiṣvapi hi śakyamevedaṃ vaktuṃ nāyaṃ vahnyanumitisamartho dhūmaḥ kiṃ tvanyadeva sādhyadarśinaḥ sādhyabuddhyajananāt | tathā ca tāvat sādhanaṃ na sidhyati yāvat sādhyabuddhirna sidhyati, yāvat sādhyabuddhirna sidhyati tāvat sādhanaṃ na sidhyatīti sphuṭataramitaretarāśrayatvamiti tannirastam |
[304,3]
na hi sākṣādasiddhicodanamidam, kiṃ tu yato na vyāvahārikasya kṛtabuddhiḥ sindhvādau ghaṭādivyāptiṃ smarato'pi tato naikajātitvamiti jātibhedamātrasādhanamidaṃ syāt | tato viśiṣṭajātīyavyāptidvāreṇāsiddhiranekānto veti yuktameva | tatra ca kṛtabuddhyabhāvo nāma sādhyabuddhyabhāvaḥ sādhanabuddhyabhāvo vetyubhayamapi nirvyūḍham |
[304,4]
yadapi bhūṣaṇakāraḥ, kṛtakatvena ca pratītau kathaṃ na kṛtabuddhiḥ ? sarveṣāṃ prāsādādiṣu api kṛtabuddhirna bhavati, yathā cirantaneṣu prāsādādiṣu vyāptyabhijñasyaiva kṛtabuddhirbhavati, vyāptivimūḍhānāmakṛtabuddhireva, tathā kṣityādiṣvapīti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ |
puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ prāsādādiṣviva kṣityādiṣu na saṃbhavatīti cet ? kiṃ prasiddhāvinābhāvānāmutāprasiddhāvinābhāvānām ? prasiddhāvinābhāvānāmapi kiṃ vyāptigrahasmṛtivikalānām, athānyeṣām ? abhraṣṭasmaraṇānāṃ tāvad bhavatyeva puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ | loke api hi vicitraṃ jagat kenacid dhātrā nirmitamityasti pratītiḥ | vyāptigrahasmṛtivimūḍhānāṃ tu prāsādādiṣvapi keṣucinna puruṣakṛtabuddhirbhavatīti na tāvatā teṣāmapuruṣakṛtatvam |
[305,1]
api ceyaṃ vedeṣvapi puruṣakṛtabuddhirmīmāṃsakānāṃ nāstītyataśca tatrāpi puruṣakṛtatvasādhanāyoktā vākyatvādayopyasiddhāḥ syuḥ | kiṃ cānityatvasiddhyartha yatkṛtakatvasādhanamuktam, tadapyasiddhaṃ syāt | na hi yādṛśaṃ kṛtakatvādi ghaṭādiṣu dṛṣṭaṃ śrotrāgrāhyatvarūpam, tādṛśaṃ śabde'stīti | tasmād dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikavaidharmyametat sarvānumāneṣu samānaṃ neśvarānumānasyaiva bādhakamiti, tadapyetenaiva pratyuktam |
[305,2]
yatpunaḥ sādhyabuddhimadhikṛtya vikalpitaṃ kiṃ prasiddhānumānabhāvānāmityādi |
atra brūmaḥ | ya ekadā sūtradhārādivyāpāre devakulakalasādisaṃbhavamupalabhya kālāntare kalasādisaṃdarśanāt puruṣakṛtimanumimīte sa kīdṛśo vaktavyaḥ, prasiddhāvinābhāvasmaraṇavānna vā ? ādye pakṣe tasyaiva nācalādau puruṣakṛtabuddhiḥ, kulālānumānasyāpi prasaṅgādityupapāditam | tatkathamabhraṣṭadarśanānāṃ tadbhāvaniyamaḥ ? tata eva vicitraṃ jagadityādimatirapi na vyāptigrahasmaraṇabalāt, kiṃ tu darśanāntaraprabhavapravādavaśāt, tamaśṛṇvatāmabhāvāt, viparītavādavat |
[305,3]
vyāptivimūḍhānāṃ tvityādi siddhasādhanaṃ ca | udāharaṇamapi pāpīyaḥ, kṛtabuddhyabhāvasya jātibhedamātropadarśanaparatvāt | na ca vādipratibādyapekṣayā tadbhāvābhāvacintetyuktam, svayaṃ vā abhiniveśenānyathāpi saṃkalpasaṃbhavāt | pratyakṣāpekṣayā tu vyāvahārikādhikāreṇa cinteyam | tasya cāviditavedādisaṃketasya vaidikavākye tatpraticchandena ca racitamaparaṃ śṛṇvato nipuṇamapi nirūpayāṃś cintaya tāvat kīdṛśo viśeṣāvasāyaḥ, kalasakuliśādivat sarvaprakārāṇāṃ puruṣaiḥ kāraṇadarśanāt, pratyakṣasvabhāvānāṃ śabdānāṃ pratyakṣabhedakalpane dhūmādiṣvapi prasaṅgāt | tataśca,
[305,4]
yadbhāvaḥ puruṣānvayavyatiricostadbhāvabhājaḥ sthitā nānyasmād vacasaśca vaidikagirāṃ bhedo'sti śakyātmanoḥ | tulyātīndriyasūcanā ca niyataṃ naikatra cāśvāsanaṃ vedastena na pauruṣeyapadavīmaprāpya viśrāmyati ||
[305,5]
yadi tadā ko'vakāśastadbhāvasya pratyakṣamahāvaijātyeṣu śailādiṣu |
tadetadāyātam,
[306,1]
ekaḥ kāryaviśeṣameva kalayan hetorviśiṣṭaṃ nijaṃ lakṣyāgneriva kāryamātramamunā vyāptaṃ mudhā manyate | tajjātīyakameva kāryamaparo nāvaiti taddhetukaṃ hanta dhvāntaviśeṣa eṣa viduṣāmadhyakṣavastunyapi ||
[306,2]
na ca laukikavaidikavākyayorvaijātyasaṃbhave samayamātreṇa parājetavyo mīmāṃsakaḥ |
na ca pratyakṣākṣiptavyāptikaṃ vākyatvameva tatra śaraṇam | kṛtakatve tu yaduktaṃ tadapi cintitaṃ cintayiṣyate cānantaramiti | nanu tathāpi tadvyāpte'pi kārye kāryatvādi dṛṣṭam itaratrāpīti yathā ghaṭādi prayatnavannāntarīyakam, tathā pṛthvīdharādyapi syāditi cet ?
nanūktamatra kāryatvādi vidyamānamapi tatrāśakyavyāptigrahatayodāsīnameveti tenābhidyamānādapi kāryāntarānna yatnavataḥ sparśo'pi labhyate, kevalaṃ kāryaṃ kāryamiti śabdamātramabhidyamānamavaśiṣyate | tad yadi tadeva dvārāntareṇa śaraṇīkṛtamāyuṣmatā tatra sākṣād dūṣaṇāśravaṇāt, tadā tadapi kākabhakṣaṇaprāyamityādarśayannāha —
[306,3]
vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ | na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśane || (pra. vā. 1. 14)
[306,4]
etena yadapyuktaṃ, nāpyatra śabdasāmyādacetanopādānatvasya samāropeṇa sādhyasiddhiḥ, anityatvādinā kṛtakatvādiṣviva pratyāsatterihāpi vāstavatvāt | na ca jātibhedo dharmiṇordharmayoḥ sarvatra vāstavīṃ pratyāsattiṃ bhinatti, kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ śabdaghaṭajātibhedena pratyāsatterabhāvaprasaṅgāditi | tadapyanavakāśam | na hi nagādāvacetanatvasya sopādānatvasya samāropaṃ brūmaḥ | tanmātraṃ tu vyāptibahirbhāvādasatkalpamiti |
[306,5]
yadi cānyadevācetanopādānatvaṃ cetanāpekṣi siddhamanyadeva cācalādau dṛśyata iti kiṃkṛto'yaṃ vibhāga iti cet ? upādhikṛtaḥ | kiṃ na bhinnadharmiṇordharmayorapīti cet — na, vaiṣamyāt | acetanopādānaṃ dhūmasthānīyaṃ kāryahetvabhimānāt na ca kaścittasya dharmibhedādbhedamāha — yadā tvacetanopādānatvādacalādau cetanāpekṣatvaṃ vivakṣitam, tadā dhūmatvena dhūmo vahnimānityevaṃprāyā sthitiḥ | evaṃ ca sati dhūmadvaye dhūmatvayorbhedaḥ prasañjanīya iti kathaṃ sāmyam ? evamevāstviti cet — na, bhidyamāno hyupādhirupādhimantamapi bhindyāt | bhedaścaikapratyavamarśabahirbhāvalakṣaṇo na dhūmamupādhi spṛśati, yena svagataṃ bhinattu, yathā kumbhāmbhodharādiracetanatvopādānatvamityacodyametat |
[307,1]
nanu na dṛṣṭastāvaddharmibhedena dharmabheda iti cet ? yadrūpapuraskāreṇa pratibandhasādhakapramāṇavṛttistasyābhede bhidyamānāpi dharmijātirabhinnavadābhāsamānā na bādhikā |
tadbhede tu tadgataṃ dharmāntaramabhidyamānamapi bhinnavadābhāsamānaṃ na sādhakamiti nyāyaḥ | anyathā jaladharārthināpi kumbhakārasya paryeṣaṇāprasaṅgaḥ | tadapāye'pi vihāyasi balāhakodayadarśanānneti cet — na, tatprabhavasyaiva ghaṭasyeva tasya maruto kṣepaḥ kiṃ na saṃbhāvyate ? atha ca vāridhāritvamātramubhayatra dṛṣṭamiti yathā tatra saṃjñābhedamātrabhedo vyavasthāpyate, tathātrāpīti yuktam | pratibandhaniścayo hi pramāṇaviṣayasvabhāvaniyame sati bhavati, tadviruddhāniyamarūpaṃ ca sādhāraṇatvam |
[307,2]
pramāṇapratibaddho hi niścayastadviṣayasvarūpollaṅghe'pi bhavan pramāṇāpramāṇasādhyaḥ syāt | na caivam, tasmānnānekāntaḥ | nāpyasiddhiradhyakṣavyāpārānusārāt | tadiha pāṇḍutvasyāgnivyabhicāro dṛṣṭa iti dṛṣṭāntasya sādhyaśūnyatāniṣedha eṣaḥ | ata eva nānumānamiti pratibandhābhāvādaniścayaphalamidamubhayatra | na tu siddhavyāptikayordahanapāṇḍutayorvyabhicāreṇa sādhanavaidhuryam, vyāptisiddhāvanumānāṇvādasyāśakyasādhanatvāt vyabhicārasyaivāyogāt | sarvopasaṃhāravatī hi vyāptiḥ, tadbhāve tadbhāvaḥ kathaṃ syāt ?
[307,3]
tato'yamarthaḥ | yathā pāṇḍutvānnāgnimattve'numānaṃ tasya tatrāpratibandhāt | sa ca vyabhicāreṇābhivyaktaḥ | anyathā tatrāpyanumānamaṅgīkṛtyaiva svasthamāsīt | sa ca vyabhicāraḥ pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpetarasādhāraṇaṃ dharmaṃ sarvamapratibaddhatve niyatamādarśayatīti yathoktasādhāraṇatvākṛṣṭādapratibandhāt | tathaiva yathā kāryatvādimātrādapi na cetanādhiṣṭhānānumānamiti | ato vyabhicāradarśanamupakārakameva parasya | tasmāt pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpaparāmarśāt tathāvidhopādhikameva kāryatvādisādhanaṃ dhiya iti siddham | tathāvidhasya ca vāstava eva pratyāsattibheda iti saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇamāpatitam |
[307,4]
tena dharmijātibhedasya dharmabhedakatvaṃ siddhamapīti kathaṃ sarvatra tanniṣedhaḥ ? atha sarvatraiva yadbhedakatvaṃ tanniṣidhyate kvacidabhedakatvamapītyarthaḥ, tadā siddhasādhanam | uktaṃ hi pramāṇaviṣayasvarūpāpekṣayā tadubhayavyavasthānamiti | tathā ca sati bhedasthitireva, kṛtakatvādisparśaścāparibhāvakatayā kriyate | na hi tatrāpi pratyakṣabalād vyāptirupapādayituṃ śakyā, kiṃ tu viparyayabādhakānumānāt, tadabhāve'nanumānasyeṣṭatvāt |
[308,1]
tato'bhūtvābhavanābhidhānadharmamātrasya bhūtvābhavanena dharmeṇa vyāptisādhakaṃ dharmiṇo yadi jātibhedamudāsayati dhūmasyāgninā vyāptisādhakameva mahānasādi, tadā prastute kimāyātam yatra pratyakṣavyāpārāpekṣayā jātibhedaniṣṭhaiva vyāptigṛhītirītiriti ? yadi tu prakṛte'pi kāryavastustomagatāḥ kāryatvādaya eva dharmāḥ pratītavyāptayaḥ syuḥ, tadāyaṃ na doṣaḥ | kevalamupāyaprakāradvayasyāpyayogādayuktaiva vyāptiriti darśitam | tatra viparyayabādhakapramāṇaparicayasteṣāmasaṃbhavo, bauddhagandhereva kasyacit tathā yatnadarśanāt | na ca prakṛte vaktuṃ śakya iti tatrāsthāmavadhūya | pradeśāntare ca, nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vetyādinā (pra. vā. 3. 34)
karaṇamātre viśeṣatyāgena kāryamātrapratibandhaṃ viparyayabādhakabalena sūcayato nirvṛtiṃ vidadhāno bhagavān vārtikakāraḥ parasya darśanādarśanamātreṇa vyāptivādinaḥ tadyogapratipādane pratyāsannaṃ pratyakṣānupalambhabalāvalambanamavalokayan tadāhatya dūṣayituṃ jātibhedakṛtaṃ dūṣaṇamudbhāvayatīti veditavyam | tasmāt pratyakṣavyāpārāvadheyajātibhedasyātyantaṃ vyaktatvāt saṃjñāmātraṃ śaraṇīkriyamāṇamapyakiñcitkaramityuktam ||
[308,2]
athavā, astu ghaṭādyapekṣayā kṣoṇīdharādīnāṃ jātibhedo yataḥ — siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi ucyeta | krīḍāparvatādayastu pauruṣeyāstadekajātibhavāḥ, taiḥ sahaikahetavaḥ kiṃ na bhavanti ? tato'yamarthaḥ, yo yaḥ śailaḥ sa sarvaḥ pauruṣeyo yathā krīḍāśailaḥ śailaśca kailāsa iti | evaṃ kulyāmahāsarovaraprabhṛtayo nadīsamudrādīnāmudāharaṇānyūhanīyānītyāśaṅkyāha, vastubhede prasiddhasyetyādi, ayamarthaḥ, krīḍāparvatakādinirmitidṛśāṃ śailādiṣu jñānumānāpi nyāyasahā skhaladgati yatastannāmamātraṃ samam | kiṃ cānekasamānamānavakṛtāḥ sidhyantyamī cennagāḥ kā vārteśvarasādhanasya kimihopāttaṃ samāptaṃ ca kim ||
jātibhede siddhe'dhikaraṇasiddhāntanyāyānusāraḥ pūrayedapi pratyāśām, abhede tu tadapi nirāspadam | na hi sajātīyakumbhāntare tadvijātīyasya nirmātuḥ siddhirityanubhavāt abhyupagamād vā bhinnaiva jātiranayorna samānaṃ hetumāvahati saṃjñāmātrasāmye'pīti |
[309,1]
kaḥ punarayaṃ niyamo ya uktaprakāradvayenaiva vyāptigraho nānyathetyāśaṅkyāha, anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit | ghaṭādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyed valmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ || (pra. vā. 1. 15)
iti | na hi sudūramanusaratāpi sa kaścitpratibandhasādhanavidhirlabdhavyo yaḥ kumbhakāreṇa mṛnmayamātravyāptiprasaṅgaparihārakārī prayatnavatā kāryamātravyāptiṃ sādhayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ |
kumbhakāreṇa hi kāryamātravyāptisādhanāya prabhavatastadviśeṣamṛnmayasya sādhane kaḥ śaktivyāghātaḥ ? astu vā prakāradvayenaiva vyāptigrahaḥ | yattūktam, no bhedena vipakṣabādhakavaśādityādi tato'nyathā bhaviṣyatīti āśaṅkya jaladharārthinā kumbhakāraparyeṣaṇāprasaṅgamuktameva prakārāntareṇa saṃbhāvayannāha,
[309,2]
anyathetyādi |
[309,3]
yadā hi bādhātmakoddeśenāpi pravartamānaḥ sāmānyenaiva vyāptiṃ sādhayati, tadā kuto mṛnmayāt kulālānumānaṃ kuryāt kāraṇamātrasya siddheḥ ? yadāpi pratyakṣāpekṣayā hetuviśeṣeṇa kulālena karaṇavyāpāropadheyaviśeṣasya kumbhādikāryaviśeṣasya vyāptistadāpi kutastatprasaṅgaḥ ? yadāpyadhyavasāyamātrāpekṣayā sāmānyena viśeṣasya tadāpyayaṃ dūrataraḥ |
evaṃ tu vyavasthāto'nyathāvyāptigrahaṇe viśeṣeṇa sāmānyasya bhavatīti kathaṃ mṛnmayāt kulālānumānamaprasaṅgi ? tatkāryakumbhādyapekṣayā atyantavisadṛśādapi prasaṅge kathaṃ kiyatāpyaṃśena pratyāsannāt na syāt ? tathā caivaṃ sajātīyādapyavāntarabhedānusāripratyakṣavyavasāyāpekṣayā nānumānaṃ pratibandhāniścayāttadā kaiva vārtā vijātīyād ?
atyantavijātīye dṛṣṭavyāptikasyeti daṇḍāpūpanyāya eṣa iti darśayituṃ mṛnmayagrahaṇam |
[310,1]
nanūbhayathā vyākhyāne'pi vyabhicārādeva nānumānaṃ, tatkathamatiprasaṅga iti cet ? uktakrameṇopakāraka eva vyabhicāro'smākaṃ na bādhakaḥ | tathāhi pramādvayavyāpārātikrame'nantaraprakārabahirbhāve vā pratijñātapratibandhaniścayābhāvasādhaka eva vyabhicāra iti | api ca, vyabhicāro nāma sāmānyena gṛhītāyā vyāpterniyataviṣayāpekṣayā vighātamātanoti, atha vyāptigrahaṇameva tanna bhavatīti vibhāvayati, atha satyapi vyāptiprasare'numānamātraṃ khaṇḍayati, ataevābādhitaviṣayatvamapi liṅgalakṣaṇam ākhyātamiti pakṣāḥ |
[310,2]
tatra prathamapakṣe sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ, anyatrāpi tadbalādeva sādhyapratyāśā, sā ca niścitāpi khaṇḍitā kvaciditi anyatrāpi śaṅkānivṛtteḥ, tata eva tadgrahaṇavaiyarthyāt |
[310,3]
dvitīye tu na viśeṣaścetane | yathā hi kumbhakāreṇa kāryasāmānyasya pratyakṣeṇa vyāptirgṛhītā vyabhicāreṇa durgṛhītā vyavasthāpyate, tathā caitanyamātreṇāpi, tatrāpi pratyakṣavyāpāre viśeṣābhāvāt |
[310,4]
tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyāmeva vyabhicāreṇānumānamapāsyata iti mahīyasīyam ayogaparamparā | kevalamatra pakṣe etadāpatitaṃ yadīdamatra sādhanaṃ sādhyaṃ vyabhicarya na sthitaṃ tadā sādhyaṃ sādhayatīti | etacca sādhyavidhuraṃ sarvārthasākṣātkāriṇo nānyaḥ kartu śaktaḥ | sa hi ya eva dharmī tathāvidhamadhyamadhiśayito na bhavati tameva vā vyabhicāragocaratayā anumānabhājanīkaroti, sarvavipakṣānīkṣaṇe tu tanmadhya eva kadācideṣo'pi syāditi śaṅkā'nivṛtteḥ |
tasmādukta eva nyāya āśrayaṇayogyo vyabhicāraśca vyāptidurgrahaṇameva sādhayatīti kāryamātravyāptiḥ prakṛtakāraṇaviśeṣeṇāsaṃbhavinyeva sādhuriti | gṛhītāyāṃ vyāptau yadi vihatirāśvāsaviraho graho nāsau vyāpteryadi ca na viśeṣo matimati | abādhāpekṣāyāṃ na sakalavipakṣekṣaṇamṛte nirātaṅkastasmānna khalu phalamātre grahavidhiḥ |
iti saṃgrahaḥ | kiṃ cādāya samastavastuviṣayāṃ vyāptiṃ punaścenmatā tattajjātiṣu bādhakakramavaśātsvavyāpyatattatsthitiḥ | tattajjātiṣu sādhakakramavaśādunnīyate kiṃ na sā yenāyāsakaśaktisaṃśayapadaṃ santo viśantīdṛśam ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[311,1]
aparigaṇito nāma vastuvyāpāraviṣayo'parigaṇitatamastvaviṣayaḥ | tatra ka evamanātmīyakāryajātinikarasya pratyekaṃ vyabhicārān dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā svakāryajātiṣveva niyantuṃ hetumapāravyāpāraḥ pārayate ? tathā ca sati yasyaiva sākṣādanīkṣito vyabhicāraḥ tadeva tasya gamakamāśaktam | tadā śaṅkāsaṃbhavānneti cet — na, kvacidatīndriye tarhi niścayamayaṃ kuryāt | yajjātīyoddeśena pravṛttamadhyakṣaṃ sāmānyaviṣayamavasthāpitaṃ tatra kaḥ sandeha iti cet ? evaṃ tarhi parāparatadīyavyāpyajātiṣu tathaiva saṃśayapravṛttipratyanīkapramāṇavṛttyanusaraṇe āyātastṛtīyapādāpatito'rthaḥ | tasmānna kāraṇaviśeṣeṇa buddhimatā kāryamātrasya vyāptiḥ pratyetuṃ śakyeti, siddhaṃ yādṛgityādi siddhāntaḥ |
[311,2]
athavā yaduktaṃ na śarīranirapekṣaprayatnavanmātreṇa kāryasya vyāptiḥ pratipattuṃ pāryate, pratyakṣeṇa pratikṣepāt tādṛśasyetyādi, tadevopasaṃharati — siddhamiti yādṛkṣo'sau śarīrādiyogī adhiṣṭhātā ceti | śeṣaṃ subodham | tādṛśaśca pratyakṣabādhādidoṣaviṣaya ityākūtam | nanu śarīravatyapi cetanatvaṃ dṛṣṭamitaratrāpi saṃbhavati iti yathā śarīriṇā vyāptaṃ kāryādi sidhyati, tathābhimatenāpi ityatrāpi prāguktanyāyāt saṃjñāmātrādavaśiṣyamānāt sādhanamanorathamunmathnannāha, vastubhede kumbhādau prasiddhasya kulālāderyo vācakaḥ śabdaścetana iti tanmātrādabhidyamānasyābhimatasya pramāṇavyāpārāpekṣayā dūrīkṛtasya na yuktānumitiriti vyāptābhimatād vastuna iti prakṛtamarthāpannaṃ vā kathamivetyāha,
[311,3]
pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśana iti |
[311,4]
ayamabhiprāyaḥ, yadi śabdamātrasāmyenābhidyamānasyānumānaṃ śabdasāmyenābhidyamānādapi pāṇḍumnaḥ kiṃ na dhūmadhvajasyānumānam ? atha tatra viśiṣṭakāryasvabhāvāpekṣam adhyakṣamanyavyāptiṃ pratikṣipatīti nānumānamucyate, tathā cetanamātrapratikṣepeṇāpi pratyakṣaṃ kiṃ na tadanumānaṃ nirasyati ? etena yadā dṛśyamapi kāryāntaraṃ tiraskaroti pratyakṣaṃ tadā kaiva kathā dṛkpathātiriktasya cetanamātrasyeti ? astu tāvad vyāpyāpekṣayā vibhāga eva, loke tathaiva pratīteḥ, anyathātiprasaṅgācca |
[312,1]
vyāpakāpekṣayā tu yadyeṣa niyamo na syāt ko doṣa ityāśaṅkyā pūrvoktameveti prasaṅgaṃ bhaṅgyantareṇa taruṇayati, anyathetyādi | valmīkasyeti valmīkajantorityarthaḥ |
tatkṛtiriti ghaṭādikṛtiḥ | ayamarthaḥ, yadi viśeṣeṇāpi vyāptimavasāya cetanamātraṃ sāmānyamanumātavyam, tadā kumbhādikaraṇasya kulāle niyatasya cetanamātraparyavasitatvāt ghaṭāderapi valmīkajantuḥ kartānumeyaḥ syāt, yathāhi kumbhādeḥ kumbhakāreṇa vyāptigrahaṇe caitanyamātreṇāviśeṣāt tasyāpyanumānamevaṃ valmīkaukaso'pi caitanyenānyāviśeṣāt kiṃ nānumānam ? yadā ca śarīriṇā vyāptigrahe śarīriṇo'pyanyasya pratikṣepaḥ, tadā kā vārtātyantavisadṛśasyeti | na cātra bahutvenopayogaḥ, ekātmano'pi caitanyād iti valmīkasyeti nirdeśaḥ | etena dhūmāderapi jāṭharāderanumānākṣepo vyaktaḥ | vyabhicāracarcāyāṃ ca pūrvavat sarvamāvartanīyamiti ||
[312,2]
yaduktaṃ, prayatnavatā yadvyāptaṃ sanniveśādi tanna siddhaṃ sindhubhūdharādau, yacca siddhaṃ tanna vyāptamiti tatraitatsyāt, nanu jātyuttaramidaṃ dharmabhedavikalpanāt, tato yathā yatkṛtakaṃ tadanityaṃ ghaṭavaditi kṛte kaścidāha, yadi ghaṭagataṃ kṛtakatvaṃ hetustadasiddhaṃ śabde, śabdagataṃ tvanityasaṃghāte ghaṭapaṭādāvabhāvādviruddham | atha sapakṣavad vipakṣe'pi nāstīti matiḥ, tadā asādhāraṇamanaikāntikamiti | na ca tāvatā kṛtakatvaṃ tattvato'śaktameva anityatvasādhane, tathedamapi | tathāhi yacca siddhaṃ tanna vyāptamityanena sapakṣāvṛttervirodhaḥ, vipakṣādapi nivṛttipakṣe vā asādhāraṇatvamākṛṣṭamiti | atha prakṛtakāryānurodhād adūṣaṇamevedamudghoṣyate ? tathā sati kṛtakatvāderapi asādhanatvaprasaṅgaḥ sūtrakāravirodhaśca, kāryasamasaṃjñayā asya dūṣaṇasya tena pratijñānāt | yadāha, kāryatvānyatvaleśena yatsādhyāsiddhicodanam | tatkāryasamametattu tridhā vaktrabhisandhitaḥ ||
iti upacāramātrakṛttvenānyatvasya leśa uktaḥ, vaktrabhiprāyeṇa traividhyaṃ ca darśitamiti |
[313,1]
tadetadubhayamapyasāram, prathamapakṣasya tāvat pūrvameva pratikṣepāt | uktaṃ hi vyāptisādhakapramāṇapuraskṛtasvarūpasyābhede bhidyamānā api saṃbandhino vidhūtabhedā iva bhāsamānā na bādhakāḥ | tasya tu bhede abhedino'pi bhinnavadābhāsamānāḥ kāryatvādayo dharmā na tadvyāpakasya sādhakā iti | vyāptigrahaṇaprakramaśca dvividho darśitaḥ |
tatra yadi nāśena kṛtakatvasyeva viparyabādhakabalād buddhimatāpi kāryatvāderavinābhāvagrahaḥ syāt, tadā abhūtvā bhavanamātramiva sanniveśādimātramadhikṛtya pravṛttaṃ pramāṇamiti kastatra dharmibhedena bhindānaḥ sādhanaṃ śobheteti yujyate jātyuttaramiti |
[313,2]
yadi tu pratyakṣānupalambhavaśāt sanniveśādikamiva kṛtakatvamapi vyāptamavadhāryeta tadā śabde'pi sādhanatvaṃ kṛtakatvādeḥ kena nivāryeta, jātiviśeṣollekhenaiva pratyakṣānupalambhavyāpārasya pariniṣṭhitatvāt ? anyathā dhūmagatā api kāryatvādayo jātiviśeṣānavacchedena dahanāvinābhāvinaḥ sidhyanto nāśakyaparihāramatiprasaṅgamanupanīya svāsthyamāsādayeyuḥ | kāryāntarasya vyabhicāropakṣepo'pi kṣodiṣṭhaḥ pratividhiḥ | tadā hi yatraiva sākṣād vyabhicārānupalambhaḥ tadeva sādhanaṃ jātamiti kiyallādhavaṃ doṣabhārasya ?
[313,3]
na ca vahnikāryāntarādapi bhasmādeḥ svapnepyalabhyavyabhicārād dhūmaikakāryavyāptiṃ gṛhītapūrviṇastadanumānamastītyapi niveditaprāyam | tasmādanukrāntapramāṇāpekṣayā dharmijātibhedadharmāṇāṃ bhedaka evābhyupagantavya iti kathamucyate jātyuttaramiti ? nyāyavādinastu tu sūtrakārasya,
[313,4]
sādhyenānugamāt kārye sāmānyenāpi sādhane | saṃbandhibhedād bhedoktidoṣaḥ kāryasamo mataḥ || (pra. vā. 1. 16)
[313,5]
ayamarthaḥ | yadā tāvadviśiṣṭaviṣaya eva vyāptigrahaḥ pratyakṣavyāpāropekṣayā tadā saṃbandhibhūtajātyantarabhedāt kāryatvāderbhedoktirdoṣo bhavatu, nyāyaprāptatvāt | yadāpi vināśādinā sādhyena viparyayabādhakavaśāt sāmānyenābhūtvā bhāvitvamātramanugatam āsthāya sādhanamanuṣṭhīyate, tadāpi saṃbandhibhedād bhedoktidoṣaḥ kvaciddarśanāt pramāṇaparirītimanālocyocyate sarvakāryasamaḥ saṃmato'smadguroḥ | anyadā tu sādhanasya doṣa eṣa ityadoṣaḥ | nanu tathāpi sarvopasaṃhāravatī vyāptirna siddheti siddham | na tu tāvatā sādhyāsiddhireva, yadi paraṃ paramatānurodhena vyāptigraho nirvyūḍhaḥ |
[314,1]
asmākaṃ tu dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭameva rūpaṃ vyāptamavadhāryate yathā mahānasaparidṛṣṭaṃ dhūmaṃ dhūmadhvajādhīnamavadhārya sādhyadharmigataṃ sāmānyenānupraviśyāpi sādhyadharmiṇi dhūmam upalabhya yatra dhūmastatrāgnirdṛṣṭo yathā mahānasa iti evamagnimanumīmahe, tathā prayatnavatā ghaṭādijātīyamātrasyaiva vyāptisiddhāvapi yatra kāryatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatra prayatnavatā kṛtiriti vaktuṃ śakteḥ | tataścaivamapi sādhyasiddheravirodhāt ko'nurodhaḥ sarvopasaṃhāravyāptigrahaṇasya ? maulasādhanānarthakyasādhanasyeti cet ? evaṃ tarhi vyaktamidamāyātaṃ jātyantare vyāptimādāya jātyantarādevānumānamiti | yadi paraṃ vyāpyaliṅgayoḥ saṃjñāsāmyamapekṣya, tathā ca sati na vastuliṅgamuktaṃ bhavati | kevalaṃ kāryādiśabdavṛttimātrameva | taccāyuktamityādarśayannāha — prayatnavato, jātyantare prasiddhasya śabdasāmānyadarśanāt | na yuktaṃ sādhanaṃ gotvādvāgādīnāṃ viṣāṇavat || (pra. vā. 1. 17)
iti |
[314,2]
nanu kāryādīti na śabdamātram, abhūtvā bhāvitvasāmānyasyānugamasaṃbhavāt, gośabdastu svargādiṣu rucimātraśaraṇo na kañcidarthamanugamya vartate iti mahān viśeṣaḥ |
etadapi plavata eva, na hyabhūtvābhāvitvamātraṃ prayatnavannāntarīyakaṃ siddham, yena tadanugamasamāśrayaḥ phalaṃ syāt | siddhau ca punaḥ sa eva sarvopasaṃhāra iti kimanena parihṛtaṃ svīkṛtaṃ vā ? tasmāt tadapi sāmānyaṃ kāryajātibhedena bhedamāveśayato na kaścid vastvanugama iti śabdamātrameva sādhanamāśritaṃ bhavatīti paśyāmaḥ | tataśca na kaścid viśeṣo gotvena vāgāderviṣāṇasādhanādasyeti |
[314,3]
evaṃ dṛṣṭānte'pyayameva ślokaḥ | tadā ca jātyantara ityanyadhūmajanmani prasiddhasya vahneriti yojyaṃ, yadi sarvopasaṃhāraparihāraḥ | yadā tu sarvameva dhūmarūpamekākārapratyavamarśavaśādekīkṛtya vyāptimavadhārayati, tadā na śabdamātrasāmyam | sa eva vyāptaḥ artho'trāpīti na sādhyasiddhivirodhaḥ | nāpyevaṃ maulahetuvaiphalyopalambhasaṃbhavaḥ | na hi yatra yatra sādhanaṃ tatra tatra sādhyamiti sāmānyena pravṛttāpi buddhirabhimatadeśakālādibhedamāspadīkartuṃ prabhuḥ | ato viśeṣasya pravṛttinivṛttiviṣayīkaraṇāya na pakṣadharmamanālambyāsituṃ śaknuyāt | tat kathamaphalaṃ maulamaṅgam ?
[315,1]
tasmād vyāptigrahe sarvopasaṃhāraparihāriṇo'pi dhūmo'pi nāgneranumāpaka iti lābhamicchato mūlasyāpi nāśaḥ | na hi yatraiva dhūmajanmani vyāpṛto vahnirupalabdhastadeva deśāntare'pi, kevalaṃ so'pi dhūmaśabdavācyo'yamapīti śabdasāmyamavatiṣṭhata iti na gotvena vācaḥ śṛṅgasādhanādasyāpi kaścidviśeṣaḥ | nanu tathāpi kīdṛśī punariyaṃ vācaḥ śṛṅgasiddhiradhyakṣakṣiptatvāt svayameva hi, vyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ ityabhidhīyata iti cet ? satyamiyānapyabhyūhaḥ saṃbhavī bhavata iti mahān lābho'smākam | kadācidevaṃ pratiṣedhataḥ saṃjñāmātrato'pi sādhyasiddhipratyāśā parigalayatīti citraṃ cātra yacchāstrapariśramānurūpam, mānagraste girāṃ śṛṅge sādhanaṃ neti paśyataḥ | saṃjñāmātreṇa sādhyasya siddhiḥ kasmāt samīhitā ||
yanna gopālāṅganājanasyāpi sāmpratam, evaṃ ca samīhamānastadapi śraddadhīteti tadanurūpam uttaraṃ parihāsaparamabhidadhāno vacasi viṣāṇānumānena sakalamanucitānumānamātramupalakṣayati | yadā hi dahanādīnāmapi gardabhādibhyo'pi labhyāvakāśamanumānaṃ tadā kasya kasmādapratītirityākūtam, yadi paraṃ sākṣādadhyakṣabādhā mā bhūt ? nanu vyāptavastusādhāraṇābhidhānavṛttestadvyāpiniścayaprasaṅgaprakrame ko'vakāśo gardabhāddahanānumānasya ?
na hi dahanavyāptavastusādhāraṇā dhūmabhasmādiśabdā gardabhe saṃbhavina iti cet — na, vastvādiśabdenāpi śabdasāmyasiddherityetacca, pāṇḍudravyādivaddhutāśane ityanenaiva prativarṇitamantarṇīya pakṣāntareṇa toṣayannāha —
[316,1]
vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā | tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarvaṃ sarvasya sidhyati || (pra. vā. 1. 18)
[316,2]
etena gardabhādiṣvapi tāvadeva dhūmādiśabdānāmasaṃbhavo yāvanna samayasamīhā |
tato'numānābhāvo'pi dhūmādiśabdāpravartanāvadhika eva | pravṛttau tu kaḥ sādhyaṃ ruṇaddhītyuktam | na tvevaṃ vastuni sādhane | tathā hi, avinābhāvaviṣayānna vinābhāvasaṃbhavaḥ | vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā ||
vāśabdo yathārthe |
[316,3]
tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarvaṃ sarvasya sidhyati ||
[316,4]
na tu pratibaddhavastuvṛttitaḥ sādhyasiddhāvabhimatāyāṃ śabdādivat sarvasiddhiḥ ullaṇṭhamātraphalā, kiṃ tu tattvata eva vyāpakasya sarvasiddhiriti bhāvaḥ | tadevaṃ dṛṣṭāntadṛṣṭamātrasya vyāptivacane vacanasāmyamātraparatantrā siddhirasiddhirevāpatatīti tāttvikasiddhinibandhanavastusādhanānveṣiṇā sarvopasaṃhāriṇyeva vyāptirupapādayitavyā | sā ca dvidhāpi na sanniveśādibhyo buddhimato'numānaṃ mānabhājanīkaroti | tanmātrasiddhāvapi vā nābhimatā viśeṣasiddhiḥ, yataḥ śreyo'rthibhiratyarthamabhidhīyamānamīśvarābhidhānasya kovidairādriyeteti saṃkṣepataḥ prakaraṇārthaḥ | tasmāt sthitametat, tādṛśi pramāṇasaṃmate anitye'pyapramāṇateti ||
{8}
<kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddhiḥ>
[317,1]
pratyakṣānupalambhena trividhenāpi sidhyati | kāryakāraṇayorātmā pañcakeneti kecana || 1 ||
[317,2]
pratyakṣānupalambhasādhanaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāva iti nyāyaḥ | tatra sāmānyena prākpravṛttānupalambhasahāyamubhayaviṣayaṃ krami pratyakṣadvayam | yadi vā sāmānyenobhayagrāhipratyakṣasahāyaṃ kramikamanupalambhadvayamiti trividhameva tatsādhanamityeke | anye tu tat trayamantyadvayasahāyameveti pañcavidhaṃ niyatānupūrvīkamityāhuḥ | ādyatrayasaṃbhave'pi hi pratipatturnāsandigdhā buddhirupajāyate, antyadvaye tu labdhe sidhyati | anvayavyatirekalakṣaṇo hi hetuphalabhāvaḥ, tatra trayeṇānvayaḥ pratīyate, dvayena vyatireka iti pañcakena sādhvī siddhiḥ | tayorekaikāniścaye tu sandeho durnivāra iti bhāvaḥ |
[317,3]
atra cintyate,
[317,4]
prācīnānupalambhaścedanyataḥ saṅgamādikam | na niṣedhati, kiṃ tena niṣedhe paścimena kim || 2 ||
[317,5]
anupalambhadvayena vyatirekasādhanārthameva hyanupalambhaḥ prārthyate | sa cānena hetvabhimatābhāve kāryābhimatasya bhāvaṃ bādhamānena sādhanīyaḥ | sa ca bhāvastridhā saṃbhāvyate | tatraiva deśe sthitiḥ, anyata āgamanam, tadviviktakalāpādevotpattiriti |
evaṃvidhabādhāvaidhurye kimatra kāraṇamayamapekṣate ? na vyatireke'syopayogaḥ |
[317,6]
kiṃ tvanvayagrāhiṇi pratyakṣe sāhāyakamāvahatītyupadarśitameveti cet ?
[317,7]
asmin satīdaṃ bhavatītyakṣajena gataṃ na kim |
[318,1]
na hi bhāve bhāvādanyo nāmānvayaḥ | sa ca siddho'dhyakṣeṇeti kimatrānupalambhasāhāyyena ? nanvevamanvayo yadṛcchopanatasyāpi syāt pratyakṣamātrasaṃbhavāt | prāgabhāvagrahaṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ tadgrāhīti nātiprasaṅgaḥ sa tarhi trividhabhedabhinnabhāvaviparyayasvabhāvaḥ, prāgabhāvo'nupalabdheḥ, siddho'bhāvamātraṃ vā ? ādye pakṣe etadāyātam,
[318,2]
asmin satīdaṃ bhavati,
[318,3]
anyathā'saṃbhavāditi vyatireko'yameva saḥ || 3 ||
[318,4]
na sthitaṃ tatra nānyasmājjātaṃ nāyātamanyataḥ | yasya bhāve bhavet kāryaṃ na cettasya na kasyacit || 4 ||
[318,5]
etaccānupalabdhipūrveṇa siddhamadhyakṣeṇeti na kiñcit paścimadvayena | tadapi hi hetvabhāve phalasya tatra sthitimanyata utpattimanyayatnenānyatra gamanam bādhamānameva vyatirekasādhanam, na pāścāttyadvayamityeva, tadvyāpārābhāve śatenāpyabhāvāt | taccādimena ekena kṛtamiti nāparasyopayogaḥ |
[318,6]
atha punarabhāvamātramādimo'nupalambhaḥ pratyetīti matiḥ,
[318,7]
abhāvamātrabodhe'pi prācyasyānupayogitā | asyaitadvyāpṛteḥ prāgityevaṃ kimavaśiṣyate || 5 ||
[318,8]
abhāvamātrapratītau tāvat kasya kenānvayaḥ ? asya bhāve'sya bhāva ityapyanvayapratītiryadṛcchopanatenātiprasajyamānopayogaparipanthinyeva | etadvyāpārāt pūrvamabhāvaḥ asyeti tu pratītau saiva trayī gatirāyāteti kiṃ pariśiṣyate, yato'ntimadvayaṃ na vaiphalyamāvahet ?
[318,9]
anvaye vyabhicārācced vyatireko'nugamyate | pratyakṣamātravyāpāre'pyevaṃ kiṃ nābhidhīyate || 6 ||
[318,10]
yadarthamarthyeta prāktanaḥ anvayavyatirekau hi pratyekaṃ vyabhicārādeva sahitau hetuphalabhāva ucyate | tata ekaikasyātadbhāvinyapi saṃbhavo'bādhaka eveti samānamāvayoḥ |
tato nāntyayorādimasyopayogaḥ, ādye vāntimayoriti siddham | na siddham |
ādimena hi prāgasya vyāpārādetannāsīditi pratiyannapi etadvyāpārābhāvaprayukto'syābhāva iti nāvadhāritam, carameṇa tvavadhāryata ityayuktam, ādimasya punaranupayogasya tādavasthyāt |
[319,1]
api ca,
[319,2]
tanmātrābhāvato'bhāvāt paścimena viniścayaḥ || tannyāyasya samānatvāt prācyenāpi na kiṃ mataḥ || 7 ||
[319,3]
etadvyāpārāt prāg nāsīdityapi hi tanmātrābhāvādevābhāvaṃ khyāpayati, yathoktasattātraividhyavidhūterākṣepāt | tatastenāniścaye paścimenāpi mā bhūt | tatra pūrveṇa dvayoḥ abhāvasya sannidhimātram, naikasyānena prayuktiriti paśyataḥ paścime'pi ka āśvāsaḥ ?
tadanāyattau tadabhāve'pi utpattiprasaṅge dvitīyābhāvasyaivāyogaḥ samānaḥ | atha vahnirāsabhayorāgamanānantarajanmano'pi dhūmasya gardabhābhāve'pyabhāvaḥ prācyenānubhūyata ityucyate | ubhayāpagame'pagacchataḥ paścāttanenāpi, ityaparāparopāyaparamparānusaṇena pañcakavyavasthāhāniḥ | tathā sati trayaṃ, na dvayamiti cet ? paścimenāpi na śakyate ityetāvaducyate | sa tu dvayostrayorveti kimanena ? astyupayogo dvayasyānyasya apyabhāve niścayāyogāditi cet ? yadaiva tarhi kevale hetvabhāve'nupalambhastadaiva prācyaḥ api samartha iti kiṃ neṣyate ? no cet sarvathānupayogādityuktam, anyathā pratyakṣamapi trayaṃ, na dvayamiti vaktuṃ śakyatvāt | ki ca pañcakavādinaḥ samānasamayatayaivāvibhāgāt prācyo'nupalambha eka iṣṭaḥ | sa cāgnigardabhāpagame'stītyanantaradhūmānupalambhāpekṣayādyāpi dvaitameva |
[319,4]
api ca,
[319,5]
prāgadṛṣṭau kramāt paśyan vetti hetuphalasthitim || dṛṣṭau vā kramaśo'paśyannanyathā tvanavasthitiḥ || 8 ||
[320,1]
tattadāśaṅkānirākaraṇārthamuttarottarapūrvapūrvopalambhānupalambhaparyeṣaṇāprasakteḥ | tatra yatheṣṭaṃ trayādivyavasthā kriyatām | na tu pratyakṣaṃ madhyamadhivāsyānupalambhayoḥ kaścid upayogaḥ, anyaśaṅkane dvayorapyanāśvāt, tadvivecane caikenaiva siddheḥ |
[320,2]
tasmāt,
[320,3]
pratyakṣānupalambhābhyāmanvayavyatirekayoḥ | niścaye saṃśayo nāma kīdṛk hetuphalasthitau || 9 ||
[320,4]
arthāntaratve tayoreva tadbhāvarūpatvāt | tayośca na pratītiniyamaḥ kaścit, dvidhāpi siddheḥ | syādetat, vyatirekadārḍhyādevaṃ vyavasthā | atastadgrahiṇo'nupalambhasyānvayaviṣayapratyakṣātivṛttirucitaiva | na, nāntarīyakatvameva hi pramāṇasya prameye draḍhimānamāropayati | na bāhulyam pramāṇābhāseṣvapi darśanāt | eka eva ca dṛśyānupalambhastadabhāve'tyantamabhāvasādhanasādhuriti kimadhikadhāvanena ? na hi tadā gandho'pi dhūmasya saṃbhāvanīyaḥ | nanu bhūyasāmabhāvāt kasyābhāve na bhūto dhūma iti niścetavyamiti cet ? ata evānvayagrāhipratyakṣamapekṣyate anyābhāvaprayuktatve hyetadabhāvasya, nāsya saṃbhavamayamādriyeta | evamanvayagrahaṇapūrvake'pi niścaye bhūyasāṃ saṃbhavāt kasya bhāvaprayukto'sya bhāva iti jijñāsāyāmanupalabdheryadabhāvaprayukto'syābhāvaḥ saṃprati tadbhāvaprayuktaḥ prāgapyasya bhāva iti sidhyati | tatra caikaikasyopanaye'panaye vā tathā pratipattuṃ śakyam | tathā ca sati prācyasya paścimasya vā vyatirekasiddhau śaktiḥ, anekopanayādau tu dvitayasyāpyaśaktiriti sthitam ||
[320,5]
avyāpinī ceyaṃ pañcakavyavasthā | bhasmānalakalasakumbhakārādiṣu paścimābhāvāt, nīrādhārādiṣu ca prācyābhāve'pi siddhaḥ | tathā hi sati setau payaḥpūrasthemānamupalabdhavatastadbhāvetadbhāvadarśinastayorhetuphalabhāvaniścayaḥ prācyānapekṣa eva | tadvadanyatrāpi trikāpekṣa eveti veditavyam |
[320,6]
atha prāgadṛṣṭvā vahnisannidhau dhūmadarśane vahnimapekṣyānya eva janayatīti ki na kalpyate ? evamapi vahneḥ kāraṇatvamevendhanasyeva | evaṃ tarhyanyasyāpi yadṛcchāsannihitasya gardabhādeḥ kāraṇatvamastu, tataśca tasyāpi dhūmādanumānaprasaṅga iti cet ? tat kiṃ vahneḥ kāraṇatvaniścaya ityevaṃ gardabhasyāpi ? atha pratyakṣānupalambhayostatrāpi vṛtteḥ ubhayasyāpyayogāt | na cānyasya tathā niṣedhāya trayāśrayaṇam, api tu vahnervidhaye | sa ca siddha ityanyasyāniṣedho'bādhaka eva | ananumānaṃ tu kāraṇatvāniścayādeva | na kadācidagnimapekṣya gardabhaḥ karotīti śaṅkaiva niścayo virodhāt, tasyāḥ saṃśayarūpatvāt | tanniṣedho'pi tasyaiva parīkṣayā nānyasyetyasthānamevaṃvidhapralāpasya | nanu tathāpi vahniḥ kāraṇamityavadhāraṇānupapatterdusthaiva sthitiḥ | na hi vahnireva kāraṇam, anyasyāpyanirākaraṇāt, indhanasyāpi paramārthataḥ kāraṇatvācca | na ca kāraṇameva, anārabdhadhūmasyāpi saṃbhavāditi na codyam, trividhasyāpi vyavacchedasya siddheḥ |
[321,1]
tathā hi,
[321,2]
sāmagryapekṣayānyasya cchede dravyavyapekṣayā | yogyatāyāmayogasya siddho'tyantaṃ ca karmaṇi || 10 ||
[321,3]
yadā hi dahanaśabdena tadupalakṣitā sāmagrī samāsenābhidhīyate, tadā sa evetyanyayogavyavacchedaḥ | yadā tu dahanadravyameva tadāpi kāraṇatvaṃ nāma yadi yogyatā, tadā kāraṇamevetyayogavyavacchedaḥ | atha kriyaiva, tadāpi bhavatyevetyatyantāyogavyavacchedaśca siddhaḥ | sa cāyamiyān vyāpārastrividhasyaiva pratyakṣānupalambhasya śakya iti yuktamatra bhāge bhaṭṭārcaṭapādavyākhyānameva |
[321,4]
bhagavato vārtikakārasyāpi svayameva,
[321,5]
kumbhasya kumbhakāreṇa karaṇaṃ bhasmano'gninā | śastrādinā vraṇādeśca bruvato matameva tat || 1 ||
[321,6]
kathaṃ punaḥ kāryatvāviśeṣāddhūmādiva bhasmano'pi nāgneranumānam ? na, deśakālādyapekṣayā abhimatatvāt | tathā hi —
[321,7]
kimapyudayamātrāya kāryaṃ hetumapekṣate | prabandhasthitaye'pyanyat kālavittadapekṣayā || 12 ||
[322,1]
tatra kalasabhasmādibhyo janmanyevāpekṣitaparebhyaḥ, ata evārthāntarāpekṣaprabandhavaidhuryebhyaḥ, atīta eva hetusannidheḥ kālaḥ śakyaniścayo, na tu vartamāna iti na pravṛttyādisaṅkaraḥ | uttarebhyaśca dhūmālokādibhyo daśāviśeṣāpekṣānapekṣaprabandhavaidhuryebhya upādānavikalatayā pravāhavicchittaye'napekṣitaparebhyo vartamāna eveti na doṣaḥ | etadapekṣayā tvācāryadharmottarasya paścimadvayasya śrayaṇayatnaḥ phaledapi | na tu pañcakaniyamaḥ tadāpi parabhāgabhāk | pratyakṣapūrvake'nupalambhe'nyāpekṣā'bhāvāditi prathamameva śreyaḥ ||
{9}
<yoginirṇayaprakaraṇam>
[323,1]
yad yad bhāvyate tat tad bhāvanāprakarṣaparyante sphuṭābhaṃ saṃbhavati | yathā kāmukasya kāminyākāraḥ | bhāvyante ca paramapuruṣārthinā kṣaṇikatve nairātmyādayo vastudharmā iti | atredaṃ cintyate bhavatu bhāvanayā mānasī sphuṭābhatā, kevalaṃ bhūtābhūtārthasādhāraṇatvād bhāvanodbhūtavaiśadyasyāpi saṃvādaniyamānupapatteḥ kutaḥ prāmāṇyamiti kathaṃ pratyakṣatā yogijñānasyeti ?
[323,2]
athānumānavyavasthāpitavastubhāvanāyāstadvyabhicāraśaṅkāvirahāt tajjasyāpi jñānasya kutaḥ śaṅkāvakāśa iti cet ? āstāṃ tāvadanumānapauruṣapratyāśā, pratyakṣeṇāpi vidyuddahanādikaṃ gṛhītvā bhāvanāprakarṣaparyantajātaṃ sthirataratadākāraṃ ca jñānaṃ bhaved yāvanna viparītabhāvanābhiyogaparyantaḥ | astaṃ gataśca tadviṣaya iti kathaṃ pramāṇopanītavastugocaratve'pi saṃvādāśvāsaḥ ? anastaṅgame'pi vā tāvatkālamanalasya nāvasthāniyamaḥ |
samudrāderapyevam | mahīruhādīnāṃ cālpālpakālena vaisadṛśyaṃ dṛśyate | mahīdharādīnāṃ ca dahanāśaniprabhṛtibhiḥ | bhāvanā tu yāmavasthāmabhiniviśya bhavati tadekāvasthāniyataḥ sphuṭābhāva iti tadviṣayāpekṣayā bhrāntirākārabhedāditi na prāmāṇyaṃ na ca pratyakṣatā |
yadā ca hālika eva havyāśanamanumāya bhāvanayā sphuṭyet, tadā na tad yogijñānaṃ paramārthaviṣayatvābhāvāditi pratyakṣāntaraprasaṅgaḥ |
[323,3]
atrocyate | na hi tāvadiyamanantarāśaṃkā saṃbhavinī | bhāvanā hi rāgaśokādyāveśād vā svayamupanamet, prayojanānurodhād vā prekṣavatā saṃcintyārabhyeta ? tatra paramaprayojanavārtāvirahāddāhapākādimātramanumitenaiva hutabhujā taddeśopasarpaṇāt siddham, anupamṛṣṭadeśe'pi bhāvanāvaiphalyam | purastāttu bhāvite parisphurati tadarthāpekṣayā bhrāntiḥ | evaṃ śokādyupanatāyāmapi bhāvanāyām | tat kathaṃ pratyakṣāntaraprasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ ?
[323,4]
astu vā yathā kathañcit tādṛgarthabhāvanā, śirasi śṛṅgabhāvanāvat | athāpyabhramapakṣe yogijñāna evāntarbhāvaḥ | yogo hi samādhirmanasa ekāgratālakṣaṇa iti na doṣaḥ | śṛṅgākārasphuṭobhāve tu pṛthvī kṛtsnetyādivadapratyakṣataiva nirālambanatvāt | yad vārtikam,
[324,1]
tatra pramāṇaṃ saṃvādi yatprāgnirṇītavastuvat | tad bhāvanājaṃ pratyakṣamiṣṭaṃ śeṣā upaplavāḥ || (pra. vā. 2. 286)
[324,2]
yat punarastaṃ gate'pi vastunyākārāntarabhāji vā sthirākāratayā bhāvanā, yasya nirālambanatvamāpāditaṃ sarvasya, tadapi vastubhāvanāpakṣe śobhate, na vastudharmabhāvanāpakṣe | vastudharmāśca kṣaṇikatvādayaḥ saṃsāravairāgyāt sphuṭībhāvabhājo bhāvayitumupakrāntāḥ | athaikatra pramāṇapariśuddhe'pi bhāvanājanitavaiśadyasya vastuni visaṃvādasaṃdarśanādanyatrāpi ka āśvāsaḥ, pramāṇapariśuddhimantareṇāśvāsahetorapyasyābhāvāt, tasyāśca saṃvādaniyatāvasāmarthyāt ? tanna, sthirāsthiraviṣayatvena viśeṣāt | asthiraṃ hi vastu pradhvaṃsavikārābhyāṃ grasyata iti na saṃvādaḥ, vastudharmāstu kṣaṇikatvādayo na kadācidvicchidyanta iti tadviṣayaḥ sphuṭībhāvaḥ sarvadā sālambana eva |
[324,3]
nanvetadapi na yuktam | na hi kṣaṇikatvādikaṃ nāma kiñcidasti vastu, sattve vā tadeva nityamāsaktamiti sarvamayatnaśīrṇam | avastutve ca tadeva nirālambanatvam | tasmād bhavanmate'pi kṣaṇikatvaṃ nāma kṣaṇikā eva bhāvarāśayo'parāmṛṣṭabhedāḥ bhedāntaratiraskāreṇocyante | tathā ca sati kṣaṇikatvabhāvanetyapi kṣaṇikapadārthasārthabhāvanetyevārthaḥ | tāvatā tānyeva vastūni bhāvyamānāni sphuṭībhavantīti sa eva doṣaḥ | athābhinnānyapi kṣaṇikatvādīni bhinnānīva tāvatpratibhānti ? tathāpyadhyavasāyād vastugatānyeva bhāvyanta iti na taddoṣānmuktiḥ, taṭasthatayā bhāvayitumaśakyatvāt | tathā ca truṭyadrūpametad vastujātamityayamevākāro bhāvanāyāḥ |
[324,4]
tatkathaṃ vastutattvabhāvanāpakṣe'pi vastusaṃsparśaparihāraḥ ? parihāre cāvastvantarabhāvanaiva syānna dharmabhāvanā | satyam | yadyapi vastutattvabhāvanayāpi sāmānyenākṣiptaṃ vastu, tathāpi na tasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ, tattvamātratātparyaparyavasānāt | tattvabhāvanaiva hi sphuṭībhavantī saṃsārāpasāraṇasaraṇiḥ | na hi kāminīkalevaraṃ sākṣātkṛtaṃ rāgasaṃkocamācarati, kiṃ tvanityaduḥkhāditvameva | atastatraiva tātparyāt tadeva vaiśadyamāpadyate bhāvanayā, na vastu |
nanu tatra tātparye'pi vastudharmaḥ sphuṭībhavati na vastviti kā saṅgatiḥ, bhāvanayā dvayorapi kroḍīkaraṇāt ? kīdṛśo vā dharmiṇamaspṛśato dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ ? tadetadākāśacitraṇam na khalu hālikasyāpi pratyayamātanoti |
[325,1]
naiṣa doṣaḥ, dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭībhāvamaspṛśato'pi dharmamātrasya sphuṭībhāvadarśanāt |
kevalaṃ vastupratyāsattyanapekṣya na sphuṭasphuraṇamiti syāt | sphuṭībhāvo'pi tasya tadviṣayasannidhau yatnamanapekṣya jhagiti tajjñāne tattadākārasphuraṇaṃ nāma, vastuprattyāsattyapekṣā tu na kṣīyate, dharmatvādeva, priyatvādivat | tathā hi nimbarasādau tāvat priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ sphuṭībhavaddṛṣṭam | na ca nimbādeḥ sa dharma iti tadbhāvanayā nimbādyapi svajanmadeśasthaṃ rasanāprasaṅgi vā sphuṭaṃ sphuradasti yāvanna viparyayabhāvanābhiyogaprakarṣaḥ | na ca sphuṭībhūtaṃ priyatvamapi taṭasthamupalabhyate nimbādyanubhavamanapekṣya, kiṃ tu yadā yadā nimbādyanubhavaḥ tadā tadā jhagiti priyatvamanubhavaviṣayaḥ, na prāgivodvejakamanubhayaṃ vetyeṣa eva dharmasphuṭībhāvārthaḥ |
[325,2]
yathā hi kāminyādivastuni sphuṭībhūte'pi na yathā samayasiddhastattvasphuṭībhāvaḥ, tathā tattvabhāvanayāpi na vastusphuṭībhāva ubhayoḥ parasparāvyabhicāre'pīti kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? atha na bāhyadharmaḥ priyatvamasādhāraṇatvād bhāvanādheyatvācceti cet ? kasya punarayaṃ dharmo'stu priyatvādiḥ pratyātmavedyatvenāpahnotumaśakyaḥ ? jñānasya cet ?
bāhyasya priyatvamabhyasyamānaṃ jñānasya sphuṭībhavatīti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ ? utkṛṣṭamidaṃ nimbāditi bhāvanākāro'pi na tajjñānamutkṛṣṭamiti | athāpi jñānasyaiva priyatayā sphuṭībhāve na jātu kaścidapriyamanubhavet | na hi bahiriva jñānamapi kādācitkasannidhānam |
jñānasyāpi kasyacideva priyatvavyaktiriti cet ? kiṃkṛtaḥ punarayaṃ vibhāgaḥ ? yadyabhyāsakṛtaḥ, yatraivābhyāso bāhye tatraiva bhavatu | tadanapekṣāyāṃ kasyacidapi pratyāsattiviprakarṣābhāvānmanomātramadhiṣṭhānībhūtamiti na kaścidviśeṣaḥ |
[325,3]
bāhye tu viśiṣṭajātinimbādikamabhyāsaviṣayīkṛtamiti nātiprasaṅgaḥ | jñānamapi tarhi bhāvitanimbagocarameva pratyāsannamiti viśeṣaḥ | evaṃ tarhīdamāyātam, yadvastu kenacid rūpeṇa bhāvyate tadvastu vihāya tatpratyāsannasya sphuṭībhāva iti kāminīṃ bhāvayatastatpratyāsannasya pitrādereva sphuṭībhāvaprasaṅgo na kāminyāḥ | atha viṣayasya viṣayiṇā jñānena saha viśiṣṭaiva kācitpratyāsattiḥ ? evamapi nimbe priyatayā abhyasyamāne tajjñānaṃ priyatayā sphuratīti nimbādikaṃ prāgvadapriyameva bhavet | tato yathā sarpādāvapriye parihārāṅgatayā tanniścayaḥ priya eva na sarpādistathedamapīti kṛtaṃ bhāvanayā |
[325,4]
atha bhāvanābalāt priyākārameva tadviṣayaṃ jñānamupajāyata iti kalpanā ? evaṃ sati nimbarasaḥ priyo bhāvyata iti tadviṣayajñānameva priyākāraṃ bhāvyata ityāpannam |
sphuṭābhatāpi tasya tadviṣayopanidhau tadgrāhijñānasya jhagiti yatnamanapekṣya priyākārasphuraṇam, na viṣayasyaivāsannihitasya sākṣādbhāvaḥ | evaṃ kṣoṇīdharādayo'pi kṣaṇino bhāvyanta iti tadviṣayajñānameva kṣaṇikākāraṃ bhāvyata iti | tasyāpi sphuṭībhāvo bhūdharādisannidhau tadgrāhakasya kṣaṇikākārodayo na bhūdharāderasannihitasyāpi sphuṭībhāvaḥ | iyameva dharmabhāvanā śabdārthaniṣṭheti na prastutavastukṣatiḥ |
[326,1]
vastutastu priyatvaṃ nāma sukhakaratvam | tatra yadviṣaye yasya priyatvabhāvanā taccittasantānaṃ bhāvanāpariṣkṛtamupādānamupādāya sa viṣayaḥ sahakārī sukhamutpādayatīti sthitau na sarvaṃ priyatvam | tatra prīṇakatvaṃ tu tasyaiva dharmaḥ, sarvaṃ ca pratīti na doṣaḥ |
sa cābhyāsādeva | evaṃ kṛpādiṣvapi mānaseṣu dharmeṣu yojyam | duḥkhinamuddharāmīti duḥkhiparoddharaṇabhāvanāyāḥ sphuṭībhāvastadviṣayasannidhau jhagiti tat jñānaṃ tadanurūpānuṣṭhānaprasavahetuḥ | evaṃ śucikapālabhāvānāyāmapi nairghṛṇyasphuṭībhāvo nāma karparopasarpaṇe veditavyaḥ | na tu saṃbandhinaiba pratyāsannenetareṇa vā sahasphurattā |
yathoktaṃ sarvajñasiddhau,
[326,2]
labdho bodhadayādibhistvatiśayastadgocaropasthitaunaivaṃ yatnamapekṣate svarasataḥ pratyātmamunmīlati |
[326,3]
tasmāt kṣaṇikatvadharmābhyāse'pi prakarṣagāmini yāvadanubhavitavyamanena, tāvat truṭyadrūpamasmadādidarśanavilakṣaṇameva | yathāsmākamatyantasadṛśe'pi bhinnadeśapaṭutarabhedānukāri darśanaṃ vikalpaśca jhagityeva tathā syāt, anuṣṭhānaṃ vā tadanurūpam, evaṃ yoginaḥ kṣaṇabhedini bhāvadvaye darśanavikalpau | sthairyādibhramodbhavarāgādikalaṅkānaṅkitaṃ cāsya ceta iti iyatī tasya sphuṭābhatā |
[326,4]
nanu paribhāṣāmātrametat iyatyeva tasya prakarṣagatiriti | tathādṛṣṭatvāditi nottaram | yadyapi dṛṣṭamevaṃ tathāpi tāvataiva sthitiriti na śakyaṃ prastute | kadācidatiricyamānaḥ prakarṣo viṣayeṇaiva saha sphuṭayediti na pūrvadoṣaśoṣaḥ | priyatvādāvapi ca kadācidanyaiva niṣṭheti cet ? bhavatviti bhāvanayā abhimatāṃ sthitimullaṅghya sphuṭībhāvaśaṅkā | yastu prekṣāpūrvakārī svārthaṃ parārthaṃ vā bhāvanābhiyuktaḥ, tasya tāvataiva kṛtārthatvaṃ jātamiti kimiti śramāntaramāviśet, anarthakatvādanarthakaratvācca ? yathā bhojyabhaiṣajyādiṣvabhimatapākaprāptau | yathā cātra saṃbhavatyapi pākāntare'bhimate tāvataiva pākaprakarṣaparyantavyavahāraḥ, tathā prastute'pīti na kaściddoṣaḥ | tadevaṃ yadyapi dharmiviṣayabhāvanāyāḥ sphuṭībhāvo visaṃvādasaṃvāsī sthairyaviparyayādviṣayasya, tathāpi na yathoktadharmagocarāyāstadāśaṅketi sthitam | yadyevamanucitaḥ kāminīdṛṣṭānta iti na codyam, bhāvanāyā vaiśadyamātranidarśanasya vivakṣitatvāt | ata eva vārtikam, ghṛṇāvairāgyarāgavat ityāha |
[327,1]
tattarhi yogijñānamindriyajñānādbhinnamabhinnaṃ vā ? kiṃ cātaḥ ? abhedapakṣe na yogijñānaṃ nāma pratyakṣabhedaḥ, indriyajñānenaiva saṃgrahāt | na ca bhāvanopaskṛtasantānasya tathodayād bhedavyavasthā, rasāyanādisaṃskārāpekṣayāpi pratyakṣāntaravyavasthāprasaṅgāt | bhedapakṣe ca bhāvanāsaṃbhavaṃ kṣaṇikatvasākṣātkārijñānamanyadanyatheti sādhvī śuddhiḥ, indriyajñānasyāpi tadavasthāyāmasthairyasākṣātkaraṇe kṛtaṃ yogijñānena | na ca tasyākasmikaḥ kṣaṇikatvabodhaḥ |
bhāvanodbhatavaiśadyasya hi tadvodhaḥ | na cendriyajñāne bhāvanā, api tu manasaḥ | tāmantareṇāpi sākṣāt kriyālābhe ca bhāvanāvaiyarthyam |
[327,2]
kiṃ ca bhinnakālaṃ vā taddvayamabhinnakālaṃ vā ? tatrābhinnakālatvamanupapannam |
indriyajñānopanītasya hi dharmiṇaḥ kṣaṇikatā sākṣātkartavyā bhāvanābhāvinā'nubhavena |
anyathā dharmiṇaṃ dharmaṃ ca svātantryeṇa sākṣātkurvato dharmidvārakaṃ dūṣaṇamanivāryam |
na ca dharmabhāvanāyā vastusākṣātkāravyāpāro nimbādivaditi niveditametat |
tasmādindriyajñānagocarādadhika eva tattvasākṣātkāra iti prathamamindriyajñānaṃ dharmigrāhi, paścānmānasaṃ kṣaṇikatāgrāhīti niyataḥ kālabhedaḥ | kālabhede ca prācīnāpekṣayā paścimasya gṛhītagrāhitvādaprāmāṇyamekārthatve | bhinnārthatve tvindriyajñānagocarādanyatra pravartamānaṃ svātantryeṇa dharmiṇamupasthāpayatīti na ca prācyadoṣānmuktiriti |
[327,3]
atra brūmaḥ | prathamapakṣe tāvanna vastudūṣaṇam, tādṛkpuruṣaviśeṣasya sādhyasya siddhatvāt | vyavasthādūṣaṇamapi nāsti, sādhyatayaiva tādṛśādaśaviśeṣasya lokātikrāntarūpatve tatsādhanaviśeṣapratipādanāya pṛthagjanasādhāraṇendriyajñānād bhedena nirdeśāt |
na cendriyajñānaśabdena koṣṭhaśuddhyā rasāyanādijanitaviśeṣasyeva saṃgrahamātreṇa śāstrasāphalyam | ata evāñjanādikṛtaviśeṣāpekṣayāpi na bhedanirdeśaḥ, lokātikrāntarūpasya viśeṣasyābhāvāt | prayojanāpekṣayā hi bahulamekaprakārasaṃgrāhyasyāpi prakārabhedanirdeśa iṣyata eva, yathā saṃprayuktasaṃskāraskandhasaṃgṛhītayorapi vedanāsaṃjñayoḥ, vikalpasaṃgṛhītasyāpi kliṣṭamanojñānasya | tasmānnendriyayogijñānayorabhedapakṣe tāvaddoṣaḥ | tadeva dharmirūpāpekṣayendriyajñānaṃ dharmāpekṣayā yogijñānaṃ, yathā dharmipratyakṣameva niṣedhāpekṣayānupalabdhiḥ |
[328,1]
bhedakapakṣe'pi na tāvat sthairyetarasphuraṇakṛtopālambhasaṃbhavaḥ indriyajñānenāpi vastu sarvātmanā gṛhṇatā truṭyadrūpasyaiva grahaṇāt | adhyavasāyo'pi pūrvaṃ durlabhaḥ sa saṃprati bhāvanābalāvalambinā manasā āsāditapāṭavena ghaṭita iti viśeṣaḥ |
nanvindriyasyāpi taddaśāyāṃ niratiśayaviśeṣalābhād dūrasūkṣmādyanubhavaṃ ko nivārayati bāhyayogivat, tiraścāmapi kutaścit karmākṣepānmātrayā tathopalabdheḥ ? vidyamānānāṃ ca kṣaṇānāmavaśyaṃ vaisadṛśyamaṇīyo'pi saṃbhavi, anyathā sarvātmanā sādṛśye tattvaprasaṅgāt | tat tathāvidhasūkṣmabhedāvadhāraṇadhūryeṇākṣavijñānenaiva sādhyasiddheranarthakaṃ yogijñānam |
[328,2]
etena duḥkhānātmādisākṣātkāro vyākhyātaḥ | puruṣavapuṣā cendriyamantareṇa bhavitumaśakyamiti yogijñānamanutpādanīyamastu | tadapyayuktam | na hi saṃbhāvanāmātropanītaṃ netrabalamavalambya saṃvyavahāriṇā prekṣeṇa pramāṇaparāyaṇo mārgaḥ parihartu śakyaḥ | tadabhyāsasahakārikameva vā tathāvidhendriyaśaktisādhanamityaparihāryeṇa yogijñānena samānakakṣatāyāmapi indriyajñānasya na kaścid doṣaḥ | vaiyarthyamekasyeti cet ?
katareṇa punaḥ svakāraṇopanidhānadharmaṇoranayoḥ svavyāpāravaiyarthyabhayānnivartitavyam, bījādiṣvivāntyakṣaṇaprāpteṣu |
[328,3]
aprāmāṇyamekasyāstviti cet ? bījādiṣvapyekasyākāraṇatvamastu | sarvaṣāṃ samānasāmarthyānāṃ katamadekamakāraṇamavasthāpayituṃ śakyamiti cet ? paricchedabalavatorjñānayorapi kimekamapramāṇīkriyatām | parasparāpekṣayā mā bhūdubhayamapi pramāṇamiti cet ?
bījādiṣvapi naikamapi kāraṇatvamastviti samānam | gṛhītagrāhitvaṃ nāma nāstyeva | tarhi doṣa iti cet — na, kālabhedena tasya svīkārāt | gṛhītagrahaṇaṃ hi taducyate, na gṛhyamāṇasya, yathā kṛtasya karaṇasvīkāre'kārakatvam, na tu kriyamāṇakaraṇe bījādivadeva | tasmādabhinnakālapakṣe naiṣa doṣaḥ |
[329,1]
nanu tathāpyākāradvayasphuraṇaprasaṅga iti cet ? satyam, satyajñānākārastāvaddhanta samānadeśaḥ, anyathā bhramatvaprasaṅgāt | atastāvākārāvapratighau kayā rītyā sphurata iti ko nirṇetuṃ kṣamaḥ, yadāha, acintyā yogināṃ gatiḥ (pra. vā. 2. 532)
iti ? tasmād dṛṣṭāntābhāvāt kimivāniṣṭaṃ kimiva vā na doṣa ityubhayorapi nāvasaraḥ |
samasamayatayā tarhīndriyajñānānapekṣāyāṃ svātantryadoṣa uktaḥ kathaṃ parihartavyaḥ ? indriyāpekṣayaiva parihariṣyata iti nottaram | tadā hi tadapīndriyajñānameva syāt, tadvyāpārānuvidhānāt |
na yogijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit |
[329,2]
tadvaramekameva svīkṛtamiti na bhedapakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ | naivam, tathā hi mā bhūdindriyāpekṣā | vīkṣaṇaṃ tu yathā svasāmarthyānurūpāṃ yogyadeśāvasthitimapekṣya svavijñānajanane pravartate tathā manaindriyamapi pravartiṣyate, aprāpyakāritāyā ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇatvāt, arthavattāyāśca manaso'pi tadānīmiṣṭatvāt | pṛthagjanasantānasya tu na tādṛśī śaktiḥ yato netraśrotravanmano'pi tādṛṅmaryādayā yogyadeśasthamarthasahakāriṇamāsādya vedanam utpādayediti nātiprasaṅgaḥ | taddaśāyāṃ tu śrutinayanayoriva manaso'pi kiyaddūreṇa viṣayasannidhivyavastheti ka evaṃ pramātuṃ kṣamaḥ ? kevalametāvaducyate, yāvattena śakyam adhigantuṃ svākārārpaṇasahaṃ sahakāri vastu tāvaditarajanāsādhāraṇatruṭyadrūpatayā tasya gocarībhavati | tathā ca sati vastvākāro vastukṛta eva na bhāvanājanita iti na visaṃvādaśaṅkā |
[329,3]
nanu cakṣurādestāvaddūrataragocarīkaraṇe dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ, manasastu nendriyātikrameṇa sarvaviṣayasyeti cet — na, paracittajñānādīnāṃ saṃbhavāt | tadapi neṣṭamekeṣāmiti cet ? adṛṣṭamātreṇa pratikṣepāyogāt | upāyābhāvāditi cet ? upāyābhāve'pi nānupalambhamātrādanya upāyaḥ | tasmād yadyevaṃ syāt tadā yogināmindriyamanojñānayorbhedapakṣe'pi na nirvāha ityupakṣepārthaḥ | nirvāhastvanyathā'pi darśita eva | evaṃ ca sati kālabhedapakṣe'pi na doṣaḥ, yadi sā prathamaṃ manojñānavṛttiḥ, yadi cendriyapathātikrameṇa vṛttiḥ | indriyajñānaṃ tu tasya tadapekṣayā prāmāṇyavirahe'pi na vyathayatītyalaṃ vistareṇa |
[330,1]
tadevaṃ yogijñāne tattvabhāvanādhikārādarthākāro'rthakṛta eva | bhāvanayā punastadīyasantāne netra ivāñjanaviśeṣeṇa śaktiratiśayavatī kācidarpitā yayetarajanāsādhāraṇaṃ darśanamasya | yathoktaṃ prāk | yadi tarhi viṣayajanyameva yogijñānamatītānāgataparijñānasya kā vārtā ? tadetatprastāvānavagāhanasya phalam | upayuktasarvajñādhikāreṇa hi vastudharmabhāvanopakṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ | na sarvasarvajñapakṣāpekṣayā tato'tītānāgatamapratīyamānamapi na bādhakam |
tāvataiva duḥkhanirodhasiddheḥ, parasmai ca niṣkampadeśanāvatārāt |
[330,2]
yat punaḥ kaṇikāyāṃ kṣaṇikāditattvabhāvanādvāreṇa taddharmiṇāṃ samastavastūnāmeva bhāvanayā tadākārajñānotpādanātsākṣātkaraṇamutthāpya dūṣaṇamabhidhīyate yogijñānasya, tadavadhīraṇīyameva, vārtikabhāṣyādivādabahirbhāvāt | anyathārabdhaiva nityaduḥkhādibhāvanā, sā ca sarvasarvajñatvamevārpayatīti yadyabhipretaṃ syāt, kathaṃ yatnenotthāpya tatparihāro vārtike, nāsmābhiḥ śakyate jñātumiti santoṣa iṣyate ityādinā bhāṣye ca ? yadi punastadavasthāprāptau nirāvaraṇāntaḥkaraṇasya kāruṇyātiśayāt sarvākāraparārthaprārthanaparatayā sakalagocaracāriṇi cetasi ciravirūḍhotsāhasya tādṛgupāyaviśeṣādhigamo bhaviṣyati, yamanutiṣṭhataḥ pratiparamāṇu sarvavastuviṣayaṃ yathādeśakālaṃ pratyavasthānukāri sphuṭataraṃ jñānamudīyāt | tadā na tāvadvastuvyabhicārakṛtaṃ visaṃvāditvam, nāpi nirālambanatvam, vastūnāmeva pratibhāsanāt |
[330,3]
athotpattisārūpyābhyāmālambanavyavasthā, bhinnakālaṃ kathaṃ grāhyamiti ced grāhyatāṃ viduḥ | hetutvameva yuktijñā jñānākārārpaṇakṣamam || (pra. vā. 2. 247.)
iti vacanāt, tataḥ sārūpyamekamakiñcitkaramiti kathamanālambanatvaparihāraḥ ?
[330,4]
tadayuktam, tat khalu lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthagjanāpekṣayā bahirarthaṃ prati samasamayabhāvinānupakāryeṇa jñānena grahaṇaniṣedhaparam, tathā prastāvāt | tattvatastu yadeva yatra pratibhāsate tadeva tasyālambanamucyate | yathendriyapratyakṣe bāhyamanyatra svākāraḥ, pratibhāsavaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇāgrahaṇe iti hi prathamaparicchedavṛttiḥ | tatra bāhyasya pratibhāso nāma tadākārotpattimātram | tathā hi bahirvicchinnākārodayasaṃvedanamātrādidaṃ dṛṣṭamiti bhavati | na khalu tatsaṃkalpakāle utpattiraparāpekṣyate, tasyāḥ paścānniśceyatvāt phalaprāptyā vā abhyāsena vā | sa ca tadākārodaya indriyapratyakṣe'rthād bhrame viplavāt |
vikalpe vāsanātaḥ | tatrārthajanye saṃvādo'nyatra viparyayo bahirapekṣayā, svarūpe sarvatra saṃvādaniyamāt | tato'bhipretasaṃvāde vedane tadutpattimantareṇa na saṃvādo nāpi tādrūpyamiti tatra tadutpattiprārthanā | ataeva tadākārataiva prāmāṇyam, sārūpyatadutpattī ca saṃvedyalakṣaṇamityubhayamavirodhi |
[331,1]
yatra tu bhāvanāviśeṣabalādeva devatādhipatyāt satyasvapnavadarthākāramarthayāthātmyanāntaroyakaṃ jñānam, tatra na kiñcit tadutpattyā | yad vārtikam — rūpādeścetasaścaivam aviśuddhadhiyaṃ prati | grāhyagrāhakacinteyamacintyā yogināṃ gatiḥ || (pra. vā. 2. 532.)
iti | tasmād bāhye pṛthagjanasya sārūpyotpattibhyāṃ vedyasthitiḥ yoginaḥ sārūpyamātreṇāpi | svarūpe yogyatāmātreṇaiveti nyāyaḥ | bhāvibhūtayostarhi yadi svarūpasphuraṇaṃ vartamānataiva syāt |
[331,2]
atha svarūpamasannihitaṃ jñānameva tadākāramiti nirālambanaṃ niyamena, tadapi nāsti | yasmādasannihite'pyarthe bhāvanābalāccet taddeśakālānukāri vijñānaṃ kathamanālambanam ? sphuraṇarītiviśeṣeṇa tu kālabhedavikalpodayāt tadanurūpānuṣṭhāne niyatatvāt tatprāpteḥ | yadbhāṣyam, yathā sa dṛṣṭaḥ śaradādikālayuktastathā tasya na bādhitatvam | (pra. vā. bhā. 2. 615)
iti | yadvā saṃcityaiva kālabhedabhāgivasturūpapratītaye samādhisamāpattervyutthāne kālabhedādhyavasāyaḥ | yathoktam, yad yadicchati vai boddhum ityādi | krameṇa tvanābhogamapi jñānamavirodhi | jñānamātrasya tattvataḥ sphuraṇācca na vartamānatāprasaṅgaḥ, yathā nirākāravāde vastusvarūpasyaiva sphuraṇāditi | yadyapi ca vartamāne'pi jñānākārasyaiva sphuraṇaṃ tathāpi vartamānatayaivādhyavasāyastatra | evaṃ dūrāsannādibhede'pi veditavyam | tatra yathādhyavasāyaprāptau niyamena saṃvādāt prāmāṇyam anyadā viparyayaḥ yathā svapnakāminyādau | pratibhāsvargasādhanāgniṣṭomādivikalpe ca bhāvinaḥ spaṣṭarūpasya pratibhāsābhāvādeva na cintā | na ca tatra prekṣavyāvahārikasya prāptiniyamaniścayo'sti |
[332,1]
prastute'pi ko niścaya iti cet ? kasya punaratra niścayaścintyate, tasya tadanyasya vā ? yadi tasya, tadā yathābhyāsāt parito nirastavibhramāśaṅke sādhanajñāne pṛthagjanasya tathā yogino'pyatyantābhyāsād bhāvibhūtādipratibhāsaḥ kena vāryate ? athānyasya, tadedamāyātam | yāvadanyasya na prāmāṇyabodhastāvanna pramāṇam | yāvacca na pramāṇaṃ tāvannānyasya prāmāṇyabodho'bhrānta iti na kiñcitpramāṇaṃ syāt | tannābhiveśapāravaśyena kiñcit | tasmādupāyaviśeṣa sacivabhāvanābhedasyāhatyāsphuraṇāt tādṛksiddhāveva saṃśayo, na tu siddhe'pi nirālambanatvādidoṣairupadravaḥ śakyaḥ |
[332,2]
yacca vikalpena bāhyasyāgrahaṇe'pyadhyavaseyatayā sphuṭībhāvamāśaṃkya, yadanumānena gṛhyate yaccādhyavasoyate te dve'nyanivṛttī na vastunī, svalakṣaṇāvagāhitve'bhilāpasaṃsargayogyapratibhāsānupapatterityāha, tadapyasaṃbaddham | tathā hi, yathā tathā vā bauddhasiddhāntagandhena vyavahāraḥ, kāminyākāravikalpabhāvanavat kṣaṇikākārasyāpi paryante viśadopādeyakṣaṇaprasavastu durnivāraḥ | yadi punarīdṛgapohasthitiḥ kṣaṇikavikalpaikatalpaśāyinī na kāminyādivikalpamanvetītyupapādayiṣyasi tathaiva grahīṣyāmaḥ | na cādhyavaseyamavastunivṛttimātraṃ vā |
dharmottare'pi hi mate svalakṣaṇamadhyavaseyamiti sthitiḥ |
[332,3]
nanu vahniḥ pratīto mayetyadhyavasāyākāraḥ | tatra ca svalakṣaṇasphuraṇamiti sāhasam, vikalpādhyavasāyayorekārthatvāt | satyam, na tu tatra sphuratīti tāvatā svalakṣaṇamadhyavasitamucyate | asphuraṇe tarhyabodhāt kathamavasāyaḥ ? sphuraṇe'pi pratibhāsa evāsau, kathamadhyavasāyaḥ ? na ca pratibhāsādhyavasāyāvapyekārthau | pratibhāso hi sākṣāt sphuraṇamasphuraṇe'pi pravṛttiviṣayīkaraṇamekavyāvṛtyullekhasāmarthyādadhyavasāyo bhāṣyamataḥ | ato yadanurūpamanuṣṭhānaṃ tadadhyavaseyam, pratibhāsamānarūpānanupraviṣṭameva |
tacca kvacidāropitamātram | kvacidvasturūpam | prakṛtaṃ tu pramāṇavyāpārasvīkārād vasturūpameveti kathamucyate nivṛttimātramavastu vādhyavaseyamityāstāṃ tāvadanārabdhanirbandhaḥ |
pratibhāso'pi vikalpe vyāvṛttākārasya, na vyāvṛttimātrasya yadyanubhavānusāraḥ | sarvadā yad vā tad vā rākṣasādi pratibhāseta | bhāvanayā punaradhyavasitākāreṇa pariṇatiḥ abādhyā tatrāropitamātre'dhyavaseye nirālambanatvam | sati tu tadevālambanaṃ yathānantaramuktam ||
[333,1]
yattvāha, arthasyālambanapratyayatvaṃ vijñānaṃ pratīndriyāpekṣatvena vyāptam | taccāsmāt svaviruddhopalabdhyā nivartamānamālambanapratyayatvamapyarthasya nivartayatīti, tatrālambanapratyayatvendriyāpekṣatvayorvyāpyakabhāvamaprasādhya pramāṇena vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhiṃ sphuṭayatīti mahadvaidagdhyam | tathā darśanāditi cet ? darśanādarśanameva tarhi pramāṇīkṛtya sthīyatām, kimevaṃvidhapramāṇopanyāsavyasanena ? tasmādindriyamanapekṣyāpi yadyālambanabhāvaṃ bhāvaḥ svīkuryāt na bādhakamutpaśyāmaḥ | athātroktameva na khalvindhanaviśeṣo dhūmaheturiti vināpi dahanaṃ sahasreṇāpi saṃskārairdhūmamādhatte | tadādhāne vā samastakāryahetvanumānocchedaprasaṅgaḥ | tasmāt jñānamapīndriyasāpekṣādarthād utpattidharmakam |
[333,2]
indriyavyāpāravirahe ca samastā parakāraṇasannidhāvasannidhīyamānasattākaṃ tatpratibaddhaṃ siddhamiti kathamindriyānapekṣyasyārthasya svavijñānaṃ pratyālambanabhāva iti cet ? etadapi paracittajñānasaṃbhavena prativyūḍham | iṣṭāśca paracittavedinaścārvākamīmāṃsakavyatiriktaiḥ | cārvākāderapi sandehānnāparā gatiḥ | sandehe ca vipakṣādekāntavyāvṛtterayogaḥ | nanu jñānakāryasyendriyāpekṣāniyamādeva nānyatra sandeho dahanāpekṣadhūmavat | yadyevaṃ rūpajñānasya vīkṣaṇāpekṣaṇe yādṛśī sāmagrī sā na saṃcaraṇaviśeṣasya caraṇāpekṣaṇe kalayāpi hīyate, tat kathaṃ na dhūmadṛṣṭāntaścaraṇavirahiṇāmuragādīnāṃ gamananiṣedhāya prabhurabhūt ? kathaṃ vā karādivyāpārasaṅgi sāvegamantrodgāraparamparāsādhyamekeṣāṃ viṣaśamanādikāryaṃ samādhimātrādanyasya ? na caivaṃ dhūmo'pi kvacidindhane dahanānapekṣodayo dṛṣṭo yato'trāpi tathā śaṅkyeta |
[333,3]
tasmād bahirbhuvo bhāvā yathā hetuphalabhāvenopalambhabhājaḥ te tathaiva niyatavṛttayaḥ | cittasantānasya tu vicitrakarmābhisaṃskārasāmarthyād vicitra eva vivartaḥ |
atastadāśrayakāryamekatra yāvadapekṣaṃ tāvadapekṣamanyatrāpīti na niyantuṃ śakyam | tat kathaṃ paracittavedanāderabhāva eva ? yadi ca dhūmavadanalamanapekṣya nendriyaṃ buddhiḥ, tadā svaviṣaye'pyutkarṣaghoṣaṇāvīkṣaṇādīnāṃ dīnaiva syāt | tathā hi yāvaddeśaṃ dahanendhanādidhūmādisādhanamupalabdhaṃ na tāvaddeśātikrame samartham | evaṃ yāvaddeśe'smākaṃ viṣayendriyādivedanamutpāditavat kathaṃ tadatikrame gṛdhrādīnāmutpādayet ? utpādane vā nendhanadahanādikakṣāṃ kṣamate cittasantānāśrayā sāmagrī | nāpi dhūmakakṣāṃ buddhiḥ |
[334,1]
ataḥ sahakāriṇo'tivyavadhānavadvaikalye'pi kiṃ na kutaścit viśeṣāt saṃbhāvyate ? jātikṛto'sau vibhāgaḥ, na cittasantānāśrayāditi cet — na, jātirapi hi vicitrakarmādhipatyādeva vicitrasvarūpopasaṃhārasvabhāvā, karma ca na cittādanyaditi na cittāśrayatvaparihāraḥ | athendriyasya prāpyakāritayā sarvaiva vijñānajananasāmagrī sādhāraṇadeśetyucyate | tathāpi kasmāt punastāvad dūradeśasthitimati kvacillocanaruḍhāṃśaśleṣaḥ kvacidarvāgeva viśrāma iti kimatra vaktavyaṃ karmādhipatyādanyatra ? tasmāt tadāśrayasya cittasantānasya citraiva śaktiḥ |
[334,2]
na hi bahirapi śakyamevam | anyathā sadṛśapradeśasthāyinoḥ pradīpayoralpakasya kasyacid dūrasāriṇī kiraṇasaṃhatiritarasya punararvācīnacāriṇī syāt | atha mantraprabhāvādevamapi syāt, sarīsṛpadṛśā ca māndyamādadhātīti cet ? sa tarhi cittasantatereva prabhāvaḥ | mantre'pi puruṣamāhātmyakṛta eva | yathā vārtike nirṇītam, apauruṣeyatve'pi mantrāṇāṃ na puruṣanirapekṣāṇāṃ śaktiḥ | tataśca puruṣa eva mantrādyupāyena bāhyavastuśaktivyavasthāṃ dusthayatīti āyātamiti prastute kimasaṃbhāvanam ?
yathā ca locanāpekṣaḥ padārthasyālambanabhāvo dṛṣṭa iti tanniyata iṣṭaḥ, tathālokāpekṣo'pi dṛṣṭa iti na saṃtamase paśyeyurulūkādayaḥ | tathā dṛṣṭatvānna doṣa iti cet ? tathā dṛṣṭatvādeva hato'si | tathā hi netrālokayoḥ samāne'pyapekṣāsādhananyāye cittasyācintyaśaktitayā anyatarollaṅghanadarśanamanyadapi śaṅkayā kalaṅkayati | na tvadarśane śakyamevam | atha tādṛśi jñānatvasāmānyavantyapi kāryāṇītarajātibhedabhāñjīti nānapekṣya sādhanasāmagrībhedamudiyurityucyate |
[334,3]
kena punaḥ prakṛtajñānasyāpyalaukikasya pṛthagjanajñānena sahaikajātitāyāṃ pratārito'si ? asattvādeva tarhi tasya na jātibheda iti cet ? asattvamiti jātibhedābhāvādevendriyāpekṣayā niyamasaṃbhavāditītaretarāśrayaḥ | tasmāt sādhāraṇakarmanirjātānāmasmadādīnāmanubhavabhedaṃ pratīndriyāpekṣatvamālambanatvasya vyāpakamapi na svanivṛttyā anubhavamātraṃ prati nivartakaṃ bhavitumarhati, viśeṣoddeśenaiva vyāptisiddheḥ |
athānubhavamātramekīkṛtya vyāptiriṣyate ? tadā viparyayādhakābhāvāt vyāptireva na sidhyati hetuphalaniyamāśrayastu dhvasto dhūmādisādhāraṇyānupapattervicitrakarmābhisaṃskārādacintyaśaktisvāntasantānasaṃbhāvino'nubhavamātrasya | viśeṣāśraye ca na sarvopasaṃhāravatī vyāptiriti sa eva doṣo viśeṣavattvaṃ nāma |
[335,1]
yadapyayamāha, bhāvanāyāścābhūtārthāyā arthānapekṣāyā eva viśadajñānajananasāmarthyamupalabdhaṃ kāmāturādivartinyā iti bhūtārthāpi tannirapekṣaiva samartheti nārthasya ālambanapratthayatvaṃ śakyāvagamamiti | tatrāpi keyamarthanirapekṣatā ? kimarthāviṣayatvaṃ sākṣādarthāpratibhāso vā, yad vā arthāhetutvamathārthavyabhicāra iti pakṣāḥ | prathamapakṣe bhūtārthatvamaviṣayatvaṃ ceti vyāhatam, tatpra bhavānumānasyeva tasyāpyadhyavasāyāpekṣayā tadviṣayatvāt | pratibhāsāpekṣayā tu mā bhūt tadviṣayatvaṃ tasyāstajjanitajñānasyaiva tadiṣṭeriti na dvitīyo'pi pakṣaḥ | tṛtīyo'saṃbhavī, svaprabhavānumānadvāreṇa tasyāpi bhūtārthakāryatvāt | ataeva vyabhicāro'pi siddha iti na caturthaḥ | atastajjaviśadajñānasya saṃvādaniyamādarthasya kathamālambanatvamaśakyāvagamam ? tasmāt prācīnarītyaiva codyaṃ cāru, parihāraścokta eva |
[335,2]
yaccānena purastāttanā evāsya viṣayakṣaṇā grāhyā yujyante na pūrvatarā ityādinā bhūtānāgatabodhiniṣedhāya prayattaṃ, tat prāgeva pratyādiṣṭam | prakṛtasarvajñapakṣe tu yāvanto jñānamupajanayantaḥ svajñānagocaratāmanubhavanti tāvantaḥ kṣaṇikaduḥkhānātmākāreṇaivetyetāvataiva sādhyasiddhiḥ | pratītātīteṣu smaraṇaṃ bhāvini saṃbhāvaneveti |
yadyatīte smaraṇameva, tat kathaṃ samudayākārāṇāṃ sphuṭībhāva iti cet ? pañcaskandhā evottarāpekṣayā samudayaḥ | tatrāyameva samudayākārasphuṭī bhāvo yadabhimukhībhūteṣu parāpekṣayā jhagiti tadanurūpavikalpānuṣṭhānādiprasavahetuḥ sphuraṇarītiḥ kācit, yayā pṛthagjanādvibhāgabhāgī bhavati pūrvavat | atīteṣu ca tathaiva paṭutarasmaraṇodayaḥ | parānapekṣasvarūpamātreṇa tu kṣaṇikādyākārairduḥkhasatyapratītiḥ | nanu vikalpā nāmasahasaṃbhavasvabhāvatvād yadā duḥkhākārāṇāmavasāyaḥ, tadā na samudayākārāṇām, paścācca nirviṣayaḥ avasāya iti cet ? satyametadekaikasatyasyāpi nākāracatuṣṭayavikalpanamekakālam |
na ca kācidevaṃ kṣatiḥ | grahaṇarītiviśeṣa eva hi sphuṭībhūtasakalākāraḥ sākṣātkāraṇam |
yato bījavikalpāvakīrṇābhimatavikalpakramāvirbhāvaḥ | yathā hi nīlacalavikacādiviśeṣaṇamutpalaṃ paśyato janasya na vikalpakrameṇa tadviṣayasakalākārasākṣātkriyāvyāghātaḥ, tathā prastute'pyunneyaḥ | aparasparāśca kṣaṇāstavaivāparāparairanubhavaiḥ sākṣāt yante | vikalpāśca yathābhimataṃ pravartante gṛhītānusandhānarūpāḥ | anubhavenaiva ca sārvajñasthitiriti veditavyam | evaṃ nirodhadharmamārgasatyayorapi svasaṃvedanena vedane sakalamūhyam ||
[336,1]
yacca sarvavastuno mithaḥ kathañcit sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa ca saṃbandhadvārakaṃ katipayadarśane sarvadarśanasya dūṣaṇaṃ tadanabhyupagamenaiva gatam | saṃbandhadvārakastu viśeṣaṇatayā samastavastuviṣayaḥ saṅkalpo yadi tadavasthāyāṃ janmaparamparāsmaraṇasaṃbhave bhavet, na doṣamutpaśyāmaḥ | yathābhyāsavato hutāśādidarśane jhagityeva edhasya kāryaṃ hetuśca pāvakasyāyamiti vikalpaḥ, tathā vikalpagṛhītānāṃ bhāvanāprakarṣe vaiśadyamapyastu | na tu saṃbandhamātreṇaikadarśanādanyadarśanaṃ saṅgirāmahe | mā bhūd vā vaiśadyamapi sarvaviṣayavikalpamātreṇaiva saṃvādinā sārvajñyakāryaparyāptestadavasthasya | athavā svālambanapratyayamātragocaramevāvikalpakaṃ samastavastuviśiṣṭālambanādhyavasāyahetuḥ | tenāvasāyānugatavyāpāramavikalpamapi samastavastuviṣayaṃ bhavati | yadāha,
[336,2]
vyavasyantīkṣaṇādeva sarvākārān mahādhiyaḥ || (pra. vā. 2. 107)
[336,3]
etattvāśaṅkya yadāha katipayavastvavalambanasyānubhavasya kutastya eṣa mahimā yataḥ samastavastvavasāyaḥ ? rāgādyāvaraṇavigamāditi cet ? tarhi yathāvad vastūni paśyet, na tu punarasmādaśeṣavastuvyavasāyanirmāṇakauśalamasya yujyate | tattvāvarakatā hi sulabhā malānāṃ na punarvijalpanirmāṇapratibandhateti |
[336,4]
atra paryanuyogaḥ, kiṃ tāvad vastuni dṛśyamāne vikalpapratibandha eva na dṛṣṭa uta kleśakṛto veti ? tacca dvayaṃ nāsti | na hyanubhavavat sarvākārakalpanaṃ kvacit | na ca tadvikalpavaikalyaṃ kleśānantareṇa | yadā hi priye vastuni dṛṣṭe doṣavatyapi doṣāvikalpanaṃ, tadā vyaktaṃ rāgo hetuḥ | yadā punarapriye guṇavatyapi guṇāvikalpanaṃ, tadā dveṣaḥ | anabhyāse tu sarvasadrūpāvikalpanaṃ mohakṛtameva | na ca kambalādivadāvaraṇam, kiṃ tu santānavaiguṇyādhānena | tato yathā yathā mohādiparājayaḥ tathā tathā yatnena vaiguṇyavyāvṛttyā tāvatsu ākāreṣu yadā dhiyo vyavasāyabhājaḥ paryante sarvākāreṣu sarvavastuṣu yadi syurna kaścidvirodhaḥ | buddhipāṭavaparamparayā dṛṣṭeṣu smṛteṣvapi smaraṇasaṃbhavādīkṣamāṇeṣu ca gāḍhatarasmaraṇasaṃskārādhānādanādyanantatvājjanmanaḥ, ekaprakāraniścayasya ca tajjātīyāśeṣaniścayasvabhāvatvānna sarvaviṣayasaṅkalpānudayakṛto doṣaḥ |
[337,1]
yaccedamūce, apramāṇaṃ ca tannitāntaviśadābhatve sati bhāvanājanitatvāt |
yannitāntaviśadābhatve sati bhāvanājaṃ vijñānaṃ tadapramāṇam, yathā anumitabhāvitaviṣayaviśadaṃ jñānamiti | tatra vahneranumāya bhāvanaiva nāstīti darśitatvāt dṛṣṭāntābhāvaḥ |
[337,2]
yaccānena kāvyāyitam, asti ceha śiśirabharasaṃbhṛtajaḍimamantharatarakāyakāṇḍasyānumitavahnibhāvanābhiyoga iti | tatra yadi jāḍyāturatayā svayaṃ cittāveśād bhāvanopanatiḥ, tadā kvānumānavārtā ? anumānaṃ hi pravṛttipāṭavabhṛtā prārthyate | tadavasthasya tathā aśaktau ca kiṃ bhāvanayā ? sphuṭībhāva eva vā purastādastu kvānumānāvakāśaḥ ? na hi kāmuko yāvanna kāminīmanumimīte, tāvanna bhāvanāyāmabhiyujyata ityasti saṃbhavaḥ | tasmāt jāḍyāturasya bhāvanājanitavaiśadyamagnijñānamātramastu dṛṣṭāntaḥ | tadapi kāminīdṛṣṭāntena svakāvyālaṃkṛtena gatam | na caikasya bhāvanābhuvo jñānasya visaṃvādādaprāmāṇye'prāmāṇyamanyasya saṃvādino'pīti nyāyaḥ, indriyodayasyāpi sarvasya keśādiviplavavadaprāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt |
[337,3]
yacca bhāvanāprakarṣalakṣaṇasya kāraṇasya sāmyena phalayorapi dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikayoḥ sāmyaniyamāya prapañcitam, tatrāpi kiṃ na cakṣureva dvicandraikacandradarśanayoḥ samānaṃ kāraṇamutpaśyasi ? timiropaghātānupaghātakṛto viśeṣaścakṣuṣoriti cet ? bhāvanayorapi bhūtābhūtaviṣayatvena kiṃ na bhedaḥ ? cakṣuṣi timirakṛto vikāra eva kaścid bhedakaḥ, bhāvanāyā tadvaiśadye vā kaścit svarūpabhedo'bhede'pi viṣayasyeti cet — na, saṃvādetarakāraṇatvena śaktibhedasyaiva balīyasaḥ saṃbhave kimapareṇa ? saviṣetarayoriva annayo rūparasadṛṣṭīnāmabhedena hetuhetvābhāsabhāvinyoriva vā sādhyabuddhyostatkṛtapravṛttyośca kiṃ ca locane'pi na vikāra ityeva doṣaḥ añjanajanite'pi vikārī doṣavyavasthāprasaṅgāt | kiṃ tu bhrāntihetutayeti śaktikṛta eva tatrāpi bhedaḥ | tadevaṃ bhāvanāprakarṣeṇa sphuṭābhatvameva sādhyate na prāmāṇyam, yato dṛṣṭāntāsiddhyādidoṣāvakāśaḥ |
prāmāṇyaṃ tu bhūtārthatvena saṃvādāt pratyakṣatvaṃ ca kalpanāpoḍhābhrāntatveneti tāvataivāsyāśeṣo'pyavidyāduṣṭanayaḥ pratihato veditavyaḥ ||
[338,1]
