nyāyaprakīrṇakakārasyāpyabhūtaviṣayatopalambhastāvat kṣaṇabhaṅgādisādhanādeva prativyūḍhaḥ | yaccānumānasya vikalpatāṃ prastutyāha, tatra yāvadvikalpairupadarśitaṃ tat sarvamasat, śabdasaṃsṛṣṭatvāt | tasmiśca bhāvyamāne asatye tāvakasya vikalpasya bhāvanayopahite viśadabhāve śabdasaṃsṛṣṭagrāhyatvanimittaṃ vikalpakatvaṃ vyāvartate | tadvyāvṛttau ca grāhyasarvaśabdasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ nivartate | ato nirvikalpakamapi yogijñānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ prasaktamiti |
[338,2]
tatra kimidaṃ nirviṣayatvaṃ nāma ? grāhyākārabhraṃśādanākāratā vā, yad vānyākāratā, atha tadākāratve'pi tadvasturūpāsaṃsargiteti ? prathamapakṣastāvadasaṃbhavī, jñānasya nirākāratvānupapatteḥ, kāminyādau bhāvanayā tadākārasyaiva vaiśadyadarśanāt | ataeva na dvitīyo'pi pakṣaḥ | yadayamevāha śokāturasyāpi niruddhendriyavyāpārasya tanayabhāvanayā pitrādipratibhāsaprasaṅgāditi | kevalaṃ na cāsmin saṃsṛṣṭe bhāvyamāne sphuṭamanyadrūpaṃ bhavatīti prastutyākulaḥ pralāpa eṣaḥ | anena hi bhāvanayā sarvathā sphuṭībhāva eva niṣiddhaḥ, vikalpamantareṇa bhāvanānupapatteḥ | vikalpasya ca śabdasaṃsargamantareṇeti kva sphṭībhāvaḥ ? tanayabhāvanāyāṃ ca pitrādipratibhāsaprasaṅgavādinā tanayapratibhāso'nujñāta eva | anyathā tanayābhāvanayāpi tanayapratibhāsaprasaṅgādityabhidadhīta | na cāniṣṭimātraṃ dṛṣṭāpalāpāya prabhavati |
[338,3]
tathā ca kaṇikākāra eva kāminyākāravaiśadyaṃ kāmukasya vacanaceṣṭāviśeṣakāvyaracanayā draḍhayati sma | svayaṃ cāyaṃ bhāvanayopahite viśadabhāve ityādivacanaṃ kenākāreṇa caritārthīkuryāt ? tasmādanyabhāvanayā nānyasphuṭībhāva ityadhyavaseyāpekṣayā anyatvavyavasthāpanaṃ sādhu | na vikalparūpasya gocarābhimatasya ca parasparam, tayorekatādhyāsāt | spaṣṭībhāvo'pi hi bahirabhimatasya paryante vikalpopādeyakṣaṇasyaiva sphuṭasyodayaḥ | tāvataiva sa viṣayastena sākṣātkṛta iti vyavahāraḥ | kevalaṃ sati vastuni tadākārajñānaṃ saṃvādi, visaṃvādi tvasatīti cintitaprāyam |
[338,4]
ata eva tṛtīyo'pi vikalpaḥ pratyuktaḥ | saṃvādasākṣātkriyābhyāmanyasya jñānena vasturūpasaṃsparśasya nirvaktumaśakteḥ | api ca tanayabhāvanāyāmityatra kastanayabhāvanārthaḥ ? tanayasya punaḥ punaścetasi niveśanamiti cet ? cetasi niveśanārtho'pi tadākāravikalpanameva | evaṃ tarhi yadayaṃ pralapati kṣaṇikatve bhāvye samāropite vāstavaṃ kṣaṇikatvameva yogijñānapratibhāsīti cet — na, sattvāsattvayorekatvābhāvātmake hi bhede satyasatyabhāvane'pi yadi satyapratibhāsaḥ, sa tarhi satyatanayābhyāse'pi śabdasāmyādabhedinastanayasaṃjñakasya kasyacidaparasya svarūpapratibhāsaprasaṅgaḥ | tasmādabhūtaviṣayādabhyāsānnirvikalpakamapi saṃvādānna pramāṇamiti, tadapi dhvastam, samāropitabhāvanāyā evābhāvāt |
[339,1]
yathā hi, tanayastanaya iti vikalpābhyāsastathā yadi samāropitaṃ kṣaṇikatvaṃ samāropitaṃ kṣaṇikatvamiti vikalpaḥ, tadā samāropitakṣaṇikabhāvanā bhavet, na caivam |
kiṃ tu kṣaṇikāḥ saṃskārā iti | tataḥ satthatanayavad vāstavameva kṣaṇikatvaṃ bhāvyate |
satyatanayabhāvanāyā vā anya ākāro vaktavyaḥ | kṣaṇikavikalpena kṣaṇikasvalakṣaṇāsparśāt kathaṃ tadvikalpo bhāvanā veti tanayavikalpe'pi samānam | adhyavaseyāpekṣayā tadvikalpatvavyavasthā ca samānaiva | na hi tanayavikalpe'pyāropitād anyasya pratibhāsaḥ | tadayaṃ tanayabhāvanāyāmāropitaśabdasaṃsṛṣṭapratibhāse'pi satyatanayasphuṭībhāvamicchan prastutaṃ pratikṣipatīti kimanyanmohamahāgrahagrāsībhāvāt |
[339,2]
etacca vikalpasphuradāropitāpekṣayā bāhyatvamātreṇa satyabhāvanāsāmyamuktam |
bāhyāpekṣayā tu śokāturasya tanayabhāvanamabhūtabhāvanaiva | ata eva tadabhūtaṃ puraḥ sphurattanayākāraṃ tadā tādṛktanayābhāvādapramāṇam | kṣaṇikabhāvanā tu sadā tatprakṛtitvād dharmāṇāṃ bhūtaviṣayaiveti, tajjanitavaiśadyamavisaṃvādāt pramāṇam | atha vikalpasyāvastuviṣayatayā tanaye tanayabhāvane'pi bhinnameva vaiśadyamāpadyate nāsmanmata iti hṛdistham |
tadapi hṛdaya eva jīryatu | yoginirṇayo hi prārabdha eṣaḥ, tasya cobhayathāpi na kṣatiḥ | apohasyāpi pramāṇena pariśuddhāvadhyavaseyasyaiva vaiśadyaṃ dṛṣṭamiti kimatra kriyatām ? anumāne vastunirbhāsābhāvāt kathaṃ tadapekṣayā pramāṇapariśuddhiriti cet ?
prastāvāntarametat |
[339,3]
yaccedam, api ca bhāvyasya vastunaḥ punaḥ punaścetasi niveśanamabhyāsaḥ | sa ca brahmacaryeṇa tapasā sādaradīrghakālanirantaramāsevito dṛḍhabhūmirasphuṭākārasya vikalpasya sphuṭābhatvajanana iṣṭaḥ | sa ca kṣaṇikanairātmyavādinā draḍhayitumaśakyaḥ | tathā hi, bhāvyagrāhī yādṛśo vikalpa utpannastādṛśa eva niranvayaṃ nirudhyate | tasmiṃśca niruddhe punarutpadyamānaḥ pratyayastādṛśa evāpūrva utpadyate | tadanena paryāyeṇa kalpasahasre apyapūrvotpatteraviśeṣānna tajjanyaḥ saṃskāro'bhyāsa utpadyate | etena viśiṣṭavijñānotpādo'bhyāso vyākhyātaḥ | niranvayaniruddhaṃ hi pūrvavijñānaṃ kathamuttarottarāvasthāntaraṃ viśiṣṭaṃ janayet ? sarvathā kramabhāvibhiḥ pratyayairavasthitameva rūpaṃ śakyaṃ saṃskartumiti |
[340,1]
tadetadasaṃgatam | na hi yādṛśa eva bhāvyagrāhī pratyayaḥ prathamo niranvayaniruddhaḥ, tādṛśa evāpara utpadyata iti niyamaniścayakāraṇaṃ kiñcidasti caṇḍadevatāsparśādanyat |
kṣaṇikatvāditi cet ? nanu kṣaṇikatvaṃ sthāyitayā virudhyate, na visadṛśotpādena | taddhi prācīnaṃ niranvayanirodhi yathā sadṛśaṃ kṣaṇāntaramārabhate, tathā yadi sāmagrībhedaleśato viśeṣaleśaniveśikṣaṇāntaramutpādayati tadā kā kṣatiḥ ? na hi bhavata iva bhāvasyāpi kṣaṇikatāyāṃ pradveṣaḥ | asti cehāpi leśena sāmagrībhedaḥ | tathā hi kṣaṇikāḥ sarvasaṃskārā ityanuvādamātrāpekṣayā saṃsāraduḥkhakṣayārthitayā bhāvanāyāmabhiprayujyamānasya viśiṣṭa eva saṃkalpaḥ, so'pi viśiṣṭamaṇumātrayātiriktaṃ janayati yāvattaratamādikrameṇāntimāt phalalābhaḥ, bījādivat | yadi tu vyāsaṅgādayo madhyamadhyāsīran mandatāditāratamyameva syāt | yad bhāṣyam, saṃskārasya balīyastve vyākṣepasya nivartanam | vyākṣepasya balīyastve saṃskāraḥ syāt parāṅmukhaḥ || (pra. vā. bhā. 2. 500)
iti | niranvayavināśe tarhi prācīnaviśeṣāsaṃkramaṇād dvitīyasya kuto viśeṣalābhaḥ ? evaṃ tarhi sāmagryantare'pi tādṛśā viśeṣeṇa bhavitavyam, asya tatrāsaṃkramaṇāt | tasmādasannapi sa viśeṣaḥ kāraṇabalādudapādi yathā, tathāyamapi | samānastarhi tenāyamiti cet — na, hetuviśeṣāt phalaviśeṣasya durnivāratvāt |
[340,2]
tathā hi prathamo viśeṣastādṛgviśeṣavinākṛtādutpannaḥ | ayaṃ tu tādṛśaviśeṣasacivāditi kathaṃ samānaḥ syāt ? anvayastu vicārāsaha eva | yo hi hetutaḥ saṃkrānto bhāgastatra nāparasya hetorvyāpāraḥ, ya eva vyāpāraḥ sa pūrvamasanneva | evaṃ yadaṅgasya nirodho na tasya sthitiḥ, sthitimataśca na nirodhaḥ | tatkathaṃ sānvaye nirodhajanmanī ?
tena sahavṛtteriti cet ? ākāśenāpi sānvayatvakalpanāprasaṅgāt | ubhayakālānuvṛttimātrajanyasya sahārthasyābhāvāt | tacca kalasakapālayornidhanasaṃbhavakāle'ntarālasya na vāryate | śeṣaṃ tu prakriyāmātraghoṣaṇaṃ pramāṇaparipanthīti kiṃ tena ? haripadavadavasthite tvātmanyutkarṣāpakarṣāyoga iti bahuśaścarvitamāstāṃ tāvat |
[341,1]
yaccāha, kiṃ ca cittamekāgramavasthāpayituṃ vikṣepatyāgārthamabhyāso'nuṣṭhīyate, na ca kṣaṇikavādināṃ vikṣiptaṃ cittamasti, pratyartha niyatatayā sarvasyaikāgratvāditi | tadapyasaṃbaddham | anubhavasiddhaṃ hi cetasaḥ kasyacit tattvasaṃmukhīkaraṇam, kasyacid viparyayaḥ, kāryādimātraparāmarśo'parasyeti | tatra nairātmyāditattvaparāṅmukhaṃ sarvameva cittaṃ vikṣiptamucyate | uktakrameṇa tu tattvekaniṣṭhaṃ samāhitamityetāvatā kiṃ na paryāptam ? yadavaśyamekasyaiva vicitragocaracāritvamanveṣitavyam | atha ca tattvasākṣātkriyākālāt prāgahamityekākārāvagrahasaṃbhavād vyāvahārikaṃ tadapyasti, yato mamaiva doṣakṣayo bhāvīti mārgābhyāsapravṛttiravyāhṛtā bhavati | prāpyasaṃkalpo hi sarvatra pravartakaḥ | sa cedasti vastutathābhāvavyatireke'pi kaḥ pravṛttiṃ nivartayati ? yena hi tarhi tathānumānena niścitaṃ kṣaṇikatādi tasya pravṛttiriti cet ? niścayasya sātmībhāvābhāvādanādyavidyāvāsanāvaśīkṛtena cetasā niścayānucitasyaiva vyavahārasya pravartanāt |
ataeva darśanamārge'pi labdhe bhāvanāmārgāpekṣaṇamuktaṃ vārtike'nveṣaṇīyam | tasmāt tatphalalābhādarvāgabhyāso'vidyayeva saṃpādyate | abhyāsācca siddhaḥ sarvajña iti ||
[341,2]
nyāyabhūṣaṇasya ca yogācārapakṣāpekṣayā dūṣaṇamaprastutam, bahirarthamabhyupagamyaiva sādhanaprakramāt | tatrāpi sarvasarvajñapakṣopakṣipto bādhastadanabhyupagamādeva nirastaḥ |
na cāsau bādha eva, saṃśayamātrasādhanatvāt | tathā hi, yattāvadatītānāgataviṣayatvaniṣedhārthamuktam, na hyasataḥ kaścidākāro'stīti, satyamidānīmevametat | tatastajjanyajñānenāgrahaṇamapi satyam | satyasvapnādivadanyathāpi tu saṃbhāvanā na śakyaniṣedheti darśitam | na ca yathedānīṃ na kaścidākārastathā kālāntare'pi bhūtabhāvinoḥ | tathā sati bhūtabhāvitvamapi na syāt, karikesaravat | abhramāvisaṃvādau ca prāgeva cintitau ||
[341,3]
yatpunarāha, na cāvisaṃvāditvamapi tvanmate yuktam, yataḥ prāpyārthadarśakatvaṃ vā pravṛttiviṣayopadarśakatvaṃ vāvabhātārthakriyāniṣpattirvā bhavatāmavisaṃvāditvamabhipretam |
na caitadatītādyarthajñānasya saṃbhavati, vartamānārthajñānasyāpi kṣaṇikatvapakṣe nopapadyata eveti | tadapīrṣyāpāravaśyamātram, upapattividhuratvād | yadi tāvad bhāvibhūtayoḥ kālavyavadhānena tathocyate, tadā deśavyavadhāne'pi eṣa prasaṅga iti pravṛttiyogyadeśe'pi pradarśakamapramāṇaṃ syāt | tadasti tāvaditi cet ? anyadapi, bhāvi bhūtaṃ vā tatkāle nāstīti cet ? taddeśe vartamānamapi nāstīti samānam | arthakriyāpi yathā taddeśasannidhau tathā tatkālasannidhāviti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ | vartamānasya kṣaṇikatve'pi ekatvāropasāmarthyānna vyāvahārikaṃ prati pramāṇatāyāḥ kṣatiḥ, tadabhiprāyāt saṃvādasya vyavasthitatvāditi ||
[342,1]
yacca kaumārilaiḥ sarvasarvavidi kāraṇānupalabdhimupakramya tasya kāraṇam indriyajñānaṃ vā mānasaṃ vā bhāvanābalajaṃ vā, bhāvanābalajamapi cākṣuṣaṃ mānasaṃ veti vikalpya dūṣaṇamārabdham, tat saṃbhāvanādaurbalyāviṣkaraṇamātraṃ nābhāvaniścayaphalam, yathendriyāpekṣālambanatvacintāyāṃ carcitam | na ca kāraṇānupalabdheraniścayaḥ phalam, tata eva dharmādharmaviṣaye'pi bhāvanābalajasya balamapalapitumaśakyam | tataḥ kāśikākārasyāpi yogināṃ dharmādharmayoraparokṣapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ nāsti, indriyasannikarṣābhāvādasmadādivadityanumānamanaikāntikam, vipakṣavyāvṛtterekāntena pratipattumaśakyatvāt | kiṃ ca dharmādharmajñānamiti karmaphalasaṃbandhamātraparijñānametat | tacca jātismaratvasaṃbhave durnivāram | tataḥ parijñānasaṃbhavāt bhāvanāpariniṣpattau idaṃ suvarṇādyevaṃ prayujyamānametatsādhanamiti jhagiti vikalpotpādanapaṭīyaḥ pratyakṣamudayamāsādayediti kimanupapannam ? kevalaṃ jātismṛtau pratipattavyam | tatra cādarśanamātramapramāṇamiti na sarvathā niṣedhābhidhānaṃ sādhu | yathā hi sannipātādibhirabhyastavismaraṇasaṃbhave'pi smaraṇamapi keṣāñcid dṛṣṭam, tathā garbhāvāsapīḍayāpi kasyacit prajñātaikṣṇyāt puṇyodayāt pīḍāmāndyācca samanantarajātismaraṇamapi bhavat sarvathā niṣeddhumaśakyam acārvākeṇa |
[342,2]
saṃbhave cāsyānekajanmāntaragocarīkaraṇasyāpi saṃbhavāt krameṇa sarvaviṣayasaṃkalpasaṃbhavāvirodhād viṣayānavagamakṛto bhāvanānudayadoṣaḥ parihṛtaḥ, āgamācca lokasanniveśaṃ yathāvat parigṛhya bhāvanāsaṃbhavāt | yadyapi nāgamaḥ pramāṇam, tathāpi gambhīrapramāṇāntarasaṃvādasaṃdarśinaḥ śraddhāvataḥ kiṃ na saṃbhavet ? tatprameyasyāvaitathye ca siddhaṃ sādhyam | samudāyavikalpābhyāmevāvayavasyāpi sphuṭībhāvo dṛṣṭa eva | krameṇa sūkṣmādyabhivyaktiśceti |
[343,1]
etena tadapi nirastaṃ yadabhyastaikaśāstrasyānyatrāśaktirubhayā vā bahu bahudhāpratirūpate paramapuruṣārthā padādibhiḥ | na hyatra vimatiḥ | idaṃ punarasti, prathamaśāstrābhyāse prayāso yāvān na tāvān vijātīyābhidheye'pyanyatra | evaṃ pāṭavaprakarṣaparamparāyām aśrute'pi kasyacit tathā prakarṣo yathā nānyasya śrute'pi | tato janmāntarasmṛtisaṃbhave bhūyo'bhyāsādanabhyasteṣvapi vasturūpeṣūhāpohasaṃbhavānna niḥkleśāvasthaḥ parārthasamarthatayā tāvataiva sthāsyati | yad vā sarvasaṃkalpasaṃbhavād bhāvanābhiyuktā vyaktīkariṣyanti sarva svecchāto yoginaḥ | ata eva sarvāvagatipakṣe bhāvanānarthakyodbhāvanamapyanarthakam, niṣpannāvaśyakāryacaturāryasatyabhāvanasya sarvaviṣayānumānasaṃbhave svecchāyāḥ pratipādanāt |
[343,2]
atha sarvavastusākṣātkāre'nyadeva sukhaṃ parārthasādhanaṃ veti paśyenna bhāvanayā parikhedaḥ kaścittadavasthasya sukaraśca sarvasphuṭībhāvaḥ saṃbhavatīti mahodadhināpi nādhikaṃ kiñciduktam | uktaṃ ca tāvataiva pratyuktam | tasmād yathā yathā cintyate saṃśayamātraphalaḥ sarvavidi dūṣaṇopanyāso naikāntena bādhe vikalpaḥ | prakṛtasarvajñasya tu sādhanamekāntenaiva | tatrāpi na deśakālapuruṣaniyama iti cet — na, tadapekṣāyāṃ sādhanasya aprayuktatvāt | sarvathāpavādinaṃ prati hi sādhanametat | tacca deśādyaniyame'pi kṛtārtham |
tathā caivaṃvidhamudbheditamasmābhiḥ sarvajñasiddhāviti ||
{10}
<advaitabinduprakaraṇam>
[345,1]
iha bahirarthābhiniveśino manoratho yad yathā pratīyate tat tathā saditi vyavasthāpyate, yathā kuvalayaṃ nīlarūpatayā | vijñānād vyatiriktarūpatayā ca pratīyante ghaṭādaya iti svabhāvahetuḥ | nātrāsiddhiḥ, grāhakāṅgād vicchinnena tarjanīnirdeśayogyena puro'vasthāyinā rūpeṇa ghaṭādyākārasya pratibhāsādhyavasāyābhyāṃ kroḍīkaraṇāt | tathā hyayaṃ ghaṭo nāyaṃ ghaṭa iti pratītiḥ pratyātmavedyā sarvapuruṣāṇāmavyutpannasaṃketānāmapi saṃjñāviśeṣollekhavimukhastadanurūpa evāntarjanyaḥ | bālo'pi sukhasādhanaṃ stanamavalokya tadabhimukhe karamukhe prahiṇvan bahiravasāyasacivamātmānamātanoti | tataśca vyatiriktena rūpeṇa ghaṭādyākārasya pratītirnāsiddhipathaprasthāyinī | nāpi virodhinī sādhyena, sapakṣe saṃbhavasya darśitatvāt | viparyayavyāptasya ca viruddhasya tadasaṃbhavāt |
[345,2]
ataeva ca nāsādhāraṇatvam, nāpi sandigdhānvayatvam, vipakṣe'darśanācca na sādhāraṇānekāntaḥ | na ca vaktavyaṃ kāmalinaḥ pītaśaṅkhapratītāvapi na tathaiva vyavasthā keśoṇḍūkapratītau vā taimirikasya, ataḥ sādhāraṇatvameveti, bādhakagrastatvena tatpratīteḥ bhrāntatvena pratyakṣavyāpāravirahāt | prastutastu bādhakābhāvādbhrāntyasiddheradhyakṣavyāpāra eva | na ca kadācidatrāpi syād bādhakamityanāśvāsaḥ, sarvatra pratyakṣavyāpārocchedaprasaṅgāt | tasmāt,
[345,3]
deśakālanarānyatve bādhake sati nākṣajam | ghaṭādibhedabodhastu pratyakṣastadabhāvataḥ ||
[345,4]
evaṃ tarhi pratyakṣavyāpāre kimanumānenetyapi na codyam, vyavahārasādhanasya vivakṣitatvāt | pratyakṣagocare hi vivādasaṃbhavo nānumānaprayojye viśrāmyati | tatra yathā pratyakṣe'pi gavi kutaścidāropāt mūḍhastadvyavahāramapravartayan sāsnādisamudāyātmakatvena pravarttyate, abhāvavyavahāraṃ vānupalabdhyā, tathā pratyakṣe'pi grāhyagrāhakayorbheda āgamāntarānusārī tathāpratītyā vyavahāryata iti na doṣaḥ | sa cāyaṃ vyavahāraḥ tanmātranibandhanaḥ sakṛtpravartanādeva siddhaḥ | na hi kuvalayādāvapi nīlādivyavahāre tathā pratibhāsādhyavasāyābhyāmanyadadhikaṃ vā kiñcit nimittamasti, tanmātrato'pravṛttiprasaṅgāt | arthakriyāsaṃvādo'pi hi prathamāyāṃ pravṛttau gaveṣyate | abhyāsavastu tanmātranibandhana evāsau vyavahāraḥ | prastute tu bhedavyavahāre sarvatra evānādikālikābhyāsapāṭavabhṛto lakṣyante | uktaṃ hi, bālo'pi hi ityādi |
[346,1]
tasmād vyavahārapragalbhasya tathā pratītimātrapratibaddhastathāvyavahāraḥ | tasmin sādhye tathā pratīyamānatvaṃ tadanyānapekṣatvena vyāpyate | yadi ca kvacit tathā pratītāvapi tathā vyabahāravirahaḥ syāt, tadā tadanyāpekṣaṃ syāditi sādhyasya tadvyavahārayogyatvasya abhāve vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhyā avadhūyamānaṃ tathā pratīyamānatvamapetabādhake viṣaye tathā vyavasthāyogyatayaiva vyāpyata iti vyāptisiddheḥ sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvamapi nopanyastasya hetorantikamupasarpatīti siddhamadhyakṣaviṣayasyāpi jñānajñeyabhedasyoktānumānavyavahāryatvamahāryamiti |
[346,2]
atrocyate | kimidaṃ vijñānaṃ nāma yato bhedena pratītiḥ tathā vyavahāraṃ sādhayet ?
yadi hi jñāyate'neneti jñānaṃ jānātīti vā ubhayathāpi jñeyāpekṣaṃ lakṣaṇametat | na ca bāhyāpalāpino jñeyaṃ nāma kiñcidasti siddham, yatastadadhigatisādhanaṃ jñānaṃ syāt | tathā hi, idaṃ jñānamidaṃ jñeyamiti vyavahāro vyāpāraviśeṣakṛto vā syāt dvaitavādino jātiniyato vā ? prathamapakṣe jñānasya vā jñeye jñeyasya vā jñāne vyāpāraḥ, parasparaṃ vobhayoḥ ?
atrāpi prathamapakṣe nirvartako vikārako veti vikalpāḥ |
[346,3]
tatra na tāvat jñeye jñānavyāpāro nirvartakaḥ śakyo'bhidhātum, adṛśyaviṣayavyālopaprasaṅgāt | na ca tathaivābhyupagamo yuktaḥ, tadaiva kenacit dṛṣṭeḥ | tajjñānena nirvartanābhyupagame ca parokṣasyāpi sthiteranapahnavaḥ | sa ca tena paścād dṛśyamānaḥ tajjñānasyaiva nirvartako jāta iti na viṣayaḥ syāt | sa na tasya dṛśyaḥ tajjñānajanyastvanya eveti cet ? ekasthānānupapattiḥ | apratighatve prakāśarūpasya pratyātmavedyasya parāgocarasya vijñānarūpataiva mukhāntareṇa samarthitā syāt | nīlarūpatvānnaivamiti cet ?
kena punarvijñānasya nīlākārotpattiniṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ, tatsādhanāya sādhanānavadhānaprasaṅgāt ?
tasmānna parokṣamasadeveti dvayavādino yuktam |
[347,1]
na cāyamabhyupagamo'pyasyeti nātra nirbandhaḥ | pramāṇābhāve prameyābhāvamicchato'pi hi na parokṣasya sarvathābhāva evābhimataḥ, api tu sannavaśyaṃ kasyacitpramāṇasya viṣayaḥ syāt stokāntareṇeti | anyathā satsaṃprayoge satīndriyāṇāṃ puruṣasya buddhijanmetyavācyaṃ syāt, jñānāt prāk sato virahāt | sa punarabhyupagamo na nyāyya iti kimanena, tanmātrasya vivakṣitatvādityalaṃ vistareṇa |
[347,2]
vikāryapakṣe tu yasya jñānasya yo vikāryo'rthaḥ sa grāhya iti vyavasthāyāṃ śokādinopahatāyā buddhervikāryamindriyamapi grāhyaṃ syāt, malinamukhacchāyādayo vā ? duḥkhajanito'sau vikāra iti cet — na, upahatākārasaṃvedanādanyasya tasyānupalabdheḥ | nirloṭhitaṃ caitacchāstra ityalaṃ prayāsena | atha naitādṛśo'tiśayaḥ prameyasya jñānāt, kiṃ tarhi prakāśarūpasyotpattiriti cet ? atrāpi pakṣe ekagocaraḥ sarvagocaraḥ syāt | tadīyajñānanivṛttau tadrūpanivṛtteranyasyāpyadarśanaprasaṅgaḥ |
[347,3]
anyasyāpi tadupāyayogānnevamiti cet ? tasyāpi nivṛttajñānasya tatprakāśaprasaṅgaḥ | tajjñānanivṛttau tadrūpānivṛttāvapyeṣa eva doṣaḥ | na hi kulālaprayatnapārahṛtāyā mṛdastameva prati ghaṭībhāvaḥ | dahanādvā dahanopadhāyakameva prati ghaṭasya gaurabhāvaḥ | evaṃ tarhi upakāritvamapi svarūpamasya sarvasādhāraṇaṃ syāt, na caivam | tato yathā ghaṭatvena sādhāraṇo'pyeṣa nārthakāriṇā rūpeṇa, tathā prakāśarūpeṇāpi na syāditi ko'yaṃ prasaṅgaḥ ?
athopakāryaviśeṣopakāritāsya sādhāraṇī ? puruṣaviśeṣāpekṣaprakāśatāpyasya sarvasādhāraṇīti samānam |
[347,4]
na samānam | upakāritvaṃ hi nāma sākṣādupakāraḥ, pravṛttiyogyatāmātraṃ vā abhimataṃ syāt ? tatra yogyatāmātraṃ sarvasādhāraṇamiti na tatra vivādaḥ | prathamapakṣe tu upakāralakṣaṇakāryakarmaṇi sahakāribhāvo'sya yathaikatra tathānyatrāpi kiṃ na syāditi codyārthaḥ | na cāyaṃ nyāyaḥ, avyavadhānādyapekṣatvāt | tato yatsantānavartinaḥ upādānasyopanidhiḥ, tatraiva sāhāyakamasyeti kathaṃ vyavahitādau puṣṭiḥ ? tathā yadi prakāśa ityapi kāryāntarajananadvāreṇa vyavahāra iṣṭaḥ syāt, tadā syādapyevam | yathāhureke, buddhilakṣaṇavyaktijanakatvameva tasya vyaktatvamiti | tadā hi yasyaiva buddherupādānaṃ samanantarasaṃkhyātaṃ nopanipātabhāgi sādhanāntaraṃ vā, tasyaiva nāsau sahakāradānavirahād vyakto yuktaḥ |
dūṣaṇāntaraṃ ca tatrāpi vakṣyāmaḥ |
[348,1]
na caivaṃ yujyate, jñānāt prakāśarūpasyaiva viṣayasyotpattirityetasya pakṣasya vicintyamānatvāt | kāryāntaradvāreṇa tu vyaktavyavahāre na tatastathotpanna iti prakṛtakṣatiḥ | tathotpattau durvāraḥ sādhāraṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ | upakārakatvamapi hi yāvadeva bhinnasantānavarti sukhādijanakatvaṃ tāvadeva tadapekṣayā sādhāraṇam | yadā tu sukhādirūpatvamevābhyupagamyeta, tadā kaḥ sādhāraṇatvaniṣedhāya prabhuḥ ? nanu tathāpi yadekasya sukhaṃ na tadanyasyeti cet ? arthasya dharmaḥ sādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ jñānasya | tataḥ tadātmaniyataṃ sukhādi na parasādhāraṇamanugrahādirūpatveneti yuktam | bāhyarūpaṃ tu svīkriyamāṇaṃ sādhāraṇameva tatkāryatve'pi hyanugrahasya, sukhasaṃvidupādeyakṣaṇāntararūpatvāt | tadvadeva sādhāraṇatvamasādhāraṇatvaṃ ceti |
[348,2]
evaṃ na caitrajanitaṃ maitrasya tatputratvaṃ nāma kiñcid gauratvamiva yat sādhāraṇaṃ syāt, api tu tajjanitatvamevāsya tatputratvaṃ vyavahriyate | sa ca jananavyāpāraścaitrasya nānyasādhāraṇaḥ | tathā tannimitto'pi vyapadeśaḥ, tajjanitavyapadeśavat | gauratvaṃ tu tatkṛtamapi na tatkṛtameva guṇāntaratvāditi sādhāraṇaṃ yuktam | na hyasau pitureva gauraḥ kiṃ tu parasyāpi |
evaṃ na jñānakṛtatvamevārthasya vyaktatvaṃ vyavahitādyaviśiṣṭarūpasya, kiṃ tu tadatiśāyinaḥ prakāśarūpasyotpattirityabhyupagamaḥ | anyathā na vyakta ukto viṣayaḥ syāt | tathāvyavahāramātraṃ tu tannimittaṃ syāt, yathā gauratvameva tajjanyatāmātreṇa vyavaharataḥ, sautrāntikasya vā tajjanakatvena | yathā ca tasya janakajñānāntarasya viṣayatāprasaṅgaḥ, tathāsyāpi janyajñānasyeti jñānārthayorhetuphalabhāvasamayātikramamātramatiricyate | sādhāraṇatvaparihārastūbhayorapi | na tu vyaktirūpārthotpattinirvāha ito'sya siddhaḥ | prakāśotpādane sarvaṃ prati prākāśyasaṃbhavaḥ | utpādanāprakāśatvasthitau naikamapi prati ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ |
[348,3]
yathā hi niviḍāndhakārapihitayorāmapakvaghaṭayorekatra vahnijanitatvameva vyaktatvamabhidadhāno nākṣayogyatāṃ tattvataḥ samādhātumīśaḥ, tathāyamapi jñānajantitvameva dṛśyatāmiti | yadi tu pradīpādiva prakāśarūpasyotpattirvijñānādapi svīkriyate, tadā parokṣaghaṭādasya viparyayaḥ paryavasyati | sādhāraṇadoṣastu dustyajaḥ |
[349,1]
pradīpavyakto'pi tarhi ghaṭaḥ sarvasya prakāśaḥ syāditi cet ? yādṛśī pradīpakṛtā prakāśatā anandhakārāvasthā yogyadeśasthatvādyapekṣajñānajananayogyatārūpā sā sādhāraṇī eva | jñānakṛtaiva tu vikalpasmṛtyabhilāṣādinā pravṛttyādisādhanī niyatā | sāpi yadi bhāsurateva tasya niṣpannā khyāyate, hanta sādhāraṇī pravṛttyādestatkālasātādinā vā sādhanī sarvasya syādityuktaprāyam | tasmāt, utpādamātre'tiśayāntare vā jñānātprakāśo na hi bāhyarāśeḥ | prakāśarūpasya samudbhave tu prasahya sādhāraṇatāprasaṅgaḥ || tasmāt jñānavyāpāro na grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇavyavasthānibandhanamiti ||
[349,2]
astu tarhi jñeyasya jñāne vyāpārād grāhyatvamiti cet — na, indriyasyāpi prasaṅgāt | sarūpajanakasya vā tattve samanantarapratyayaviśeṣeṇa vyabhicārāt | bāhyatve satīti viśeṣaṇasya ca tadvādinyeva śobhāsaṃbhavāditi nāyamapi pakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ | mā bhūt sārūpyamarthādutpadyamānaṃ jñānaṃ tadadhigativyāpāreṇa grāhakamityubhayavyāpārapakṣo'stu |
tatrārthavyāpārānnāvyāpṛtānāṃ grahaṇaṃ jñānavyāpārāśrayānnendriyasyāpi |
[349,3]
na hi jñānasya tatrādhigativyāpāra iti cet ? nāyamapi nyāyaḥ | sā hi adhigatirviṣayasvarūpā jñānarūpārthāntaraṃ jñānāntaraṃ vā syāt ? prathame pakṣe viṣayātmavat tasyā api siddherjñānavyāpāravirahaḥ | tadvad vā viṣayasyāpi jñānavyāpārāpekṣaṇe prācīno doṣaḥ | dvitīye tu jñānasyātmanyeva vyāpāra iti vyāhatam, vyāpāra evādhigatirityatrāpyetadeva dūṣaṇam, vyāpāratadvatorabhedasiddheḥ | evameva jñānajñeyadharmatvaparikalpanamapāstaṃ draṣṭavyam |
[349,4]
arthāntaratve ca viṣayasya kimāyātam, yathendriyasya ? yato nīlaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nendriyamiti syāt, tasya sādhigatiriti cet ? jñānajanyāyāḥ kiṃkṛtastatsaṃbandhaḥ ? tasyāpi vyāpārāditi cet ? evaṃ tarhi ubhayorubhayavyāpārasiddhā sādhigatiriti parasparaṃ grāhyatvaṃ grāhakatvaṃ vā syāt | na caivamindriyagrahaṇaprasaṅgaparihāraḥ | na hi cākṣurvyāpāram antareṇa rūpe'dhigatiḥ |
[350,1]
athendriyasya jñāna eva vyāpāro nādhigatau, rūpasya tu tatrāpīti cet ? ko nāma vibhāgamīdṛśaṃ kartu samartho'nyatra jāḍyāt ? na hi jñānajñeyābhyāṃ bhinnamarthāntaram adhigamarūpameva kiñcidupalabhyate, yatra yāvat jñānasyaiva vyāpāraḥ parikalpyeta, tatra ca viṣayasyāpyasti nendrivasya, kalyāṇakāmatāmātrametat | adhigaterarthasya ca viṣayaviṣayībhāvalakṣaṇa eva saṃbandha iti cet ? nanu sa evāyaṃ viṣayaviṣayībhāvo vyāpāravikalpena parīkṣyate | sa ca yasya na jñānajñeyayoḥ siddhaḥ tasyādhigamaviṣayayorapi kathaṃ sidhyet ? adhigatervā viṣayatvamakasmādicchan jñānasya kathaṃ pratikṣipet ? asti tāvadayaṃ vyavahāra iti cet ? asti, kevalaṃ kimasya mūlamiti cintyate — asaṃkīrṇalakṣaṇasvarūpavyavasthā vā, anādivitathavikalpābhyāsavāsanā veti |
[350,2]
kimasyā bojamiti cet ? kimanena ? na hi pareṇa tadaparijñāne asmābhirabhimatāsaṃkīrṇamanayorlakṣaṇamupadarśitaṃ bhavati | etena jñānāntaratvaparikalpanamadhigaterapāstam, tasyāpi tadvadeva tadviṣayatvasyāsiddheḥ | atadviṣayayā cādhigatyā so'rtho jñāta iti mahatī prekṣā | etena jñānavyāpāraṃ vādakāle nārthaṃ kurvatī vikurvatī vā buddhistadviṣayocyate, kiṃ tu tadadhigatimātramātanvatīti kalpanamapāstam | tasmānna vyāpāradvāreṇāyaṃ jñānajñeyavyavahāra iti sthitam |
[350,3]
nāpi jātiniyataḥ, kvacit kadācit kasyacit kenacit jñeyatayā vyavasthāpanāt | na hi nisarganiyatānāṃ gotvādīnāmīdṛśī vyavasthā | adyāpi vāvaśyavācyo lakṣaṇabhedo na ca śakya iti tadabhāve tu sattāmātraṃ jñānasya jñeyasya vā tattvanimittamiti sarvaḥ sarvārthabodhaḥ sidhyet | na vā kaścidapi, viprakarṣābhāvāt | nanu cāsti pratyāsattirindriyāṇāmarthaiḥ saṃyogasamavāyādilakṣaṇā, tadbalādupajāyamānaṃ jñānaṃ tattadarthaniyataṃ ṣoḍhāsannikarṣavirahaviprakṛṣṭārthavyāvṛttaṃ ca sidhyatīti kathamatiprasaṅgaḥ ? etadapi yatkiñcat | utpattiniyamo hyanena sidhyet, na tu kañcit prati grāhakatvaniyamo vijñānasya | tathā hi saṃyogādisannikarṣabalādarthena jñānaṃ janyate na tadvirahiṇā vyavahitādineti bhavatu, kasya punastadgrāhakamiti na niścayaḥ ? yenaiva tajjanitamiti cet ? ātmamano'kṣasaṃyogādayo'pi grāhyā iti nātiprasaṅganivṛttiḥ | na hi viṣayābhimate'pyasya kaścidupayoga indriyādiṣu saṃbhavī, yena grahaṇavibhāgaḥ syāt |
paricchittijananaṃ vyāpārāntaraṃ vā anantarameva cintitam |
[351,1]
tatra tasyaiva prakāśanaṃ, tena nātiprasaṅga iti cet ? grāhyagrāhakābhimatabhāgayoḥ aśakyāpahnavaḥ prakāśo'sti, karaṇādhikaraṇaśaktinibandhanaṃ tu yadi kiñcidasti, tad ucyatām | na ca sahaprakāśanamātrameva nibandhanaṃ candradvayasya, tayoreva vā parasparagrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ | nīlapītayorvā | ekaścandro mṛṣā, dvitīyabhāgo jaḍaḥ | manasaśca dvayorekadā vṛttyabhāvādityādi tu bāhyārthavādasthitau yuktam | tadarthaścāyaṃ vicāra iti | yadā tu bhāgayorapi na sahaprakāśanaṃ jñānasya jñānāntareṇa sahabhuvānanubhaveṣṭeḥ, tadeyamapi gatirnāsti | yadi tu durnītasamayānurodho na bādhakastadāntaḥparisphuratprītiparitāpādyākārastuṣārakarādyākāraśca samasamayameva vedyata iti tadapi nibandhanamanucintyate, na ca kṣamata iti sthitam |
[351,2]
kiṃ ca ghaṭenendriyasannikarṣo noṣṭreṇeti tadanubhavādeva niśceyam | tadanubhavatvaṃ cāsya tatsannikarṣeṇotpatteritītaretarāśrayadoṣaḥ, prakārāntareṇa tadanubhavasiddhau vā sannikarṣottarasya vaiyarthyāt | api ca tatsannikarṣeṇotpattestadanubhavatve vikalpamātravyavasthāpito'spaṣṭapratibhāso'rthasyānubhavaḥ syāt na spaṣṭaḥ, maitrasya caitraputratvatadgauratvavacceti dṛṣṭakṣatiḥ | tadayaṃ spaṣṭatayā pratibhāsamāno'rthābhimato bhāgaḥ kārakāntaravyāpāracintāvaidhuryāt prītiparitāpādivat svayaṃ viditamevātmānamākalayati |
[351,3]
yo'pi manyate, pūrvikaiva tu sāmagrī sajñānaṃ viṣayakṣaṇam | sālokarūpavat kuryād yena syāt sahavedanam ||
iti | tasyāpi, sāmagryā yadi niṣpanno vyakto'rtho vedanena kim | sādhāraṇatvadoṣaśca nāvyaktau ca sphuṭābhatā || ekasāmagrathadhīnatvamātreṇaivaṃ vyavasthiteḥ | kiṃ caivamindriyasyāpi prakāśatvaṃ prasajyate || sthairye tu viṣayo'pyekasāmagrījanitaḥ katham | viṣayeṇa ca vijñānaṃ saṃvedyata sahasphurat || atha vittirasaṃvittiḥ sarvameva subhāṣitam | svasaṃvedyatvapakṣe'dya duḥsaṃvedyamidaṃ bahiḥ || sāmagryā eva śakteścedvibhaktau vedyavedakau | rasarūpavadutpannau svabhāve ko'nuyujyatām || vedyavedakayo rūpaṃ niyataṃ yadi lakṣitam | tadutpādanaparyeṣṭeḥ sāmagrī śaktirucyatām || nairogye tu svarūpeṇa siddhe vācyaṃ bhiṣagbalam | vedyavedakayo rūpaṃ na cādyāpi nirūpyate || tataḥ svarūpe vaktavye sāmagrīparivartanam | aprastutābhidhānaṃ vā ḍiṇḍikācāra eva vā || tasmānna vedakaṃ kiñcinna vedyaṃ na ca vedanam | yadapekṣya tadā stheyaṃ svaprakāśamidaṃ jagat || prakāśate hi nīlādirna cānyat tatprakāśakam | tatsvaprakāśatā siddhā vijñānatvaṃ tadeva naḥ ||
ityantaraślokāḥ ||
[352,1]
evaṃ sati na vijñānaṃ nāma kiñcit niyatamasti, yato bhedena pratīyamānatvaṃ ghaṭādyākārasya tadbhedaṃ sādhayedityaprasiddhaviśeṣaṇo heturasiddhidoṣagrastaḥ | sādhyaśca tato bhedavyavahāro viśeṣaṇāsiddhereva na prakṛtopayogaṃ puṣṇāti | vijñānarūpatve'pi hi ghaṭasya yataḥ kutaścidvijñānāntarādapi bhedasiddherna bhedamātrasiddhyopayogaḥ | tasmād viśiṣṭāvadhitvena sādhyo bhedo na ca tamabadhiṃ sphuṭayituṃ śakta iti vyartha upanyāsaḥ |
[352,2]
nanu vijñānavādino'pi vijñānavyavahāro'sti | sa yathā tathā vā bhavannasmākamapi tadupādhisādhane śaraṇībhaviṣyati | loke ca kiñcid vijñānamiti pratītamasti | tata eva bhedaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | nātrāsmallakṣaṇena kiñcit |
[352,3]
na ca vastubalapravṛttānumāne samayānurodha iti cet ? vijñānavādinastāvad vijñānatvaṃ prakāśatā | grāhyagrāhakasaṃkhyātabhāgayoḥ sadṛśī ca sā || jñānānnāma tato bhedaḥ prakāśatvādvibhinnatā | sā pratijñāyamānaiva vyastāmīṣu ghaṭādiṣu || hetvasiddhiśca na hi na prakāśante ghaṭādayaḥ | ebhyastvanyo yadā dharmī dharmāsiddhistadā sphuṭā || bhedena jñāyamānatvasvarūpāsiddhireva ca | punaḥ prakāśamāsthāturhetvasiddhyādayaḥ punaḥ ||
tanna prativādimatāpekṣayā kṣamaḥ | loke cāntaḥsphuradidaṃ vijñānamiti gīyate | tadajñeyātmanastasmādbhedasiddhyāpi kiṃ phalam || vedyavedakarūpeṇa siddhayoryadi sādhyate | bhedavyavahṛtirnīlajñānayoḥ pauruṣaṃ bhavet || avedyavedakākārasvaprakāśasvabhāvayoḥ | asādhāraṇayorantarbahirvyavasitispṛśoḥ || ahaṅkārāṅgaghaṭayorbhedena yadi tuṣyasi | bhinnasantānayoḥ kiṃ na bhedasiddhirmude tava || atha na sphuraṇaṃ bhinnasantānapathavartinaḥ | vedyavedakatāhānirbhāne'pi na kimīkṣyate || bhinnasantānayoraikyaṃ na kaścinmanyate yadi | yadi manyeta tatrāpi bhedasādhanasādhunā || aho mahatparākrāntaṃ sthāne bāhyāpavādinā || santānabhede'pi yadā tu buddhyorvedāntikādiḥ pravadatyabhedam | na nīlabuddhyorapi caikyamanyastadā ka eṣa vyasanābhiyogaḥ ||
santi hi vijñānavādino'pi vicitrasthitayaḥ | tathā hi,
[354,1]
grāhyagrāhakabhāgabhāgiva jagatyekaṃ mano bhāsate bhinnaṃ vā dvayamātmavedanamidaṃ śītādi śātādi ca | śātādiḥ paramo'thaveha nihitaṃ nīlādyavidyāvaśāccitrākārakamekameva yadi vānākāramevāthavā ||
[354,2]
teṣāṃ ca balābalacintāyāḥ ka idānīmupayogo bahirarthasādhanābhiniveśena prayuktasādhanasya ? tasmāt pratyātmavedyatvādisiddhayathoktavijñānarūpasya ghaṭākārasya vijñānāntarasaṃmatād bhedasādhane na kiñcitphalamiti vyarthaḥ prayāsaḥ | nanu na pratyātmavedyo ghaṭākāraḥ sarvasādhāraṇatvāt, tataḥ svaprakāśaḥ sannapi sādhāraṇatvādartha evāyaṃ tato'pyabhedena pratītirvyavahārasādhanī prayukteti cet — na, sādhāraṇatvasyāpi prāgeva pratikṣiptatvāt | na hi tat prakāśamānaṃ rūpamavikalakāraṇādīnāṃ sannihitānāmiva vyavahitānāmapi pravṛttinivṛttī aprayojya sthātumarhatīti nivedanāt | asādhāraṇatve tarhi sannihitānāmapi na syāt | na vai sannihitānāmapi tadekameva rūpam, kiṃ tu tādṛśam |
[354,3]
bhede tarhi ekasaṃpratipattiḥ katham ? naiṣa doṣo bhinne'pi keśādau tasyā darśanāt | tatra bādhakadarśanānna prameti cet ? ihāpi vyavahitasyāpi pravṛttyādiprasaṅgaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate bādhakaḥ ? tādṛśatve'pi pravṛttyādireva hetuḥ, kevalaṃ tādṛśasyaiva prakāśasya keṣāñcit saṃbhavo nānyeṣāmiti kimatra bījamiti praśne vāsaneti brūmaḥ | keyaṃ vāsanā ?
tadupādānaśaktimātraṃ pūrvapūrvānādikālikavijñānaparamparāyātamabhinnaṃ bhinnamiva kayācidapekṣayā dṛśyaṃ kalpyata iti nirloṭhitamanyatra | tādṛgbījapariṇatisāmyāt keṣāñcit tādṛk jñānaṃ nānyeṣāmiti nātra kaścidupālambhaḥ, niyatatvādupādānopādeyabhāvaparamparāyāḥ, taimirikadvayadṛśyakeśādivat | tadvadeva vā pratighatvādekadeśāvasāyo'pītyalaṃ vistareṇa | ekaṃ kasmād vyavasitivaśād bhinnabhinne'pi neyaṃ bādhātaścenna mitiradhunā kiṃ na bādhopalabdhiḥ | sādṛśyaṃ tu sphuritumucitaṃ vāsanābījasāmyād vijñānānāṃ pratighavirahādekadeśo'pyadoṣaḥ ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ |
[355,1]
tasmāt siddhaṃ pratyātmavedyatvamapi | tathāpi kāṭhinyādayo na jñānadharmā iti cet — na, prakāśarūpatayā sarveṣāṃ jñānatvāt | nīlimānaṃ ca nāma jñānadharme sahate na kāṭhinyamiti sukumāraprajñaḥ | nanu yadeva nīlamālokitaṃ tadeva kaṭhinamanubhūyate, na caivaṃ vijñāne yujyata iti cet ? bahirapi bhramopalambhavataḥ nīlaṃ hi rūpamātraṃ, kaṭhinaśca sparśaḥ | na ca tābhyāmanyaḥ kaścidupalabdhigocaraḥ | guṇasya dravyāpāratantryāditi cet ? kimidaṃ guṇatattvam | yadi pāratantryameva, tadā sādhyāviśiṣṭo hetuḥ |
atha vyāvṛttibhedenānyadeva tataḥ, tathāpi viparyayabādhakapramāṇasyopapādayitumaśakyatvāt sandigdhavipakṣavyāvṛttikatvam | yadapyayaṃ, dravyāśrayyaguṇavān saṃyogavibhāgeṣvakāraṇamanapekṣaḥ iti paṭhati | tatrāpi,
[355,2]
dravyāśrayatvena guṇatvasiddhiḥ, guṇatvasiddhau ca tadāśrayatvam | parasparāpekṣamato dvayaṃ syāt svanītimātraṃ śaraṇaṃ tadasya ||
[355,3]
na tāmapramāṇayatā vivāde sopayogamityalaṃ carvitacarvaṇena | astu vā bāhyo guṇadvayādhāraḥ kaścidanyaḥ, so'pi yadi prakāśastadā na jñāne'nantarbhūya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ |
aprakāśatve hetorasiddhistadavasthā | nīlakaṭhinayoścaikadādhyavasāyo bhrāntireva | bādhakaścāsya parasparaṃ jñāne anantarbhāva eva yathoktakrameṇa | bījaṃ ca nīlanirbhāsajñānasya pravṛttyapekṣakaṭhinanirbhāsajñānabāsanāprabodhasādhanatvaniyama iti naivaṃvidhā jambukavikrośā yogācārakeśariṇamabhidravatīti |
[355,4]
yadapyuktaṃ nāhaṃ ghaṭa iti pratītiriti, tatrāpi yeṣāmiyamahaṃpratītirātmaviṣayā teṣāṃ ghaṭādāvabhavantīti ātmatvameva nivartayenna jñānatvam | vijñānaviṣayatvāśraye'pi na vijñānamātre maitrasyāhaṃpratyayaḥ, tasya caitracitte'pi prasaṅgāt | caitrasya tatrāstyeva sa iti cet ? maitrasyāpi kiṃ neti cintāyāmanyasantāne'nabhyāsa evottarīkartavyaḥ | sa cānabhyāso bahirmukhanirbhāsini ghaṭādyākāre'pi samastyeva | tadiyamahaṃkāravyāvṛttiḥ anyathāpyupapadyamānā na vijñānarūpatopatāpāya prabhavati |
[356,1]
athāpi syād yadvijñānaṃ tadavaśyaṃ svasya parasya vāhaṃkārasya gocarībhavati, na caivaṃ ghaṭākāra iti cet — na, viṣayiṇā jñānena viṣayasya vyāptyasiddheḥ | bhinno hi viṣaya iṣṭo, na kāryaḥ, kāraṇaṃ tu syāt | na ca kāraṇasya kāryasattāniyama iti vipakṣavyāvṛttisandehādanekāntaḥ | tadayamākārasya bāhyatāmabhivāhya bāhyavādavyasanino bhedasādhanavidhistapanīyamapanīya granthikaraṇavṛttāntamanuharati | na coktamātraṃ sādhyam, api tu prakaraṇāpannamiṣṭamaprakāśasya prakāśakavyāpāreṇa prakāśasya sato ghaṭādeḥ prakāśakād bhinnatvam, na ca tathā siddhiriti sādhanavaiyarthyādasādhanāṅgavacanaṃ vādino nigrahasthānam | naivaṃ vā, tathāpi suptataimirikādipratibhāsairanekāntaṃ ko nivārayati ? sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam |
iti cet ? sarvatrālambanaṃ jñānaṃ deśarūpānyathātmakam ||
ityapi tarhi vaktuṃ śakyam | kathaṃ grahaḥ svarūpasya parasyāpi kathaṃ grahaḥ | buddherātmani bhinne vā vyāpāravirahaḥ samaḥ || savyāpāre ca nirbhāti yathānyatra tathātmani | dīpavad vyavahāro'yamaśakyāpahnavo dhiyaḥ ||
ityantaraślokau |
[356,2]
tasmād yathānyathākhyātīti matiḥ, tathā,
[356,3]
abahirbahirākāramanīlaṃ nīlarūpataḥ | jñānameva na bhātīti sapathairyadi nirṇayaḥ ||
[356,4]
kimatra bījaṃ vyasane jñānasyārthātmano'pi kim | pradeśaniyatakhyātau codyametad dvayoḥ samam ||
[356,5]
āntaropaplavastatra śaktibhedayuto yadi | khyāyate heturatrāpi sa vaktuṃ kiṃ na śakyate ||
[357,1]
kiṃ ca,
[357,2]
sadanyathā vibhātīti deśabhede'stu sā gatiḥ | kālabhede tvasattvena prathanaṃ kathamanyathā || jīvannaṭo'nyathā nāma khyātīti na mṛto'pyalam | cittameva tataḥ sarvatrānyathā khyātumarhati ||
[357,3]
tato'nyathākhyātipakṣe'pi nānekāntaparihāraḥ | kālabhede'pi nātyantamasanneva, svakāle sattvāditi cet ? pratibhāsakāle'satastasya kālāntarasattāmātraṃ kvopayogi ? yatra yasya svasattopadhānenopayogo na sa tatra cirātītaḥ kṣamaḥ, yathā dagdhaṃ bījamambaraṃ vā, aṅkure kālimni vā | svasattopadhānena copapadyate'rthaḥ pratibhāsa iti viruddhopalabdhiḥ, yato vinaṣṭasyāpi śaktisaṃbhavaḥ | svasattopadhānena copayoga iti viruddhau dharmau | ihātītamapi kuśūlasthaṃ bījamaṅkure paramparayopayujyate, na tu svasattopadhāneneti viśeṣaṇaṃ tadartham |
pratibhāsamānaścārthaḥ pratibhāse svasattopadhānenaiva upayukto vaktavyaḥ, na paramparayā | pratibhāso hi tasya dharmo vā kāryaṃ vā syāt | tatra dharmatve sahabhāvaḥ | kāryatve svasattānantaryaniyama iti na kṣaṇenāpi vyavadhistadbhāvaṃ sahata iti svasattopadhānenaiva pratibhāse arthasyopayogaḥ siddhaḥ | tadabhāvāccātītaḥ prakāśitumaśakyaḥ |
[357,4]
tataḥ prakāśamāno'yamasanneva prakāśate | atītatvāt svasattāyā upadhānavidhūtitaḥ || tadabhāve'pi bhāse ca bhāsaḥ prāpto'sataḥ punaḥ | svavācaiva yataḥ sattvasyābhāve bhānamicchati ||
[357,5]
tadavaśyaṃ bahirarthapakṣe'pi bhrāntijñāne duṣpariharo'satkhyātipakṣaḥ | astu vānyathākhyātirubhayathāpi jñānavivarta eva sadṛśastasya sattvādaniṣṭimātreṇa nivārayituṃ na śakyate iti vyāpterabhāvādanekānta eva bhedena pratīyamānatvaheturbhedavyavahārasiddhāviti sthitam | nanu bhrānteṣvevaṃbhāve'pyanubhave kimāyātam ? tataḥ abhrāntatve satīti viśeṣaṇasyābhimatatvāt nānekānta iti cet — na, bādhakādhīnā hi bhrāntisthitiḥ, tasya coktenaiva krameṇātrāpi siddhatvāt | tathā hi,
[358,1]
svayaṃ prakāśādvijñānādasādhāraṇarūpataḥ | bhinnatve paravedyaḥ syādarthaḥ sādhāraṇastathā ||
[358,2]
na caivamupapanno'yaṃ niyamaḥ proktayuktitaḥ | tataḥ keśādivat kumbho jñānādbhinnaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ||
[358,3]
yaddharmavyatireke na yato dharmavyavasthitiḥ | anvayastasya dharmasya tato bhedaṃ nirasyati ||
[358,4]
tadayaṃ bāhyatvalakṣaṇasādhāraṇāsvaprakāśarūpatvaviruddho'sādhāraṇasvaprakāśatārūpo dharma upalabhyamāno ghaṭādiṣu tadbhāvamapākarotīti bādhakasāmarthyāttathāpratītirbhrāntireva, vṛttameva cedaṃ bādhakaṃ pramāṇaṃ notprekṣāmātreṇeti nātiprasaṅgopālambhaḥ, yadapi vijñānavādī pramāṇayati,
[358,5]
yadyat prakāśate tat tad vijñānaṃ svapnadṛṣṭavat | prakāśate ca nīlādiḥ svabhāvo heturityayam ||
[358,6]
tadāpyayaṃ prabandho'stu pratibandhasya siddhaye | jñānānvayavikalpānāmavakāśaśca dūrataḥ ||
[358,7]
svaprakāśamasāmānyaṃ vijñānamiti saṃmatam | tadrūpeṇa prakāśasya vyāptiścānyairatatkṛte ||
[358,8]
prakāśate ca nīlādi nānyeneti svayaṃ yadi | prakāśate svayaṃ nātaḥ pareṇeti na kiṃ matiḥ ||
[358,9]
dṛṣṭo'pi bhedavyāpāraḥ prastute yadi nocitaḥ | adṛṣṭaḥ sthāpyabhede tu bhavadbhiḥ kalpyate katham ||
[358,10]
nanu prakāśabhedī yaḥ svayamityādi dṛśyate | tatrāpi nātmani vyāptasvabhāvastu tathocyate ||
[358,11]
evaṃ prakāśate buddhiḥ svayamityapi gamyatām | khe svayaṃ śūnyatā yadvat paravyāpāravāraṇāt ||
[359,1]
tathātmavyāpṛtibhrāntibhraṃśanāya paraśrutiḥ | na vyāpāravaśā vṛttistadrūpaṃ tu tathā tadā ||
[359,2]
yathā nirlepamākāśaṃ prakāśaṃ ca svayaṃ tathā | asādhāraṇametacca pūrvameva samarthitam ||
[359,3]
tataḥ prakāśatā nāma sādhāraṇyaparakriye | sarvatra tulyadoṣatvānnirākṛtya vyavasthitā ||
[359,4]
tābhyāṃvirodho yuktyāto labdhastādrūpyanirṇayaḥ | tasmādviparyaye hetorvirodhādeva na sthitiḥ ||
[359,5]
prakāśatā ca siddheti jñānarūpāḥ śitādayaḥ | tadbāhyarūpapratyāśā pratyāśaiva hi kevalā ||
[359,6]
yadi svarūpamākārāścitrataikadhiyaḥ katham | bhedaḥ pratyaṇu vā buddheḥ tathā nānyonyavedanam ||
[359,7]
mithastathāpi vā vittau bāhyavallakṣaṇakṣatiḥ | bhede'pyevaṃ dhiyasteṣāṃ prakāśaghaṭanā katham ||
[359,8]
athaivameva nirbhāsaḥ svasantānadhiyo dhiyā | alīkākārarāśervā ko'parādhī bahirbhuvaḥ ||
[359,9]
alīkavedane kiṃ ca prakāśaṃ ca na cāparam | ato vipakṣasāmānyo hetuḥ saṃśayasādhanaḥ ||
[359,10]
alīkamanyatvetīdaṃ vyāvṛttyantaramīritam | tasya sandehavattve'pi prakāśe jñānatā sthitā ||
[359,11]
evaṃ prakāśamānasya jñānatve pratipādite | kvacit sarvatra vā vādādalīkatve'pi bodhatā ||
[359,12]
jñānameva tataḥ satyamalīkaṃ vā bahirna tu | bahirapyastu vā vastu prakāśasyāstu bodhatā ||
[360,1]
bhedābhedavikalpo'pi na prakāśasya bādhakaḥ | na vā yathoktasādhyena vyāpteriti kimarthakaḥ ||
[360,2]
pareṇa parasaṃvittiṃ yo'bhimanyeta taṃ prati | śeṣaṃ syādapi doṣāya brūmaḥ svapne'pi na tvidam ||
[360,3]
ekānekatvavirahāt niḥsvabhāvamidaṃ jaḍam | yathā tathā na kiñcittaṃ sattaikasya kathaṃ tataḥ ||
[360,4]
prakāśamānaṃ nīlādi jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā | iti prakaraṇe'smābhirbuddhitve heturucyate ||
[360,5]
tatraikānekaviraho yadi dharmāntarārpakaḥ | kiṃ naśchinnaṃ tāvatāpi nīlāderjaḍatā na hi ||
[360,6]
sattāyāṃ nanu siddhāyāṃ jaḍaṃ vājaḍameva vā | asatturaṅgaśṛṅgādi na hi tattve'numīyate ||
[360,7]
tathāpyaprastutamidaṃ sattācintāviyogataḥ | siddhāyāmeva sattāyāṃ viśeṣaścintyate yataḥ ||
[360,8]
sattāyāṃ saṃśaye'pyasmāt sacced vijñānameva tat | tataścādūṣaṇākhyātirasattāsiddhibādhayoḥ ||
[360,9]
prasiddhimātrarūpeṇa dharmitvānnāpyanāśrayaḥ | anyathā niḥsvabhāvatvahetorapyāśrayaḥ katham ||
[360,10]
tasminna bhāvamātraṃ cet jñānatāmātramatra ca | bāhyavastutvasiddhistu dvayorapi virodhinī ||
[360,11]
vastutopādhibodhatvaṃ sādhyamatra tvayeti cet | bodhatvamātraprastāve viśeṣaḥ kuta īdṛśaḥ ||
[360,12]
jñānatvaṃ vastutāvyāptaṃ tadabhāve bhavenna cet | viruddhāvyabhicāraḥ kva doṣo yadvāstu vastutā ||
[361,1]
kiṃ ca prakāśamātrātmavyatiriktānyathāthavā | sattā niṣeddhyābhimatā niḥsvabhāvatvahetunā ||
[361,2]
niṣedhe vyatiriktāyā na prakāśātmavāraṇam | asyaiva vāraṇe kena vāraṇādhyakṣabhāsinaḥ ||
[361,3]
anumānaṃ pramāṇatvād bādhakaṃ yadi kasyacit | pratyakṣamapi tadbhāvāt sādhakaṃ kiṃ na kasyacit ||
[361,4]
avaśyamante'dhyakṣasya prāmāṇyamanumāśrayet | prakāśamātrarūpe ca nānumāpekṣamakṣajam ||
[361,5]
athāyamanumānasya viṣayo'kṣadhiyo'paraḥ | prakāśarūpe'dhyakṣatvādanumāvasaraḥ kutaḥ ||
[361,6]
atha pratyakṣasiddhaṃ yanna tasyaiva nirākriyā | vyāvṛttibhedaḥ kaścātra vicārāsahatā yadi ||
[361,7]
vijñānasyaiva dharmo'stu śaśaśṛṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ | arthaśaktiviyoge vā dharmo'stu dhiya eva saḥ ||
[361,8]
arthaśaktiviyogaśca vicārāsahatā ca sā | jñānasyaiva na bāhyasyetyarthyate kimataḥ param ||
[361,9]
prakāśasyaiva cinteyaṃ tadgandho'pi bahirna hi | tannāgaśṛṅgasāmye'sya siddhe kiṃ na kṛtārthatā ||
[361,10]
bahirvadavabhāseṣu prajñaptā rūparāśitā | saṃskārādvedanāsaṃjñeabhinne kiṃ na bhedi te ||
[361,11]
mūlamevāprakāśasya duḥsthaṃ sattāvyavasthiteḥ | prakāśarūpasya sato dharmāntaramabādhakam ||
[361,12]
prakāśasyāpi taddoṣād yadi sattā davīyasī | aprakāśo'pyasattāyāḥ kimanyat sādhayiṣyati ||
[362,1]
asattaivāprakāśasya prakāśasya tu nātmanā | tenaivāsattvamityuktaṃ kalpite na tu yujyate ||
[362,2]
prakāśamānasya punaḥ prakāśādeva satyatā | abhāvo'vasitenaiva keśasyāpi jaḍātmanā ||
[362,3]
prakāśasaṃmatasyāpi nīlāderata eva hi | satyamarthakriyaivoktā tāṃ vinā na bhidā dvayoḥ ||
[362,4]
kriyāmātrānubandhācca vijñānasyāpyanityatā | kriyā'bhāvo yadā tvasmin sattā mukhyaiva bhāsanāt ||
[362,5]
na kṣaṇitvaṃ tadā tasya sattvaṃ ca vyabhicāryataḥ | sattvamarthakriyārūpaṃ sādhanaṃ tanna duṣyati ||
[362,6]
na vā tasyāpyanityatvaṃ parihṛtya daśāntaram | tatkṣaṇasyaiva saṃvitteranyathā na bhidā kvacit ||
[362,7]
kāryakāraṇabhāvo'yamāyātastarhi cennanu | sāṃvṛtasyāniṣedho'tra kṣaṇitāpyasya sāṃvṛtī ||
[362,8]
tattvato nityarūpaṃ cet saṃvṛtāvapi yanna sat | anityapratiṣedhāccet tathāpyasyāgatiḥ kutaḥ ||
[362,9]
bhāvaṃ kañcit puraskṛtya bhedābhedāvudīrayet | deśakālādibhedena svavinmātre tu kaḥ kramaḥ ||
[362,10]
svarūpaṃ buddhiraparairna yauti na bhinatti ca | svaparapravibhāgo hi dhiyo yācitamaṇḍanam ||
[362,11]
anyasyāvācyatā nāma svabhāvabhāvaśaṃsinī | tadeva rūpaṃ tattvasya taccādvaite pratiṣṭhitam ||
[362,12]
paraṃ hi vidvan niyataṃ niyataṃ pratipadyate | anyathāvittimātreṇa na pravṛttinivartane ||
[363,1]
prathamaṃ grāhakākāro bhinatti grāhyamātmanaḥ | deśarūpādibhedena tathā grāhyāntarādapi ||
[363,2]
advaitamevetarathā tadabhāve bhidāṃ dyati | bhedābhedau tato dvaite niyato nādvaye tathā ||
[363,3]
yāvacca svapnabodhāya kālabhedaṃ parāmṛśet | dhīrvikalpāntareṇeyaṃ kṣayeṇa grasyate'nyavat ||
[363,4]
tasmānna nityatā nāma tattvato na ca saṃvṛtiḥ | kṣaṇitātattvayoge'pi gṛhyatāmanumānavat ||
[363,5]
citraikavyavahāro'pi bhedāpohaparo mataḥ | ekānekaviyukto hi prakāśaḥ kevalo'tra san ||
[363,6]
sarvaśaktiviyuktena prakāśena satāpi kim | śakyabhāvānna kāryaṃ syāt svarūpaṃ tu kva gacchatu ||
[363,7]
prakāśasyāpi rūpaṃ cet vicāreṇa na labhyate | vicāramanumāṃ vidmo na sā pratyakṣabādhanī ||
[363,8]
guñjānalaviparyāsau bādhyate'kṣakṛto'pi cet | pararūpe bhramānnākṣaṃ svarūpe bhrāntatā kutaḥ ||
[363,9]
pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ ced vicārāvasaro hataḥ | bruvatā niyataṃ kiñcit sādhyaṃ vā bādhyameva vā ||
[363,10]
tatrāyuktiṃ bruvāṇasya ślāghā sadasi kīdṛśī | nānumāyāḥ parā yuktiḥ kiṃ siddhaṃ tadanādare ||
[363,11]
svīkṛtā tena setyasmāt tanmatyā bodhanaṃ yadi | abādhane'syāḥ svīkārāttaddhiyābodhanaṃ katham ||
[363,12]
sādhyaṃ na kiñciditi cet bādhāyā api sādhyatā | sāpi neti vaco vyartha praśnamātre'pi kiṃ phalam ||
[364,1]
phalaṃ yadi giraḥ kvāpi nānyat taccāvabodhanāt | vācaḥ pratyāyane śaktā nākṣadhūmādi sundaram ||
[364,2]
yadi hetuphale saṃvṛttadbhāvaḥ kena gṛhyatām | phalācca hetudhīrnūnaṃ na ced vyarthā vratādayaḥ ||
[364,3]
yo'pi tāpārdito'bhyeti candanaṃ na hutāśanam | vaktuṃ kiñcidanāśritya sajñānaṃ tu na vartate ||
[364,4]
vastu kiñcidupanyasya nyasyante yadi yuktayaḥ | śāstre pakṣagrahaḥ kiṃ na nacettat kena gṛhyatām ||
[364,5]
mokṣamārga yadā pṛṣṭo vyākuryāt śūnyabhāvanām | bodhayan śūnyatāṃ tarhi garhetpakṣagrahaṃ katham ||
[364,6]
tasmāt saṃvṛtimāśritya sādhyaṃ sādhanamasya vā | durvāramiti durvāraḥ pramāṇasya parigrahaḥ ||
[364,7]
saṃvṛttau mānamiṣṭaṃ cet vicāro'pyeṣa saṃvṛtiḥ | saṃvṛtāvapi neṣṭaṃ ced bruvan jetā yathā tathā ||
[364,8]
yathā hetuphale saṃvṛttathā saṃvādidhīrapi | anumāmicchato'dhyakṣaṃ neti ko'pyeṣa niścayaḥ ||
[364,9]
svavedane vivādaścet na saṃvṛtyaiva sādhanāt | tasmādaparamārthatve'pyāttā vittiḥ prabādhikā ||
[364,10]
saṃvṛtiścet kva niṣkarṣaḥ paramārtho'stu tāvatā | tataśca saṃvṛtāveva sāṃvṛtaṃ tyajyate katham ||
[364,11]
tatprakāśānvayaḥ sattāvyavahāro'stu cetasaḥ | na prakāśo na vā śaktiryasya tena tulā katham ||
[364,12]
tato vicārāsahatādidharmaḥprakāśāmānatvamabādhamānaḥ |
[365,1]
yadīṣyate cetasa eva so'stusthitā prakāśānmanasaḥ prasiddhiḥ ||
[365,2]
prakāśamūrteryadasattvamucyatesvakalpitaṃ sattvamapekṣya na kṣatiḥ |
[365,3]
prakāśamevaiti parastu vastusatsamaṃ dvayaṃ laukikasiddhabādhane |
[365,4]
nāsatprakāśavapuṣī na ca sattadanyairekena na dvitayamadvitayaṃ na tābhyām |
[365,5]
itthaṃ jagad yadi catuḥśikharīviyuktaṃko bhāṣyakāramatamadhyamayorviśeṣaḥ ||
[365,6]
arthakriyāpi paramārthata eva yeṣāṃyeṣāṃ prakāśavapuṣo'pi niṣedha eva |
[365,7]
teṣāṃ bhidā bhavatu kiṃ tu nisargadurgomārgo'yamātmavidi sāhasabhārasāraḥ ||
[365,8]
tadetat parasyottaraprabandhānurodhenaṃ prāsaṅgikaṃ kiñcidāyātamityalaṃ vistareṇa |
sthitametat prakāśamānatvena vijñānamātraṃ tribhuvanamiti ||
<sākārasiddhiśāstram>
{11.1}
<prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[367,1]
vidhūtakalpanājālagambhīrodāramūrtaye | namaḥ samantabhadrāya samantasphuraṇatviṣe ||
[367,2]
jīyānmunīndramatavārtikabhāṣyakāraḥsākārasiddhinayanāṭakasūtradhāraḥ |
[367,3]
saṃsāranirvṛtipathaprathamānagarva_sarvārivīraduratikramavikramaśrīḥ ||
[367,4]
vijñaptimātramakhilaṃ sthitametajjagattrayam | tatrāvāntarabhedasya balābalamihocyate ||
[367,5]
tathā hi bahirarthadūṣaṇādikrameṇa,
[367,6]
bāhyaṃ na tāvadidameva yataḥ prakāśarūpaṃ svato niyamataśca sahopalabdheḥ | yuktyā na cānyadiha saṃbhavi saṃbhave'pi na grāhyalakṣaṇamato matimātrametat ||
[367,7]
gauragāndhāramadhurasurabhisukumāraśātetarādicitrākāraṃ jagat | tathā ca sūtram, vijñaptimātraṃ bho jinaputrā yaduta traidhātukamiti, yadarthaṃ vārtikakāraḥ prayatnaparamparayā bahirartha eva sākāravādamuddīpayati | kathaṃ tarhi bhāṣyakāropajñamidamucyata iti cet ?
nirākāradiśānyairyojitatvāt, sattāmātrasthita ivānena prasādhita ityucyate, na punastasyaivopajñeti |
[367,8]
tatrāpare prāhuḥ | bhavantu sitaśātādayaḥ prakāśaikasvabhāvāḥ, svabhāvaśūnyatāṃ tu nātivartitumīśate | yadi yuktirekānekavirahalakṣaṇā bāhyamasaṃbhavi saṃbhāvayitumupanīyate, sā na vijñānasvabhāvatāmābibhrāṇebhyaḥ śubhrādibhyo bibheti | tasmāt sarvadharmaśūnyataiva jyāyasī yathā prathitamāgame bahuśaḥ | vārtike'pi, yathā yathārthāścintyante viśīryante tathā tathā || (pra. vā. 2. 209)
iti | saṃvṛtimātraṃ tu vijñānanītiriti |
[368,1]
atrāpare samādadhati | bhavatvākārāṇāṃ bādhanādalīkatvaṃ prakāśamātraṃ tu satyamāmnāyaḥ, tadātmavedanasya bhrāntatvāyogena pratyakṣatvāt | prakāśasya prakāśa eva nijaṃ rūpamiti na tat tasya viplavopanītam, yena tadvedanaṃ bhrāntiḥ syāt | nīlaṃ tu rūpāntaratvāt viplavopanītamapi syāditi syāttadvedanaṃ bhrāntiḥ | tato'sti nīlādau bādhakasyāvatāro na prakāśe | kalpitālīkayostu niṣedho boddhavyaḥ sarvatreti ||
[368,2]
atra cintyate | ko'yaṃ prakāśo nāma nīlādibhyo vyatiriktaḥ, avyatireke bādhābhayanivṛtteḥ ? na ca vyatirikte kiñcit pramāṇamasti | na tāvat pratyakṣam, prakāśamānarūpānnolādaparasyopalambhāsaṃbhavāt | na cānumānam, kadācidapi pratyakṣatāmananubhavataḥ kenacit saṃbandhagrahaṇānupapatteḥ |
kiṃ ca,
[368,3]
prakāśa ātmasantāne'numānena pratīyate | parokṣaviṣayeṇeti kā dhikkṛtirataḥ param ||
[368,4]
vyaktamidaṃ śabarasvāmidarśanaṃ śaraṇīkṛtamiti kimatra vaktavyam ? tadayaṃ dṛśyātmā kumbhādibhyo vyatirekeṇānupalabhyamānaḥ sāmānyādivanna sadvyavahāragocarībhavitumarhati |
anyathā teṣāmapyaniṣedhaḥ,
[368,5]
nityatvāṅgīkṛtestaccet kramādivirahādasat | na pramāvyāpakābhāvo dṛśyādṛṣṭeranādare ||
[368,6]
kathaṃ vā viṣāṇaguṇakarmāderniṣedha iti yatkiñcidetat | atha nīle bodharūpe pratīyamāne nīlabodhātmanoḥ pratītiraśakyāpahnaveti na siddhānupalabdhiriti cet ? tarhi gavi śābaleye pratīyamāne ubhayātmapratītyā pratyavatiṣṭhamānaḥ kathaṃ niṣedhyaḥ ? pṛthakpratītyabhāvastu sādhāraṇaḥ | avidyāvaśāt prakāśanīlayorapṛthakkathanamiti cet ? guṇadravyayorapyevaṃ bhaviṣyati | yadi samavāyaniṣedhe nirbandhaḥ, kimavidyāvaśāt pṛthagadarśanamathābhāvādeveti sandeha ubhayorapi śakyaḥ | tadeva tasya darśanamiti karmāderapi śakyam | tṛṇāgre kariśatasya vā, yadrūpaṃ dṛśyatāprāptaṃ pṛthak taccenna dṛśyate | śatadhā viprakīrṇe'pi nīle tadvidyate katham ||
tasmāt, na santi sāmānyaguṇādayo yathā sitādibhedeṣu niraṃśabhāsiṣu | tathā prakāśāntaramapyasattataḥ sitādibādhe kimabādhasaṃbhavaḥ ||
kiṃ ca,
[369,1]
deśasyāpi bhidā yadi svatanuvad bhidyeta bhāso dvayoratyantaṃ tulayaikadhībiṣayayorapyevamālokanāt ||
[369,2]
māyāgolakayorhyatyantasādṛśyenaikabuddhirbhinnakāla eva, ekadā tu bhinnadeśayorbhedaniścayanāntarīyaka eva paṭurābhāsabhedaḥ | tasmād deśabhede nirvibandhaḥ pratibhāsabhedastanniścayaśca |
[369,3]
deśe vā bhidirūpameva na paraṃ rūpaṃ na deśo'paraḥ |
[369,4]
nanu vātātapayordeśābhede'pi svabhāvabheda iti cet — na, tayoravayavirūpatayā utpatteḥ, ekaghanākārayoḥ sapratighayoranyo'nyadeśaniveśaḥ | paramāṇunikarastu vyatikaramāsādayati | tathā ca sati,
[369,5]
bhinnātmā marudātapāṇunicayo bhinnapradeśo na kim ||
[369,6]
tato yathā svabhāvabhedastathā deśabhedo'pīti na deśo nāmānyaḥ svarūpāt | tatastadabhede svarūpābheda eva prakāśasyāpi |
[370,1]
tadvad yadyaṇusaṃhaterupagamo doṣo'pi tadvad bhavet sthūle vā pratighe'pi deśabhidayā doṣastathaiva sthitaḥ | kiṃ ca vyāptirihānyathāpyuparatā khaṇḍe'nyathā bhāsanaprāptestadvaśataḥ sitādini tato yāvat prakāśasthitiḥ ||
[370,2]
yāvaddeśo hi nīlādyākārastāvad vyāptivirahe khaṇḍapratibhāsanaprasaṅgo nīlādau tadvaśataḥ pṛthagiṣṭaprakāśavaśāt | tato yāvat prakāśanaṃ sitādestāvattasya prakāśākhyasya sthityā bhāvyam | tatastāvaddeśavyāpinastasyāpi nīlasyevāvayaviparamāṇurūpacintāyāṃ punaḥ sādhāraṇadoṣānna muktiḥ | tasmānna nīlādiniṣedhe kasyacit sthitirbhedasyaivābhāvāt pratibhāsabhedābhāvāditi ||
[370,3]
atha kṣaṇayorabhedabhāsane'pi yathā bhedasiddhirbādhakāt, evamihāpi | yathā hi kāryaviśeṣasya bhāvābhāvāvanyathānupapadyamānau tayorbhedasādhanau tathā bādhakasya bhedena vṛttiḥ prakāśanīlayorapi | tato bādhyānnīlādabādhyaḥ prakāśo bhinna eveti cet ? ucyate, abādhyatā nāma paryadāsaprasajyabhedena dvidhā | paryudāso'pi prakṛtavyaktiviṣayaḥ aspṛśyādivadbādhāntaramebopanayediti, abrāhmaṇakṣatriyavajjātiparyudāsāt |
[370,4]
abādhā nāmeyaṃ pramitibalasiddhiryadi matā pramityornaikāpi svavidi bhidurāyāṃ prabhavati | abhāvo bādhāyāḥ punarasati sādhāraṇatayā pade saṃdehasya prathayatu kathaṃ bhedamamutaḥ ||
[370,5]
prasajyapratiṣedhapakṣe hi bādhāsphuraṇamātramabādhārthaḥ | tacca sandigdhasattāke'satyapi samānam, kathaṃ tato nīlāderbhinnavasturūpatāṃ prakāśasya sādhayet ?
nīlādibādhyamabādhyastu prakāśa iti bhinnarūpasiddhau kaḥ sandeha iti cet ? naibam, abādhāyā bādhakāsphuraṇamātratvāt, sattāsandehe bādhitādapi nīlādbhinnarūpasiddherayogāt |
ataeva pade sandehasyetyuktam |
[370,6]
kṣaṇabhaṅge tu bādhakāntarabalādaśakyastatparihāraḥ | naitādṛśāsārasādhanapratyāśā |
na ca tadvadatrāpi śakyamabhidhātum | tatra hi kadācinmadhūdakāharaṇādivat sthūlakālāpekṣayādhyakṣeṇa vyavahṛto'rthakriyāśaktikramaḥ kadācidaśakyo'pi kṣaṇāpekṣayā sāmarthyāyātaḥ svabhāvabhedaṃ vedayet | sakalakriyākṣayiṇi kṣaṇe'bhāvaprasaṅgāt, kṛtasya kartuṃ na śakyatvāt |
[371,1]
so'yaṃ kāryakramo na kāraṇakramamatikramituṃ kramata iti yuktam | na ca tatheha prakāśamātrasādhyaṃ kiñcit siddhamadhyakṣataḥ, sāmarthyāyātaṃ veti | na cāpoddhāreṇa kāryabhedavyavasthāpito'pyātmabhedaḥ sakṛdabhedabhāsini tāttviko bhavitumarhati vikalpamātraniveśino'nyatra, pradīpe tamaḥkṣayāvakāśapiñjaraṇopayogiprakāśapiśaṅgarūpavat | abhinnāvabhāsini ceyaṃ cintā | na ca kṣaṇānāmabhedāvabhāsanam, sakalakālakalāvyāpirūpapratibhāsasya sakṛdeva paryavasāne sarvasya trikālālokaprasaṅgāt | na caivamadhyakṣavyavahāryo'pi kāryabhedo bhāvābhāvadaśābhyāṃ kāraṇabhedāya prabhavet | ekīkṛtya grahaṇe hi ya evaikakṣaṇe bhāvo'bhāvo vā kāryasya sa eva kṣaṇāntare'pi, vivekābhāvāt |
[371,2]
tasmāt kṣaṇamātrasthāyinaiva rūpeṇa yathāsya viṣayo janakastathedamindriyajñānamapi tadanukāri tenaiva rūpeṇa grāhakam | avasāyastu tadvyāpāraṃ tirayati | atra tu pratibhāsa evābhedena sphuṭataro'nubhūyate | tathāpi bhedakalpane kimaparāddhamupādhisahasreṇa ? na cānupalabdheranyad vārakaṃ nāmetyuktaprāyam | tadiyamabādhā dṛśyānupalabdhisaṃbhave pratijñāyamānā svayameva viśīryate nottarāntaramapekṣata iti |
[371,3]
kiṃ ca bādhātra nātreti pṛthagbhāse dvayorbhavet | anirbhāse tadaṅgasya tatrāsiddhisthitaḥ kutaḥ ||
[371,4]
siddho'pi tatra hetuścenna samarthaḥ prakalpate | nūnaṃ na sādhyasaṃbaddho nākāre'pi tataḥ kṣamaḥ ||
[371,5]
svabhāvaṃ kāraṇaṃ vārtho'vyabhicāreṇa sādhayan | kasyacid bādabādhāyāṃ svabhāvānna nivartate ||
[371,6]
nanu prakāśo nīlādau pratibhātyeva dehinaḥ | tanmātre bādhakābhāvaḥ khyāyamānaḥ kṣamo na kim ||
[371,7]
nīlasvabhāvābhiduraprakāśakathanena kim | na hi tasyaiva bādhāyā virahaṃ vaktumudyamaḥ ||
[372,1]
nīlasya syāt prakāśaścetprakāśaḥ kimataḥ param | parato'pi bhavannasya prakāśaḥ śakyavāraṇaḥ ||
[372,2]
nānyato'pi prakāśo'sya prakāśo'syānya eva cet | na tannīlaṃ prakāśyeta prakāśe'nyasya tasya kim ||
[372,3]
saṃbandhasya ca bādhyatvāttasyeti na samanvayaḥ | ṣaṣṭhyā lābhe'pi kathamapyaśakyo rūpasaṃkaraḥ ||
[372,4]
yataḥ kuto'pi vā tasmāt prakāśo'syānapahnavaḥ | tadabādhe ca na phalaṃ na tanmātraṃ ca kiñcana ||
[372,5]
pratyāśayā tvabhimataṃ prasiddhamabhidhīyatām | āśrayāsiddhinirdhūtā hetavo'pyata eva ca ||
[372,6]
abādhyatvaprasiddhārthāḥ saṃkalpakalite'tha cet | tasyāmarthasamānatvād vidhisiddhau na sādhutā ||
[372,7]
abādhayaiva sattvaṃ cet sattve hetustataśca sā | iti cakrakamāyātaṃ māyāmetāmapohati ||
[372,8]
athāpyabādhā bādhāyāḥ sphuraṇe satyapodyate | tadabhāve tu siddhaiva saṃdehapadamīdṛśī ||
[372,9]
vargadharmastvāśrīyamāṇo na cakrakamatikrāmati |
[372,10]
āśrayo'pyastu hetustu kathyatāṃ bādhabādhanaḥ | svayaṃvedanamevātha pṛthag nāstīti darśitam ||
[372,11]
na ca svavittirityeva yuktaḥ saṃpratyayo'pi vaḥ | svavittāvapi nīlāderyadā bādhābhidhāvati ||
[372,12]
svasaṃvittirna nīlasya yadi kiṃ na prakāśate | prakāśyantāṃ pareṇeti na śakyamidamīdṛśam ||
[372,13]
pareṇa parasaṃvido'nyatra vistareṇa nirastatvāt | asattvānna paramiti cet ?
mā bhūt paratvam, svattvaṃ saṃbhavatītyetāvataiva tena vedanasiddhernāparamupayogi, svavinmātrarūpatvāttasya | kalpitatādātmyanna doṣa iti cet ? bālapratāraṇametat | pratibhāsādeva hi tādātmyakalpanam, tatkṛtaśca pratibhāsa iti vyaktamitaretarāśrayatvam |
[373,1]
na pratibhāsanāt kalpanam, api tu pratibhāsāvasāyāditi cet ? so'pi pratibhāsāvasāyaḥ pratibhāsāditi cakrakamastu, tādātmyakalpanātaḥ pratibhāsastatastadavasāyastatastatkalpanamiti | tatkalpa namapi na tādātmyakalpanātaḥ, kiṃ tu kalpanāviṣayīkṛtaṃ yattādātmyaṃ tata iti cet — na, tasya kalpanātaḥ prāgabhāvāt, anyathā kalpitatvānupapatteḥ | na ca kalpitaṃ kvacidarthakriyāyāmupayujyamānamupalabdham, tathātve satyatāyā eva prasakteḥ |
[373,2]
etenālīkatādātmyakīrtanamapi pratyuktam, kvacidupayoge'līkatvasyāpyanupapatteḥ |
anyathā nāmamātrakriyāyāṃ niṣedhānirbandhāt | kvacidupayoginaḥ prakāśamānasyāpi bādhanādalīkatvamaviruddhamiti cet ? prakāśasya na tarhi bādhitumaśakyatvāt kvacid upayogamapi yadi na bādhate bādhakaṃ kimavaśyaṃ bādhakamabhidheyamiti kuto'līkatādātmyasya ?
atha sāmarthyādarthaśaktiṃ bādhate na sākṣāt ? bhavatu kimatra nirbandhena śaktibādhāyāḥ siddhatvānnālīkamupayogi tādātmyamiti sthitam |
[373,3]
yadapyucyate | vijñānameva prakāśarūpatvāt prakāśamānamanādibhrāntivāsanopaplavatvād bhrāntamalokairnīlādibhirākāraiḥ prakhyāti svapnādivaditi, tadapi etena prativyūḍham |
[373,4]
nīlādivyatiriktasya vijñānanāmno'nupalabdheḥ prakriyāghoṣaṇāmātrametat | sādhyaśūnyaḥ svapnadṛṣṭāntaśca | api caivamalīkatayā kārakaśakterabhāvānnīlādiriti itthaṃbhūtavivakṣāyāmapi sahaprakhyānamātramartha iti vyaktamuktastatprakāśyatāvirahaḥ | tat kathaṃ svasaṃvedanātikramaḥ ? athāvidyāvāsanāvaśāt tathā khyātīti tatprakāśyataiva bhaviṣyatīti cet ? evaṃ satyavidyāhetureva syānna prakāśikā | prakāśarūpasya tu tasya tasyāḥ sakāśādudayaḥ, pradīpasyeva svahetoriti kutaḥ svaprakāśanāśaḥ ?
[373,5]
evamapi paraprakāśyatāvyavasthāyāṃ cānubhavasyāpi prasaṅga iti na kiṃcit svaprakāśaṃ nāma | tathāpyasaṃbhavādeva svasaṃvedanānna kvacit sattāsiddhiḥ | tannāyaṃ nyāyaḥ, prakāśarūpajanakāpekṣayā kṣayaḥ svasaṃvitteriti, evaṃ nīlāderapīti siddhā svasaṃvittiḥ |
athānīlasyālīkatvānna kāryatā tataḥ prakāśanamātramavidyayā prakāśena vā, anubhavasya tu vastutvāt samanantarapratyayena jananamevocyata iti cet ? tadapi yatkiñcit | anubhavo'pi hi svasaṃvedanādeva vastu tato nīlasyālīkatvaṃ nāma tadabhāvāt, tadabhāvaścālīkatvāt kāryatāparipanthina iti ||
[374,1]
api ca, nīlamalīkamastu na vā, kāryatā tu kathaṃ vāryate ? apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi svabhāvaniṣpattau bhāvaḥ kārya uktaḥ |
[374,2]
kādācitkatayā siddhā nīlasyāsya sahetutā | nityaṃ sattvamasattvaṃ vā hetoranyānavekṣaṇāt ||
[374,3]
evaṃ deśādyaniyamo'pyupalakṣaṇīyaḥ | na cānyasyāpi kāryatāvyavahāranibandhanam anyadasti deśakālapratiniyamasiddhāṃ parāyattatāmavadhūya | anyathā cānubhavasyāpi mā bhūt |
tadayaṃ śraddhāmātraviṣayasya tādṛśādeva janmajalpanaṃ dṛṣṭāt kutaścidākārāntarasya dṛṣṭānutpattiṃ pratikṣipatīti kimatra brūmaḥ ? etenābhūtvābhāve'pi śaktyabhāvānna kāryatvamiti nirastam, uktakrameṇa śaktivyavasthānāt | śraddhāviṣayasya tu cintyatāmadarśanāt | mā bhūt śaktiḥ, parāpekṣodayatayā kāryatvaṃ tu kiṃ nivartate, atadvyāvṛtteranapāyāt ?
[374,4]
atha vastudharmaḥ kāryatvam, na ca śaktimantareṇa vastutvam | tarhi śaktirapyastu, tadvyāptavastudharmakāryatvasya darśanāt | śaktyabhāvāt tadeva nāstīti cet — na, asiddhatvāt | kāryatve tu na sandehaḥ kāryāntaravat | tasmād yadi śaktikāryatvayoḥ pratibandhaḥ śaktiranumīyamānā kvacidastu nānūhamātreṇa pratikṣepaḥ | pratibandhābhāve tu siddhaṃ kāryatvam | ataḥ kathamucyate nīlasyākāryatvāt prakāśamātrahetubhiḥ yato na svasaṃvedanamiti |
[374,5]
kiṃ ca prakāśanamātraṃ kasyacit kenacidityapratītopādānāntarasaṃbhave pūrvāparakṣaṇānāmabhedādhyavasāyād ghaṭādivadālokena syādapi vaktum, alīkābhimate tu kīdṛśī durgṛhītiriyam ? apūrvotpattistu na virudhyate kevalaṃ nīlatayeva prakāśatayāpīti | mā bhūd vā sarvathā kāryatvam, tadāpi parāpekṣāniyame paraprakāśyatāśaṅkāpi syāt | sarvathā nirapekṣatve niḥsaṃśayaḥ svayaṃ vedanābhāvaḥ sarvākārāṇām | tatra ca bādhasandarśane'nyatrāpi siddhaḥ sattāśvāsavirahaḥ | athavā,
[375,1]
nīlādbhinnamabādhayā yadi mataṃ bādhāvidhūtiḥ kuto'nāropāditi yadyabādhanaphalādanyo'nyabhāvāśrayaḥ |
[375,2]
bādhyamānameva nīlamāropitamāhuḥ | tadā bādhyatāyā eva phalamanāropitatvaṃ kathamabādhasiddhaye prabhavet ?
[375,3]
vijñānasya tadeva rūpamiti cennīlātmanastanna kim |
[375,4]
yathā hi prakāśasya prakāśa eva rūpam na tu tasya viplavopanītamityucyate, tathā nīlasyāpi nīlataiva rūpaṃ na tat tasya viplavopanītamityucyamānamapi na vaktraṃ vakrīkaroti |
na ca nyāyasya vibhāgena vṛttiḥ, yataḥ ekamupādeyaṃ heyamanyaditi syāt | atha prakāśamantareṇa na nīlasthitiḥ, nīlamantareṇāpi na prakāśasthitiḥ | pīte'stīti cet ? astu, na tu nīladharmaḥ | prakāśaśabdasāmyāccet ? tarhi pītadharmaprakāśāpekṣayā prakāśavinākṛtasyāpi nīlasya sthitirapahnavasya viṣayaḥ |
[375,5]
tatastasya tadeva rūpamiti neyaṃ prakāśaikaniyatā kalpanā, yatastasyaivānāropitatvena bādhāvaidhuryāśvāsaḥ | ubhayostarhi parasparaṃ vyabhicārādanāyāsasiddho bhedaḥ sidhyatu |
nīlotpalaṃ ca nidarśanaṃ smārayāmaḥ, vastrodakasya nidarśayitumaśakyatvāt | sthitipracyutilakṣaṇayoriva viruddhayordharmayoruddiṣṭādhārayoranupalabdhereveti bhavanta evātra pramāṇam |
tadalamabhiniveśavaśatayā | tasya tadeva rūpamiti śraddheyasya,
[375,6]
saṅkalpaikaniveśino yadi tathā nirbhāsinaḥ kiṃ na tat ||
[375,7]
satyatvaṃ nīlasya, kevalaṃ svarūpanirbhāsa evāsya sattāsiddhāvadhiko'parādhaḥ |
kiṃ cāpūrvo'yamupāyastasya tadeva tattvamiti bādhāvidhūtaye | bādhyamapi hi pradhānasāmānyādi, yad yena rūpeṇa vikalpitaṃ vā vibhāti vā tasya tadeva tattvaṃpramāṇatastattu sadanyathā vā bādhāvakāśo dvitaye'pi tasmāt |
nīle prakāśe vā | yadi paramasiddhyādidoṣasya vibhāgena vṛttau vibhāgaḥ, na tu tadeva tattvamiti kṛtvā | kiṃ ca,
[375,8]
āropitaṃ kalpitameva bādhyaṃ prakāśabhṛd bādhyamalīkamāhuḥtattvaṃ tataḥ kalpitaniṣṭhameva mā vāstu dṛśyaikagataṃ kathaṃ syāt ||
[376,1]
āropitatvaṃ jalavat kalpita eva vyavahriyate kevalaṃ bādhye | prakāśamānaṃ tu bādhitamalīkamapi vyapadiśanti, dvicandravat | tato yadi dṛśyamapyāropitamiti vaktavyam, ucyatām | dṛśyamevāropitamiti tu kuta etat ? tasmānna kalpitamāropaparihāreṇa vyavasthitaṃ pramāṇasiddhādanyatra | ataḥ pramāṇena siddhirbādhā vā nirūpaṇamarhati |
na tu tasya tadeva tattvamityeva bādhoddhūtiḥ siddhirvā |
[376,2]
tadayamapi vibhāgaḥ kriyamāṇo nīlādayaḥ saṃvṛtisantaḥ pratīyamānatve'pi bādhyamānatvāt | nīlādipratibhāsaṃ tu prakāśaśarīraṃ vijñānaṃ paramārthasat, bādhakāyogāt, pramāṇasiddhaśaktiyogācceti hastasamāracita eva pratibhāti | nīlavyatirikte hi prakāśe nīlavad vyāpakānupalambhasya pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro nānicchāmātreṇa nivarteta ityādyuktam |
bādhā ca prakāśābhimatasyāprakāśāt kīdṛśī paretyapi | tathā śaktirapyākāragocaraiva ityanantaram |
[376,3]
vyatirekaścāyaṃ kṛtakānityatvavat kalpanāmātropanītaḥ pratibhāti, na sākṣānnirbhāsī | yamalakavat, dvicandravad vā | bhinne ca pratibhāsamāne dharmiṇi śakyamadhigantumatra dharmo'yaṃ saṃbhavī, na saṃbhavī cātreti | viśeṣato vyāpakānupalambhasya viparyayeṇa vastudharmasyaivopaneyatvāt | sarvaśca bhedasādhano vyavahārasādhana eva, viruddhadharmasaṃsargamantareṇa kvacidapi bhedāsiddheḥ | anyathā na kvacidabhedo nāma viruddhau ca dharmau na kalpanāmātreṇa bhintaḥ |
pramāṇataśca bhinnādhikaraṇāveva pratyetavyau, nirādhārayoḥ bhinnādhārayorvā pratītau na pramāṇāpramāṇayoranyataravyāpāro virodhasiddhirvā | bhinnadharmiṇośca tayoḥ siddhau ko'paro dharmibhedasādhanavyavasāyaḥ ?
[376,4]
ataeva vyavahārasiddhirmukhaṃ pratīti nirṇayaḥ | tatra dharmibhedasiddhiḥ kvacid deśabhedena golakavat, kvacit kālabhedena | yadadhikāreṇocyate, ata eva tayoravasthayoḥ vastubhedo niśceya iti | na hi tatrāpīyaṃ kuśūlāvasthā, iyaṃ kṣetrāvasthā ceti | kālabhedenānupadarśane karaṇākaraṇābhyāṃ bhedaḥ śakyadarśanaḥ |
[376,5]
tāvatā ca bhedasiddhiravasiteti kriyākriyopanyāso vyavahārasādhana eva | yatra tu na deśakālābhyāṃ bhedollekhaḥ, tatra pratibhāsabheda eva śaraṇamindriyabhedo vā |
pānakasya rūparasādivat, cārvākasya svābhyupagama iva buddhiśarīrayoḥ | sa hi śailādivikalpaṃ karacaraṇādyākārāccharīrādvisadṛśamanudāharaṇe kenākāreṇa śailādivikalpatāṃ sphuṭayet ? yatra tu pratibhāsabhedagandho'pi nāsti kalpanākārādanyastatra nīlotpalādivadabheda eva tāttvikaḥ | abhinnavedanasyaikye yannaivaṃ taddhi bhedavat | sidhyedasādhanatvasya bhedābhedau kimāśrayau ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[377,1]
tasmād bādhābādhalakṣaṇaviruddhadharmādhyāso dharmiṇaḥ pratibhāsabhedamantareṇa na bhedavyavahārāya prabhavati | kevalaṃ bhedasādhanaṃ sattāsādhanarūpatvānna trayīṃ doṣajātimatipatati | yadapyucyate, yadyena rūpeṇa naikaṃ nānekaṃ, na tat tena sat | tad yathā duḥkhaṃ sukharūpeṇa | naikaṃ nānekaṃ ca vijñānaṃ nīlādirūpeṇeti vyāpakānupalabdhiriti, tadapi hṛdayaparitoṣamātrametenaiva nirastam | tathāhi na vijñāyate na vijānātīti vā vyāpāranibandhanaṃ vijñānatvamiṣṭamanyatra niṣedhāt, kiṃ tu svaprakāśatāsvabhāvam | sa ca prakāśastenātmanā asanniti na tādātmyaniṣedhamātramabhimatam, kiṃ tu svenātmanā sanneveti |
[377,2]
anena tadvad doṣānavatārādityapyākṣiptam | anyathā na vyatirekasiddhirbandhyāsute'pi vyavacchedamātreṇa prasaṅgāt | tataśca bādhābādhābhyāmeva bhedasiddhirityasmānna kaścidatirikto'rtha upātta iti tenaiva gatametat | tathāpi kiñciducyate | ihākāravyatiriktaprakāśasādhanaprakaraṇe'pratibhāsamāna eva vā prakāśo'numānena sādhayitavyaḥ, pratibhāsamāna eva vā ākārād vyatirikto vidhātavyaḥ, ubhayathāpi tu vidhisādhanādhikāre kaḥ prastāvo vyāpakānulambhasya ? tadāhitena rūpeṇa sattve'pi svarūpeṇa yadi asattvaśaṅkāyāḥ na nivṛttiḥ śṛṅgasyeva kuto bhedasiddhiḥ ?
[377,3]
atha tayorabhāvo bhāvāntarasvabhāva evābhimataḥ tadā svabhāvahetureva prayoktavyaḥ, vidhiviṣayatvād vivādasya | yadā tu tadabhāve'pi tat syāditi saṃśayīta kaścit, tanmātre yukto vyāpakānupalambhaḥ | na caikānekaviyoge'pi sattvaśaṃkāyāḥ prastāvaḥ | na ca viparyayavivakṣāyāṃ kṣemaḥ | tadā hi yad yena rūpeṇa sat, tat tena ekamanekaṃ veti darśanīyam | na cātra dṛṣṭāntaḥ pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro vā śakyanirvāhaḥ | na hi prakāśamātraṃ kvacit siddhamanyasya cāsattvāditi kuto dṛṣṭāntaḥ, kva pakṣadharmopasaṃhāro vā, anyasādhanābhāvāt, tatsādhanatve vā anavasthāprasaṅgāt ?
[378,1]
prakāśaśca prakāśarūpeṇa sanniti pakṣadharmopasaṃhārakāle vā nāprakṛtopālambhaparihāraḥ | na hi svarūpeṇaikānekatve vivādaḥ | kiṃ tvākāreṇa saha bhedābhede | ekānekatvavivādino vā sattvasiddhiriti kutaḥ ? śaktyabhāvādeva tarhi nīlādirasannekānekatve'pīti kiṃ tadupanyāsaprayāsena, tadabhāve'pi prasajyaśaktyā sattvavyavasthāpanāt ?
anyathā tatsaṃśaye ca kathamavasthāpayet ? sā ca cintayiṣyate |
[378,2]
atha tenaikānekabhāva iti svarūpeṇa ekānekabhāvaḥ, tatastenaiva sattvamityabhimatam ? tadāpi kiṃ punarasya tatsvarūpaṃ yenaikānekatāyoga iti praśne yadīdameva tarjanīnirdeśayogyamiti ucyate, tadā nīlametaditi na tenaikānekaṃ vijñānamiti plavata etat |
athānyat ? tanna siddham | siddhau vā kimanena ? sa caupālambhastadavasthaḥ |
bhinnasya hi siddhāveva vivādaḥ, na tu tasmin siddhe'pi kiṃ pararūpeṇāpi tasya sattvam iti prastāvaḥ |
[378,3]
atha siddha evāyaṃ prakāśo dharmī, tasya nīlādirūpeṇāsattvasiddhau sāmarthyalabdho bhedaḥ, tāvatā ca siddhamabhimatamato na vidheranurodha iti vyāpakānupalambha eva prakṛtopayogīti cet ? mahatīyaṃ vaidagdhī, kevalamavidyāpi nīlādinā asan prakāśo yadi svenāpi rūpeṇa tathā, tadā kā bhedasiddhiḥ ? nanu tasyāsattvāśaṃkā nāstyeva, svasaṃvedanapratyakṣasiddhatvāt, svabhāve bhrāntyabhāvāt | bhede eva hi vivādaḥ | tādṛśī tarhi siddhiḥ nīlasyāpi kathaṃ bādhā ? prakāśasya prakāśa eva rūpamityādābuktameva | śakyaṃ ca nīlaprakāśasya nīlaprakāśa eva rūpamityādi vaktum | tato bhedādhikṣepe'pi yadi svānubhavo bādhakamanavakāśīkurvan prakāśasattāṃ sādhayet, tathāpi kimanena ? tathā aśaktāvapi kimanena, nīlavattatrāpi hastakatyāgāvarjanāt bhedāsiddheḥ ?
[378,4]
atha parasya paramārthasattvena siddhaḥ prakāśo bheda eva vivādastataḥ sanneva prakāśo na nīlātmaneti sādhyasiddhiḥ | sarvopāyaparikṣīṇanyāyaparyavāsanā tarhi vaidagdhī |
tadetadātmavādino ghaṭanairātmyasiddhinyāyena helāmarhati | kiṃ cāsmin sādhane'bhedāvabhāsinoranubhavākārayorbhedaḥ pratijñārthaḥ, tadrūpeṇa ekānekaviraho hetuḥ | na cāsya yathoktasādhyenānvayo dṛṣṭānte darśayituṃ śakyaḥ | tatrāpi duḥkhādyākāravyatirekiṇaḥ prakāśasya asiddheḥ | siddhāvapi yathā śātamaśāteneti na vaktavyam | yathā duḥkhānubhavo duḥkhādyākāreṇeti yuktam |
[379,1]
anyathā hyākārāntaraparigṛhītaprakāśasyākārāntareṇāsattvakhyāpane tadapekṣayaiva bhedaḥ syāt | tataśca sādhyakāle nīlākārasya pītānubhavād bhedaḥ sidhyet | tato yadi svaprakāśāpekṣo bhedo dṛṣṭānte nopadarśayituṃ śakyaḥ sādhyo'pi kathaṃ bhaviṣyati, anvayasya evābhāvāt ?
[379,2]
yad yena naikānekamiti sāmānyenānvayo'trokta iti cet ? tadasat | yataḥ,
[379,3]
anukto'pīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhya ātmārthavanmataḥ |
[379,4]
tadetadapi cakṣurādipārārthyasādhanādinā samānam | athavā yad yena naikānekam ityatra yadabhinnābhāsi yenāvabhāsineti vivakṣitam, atha sāmānyeneti vikalpya,
[379,5]
viśeṣe'nugamābhāvaḥ sāmānye siddhasādhanam |
[379,6]
sukhaduḥkhayoriva nīlapītānubhavayoraparaspararūpatayā tenātmanāsattvākṛṣṭabhedasiddheḥ, abhedagrāhiṇastu pratyakṣasyobhayatrāpi na kṣatiḥ | śeṣamasmad bṛhadīśvaravādavat | api ca yadā prakāśaśca naikāneko nīlādineti pakṣe hetorupanayaḥ, tatra ko'yaṃ prakāśo nāma, prakāśanam, prakāśata iti vā ? athārthāntarameva kiñcit prakāśaśabdābhidheyaṃ prakāśayatītyādivyāpārāpekṣayā vyavasthiternirastatvāt ?
[379,7]
prathamapakṣe prakāśamānānāṃ nīlapītādīnāṃ prakāśo nāma dharmamātrametat, bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇa bhinnavadābhāsamānamapi kalpanābuddhau na dharmirūpavighaṭane taṭastham āsituṃ śaktam, tat kutastattvato bhedasiddhiḥ ? na hi dharmirūpamuddhūya dharmāṇāṃ kvacidapi sattvamasti, guṇakarmādivat | kartṛsādhanapakṣe tu nīlādireva prakāśata iti tasyaiva tena rūpeṇa śūnyateti pūrvavat |
[379,8]
arthāntarapakṣe ca yadi prakāśata iti sānvayapadaṃ, tadā nīlādivyatiriktasya tasya dṛśyānupalabdhibādhitasya tenātmanāsattve'pi na sādhyasiddhiḥ | niranvayanāśapakṣe'pi na pramāṇasiddhiḥ, tatra ca vyavacchedamātrayoḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvāśrayādāśrayāsiddhiparihāre'pi na prakṛtopayogaḥ | athāyameva pratividitaḥ prakāśo dharmī | nanu pratividita iti pratibhāsamānaḥ sa ca nīla eva, na tadvyatiriktaḥ kaścit |
[379,9]
nanu tadvyatiriktasādhanāyaiva yatna eṣaḥ, kathaṃ prathamatastatprārthanamiti cet ?
kimapi sādhyamastu bhavataḥ, sādhanādhārastu niṣṭhitasvarūpo darśanīyo yadi prakāśo nāma vasturūpo dharmī saṃmataḥ | yadi tu sādhyasādhanayorvyavacchedamātratānurodhāt avastu saṃdigdhavastubhāvo vā dharmī, tadā nāyaṃ niyamaḥ | prakṛtasiddhistu dūre | atha prakṛtasiddhyanurodhād vastubhūtaḥ prakāśo dharmī, tadā niṣṭhitasvarūpaḥ svīkriyamāṇo nīla eva syāt | tatra rūpaṃ rūpasvabhāvena śūnyamityāyātam, tathāpi na prakṛtasiddhiḥ | na ca tena śūnyatayānyena sthitirityanākārapratyāśā | mā bhūdanyarūpeṇānyasya śūnyatayā siddhasādhanaśaṃketi tāvatāpi tenetyasya caritārthatvāt |
[380,1]
sākāranaye vā taimirikadṛṣṭacandradvaye candradvayarūpaśūnyatāvadadhyavasitabāhyaniṣedha eṣaḥ | sarvatra cāropitasyaiva niṣedhāt sarvatra ca svākāre bahirāropa eva pṛthagjanasya, anyathā tattvahāneriti | tasmānna nīle dharmiṇi prakṛtasiddhiḥ | atha kimanayā viśeṣaniṣṭhayā, prakāśo nāma sāmānyena dharmī mataḥ | viśeṣaniṣṭhayā ca sādhyāvadhūteḥ sādhanopanyāsapratibandhaprasaṅgāt | na ca sādhyamanabhisandhāya sādhanaprayogaḥ kasyacit | nāpi nirastasādhyo dharmī kvacit kriyate, siddhasādhyavat | ato na viśeṣaniṣṭhāyāṃ bharaḥ |
bhavatu vā sāpi |
[380,2]
ayamevāsau puraḥprakāśo nāma nīlena saha yasya pṛthagbhāve sāṃśayiko'sīti bhavatu dohadoparamaḥ | dṛṣṭaśca vyāvṛttibhedena dharmadharmibhāvo yathā svabhāvahetau tadekā vyāvṛttirdharmiṇī, anyayā saha pṛthagbhāvaḥ sādhya iti na kaściddoṣaḥ | tadapyasaṃgatam |
yataḥ
[380,3]
yuktā vyāvṛttimātreṇa sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ | dharmirūpaṃ tu bhedena dṛṣṭamevopayujyate ||
[380,4]
sāmānyākāramantareṇa hi pratibandhabodhasyāśakyatvāt plavamānarūpayoḥ sādhyasādhanayordharmisvarūpaniṣṭhayaiva tattvasthitiḥ, na tu dharmirūpasyāpi plavamānatāyāṃ vyāvṛttimātreṇa, idaṃ ca tatheti śākhiśabdādeḥ svalakṣaṇānupadarśane'pratīteḥ | vyāvṛttibhedastu bhedavyavahārārthamapekṣyate, na dharmisattārthaṃ, vyaktiviśeṣaniṣṭhatayāpratītau tasyā evāsiddhiprasaṅgāt | yathā cāyaṃ śākhādimān śravaṇagrāhyo ghaṭādiśabdo bādhadharmīti svalakṣaṇe dharmiṇi pratīte'pi virodhābhāvāt vṛkṣakṣaṇikatvādisaṃdehe sādhanānusāraḥ, tathā na prastute'styavakāśaḥ |
[381,1]
tathā hi yāvadevāyamiti tarjanīnirdeśayogyo dharmī nīlatayā upanītastāvataiva bhedasandehapracyuterna sādhanāvatāraḥ, tannīlarūpamantareṇa prakāśasya rūpaviśeṣaniṣṭhānupapatteḥ | aprakāśavyāvṛttimātrasya hi kvacid vyaktau niṣṭhāyāmātmalābhaḥ, aśabdavyāvṛtteriva, na pratyekāpohe | tato'bhāvaśaṅkāvaśānna vastusan dharmīṣṭaḥ siddhaḥ | tato vastvapekṣāyāṃ sarvasya sāmānyasya viśeṣarūpeṇaivārthakāritayā vastutvānnīlasyaiva dharmiṇa upanaye paryavasito bhedābhedanirūpaṇaprakramaḥ | kṣaṇikādirūpatā tu sandehaviṣayaḥ syāt, apratikṣepāt |
[381,2]
iha punarayameva sa dharmī prakāśata iti nīlarūpatayā vādinaiva darśite kimidānīṃ sabhyairveditavyam ? atha paścāt pakṣadharmopasaṃhāre na doṣaḥ ? doṣa eva, prakāśaśca nīlena naiko nāneka iti paścādukto'pi, ko'sau prakāśa iti nīlarūpatāyāmeva niṣṭhānāt, bhedāntarasya darśayitumaśakyatvāt, viśeṣādarśane ca dharmiṇaḥ sadrūpasyāśakyanirvāhatvāt |
yadyapi ca svabhāvahetāvatadrūpaparāvṛttamubhayamapi vastu, tathāpi naitadeva kṛtakatvādi kiṃ tvetadapi | tato dṛṣṭāntasādhāraṇatayā sāmānyamucyate na dharmirūpam | etadevamiti asādhāraṇenaiva rūpeṇa pravṛttinivṛttyarthitayāpekṣaṇīyatvāt |
[381,3]
ataeva sādhye'pi dṛṣṭāntadvāreṇa viśeṣajijñāsocchedaḥ | mā bhūt sarvavyaktiviyuktāvasattvameva | antataḥ pakṣe'pi tallakṣaṇānna vyaktivirahaḥ | kṣaṇikatvāderapyeta eva vyaktibhedāḥ | kālpanikaṃ tu bhedamāsthāya tattvato vyatirekaviveke'pi sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ | tathā yadi kālpanikena bhedena dharmibhāvo'pi syāt, astu tenaiva rūpeṇa tasya vastutvamiti svayamupagame kastanniṣedhāya yogaḥ ? paro vā kathamanyadādriyeta yaddharmirūpanirūpaṇenaiva pratihatam ? ataeva yathā tasya sādhyārtho yatnastathā parasyāpi sādhyārthina eva dharmirūpagaveṣaṇam | so'yaṃ tadanādarodāravat prasavārthino na prekṣāṃ lakṣayati | tato yasya sādhyasya dharmisvarūpaviśeṣaniṣṭhayaiva pratihatistadanumānenālam | siddhe dharmiṇi saṃdigdho dharmaḥ sādhanamarhati | dharmirūpaviśeṣasya niṣṭhāyāṃ tu hato hataḥ ||
ata eva,
[381,4]
samayāhitabhedasya parihāro'pi dharmiṇaḥ | pramāsiddhaviśeṣe hi dharmiṇyevamasaṃbhavaḥ || anumānaprasiddhe'pi saṃbandhavidapekṣayā | rūpaṃ tadanusāreṇa viśiṣṭamupakalpitam ||
[382,1]
tathā saṃbhave'pi punarayaṃ ca prakāśastatheti vaktumaśakteḥ punastadavasthaḥ prakṛtahānidoṣaḥ |
[382,2]
nīle dharmiṇyabhyupetasya bādhā siddho nānyaḥ satya iṣṭo vṛthā ca | rūpāniṣṭhā saṃbhave tattva evārekaḥ kekāsādhane yadvaduktaḥ ||
[382,3]
kiṃ ca yad yena rūpeṇetyādiprayoge yadi naikaṃ nānekaṃ ca nīlādivijñāneneti pakṣadharmopasaṃhārastadā ko doṣaḥ ? tataśca śakyamevaṃ paṭhitum,
[382,4]
yena rūpeṇa yannaikaṃ nānekaṃ tena tanna sat | yathā śātamaśātena prakāśenāsitaṃ tathā ||
[382,5]
tāvaddeśavyāpino nīlasyeva prakāśasyāpi sthūlāṇurūpavirahaḥ kena vāryate ?
tato'sti nīlaṃ na tu prakāśarūpeṇeti | tato bhinnajaḍarūpasiddhiḥ | alīkastu prakāśātmā |
yuktaṃ caitat,
[382,6]
vidyududyotasaṃkāśaḥ prakāśaḥ kasyacit kvacit | tamapekṣya sthiro bāhyaḥ prakāśe'lokatā tataḥ ||
[382,7]
alīkanīlajanane yathā śaktirmatā dhiyaḥ | alīkabodhajanane tathā śaktirmatā bahiḥ ||
[382,8]
naivaṃ tvayāpyaniṣṭerityetad vaktuṃ na labhyate | īdṛksādhanamajñātvā mamāniṣṭiryato'bhavat ||
[382,9]
prakāśaḥ kevalo nāpi kvacit kenacidīkṣitaḥ | sukhādirapi vijñeyākāro buddhistataḥ parā ||
[382,10]
pratibhāsādyabhijñānaṃ sukhaṃ so'sti śiterapi | pratibhāse'pyabhedena pratibhāsaḥ śiterapi ||
[383,1]
atha vyāpakānupalambhastasya tatrāvatārayitumaśaktiḥ ? evaṃ tarhi duḥkhamapi prakāśātmaiveti na kadācit prahīyeta | api caivamavayavyādeḥ pratyujjīvanaprasaṅgāt sarvamāditaḥ prabhṛti śīrṇam | tasmānna kvacidabhedapratibhāse bhedasiddhiḥ | ataeva sarvo bhedaheturvyavahārasādhana ityuktam |
[383,2]
ye'pyāhuḥ dvaitābhāso dharmī bhrāntatvāt satyasaṅgato'vaśyaṃ taimirikacandrabimbadvayanirbhāso yathādṛṣṭa iti, teṣāmapyasatprakāśo bhrāntirabhimatetyeṣā pratyāśā |
sā ca nityasyeta eva nirastā | evaṃ māyākhyātirasatyetyādyapi nirastam | na ca māyākāro nāma svaprakāśākāravyatiriktaḥ siddhaḥ | jñānāntarabhavaṃ ca jñānāntaramiṣṭam iti |
[383,3]
ye'pyanuvṛttavyāvṛttarūpatayā bhedamāhuḥ, teṣāmapi kalpanāmātrametat, sāmānyavat pramāṇasiddherabhāvādityuktaprāyaṃ vastrodakaprastāve | tadayam, prakāśaṃ nīlamityetad bhinnopādhinibandhanam | viśiṣṭapratyayatvena kuṇḍalīpratyayo yathā ||
ityetatparyavasāno vādaḥ | tasmād yathāsvaṃ samanantarapratyayaprabhaveṣu nīlapītādiṣu prakāśabhedeṣu parāpohamātravyavasthāpitaśarīraḥ prakāśo nāma kalpitaṃ dharmamātrametat, teṣāmapāye'pyanupahatamiti sthavīyasī bhrāntiḥ |
[383,4]
atha viparīto dharmadharmibhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ, tatrāpi na pramāṇavyāpāraḥ, viparyayastvasti |
[383,5]
bhedo'nubhūtimān dharmī dharmo jātyādikalpitam | viparyayaḥ punaḥ kasmādiṣṭaḥ śraddheyanīlayoḥ ||
[383,6]
kevalamanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ bhedamāsthāya vivekadurbalo loka eṣa mṛdi saṃsthānādivat bhedaṃ dharmadharmitāviparyayaṃ ca vyavaharatīti nātrābhiniveśaḥ | na ca pṛthagdharmitvamanayorupagamakṣamaḥ,
[383,7]
yadi prakāśo nīlādiḥ kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa vaḥ | athāprakāśo nīlādiḥ kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa vaḥ ||
[384,1]
na khalu svayamaprakāśaṃ pareṇa nāma prakāśībhavati, yo hi yasya svabhāva ityādivacanāt | athālīkābhimāninaḥ svabhāvāntarābhāvānnaivamiti matiḥ ? svabhāvāntaravirahādeva tarhi prakāśamātramasya svabhāva iti kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa ? kvārūḍhaṃ tadalīkam ābhāsatāmiti tu jñānādisamāśrayātmavādena tulyam | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ, prameyasyātmano'prakāśatayā sthitiraviruddheti prahārāntaramapekṣate, prakāśātmanastūccāraṇamapi na kṣamata iti kiṃ viphalagurubhirāyāsaiḥ | mā bhūd vālīkatve svaprakāśāvarjanam | tena tasyānātmabhūtasya prakāśane bāhyena kīdṛśaḥ kṛto'parādhaḥ ? alīke tasya śaktiśced vastunyastamayet katham | nirvibandhamataḥ siddho dharmottaramanorathaḥ || yadi sāhāyakāpekṣā vastunyeva sphuratyasau | tādātmyakalpanāyāśca pātraṃ vastveva yujyate || alīkabhedasphūrttau ca nākārasya yathāśrayaḥ | bāhyabhedaprakāśe ca tathākāreṇa kiṃ phalam || atha bāhyānyayornaikayogakṣematvamiṣyate | bādhāpi bāhyasyaivāstāmalīkatvamataḥ kutaḥ || bāhyasya siddhiriva buddhikṛtāstu bādhāpyaucityametadasakṛd vyavalokitaṃ ca | siddhirdhiyaḥ paradhiyo na yathā tathā nabādhāpi na svamupahanti bahirmato'pi ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[384,2]
na cālīkasyāsadrūpatvāt kvacicchaktiriti sādhakatamatvāpekṣaḥ karaṇabhāvo'pi yatnasādhito'yatnaśīrṇaḥ | vijñānanayāvatāraṇārthaścāyaṃ kramaḥ saṃmataḥ | ataścaivaṃ yat dvaitarūpasiddhau punarasādhāraṇo nirbandhaḥ pramāṇavārtike, tato yadi nirākārameva tattvatī jñānamabhimatam, āstāṃ tāvadākārasya kāraṇatāsthitiḥ, ākāravad bāhyasyāpi vedanānapahnavatvāt kuto vijñānamātratāsiddhirityalīkākārasādhanaṃ svavadhāya kṛtyotthāpanaṃ yatnenetyāyātam | abhinne tvākāre svarūpaviśeṣānnīlaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na pītamityavasāyasādhanasāmarthyād bahirabhāve'pyābhimānikī pramāṇavyavasthā tāvat sidhyati |
tataḥ prārabdhavicārasya grāhyalakṣaṇābhāvāt svavedanamātrasiddherapratibandhaḥ | ataeva tadante, nīlādirūpastasyāsau svabhāvo'nubhavaśca saḥ (pra. vā. 2. 328)
ityādi bruvāṇaḥ śobheta | athaivamapi paścādvyāpakābhāvād bāhyasyākārasya vā vastutāṃ nirasya prakāśamātraṃ sthāpayiṣyāma ityabhiprāyaḥ ? tarhi kimāditaḥ prabhṛtyākārarākṣasaprasādhanaprabandhena ? yathaiva nirākāreyaṃ buddhirākāravān saṃvādo bāhya iti svaparamatiḥ, tathaiva vyavasthānupalambhamavatārya kāryasiddhirastu | tataḥ kuto grāhyalakṣaṇacintā ? na vā prakāśamānasahopalabdhau hetū vaktavyau, ākārasādhanadvāreṇa doṣāt, vyāpakānupalambhasyāvaśyamapekṣaṇācceti sādhu siddhaṃ dharmottarasamīhitena |
[385,1]
etadeva ca prakāratrayamācāryasya sarvatra vijñaptimātratāsādhanamāñjasaṃ paśyāmaḥ, samarthanatātparya cātraiva, vyāpakānupalambhe tu pūrvācāryacarcite'numatimātram, sthūlavat paramāṇudūṣaṇābhāvāt | tato yadi dhārmottare paramāṇupratividhāvanavadhānam, ekamanekaṃ ca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ neti vacanādayatno mukhyatayā cānupaśyāmaḥ siddha eveti sakalamākulamācāryamatamatra mate | na ca tāvatā kṣatiḥ kācid, yadi nyāyagandhaḥ syāt | tatra kiñciduktameva | kiṃ ca mā vedi bāhyaṃ prakāśavedyamalīkamityapi prakārāntareṇa grāhyagrāhakasthitirupanatā | tenāprakāśane ca prasajya svaprakāśatāvakāśinīti kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa ? tasmāt siddhāḥ svasaṃvedanatvena jñānarūpā rūpaśabdādayaḥ, asādhāraṇatvasyāpi bahirarthadūṣaṇe'smābhiḥ prasādhanāt | atrāpi svasaṃvedanamātramanaikāntikaṃ tāttvikaṃ cāsiddhamiti bālavibhīṣikāto na bhetavyam | kalpitasyānupapatteḥ tāttvikasyaiva sādhitatvāt na vikalpadvayāvakāśaḥ |
[385,2]
ata eva vijñānasyāpyākārānatirekādalīkatāṃ sādhayato nāsiddhiranekānto vā śakyaḥ | yadapi viparyayeṇocyate, yasya yadabādhyaṃ rūpaṃ tasyāsau prakṛtiḥ, tadyathā sarvadharmāṇāṃ bodhātmā | abādhyaṃ ca rūpaṃ bodhātmanaḥ sattvamiti svabhāvaheturiti, tadapyanenaiva nirastam | bhinnasya dharmiṇo'siddhernīlasya ca bādhanāditi ||
[385,3]
tasmāt,
[386,1]
nākārabhedamavadhūya dhiyo'sti vṛttistadvādhake balini madhyanaye jayaśrīḥ | nocedanindyamidamadvayameva citraṃ ceto nirākṛtimatasya tu ko'vakāśaḥ ||
{11.2}
<dvitīyaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[387,1]
yadi tarhi nirākārasya cetaso'sattvaṃ tattvata iti saṃkleśavyavadānavyavasthāvilopaḥ, upapluto hyākārakalāpo'tasmiṃstadgrahād bhrāntireva saṃsārastatprabhavavāsanāsaṃghātasamuddhāte copaplavavigamādanābhāsamamalaṃ prakāśamātramavaśiṣyamāṇaṃ nirvāṇamiti na kṣatiḥ | anyathā tu,
[387,2]
sākārabuddherbādhāyāṃ vyavadānamasaṃgatam | abādhāyāṃ tu saṃkleśavyavasthādausthyamāgatam ||
[387,3]
tathā hi sattvaireva prakāśairaviparītasvarūpasaṃvedanāt bhrānteratyantamabhāvaḥ syāt | tataśca sarvasattvāḥ sadaiva muktāḥ sadaiva samyaksaṃbuddhā bhaveyuḥ | vikalpikā buddhirbhrāntiḥ, svapratibhāse'narthe arthādhyavasāyāditi cet ? kathamavasīyamānastayā so'rtho na prakāśate ? prakāśyamāne vā kathamasau tasyāṃ na prakāśate ? atha prakāśata eva, tadā arthasya tādātmyaprasaṅgaḥ | asati cārthe sā na syāt | abhūnmāndhātā, bhaviṣyati śaṅkho'styātmā, nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sarvātmanā ca niścayaḥ syāt | gauriti spaṣṭena ca svena lakṣaṇena prakāśeta | svalakṣaṇe ca saṃketāyogād vikalpikaiva sā buddhirna syāt |
[387,4]
