tasmādaśeṣagovyaktisādhāraṇena gotvena gobuddhiralīkena sābhilāpena viplavāt prakhyātīti tathā prakāśanamasyā gavārthāvasāya ityeṣṭavyam | evaṃ hyete doṣā na syuḥ, apratibhāsamānasyāpi svalakṣaṇasya bhrāntyāvasāyāt | yathā cālīkasya gotvasya gobuddhau prakāśastādātmyaṃ ca, tadvyatirekād vastutvamanāropitatvaṃ vā, tathā nīlādiprakāśe nīlādīnāmalīkānāṃ prakāśasiddhyaiva tādātmyasiddhiḥ, nānārūpaniṣṭhayoralīkatvānalīkatvayorekatrāpi vastunyavirodhāt | yadi ca vastutve'nāropitatve sā sādhye tādātmyamātraṃ hetustadā gotvādibhiranekāntaḥ | athānāropitaṃ tādātmyaṃ hetustadasiddhamiti | atrābhidhīyate,
[387,5]
atasmiṃstadgraho nāma bhramaścet sarvasaṃmataḥ | alīke'pi tadākāre satyavanna samañjasaḥ ||
[388,1]
marīcāvajale jalagraho bhrama iti loke, śāstre ca svapratibhāse'narthe'rthādhyavasāyena pravṛtterbhrāntamanumānamityādi bahudhābhidhānāt | atasmiṃstadgraho nāma bhrāntirviditā | tasyā yadi sākāranaye'nupapattiralīkākāra eva kathamupapattiriti cintyatām | jñānaṃ hi kenacidākāreṇa satyena vālīkena vopajātaṃ nāma, bāhyāropastu tadākāre tatkṛto'nyakṛto vā syāt, tatkṛtatvena tāvattatkāla eva vyāpārāntaramanubhūyata iti kutastadāropaḥ ? kālāntare ca svayamevāsan kasya vyāpāraḥ syāt ?
[388,2]
dvitīyapakṣe jñānāntaramapi nākāroparāgasaṅginīmutpattimantareṇa vyāpārāntareṇa kvacit kiñcitkaraṃ nāma | tadetadarvācīnaṃ prācīnajñānākāragocarīkaraṇe'pi na bāhyāropavyāpāramaparaṃ spṛśati tadākāraleśānukāramapahāya, śabdākārasyāpi svarūpe'ntargatatvāt | yadi ca vyāpārāntaramapi saṃbhaved bāhyāropāya, nākāram, anumāne'pi sādhanamabhidadhyāt | adhigataye tatsādhanaṃ nāropāyeti cet — na, svarūpanirbhāsasya anumāne pratikṣepādāropa evāsau | āropa iti asatyaviṣaya iti cet ?
nanu rūpādhigatireva tarhi vahneranumānasiddhasya syāt | tasmādāropo'vasāyo'bhimānam ityanarthāntarametat | saṃvādeta rābhyāṃ tu viśeṣaḥ, yato na vikalpamātraṃ pramāṇamiti syāt |
[388,3]
tasmānnākārādanyo jñānasya vyāpāraḥ, āropyamānaścāsāvartho bāhyastatra buddhau yadi svarūpeṇa parisphurati satyapratītirevāsau ka āropārthaḥ ? sphuraṇe ca dvitīyākāravedanaprasaṅgaḥ | tadākārasphuraṇameva tasya sphuraṇamiti cet — na, tasyāropaviṣayatvāt |
na hi marīcivisphuraṇameva jalasphuraṇam, tena sahaikīkaraṇāditi cet ? ko'yamekīkaraṇārthaḥ ? yadyekatāpattau prayojakatvam, tadāropyāviṣayayoḥ kadācidekībhāvābhāvādasaṃbhavameva | na hi śaśaviṣāṇe kāraṇaṃ kiñcit | na ca pūrvamanekamekatāmetīti kṣaṇikavādinaḥ sāmpratam | arthāntarotpattimātraṃ tu syāt, na ca tadapyupalabdhigocaraḥ anyatrāropaviṣayāt | na ca tāvatāpyarthasya kiñciditi kutastasyāropaḥ ? athaikapratītiḥ ekīkaraṇam ? tathāpi na dvayoḥ, āropyānubhavābhāvāt | na ca dvayoḥ pratītirityevāropaḥ, nīlapītavat, āropyabodhagandhābhāvāccaikatvena pratītirityapi nirasanīyam |
yadi hi bāhyaṃ pratibhāseta, ekatvenānekatvena vā satāsatā vā pratītiriti yuktam |
[388,4]
sarvākāratatsvarūpatiraskāreṇa sā pratītirityekapratītiriti cet ? tatsvarūpatiraskāre tarhi tadapratibhāsanameva | kasyacidaṃśasya pratibhāsanāditi cet — na, niraṃśatvād vastunaḥ sarvātmanā pratibhāso'pratibhāso veti śāstramevātra paramate vistareṇa |
adhyavasāyāditi cet ? so'pi vikalpāparanāmā svākāramantareṇa vārtāmapi bāhyasya na jānātīti uktaprāyam | athābhedena pratītiḥ ? adyāpi paryudāsapakṣe aikyapratītirevoktā bhavati pratyuktā ca | bhedena pratītiniṣedhamātre'pi na bāhyasya pratītirukteti kutastadāropaḥ ? bhedena neti ca nirupayogam, abhedenaikyena pratītivyavasthāvirahāt, āropaviṣayamātrapratīteścāpahnotumaśakyatvāt | tanmātrānuvādinā na kaścid viśeṣa ukto bhavati |
[389,1]
tasmād yāvaccintyate tāvadāropyasparśābhāvannāropo nāma | yathā kathañcit tatpratibhāsaparibhāṣayā ca tadāropeṇa bhramavyavasthāyāmalīka iva satye'pyākāre uparodhaḥ, na tu tāvatā tāttvikatvamuktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ tarhi tasya svarūpanirbhāse'pi sutarāṃ na bhrama iti kathaṃ bhrāntisthitiḥ ? na kathañcit, yadi vicāre ādaraḥ |
avicāraramaṇīyamābālasiddhaṃ vyavahāramupādāya pudgalādivadāropamapi vyavaharāmaḥ |
vicāryamāṇastu viśīryata eva ||
[389,2]
ātmā yathā yathā bāhyaṃ yathā saṃvādataḥ pramā | tathānekaviparyāsau vyavahāraparāyaṇau ||
[389,3]
tatra yāvadavicārastāvat saṃsāro yāvacca svarūpaparicchedaniṣṭhā tāvannirvāṇam | parijñānaṃ bhavasyaiva nirvāṇamiti kathyate |
iti nyāyaḥ | kathaṃ tarhi bhavaparijñānam, kathaṃ vā tattvato'sato bhramāt pravṛttyādiriti vakṣyāmaḥ | yathā tu nirākāravādī tattvato bhramavyavasthāmupasthāpayati tathā pratīmaḥ tāvat | tasyāpi tarhi parāroparūpā bhrāntirmā bhūt | alīkākārayoga eva bhrāntiḥ |
tatkṣepaḥ kṣemaśceti kimayuktam ? prathamamideva tāvat yallokaśāstrayoratikramaḥ, rajjau hi janaḥ sarpāropād bhramaṃ vyavaharati, na tu jñānaṃ kenacidākāreṇa janaṃ spṛśati | sa ca sarpāropo nirūpyamāṇaḥ kiyatīṃ koṭimāṭīkata iti nodyamaḥ, nāpi paryantanayanaśaktiritarasya | tallakṣaṇāṃ tāvad bhrāntimayaṃ vyavaharatīti siddham |
[389,4]
śāstre'pi svapratibhāse'rthādhyavasāyena pravṛttirbhrāntirucyate | na tu svapratibhāso'narthaka ityeva | tathā dṛśyavikalpayorekīkaraṇāderapyayamevārthaḥ | na tvatrāpi vikalpyamalīkamityeva, kiṃ tu dṛśyāropāditi | nirvikalpe'pi candradvayamiddhaṃ dṛśyata iti vikalpena svavyāpārasya tatraivāropādavicāritaramaṇīyaṃ syāt |
[390,1]
bhramatvamavikalpe'pi vikalpānna tataḥ param | ato vikalpe viśrāntamavikalpe'pi kathyate ||
[390,2]
tasmāt sarvatra parāropādeva bhramasthitiriti | tadasamādhāya paribhāṣāntaraṃ nāmeti kimaprayuktamataḥ ? athāyogādeva parihāra iti ka eṣa doṣaḥ, samarthanāsāmarthyasya svīkṛtatvāditi cet ? yadyevam,
[390,3]
samasti tāvad vyavahārasiddho bhramo vicāraśca virodhako'sya | etāvataivābhimataprasiddheḥ śeṣo viśeṣo'bhiniveśaleśaḥ ||
[390,4]
sa hi sāṃvṛto bhramaḥ satyālīkapakṣayoraviśiṣṭaḥ kevalamākārasyāpi mayā alīkatvamabhyupetamiti tasyāpi paryante sthitirmābhūditi bhramatvāpādanamabhinibeśamātraṃ saṃkleśavyavadānayoranyathāpi siddheḥ | yāvadeva vicāreṇa bhramabhraṃśo'stu śobhanam | sarvathāsanniti punaḥ sundarādapi sundaram || ata eva prayatnena vicāra ucitaśramaḥ | sato'panayane jātu śaṃkā syādapi dhīmatām ||
ityantaraślokau ||
[390,5]
tasmādalīkasaṃbhavo bhrama iti kimanena ? tadasvīkāriṇo'pi paramatānupagamamātrametat, na dṛṣṭanyāyātikramaḥ | yadapyucyate, ayogāt tatparihāra iti tadayogadarśino'satyaprakāśo bhrāntiriti kīdṛśī yogadṛṣṭiḥ ? tathā hi asatpratibhāsa iti asadīśvarādeḥ khyātiḥ, bhāsamāno vā ākāro'san, san vā kaścit na khyātīti vivakṣitam ? tatra,
[391,1]
yasya svarūpanirbhāsastadevāsat kathaṃ bhavet | bādhāto yadi sāpyekā pratyakṣānumayornanu ||
[391,2]
pratyakṣe yadyaviśvāsa ekatrānyatra kā gatiḥ | tatpūrvamanumānaṃ vā kathamāśvāsagocaraḥ ||
[391,3]
svarūpasākṣātkaraṇādadhyakṣatvaṃ na cāparam | vikalpabhramabhūmitvamata eva hi bādhitam ||
[391,4]
yadi nādhyakṣatā tasya rūpanirbhāsa eva na | tatastadasadīśādi pratibhātītyasaṅgatam ||
[391,5]
yadi tu pratibhāseta rūpamasya sadeva tat | tadasatpratibhātīti pratibhātyasadeva vaḥ ||
[391,6]
etena dvitīyo'pi pakṣaḥ pratikṣipto veditavyaḥ | pratibhāsādeva sattāsiddherbādhakāvakāśābhāvāt | nanu,
[391,7]
dṛṣṭameva dvicandrādipratibhāse'pi bādhitam | na dṛṣṭe'nupapannatvaṃ tatpūrvoditamapyasat ||
[391,8]
tadapyasat | bādhyasyāpratibhāsanāt, pratibhāsinaścābādhyatvāt | tathā hi,
[391,9]
buddhyākārasya nirbhāso bādhā bāhyasya vastunaḥ | rūpasyaiva hi nirbhāsaḥ sparśāderapi bādhanam ||
[391,10]
sa hi rūpamātrapratibhāso rūparasagandhasparśasamudāyaviśeṣatayā adhyavasīyate |
ataeva keśādau karaparāmarśodyamādisaṃbhavaḥ | tato bādhāpi tatsahacaritasyaiva rūpasya, na rūpamātrasya | tathāvidhārthakriyārthī hi sarvastatsādhanasyaiva siddhibādhayoravadhatte, na yasya kasyacit |
[391,11]
ṣaṇḍasya rūpavairūpye kāminyāḥ kiṃ parīkṣayā ||
[392,1]
tattvacintakā eva tu prayojanāntarāpekṣayā sāmānyādikamapi parīkṣante | tatra yadrūpamātramābhāti ye ca sahacāriṇaścatvāraḥ samudāyarūpatayādhyavasīyante tadubhayeṣām abhedābhimānī jano vivecanābhāvādidamasadalīkaṃ veti vyavaharati | atastadabhimānādeva yāvānatra vidhiḥ pratiṣedho vā sarvo'dhyavasitaparyavasāna eva, anyāropeṇa tadrūpasya pracchāditatvāt | tato na tattvatastasya bādhā, śabdārthavat | yasya ca kalāpasya bādhā na tasya pratibhāsa iti siddham |
[392,2]
tato'bhimānamātrakṛtā bādhā'pi pratibhāsino yadi syāt tattvamastu mābhūditi na kṣatiḥ sāṃvṛtamuccāvacamīdṛśamanubhūyata eva jagati | ataeva tattvacintāvatāraḥ |
kevalamuktaprakrameṇa tadasphuraṇe kathaṃ tadavasāya ityāyātamasatprakāśanam | tathā abhedābhimāne abhedasyāsataḥ khyātiḥ, pracchādanamanyāropeṇetyapi nānyapratibhāsanaṃ vineti sphāragalamutthānaṃ syāt | tatrākṣiṇī nimīlya yadi cintayet svayamātmānamupahaset |
tathā hyaktametadadhyavasāyasyāpi nākāraviśeṣollekhamuddhūyāparaḥ parāropaprakāro nāma |
na cānātmanaḥ saṃvedanam | na ca svākāraniṣedho'bhimato janasya, śakyo vā, svarūpanirbhāsino niṣedhavirodhāt | na ca tadevāsatāmīśvarādīnāṃ rūpam, asattvasyaivābhāvaprasaṅgāt | tato yat sākāravāde jalpitaṃ, nityādayaḥ santa eva syuriti tadātmana evāpatitam |
[392,3]
pratibhāse'pi bādhā cenna sattvamasatāṃ matam | nāniṣiddhopalabdhīnāṃ niṣedhasya niṣedhataḥ ||
[392,4]
yasya svarūpanirbhāso bādhakād yadi tanna sat | bādhake'pi ka āśvāsaḥ svarūpāntarabhāsinī ||
[392,5]
anyasvarūpopanayāt tatsvarūpanivāraṇam | tatrāpi saṃśayo jātaḥ pūrvabādhopalabdhitaḥ ||
[392,6]
iyamevāgrahe bādhā nākṣajasyāparā yadi | asyāḥ pūrvaiva bhavatu rūpanirbhāsanaṃ samam ||
[392,7]
nānyāvabhāsinītyatra pramāṇaṃ kiñcidasti baḥ | api svarūpanirbhāse yadā bādhakasaṃbhavaḥ ||
[393,1]
tasmāt, anirbhāse svarūpasya hetuśodhanaviplave | bādhaśaṃkāvinirbhāse'pyevaṃ ced viplavo mahān ||
ityantaraślokāḥ ||
[393,2]
tataḥ sarvathā nirastamasatprakāśanamanavadhāritārthavyavasāye śabdaśravaṇamātreṇa pratyujjīvayituṃ saṃrambha iti kimaparamupahāsakāraṇam ?
[393,3]
pramāṇena nirastasya śabdādujjīvanaṃ punaḥ | daṣṭasya phaṇinā mantraprabhāvādiva kautukam ||
[393,4]
tasmādātmagotvādiśabdaprayogavat vyavasthātadvījayoranveṣaṇamātraṃ svataḥ parato vā ādriyante santa ityeva sādhuḥ | tadayamatra paramārthaḥ, vividhānādivāsanāvaśāt prabodhakapratyayaviśeṣāpekṣayā vikalpaḥ kenacidākāreṇopajāyamāna eva bahirmukhapravṛttyanukūlamarthakriyāsmaraṇābhilāpādiprabandhamādhatte | tataḥ puruṣasyārthakriyārthino bahirarthānurūpāṇi pravṛtinivṛttyavadhīraṇāni bhavanti | pṛthagjanasantānajñānakṣaṇānāṃ tādṛśo hetuḥ bhāvasya niyatatvāt | aniścitārthasaṃbandhavikalpakāle'pi sadasattādinirṇayādipravṛttiprasavaḥ |
[393,5]
tatra yadubhayathāpravṛtte sādhanasāmarthyamasya svahetubalāyātamayameva pravṛttiviṣayavastvāropo'dhyavasāyāparanāmā, yathā candrādijñānasya bhrāntasyābhrāntasya vā taddarśanāvasāyajananameva grahaṇavyāpāraḥ | svacidapīyamarthavideva kāryato draṣṭavyeti nyāyāt, tathā vikalpasyāpyagniratretyādinākāreṇotpadyamānasya pravṛttyākṣepakatvameva bāhyādhyavasānam | yathā ca nirvikalpasya candrādyākārataiva tathāvasāyasādhanī, evamavasāyasya api tādṛśākārataiva viṣayāntaravimukhapravṛttisādhanī | tatastadākārāvabhāvo'syānaghigatārthakāraṇabhāvo'pyāropaviṣayatvena pṛthagiva vyavasthāpyate, āropyajñānaṃ ca |
[393,6]
evaṃ tarhi tadeva trayamasadvyavasthāpyate, vyavasthā ca pratītiriti nāsatpratītermuktiriti cet ? so'yaṃ pravāhe'ṅganyāsaḥ | uktaṃ hi tadanurūpapravṛttyākṣepa eva tadāropo na paramapratītirnāmeti | tato'dyāpi trayasyāsato'dhyavasāya iti tadanurūpavyavahāramātram asatpratītivādānādarādyavasthālakṣaṇamasadidamityākāraṃ jñānaṃ ca phalamiti na kaścit doṣaḥ |
[394,1]
evamanyatrāpīdṛśi kṣudropadrave'bhyūhyam | iyamīdṛśī sarvavikalpānāmatarsmistadgraharūpā bhrāntiranubhavānusāriṇī | etadeva dṛśyavikalpyayorekīkaraṇaṃ vyavahriyate svapratibhāsavedanamātrāt paratra pravartanaśaktiryā tadapekṣā ca pararūpeṇa svapracchādanasthitiḥ | pratibhāsāpekṣayā tu pararūpaṃ svarūpeṇa saṃvriyate ityucyate, tasyaiva prakāśāt |
sato'pi bāhyasya prakāśādeva tattvato nirviṣayatvam | ākārasya cātmarūpatvāt, anadhyavasāyācca | ataeva yathādhyavasāyam, yathā pratibhāsam, yathātattvaṃ ca tridhāpohasthitiḥ ||
[394,2]
vijātivyāvṛttaṃ dhvanibhirabhidheyaṃ yadi bahirvikalpe tatkalpo bhavatu punaraṅgaḥ kṛta iti | nidānenedānīmubhayamapi bhāsādhyavasiterapohena
[394,3]
abhāvena bāhyasya hi pratibhāsābhāvaḥ | dhvanijanitavijātivyāvṛttavastusadṛśasyākārasya cādhyavasāyābhāvo yadi tarhi na kiñcid vācyamiti kastattvataḥ apohārtha iti cet ?
[394,4]
apohaḥ sphuṭamayamasau yanna kimapi ||
[394,5]
abhidheyamiti saṃbandhaḥ pūrvavākyavat | ayamarthaḥ, apoho vācya iti tattvato vācyasyaivāpohaniṣedha ityarthaḥ | yathā abhāvo bhavatīti bhāvo na bhavatītyarthaḥ |
tasmāt śabdaviṣayaḥ svalakṣaṇamiti siddham |
[394,6]
yatsūtram,
[394,7]
yena yena hi dharmeṇetyādi |
[394,8]
etāvati mūle kiyantaḥ pallavāḥ prādurbhavantvapohavādināṃ nātra nirbandhaḥ | yataśca vikalpasya bāhyaniścayanaṃ nāma dharmo bahirmukhapravṛttihetutattvalakṣaṇo niṣṭhitastata eva sarvākāraniścayo'pi prasajyamānastadanurūpapravṛttyupayoganiṣṭhitātmā syāt | na caikākārollekhino vikalpasyākārāntareṇa pravartanaśaktiranabhavaviṣaya iti kutaḥ śabdapramāṇāntarāpekṣeti yuktam | tatra nirvikalpakaṃ bhrāntamapi spaṣṭapratibhāsavaśāt grāhakamavasthāpyate |
vikalpastu vimarśākāratayā svayamanyānapekṣapravartakatve'pyaspaṣṭaikavyāvṛttyullekhādāropakādivyavahārabhājanam | sarvaṃ eva vikalpo bahiraspṛśanneva satyasati bāhye pravṛttiprayojakatayā bhrānta ucyate | asati tu tādṛgvikalpotpādanaśaktigarbhākārayogo nirvikalpakasya bhrama iti sthitam | sarvā nirviṣayaiva kalpanamatirvyāvṛttibhedānugasvākārotkalitā tu vīkṣitaphalasmṛtyādimātanvatī | lokasyākṣipati pravṛttimanapekṣaivānyadadhyakṣavad vastvāropa itīrito'rciṣi jalāropo jalānāmiva ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ ||
[395,1]
evaṃ ca sati yadadhyavasitaṃ bahiḥkalāparūpamiti pravṛttiyogyatāṃ nītamuktakrameṇa bādhyaṃ ca tasya na pratibhāsaḥ | pratibhāsinaścākārasya na bādhaka iti sthitam ||
[395,2]
na hi tadarthakriyāyāṃ kaścidvivādaḥ | arthakriyāpahitasya pṛṣṭhajo'dhyavasāya eva na ca tasyāḥ kṣatiḥ | kṣatistu kalāpaviśeṣasādhyāyā eveti tasyaivābhāvaḥ | tatkathaṃ pratibhāsamānasya bādhā iṣṭetyucyate, vyāpakānupalambhāpekṣāyāṃ ca sarvaṃ pūrvamāvartata iti || vyāpakābhāvacintāyāṃ na poto na ca pippalī | doṣontareṇa sākāre saṃkleśādiparīkṣaṇam ||
ārabdham | tatra satyasvākārasaṃvedane'pi sarvajñānānāṃ vyavahāraprasiddhamanantakālabījanirjātavyavasthaṃ bhramatvamāśritya na saṃkleśakṣatiḥ | yathā ca bāhye sati kvacid bhramavyavasthā, tathā nirṇaye sarvatra | kevalaṃ bahirmukhapravṛttyapekṣayā kriyamāṇo nātmani kaścid bhrama ityuktaṃ bhavati |
[395,3]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ rūpaṃ tasya tadeva hi |
[395,4]
evaṃ śabdayojanāyāṃ bahiravasāyāt tatraiva vikalpakatvamaspaṣṭatvaṃ ca, jñānāntarāpekṣayā tasyaivārthasya kevalasya spaṣṭasya cāvasthānāt | ātmarūpe tu tādṛśākārāvyabhicārāt tasyā buddheḥ sāmagrīviśeṣajanmanaḥ kutastathāvyavasthā ? yadāpyanayaiva anyāviṣayīkṛtya yojayitumiṣyate śabdena, tadāpi paratraiva yojanā nātmanīti śāstramatra cintyam | tasmād vikalpikaiva na syāditi svāpekṣayā siddhasādhanam paratra tu vikalpakatvamevādhyavasāyavyavasthābalāt |
[396,1]
atha vastusvarūpanirbhāsabalādevamucyate, tadetat sākārapakṣe'bhidhātumapi mahat sāhasam | adhyavasāyena tadākṛṣṭeriti cet — na, tasyānyathāvyavasthāpitatvāt | na hi tatsphuraṇe'vasāyo nāma, pratibhāsasyaiva prāpteḥ | ataevāpratibhāsamānasyāpi svalakṣaṇasya bhrāntyā tatrāvasāyāditi na yuktam | avasāyena tadvittisparśe pratibhāsaḥ ko'paraḥ ?
aspaṣṭatvāditi na yuktam | tadrūpavittau tasyaivāsiddheḥ | jāto nāmāśrayo'nyonyaḥ (pra. vā. 2. 235)
ityādi smaryatām |
[396,2]
na ca tadā bhrāntirbhavitumarhati, vasturūpasyeva nirbhāsāt, alīkavitteriti cet ?
saivāstvarthādhyavasāyaḥ katham ? saiva sa iti cet — na, alīkamidamiti viduṣo bāhyādhyavasāyavyavasthābhāvāt | nālīkavijalpanamapi tu tatsaṃvedanaṃ bāhyādhyavasāya iti cet ?
evamapi paryāyatāmātraṃ syāt, nābhimatārthavyaktiḥ | bahiḥsvarūpasparśavirahe hi yāvaduktamalīkākārajñānamiti tāvaduktamavasāya iti | tato na viśeṣaḥ kaściduktaḥ | tathā ca sati yathālīkākārajñānaṃ na bāhyasyeti saṃbandhamarhati, tathāvasāyo bāhyasyeti na sambandhī bhavet | tadbodhābhimānadvārikā hi ṣaṣṭhī tadabhāve bhavet katham ||
[396,3]
tataḥ paramparāyātamalīkaṃ yadi tasya tat | tāvatā ca bhramo naivamanalīke'pi duṣyati ||
[396,4]
tato yaducyate, tadayamabhilāpasaṃsargayogyaḥ pratibhāsaviśeṣa eva buddherarthādhyavasāya iti tannirastam, arthasyeti sambandhānupapatteḥ, bodhe ca bhramābhāvāt | api cālīkaḥ pratibhāsa ityevāvasāyo'stu kimabhilāpasaṃsargayogyaviśeṣaṇena ? nirvikalpavyavacchedārthamiti cet ? yadyevamanalīkavāde'pi tadviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭameva jñānaṃ bhramo na sarvamiti na sarvathā saṃkleśaviśuddhivaidhuryam, bhramabhraṃśe'pi jñānajātiviśeṣasyaiva viśleṣāt | ubhayamate'pi cābhilāpasaṃsargayogaḥ parāpekṣa iti na kṣatiḥ | kevalaṃ tadapratītau tadavasāyavyavasthā dustheti doṣaḥ | sa cāvayoḥ sādhāraṇa iti |
[397,1]
tasmāt sudūramapi dhāvatā pratītimantareṇāpi śaktiviśeṣādeva bahiṣṭhāṃ vṛttim ākṣipaṃstadgrahopacārādavasāyo bāhyasyeti saṃbandhayadvṛttimadhyāsta ityupagantavyam |
tadā cālīkaḥ satyo vā ākāra iti na viśeṣaḥ | evaṃ cāvasāyārthe'vasīyamānatvena prakāśyatāmāsañjyārthasya tādātmyamasatyarthe'bhāvādikaṃ ca yaduktam, tatsarvamanupapannam |
adṛṣṭvā buddhirarthaṃ pravartayatīti ayameva viplavaḥ | ataeva vikalpākāre'pyapohe vācye arthasya sparśābhāvāt kva sarvākāraparicchedaprasaṅgadoṣa ityāha, upaplavaśca sāmānyadhiyastenāpyadūṣaṇā | (pra. vā. 3. 169)
iti, ekavyāvṛttyākāratayā tatraiva pravṛttyākṣepāt | tāvatā ca puruṣaḥ paritoṣalābhāt nāparaṃ vivecayati | tanmātrasyālābhe tu visaṃvādamāha — yasya ca sato'pi na vikalpabuddhau kasyacit prakāśaḥ, tasyāsato nāmeti yuktidūrametat | na ca prakāśamānasyāsattvamiti |
tat kathaṃ gotvadṛṣṭāntena nīlasyāsataḥ prakāśanaṃ, tādātmyakalpanaṃ ca | etena nānārūpaniṣṭhayorityādyapi nirastam | asatprakāśayorvirodhasādhanādekavastunīti cāyuktam, prakāśasya nīlavyatiriktasya vastuno'bhāvāt bhedakalpane ca na prayojanam, dvayorekaniṣedhamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt | sa caikatra pratibhāsinyanyatra kalpite syāt, ghaṭa iva paṭatvasya, bhinnapratibhāsayorapi vā śaśakamaśakayoriva | abhinnapratibhāsayoḥ punaratadvyāvṛttimātravyavasthāpitabhedayorna kvacidayaṃ nyāyaḥ siddhaḥ |
[397,2]
varṇasaṃsthānayorabhinnapratibhāsane'pi saṃsthānamasaditi cet — na, vyatiriktasyaiva avayavasaṃsthayogākhyasya kalpitasya saṃsthānasya tatrāpi niṣedhaḥ, parimaṇḍalādivyavahāragocaradaśāvyāvṛttodayaścaturasraśabdābhidheyo varṇātmā kathaṃ niṣedhyaḥ ? tathehāpi bhinnasya kalpitasyaiva niṣedhaḥ prakāśasya nīlasya vā nīlātmā prakāśātmā vā nīlo na niṣeddhuṃ śakyaḥ, avyatirekapratibhāsādeva | tataśca vastutve'nāropitatve vā sādhye nīlasya bhāvāt |
[397,3]
prakāśabhūtabuddhyākārāpekṣayā ca na sādhyābhāvaḥ | na hi gotvākāraprakāśasya kenacidāropaḥ tadvyatiriktasyāropakasyābhāvāt, svayaṃ ca svahetorgotvākārasyaiva prakāśasya niṣpatteḥ | na cātmanaivātmana āropaḥ, nāpyanyenānyasyāropo, nāmakaraṇaṃ tu syāt tataśca prakāśātmakatvaṃ sarvatrānāropitameveti nāsiddhigandhaḥ | kiṃ ca, āropitaṃ jalādivadasphuṭameva bhavitumarhati | nīlasya ca prakāśatā sphuṭataraiva vedyate |
na tu bhinnaprakāśasya tu bhinnanīlatvasyeva, sphuṭatve vā nīlavat prakāśasya sataḥ khyātirāyāteti |
[398,1]
evaṃ yatra yatra tarkāgamayorasadalīkaṃ vā pratibhātīti pratītiḥ bhāṣyakāravyākhyānādanyatra tatrādhyavasitāpekṣayaiva vyāvahārikābhiprāyād vā | sa hi tadākṛtikalpitabāhyasādhyārthakriyābhāvamātrādalīkādi vyavaharati | tadanuvādena bāhyaniṣedhamātrametat | tattvatastu sadantaramevāsat, iṣṭādanyatayā cālīkamucyate | athāpi syāt |
yadā nityākārā buddhiḥ, tadānekakālavyāpitayodayādākāravannityaṃ sadeva syādityapi yatkiñcit | anukāramātreṇa hi tadākāratā, na tu tādātmyena, agnivikalpamātreṇa dāhaprasaṅgāt | tato yathā tāvaddeśavyāpako vaṭaviṭapī patramātrapidheyenāpi darpaṇatalapratibimbenānukṛtaḥ kuto'pyākārabhedāttathā kṣaṇikenāpyākāreṇa nityaḥ | anubhavaścātra, nityātmādivikalpanakāle buddhyantarāvakāśaparipanthinīṃ sakalakālavyāptimantareṇaiva tadanukāraḥ |
[398,2]
alīkatve'pi hi na tāvatkālavyāpinaivālīkena bhavitavyaṃ nityākāreṇa, anyathā tadanurūpasadasattāvicārādipravṛttyākṣepakatvābhāvāt | ato leśena tadanukāraḥ kālavyāptiṃ vināpīti yuktam | yathā cordhvadaṇḍādipratikṛtiryadākadādriyate | adhaūrdhvamadhyabhāgairatītānāgatapratyutpannarūpopalakṣaṇaparairnityasya sarvāvasthājanyamekasyāmeva syāditi darśayitum, tathā buddherapi kṣaṇameva tadākārāyā nodayavirodha iti | tasmāt yadasat tanna prakāśate, adhyavasitamātraṃ tu syāt | yathoktaṃ prāk | yaśca prakāśate svātmanāsāvasanniti siddham | tataśca nāsataḥ khyātirnāma bhramalakṣaṇamasaṃbhavāt |
ata eva sanna prakāśata iti na tṛtīyo'pi prakāraḥ, prakāśavyāptatvāt sattāyāḥ, aprakāśasyāsattayā grasteḥ |
[398,3]
nanu prakāśo nāma vastunaḥ sādhakaṃ pramāṇam | na ca pramāṇanivṛttāvarthābhāvaḥ |
arthakriyāśaktiśca vastusattvam | tacca nāprakāśasyāpi virudhyata iti cet ? satyametad bahirarthavāde'prakāśasyāpi tasyābhyupagamāt | keśādipratibhāse'dhyavasitasyārthaśaktiviyogādevābhāvasiddheḥ | sarvathā bahirarthābhāve tu jñānasya prakāśāvyabhicārāt tāvataiva sattve kimarthakriyayā ? kathamanyahṛdaḥ sattvaṃ prakāśādeva nāsya cet | nārthakriyāpi sarvasmai kvacicced bhāsanaṃ na kim ||
api ca,
[399,1]
bāhye'pyarthe prakāśena sattvaṃ tattvata iṣyate | pratipatturabhiprāyāt śaktyā sattvavyavasthitiḥ ||
[399,2]
śakterapi prakāśena vinā sattāprasiddhitaḥ | śaktyantarabaleneti kathāyāmanavasthitiḥ ||
[399,3]
kāryeṇa jñāyate śaktiḥ parāpekṣā ca kāryatā | śakteraniścaye'pyasti bhinnavyāvṛttito yadi ||
[399,4]
śakteraniścaye tasya kāryatāpi kathaṃ nanu | vastusvabhāvaḥ kāryatvaṃ bhinnavyāvṛttibhāgapi ||
[399,5]
anyathā kiṃ na keśādeḥ kāryatākāryataiva cet | tarhi prakāśa evāstu sattvamavyabhicārataḥ ||
[399,6]
nāropitānāṃ kāryaṃ cet prakāśo'pi na kiṃ tathā | ekīkārāt prakāśaścet kāryatāpi kathaṃ tathā ||
[399,7]
phalābhāvād yathā nāṅgaṃ nāṅgābhāvāt phalaṃ tathā | tato vastutvasandehe sandehaḥ kāryatādiṣu ||
[399,8]
tasmādabhyāsasāmarthyāt sāmarthyasya viniścayaḥ | prakāśa eva sattvaṃ tatkāryaṃ dhīreva tasya vā ||
[399,9]
na ca kāryāntareṇāsyāḥ sattvaṃ kiṃ tu svasaṃvidaḥ | gocaraṃ hi vyabhicarenna svaṃ buddhiḥ kadācana ||
[399,10]
kasyacit tatra saṃdehe kārye'bhyāsād viniścayaḥ | sattvaṃ tato bahirapi prakāśādeva tattvataḥ ||
[400,1]
na kṣaṇitvakṣatiścaivaṃ jñānenaikakṣaṇagrahāt | kādācitkaṃ ca tajjñānaṃ liṅgaṃ nityabalavyaye ||
[400,2]
uktā ca śāsre dhīḥ sattā dṛśyasyāsattvamapyadhīḥ | vyapadeśārthakṛtyādihānyapekṣā vinākṛtā ||
[400,3]
aśaktirapi tatrepi na bādhakamiyān punaḥ | viśeṣo dṛṣṭyadṛṣṭī ca sattvāsattve udīrite ||
[400,4]
kadācit kasyacit kvāpi prakāśo'styanumāntataḥ | mṛṣā prakāśābhāvastu vibhāvyo bahirādare ||
[400,5]
vikalpa evānumiterabhāve'pi prakāśanam | tādṛśāṃ yādṛśī sattā prakāśo'pyastu tādṛśaḥ ||
[400,6]
arthakriyārthī sakalaḥ phalenaivaiti vastutām | pratibhāsaṃ ca tatraiva nyasyatīti kriyāśrayaḥ ||
[400,7]
na caivaṃ kṣatirārabdhaṃ mānaṃ ca vyavahārikam | śaktiruktā tataḥ sattā svabhāvaḥ śuddha eva ca ||
[400,8]
tasmād bāhyārthavāde'pi yadyapi vyavahārataḥ | śaktiḥ sattāprakāśastu tāttvikīti dvidhā sthitiḥ ||
[400,9]
ityantaraślokāḥ ||
[400,10]
athākārasya pratibhāsino'pi śaktiviyukteḥ sattvaṃ mābhūdityamunā manorathena śaktiḥ sattvamucyate, tadapi tadvyatirikte pramāṇābhāvāt kīdṛśī iṣṭasiddhiḥ ? na cākārasyārthakāritvaniṣedho'pi śakyaḥ, upādeyakṣaṇasyādhyavasāyasya tadārabdhaprabandhasya ca sadasadādinirṇayarūpasyādyāpyanucchidyamānasya janmani niyataprāgbhāvitvasya darśitatvāt, anyathā na kvacidapi hetuphalabhāvasiddhiḥ syāt | vyatiriktaṃ prakāśamātraṃ tatra heturiti cet ?
[400,11]
anvayavyatirekābhyāmākāro dṛṣṭaśaktikaḥ | hetutvamanyo labhata iti rājakulasthitiḥ ||
[401,1]
yadi tasyāpi hetutvamākārasya na vāraṇam | na hīndhanasya hetutvaṃ dhūme vahnirapahnute ||
[401,2]
ekāpekṣaṃ parasyātha kartṛtvaṃ taddvayorapi | bhāvānuvṛttisāmarthyād dahanendhanayoriva ||
[401,3]
nīlāpekṣaḥ prakāśo'nyaḥ karotīti viniścaye | piśāco vahnisāpekṣo dhūmāṅgamiti cāgatam ||
[401,4]
avidyāpyata evāṅgaṃ kevalā na prakalpate | dṛṣṭasāmagryapekṣā hi na kvacid vinivāryate ||
[401,5]
anyathā citramakhilaṃ karmaṇaivopajanyate | anyahetuvilopaḥ syānna ca syāt pauruṣaṃ phalam ||
[401,6]
bhāvābhāvānanukṛtau na hetuphalatā kvacit | bhāvābhāvānukāre ca nāhetuphalatā kvacit ||
[401,7]
nīladṛṣṭyavasāyaśca nānīlākāradarśanāt | śuktau hi rajatāropo na varṇasya vyatikrame ||
[401,8]
rūpe samānajātīyād bhedagrahaṇaviplave | rūpyāropaṇamaṅgāradarśane tadadarśanāt ||
[401,9]
astu vā daivato'kasmādanyathāpi samīkṣaṇam | jātibhedastadonneyo yoginirmitadhūmavat ||
[401,10]
yathā bāhyasya bījasya sattvahetutvasaṃgare | bījākāradhiyastadvadaṅkurākārajanmani ||
[401,11]
tathā cārthaṃkṣipan bāhyaṃ tatsthāne jñānamādiśan | utpadyante nirudhyante pratyayā ityavocata ||
[401,12]
vyāpakastasya dharmaścet pārthivatvādikāraṇam | prakāśo'pyastu na vyaktiriti sādhvī vyavasthitiḥ ||
[402,1]
yadeva tarhi nīlasya bāhyasya phalamīkṣitam | tadabhāvānna keśādijñānadṛṣṭasya vastutā ||
[402,2]
tatkriyāvirahāttarhi tattvameva niṣidhyatām | na kriyāntarayuktasya vastutāmātravāraṇam ||
[402,3]
ahergiriguhāgarbhānniryato nirjharabhrame | tatkriyātikramādastu vastuto vastutaiva kim ||
[402,4]
avaseyakriyāhānestadarthārthī janaḥ punaḥ | tatraiva sattābhyāsena buddhirūpamasad vadet ||
[402,5]
atastadanurodhena nirbhramābhimate grahe | kalpitasya niṣedhārthamasadbhātyādibhāṣaṇam ||
[402,6]
taddhiyā na svavedyaṃ tat kiṃ tvanyat tacca naiva sat | ato'sadeva gotvādi nākārasyāprakāśataḥ ||
[402,7]
yathā vā candrayugalaṃ tathaiko'pi na candramāḥ | avaseyātmanābhāvastatrātrāpi tatheti dik ||
[402,8]
iyaṃ yathādhyavasitivyavasthā tattvataḥ punaḥ | keśādayo na sāmānyamanarthābhiniveśataḥ ||
[402,9]
ityāha na tvanarthatvādityanyacca sphuṭābhatā | jñānarūpatayārthatvāt keśādīti matiḥ punaḥ ||
[402,10]
sāmānyaviṣayaṃ keśapratibhāsamanarthakam | indriyajñānasaṃkhyātamasad bāhyāvasāyataḥ ||
[402,11]
tathā
[402,12]
jñānarūpatayārthatve sāmānye cet prasajyate | tatheṣṭatvādadoṣo'rtharūpatvena samānatā ||
[402,13]
apratikṣepabhāg dharmī śabdārtha iti cāsakṛt |
[402,14]
tasmāt, yathāpratīti kathitaḥ śabdārtho'sāvasanniti || svayaṃ vibhaktamuktā ca bhāṣye jñānātmabhūtatā | yathāpratoti sattvaṃ cet pratītiryadi bhāsanam || saiva sattā bahiriva jñānatve ca na bādhakam | na bādhāvyāpakābhāvo'śaktyādistu bahirmatau || yuktaḥ pratītyā śabdārthaḥ śābde tadrūpabhāsanāt | svākāre'dhyavasāyaśca bāhyatvenaiva dehinām || tenāsattve ca sattvoktiryathā tattvamiti sthiram | tathā tridhātudhīmātramiti citraiva sā matā || sarvaśūnyādiśabdeṣu tulya eva pariśramaḥ | sākārameva taccittamarthābhāsamitīritam || vikalpitasya bāhyasya niṣedho hi svayaṃ kṛtaḥ | vāsanopahatatvaṃ cāniṣṭe rūpodayānmatam || pravṛttyākṣepisaṃkalpasūtisāmarthyagarbhataḥ | advaitaśikharārohe na pravṛttinivṛttayaḥ || tā eva saṃsāra iti tadvettuḥ kathamiṣyatām | darpaṇe dṛśyate rūpamiti bālābhimānataḥ || anūdya vedanākāre tadāropanivāraṇam | tathā bhāveṣu bhāvatvaṃ jñānākāreṣu bāhyatā || yathā timiriṇā dṛṣṭacandrayoścandratāsatī | nimnācca virahād bāhyenaikatvaṃ darpaṇe'sti na || nāntaḥpraviṣṭanirbhāsāt pṛthaktvaṃ pratighātinā | bhāvairākārasaṃjñairvā lakṣyate bodharūpatā || sāmānyaṃ jñānasaṃkhyātamata evaṃ pṛthagvacaḥ | loke ruḍhaṃ pṛthagiva jñānamādarśasannibham || ākārāḥ pratibimbābhā ubhayoḥ kalpitaṃ na sat | bodhasya naikatā bāhyaiḥ svarūpavirahāptitaḥ || nānyatvamagrahaprāpterna sattā cāprakāśinaḥ | rājakrameṇa cādarśe ekānekatvavarjitam || iti yuktaṃ na vā bhāvā yujyante darpaṇopamāḥ | nirābhāse sthito yogītyābhāsaḥ kalpanā matā || ekāpohena yattasyāmīṣadābhāsate bahiḥ | samantabhāsādābhāsaḥ prapañco vā kadambavat || vicitrakalpanāruḍho heyaścitre'pi cetasi ||
śeṣaṃ samānam | athavā, bāhyagrāhyasya hāne'pi grahaṇasthitivāraṇam | tathatārakṣaṇe sthitvā cittamātravyatikramaḥ ||
yadāha, tatraikasyāpyabhāvena ityādi || āropyahānāvāropaviṣayasyāpi māsma bhūt | citrasyocchedadṛkpāta ityanābhāsavāraṇam ||
tathā ca, tiṣṭhanti citrāṇi tathaiva loka evaṃ hi dhīrā vinayanti tattvam ityādi ||
[404,1]
āryanāgārjunapādāśca, mahābhūtādivijñāne proktaṃ samavarudhyate | tajjñāne vigamaṃ yānti nanu mithyā vikalpitam || tatrāsattvādhimokṣo'rtharodhaścintāmaye hṛdi | tajjñāna iti ca jñānarūpasākṣātkṛtau kṣayaḥ || bādhe nāmanimittānāmākārasya ca na kṣatiḥ | nāmamātraṃ munerdharmāḥ santu vā kalpitātmanā ||
evamanyadapyūhyam ||
[405,1]
tadāgantumaladhvaṃsāt tadākāśatalopamam | jñeyenābhitulā jñeyanirviśiṣṭatayā sphuṭā ||
[405,2]
prakāśamātraṃ tadidaṃ dīpasantānasannibham | aprakāśāṅgavirahānna svākārāprakāśanāt ||
[405,3]
aprakāśakaṇasyāpi na pūrvamapi saṃbhavaḥ | bhramavyavasthāpekṣā tu samalāmalatāsthitiḥ ||
[405,4]
tatraiva hetuparatantravicitrarūpe yat kalpitaṃ grahaṇakarma ca kartṛ cāsat | tasyaiva taddvayavivekividekarūpaṃ niṣpannamāha parito yuvarājarājaḥ ||
[405,5]
tasmānna mukhyapramāṇāgamaśāstrabādhā kācit sākāranaye | nāpyalīkatvamākārāṇāmarthasāmarthyasya samarthitatvāditi | astu vā alīkatāpi, bhramanāmamātraṃ vā | na tu tattvataḥ saṃkleśasaṅgatiḥ, svasaṃvedanapracyuterabhāvāt, parāropavyavasthāvirahāt |
sarvadā muktā eva sarvadehina iti dīrghābhyāsaprabandhapratibandhaḥ | svahetorhi svasaṃvedanarūpasyotpannasya na pareṇa śaktimatāpyanyathākartuṃ śakyam, kiṃ punaralīkābhimatena ?
svahetorekībhūyotpattau ca bhavatu tasya rūpamabhinnavedanam | kimatra gātrāmreḍaparigraheṇa ?
[405,6]
svahetośca tathotpattirvedanaṃ ca tadātmanā | bhāvaiḥ svīkṛtamekatvaṃ vādināṃ mahatī vyathā ||
[406,1]
avidyātastathotpattipratibhāsāviti na tattvamiti cet ? naitadapi sāram, yataḥ, hetoḥ kuto'pi janmāstu hetunā cintitena kimaniṣṭajāto'niṣṭo'pi yādṛśastādṛgeva saḥ || ityanākāravādāya deyo yatnājjalāñjaliḥ | kadāpi bhedo bhāvīti śraddhāgamyaṃ paraṃ yadi || kṣīranīravadekatvagraho bhinnodaye'pi cet | na bhinnena grahābhāvānnātmanaivānyathāgrahaḥ || ātmanā hi yathaivātmagrahaḥ svātmā tathaiva saḥ | parāpekṣaṃ dhiyo vyaktibhramārekavikalpanam || bādhābhāve paratrāpi na bhavyo bhramasaṃbhavaḥ | kiṃ punaḥ svātmasaṃvittau bādhāgandho'pi yatra na || abhedādhyavasāyaścet paścāttenāpi na kṣatiḥ | nirvikalpavadasyāpi svavido'līkamātrataḥ || na ca tatra parāropaḥ sa cālīkaḥ svavedanaḥ | tatpravṛttinivṛttīnāṃ vyāvṛtteḥ ko'paraḥ śamaḥ || alīkamātraṃ sadapi na hi kvāpi vibandhakṛt | vibandhakatve'līkatvamevālīkaṃ prasajyate ||
kiṃ ca,
[406,2]
gocarāntarasañcāro neṣṭa eva kva bandhakṛt | svasaṃvittau punastasya śatenāpi na bandhanam || svavittibandhe hi jaḍaḥ prakāśaśca svahetutaḥ | ityayuktamate'śakyaṃ svābhedenāpi vedanam ||
[406,3]
na hi svahetoḥ sakāśāt prakāśātmano jāyamānasya svavittirvibandhopanītaṃ jāḍyamasya yuktamalīkākārabalāt | ata eva so'līkaḥ svābhedena tadātmānaṃ veda yed ityapi na śakyam, virodhādeva | svavinmātrasya hi niṣpādyamānasya tadanyathābhāvo viruddhaḥ tadatadvodhasvabhāvotpattau ||
[407,1]
atanmātrasya bodhe ced vibandho guṇa eva saḥ | athāsau svayamevāsan śiṣyatāmākṛtigrahaḥ ||
[407,2]
yadyabhinnena rūpeṇa tadā tādātmyamacyutam | vibhinnenāpyalīkena yadi nāsti kṣatiḥ kvacit ||
[407,3]
alīkamanalīkaṃ ca dvayaṃ bhedena gṛhṇataḥ | alīkamanalīkena rūpeṇa yadi paśyati ||
[407,4]
nālīkabodhavārteti nātmālīkena bodhitaḥ | yathā tathā vā cintāyāṃ bāhyāropo na cenmataḥ ||
[407,5]
bāhyārthakarmakāmasya na pravṛttyādisaṃbhavaḥ ||
[407,6]
svavidi niyataṃ cetastasmādalīkamalīkatākalitamitarānāropānna pravṛttinivṛttayaḥ | iti tanubhṛtāṃ sākṣānmokṣe kimaṅga pariśramaiḥ śravaṇatanujākārākārasthitāvapi kā kṣatiḥ ||
[407,7]
tataḥ sarvaprāṇināṃ sarvadā nirvṛtatvāt samyaksaṃbuddhatvenāpi nopayoga iti na kaścidupāyābhyāsamārabheta | tadayamatasmiṃstadgrahalakṣaṇo bhramaḥ svarūpeṇa vicāravidhuro yadi tathā pravṛttyākṣepasāmarthyavyavasthāpito na syāt, nālīkamātrasaṃbhave'pi doṣa iti noktopālambhaparihāraḥ | na pravṛttimanākṣipya so'līko yadi vartate | aśaktiḥ kānalīkasya paśya dhārṣṭyavijṛmbhitam || pravṛttirasyālīkena sadākāraguṇairna tu | viparītarataḥ so'yaṃ yogācārī na tāttvikaḥ ||
tasmāt,
[408,1]
nālīkamātramupayogi bhave bhramātmā nānyatra tadvyavasitiśca vicāracāruḥ | bāhyocitavyavahṛtivyavakalpitastu sākṛtyanākṛtimate dvitaye'pi tulyaḥ ||
[408,2]
tat kathaṃ saṃvaleśavyavadānavyavasthābhraṃśabhayāt sākāraparihāreṇa nirākāra evātrābhiniveśavāsitā matirmatimatāmiti ?
[408,3]
yadi tu parāmarśe'bhiyogaḥ, satyākāramate yuktā śaktiyogādisaṃsthitiḥ | nirākāramate tvantaḥsaṃkleśavyavadānayoḥ ||
iti mahadantaram | tathā hi, ākārasya hi vastutve tādātmyāttadyogādvā viśeṣamanubhavannanubhavastathāvidhamadhyavasāyaṃ prasuvīta, so'pyavasāyo viṣayaviśeṣācitāṃ pravṛttim iti na pravṛttisaṅkaraḥ | yadārtho hi kaścit svabhāvabhūtaviśeṣopayogāt kriyābhedam ādadhīta nolapītavat, kaścit sahakāriviśeṣayogāt, utpalopalapāṇivat |
tatastādātmyasahakārau vastupratibaddhau siddhau | ākārasya cāvastutve na kaścidviśeṣo jalajvalanamanasoriti jalānubhavādapi jvalanavikalpaprasaṅgaḥ |
[408,4]
evaṃ jvalanavikalpāt pānāvagāhanārthinaḥ pravṛttiḥ syāt | na cāgniratreti manyamānaḥ pānakāmaḥ pravartate | svacchatayā sphaṭikamaṇikiraṇaparibhavinyanubhave'bhūtena ākāreṇa ko viśeṣaḥ ? na hi sphaṭika eva nīlapītādivastusāhāyakaṃ vihāya pratipattikriyābhedahetuḥ | asato'pyākārasya pratibhāsādalokavyapadeśabhājaḥ saṃsargācchaktibheda iti cet ? tadayuktam | yataḥ,
[408,5]
pratibhāse'pyasattvaṃ cet saṃsargārtho'tra kīdṛśaḥ | alīkavyapadeśo'pi na satvāpahnavakṣamaḥ ||
[408,6]
tasmādabhinnarūpameva vastu nabhastāmarasayogādvagāhanādikṣamamakāṇḍakruddhabandhyāsutasannidherdāhadāyakamityapi śraddheyamevaṃvādinaḥ | asattve'pi tayoradṛṣṭerākārasya tudṛṣṭerasti viśeṣa iti cet — na darśane'pi sāhāyyasamīhāvirodhino'sattvasyānayanād ityukteḥ | na cāsato'nādheyātiśayasya kutaścit kaścid viśeṣaḥ na tasya kutaścidviśeṣo nāpi tataḥ prakāśasya, upalakṣaṇamātraṃ tvākāra ityapi na saṃbaddham, upalakṣakatvasyāpi vastunyevopapatteḥ śikhādivat | na ca tathopalakṣito'pi prakāśaḥ svayam aviśeṣāt kriyābhedopayogī bhavitumarhati |
[409,1]
karmasāmarthyāt tasya tādṛśī śaktiriti cet — na, karmaṇo dṛṣṭasādhanamanapekṣya śakteradṛṣṭeḥ | na cākārabhedamantareṇa tādṛkkriyābhedo dṛṣṭaḥ, tathāpi tasya sākṣitvamātrakalpane pākādiṣu pācakāderapi tatkalpanāprasaṅgaḥ | tato durapahnavā tatra śaktirākārasya |
na ca bhinnānubhavavyavasthābījaṃ kiñcit | tataḥ prakāśata iti prakāśa ākāra eva |
prakāśanaṃ prakāśa iti tu taddharmamātraṃ bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇeti sthitiḥ ||
[409,2]
ākāra eva niyatā hi bahiḥ pravṛttistasyāṃ bhramasthitirado virahe kathaṃ syāt | tasmānnirākṛtimate sunirākṛteyamārabdhasiddhiriti sākṛtivāda eva ||
[409,3]
evaṃ tarhi yāvadvodhastāvadākāro yāvaccākārastāvadvahiṣṭhā vṛttikṛtā bhrāntisthitiriti na kadācid vyavadānam, alīkatve tvākārāṇāṃ svaprabhavavāsanāsamūhasamuddhātādatyantamatyaye nirābhāsamākāśasaṃkāśaṃ prakāśamātramavaśiṣyata iti vyavadānamucyate | ākārasatyatāmate tu durlabhametaditi ced ? bhavatu kiṃ tādṛśā tena kartavyam ?
mahāprārambhasaṃbhogakāyavilopalolupenāsadvāsanāsamuddhāte hi prakṛtivitathaḥ saṃkalpa eva mā bhūd bahiḥ pravṛttirvā | yadvā ākāro'pyaniṣṭo mā bhūt | cittākāraviśeṣabhāvanāyāḥ śubhasaṃbhārābhiyogasya ca sāmarthyāt abhimatākāraviśeṣasya samudaye kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? na ca kadācidākāre doṣadarśanāt sarvadā tanniyamaḥ, sāmagrībhedasyātyantikasya saṃbhavāt, anyathālīkasaṃbhavo'pi sadātanaḥ syāt | tasmāt,
[409,4]
yātaṃ kāñcit pariṇatiśikhāṃ lakṣaṇavyañjanaśrīcitraṃ cetaḥ śubhaśatasamullāsatābhyāsabhūmnaḥ | saṃbaddhātmā guṇanidhirasadvāsanāsannibaddhā śuddhākāraprakararahitaṃ na tvanākārameva ||
[409,5]
saṃvṛttivinivṛttau syāddharmakāyavilopanam | ākāravinivṛttau ca saṃbhogasya parābhavaḥ ||
[410,1]
daśabhūbhibhujāṃ buddhestadākārāttathā sthitiḥ | piṇḍaṃ vihāya hastasya lehanaṃ sphuṭamīdṛśam ||
[410,2]
saṃbuddhakalpā daśabhūbhujo'pi yadā nirākāratarāntaraṅgāḥ | tadā kraśīyaḥ karalehanaṃ ca varaṃ ca nirmāṇadṛśo varākāḥ ||
[410,3]
buddhādhipatyena tathā prabodhe daśāvanīnāṃ paramaḥ sa lābhaḥ | aṇubhramāṇāṃ bhramabhārayogaḥ sukhaṃ na cāmedhyaviśeṣato'pi ||
[410,4]
taddharmasākṣātkaraṇāditi ceddharmakāyadṛk | prasaktā na tu saṃbhogakāyadṛk tasya sidhyati ||
[410,5]
tadākāratayā tasya tadākārodayo dhiyaḥ | tadbhogaḥ sārvabhaumānāṃ śubhasaṃbhārasaṃbhavī ||
[410,6]
śuddhalaukikavikalpasaṃmukhībhāvabhāvi paṭudharmadeśanam | uddharapraṇidhipākato'thavā sarvavittirapi tattadarthataḥ ||
[410,7]
grāhyādyabhāve'pi tattadarthināṃ tattadarthasaṃvādasaṃbhavāt, sarvajñatāvyavasthāpi sarvasvabuddhyākāravilāsa iti | athavā, yathā sakaladehināmanubhavasya citrā sthitiḥ samantasamayatraye tadanukārisarvākṛteḥ | dhiyaḥ praṇidhipākataḥ samudaye svarūpaśriyā sahaiva vividhākṛtivyatikaraikarūpo vibhuḥ || sūkṣmatarābhrapatrapihito'yamarūpadṛśaḥ sarvamidaṃ svarūpamadhiyanti daśāvanayaḥ | tatra ca niścalāpratimabhāgamuśanti vapurgocarabhāga eṣa iti śeṣamaśeṣamapi || citramanekamekamiti kiṃkṛta eṣa vidhiḥ pārthiva eka eṣa iti kiṃkṛta eṣa vidhiḥ | saṃvṛtisatyametya yadi sā sthitirevamiyaṃ jñānaśubhorubhārajanitastu mahātiśayaḥ ||
asya ca citrākārarāśeḥ nirupadravabhūtārthasvabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ | na bādhā yatnavattve'pi buddhestatpakṣapātataḥ || (pra. vā. 1. 212–3)
tathā hi, saṃbhārābhyāsajanmā niratiśayarucergocarasvaikavittisthityāgantuprapañcāpacayaparicitākāśakakṣāprabhābhūḥ | nānānirmāṇavṛndairanuparatajagatkṛtyarāśirdaśeyaṃ heyā kenāstu yasyā yadi paramucitā vyutthitiḥ kalpanaiva ||
{11.3}
<tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[412,1]
kathaṃ punaḥ svasaṃvedanamātrasthitau hetuphalabhāvasiddhiḥ, yataḥ prakṛtaphalahetupaddhatiravadhānabhājanībhavatu ? tathā hi, na pūrvā na parā nāpi tadubhayavāsanāprasūtānusandhānarūpā buddhirasmādidamiti bhedagrahaṇanāntarīyakaṃ hetuphalabhāvānubhavavyavahāramavatarītuṃ śaknoti, sarvāsāṃ svavinmātramayatayānyadīyavārtāparicayānupapatteḥ | yadyapi cādya dhiyāvadhimātramadhigataṃ tathāpi nāvadhimat, parayā cāvadhimadeva nāvadhiḥ | anusandhānadhiyā tu naikayāpīti ko'paraḥ pratipattā ? avadhiravadhimadityapi tadvalādeva yasmānnaikamapi viṣayaḥ tataśca tayorapi śuddhasvarūpameva viṣayaḥ |
[412,2]
etena pūrvāparabhāvaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ, pūrvāparatayāpi kayācidagrahāt, yena tadātmaka eva hetuphalabhāva iti manorathasiddhiḥ | na hi pratyakṣasyātra vyāpāraḥ, bhinnapratītyabhāve pūrvāparatvāderdūrīkṛtatvāt | athāpi syāt, krameṇodayāt pūrvāparībhāvastāvadasti, tataḥ pūrvāparā buddhirātmānaṃ pūrvāpararūpamevānubhūtigocarīkaroti | vimarśākāravirahāttu śabda eva paramapravartitaḥ | na ca tāvatā vastvanubhavahāniḥ, na hi nāma rūpaṃ vastūnām, tadapi paścādanusandhānabuddhyā pravartate | na ca tāvatā tasyāḥ svavedanakṣatiḥ |
svasaṃviditaiva hi paratra bādhakamupasthāpayati, pūrvapūrvāhitaviśiṣṭasaṃskāradvāreṇa niyatapūrvāparabhāvabodha eva ca hetuphalabodha iti |
[412,3]
atrocyate,
[412,4]
anātmasaṃvittyabhimānakāle samastametad vyavahārayogyam | svarūpasaṃvittiparāyaṇatve kva bhedapūrvāparabhāvayogaḥ ||
[412,5]
bahiryathā bhinnadhiyā grahārhaṃ parasparaṃ tasya tathā bhidāpi | tathaiva pūrvāparatāpi nocenna bāhyamastyeva ca bāhyamānaḥ ||
[413,1]
bāhyasya pūrvāparatā yathaiva tathā dhiyo'pi grahaṇaṃ svayaṃ tu | smṛtiśca saṃvādavatī dvaye'pi kiñcitkaro nānubhavo'nyathā hi ||
[413,2]
tato'nusandhānadhiyā vyadhāyi yat svasiddhamevāpramayāpi tat kila | pramāvatāre tu parāpravedane sphuṭaṃ viyaccitraṇamīdṛśī sthitiḥ ||
[413,3]
na koṣṭhaśuddhyāpi tathocitā sthitiḥ yato na jātu pratipattigocaraḥ | kadāpi kenāpi hi dṛṣṭamanyadā saheta sandehamabādhitaṃ yadi ||
[413,4]
kramo'pi tasmādavasāya paddhatiṃ vinā na so'pyandha ivānyavedane | tato bahirviplata eva na pramā na viplutaḥ svātmani tatra na kramaḥ ||
[413,5]
tathā dhvanereva na siddhirityasat parāparībhūtamapīkṣitaṃ na hi | parasya vittirna na cātmano bhramaḥ bhrame'pi na svasya tathā vivakṣitam ||
[413,6]
nanu hetuphalabhāvavilopastvayāpi kathaṃ sādhyaḥ, pramāṇābhāvāt ? na hi pratyakṣaṃ niścāyakam, avikalpakatvāt | nāpi vikalpamātram, atiprasaṅgāt | pratyakṣaje liṅgaje vāvasāyaḥ svakāraṇasyārthasya niścāyakaḥ pratibandhāditi cet ? pramāṇasiddha eva tarhi hetuphalabhāvaḥ kathaṃ bādhyaḥ syāt ?
[413,7]
tadayuktam | na hyevaṃ pramāṇasiddhirupapāditā bhavati, pratyakṣasya hetuphalabhāvagrahaniṣedhe'pravṛttiniṣedhākṣepāt | paropagamāpekṣāyāṃ na ca svatantrasiddhiḥ, prasaṅgasyāsādhanatvāt | kevalaṃ parasya pratiṣedhapratibandhamātramupasaṃharedayamupanyāsaḥ | yadi hetoḥ kuto'pi syād bādhā hetuphalasthiteḥ | sa eva heturatha na siddhā hetuphalasthitiḥ ||
tathā ca, na heturastīti vadan sahetukram ityādi | na ca parasya niṣedhapratibandhe kṛte svayaṃ sadvyavahārasiddhiḥ | atha parasyāpi parāmarśasiddhipratibandha eva, na kenacit pramāṇena hetuphalabhāvasiddhiriti nāsadvyavahārasiddhiriti cet— na, pareṇa tanmātrasyaivārabdhatvāt | sattāvyavahāro'pi hi prasādhakapramāṇādhīnaḥ siddhaḥ, tadyadi hetuphalabhāve'pi kiñcit pramāṇaṃ syāt, syāt tadbhāvaḥ | tadabhāve kathameṣa iti ? tadayaṃ hetuphalabhāvaḥ kvacit kadācidupalambhasaṃbhāvanāvinākṛto bahirarthena sārdhaṃ niratyayāṃ maitrīmāvahati ||
[414,1]
bāhye doṣantarasyāpi saṃbhavānna tuleti cet | dūṣaṇāntaramatrāpi yathābhāṣyakṛtoditam ||
[414,2]
vinmātrānavatāre'pi sūtravārtikayorgiraḥ | tathaiva balanād bhāṣye svakasvātantryabimbanam ||
[414,3]
naivaṃ vā kiṃ na bāhye'pi doṣo'yaṃ kevalo mataḥ | yadi bāhyo'nubhūyetetyādi yatno'nyathā katham ||
[414,4]
tadasya tanmaitrīkṛto vidhiḥ pratiṣedho vāvadheyo dhīmatāmastu, kimapareṇa ?
nanu tathāpyata upapatteretadāyātamiti nigamayato'pagata eva hetuḥ, avaśyaṃ cāntato'nupalambho'pi samāśreyaḥ, tat kathaṃ hetuparihāreṇa kaścid yuktinyāsaḥ ? na hi tādṛkprastāve śakyaṃ mūkena sthātum ||
[414,5]
bruvatā niyataṃ kiñcit sādhyaṃ vā bādhyameva vā | tatrāhetuṃ bruvāṇasya svavyāpi pratyayaḥ katham ||
[414,6]
tato dustyaja evāyaṃ satā hetuparigrahaḥ |
[415,1]
kiṃ ca svavacanavyāhatamapyetat, ato hi vacanādarthapratītirasya syāditi bacanoccāraṇamañjasā hetuphalabhāvābhyupagamanāntarīyakamiti kathamapavadet ? api ca, hetuphalabhāvaprabhāvitatvāt sarvavyavasthānāṃ prāṇaprayāṇamāyātametasmin mata iti |
etadapyasaṅgatam | na hi sarvathādhyavasāyasiddho'pi nāsti hetuphalabhāva iti, kiṃ tu tattvataḥ | tato,
[415,2]
yāvat prakṛtyā bhrāntasya vyavahārasya na truṭiḥ | tāvattathā tathā hetorupādānaṃ na duṣyati ||
[415,3]
svavittimātrasidhyarthaṃ yathā hetuparigrahaḥ | tathā tannāntarīyau ca kāryakāraṇanihnave ||
[415,4]
vyavahāraprasiddhā cedastu hetuphalasthitiḥ | adhyakṣasiddhā yadi tu mucyatāmātmavedanam ||
[415,5]
na khalu pūrvāparabhāvavyāpibhedagrahaṇavirodhini svasaṃvedane ca sthitiḥ pūrvāparībhūtahetuphalasvabhāvavedanaṃ ceti sacetasāmādaraviṣayaḥ, tadvaraṃ hetuphalagrahaṇamāñjasaṃ mṛṣyatāṃ vijñānavādavyasanaparityāga eva yuktaḥ | tato yathā prakāśādihetavo nirālambanasādhanāḥ saṃvṛtimāśritya vyavahārasmāraṇopayoginaḥ, tathā śaktisādhanānyāpi pramāṇavacanāni na virudhyante | bhedagrahaṇapūrvakaśca hetuphalabhāvo viditaḥ sāṃvyavahārikasya |
abhedagrāhiṇi pratyakṣe upajāte svayameva parigalati, kadācidabhedameva na gṛhṇīyāt |
tatra dvayorapi vādinoryāvaddhetuvyāpāraparisphuraṇaṃ tāvat sādhu, saṃvṛtisthitayoreva vivādāt | tatra ca hetumantareṇa kva siddhivārtā ? tarhi hetunā hetvabhāvaḥ sādhya iti heturātmānamapākarotītyarthaḥ syāt | nāyaṃ virodhaḥ, paramārthe tāvaddhetorevābhāvāt |
[415,6]
evaṃ sarvavyavasthānāṃ vilopo'pi na bādhakaḥ | kramāt sarvaprapañcopaśama eva śivaṃ yataḥ || sarve hi vastusaṃbandhāḥ phalahetutayā gatāḥ | pratītyotpannatāmātraṃ niraṃśaṃ svavidāgatam ||
[415,7]
saṃvṛtau tu heturapi san sādhyamapi sādhayati, vyavasthā api svasthāḥ | kvātmavadhopālambhaḥ ?
[416,1]
yathā bāhyaṃ grāhyaṃ sahitaparapūrvasthiti tathā yathānyat tadgrāhismṛtimapi tathā saṃprathayati | yadā mūlānveṣe prayati vidhurāṇāṃ sthitiriyaṃ prapañco'yaṃ citraḥ kathamiva tadāpahnavasahaḥ ||
[416,2]
iti saṃgrahaḥ ||
[416,3]
kathaṃ tarhi hetunā hetvabhāvasiddhiriti | ayamasyārthaḥ | hetudvārāyātaparamārtharūpānukāriṇi vikalpe yaḥ pūrvāparākāravirahapratibhāsaḥ sa eva hetuphalabhāvagrahābhāvaḥ, tataḥ savyāpārapratītatāmupādāya nirvyāpāro'pi svapratibhāsa etasmin savyāpāra iva lakṣyate | tataḥ sa heturhetvabhāvaheturiti prakhyātiḥ | na ca kalpanākāravivartaviśeṣādanyastattvābhyadhigagopāyaḥ | na tu svavidekalakṣaṇaparamārthaniṣṭhāyāṃ kasyacit kvacid vivādaḥ, sādhanadūṣaṇāvatāro vā | saṃvṛtau ca tasya dūrabhāve'pi kathañcit tadākārasphuraṇameva śaraṇam |
[416,4]
ataeva ca vacanādarthapratītiḥ syāditi jānānasya heturnāstīti prayogastattvata iti viśeṣaṇāpekṣa eva | tathā ca na virodhaḥ sarvathāpahnave tu syādeṣa doṣaḥ, yathā avācakaḥ śabdaḥ, nānumānaṃ pramāṇamiti, tatrāpi tattvata iti viśeṣaṇānna kvacid vyādhātaḥ anumānamapīndriyapratyakṣavat saṃvyavahārata eva pramāṇaṃ, na tattvataḥ, saṃbandhagrahaṇādyapekṣatvāt | na ca svavinmātramagnena tacca śakyam, svabhāvahetāvapyanvayavyatirekayoḥ pratītibhedasādhyatvāt | saṃvādācca prāmāṇyaṃ, na ca kvacid bhinne vastuni saṃvādaḥ | tasmāt svavedanātiriktasya prāmāṇyaṃ sāṃvṛtameva, tathā hetuphalavyavahāro'pi sāṃvṛta eva, ekapratītikatvādubhayoḥ, na paratra yathā mānaṃ tathā hetuphale ca na | yathā ca hetuphalate paratrāpi tathā pramā || tat kasmin bharamādhāya mānasiddhirihocyate | tattvato'nyagrahāsiddheḥ saṃvṛtau siddhasādhanam || avicāritaramyā dhīḥ saṃvṛtiryāvadanyavit | uttarottaradhīgrāhyaṃ tattvaṃ syād yāvadadvayam ||
idamito jātamiti ca, liṅgāt paravido vāsya vikalpasya samudbhavaḥ | iti saṃvṛtireveyaṃ vyāpāraḥ svavido'tra na || tathābhimānamātraṃ syādanusandhānadhīrapi | tato'bhimānamātrād yat siddhaṃ sāṃvṛtameva tat || yāvacca saṃvṛtistāvaddhetvādiniyamaḥ sthiraḥ | aniṣṭaparihāreṇa pravṛttiśca na duṣyati || atha śaktiṃ vinā na syāt saiva śaktestu saṃbhave | sāṃvṛtatvakathā mithyā śabdabhedena kiṃ phalam || kevalaṃ hetuphalayoḥ sahyaṃ bāhyatvameva na | bījākāradhiyastu syādaṅkurākāradhīriyam || tayostarhi dhiyorhetuphalabhāvavido dhiyaḥ | bhedabāhyavidevāsau śabdabhedena kiṃ phalam || abhede dvaitavirahānna hetuphalatāsthitiḥ | te eva vā dhiyau syātāṃ vyatirodhavirodhike || na pūrvā na parā buddhirnātmā tadgrāhako'paraḥ | paścād vikalpo grāhīti śalyo jeṣyati pāṇḍavān || yadi śaktigraho bāhyagraho'pyastu hriyātra kim | atha nyāyaruco rucyā muktiḥ śaktigrahasya ca || dṛṣṭamityavasāyaścedvahiraṣyeṣa vidyate | svavinniṣṭhaiva bāhyasya bādhā saiva phalāṅgayoḥ ||
tathā ca sūtram,
[417,1]
hetupratyayavyāvṛttiṃ kāraṇasya niṣedhanam | cittamātravyavasthānamanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham ||
[418,1]
anutpādamiti phalaniṣedhaḥ | cittamātrasthitireva hetuphalaniṣedho vyaktaḥ |
[418,2]
hetunaiva bhavato yadi vṛttiryāvadeva bahiradhyavasāyaḥ | yāvadātmamatirapratibhāvād vyāpṛtiṃ na parato na tu yadvat ||
[418,3]
nānumānamapahāya nirṇayo nānumā ca paramāṃ vidaṃ vinā | svaṃ paraṃ ca vinihanti sā yathā svaṃ paraṃ ca mama hetavastathā ||
[418,4]
rūpatrayanirūpaṇaviśuddhasādhanaprabhavaṃ prakṛtyā bahirmukhapravṛttikamanumānamanyavittināntarīyakamapi parabodhasādhanāya sādhanīkurvantaḥ kvacit prakaraṇe tadarthānuvādinameva virodhadūṣaṇena codayantīti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ | kevalaṃ yathā pṛthagjano nānumānaprāmāṇyaṃ parihṛtya jīvituṃ śakto dvaitābhiniveśāt, tathā tadavasthāpitasatyādhimokṣamapi | ya eva ca tatsiddhasvabodhamātratāyāṃ satyādhimokṣaḥ sa eva bāhyānumānayorapamānaḥ | na ca tathā sthātuṃ śakyam, anyathā tadaiva sādhyasiddherabhyāsalakṣaṇaprayāsanirāsaprasaṅgāt |
tatasta eva viplavamahimna ātmādhimokṣādiva pravṛttau sākṣātkriyālābhe pratiṣiddhaḥ sarvatrago dharmadhāturiti nānumānasyāpalāpe punaḥ pratyāvṛttiḥ kṣoṇendhanaśikhinaḥ kṣaye'pi bhasmavat | ata eva,
[418,5]
nirālambā praśāmyatīti
[418,6]
saṃvṛtisaṃjñitā vikalpabuddhirityarthaḥ | ayameva cārtho hetuphalavicāraprastāve anūdyate, nādhikaṃ vidhīyate | yāvadeva bahirmano'numānamānanaṃ ca, ayameva hetuphalasvīkāraḥ, tadaiva tadāśrayasyaiva liṅgasya, parokṣe jñāpakatvāt, tatpratītau kārakatvāt |
yaśca paścādātmavedanamātrasthitau tatparibhavaḥ sa eva hetuphalabhāvasyeti kimatrābhiniveśena ? kathaṃ tarhi vijñānavāde vārtikakārasya kārakajñāpakavyavasthā ? satyamavāntaravyavasthāmātrametat | ataeva buddhirāśritya kalpyeteti vacanarītiḥ | tattvaniṣkarṣe tu, aśaktaṃ sarvam (pra. vā. 2. 4)
ityādi |
[419,1]
tadayamarthaḥ, advaitādarvāk pratipādyajanasya mṛdumadhyādhimātrabuddhibhedād yathā tathā vā vyavasthā kriyeta, krameṇa matipāṭavāt tatra tatrānavasthitāvadvaite viśvāsaḥ |
ata evottarottaraparamārthavatsaṃvṛternānātve'pi tadapekṣo hetuphalabhāvāvatārastrividhapratyakṣānupalambhasaṃbhava eva tattvam | svābhiprete'pi vañcanā mā bhūditi tataḥ saṃvṛtyantarādiyameva saṃvṛtirupādeyā, na punaraparamārthābhiniveśāviśeṣe'pyadhamā, abhiprāyasaṃvādetarābhyāṃ viśeṣāt | tadayamaparyanuyoga eva kathamapramāṇāt pratītimātrādarthasiddhiḥ kiṃ punarvicārabādhitāditi ? na hi tatra kācidarthasiddhiḥ puruṣaparitoṣamātrādanyatra | yādṛśī sā pratītireva pratītiḥ, tathānarthasiddhirevārthasiddhiriti yakṣānurūpo baliḥ | yadyāryahṛdayānurodhaḥ, asmadīyahṛdayena tu sarvamasti, nipuṇena tu pratipattrā tathā pratipattavyam, yathā paritoṣamātre'pi vipralabhyeta | ata evāha,
[419,2]
sāṃvyavahārikasya cedaṃ pramāṇasya rūpamuktamityādi |
[419,3]
tasmānna sāṃvyavahārikasya pratiniyatasādhanānusāradoṣaḥ, anyasya kva paritarṣaḥ ?
nanvasmanmatena tāvat sarvamasti, tattvasākṣātkāriṇāṃ tu nāstīti kvāvasthānamastu ?
satyam,
[419,4]
jñātatattvasya loko'yaṃ jaḍonmattapiśācavat | jñātatattvo'pi lokasya jaḍonmattapiśācavat ||
[419,5]
tadatra svātantryamicchāyāḥ |
[419,6]
lokasyāsatprakāśced vyavasthāto'stu nāñjasā | svābhāsakalpanādanyaddhetvāderna hi bhāsanam ||
[419,7]
tasmāt tattvataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvābhāve'pi saṃvṛtāvaśakyaparihāratvāt katham anavadheyaḥ ? prakṛtasya phalasya hetusaṃbhārāt saṃbhavaḥ, sāṃvyavahārikasyaiva tadanuṣṭhānārthitayā tadanusaraṇāt | tattvasākṣātkāriṇastu yathā na hetuphalabhāvasiddhiḥ kvacit, tathānuṣṭhānamapi na kvacit | kathamanarthakāriṇaḥ sattvamiti cet — na, asmadapekṣayā strakṣaṇākṣīṇaparārthakriyāprabandhāvicchedāt | tattvatastu prakāśa eva vāstavī satteti vyavasthāpitaṃ citrasyaiva rūpasyeti sthitam |
[420,1]
nanu tathāpi,
[420,2]
citraṃ tadekamiti cedidaṃ citrataraṃ tataḥ | (pra. vā. 2. 200) tataścitratamaṃ cedaṃ yad bhede vedanaṃ mithaḥ ||
[420,3]
nānākāraṃ hi citramabhidhīyate, tataḥ parasparaviruddhadharmādhyāsināmākārāṇāṃ kathamabhedaḥ ? bhedo'pi tarhi kathamekavedanāntargatānāṃ bhinnasantānavat parasparamasaṃvedanāt ekasyaiva kasyacit pratibhāsaprasakteḥ | tadayuktam, viruddhadharmādhyāsasya tadavasthatvāt |
tasmādanekamevedam, abhinnopādānajanyatvāttu parasparamadhyakṣabhāvaḥ sāhityapratibhāsasvabhāvaḥ | santānāntarabhuvāṃ tu buddhīnāmabhinnopādānatāvirahānnātivyāptiḥ |
[420,4]
atra cintyate,
[420,5]
ekopādānatā tāsāṃ nānātvaṃ kimapohati | nānātvādeva cānyonyavedanaṃ tāsu neṣyate ||
[420,6]
na hi saṃvit parasaṃvidamāviśati | ekasaṃvidargalavigamādeva ca svaparavidām anyonyavedanāpavādaḥ | sa cāpracyutaḥ prastute'pīti na viśeṣaḥ | nanu sāhityapratibhāse vyavasthāpye kimekasaṃvidāveśena, sādhyavirodhinā tamantareṇāpi kṣaterabhāvāt ? nanu sāhityamityapi sahacāramātraṃ taddeśakālopaniyate lakṣaṇaṃ khyātam | pratibhāsaśca teṣāṃ svasvarūpasākṣātkaraṇamiti nānyonyavedanamupapāditam, santamasamagrasannihitānekapuruṣavat | tataḥ parasparasaṃvidāveśa eva parasparavedanavyavahāropayogī kimatra sāhityamātreṇa ? atha sarveṣāṃ sarvatra pratibhāsa eva sāhityapratibhāsaśabdenābhimataḥ, tadā sāhityapratibhāse'pi sādhye viruddhaḥ sarvatraikasaṃvidāveśa iti riktā vācoyuktiḥ |
tadarthatve hi sahāya evāyam |
[420,7]
ekasaṃvidi nānyonyadhvaniścet tadapahnave | pratītireva nānyonyamarthadoṣo'tra duḥsahaḥ ||
[421,1]
mā bhūd vā sāhāyyaṃ sāhityapratibhāsasya tu parasparapratibhāsārthatve abhinnopādvanatve'pi bhedāniṣedhāt, na hi svasaṃvitparasaṃvidamāviśatītyatra dūṣaṇe kimuttarīṃkṛtamiti na vidmaḥ, paryāyamātraghoṣaṇe viśeṣāpoṣaṇāt || ekopādānabhāve'pi na hi tāḥ sahitā api | āviśanti mitho vittimanyathā bheda eva kaḥ || svavidekanimagnāstā na spṛśantyanyasaṃvidam | sākṣātkurvanti cānyonyaṃ kimapyetanmahādbhutam ||
api ca,
[421,2]
upādānābhedād vyatiparicayaśced varamataḥ svabhāvasyābhedo bhavatu na tu bhinne'pyanubhavaḥ | tathaikā sāmagrī yadi niyatavastugrahasahaṃ sṛjeccetastat kiṃ bhayamubhayathā lakṣaṇahateḥ ||
[421,3]
evaṃ hi satyutpattisārūpyābhyāṃ yad grāhyalakṣaṇaṃ tasya dūṣaṇād bhītirna kācid, bahirarthavādino'nyathaiva grāhyagrāhakabhāvasya sulabhatvāt | tatropādānābhedāt parasparamanubhavaḥ sarveṣāmanubhavasvabhāvatvāt | ekasāmagrījanyatve tu jaḍānubhavayoḥ pratiniyataṃ vedyatvaṃ vedakatvaṃ ca syāt | tatpratibandhācca nātiprasaṅgaḥ | atha jaḍasyāpi tadānīṃ sphuraṇāt kutaḥ pratiniyamaḥ ? jaḍopādānatvādeva grāhyaṃ, tadanyad grāhakamiti | indriyeṇātivyāptiriti cet — na, sāmagrīsāmarthyādeva nīlasyaiva vedyatvenotpatteḥ |
[421,4]
sahabhāvitayānyonyamupakāraviyogitā | tādātmyavyativṛttiśca yuvayorubhayorapi ||
[421,5]
atha prakāśotpatteḥ sādhāraṇatvadoṣa iti cet ? vedyatvenotpattirna prakāśatvena |
kimidaṃ vedyatvamiti cet ? svasaṃviditayoḥ kimidaṃ parasparavedanamiti samānam | atha na vedyatvaṃ prakāśotpatteranyaditi cet ? tathāpi sādhāraṇatvaṃ sāmagrībalādeva parihariṣyate |
athaikarūpatvād vastuno nīlatvavat prakāśenāprakāśenāpi nanvasādhāraṇena abhūtvā sthātumaśakyam | śakyameva sāmagrībalāditi tūṣṇīkāmāsyatām |
[422,1]
atha pramāṇavyāhato'yamartha iti kva sāmagryāḥ śaktirupanīyatām ? yastarhi tadavatāramapi nāpekṣate svarūpanirūpaṇe svayameva parigalati, tatra kathamupādānābhedanirdeśaḥ ?
na hi dvayoḥ prakāśayorutpannayorekenānyaḥ prakāśyate, ekasyānyaḥ pratibhāti, ekasmin veti kācidarthasaṅgatiḥ | yathā hi pradīpasya svaprakāśaḥ kathañcid vidito jñāne tadanusāreṇānugamyate, tathā na pradīpānāmanyonyaprakāśatāpi kācidupalabdhā, tato yathā dīpena dīpāntaraṃ prakāśitamiti viplavastathā jñānena jñānāntaramiti | tat kasminnarthe ekopādānamuttaramastu ?
etena svasya vedanamityayogavyacchedasyāpi nāpahnava evātivyāptiparihāraścet sulabha ityapi nirastam, paravedanārthasyaivāpratiṣṭhānāt |
[422,2]
paraprakāśo'pi dṛṣṭa iti cet ? so'pyaprakāśopādānasya prakāśakṣaṇāntarajananadvāreṇetyanavasara eva jñānadīpādiṣu | yastu tatrāpi sahabhāvinamālokaṃ paṭasya prakāśakamicchati so'pi na lokādhyavasāyamātreṇa tattvavyavastheti, idamasyeti vyavasthānibandhanānumāne yadi tajjñānajananamāśrayet, tat tarhi jñānena sahabhuvārthasya prakāśanasvīkāre nāstīti duḥsthā vyavasthā | athehāpi pṛṣṭhajavikalpajñānāpekṣayā sāmyam ? tarhīdameva grāhakaṃ na pūrvakam | idantvabhinnakālamiti sautrāntikamatāvatāraḥ |
[422,3]
atha nālokasya jñānajanane'pi tāvatā prakāśakatvam, jñānamapi sahabhāvyeva, kiṃ tu sāmagrītaḥ sahotpattimātreṇa, tarhi tadātanendriyāṇyapi prakāśakāni prasajyeran, teṣāmaprakāśarūpatvāditi cet ? prakāśo'pi prakāśa evāstu, prakāśakastu katham ? na hi pītasya sahabhāvamātreṇa nīlaṃ pītakaṃ bhavitumarhati | tasmānnākiñcitkaraṃ kasyacit saṃbandhapaddhatimadhyāste | kāraṇopakāradvāreṇa tu pradīpo'prakāśasvabhāve ghaṭādau dṛṣṭaḥ tadvyavahārabhāk, tatastajjñānasya jñānāntaraṃ prakāśamiti gamyamānaikopādānabhāve na ṣaṣṭhīṃ prayuñjīta nāma |
na punaradhyakṣatāpekṣayā, caitrasya maitraḥ sundara ityatra yathā gamyamānasaudaryatāpekṣayā, na tu saundaryāpekṣayādhyakṣatā, saundaryayorekātmaniṣṭhatvāt |
[422,4]
naivaṃ kaścit prayuṃkta iti cet ? yadi paribhāvakaḥ syāt tadapi kathaṃ prayuñjīta, samānatvāt nyāyasya ? tadasyāndhadugdhanyāyena grahaṇe gatametad grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇavaidhuryadvāreṇādvayasādhanaṃ nyāyanāyakasya | na cāyaṃ nyāyaḥ, tat kimanena vārtikakāradveṣāt śubhaguptajuṣṭaloṭanena ? anekapradīpavadeva tarhi saṃvidaḥ sahitāḥ pratibhānti bhinnāśceti vedanenāpi ko'rtha iti cet — na, vyatiriktapratipatryapekṣayā hi sahitāḥ prakāśanta iti vyavahāraḥ | nanu tadabhāve'pi sahitānāṃ prakāśanaṃ na kṣīṇam | evametat | na tu eko'pyanyasya prakāśa ityasti | svasvaprakāśarūpatā punarayoghaṭīpihitānāmapyastīti na prastutasiddhiḥ | tasmādanyonyasaṃvidantarbhāva evānyonyavedanavyavahārasiddhiḥ | na hyekadīpaprabhavā api parasparaprakāśino dīpā iti vārtāpyasti ||
[423,1]
bhinnā evāṇavastatra jīvaṃ cet sutarāṃ priyam | kvāpyadṛṣṭestathā hetorasādhāraṇatā sphuṭam || svaprakāśo yathā dīpo dṛṣṭo'nekastathā yadi | bījābhedānmitho bhāsastatra dṛśyeta sādhvidam ||
[423,2]
tadayamekasāmagrīsaṃbhavo'vyabhicāradvāreṇa kvacidekadarśane'nyānumānāya prabhavet, nānyādhyakṣatvāya, rasarūpādivat | evamekopādānatāpi sajāyīyatāmadhikāṃ prasādhayet, na svabhāvasaṅkarasādhyamanyaprakāśam | anyathā kvacidekamanyasya jaḍamityapi syāditi |
etenābhinnopādānatvameva parasparapratibhāsa ityapi kalpanamapāstam, ekopādānānāṃ jaḍānāmapi parasparajaḍatvaprasaṅgāt | ātmātmarūpeṇa hi teṣāmapi jaḍatvam, evaṃ prakāśatvamapi ||
[423,3]
api ca,
[423,4]
na rūpajananadvārā yathā vastumati sthitiḥ | ekopādānabhāvena tathāstu paribhāṣayā ||
[423,5]
yathā hi, sautrāntikasya sarūpajananameva grāhyatvaṃ, na tu tasyāpi sphuraṇam, evamekapratibhāsa evānyapratibhāsaḥ syānna citrapratītiḥ | kiṃ ca, ekopādānatvamapi śuddhāvadheyametat, svapnajāgradavasthayościtrākārasyaiva hetutvāvadhāraṇāt | vyākulakāle'pi vikalpasyānekākāravivartatvāt, ekavastuvikalpane'pi pradeśabhedenākārasya citratvāt | puñjāt puñjotpattau cānyatamasyaiva sāmarthyakalpane ca kvacidanekasya janakatvaṃ bhāvābhāvānukāraṃ samānam | vicchinnatīlākārādapi nīlākārodayadarśanāditi nottaramacitrāt citrotpattivādinaḥ | aśakyasaṃkhyānatvācca na nyūnādhikabhāvaḥ | kiṃ ca vaṭavat,
[423,6]
nyūnādhikatve'pi bhavet kiñcidekamanekakṛt | na tvekabhāvo nyūnasya bhāve vā citramadvayam ||
[424,1]
tajjñānaṃ tadvadanyadapi gāḍhasvāpādyavasthānantaraṃ cālayavijñānāt pradeśabhedena citrādeva citrāntarotpattiḥ | astu vā saṃmūrcchitākārādekasmāt kadācit kutracit citrasya krameṇākrameṇa vā bhāvaḥ | yadā tāvat jāgarānantaraṃ yāvatkālamanavaruddho middhādibhistāvat prathamakṣaṇabhuvo vihāya nāpareṣāṃ parasparamanubhavaḥ syāt, upādānabhedāt | paramparayā tadekaprabodhāditi cet ? yathā yathā tarhi vyavadhānaṃ, tathā tathā mandatātāratamyādanyo'nyaprakāśapraṇāśaḥ kiyatāpyantareṇa syāt | citraprakāśāvināśaśca jāgarādibhiranekaṃ dinamanubhūyate, nāpi mandatātāratamyam | naivaṃ jñānākāre śakyamiti cet ? ekākārasaṃvedanena bhinnasya saṃvedanamityapi kathaṃ śakyaṃ yadi nāmopādānābhedaḥ, svagatasyaiva bhedābhedasya prayojakatvāt ? na ca prasaṅge tattvameva, viparyayaparyavasāyitvāt |
[424,2]
kiṃ ca,
[424,3]
upādānena saṃbandhādupādeyasya ced grahaḥ | upādānasya kiṃ neti saṃbandho na prayojakaḥ ||
[424,4]
svabhāvaviprakṛṣṭo hi parasparasya bodhaḥ, tāṃ ca sīmānamatikramya sannikarṣaḥ svaprabhāvamādarśayati, sa copādānenaiva sārdhaṃ mukhya iti ekasāmagryadhīnānumānavaddhetupratītidvāraka eva sahabhuvo bhinnasyānubhavaḥ syāt | atītatvānneti cet ? svabhāvakālaviprakarṣayorna kaścid viśeṣaḥ | athopādānasya dvayamapyetat, sahabhuvastu svabhāvaviprakarṣamātram | atra tarhi sannikṛṣṭatvamapi nikṛṣṭam | upādāne tu prauḍhamiti godhāśaśanyāyaḥ | sannikarṣabalācca grahaṇasthitiḥ | athātītasphuraṇe vartamānatvameva syāt, kathamatītatvam ? tato nātītasphūrtiḥ | yadīdṛśī tattvadṛṣṭiḥ parasyātmabhūtayā saṃvidā saṃvedyamānaṃ paraṃ svarūpameva syāt kathaṃ paravittiḥ ?
[424,5]
tatrānunmīlitākṣasya sannikarṣaghoṣaṇamanyatrāpyastu | yogivad vātītagrahaṇamapi syāt | evaṃ prabandhapravṛttau pūrvapūrvasarvakṣaṇavīkṣaṇaprasaṅgo yāvadekamupādānamanavadhirvā |
yathā vyavadhitāratamyaṃ tathā sannikarṣaprauḍhitāratamyamiti | evaṃ svopādeyasyāpi pratibhāsaprasaṅge sarvaṃ tadvat | api ca yadi citrapratibhāsasya bheda eva tadā nīlapītavannīlakhaṇḍayorapīti paramāṇuparyantadarśanāt na kiñcidekaṃ saṃviditamasti yasyānyadekopādānaṃ syādityapratirodhamāndhyamaśeṣasya jagataḥ | na vā kiñcidityetatparyavasāno'yaṃ vādaḥ |
tad yadīdameva vivakṣitaṃ kimanena phalguvalgitena ? ṛjunā krameṇānekatvamapi bhāvānāṃ nāstītyetadevocyatām | ākārāṇāmavastutvamiṣṭameveti cet ? tathāpi kimanena nyāyamasahamānena ?
[425,1]
api ca, ākārāṇamavastutvānnaikopādānasaṃbhavaḥ | prakāśamātrasya punarbhedābhāve'pi na kṣatiḥ || athāpi bheda iṣyeta na mṛṣyeta mithaḥ prathām | mithaḥ prathāyāḥ kṣāntau tu grāhyagrāhakatā parā ||
iti siddhāntaviplavaḥ | tadayamācāryanirapekṣamākhyāyamāno'pyupādānābhedaḥ svabhāvabhedamanākṣipannaiṣāmākārāṇāṃ parasparānubhavavibhāvanāya prabhavati | dṛśyate tāvadevaṃ cet dṛśyatāṃ kiṃ tvabhedataḥ | bījasya svātmano veti vicāramidamarhati || ekatve citratā'bhāvo nānātve sutarāmayam | naikatvaṃ nāpi nānātvaṃ buddhīnāmupapattimat ||
tat ko'tra paramārthaḥ ? tathā hi,
[425,2]
ākārā yadi rūpameva manasaścitrāḥ kathaṃ kiṃ nu vā cetaścitramanekameva yadi tat kutraikyamāsthīyatām | aṇvākāradharā ca dhīraviṣayo nāpi kṣamā saṃhatau bhāsante ca parasparavyatikaraṃ ko'pyeṣa māyāvidhiḥ ||
[425,3]
tasmāt, idaṃ vastubalāyātaṃ yadvadanti vipaścitaḥ | yathā yathārthāścintyante viśīryante tathā tathā || (pra. vā. 2. 209) bhāvā yena nirūpyante tadrūpaṃ nāsti tattvataḥ | yasmādekamanekaṃ ca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate || nāṅgāni dhārayantyete vicāraviṣadūṣitāḥ | varaṃ hyapekṣitā bhāvāḥ kṛtvā gajanimīlanam ||
iti | svapnamāyāmarīcigandharvanagarapratibhāsavat sarvadharmaśūnyataiva nyāyaprāpteti paramārthaḥ | nanu bhagavantamadhikṛtya prakrānto vicāraḥ, tat kimīdānīṃ buddho'pi bhagavān māyopamaḥ svapnopama iti cet ? kasya punaratropālambhaḥ svayameva bhagavatā tathā prathanāt, sollāsaṃ tadvyāhṛteścāryairudyotanāt, tathatayā ca tathāgatapṛthagjanayoraviśeṣasvīkārādāgamopagītagāmbhīryaudāryaviśeṣādanyatra ? nanu vyāpakānupalabdhibādhitatvāt lakṣaṇādyākārāṇāmalīkatvāt kvaudāryamasatkhyātiprasaṅgaśca ? asatpratibhāsijñānasvabhāvatvena bhrāntatvāt kva gāmbhīryam ? tadayuktam, atasmiṃstadgraho bhrāntirbhrāntiranyā nirākṛtā | alīkaṃ cānalīkena rūpeṇa na sa paśyati || yathā sthitā dharmateyaṃ tathā jñānāt tathāgataḥ | vyavasthāmātrato'pyasya bījābhāvād bhramo na hi || yataḥ pravṛttivyāvṛttī vikalpād vāsanābhuvaḥ | tayoḥ samūlamunmūlānnirvikārapadasthitiḥ || asatkhyātirmate cātra nāniṣṭābhāsateha yat | asattattvena tatsarva na cāstyanyadabādhitam ||
pūrvaṃ vistareṇa nirastatvāt |
[426,1]
athāpi dharmottaramārgasaṅgādanaṅgamaṅgīkṛtametadeva | dakādikākāraviviktamantaḥ parisphuradduḥkhasukhādi cetaḥ ||
[426,2]
nātra kila bādhakāvatāro deśavitānībhāvāditi | tadapi viplutam | yataḥ,
[426,3]
antaḥ sātādiviṣayaṃ bahiḥ śītādigocaram | vedanaṃ tattadākāraṃ bādhakagrastameva ca ||
[427,1]
vyaktiviśeṣameva hi jñānasyākāraṃ vidmaḥ | deśavitānābhāvaśca deśasyālpatvaṃ vā syādabhāva eva vā ? tatra paramāṇuparimāṇe'pi deśe prasaṅgī doṣaḥ kiyatyalpe pratihanyeteti na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ | dvitīyastu asaṃbhavī saṃbhavinaḥ, saṃbhavinā hi niyamena kvacid bhāvyam | kvacidapyabhāve'bhāva eva vibhāvito bhavati | saṃvedyante cāsukhasaumanasyādayo dehāntastadvahirdeśavyavacchedena sphurantaḥ | anyathā prakāśavannīlādibhiḥ abhede tadvadeva doṣaḥ |
[427,2]
tatra ca kāye kiyantamabhivyāpya deśamāsata iti kimanena ? kā vā sadeśatā, rūpe'pi svarūpātirekiṇo deśasaṃjñitasya kvacidanupalabdheḥ ? nāpyādhāra eva deśo, vātātapayorapyadeśatāprasakteḥ | na ca tadapekṣayā bādhakapravṛttiḥ, kiṃ tu svarūpāpekṣayā |
svarūpaṃ ca niraṅgamapi kalpanābuddhau yathā vyatiriktairiva dharmāntaraiḥ parikaritamābhāti, tathā ihedamiti kālākāravimarśapratyanīkapratyayakalpito nabhogatipratidvandvīva deśo na nāma vyavahāramavatarati | na ceyaṃ gatirantaḥsukhasaumanasyādivedane dūravartinī sparśāntavadityuktaprāyam | atha yathā nīlādau viśadatarordhvādharādibhāgatvaṃ vitastiḥ hastahastipuruṣādiparimāṇaparicchedyatvaṃ copalabhyate, na tathā sukhādiṣviti matiḥ, tataḥ kiṃ deśavattāmātraparijñāne ? evaṃ hyasparśanendriyagandharasadhvaniprabhṛtīnāmapyadeśatāprasaṅgaḥ |
na ca parokṣe vahnyādāvapi pratiniyatadeśatādi śakyam |
[427,3]
atha yatra phale gandharasasaṃbhavastāvati vartamānau niyatadeśāvūhituṃ śakyau, parapūrvādibhāgena ca grahaṇakāle cendriyaśeṣaparimāṇeneti cet ? sukhādyapi dehāntargatābhogāddeśaparimāṇena kiṃ na śakyaṃ pratipattum ? avyāptistu phale gandharasayorupalabdhā |
bhokturniyatadeśopalambha iti cet ? so'pi sthūlagrāhī nāṇuśaḥ pratiniyamena deśamavasātuṃ śaktaḥ | tasmādatra tāvad vartate kiyantamapi deśamabhivyāpyeti samānam |
evaṃ grahaṇakāle'pīndriyadeśaparimityasya pratiniyamaniścaya eva | sukhāderapi vā sa eva nyāyo darśanaśravaṇajanitasyāpi | apriyāvalokanataptaṃ hi locanameva priyadarśane śītalībhavadanubhūyate | kharāṃśutaptasya taḍāgāvagāhane tu vyaktaḥ parimāṇaviśeṣa ūrdhvādharabhāgo vā | anyadeśodayasya tatrāropakalpane'pi sa eva deśaḥ syāt | parimāṇaniyamo bhūmiṣu bhūbhujāmucitaḥ | idameva ca nṛsukhaṃ yacchābdaṃ saṃvedanamiti na bhinnasiddhiḥ, spaṣṭapratibhāsād vā | saumanasyasya tu mānasatvādaspaṣṭapratibhāse'pi tadanusāreṇa saṃbhavina ihaiva kvacid deśa iti sāmānyena siddherapratibandhāt | nāpi nirbandhaḥ tatropayogī, sādhyasyāpi vikalpakatvaprasaṅgāt |
[428,1]
kiṃ ca parimāṇaniyamānavadhāraṇe yadi deśavattāniṣedhaḥ kvacit, kālavattā tu sarvasya mā bhūt kṣaṇasya parimāṇenāvadhārayitumaśakyatvāt | kevalaṃ pūrvaṃ nāsīt paścācca na bhavatīti pratiniyatakālatāmupasthāpayati sthavīyasī buddhiḥ | ihāpi na bahirdehādihaiva tu saumanasyādīti niścayaḥ sthita eva | kiṃ ca, kālayogastāvadiṣṭa eva saumanasyādeḥ, anyathā kadāpyabhavataḥ sādhvī bādhakayuktiḥ, sa eva ca deśavattāmupanayati, kvacidabhavataḥ kadācid bhāvayogāt | yatraiva cāsti sa eva deśaḥ, sa tu sthūlaḥ sūkṣmo veti kimanena ? kāle tu prayojanāntarāpekṣayā niyamasthāpanamiti ||
[428,2]
yathā niyatakālatā niyatadeśataivaṃ sphuṭā, pradeśaniyamastvasāvaṇutayādhimātreṇa vā | dvidhāpi tu na bādhakavyuparatiḥ sukhādāvato nirākṛtagirā kṛtaṃ kimu viśeṣaparākṛteḥ ||
[428,3]
tadevaṃ sattāmātrānubandhinī kālavatteva deśavattā na kvacid vyāpakānupalambhasaṃbhavaṃ bhayamanavakāśayituṃ śaknoti maivaṃ vā svayamapi sattāvyavahārasiddhiḥ kathaṃ sukhādau ?
[428,4]
ekānekavivekāsiddhiryadvadasya bhavato'pi na siddhiḥ | eketarayoranyatarasya svavido mita iva dhāma nirasya ||
[428,5]
yathā hi, nīlasyeva puro'vasthitākārasya sukhāderapratibhāsanāt ekānekarūpavyatirekaḥ pratipattumaśakyaḥ, tathā tata eva tayoranyatarasaṃbhavo'pi puraḥsphuratyevedamekamanekaṃ veti nirūpaṇopalabdheḥ | parokṣe'pi darśanānusāreṇa tathā vyavasthāyām apuraḥsphuratyapi rūpe puraḥsphuradrūpānusāreṇa deśapratiniyamāttigmabhaṅgajāgnikaṇikādivattayorabhāvo'pi vyavasthāpyatām |
[428,6]
satā avaśyamekadhā bhāvyamiti cet — na, vyāpakatvāt tayoranyatarasandehe sattvasyaiva sandehāt | svasaṃvedanasya tu śaktiṃ śvetādivadeva dūrīkuru, mā tatpratyāśayā sthāḥ | na ca pramāṇāntaramastīti parasya sandigdhāsiddhimudbhāvayato'pi na svayaṃ sadvyavahāraḥ | sādhakabādhakavaidhurye sandehasya nyāyaprāptatvāt | svasaṃvidite ca nīlādijñānasvarūparāśau bādhādarśanameva balavad bījamasya | tata eva tarhi bhavatu svasaṃvido'prāmāṇyam, bādhāyā abhāve tu prāmāṇyamiti cet — naivam, adarśanamātreṇābhāvasiddheḥ | bahiḥ samastamabhyastamabādhakasya ca sādhakasaṃbhavānnāparo dṛśyānupalambhaḥ | śāstra eva tu cintito'yamabādhavāda ityāstāṃ tāvat |
[429,1]
vedotpādyakathādīnāmapi caivaṃ pramāṇatā | utsargasiddhaṃ mānatvamityapi grastamagrimaiḥ || svato yatrāpi mānatvaṃ tadabhyāsaphalaṃ viduḥ | bahiḥ samastamabhyastamasadantastu cintyate ||
[429,2]
nanu grāhakākārabalādalīkasyāpi grāhyākārarāśeravabhāsa ityaśakyāpahnavaḥ sukhādiriti cet— na, svaprakāśasvabhāvatvād bhāgayorubhayorapi | kiṃ grāhyaṃ grāhi vā kiṃ syānna cānyenānyabhāsanam ||
iti bahirarthadūṣaṇe prāgeva nirūpaṇāt | na cābhimānamātrād vastusthitiriti | kiṃ cātra mate duḥkhādivannirākārajñānarūpatayā,
[429,3]
rāgadveṣamohamānādinikhilakleśagaṇaḥ sahajo yadi | iṣṭāniṣṭatayā ca vibhāgaḥ kaḥ sākāramate'ṅga virāgaḥ ||
[429,4]
alokākārayogo hi bhrāntirbhavatām | tadabhāvādavidyādayaḥ svabhāva eva bhavabhājāṃ bhaveyuḥ, ālambanadvāreṇālīkatve sukhāderapi prasaṅgāt | tato'niṣṭatayā hānamupādānamanyathā keṣāñciditi sākārapakṣa evākṣarāntareṇoktaḥ | ākāracakraikadeśadṛśyaspṛśyaparyavasānaṃ tu vaimatyamiti na kiñcidetat | yathā bhrāntitve'pyaniṣṭatayā kasyacit tyāgaḥ tathālīkatve'pīṣṭatayā ākāraviśeṣasya sthitirastviti sādhyakṣatiḥ | caittāścaite sukhādaya iṣyante, cittaṃ viṣayagrāhitayā ākārasvarūpaṃ heyam, caittaṃ cāvasthāyīti nāyaṃ saṃprayuktadharma ityāgamavirodhaḥ | abhede ca cittavadevālīkatvaṃ teṣāṃ tadvad vā cittasyāpi satyateti kathamanākārasya sādhyasya siddhiḥ ?
[429,5]
nanu yad yathā bhāvyate tat tathā sphuṭībhavatīti vyomākāramapi cittaṃ bhāvyamānaṃ tathā sphuṭībhaviṣyati, prasiddhākāravirahācca nirākāraṃ tadeveti kathaṃ sādhyasiddhiḥ ?
na, prayojanābhāvāt,
[430,1]
saṃsāradoṣairaspṛṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇavyañjanojjvalam | ātmabhāvaṃ vihāya tvaṃ vihāyastvaṃ yadīcchasi || nanu saṃbhogakāyo'yamiṣṭa evārhatāṃ sutaiḥ | dharmakāyasya lābhecchurbhajed vyomopamaṃ vapuḥ ||
[430,2]
iti cet ? tattarhi na tāvat sādhyaṃ, yathokta evecchāparisamāpteḥ | nāpi sādhanaṃ kasyacidarthasya, nirākārāt kvacidarthasiddherasiddheḥ | parārthasiddhirapi viśiṣṭākārapratibaddhaivetyuktaprāyam | idānīmākārādevārthasiddhiḥ paratastu nirākārāditi ka evaṃ pratyeṣyati syādvādādanyatra ? āgamādevamiti cet ? kva yuktibādhite'rthe śaraṇamāgamaḥ ? puṇyajñānasaṃvalitākāraviśeṣeṇa viśiṣyamāṇārthaśaktiḥ tatprakarṣaparyante svayamapi prakarṣaparyantavartinyeva syāt, kathaṃ tato vicchidyeta, anyato vā saṃbhavet ? kasya kadācit pratītirevāsaṃbhavinī, na cāgamo'pi mukhyākṣara īdṛgarthaḥ, vyākhyāntarāśrayastu yuktiprāgalbhye bhavet, sā ca kṣīṇeti cintitam | tathāpi bādhabhayāt bhaktavyameva tadvapuḥ, abādhatvācca tadevārthasamarthamityapi sidhyatu, tata eva ca prāgapi tadupāyinyevārthaśaktiriti cet ? na so'sti kaścit samayaprakāroyatra sthitaṃ nābhinihanti bādhaḥ |
tathā hi, yadvyomo'yamanalākāram, yadi tāvad khavad vyāpi tadvadevāsya dūṣaṇam | jyotsnātaḍinmaṇijvālāsphuliṅgāditulāsvapi ||
tadvadeveti saṃbandhaḥ | na svarūpeṇa yad dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭāntadvārato'thavā | bhāvyaṃ kathaṃ tadā rūpe tulā teṣveva kenacit ||
bhaviṣyati ? rūpavirāgiṇo hi samyaṅmārgaparicayādeva śuddhibuddhyā tajjñānam | na tadbhāvanādeva vyāpakānupalambhasaṃbhavabhayabhraṃśabhāgī | kiṃ bhūyaḥ ? sāṃśe'vayavivad doṣo niraṃśe paramāṇuvat | nāparaṃ vastu cāstīha sarvagrāsā hi śūnyatā ||
tasmād bādhābhayabhraṃśaśaṃsināpi tadbhāvyamaśakyaṃ ca | pravacanoktatvād bhāvyameveti cet ? tat kimidānīṃ pitṛkūpa iti kṣāravāripānam ? kiṃ vā dhātugatiyoniśrāvakādimārgo na taduktaḥ ? atra ca yasyāpi heyatayā nirdeśaḥ, tasyāpi nājñatayā heyatvam, api tu vineyasyābhilāṣādivaśāt | svargopadeśādeva hi bhagavān pramāṇam |
tasmāt tatropayogabuddherabhāvāt svayamadṛśyasya bādhātikramākāranidarśanasyābhāvācca kuto bhāvanāmayī siddhiriti saṃbhoga eva paryavasānaṃ vyāpārasya,
[431,1]
guṇāstadekaniyatāstadekaniyatā ruciḥ | tadekaniyataṃ mānaṃ bādhenaiva samaḥ paraḥ ||
[431,2]
para eva jino yeṣāṃ taiḥ svaśāstāpi hāritaḥ | śṛjukramagṛhīto ya āgamāllakṣaṇojjvalaḥ ||
[431,3]
śūnyatā saṃvido nānyad gāmbhīryaṃ sā ca tadgatā | sā tu kalpitadharmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ veti carcitam ||
[431,4]
āgame'pi svavācā na nirākārasya dharmiṇaḥ | śrūyate dharmakāyatvaṃ vyākhyānyāpi kṛtā na kim ||
[431,5]
iṣṭaṃ khadṛṣṭāntatayā niraṅgaṃ mano'tha śūnyaṃ nanu sarvathāstu | na sarvathā cedupamā niraṃśatyāgo'pi kiṃ na praṇayī priyasya ||
[431,6]
āgantukamalaprapañcavigamenaiva hi vihāyaḥsādṛśyamiti darśitaṃ prāk | ataeva mahāyānotaratantre nirdiṣṭenaiva sādharmyeṇa sarvatra vyomopamā, yathā vyapagatavikalpaṃ gaganavadityādi | tasmānnākāraviraheṇa | yattu, akiñcane nirābhāse nirālambe nirāśraye | cakṣuṣyatha vyatikrānte'pyarūpiṇyanidarśane || yathā nimnonnataṃ vyomni dṛśyate na ca tattathā | buddheṣvapi tathā sarvaṃ dṛśyate na ca tat tathā ||
iti | tatrākiñcanādiviśeṣaṇaṃ vyomna eva rajonīhārādādikṛtasya nimnonnatasya darśane'pyabhāvavibhāvanāyeti vyaktametat | saṃbuddhe'pītyanuktvā buddheṣviti sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ bādhakabahuvacananirdeśayatnāt | sugate tu bhagavati yathoktākāre evāpavādasamāropalakṣaṇasya nimnonnatasya darśane'pi na bhāva itīyadeva vivakṣitam | astu vā vacanapariṇāmena bhagavatyapi yojanam | yathā tvācāryavasubandhupādairdharmadharmitāpravibhāge nirvikalpajñānalakṣaṇaprastāve dvayena grāhyagrāhakabhāvena nirūpayitumaśakyatvādarūpi, saviṣayatvādanābhāsamiti vibhaktam, tatheha buddha iti prayukte'pyastu | akiñcanatvamapyāgantukarāgādivigamājjñeyam | śeṣamaviruddham | ataeva dharmadharmitāpravibhāge eva, asatkhyānātmato'khyānāditi bhrāntivyavasthitau | khyātiradhyavasāyārthā boddhavyeti nirākulam || kathaṃ paśyasi tasyaivaṃ vibhāti pratibhāsate | ityādivad vikalpe'pi khyātyuktirna virudhyate ||
madhyāntavibhāge ca suvyaktatvāt | yadi tu khyātirākārasyāsato'bhimatā bhavet | yauvarājakarājasya muneḥ saṃbhoga ityasat || tadādhipatyāt tatkhyātiḥ parasyetyuktavān na kim | nityavyāpitayorartha yathā vyaktaṃ vibhaktavān || tasmādadhyavasāyo'yamasataḥ khyātirīritā | śulkavyayabhayānnāto ratnarāśirapāsyatām || taduktidharmakāyasya tyāge'pyeṣa na kiṃ nayaḥ | nanu tasyāpavādena ko buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ || vastuno dharmirūpasya dharmaḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇaḥ | śūnyatākhyo mato dharmakāyaḥ kātaratāraṇaḥ || śūnyatātathatādharmadhātubhūtaśikhādibhiḥ | padaiḥ khyātaḥ svabhāvo'sau svābhāvika iti śrutaḥ || yogācāramate gītaḥ pariniṣpanna ityapi | dvayābhāvatayā sarvaśūnyatā madhyamādhvani || āśravasya parāvṛttiḥ saiva dhāturanāsravaḥ | tattvaṃ ca paramārtho'sau tadvodhād buddha ucyate || tanniścayaphale māne tadvalālambino guṇāḥ | na śakyo nihnavastasya vibhinnasyeva dharmiṇaḥ ||
avaśyaṃ hi prakāśamānametaccitraṃ śūnyatayā sākṣātkartavyam, tāvataiva bodhisiddhiriti kimapareṇa ? na ca svasaṃvedanādanyat sākṣātkāri | sā ca tathatā saṃkleśavyavadānāvasthāsādhāraṇaścittadharma iti svābhāvikaḥ sahajaḥ prakṛtiriti cābhidhīyamāno'pi vyavadānāpekṣayā dharmakāyavyavahāragocaraḥ | tatra kṣaṇikatā tāvadākāraviśeṣānapekṣāsau bhāvyamānā yo ya evākāraḥ sannidhīyate, taṃ tameva pratividhyatīti dharmitāniyatatallakṣaṇādiniṣpādakapuṇyasaṃbhārasahakārikāraṇopanītamantimaṃ tamevākāram āśrayīkaroti | tatra prāgavasthāyāṃ citrameva tatparatantramucyate | abhūtaparikalpo vikalpa iti coktaḥ | paryante tu citra eva vitathakalpanāyāmaprayojakatvānna tathocyate |
tadrūparahitastūcyate | hetupāratantryamātrasaṃbhave'pi cāsadvāsanāpāratantryābhāve paratantro'pi nābhidhīyate, kiṃ tu saṃbhoga iti, dharmasaṃbhogād daśabhūmibhiḥ saṃbhujyamānatvācca | tattvato vā hetuphalabhāvāt kva pāratantryamiti ? tasmād dharmarūpa eva dharmakāyaḥ | nanu, sarvākārāṃ viśuddhiṃ ye dharmāḥ prāptā nirāśravāḥ | svābhāviko muneḥ kāyasteṣāṃ prakṛtilakṣaṇaḥ ||
iti siddhāntaḥ, kathaṃ paroktākārasya śūnyatākhyo dharma ityucyate ? tadayuktam | na khalu śūnyatāto'nyā prakṛtirdharmāṇāmāgame śrutipathāvalambinī, sthitibhedena tu yathādhimukti veditavyā | tathāhi, nairātmyaṃ vidurīśvarādivirahānnityasya caivātmano 'vācyasyāpi ca ke'pi kecana jaḍaprākāśyayogasya ca | bāhyasyāṇutanorapi vyapagamādanye punaḥ svapnavatkecid rūpanirūpaṇāsahatayā tasyāḥ svavitterapi ||
tarkacintāyāśca krameṇa tadekapravaṇatvāt ||
[434,1]
pratyakṣādanumānād vā na hi bhāvaprasiddhayaḥ | tābhyāmeva tu bādhaiṣāmaidamparyamatastayoḥ ||
[434,2]
na ca lakṣaṇādimātrasyaiva dharma iti brūmaḥ | kiṃ tu yāvantaḥ svalakṣaṇadhāriṇaḥ cittaprakārāḥ śarīrabuddhisaṃkhyātarūpāsteṣāṃ sarveṣāmeva saṃbhogapoṣaṇaṃ tūpalakṣaṇaṃ tadapi parityāgena bodhibodhanārtham | abhisamayālaṅkāre ca, ye dharmāḥ sarvākārāṃ viśuddhiṃ prāptāsteṣāṃ prakṛtiḥ |
iti sāmānyena nirdeśāt na saṃbhogatyāgaḥ, sa tu pṛthakkāyatvena vyavasthāpyata iti |
sarvākārajñatārṇyantaparigaṇanāt pṛthageva parigaṇitaḥ | tasmād dharmadharmibhāvena bhittvā kāyadvayavyavastheyam | tadasya bhagavati tādātmyaṃ saṃbandho, nirmāṇasya tu tadutpattiḥ |
yadā tu sadātanaṃ tadrūpaṃ sakalaśukladharmākāratayā vivakṣitam, tadā tatrāpi tadutpattireva |
yathoktam, dharmakāyaprabhāvitā guṇāḥ iti | evaṃ ca sati yadyapi sādhanamapi tat, tathāpi na tanmātreṇa tatrādaraḥ, kiṃ tu tattvamityeva | sādhyasādhanayoranantabhāvo'pi kuta iti cet ? tattvasākṣātkārasyaiva sādhyatvāt, tadbhāvanāyā eva ca sādhanatvāt, tadabhāve'niścaye vā tayoreva lopāśakteḥ | tasya ca pratibhāsinaiva dharmiṇā caritārthatvānniścāyakapramāṇaparyeṣaṇaiva paramavaśiṣyata iti samāptaḥ puruṣārthaḥ | tacca sāmānyarūpameva bhāvyam, kṣaṇikatvādivaditi svabhāvāntaramavasthāpyate | tadadhigamādhīnaśca buddhadhvaniriti tadeva pradhānaṃ buddharūpam, sa eva vā buddha ucyate, pratāpa eva rājetyādivat | lakṣaṇādicitratā hi cakravartinītyuttaratantram | na caivamarthāntarasya kathañcit sattve'pi kaścidupayogaḥ | tato dharmakāyasaṃjñāpyasya yācitakamaṇḍanamiti na nirākāradarśanānurodhaḥ kaścit | ata eva dehabhogapratiṣṭhāviśeṣaśālini, akaniṣṭhe pure ramye śuddhāvāsopari sthite | budhyante tatra saṃbuddhā ārūpyeṇa kimanyathā ||
tasmāt, saṃbhogakāyasthita eva nāthaḥ svavittisākṣātkṛtadharmakāyaḥ | daśāntaratve hi tadeva sādhyaṃ bādhye tu bandhyo vividhaḥ prayāsaḥ ||
tathā ca sati, grāhyagrāhakavaidhuryād vijñānaṃ paramārthasat | ekānekaviyogena vijñānasyāpi śūnyatā || saṃvṛttyāpi na tadrūpaṃ traidhātukavivartinām | tāvataudāryamiṣṭaṃ ca dharmatātikramānna tu || yathā kṣaṇitvaṃ bhavatā soḍhaṃ taccedalīkatā | kiṃ na sahyā kṣaṇitvaṃ vā maraṇaṃ sahyate katham || maraṇānna bhayaṃ yasya tasyānyasmāt kuto bhavet | sarvākrośo hi maraṇaparyantatvena bhīṣaṇaḥ || mṛtād varaṃ durbalatā sadā cet saiva naḥ priyā | varamiṣṭasya na prāptiḥ prāptau vighaṭanaṃ na tu || tasmāt prakṛtireṣaiva nātikramitumiṣyate | tathāpi ko'pyatiśayaḥ prāptumiṣṭa iti sthitiḥ ||
kṣaṇikālīkayośca sādhāraṇīti na doṣaḥ kaścit | kṣaṇikatvavaddhetuparādhīnatādyapi draṣṭavyam | tadalamasthānakātaratayā | api ca,
[435,1]
nabhastalālīkakalaṅkahānayenabhastvamevāstu calatvaśāntaye |
[436,1]
na vastudharmasya yadi vyatikramaḥpramāṇato'līkamate'pyasau samaḥ ||
{11.4}
<caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[437,1]
athavā keyamalīkatāpyanubhavasvabhāvasya, bādhakāditi cet ? kasya kena bādhā ?
citrākārarāśervyāpakānupalambhena | tadetad vikrītagavīrakṣaṇam,
[437,2]
bādhyabādhakabhāvasya sāṃvṛtasyopapādanāt | bhāṣye tadvyāpyasatkhyātervirodhasya prasādhanāt ||
[437,3]
api ca, na tāvajjñānamātmānameva bādhate, svarūpasaṃvedanasyaiva balavattvāt |
pareṇāpi tadviṣayeṇa bhinnaviṣayeṇa vā bādhā syāt, samakālenāsamakālena vā ? tatra tadviṣayaṃ tacca bādhata iti asaṃbaddham | bhinnaviṣayeṇāpi tasya kīdṛśo bādhā ? svaviṣayopasthāpanamātrāccet ? tenaivāsya kiṃ na bādhā ? na ca samasamayena | ekakālamanekasya sajātīyasya vijātīyasya vā pratibhāse kasya kena bādhā ? kālabhede tu sutarāmanavakāśo mahāsaṃmataśroharṣayorapi prasaṅgāt |
[437,4]
athaikasya jñānasya jñānāntareṇa nirviṣayatvapratipādanaṃ bādhārthaḥ, sa ca bhinnakālayorna virudhyate | so'rthastatra jñāne yadi pratibhāsate, tadā sanneveti kuto bādhā ?
apratibhāse tu svayamevāsan kiṃ niṣedhāntareṇa ? na vā tadviṣayaṃ bādhanamuktaṃ bhavati |
āropitasya niṣedha iti cet ? āropo'pi vyavahāramātrasiddha iti pratipādanāt, tadāśrayā bādhāpi na sāṃvṛtamatikrāmati | atha yathaiva pratītyasamutpādabhedasamāśrayeṇa jñānāntaraprasavamātralakṣaṇo bhramaḥ, tathaivaivametannānyathetyapi jñānākārodaya eva bādhā bhaviṣyati |
[437,5]
yadyevaṃ tattvato na bādheti siddhametat | kenacidākāraparigraheṇa jñānamidaṃ jātaṃ nāma, na tu kiñcidanena bādhitaṃ sādhitaṃ vā, nīlajñānānantaraṃ madhurajñānavat | anyatra bādhādhyavasāyena viśeṣa iti cet ? adhyavasāyamātrasiddha ityeva sāṃvṛta ucyate |
tasmānnālambanaśūnyatāpratipādanaṃ bādhārthaḥ | kiṃ ca, sālambanetarabhedena dvaite gatiriyaṃ syādapi | advaite tu svarūpamātraparyavasitavedanasthitīnāṃ matīnāmanyo'nyaṃ bādha iti mahatsāhasam | uktaṃ ca, siddhirdhiyaḥ paradhiyo na yathā tathā na bādhāpi iti | nanu vijñaptimātratāsiddhirapi parata eva, tathā bādhāpi bhaviṣyatīti cet ?
asārametat | saṃvṛtivyavasthito hi nānumānamanāsthāya sthātuṃ śaktaḥ, anyathā na kvacit pravṛttinivṛttyādikamācaret | anumānāśraye ca balādvijñaptimātratāsiddhirāpatati | na tu tattvapariniṣṭhāyāmanumānāvakāśaḥ | tathā yadi saṃvṛtāveva bādhasvīkāraḥ, tadā punaḥ pratibhāsamānametat bahiravasitamiti bādhastatraiva syāt | yatkiñcidetat buddhirjaḍaṃ vā tatraiva bādhasiddhiḥ, tadāpi na bāhyarūpātikrameṇa sādhanavṛttiḥ | atha kimatra vikalpena buddhirūpameva citramālambya dharmīkaraṇamiti na bāhye sādhanavyāpāraḥ |
tadetadaśvārūḍhāśvavismaraṇavṛttāntamanuharati || vedanaṃ kiñciduddiśya yad bāhyaṃ bāhyameva tat | tacca jñānaṃ jaḍaṃ vā syāditi cintā nirarthikā ||
sarvathā bāhyagrāhyavyavasthānāntarīyako bādhaka iti siddham | nanvetadeva nīlādibādhāyā viṣayo mataḥ | tacca jñānaṃ jaḍaṃ vā syāditi cintā nirarthikā || na ca tatra dhiyo rūpamiti bhītiḥ prabādhituḥ | nāpi paścāt tathā jñāne śakterutkīlanaṃ bhavet || bāhyagrāhyavyavasthāyā vyapekṣāniyamo na ca | idaṃ hi bādhitaṃ nīlaṃ bahirastu mano'stu vā || astu vā tadvyavasthāpi tathāpyetasya bādhanam | vairabuddhyā na kiṃ bandhoḥ prahāro maraṇapradaḥ ||
iti cet ? punarapi brumaḥ na vijñaptimātratāsiddhau bādhakāvakāśa iti prakṛtam | tatra grāhyagrāhakavyavasthā nāntarīyake bādhake sidhyati nāniṣṭamāpāditaṃ bhavati, yathā hi tasyā viplavastathā bādhakasyeti sādhyasiddheḥ | na ca tannāntarīyakatāparihāraḥ śakyaḥ |
na cāviṣayīkṛtasya bādhaḥ, idamanena bādhyata iti bādhādhyavasāyāt | viṣayīkaraṇaṃ ca bādhyasya bādhakādanyena, bādhakenetareṇasvayaṃ svapareṇa veti vikalpāḥ | bādhakād anyena viṣayīkaraṇe tāvadabādhyameva | bādhakenāpi viṣayīkaraṇe kva bādhakāvakāśaḥ, viṣayīkaraṇasya svarūpanirbhāsa tvāt ? bādhyamānatvenaiva svarūpasya nirbhāsa iti cet ? vyāhatametat | svarūpanirbhāsa iti svarūpasattvaṃ, bādhyamānatā cāsattvam |
krameṇa dvayamapīti cet ? na tāvat prathamaṃ bādhā, saṃbandhino'pratīteḥ | atha svarūpanirbhāsastadā tāvataiva sattvākṛṣṭeḥ kva bādhā ? na khalu kālāntare bhavantyapi tasyāḥ syāt, tadā tasya svayamevābhāvāt | bhāve vā bādhakaśatenāpi na kiñcit | ubhayena tu viṣayīkaraṇe saṃvādasiddhireva kva bādhāgandhaḥ ? na ca tena vānyena vānyasya viṣayīkaraṇaṃ nāmopapattimat, vijñānasiddhau cintāyāḥ prārabdhatvāt | nāpi svayameva viṣayīkaraṇe bādhāvakāśinī,
[439,1]
svayaṃ nirbhāsamānasya pareṇa viṣayīkṛtau | bādhakenātmano mūrddhā bādhitavyo balīyasā ||
[439,2]
