tataśca nīlamidaṃ bādhitaṃ mayānayā yuktyeti svākāramātraparyavasāyivyāpāro vikalpastasya vārtāmapi na spṛśati bhede, abhede'pi temātmānameva bādhata iti sāhasam |
svaparavedane ca pūrvavat saṃvāda eva | aviṣayīkṛtasya tu bādhane'tiprasaṅgaḥ bāhyagrahādhimuktau tu tadasparśinyapi jñānodaye tatsiddhabādhavyavahāra iti syāt pratyāśā | sa cādhimokṣe viplava iti tatkṛtā bādhāpi viplava eva | bāhyagrahavyavasthāparibhave hi svasaṃvedanamagnamaśeṣamiti kasya kena kiṃ kriyā syāt ? na hi tadāpīdamevamiti śakyaṃ kartum | tathā sati punardvaitaprāpteḥ | yadāhuḥ, vijñānamātramevedamityapi hyupalambhataḥ | sthāpayannagrataḥ kiñcittanmātre nāvatiṣṭhate ||
iti | atha tattvaniścaye'pyasākṣātkaraṇāvasthasya pravṛttyādivad bādhakamapyavakāśeteti cet ? tathāpi na doṣaḥ | yathā hīdamato vedyaṃ prāpyaṃ veti sahajāvidyayā bahiradhikāreṇaiva pravṛttyādiḥ, tathā bādho'pi tanmūrdhanyeva nipatet | vinmātracintāyāṃ punaḥ sarvavyāpāroparamaḥ | tadayaṃ bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ sāṃvṛta eva, na tattvarūpāmukhīkaraṇakāle avakāśamāsādayati | tadā ca kāmaṃ sādhanasyāpi nāvatāraḥ, kevalamanavatāro'pyasya na bādhate, sādhyasya siddhatvāt |
[440,1]
tadasiddhāvitarasyānavatāraḥ paraparitoṣādanyatra kamarthaṃ puṣṇāti ? yadi tarhi tatsādhakapramāṇavṛttimapekṣya bādhakaprayogaḥ, tadaiṣa doṣaḥ | kaḥ punarevaṃ vilambiṣyate ?
prathamata eva bādhakaprayogo'stu | bhautācamanamātrametat | yadā hi vijñaptimātratāpratītau nāsyāvatāra iti siddham, tadā tadātmatāvirahamapekṣyaiva tatprayoga iti tannirūpaṇāpekṣāyāṃ prakāśatayaiva vijñānatāsiddhau vidhūto bādhakāvatāraḥ, bhavan vā yadi nedaṃ vijñānamitthanenākāreṇa bhavet | tasmād yāvad bādhastāvad bahirātmanyeva na vijñānarūpa iti siddham | kaḥ punarevaṃ sādhanadoṣa iti cet — na, vijñaptimātratāsiddhau anumānasyaivotthānābhāvāt kva sādhanadūṣaṇāvakāśaḥ ? tathā hi, bahirbodhe'numānādi mānaṃ na svaikasaṃvidi | svaikasaṃvitprasiddhau tu tadgrahādeva tadbhavaḥ ||
tathāpi yadi doṣoktyā santoṣaḥ,
[440,2]
asiddheḥ pararūpasya dharmihetusvarūpayoḥ | na siddhirnāpi ca vyāptiriti kiṃ vā na dūṣaṇam ||
[440,3]
kiṃ ca, ayaṃ vyāpakānupalambho'nyo vā bādhako vicārādināmā nānumānāt anyaḥ saṃbhāvanāviṣayaḥ | sarva hi vivādarūḍhasya vacanamāvirbhāvitasādhyasādhanadṛṣṭāntāditayā nānumānamanākṣipya prakṛtopayogi bhavitumarhati | ataeva saṃvṛtāvavaśyaṃ pramāṇasvīkāra ityadvaitabindau darśitamasmāmiḥ |
[440,4]
anyathā yathā tathānuvādamātreṇa kasya kīdṛgarthasiddhiḥ ? na cānumānamadhyakṣamadhikṣipya yathārthaṃ bhavitumarhati, saṃbandhagrahaṇādau paramparayāpi niyatopayogitayā tenaiva janyatvāt | tadapyatadapramāṇane pramāṇamiti janayiturakulīnatāyāṃ kulīnatāśaṃsanametat | svarūpe caitadākāravedanaṃ dūrīkṛtabhrāntikalpanatayā pratyakṣamiti kuto bādhāvasaraḥ ?
[440,5]
svavittirevāparamānayonirna cet pramāṇaṃ kimiha pramāṇam | atastayā sādhitabādhiteṣu na bādhasiddhyoraparasya śaktiḥ ||
[441,1]
atha vijñaptisādhanakāle kathaṃ svayonipratthakṣaparibhava iti cet — na, sādhyasiddhau svasyāpi paribhavāt | dahati drumamāśrayāśano nijaśākhāpugaghṛṣṭijo yathā | paravittirapītthamātmano yadi hantrī ka ihāparādhyatu ||
na khalu vijñaptisādhanaṃ paravedanamaparaṃ bādhamānamātmanaḥ prāmāṇyamāśaṃsati | paravedanasāmānyena tu tathotthāpito vicāraḥ, vahniryathā sarvasyaiva dāhaka iti naikasya kasyacit aparādhaḥ | vyāpakānupalambhastu prāyakṣaparibhavenaiva prāmāṇyamākāṃkṣatīti na nyāyaḥ |
vijñaptisādhanasya tu paravedanāntaraprāmāṇyāvadhikameva prāmāṇyam | yadā punararthakriyāśaktipratītivyavahṛtasattākastasyāvimarśenādarśanānna tathā vyavaharati, na tadā vyāpakānupalabdheraparādhaḥ, svayamabādhanāt, paratastu samānatvāt daṇḍasya | na hi svasaṃvedane śaktipratibhāsaḥ | yadā tu vyāpakānupalambha eva nāyakastadā pratyakṣāntarasyāpi na prāmāṇyamupahantuṃ śaktaḥ, prāgeva svasaṃvedanasya jātyaiva dūrīkṛtabhrāntivikalpaśaṅkākalaṅkasya | tasmānna saṃvedanarakṣitasya kṣatiḥ kutaścit |
[441,2]
nanu,
[441,3]
aprāmāṇye yathākṣasya nānumāyāḥ pramāṇatā | tathānumānāprāmāṇye nākṣasyetyapi śakyate || tadgṛhītāṅgato liṅgājjātānumitidūṣaṇe | tasyaiva doṣo'doṣe hi kiṃ kṛtaṃ tajjadūṣaṇam ||
[441,4]
tato yadyubhayasyāpi prāmāṇyam, tathāpi saṃvittiḥ sthitimātmanaḥ prathayatu svasmin bhramāsaṃbhavād ekānekatayātyayaḥ punarayaṃ krūraḥ kathaṃ vāryatām | tatsādhyasthitināntarīyakatayā tulyaprabhāvaśriyoradhyakṣānumayorayaṃ vyatikaraḥ ko vetti kasyorjitam ||
tadapi naupayikam | vyāpakānupalambhasya hi paravedanaikaniyatasya vyāptyādigrāhiṇā paravedanenaiva pratyakṣeṇa samakakṣatā bhavatu, yata ekaprāmāṇyasvīkāranāntarīyakamaparaprāmāṇyam | svasaṃvedanaṃ tu dvayorapyāśrayaḥ taddvayānāśrayaṃ ceti kastena saha tulārohaḥ ?
viṣayabhedācca parokṣaviṣayatvādanumānasya, pratyakṣe tadanavatārāt kva balābalacintāvakāśaḥ ?
ataeva pratyakṣādibhiranirākṛtaḥ pakṣa ākhyātaḥ |
[442,1]
nanu pratyakṣe'pi svabhāvāntaramavyavahṛtaṃ vyavahārayitumanumānamanumatameva |
na ca pratibhāsina eva kvacid vidhirniṣedho vā | pratibhāsamāne hi śṛṅgalāṅgulādisanniveśaviśeṣe gavādiśabdapravartanam, kvacit kevalabhūtalopalambhe kumbhādiniṣedhavyavahāraḥ | jñānagatacandradvayākāre cābahirinduyugalasya | na tu pratibhāsināmeva vidhiniṣedhau | tathehāpi niṣedhaprastāve pratibhāsino nīlādyākārasya yāvantaḥ kalpitā dharmā niṣidhyante, tāvanto niṣidhyantām | yathātmaparagrāhyagrāhakajñāpyajñāpakanityakṣaṇikaikānekatvādayo dravyaguṇatriguṇīmayatvādayo vā sparśādilakṣaṇarūpāntarasahacāraparamāṇurūpatārthakriyāśaktiparyantāḥ prapañcaśabdavācyāḥ, sarveṣāṃ kalpitamātratvāt | tasmāt prakāśamāne dharmiṇi dharmāntarasyāpratibhāsina eva niṣedho vidhirvā vyavahāramāśritya, śabdādivyavahāravirahe'pi tadyogye'pi tadyogyatāyāḥ parokṣarūpatvāt | na tu pratibhāsinaḥ kvacinniṣedhaḥ | yadāha nyāyaprasūtiḥ, tasmin bhāvānupādāne sādhye'syānupalambhanam | tathā heturna tasyaivābhāvaḥ śabdaprayogataḥ || (pra. vā. 3. 205–6)
iti | vyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ | (pra. vā. 4. 91)
iti ca | yadi tarhi pratibhāsino vidhiniṣedhau vyarthāsamarthau, apratibhāsino'pi sa eva niṣedha ityasamarthavyarthau, kva tarhi śabdavyāpāraḥ ? na kvacit tattvataḥ, pratītyasamutpādāśrayavyavahāramātrametat śabdena kiñcid vidhīyate niṣidhyate veti | yathā hi vṛkṣo'stīti saṃketavaśāt tadanurūpapravṛttyākṣepaparikalpotpādanameva śabdena vṛkṣasattāvidhiḥ, tathā vṛkṣo nāstīti tadarthivyāvṛttyākṣepakavikalpotpādanameva tanniṣedhaḥ, nañastyoraprayoge tu kevalaṃ vṛkṣaśabdasya pravṛttinivṛttyasamarthaśākhādimadākāravikalpotpādanameva vidhiniṣedhākaraṇaṃ nāma | tasya cāstipadasannidhau sa eva śākho sattayopacīyamāna iva pratibhātīti pūrvāpekṣayā ākāraviśeṣollekhamātram | nañyogepyapacoyamāna iveti vidhyanubhavāpekṣayā kṣīṇākārollekha eva | tatastadanurūpapravṛttyādiḥ |
[443,1]
evaṃ liṅge'pi vikalpavivartino vahnerdhūmajaladarśanādau, saṃvādaniyametarābhyāṃ tu viśeṣaḥ | tathā ca na sphurato buddhyākārasya kvacid vidhiniṣedhau | nāpi bāhyasyāsphurataḥ sato'sato vā tattvataḥ | tathāpi vikalpodayadvāreṇa tu bāhyasyaiva vidhiniṣedhavyavahāraḥ kevalaṃ kalpitasya, puraḥparisphurato nañśatairapi niṣedhābhāvāt | kalpanaṃ ca bahirmukhaparāmarśādanyat, tarumātravikalpe sadasattānirṇayāvadhānāvasthākṣepāt | ataevākāro bahīrūpatayāropitaḥ śabdavācyo'poha iti cocyate, śābde jñāne tasyaiva pratibhāsāt | adhyavasāyāttu vijātivyāvṛttaṃ bahiriti niveditaṃ prāk | tasmāt, nākārasya na bāhyasya tattvataḥ pratiṣedhanam | bahireva hi saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛttyāpi tu nākṛteḥ ||
tayā anarthitvāt, prakṛtyā ca bahirmukhatvāllokasya | yadā ca bāhye'pi parisphurati nāvakāśo niṣedhasya, kutaḥ svātmani ? tasmāt, na pramāṇapratikṣipte hetubhistrāṇasaṃbhavaḥ | svasaṃvittyā ca yat siddhaṃ tattvataḥ siddhameva tat ||
yadyapi sāṃvṛta eva sādhyasādhanabhāvaḥ tathāpi satsaṃvṛtisamāśraya eva kartavyaḥ | pratipuruṣaṃ hi bhinnabhinnasādhanādivyavasthitau sarva sarvasya sidhyet | na ca samayāntarasthāyino'pi bādhite hetubhistrāṇavārtā | svasaṃvedane yadi paraṃ pareṣāṃ vimatiḥ, tatra ca,
[443,2]
na svavittiṃ vinākṛtya pramāṇairjīvituṃ kṣamam | viśveneva pramāpāye śāstre nirṇītameva tat ||
[443,3]
tasmāt svasaṃvedanādhyakṣasiddhe vyāpakānupalambhādyanumānamanavakāśayantī pratijñāyāḥ pratthakṣabādhā | athavā kīdṛśī punaḥ sattā sādhanairebhirapākartumiṣyate ? tatra yadi tāvaddarśanāntaraprasiddhā sattā, sattāyogasvarūpasattvatrilakṣaṇādilakṣaṇā, svakalpitā vā kācit, tadā na vivādaḥ | atha lokaprasiddhā, sāpi śaktilakṣaṇā prakāśalakṣaṇā ca | tathā hi yuktopalambhamanupalabhamānā nāstītyāhuḥ |
[444,1]
tatra śaktilakṣaṇāyā bādhane siddhasādhanam | pratibhāsalakṣaṇāyā apyagṛhītaśakterbādhane sa eva nyāyaḥ | na vā tadā pratibhāso lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ tu śaktireveti na kṣatiḥ |
kalpitaśaktyādyupādhividhuraprakāśamātrasvarūpāttu rūpādiṣu sattā kathamapahnotuṃ śakyate, svasaṃvedanapratyakṣasiddhatvāditi pratyakṣabādhe ca pratijñāyāḥ ? evaṃ niḥsvabhāvā amī bhāvā iti rītibhede'pi svabhāvaśabdavācyo'rthaḥ prakāśādanyo yathoktaścet siddhasādhanam | pratibhāse cāśaktireveti veditavyam | ekānekavirahastvabhimata eva, sarvaprapañcapraśamasya vivakṣitatvāt |
svabhāvahānibhayāddhi tadaniṣṭaḥ syāt | sattvaṃ ca pratibhāsāt siddhamiti kimanena vyāhatam ? kathaṃ tarhi citrādvaitamiti cet ?
[444,2]
grāhyagrāhakahānito'dvayamidaṃ yad vā jaḍasyātyayād ekānekahateśca sākṛtitayā citraṃ tathāścaryataḥ | citrādvaitamiti smṛtaṃ tṛpativaccaikadhvaniḥ sāṃvṛto'nekatvaṃ ca na tattvato na ca phalaṃ tenāsti satsaṃvṛtā ||
[444,3]
ekānekavirahe'pi sattvamityāścaryārthaśca citraśabdaḥ | eko bhagavāniti saṃvṛtau vā, yathoktaṃ prāk | na caivamanekavyavahāreṇopayogaḥ | yathā hi sa bhagavānāśrayaṇīyo mayā, mayāpi ca tathaiva bhāvyamityekatvādhyavasāyinī pravṛttirupayogavatī, tathā nānekatvena kiñcit phalamākalayāmaḥ | pṛthagdharmiṇi kvacid vyāpṛterasiddheḥ | tataḥ tattvato dvayorapyanupapannattve ekatvaṃ phalāpekṣayā vyavahriyate nānyat, yathā anityatvaṃ praśamānukūlatvena | nanvetadapi nīlāntarālavalayaparyantaṃ sajātīyetarajñānacakraṃ citramekameva vyavahriyate bhavatāṃ, tat kathamucyate —
[444,4]
yāvadeva bahiradhyavasāyastāvadeva pṛthagetadidaṃ ca | tanmatistu sakaleti sa eva jñānapāṇicaraṇādirasau hi ||
[445,1]
na khalu manovivartān vihāya karādimātraṃ caitraḥ | tato vivartāntaravaccaitravācyatāyāmantarbhāvādekavyavahāraḥ kevalaṃ vijñaptimātratāparāmarśe | tatrāpi bhagavatīva gocarabhāgavyavasthāntaramuktaṃ smartavyam | tattvato vānekavyāvṛttimātrapara ekaśabdo'dvaitaśabdavat |
tasmāt prakāśatayā sanneva nīlādirekānekavidhuraśceti saṃgrahaḥ |
[445,2]
nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk | aśakyadarśanastaṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || (pra. vā. 2. 220)
[445,3]
atra citra ityekatāniṣedhaḥ | vijñāna ityekapratipattuḥ | pratibhāsamānatayā ekasaṃvidantargamādanekatāniṣedhaḥ | jñānopādhiriti jaḍād vyāvṛttyā jñānātmatayā bādhakābhāvaḥ | ākārāntaraṃ pītādimabhajan na śakyate draṣṭumityanena bhedavyavahāre prayojanābhāvamāha | yadi hi tataḥ pṛthagapyeko labhyaḥ syāt, tasmācca tatsādhyasiddhiścaitramaitrādivaducito'nekavyavahāraḥ | na caivaṃ, tata eka evocitaḥ | taṃ hītyādinā ca yāvadeva bahirityādikamarthamāha | buddhirūpatāparāmarśe hi buddhyādikalāpe vihitacaitrādyekaśabdaṃ tatrāpi tathaiva pravartayet | vivecayan bhindan punarartha eva patet, arthasyaiva janmagrahaṇaṃ vā pṛthak, na jñānasya | yataḥ,
[445,4]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānubhūyate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākāre'pi cetasi || (pra. vā. 2. 221)
[445,5]
nāma saṃjñāvācakaḥ śabda ityarthaḥ | sa evaikabhāvo na tāttvikaḥ | bhāsata iti jāyata ityarthaḥ, prakāśamānasyaiva janmetyabhiprāyāt | tadevamekānekasvabhāvavidhurameva jñānaṃ citrādvaitamapetabādhanam | saṃvṛtau caikavyavahāragocara eva kṣaṇikatvādivaditi darśitam |
nanu tathāpi tacca nāsti tadvyāptaṃ cāstīti kathaṃ saṃpratyayaviṣayaḥ ? na caivaṃ kvaciddhetāvāśvāsaḥ | ekaniṣedhena cānyavidhāne rāśyantarābhāvād bhāveṣu ubhayapakṣavadanubhayasyāpi kutaḥ saṃbhavaḥ ? ato lakṣaṇakaraṇakāla eva prakārābhyāṃ siddhā vyāptiḥ | parasya tu vastusvabhāvādubhayābhāvo na bādhaka ityasaṃbaddhametat |
[446,1]
satyamasaṃbaddhametat, taddvayīmantareṇāpi sattvasiddhervyāpterevāyogāt | kva caivam ? nanvihaiva buddhivapuṣi | tat kimidānīṃ pakṣībhūtenaiva vyabhicāraḥ ? ko vā doṣo yadi vyabhicāre pramāṇavṛttiḥ ? dharmyantare'pi hi tayaiva sādhāraṇānaikāntikaḥ kriyate | yadi cātra pakṣīkaraṇamātreṇa trāṇam, tatrāpi kaḥ pratirodhaḥ ? yadā ca vipakṣe sākṣādīkṣaṇe'pi na sādhyakṣatiḥ, tadā sandehamātramakiñcitkaramiti nānaikāntikatvaṃ tāvad doṣaḥ |
[446,2]
nāpyasiddhyādiḥ, yataḥ kutaścit hetoḥ siddheḥ, adhyakṣabādhanādarāt | evaṃ ca pramāṇavyastasādhyāddhetoranāśvāse'pi na kṣatiḥ | anyatra tu kaḥ śaṅkāvakāśaḥ ? tata eva lakṣaṇakāle'pi na vyāptisiddhiḥ | ekaniṣedhenānyavidhāne rāśyantaraniṣedho bāhya eva | na hi tatrāpi pratyakṣabādhopadarśanaṃ śakyam, idaṃ tadetadapekṣayā na bhinnaṃ nābhinnamiti vaktumaśakteḥ | svasaṃvedanaṃ ca nisargadurgameva, bāhyasya bhedābhedābhāve ca saṃvyavahāravilopaprasaṅgāt | yadāha, na hyanalaṃ paśyan ityādi | tasmād bāhya evāyaṃ nyāyo niyataśca, tadanurodhāttu yadi buddhirapi vyavasthāpyeta vyavasthāmātramastu | yathoktam, yathā bāhyaṃ grāhyam ityādi | na tu tadāpyāñjasaḥ | yattu, anyathaikasya bhāvasya (pra. vā. 2. 358)
ityādi buddhyadhikāre'pyuktam, tanmādhyamikaviśeṣābhiprāyāt yathā yathārthāścintyante (pra. vā. 2. 209)
ityasya sphuṭīkaraṇārtham | yathā tarhi naikaṃ nānekaṃ, tathā na prakāśaṃ nāprakāśamityapi syāt — na, prakāśaniṣedhasya prakāśenaiva bādhitatvāt | naivamekānekatvayoḥ śakyam | parasya tvityādinā ca nopanyastenopayogaḥ |
[447,1]
ekānekatvayorhāniravastutvena rakṣitā | avastutvaṃ svavittyā tu ko rakṣedbhakṣyamāṇakam ||
[447,2]
tasmānnaikānekavivecakasya buddhāvadhikāro'sattvasādhanāya, viṣayaviśeṣāpekṣatvād vyāptisiddherityanaikāntikatvam | yadi ca sāmānyenaiva vyāptisiddhyadhyavasāyastatrabhavatām, vyāpyasya sattvasya siddhatvādekānekatvayorevaikeneva bhavitavyam, na cānekatvaṃ kṣamamityekamevāstu | anekatve hyāparamāṇudalanātparamāṇupratibhāsena bhavitavyam |
na caivam, tasmād, yad yathā bhāsate jñānam anaṇurūpatayānekavyāvṛttyetyarthaḥ | tat tathaivānubhūyate |
prāptyarthattvādanugamyate upagamyata iti yāvat |
[447,3]
iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākāre'pi cetasi || (pra. vā. 2. 221)
[447,4]
nāmeti avyayamupagame | etacca na jaḍasya saṃvitterevābhāvāditi jñānamityanena darśitam | yadā tu jñānaparamāṇorapi digbhāgabhedādanupapattireva, na cānaṃśaiḥ sāṃśarāśerārambha ityanābhāsa eva syāt nānātvapakṣe, ato'yamābhāsa ekatva eva viśrāmyatīti | yad yathā yataḥ prakārādabhedalakṣaṇāt bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānubhūyate abhedenaivāsti, anubhavaḥ satteti nyāyāt | iti nāmetyādi sugamam | nāma saṃbhāvanāyām | etena tadabhyupagamāyātamasiddhatvam ||
[447,5]
nanu citramekamityanubhavaviruddhametat, nīlapītādīnāṃ bhedenaiva bhāsanāt | kiṃ ca, citraṃ nānekamityanarthāntaram, taccaikaparyudāsena sthitamiti tatkathaṃ citramekam ? anyathā prakāśo jaḍaḥ syāditi cet — na, nīlāditve hi saṃvedanavyāpāro, na bhede | bhedābhedāvyavasthā tu nibandhanānusāramarhati | nanvidaṃ nīlamidaṃ pītamiti parasparātmatayaiva pratītirbhedapratītiriti cet ? bāhyārthavāde evametat | abhyāsavāsanāvaśāt tu buddhāvapyāropyate | buddhau tvetāni rūpāṇi bhinnānyabhinnāni veti cintāmarhati | buddhāvapi tadanusāreṇaiva vyavastheti cet ? na khalu sarvā | tathā hi,
[448,1]
sthiretaratve niyataṃ pareṇa prakāśyamarthakriyayā bahiḥsat | ākārabhedānnitarāṃ vijātirnābhyāsavaśyaṃ viparītamantaḥ ||
[448,2]
antariti cittaṃ tadviparītam | kathaṃ punaḥ sthiretaratve niyataṃ na buddhirūpam, tattvataḥ pūrvāparāpratīteḥ ?
[448,3]
pūrvāparatvavittau hi nityatvaṃ calatāthavā | ekānekādhimokṣeṇa tadabhāvādasad dvayam ||
[448,4]
tatra bhede vyativitteḥ sthūlābhāsasya cābhāvaprasaṅgo'nābhāsaprasaṅgaśca durnivāraḥ |
athaikatve'pi nīlaṃ pītameva syāt | taduktam, abhede'pyekatā citratvavirodhinī syāditi |
na caivaṃ bhāsate | tathāpi, yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivopagamyate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākārasya cetasaḥ || (pra. vā. 2. 221)
nāmetyaṅgīkāre | ayamarthaḥ, satyamanekavadekabhāvo na syāt, prakāśamānasya tu sattāpahnavo mā bhūditi nāniṣṭaṃ kiñcit | ayamabhiprāyaḥ,
[448,5]
satyaṃ cet saṃvidaḥ siddhamanekatvaṃ ca bādhitam | ekatve ca tavaivecchākṣatirnobhayathāpi naḥ ||
[448,6]
sattāsiddhau cānekatvenāpi nāparāddhamasmākaṃ kiñcit | kevalaṃ nyāyānusāriṇa ekatvamanuśiṣmaḥ | tathā hi,
[448,7]
samānayogakṣemattvāt sattāyāṃ naikatākṣatiḥ | tadvirodhi tvanekatvamatastasyāṃ tadatyayaḥ ||
[449,1]
yat tūcyate, ekatve nīlaṃ pītameva syāditi | sa bāhya eva doṣaḥ, tadarthakriyārthināṃ tatrāpi pravṛtteḥ kriyāyāśca prasaṅgāt | kriyārthitāvyatireke'pi yannīlaṃ tat kiṃ pītaṃ bhavitumarhatīti cet ? tat kiṃ svarūpasattayā viyujyatām ? varamevamiti cet ? yadi parokṣatā syāt syādapyevam | tasmād bāhyatve nānātvameva nīlapītayormā bhūt pravṛttisaṃkarādiriti | jñānatve tvekatvameva | bahirvyavahārābhyāsāt tu mahataḥ saṃmukhamadhyandināditya iva duḥsahapakṣa eva iti kimatra kurmaḥ ? tadiha pratyakṣavirodhādayo'pi plavanta eva | pītādanyat nīlamiti vikalpasya svabedanavyāpāramanādṛtya vṛtteḥ, indriyajñānavyāpārānusārasyekasya svarasavāhitvāt | ataeva ca citramekamiti na virodhaḥ | nīlapītāditayā hi citraṃ, na tu nānātvena | kevalaṃ nānātvena vyāptyabhimānāt tathocyate | vyāptiśca bāhya eva | athavānuvādamātraṃ citramiti, yannāneti bhavatāṃ saṃmatam, tad buddhirūpaṃ sadekameveti nāśvārūḍhavaddoṣaḥ |
[449,2]
nanu viruddhadharmādhyāso bheda ucyate, sa ca bāhyasya buddherveti nātra niyama iti cet ? niyama eva | bāhyābhede hi nārthakriyāpratiniyama eva, tadanādare ca pratibhāsamātrāt na viśeṣa iti tadabhāva eva syāt | buddhestu bhede eva svarūpahāniḥ, arthakriyānapekṣāyāstasyāḥ prakāśādeva sattvāt | bhede ca prakāśābhāvaprasaktistadavasthāyāḥ | yadyapi ca bhedena nirbandhe dvayorapi svabhāvahāniḥ, tathāpi tāvaddūramanītvā yathāṇusaṃghātasaṃkhyātaṃ bāhyaṃ bhede'pi sattvaṃ sahate, aṇvākārollekhābhāve'pi caikaghanasthūlākāreṇa jñānena saṃvādaleśād grahaṇasthitiṃ ca, na tathā jñānamityucyate | na vā bāhyasya hānirapi pīḍayati, abhimānamātravyavasthāpitatvāt | abhimānādeva vā nirvahed bahiḥ |
adhyakṣasiddhāyāstu buddheḥ kuta eva tad dvayamapi bahīrūpaparāmarśaprāpteśca bhede niyataḥ svabhāvabhraṃśaḥ | yadāha,
[449,3]
taṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayanniti | (pra. vā. 2. 220) yathārthaśaktivirahe bhāsaḥ keśādisannibhaḥ | tathānyo'smādayamiti bāhya eva vivecanam ||
[449,4]
naiṣa svasaṃvedanānusāraḥ, kiṃ tu bāhyābhyāsavāsanāvilāsa eva | tasmād yathā aparādhīnavedanatvādibhirdharmairbahirasādhāraṇaṃ dhiyaḥ svarūpam, tathā viruddhadharmādhyāsakṛtabhedavyavasthāparibhavenāpi nyāyasāmarthyāditi yuktam | yadi tarhi bahireva viruddhadharmetarakṛto bhedā'bhedo vānubhavākāre kā gatiḥ ? iṣṭaśca tatrāpyeko bhagavāniti vyavasthā, niyamanibandhanābhāve hi santānāntareṇāpyabhedaprasaṅgaḥ ityāha, nīlādiścitravijñāne (pra. vā. 2. 220)
ityādi |
[450,1]
buddherekabhāvo nāma syādaśakyavivecanātmā nānekatvam | yad vā buddhernāma syānna jaḍasya | pratiyogyakṣamāyāṃ nāmaśabdo'vadhāraṇaparaḥ | yacca yathā bhāsate citramapyekasaṃvidantargatam, tattathaivānubhūyate ityekatvamekasantānaprajñaptigocarasya nāma cetasaḥ syāt, natvetādṛśamaśakyavivecanatvaṃ parābhimatasyeti na doṣaḥ | tadevaṃ svatantre ca vyāpakānupalabdherasiddhiḥ, buddhyākārāṇāmekatāyā evopapatteriti | api ca, kimidamekatvamanekatvaṃ vā kva vā, vastutvavyāptiranayoḥ ?
[450,2]
atrottaram, niraṃśamekamanekaṃ ca samuccitaṃ tadeva | loke caikānekatayaiva vastusthitirāsthīyate | atha parārthānumāne svadṛṣṭamupayogīti ucyate, vicārāśraye saṃvṛtau svayameva tathopalabdhamiti na doṣaḥ ? atrocyate, saṃvṛtāvapi tadeva dṛṣṭamabhidhīyate yatsiddhamadhyakṣānumānābhyāṃ, na cābhyāṃ kvacidupalambhagocaro niraṃśaḥ | tatastatsamuccayarūpamanekamapi nopalabdham, tatkathamābhyāṃ vastuvyāptisiddhiḥ ? nāpi kiñcidasti vastu, paropagamastu na svatantrahetāvadhikriyate | prasaṅgasādhanatve ca viparyayaparyavasānāt sādhyavirodhaḥ | yasya caikānekatvābhyāṃ vastuvyāptirabhimatā tasyāyamastu daṇḍaḥ | yasya tu prakāśamātreṇa vastutā tasya kastadanurodhaḥ ?
[450,3]
tasmāt svayamupapādayitavyā vyāptiḥ | yadi ca kvacit saṃbandhabodha ekānekatvābhyāṃ vastunaḥ, tadeva na śūnyamiti vyāptiśūnyatā sādhanoddhūtiḥ | nanu vastusthitiḥ ekānekavyavahāraḥ pramāṇasiddhyavasāyaśca loke tāvadasti | vicāre tu nāstītyetadeva sādhyamasmākaṃ kathaṃ bādhakaṃ bhavitumarhatīti cet — na, svabhāvābhāvo hi bhavatāṃ sādhyaḥ, naikānekatvābhāva eva sādhanatvenopanyāsāt | na cedamasiddhatodbhāvanam | kiṃ tu vyāptyasiddhirabhidhīyate | viparyayavyāptiśca vyāpakānupalambhādau śaraṇam, sā ca kvacid vyāpyavyāpakayorasiddherasiddhaiva, sāṃvṛtenāpi pramāṇenāviṣayīkaraṇāt | na ca vyavahāramātraṃ pramāṇam, na ca lakṣaṇāntaram | apramāṇe'pi pramāṇasya na vyavasthāniyamaḥ | saṃvṛtau mānamiṣṭaṃ ced vicāro'pyeṣa saṃvṛtiḥ | saṃvṛtāvapi neṣṭaṃ ced bruvan jetā yathā tathā ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[451,1]
tato yadi pramāṇanirastenaiva rūpeṇa vyāptimavakalpya sarvatra tadabhāvādabhāvo bhāvānāmabhimataḥ, abandhyastarhi bandhyāsutaviyogo'pi tatsādhane syāditi sādhvī sādhyapratyāśā | tasmāt kvacid vyāpyavyāpakayorupalambhe vyāptigrahaṇanibandhane'dhyakṣarūpe viparyayabādhakasamākhyātānumānarūpe vā pravṛtte kvacit tadabhāvāt anyābhāvaniścaya iti yuktam | kṣaṇikatvenāpi sattvasya vyāptisādhanaṃ kṣaṇikasattāniścayanāntarīyakameveti saivopalabdhirasya | prakṛte tu tadvat tayoḥ sāmānyenāpi sattākṣepe tannāntarīyako heturiṣṭavighātakṛd viruddhaḥ | anākṣepe'pi na vyāptiriti anekāntaḥ |
[451,2]
tataḥ kutaścitrākārabodhaniṣedhaḥ ? bāhyasyāpi kutastarhīti cet ? tattvato'prakāśādeva | na hyanupalabdheranyo'bhāva iti suprasiddham | na vā niraṃśataikalakṣaṇamiti kaḥ śaktipratibandho bahirarthe vyāpakānupalambhasya ? kiṃ punastadekatālakṣaṇam, yato noktopālambhasaṃbhavaḥ ? vivecyāśakyadarśanatvaṃ, tattu na bāhyasya | tadabhāvāt tatsaṃhatirūpamanekamapi nāsti | atha śakyavivecanamanekaṃ bhaviṣyatīti cet ? yadyaśakyavivecanaṃ kiñcidantimaṃ syāt, tadā tadapekṣayā śakyavivecanatā parasparaṃ syāt, na caivam, paramāṇorapyanavasthānāt | buddhau tu svasantānabhāvinyāṃ citrāyāmaśakyavivecanatvamasti, na tu santānāntareṇa saheti darśayati | etena buddhau vyāpyavyāpakabhāvasiddhiranyatra vyāpakānupalambhavyāpāra iti vyaktamuktam |
[451,3]
ata evācāryavasubandhupādairapi bāhyādhikāreṇaiva vyāpakānupalambha udbhāvito, na jñānādhikāreṇa | samānanyāyatayā tatrāpyavakāśamāno durvāra iti cet— na, vijñānamātramevedamityādinā samānanyāyatayā niṣiddhatvāt | ataeva grāhyagrāhakadvayāsattayā traidhātukacittacaittalakṣaṇābhūtaparikalpasattayā ca samāropāpavādapratiṣedhanirvṛtiḥ kṛtā, netarasattvāsattvamuktam | tadvadūhituṃ śakyatvādanuktiriti cet ? grāhyasya tarhi sākṣādeva bādhakamuktamiti tadabhāva eva nābhidheyaḥ | tasmāt tasyaiva bādhakamuktam itīṣṭaṃ cetyalaṃ vistareṇa | tathā vivecyāśakyadarśanetaratvamevaikānekatvamanyonyaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayā vyāpakaṃ svabhāve dṛṣṭatvāt, na niraṃśarāśitvaṃ, aṃśacintā tu parānurodhena | athavā taddvāreṇāśakyavivecanatvābhāva eva vyajyata iti veditavyam, santānāntaravaditi | nanu svavidekatattvavādino'nekavyavasthāśrayaḥ, santānāntarabhāvo'yaṃ na siddhaścet phalāṅgavat | santānāntarasiddhiḥ kiṃ saṃvṛttyā tu yathā tathā ||
vā astu kimatra nirbandhena ? evamapi hi buddheranekatvameva mā bhūt, ekatvenāpyekena vyāpakānupalabdherasiddhisiddheḥ | kalpitānekavivekena caikaśabdo bhaviṣyati yāvad vyavahāraḥ | tasmānna bahiriva buddherviruddhadharmādhyāsakṛto bhedaḥ |
[452,1]
astu caivaṃ, kiṃ punastatra pramāṇam ? ekatve'pi kiṃ pramāṇam ?
pratyakṣameva | vikalpenānanugamānneti cet ? vikalpasyaivāyamaparādhaḥ | adhyakṣasyaiva kiṃ neti cet — na, anyonyasaṃvidantargatapratibhāsādeva | kiṃ ca mayā dṛṣṭā nīlapītādaya ityekakarturullekhaḥ | mamāyaṃ citraḥ pratibhāsa ityekasaṃbandhinaśca | ekapratyakṣavikalpa evāyamabhedena paṭavatyanubhavākāravān | evamekataiva buddhirekastasya vikalpastribhuvanavikalpo vā ? ekasyāṃ buddhau citraḥ pratibhāsa ityapi śilāputraśarīravat, śarīre pāṇipādādivad vā | ekāvasāya evāyaṃ, bahirabhimānāt tu samuccayamātramucyate |
tadabhāve tvekatvamevedamullikhyate | evaṃ vṛkṣakṣmādharādāvapi dhīmātratve tūbhayatra ekavyavahāraḥ |
[452,2]
tasmānna pratyākṣāparādhaḥ | nāpi vikalpasya bhāva eveti siddhamadhyakṣamabhedagrāhi |
bhede'pi tarhi pratyakṣameva śaraṇam | na caikā parvatabuddhirityādau viparītodayādvikalpena ananugamo, bhūyodṛṣṭatvāt | tat kimidānīmubhayamastu ? ato vyāpakānupalabdherviplavaḥ |
so'yamubhayaniṣedhena śūnyatāsādhanārambhe ubhayasādhanena syādvādamuddīpayituṃ pravṛttaḥ iti prahārapātaḥ | athaikaikasādhanamanyānyabādhanaparaṃ, na tu sthitireva tasya vivakṣitā, paryāyeṇa tasyāpi bādhanāt | yadyevaṃ yadaikyaṃ siddhamadhyakṣeṇa tadā dvitīyabādhaiva jātā, kathaṃ tadāśrayaḥ parasya bādhaḥ ? na hi pūrvabādhitasya kutaścit pratyujjīvanam | tathābhāve anenāpi bādhyamānasya punaḥ pratyujjīvanāśaṃsāyāṃ kīdṛśī manorathasiddhiḥ ? punaritareṇa bādhanajīvanaparamparāyā anuparamādekaikasanāthatayā dharmiṇo na kadācid vyāpakānupalambhasaṃbhavaḥ |
[453,1]
tadayamarthaḥ, yaducyate na tāvadekaṃ buddhirūpaṃ, nīlapītādīnāmavyatikarapratibhāsanāt |
nāpyanekaṃ, paramparāsaṃvedanaprasaṅgāditi | tatra yadekatvaniṣedhāya pratibhāsabhedo dūṣaṇīyate, tadā yadyasau svasaṃvedanasiddhaḥ, tasya kena punarapohaḥ ? tasyādṛḍhatve ekatvasyāpi kuto bādhā ? evaṃ nāpyanekamityatrāpi vācyam | yadi punaḥ pratiyogisaṃbhavānapekṣaḥ paraparibhavaḥ sādhanāntarakṛtaḥ syāt, tadā na doṣaḥ | svayameva tu pramāṇasiddhasaṃmatasya punaḥ prativahanamityasaṃbaddham | na ca pramāṇāntaramekānekatvaviparyāsanamasti | tatsaṃbhavābhimāne'pi naikasyāpi svasaṃvedanasiddhasyoddhūtiḥ | avastutvānnaikamapīti parasparāpekṣam | viruddhayorekatrāsaṃbhava iti na dvayorniṣedhaḥ | tadatra yasyaiva na saṃvedanamityupapādayituṃ śakyaṃ tadevāsadastu |
dvayorapi na saṃvedanamiti tu sarvathā saṃvedanābhāve syāt | taccāsiddhamiti |
athāpi syāt svasaṃvedanavādino'niṣṭāpādanamātrametat, tatastasyaivāyaṃ doṣo nāsmākaṃ tadaniṣṭe ceti cet ?
[453,2]
aniṣṭirnāma mahatāṃ parihāro mahānayam | sarvānarthānuṣaṅgeṣu yadyevaṃ syāt kṛtārthatā ||
[453,3]
vyāpakābhyupagamavādino hi prasahyāyātaḥ svasaṃvedanābhyupagama ityuktam | tato yadyabhedavadadhyakṣasiddhirbhede'pi na śakyaḥ syādvādaparihāraḥ | pramāṇānupagame ca sarvasya yatheṣṭasiddhāvapi kastatparihāraḥ ? evaṃ tarhi,
[453,4]
bhedābhedadvayīsiddhau syādvādaḥ samupāgataḥ | vedāntavādastvekatve dustyajastattvaviplavaḥ ||
[453,5]
atrocyate,
[453,6]
maccittacakraṃ yadapīdamekamātmā nabhasvanna vibhustathāpi | tathāgatasya prathate tathā cen manaḥsamādhyātiśayo na tattvam ||
[453,7]
na khalu jñānasya tādṛgvyāpakatvaṃ nāma tattvameva, anyadā anyasya cābhāvāt |
bhagavatastu siddhiviśeṣo'sau | pūrvāpararūpasaṃsparśastu saṃvedanenāstīti kuto nityatā ?
etena hrasvatāntaparihāraḥ | na ca svasaṃvedanameva kadācidātmānaṃ viramantamanubhavatīti ucchedāntasya prabandhadvāreṇa tu śāśvatocchedaparihāro'vāntaravyavasthāpekṣa iṣṭa eva |
atītādināpyabhedo bhāṣyakārasyeti sthavīyasī bhrāntirlokasya, prakāśamānasyaivātītādibhāvanāniṣedhāt | tasmānna tāvanmātramekatvaṃ gaganavad vaibhavadoṣākarṣi | nāpi nityatāpratītiriti kathaṃ vedāntasiddhāntaśaṅkā ?
[454,1]
atha tāvaddeśavyāpīdamidaṃ cānyathetyapi pratyayaḥ katham ? yadyevaṃ kālavad deśasyāpi na dairdhyapratītiriti natarāṃ nityavibhutve | ubhayasiddhivādastvahrīkasyaiva |
nanu digambarasya bāhyamapyasti | tatrāpi kathañcid bhedābhedau, bhāvānāṃ ca naikāntena bāhyatvamāntaratvaṃ vetyādyavakaraparihāre'pi pratyakṣasiddhabuddhirūpaikānekatvamātreṇa kaḥ tanmatopanipātaḥ ? na khalu sarvathā sāmyaparihāraḥ śakyaḥ, parasparavirodhastu dhvasto buddhyadhikāreṇa pratibhāsādeva | tasmāt,
[454,2]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānubhūyate | bhāsate dvyātmakatvena tathaivāsya sadā sthitiḥ ||
[454,3]
jñānagrahaṇenaitadāha | na bahirdvyātmakaikatvena kvacit pratibhāso bhramasyāpi saṃbhavāt, pramāṇāntarāvatāradarśanāccandradvayādivat | tat kathamekatvaṃ citrākārasya ?
ucyate, nāhrīkavādamuktirvaḥ prakṛtārthavimarśane | asmābhiryadanuṣṭheyaṃ bhavadbhistadanuṣṭhitam || ekānekatvayorekasyāpi siddhau yadepsitam | kā kathā dvayasaṃsiddhāvekaṃ syādapi durbalam ||
citraikatācodye'pyuttaram,
[454,4]
ekānekatvayoḥ siddhāvekatvaṃ siddhameva tat | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākāre'pi cetasi ||
[454,5]
citrākāre ekānekākāre rūpe ityayamapyarthaḥ | cetasi nāma syānnajāte jaḍe ekabhāvo'pi, na tvekabhāva eva | na hi nīlaṃ caturasraṃ na nīlamiti yuktam |
athavā,
[455,1]
naikaṃ citraṃ virodhena virodhaśca na darśanāt | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākārasya cetasaḥ ||
[455,2]
anekavyavahāro'pi tarhi syāt | yadi prayojanamasti ko nivārayati ? yathā hyeko bhagavānucyate, tathā catvāri vaiśāradyāni, dvātriṃllakṣaṇānītyādi dṛśyate eveti kā kṣatirasmākam ? bhavatastu svavadhāya kṛtyotthāpanametat | nanvevaṃ parahetudūṣaṇamastu, svābhimatacitrādvaitasiddhistu katham, pratyakṣapratikṣiptatvādekatāyāḥ, nīlapītayoḥ pratibhāsaṅkarāt ? yadapyaśakyavivecanatvamuktaṃ tadapi samānasāmagrījanyatvenāvyabhicāranimittaṃ bhedahetuḥ, buddhirūpatvāttu samudāya ekadeśo vā na gocaraḥ parasyeti kimekatvamastu ?
[455,3]
aupacārikamekatvaṃ vivekāśaktito yadi | vyāpakānupalambhasyāsiddhiḥ satyaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
[455,4]
yaccedamucyate, ekatvanāntarīyakaḥ pratibhāsa iti, tadapyayuktam,
[455,5]
deśavyāptyā hi nirbhāso na caikasya bhavedayam | tadbhedanāntarīyatvamapyābhāsasya kiṃ na vaḥ || abhedanāntarīyatvaṃ yathābhāsasya dṛśyate | nīlapītāditantratvamevaṃ bhedaḥ sa eva ca ||
[455,6]
tasmāt,
[455,7]
vyāḍibrīḍākaraṃ kṣāradadhnorekatvaśāsanam | tadeva kiṃ na bhavato guḍagorasakāriṇaḥ ||
[455,8]
atrocyate,
[455,9]
iyatā yadi bhedo'pi kathyate'stīti kā kṣatiḥ | ayogasya vyavacchedenaitaduktamanantaram ||
[455,10]
tathaiva citrādvaitaṃ ca mukhyamityapi darśitam | anyathā hyekameva syāccitratvaṃ nopapattimat ||
[456,1]
parasparavirodhena rūpasaṃkarabhīrave | avaśyaṃ kathyamekatvaṃ nirbhāsāttyajyatāṃ bhidā ||
[456,2]
nirbhāse sati bhinnatvamabhedo vā tadākṛteḥ | nānekatve ca nirbhāsastasmādekatvameva sat ||
[456,3]
deśavyāptiranekasya jaḍasyaivopapadyate | svasaṃvedyasya tu kathamekaikapratibhāsane ||
[456,4]
nīlapītāditantratvaṃ tathāstu na tadeva bhit | ekasya svīkṛtasyaiva tathotpatteḥ svahetutaḥ ||
[456,5]
ekatāsvīkṛtaṃ yadvanna bhedasvīkṛtaṃ tathā | dvitīyasyāpratībhāsādabhidaiva vaśīkṛtam ||
[456,6]
mitho virodhapakṣe ca na dvitīyāvalambanam | virodhānabhyupāye'pi citrādvaitaṃ prasādhitam ||
[456,7]
tannāśakyavivekatvaṃ dhiyāmadvaitasādhanam | ekasaṃvittisiddhe'smiṃstadevaikatvamucyate ||
[456,8]
tatreti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāditi ko'rthaḥ ? etadaśakyavivecanatvamekatvamityarthaḥ | tadevamekabhāvo hyasyānyathaivānyathā dhiyaḥ | idaṃ vastubalāyatamaruciḥ kvopayoginī || bāhye sati dhiyo grāhyamiva bhinnaṃ śiteḥ sitam | tadaikyavādī nigrāhyo bāhyaiṣī bāhyaviplavāt ||
etenābhedena pratyakṣapratikṣepaḥ prayuktaḥ ||
[456,9]
kiṃ ca,
[456,10]
adhyakṣameva hi bhinatti śiteḥ sitaṃ cet tadbhidyamānamathavābhidameva bhindyāt | bhede'nyaleśamapi neti kuto bhinattu bhindyādabhedi mana ityapi kasya śakyam ||
[457,1]
bahirapi hi bhidyamānaiva buddhirarthān bhinatti | na cātra buddhisvarūpe pramāṇāntarāṇāmavakāśaḥ svasaṃvedanādanyatra | taccaikaṃ bhinatti ceti vyāhatam | bahistu nirākārapakṣe'bhidyamānāpi buddhirarthakriyādibhedena dṛḍhīkṛtād bhinnasvarūpagrahaṇābhimānāt arthān bhindyāt | saṃvedanaṃ tu svadharma eva svabhāvātmā nīlapītayorna bhidyate |
bhinatti caitāviti mahat sāhasam | pratyātmaṃ bhidyamānaṃ tu bhindyāt | kevalamanyānyavārtāvirahāt citrapratibhāsa evāsaṃbhavī tadeti kuto bhedasthitiḥ ? athavā kutaḥ sakāśād bhinattvavadherapratīyamānatvāt ? na ca kimatrāvadhipratītyā kartavyam yata eva tasya na pratītistata eva tasya tato bhedasthitiḥ | na cānyopalambhe'pi pararūpeṇa bhāvo bhidyate, kiṃ tu tādātmyena pratītirevānyato bhedapratītiḥ sā cāpratīte'pi parasminnavikaleti na bhedapratītikṣatiḥ |
[457,2]
atrottaram, yadi tāvadapratīyamānasyāpi sattvapakṣāpekṣayedamabhidhīyate tadā bāhyavāda eva yuktametat; na vijñaptimātratānaye | tathā hi,
[457,3]
sattā ca nāmātyakṣāṇāṃ svavinmātre ca saṃsthitiḥ | yatparairucyate rucyamatra vismīyate mayā ||
[457,4]
tasmāt nāprakāśādasattvādeva tadapekṣābhedasaṃsthitiḥ | na cāsadapekṣaiva bhavitumarhati, na hi śaśaviṣāṇāpekṣayā kasyacidabhedasthitiḥ, aikyaniṣedhamātraṃ tu syāt, tacceṣyata eva | yadi na tato vyāvṛttaṃ tadeva kiṃ bhavatu ghaṭa iti cet ? ata evaikyaniṣedhamātraṃ brūmaḥ | nanvasato vyāvṛttaṃ sadabhidhīyate, yaccāsato vyāvṛttaṃ tad bandhyāsutādapi, na hi vṛkṣād vyāvṛttaṃ na plakṣāditi yuktam | tat kathaṃ kharaśṛṅgānna vyāvṛtto ghaṭaḥ ? yadyevaṃ khapuṣpasyāpi kumbhādibhyo bhedaḥ sutarāṃ durnivāraḥ | na hi yad yato na vyāvartate tatastad vyāvṛttimat | tataśca vindhyād bandhyāsutasya na bhedo nābheda iti na vaktavyam | ubhayaniṣedhasyābhāvaniyatatvena sāmānyapudgalādyabhāvasādhanāyānupanyāsaḥ | tato vyāvartata iti hi prathamārthaḥ pañcamyartho vā sādhāraṇa eva, vastudharmatayā kalpitadharmatayā vā | tadidamatrārthasatattvam | asmādidaṃ bhidyata iti yadi vakturekasvabhāvatāniṣedhamātramabhimatam, tadā ghaṭaturaṅgaśṛṅgayoḥ parasparato vyāvṛttirastu, kā kṣatiḥ ?
[457,5]
athātmātmīyavasturūpasthitirabhimatā, tadā ghaṭapaṭādīnāmeva, na narakharaśṛṅgayorna vā narasya kharaśṛṅgasya ca, ekasyaiva vastutvāt | tathā ca sati pudgalaḥ skandhānna bhinna iti nātmātmīyarūpeṇānayoḥ sthitirityeva vivakṣitam | nāpyeka iti bandhyāsūnusamānatāmanubhavatīti na doṣaḥ | bhāvābhāvayostvabhāvasya kalpitaṃ rūpamāśritya parasparaparihāreṇa vyavasthitalakṣaṇatvamucyate, na vasturūpatvamubhayoḥ | ataevātmātmīyavasturūpasthitirityuktam | tasmād yāvadapratibhāsamānamapi na vastutāmatikrāmati tāvat parasparāsaṃkīrṇatve'nupalabhyamānādapi bhedagrahaṇamiti syāditi matisattāsādhane | anyathā tu tadāpi saṃśaya eva | prakāśaikasvabhāve tu sattvena pratīyamānaṃ naikaṃ na nānā | pratibhāsī tu bhāvo'bhāvo na bhavatīti bhedārtho'bhimata eva | taccodbhāvanāsaṃvṛttyābhidhoyate, na tu tatrābhāvāṃśasya niṣedhasyollekhaḥ, ullekhe tādātmyāparihārāt kuto'bhāvatā ? ataeva bhāvābhāvatayāpi na dvaitaprāptiḥ | tasmādanyābhimatasya leśasyāpi na pratītirityabhāvādeva kuto bhinattviti yuktamuktam | ataeva pūrvāparayoḥ sahānupalambhe'pi bhedaḥ prasidhyatyeveti vyaktamātmapratāraṇamātrametat | pūrvāparatvasyāprakāśāt prakāśasya ca pūrvāparatvāyogāt | tasmādasattvādeva nātītādivedanaṃ nāma, prakāśasyaiva sattvāt | tathā ca, bhramātra saṃkalpanakalpanāni śātāsitādinyakhilākṣajāni | jñānānyabhinnāni sahopalabdheḥ pūrvāparatvaṃ tu na vedyameva ||
iti saṃgrahaḥ ||
[458,1]
athavā kuto bhinattviti bhedāvadherapratibhāsādeva, kimatra bhāvābhāvacintayā ityarthaḥ | tathā hi,
[458,2]
asmād bhinnamitīdaṃ cet svarūpaṃ grāhyavastunaḥ | sāvadherasya bhāsaḥ syānna vā grāhyaṃ tadātmanā ||
[458,3]
nanu saṃbandhyantarāpratibhāse'pi saṃbandhinaḥ pitrādeḥ pratītirastīti cet ?
tatrāpi kālpanikameva saṃbandhitvaṃ vidmaḥ, vasturūpatve sarvasya saṃbandhino bodhākṣepāt |
avadhirapi hi saṃbandhiviśeṣa eva | ataeva hetuphalayorekapratītiranyapratītivinākṛtā bhavantī śuddhasvabhāvaviṣayā parasparāpekṣālakṣaṇasaṃbandhaviplavasaṃkalpaśilpinirmitamevopapādayati | tasmādavadherabodhe'vadhimato matiriti vimatireveti kutaścid bhedagrāhi pratyakṣamapratibhāsinaḥ | nanu nīlamanīlād bhinnamavaśyameṣitavyam, tadgrāhiṇā ca pratyakṣeṇa tathā na gṛhyata iti na gṛhītameva nīlam | vayamapyevaṃ brūmaḥ | anīlāgrahaṇe tato bhidyamānaṃ na gṛhyata iti nīlameva kathaṃ gṛhītam ? yata eva tasyāgrahaṇaṃ tata eva tato bhedagrahaḥ, anyathā hyapalambhānupalambhāveva na sidhyeyātā miti cet ? yathā tarhi tasya nopalambhaḥ tathā tadavadherbhedasyāpi kathamupalambhaḥ ? tataśca tadgraho nāma yathaikatāmasya viruṇaddhi, tathā tadavadhikabhedagrahamapi | athāsyaitadrūpapratītireva bhedapratītirityucyate ? bhedapratītiniṣedhe'pi samānametat |
[459,1]
vināvadhiṃ pratīto hi bhedo bhedaḥ kathaṃ nu saḥ | śabda eva tathā mābhūditi ced bhāsatāṃ tathā ||
[459,2]
ubhayāvabhāsane hi tadapekṣaḥ svabhāva evāsya na sphuratītyucyate, na vikalpamātrapratikṣepaḥ | tasmād yathānyasaṃkīrṇarūpabhāsanameva bhedapratibhāsa ucyate, tathāvadhinirapekṣamīkṣaṇamevāsya bhedapratibhāsabhraṃśa ityucyate, svarūpamātrapratibhāsāt | yadyevam, na bhedyabhāsādavadherjñātaṃ nābhedyasaṃkarāt | nānyacca bhedābhedābhyāṃ vastu vastugrahaḥ katham ||
yadi samīcīnamālocyata evametat,
[459,3]
arthasyāvyatibhede hi jñānādapi bhidā kutaḥ | bhede cāvadhibodhe'pi sarvaḥ sarvasya gocaraḥ ||
[459,4]
kevalaṃ bahirabhiniveśapāravaśye cinteyam, tatra ca samānameva dūṣaṇamidam |
yathā hi bhedagrahānaṅgīkāre ekasya, tathā bhedagrahanibandhanasyāvadhigrahasyābhāve dvitīyasya |
tatra yadi cakṣuṣī nimīlya bāhyagrahavadavadherabodhe'pi bhedagrahavyavasthaikasya, tadā cakṣuṣī nimīlyaiva bhedagrahābhāve'pi vastugrahavyavasthā kiṃ nāparasya, yathā paramāṇurūpānullekhe'pi ? na hi paramāṇubhyo'nyadasti vastu, tatastatrāpi nimīlitākṣasyaiva tadanullekhe'pi vastugrahavyavasthā | evaṃ bhedāpratītāvapi na doṣaḥ |
[459,5]
kathaṃ tarhi bhedagrahaḥ ? na kathañcit | bhedagrahavyavasthāmātraṃ tu paścimaniścayāpekṣayā syāt | sa hi nīlamanīlarāśiṃ ca svānurūpapratibhāsaviṣayīkṛtamanyo'nyapratyanīkatayā vibhajan svavyāpāramapi nīlamidaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nānīlamiti pratyakṣa eva kṣipatīti tadapekṣayādhyakṣameva parasya vyāvṛttiṃ gṛhṇātīti vyavasthāpyate, so'pi vā smṛtiriti, yathā dhārāvāhijñānāntarasya gṛhītagrahaṇamagṛhīte'pyekatvaniścayāpekṣayā | etena tat paricchinattītyāderavirodho vyākhyātaḥ | tadanenāvāntaravyavasthāmātreṇa na pratyakṣasyābhedagrahanisargavisargayogaḥ | tat kimidānīmupalabdhānupalabdhayoraikyamastu ? na, bhedagrahaniṣedhamātrasya vivakṣitatvāt | vikalpastu saha krameṇa vā pratiyoginaḥ pratipattau saṃkalpe vā bhedamabhedaṃ vā vyavahārayet, pratyakṣāpekṣayā tvapratibhāsamānaṃ naikaṃ na nānā |
pratibhāsamāne kā gatiriti cet ? tatrāpi yadi grāhakayorbhedaḥ, tadānyaviṣayānullekhāt pūrvavadvikalpa eva bhedagrāhī | abhede siddhaścitrādvaitavādaḥ, buddhirūpa mevābhedagrāhakameva pratyakṣamityapi | saṃgrahaḥ, bāhyasya sattve'sattve vā nādhyakṣaṃ bhedavedanam | abhedavedanaṃ buddhau bhāsamānātmanaiva tu ||
tasmād vyavahāraparāyaṇameva bhedaḥ ||
[460,1]
nanu puraḥ spaṣṭākāraṃ nīlapītādiviruddhadharmādhyāsi bhāsamānaṃ kathamapahnotuṃ śakyate ? nedamapahnayate, ataeva citramucyate | tasya citraśabdābhidheyasya nīlapītādeḥ pratisvaṃ bhedaṃ tattvato na kṣamate, svasaṃvittirityucyate | tatra ca viruddhadharmādhyāsa iti viruddhau vā dharmau viruddhayorvā ? prathamapakṣe apyāśrayadvāreṇa vā, svarūpeṇa vā ?
āśrayapakṣe, saṃvedanādevādhikaraṇatāsiddherasiddhirviruddhadharmādhyāsasya, svasaṃvedanasvīkṛte pramāṇāntarāvatāravirahāt | atha svarūpeṇa, tanmātraṃ na vyathate'bhedinyāśraye pratibhāsamānau maitrīmevāvahato hato virodhaḥ kṛtakanityatvavat |
[460,2]
tayoḥ kalpanākṛta eva bhedo'tra tu pratibhāsakṛta iti cet ? abhinnāśrayatvamātreṇa nidarśanametat | āśrayābhedastarhi tatra pratibhāsābhedādeveti cet ? atrāpi svasaṃvedanābhedāt | pratibhāsabhedāt tarhi bheda eva kiṃ na veti cet — na, bāhye hi pratibhāsaḥ pramāṇamākārāparanāmā, tadabhāve tvābhāsa eva viṣayaḥ | pramāṇaṃ tu svasaṃvedanam, sa tenaikīkriyamāṇaḥ kena bhettuṃ śakyaḥ ? viruddhayordharmāviti tu dūrotsāritam, bhedasyaivābhāvāt kva virodhaḥ iti | tasmānna bhedasādhanaṃ kiñcit | abhedasādhanaṃ tu svasaṃvedanameva bhedabādhanaṃ ca svarasavāhī bahirvyavahārastūpasthāpayatīti sthitam |
etadapyāha, nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk | aśakyadarśanastaṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || (pra. vā. 2. 220)
iti | ananyabhāgityananyasvabhāvabhāk | pītādisvabhāvamabhajannīlādiraśakyapratibhāsaścitravijñānastha ekākī śakyadarśanaḥ syādapi pītādyekaikaniyatatvāt taddharmatāpannasya pratibhāsasya |
parasparasvabhāvastyajanneva śakyapratibhāsa ityarthaḥ | taṃ hi vivecayan bhindan niyataṃ taddharmatāmanāpannatāṃ pratibhāsasya svīkuryāditi bahirarthavāda eva nipatet | jñānopādhiścāyaṃ nīlādiḥ, tasmād, yad yathā bhāsate jñānam (pra. vā. 2. 121)
nīlapītādibhāsitvena tattatraivānubhūte pītāditvena svasaṃvedanāt parasparātmatveneti ityarthaḥ | śeṣaṃ sugamam | ato yuktamāha bhāṣyakāraḥ,
[461,1]
na vā taccitram, acitrād bhedena vyavasthāpanāsaṃbhavāditi | (pra. vā. bhāṣye pṛḥ 290)
[461,2]
atra hyacitrādanānārūpāt svasaṃvedanād bhedenāvyavasthāpanamiti, abhedena vyavasthāpanaṃ paryudāsaparyavasāyi vivakṣitam | tacca prasādhitaṃ svayameva | pūrvamaśakyavivecanatvamavyabhicāralakṣaṇamekatvamuktam, adhunā tvekasaṃvidantargatatvameveti vāśabdaḥ | tena citrākāratāpi saṃvṛttyocyate | paramārthataḥ punaradvaitamevetyarthaṃ parikalpya bhedapratītiniṣedhamātrābhiprāyeṇa yaduktam, yadyevaṃ na vā tadadvaitaṃ dvaitād bhedenāpratibhāsanāt, evaṃ na vā jñānam, na vā svasaṃvedanamiti, tannirastam | dvaitaṃ hi bhedaḥ, tasya ca kva pratibhāsaḥ ? tena tato bhedapratibhāsābhāve'pi kuta ekatvam, ekasyaikasaṃvidantargameṇa pratipāditatvāt ? evaṃ śeṣamapi, pratibhāse hi sarvasya viparyayasya svabhāvabhaṅgaprasaṅgaḥ ?
[462,1]
udbhāvanāsaṃvṛttyā cātra citravad bhedo'pi vyavasthārha ityapi na yuktam, anubhavasya bhedavirodhenodayapratipādanāt | nīlapītādimātreṇa citrasyādvaitavacanamevodbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ, na bhedavacanam | abhyāsabhāvitaṃ tu bhedavacanamanabhyūhitatattvasya na tattvoparodhīti | vastutastu, prasajyapratiṣedha evāyaṃ vācakākṣaraḥ, ekatvasādhanāyeti tu bhrāntirlokasya | tadayamarthaḥ, athavā tadgrāhyagrāhakābhimataṃ nīlapītādi vā citraśabdābhidheyaṃ na citraṃ, na nānā, acitrāt svasaṃvedanāddhetorbhedena vyavasthāpanābhāvāditi nānātvaniṣedhamātramiṣṭam, pareṇa caikatvaniṣedho'dhyakṣādeva kuta ityubhayavinirmukta eva prakāśaḥ |
kṣaṇikaṃ kṣaṇitvamukta iva sannityuktaṃ bhavati, yathā prathamaṃ prathitamasmābhiḥ | ata evānyasya jaḍasya grāhyagrāhakasya vā abhāvāt kevalārtho'yamadvaitaśabdo na dvaitaparyudāse naikārtha iti darśayannāha, tasmāt svasaṃvedanameva kevalamadvaitamaparasyābhāvāditi | (pra. vā. bhāṣye pṛḥ 290)
tena yadeva codyamukhena pūrvamāha, atha pratibhāsamānaṃ kathamekānekatvavikalpanādeva na bhavati, vikalpyamānamapi tatpratibhāsata eva, abhāve kathaṃ pratibhāsaḥ ? pratibhāsaścet, kathamabhāva iti ? ṭīkā cātra ekānekarūpaparihṛtasyāpyupalambhātmatayopalambhaḥ satteti nyāyāt sadeveti | tadeva siddhāntāntaratvena vyaktīkṛtam | tadevamekatvopādhiścitrādvaitavādo vārtikakārasya mukhya upalakṣyate | bhāṣyakārasya tūbhayavyāvṛttiviśeṣaṇaḥ | tattvatastu ubhayorapyeka evābhiprāyaḥ | abhivyaktirītibhedāt tu mukhyetaravyavasthā ||
[462,2]
anālocya tataścitrāṃ citrādvaitavyavasthitim | bhāṣyāpadeśādācāryadūṣaṇaṃ kasya bhūṣaṇam ||
[462,3]
yadi cācāryasyānyo'bhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasyāpyakṣaravyākhyeyamabhiprāyastvanya iti nāśakyamiti dhik prakāśa eva skhalanam ! tadevamekatāyā eva buddhirūpe citre'pyupapattervyāpakānupalabdherasiddhiḥ | nopayogaścitrādvaitena vyavahāriṇāmiti tu na bādhakaṃ buddhagocaratvāt, śūnyatāvat | tattvāvabodhetarayorabhedād doṣa eva cet | anīkṣamāṇaḥ svamukhaṃ sukhaṃ jīvati pecakaḥ ||
tathā hi, na sā kṛtau cetasi vipratītiḥ prakāśamānasya manastvasiddheḥ | prakalpitenaiva tu nātmanāsat prakāśināpīti viśeṣa eṣaḥ || tayā ca kiṃ dharmatayā kadācid vimucyate cakramidaṃ matīnām | na cātmarūpānubhavo na pūrvaṃ cittasvabhāvatvahatiprasakteḥ || tataśca tanniścaya eva nāsīd ākārabhedotkalitaśca so'pi | na tattvasaṃvṛtyanugamya cāsya paravyapekṣāvirahe'sti bhedaḥ || na ca kvacinnāma parasya bodhaḥ svabhāvaśūnyatvamapi dvayoḥ samam | tadekadā saṃvṛtiranyadā netyayaṃ vibhāgo bhavato'pi kiṃkṛtaḥ ||
athavā, na śūnyatāyā virahaḥ kadācitsākṣātkriyā vāpi parā na kācit | na doṣanāśo na guṇodayo vāna saṃvṛtiḥ kāryavicāryamāṇā || tadatra yāvanna vicārasaṃbhavobhavo'yamanyaḥ śama ityayaṃ nayaḥ | vicāralīlālulite tu mānasebhavaḥ śamo vā ka iheti kathyatām ||
tathā ca sūtrālaṅkāre, na cāntaraṃ kiñcana vidyate'nayoḥ sadarthavṛttyā śamajanmanoriha | tathāpi janmakṣayato vidhīyate śamasya lābhaḥ śubhakarmakāriṇām ||
sadarthavṛttyā paramārthavṛttyā, śeṣaṃ saṃvṛttyā | abhisamayālaṃkāre'pi, svapnopamatvād dharmāṇāṃ bhavaśāntyorakalpanā | (abhisamayālaṃkārāloke pṛḥ 440)
ityādikam | tataśca jātisiddham | nirvāṇaṃ ca bhavaścaiva dvayametanna vidyate | parijñānaṃ bhavasyaiva nirvāṇamiti kathyate || (nāgārjunasya)
iti | asya dūṣaṇaṃ niraparādhamātṛvadha eva tadayaṃ prakaraṇārthaḥ,
[464,1]
bhedo'bhedo dvidhā'dvedhā dhīrūpe'stu yathā tathā | nālīkatvaṃ prakāśasya bādhagandhavirodhinaḥ ||
[464,2]
vijānātīti vijñānamityādikalpitaprapañcaśūnyatā tu sarvatra | tathā ca na hi te svabhūte dharmāstathā saṃvidyante yathā bālapṛthagjanā aśrutavanto'bhiniviṣṭa ityādi vistaraḥ |
buddhidharmā api hi buddhyantaraparikalpitena rūpeṇa santa eva na svasaṃvedyatayā eva sattvāt |
etena svapnamāyopamatvaṃ bhagavato vyākhyātam | dṛṣṭānteṣvapi hi niṣedho'dhyavasitasyaiva na pratibhāsamānasya | tasmāt sākārasyaiva bhagavataḥ siddhirbādhāvinākṛteti sthitam | tathā ca namaskāraślokasyārthasiddhiḥ — sānnavyañjanalakṣaṇairadhigataudārya nijenātmanā yadgambhīramananyagocaratayā śūnyaṃ prapañcormibhiḥ | nirmāṇaiśca yataḥ sphuranti jagatīṃ jñānatviṣastannacālīkatvena kalaṅkitaṃ vapurato bhadraṃ samantānmuneḥ ||
kiṃ bhūyaḥ, yathā suvarṇaṃ guṇarūpasaṃpadaḥ prakarṣaparyantamupetamakṣayam | vimuktamālīkyakalaṅkaśaṅkayā tathaiva bauddhaṃ vapurastu dehinām ||
{11.5}
<pañcamaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[466,1]
nanu svasaṃvedanavilāsaḥ sarvo'yaṃ pūrvo vistaraḥ, svasaṃvedanaṃ ca nāma nāstyevaitat, yuktyāgamanigṛhītatvāt | tadabhāve kutaścitrā citrādvaitavyavasthitiḥ | na vā samantabhadratvamālīkyāparihārataḥ ||
atra praśnaḥ, videva kiṃ nāsti kimastu na svayaṃ prameyahatyātha kathaṃ pravedanam | hatiḥ svavittau paravedane'pi vā samastametanna samasti nirṇaye ||
tathā hi, saṃvittirmama neti na prathayituṃ śakyaṃ vibhinnairmṛdo nāpīyaṃ parataḥ kvacinna ca parisphūrtāvapīdaṃ na sat | na sphūrtau svayameva satyamiti cedanyena vittau kutaḥ sattvaṃ nobhayathāpi ceti gadituṃ caitatsvato'sāṃpratam ||
ayamarthaḥ,
[466,2]
saṃvittireva nāstīti brūyānniścetano'pi kim | na vaktā cenna ca śrotā svanirbhāsastathāpyayam ||
[466,3]
paratastu vedanamiti nirastamanyatretyāstāṃ tāvat | atha na sarvathā vāryate svasaṃvittiḥ, kiṃ tu sāṃvṛtītyucyate, tarhi sarvathāpratikṣepābhāve bādhakādhīnamasyāḥ sāṃvṛtatvam | bādhā ca prameyād bhedenānubhavād vā | prameyabādhayaiva na tasyāḥ sthitiriti |
tatra,
[466,4]
bhedenānubhave bhedāt svānubhūtiḥ kathaṃ bhavet | prameyabādhā tu punaḥ śakreṇāpi na śakyate ||
[467,1]
na hi sphuradrūpameva nāstīti śakyamavasātum | atha na sarvathā sphurato niṣedhaḥ, svayaṃ vedyameva tu mā bhūt, paravedyaṃ punarastu | naivam, svavedane'pyanāśvāsaḥ kā vārtā paravedane | svavedanasyābhāve hi paravedanamapyasat ||
yadi pareṇa paraṃ vedyamānaṃ sadbhavet, parameva kathaṃ sadbhaviṣyati ? na cāsadevānyasattāvyavahārakāraṇam | tasyānyena vedane sati sattve'navasthā | evameva parasatteti cet ? prameye'pyevamevāstu | svayameva ca sattvaṃ cet prakāśo'pi svayaṃ bhavet |
jaḍasya | svakāritravirodho hi tāvatāmanayoḥ samaḥ ||
atha paravedanamapi yena svīkṛtaṃ bhavatu tasyaiva doṣaḥ, mama tu svavedyaṃ na paravedyaṃ kimapīti cet ? naivaṃ cetanāvān vaktumarhati | tathā hi, svataḥ parato vā sphuranneva nāstyartha iti nāniṣṭyā vacanamātreṇa vā nivartayituṃ śakya iti | yadi pramāṇamanusaret tadā pratyakṣamādāvādāya pramāṇāntaraparigaṇanam | anumānādau hi dṛṣṭāniṣṭiḥ, na tu pratyakṣe |
parīkṣaviṣaye ca śeṣamaśeṣaṃ na tadviṣaye vidhibādhayorutsahate | tadeva ca pratyakṣasiddham abhidhīyate, yatsvarūpasya sākṣānnirbhāsaḥ | sa ca svena pareṇa veti kimanena ?
[467,2]
paravyāpārābhāve'pi yadi nāsya svarūpavit | svarūpapracyutiḥ saiva kimanyairbādhakairapi ||
[467,3]
yata evātmanirbhāsastata eva na bādhyate | svārthāvabhāsanādeva bādhakasyāpi bādhitā ||
[467,4]
so'pi tenaiva bhāṇḍena vaṇigityavagamyatām | tasmātprakāśamānasya na bādho nāma kaścana ||
[467,5]
nanu pareṇa prakāśane tenaiva rakṣā syāt, svayaṃ bhāsanamanāthaṃ pareṇa prabhavatā bādhyeta | uktamatra, paro'pi svarūpaprakāśanenaivopayujyate na sattāmātreṇa, nāpi bhujaṃ prasārya prahāravāraṇena, tatsvarūpaprakāśanaṃ yadi svarūpamapi saṃbhavennāparamupayogi |
pratyuta, svabalenaiva balavān yaḥ pareṇa sa durbalaḥ | yathātmarakṣāvahito parastatra parastathā ||
tathā cāsatkhyātiviparītakhyātismṛtipramoṣadṛṣṭimoṣādayaḥ,
[468,1]
pareṇa bhāsane dṛṣṭā vividhā bhramakalpanāḥ | svahetostu prakāśasya niṣpattau prabhavanti na ||
[468,2]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tat tathaiva vyavasthitam | nānyatra rūpamādhāya bhāsate jñānamanyathā ||
[468,3]
yadā yadeva sphurati rūpaṃ tasya tadeva hi | svākāreṇaikyakaraṇād bahirapyucyate bhramaḥ ||
[468,4]
yadā tu bahirapi parito nirastavibhramāśaṅkamabhyāsāt svarūpanirbhāsi jñānam anubhavaviṣayastadā kva bādhaśaṅkā ? kiṃ punaḥ svānubhave ? kevalaṃ tādṛśasya kathamutpattiḥ kathaṃ vā niścayaḥ syāt ?
[468,5]
yathā nīlasvabhāvena janma bodhātmanā tathā | dhiyaḥ svahetordīpasya pītabhāsātmanā yathā ||
[468,6]
kathaṃ punaḥ svasaṃvedanamevedaṃ na paravedanamityanyatroktamityuktam ? kevalaṃ svavedyaṃ paravedyaṃ vā pratibhāsamānameva rūpamabādhyamiti prakṛtam | tacca siddham,
[468,7]
pramāṇasya pramāṇena nāparasyāpi bādhanam | prāgevādhyakṣarūpasya svasaṃvittestu kā kathā ||
[468,8]
trairūpyapariśuddhibodhajanmano'numānasyāpi na mānāntareṇāvamānaḥ śakyaḥ, śabdādervā yathāyatham | na hyekadaikatraiva dharmiṇi parasparapratyanīkadharmadvayasādhanasamarthayoḥ saṃbhava ityākṣiptaprāyam | ekasya tu svaviṣayadārḍhyavirahe bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ syāt |
svaviṣaye ca dārḍhyamadārḍhya vā dvayoḥ paryante pratyakṣasyaiva skhalanetarābhyām | pratyakṣasya ca skhalanaṃ viṣaye bhrama eva | bhramaśca paravittiniyata iti kaḥ saṃvedanasya pratimallaḥ ?
[469,1]
yadi bahirapi nirastavibhramāśaṅkasya na bādhaḥ, kathamadvayānumānena svaprabhavasya bādhaḥ ? uktamatra paravitterevāyaṃ viplava iti na śakyam, vyāpakānupalambhe'pi svavitterevāyaṃ viplava iti śakyamabhidhātum, paravedanādhyavasāyena tadvyāpārasyānanuvidhānāt |
tadāpi sattāmātreṇa bhāva iti saṃskāriṇaḥ śrutasaṃskārakṣālanavat mahāmohasāmarthyametat |
saṃskāramantareṇāpi skhalanamiti cet ? tarhi jīvitamantareṇa na skhalanamiti maraṇameva skhalanapratīkāra iti sādhvī bauddhasthitiḥ | kiṃ ca svavedanasya vyāpakatayā vyatireko'śakyadarśana iti anādyavidyāprabhavo'pi viplavastadīya iti vadato vyāpakānupalabdhisādhyāyā niḥsvabhāvatāyā api svabhāvāroparāgādayo viplala iti na dūram, pratyanīkākāratā tu sādhāraṇī |
[469,2]
tasmānna sattāmātreṇopayogavyavasthā, upayoge'pi vā na tadvyāpārānanuvidhāyinā vikalpenotthāpito vyāpakānupalambhastasmai prabhavati | tadaprabhavo hi saṃbandhādigrāhakamevāpramāṇīkurvan tenaikaviṣayatayā paravedanameva doṣeṇa sparśayet, na svasaṃvedanam atyantabhinnaviṣayatvāt | tato yathā tatra sādhane yadi paravitteḥ prāmāṇyaṃ svīkuryāt, svabādhanamanumānamapi pramāṇayet | atha na, tathāpyanumānasādhyaṃ siddhamiti tasyā eva viplavaḥ sphuṭībhavatyanumānodayena, tathā na vyāpakānupalambhena svavitteḥ, uktasāmarthyasya vaktumaśakteḥ, svecchayā tu pratipattā svavedanaviṣayamapi pakṣīkuryāt, kevalaṃ pratyakṣaviśeṣabādhitatvāt na sādhanāvadhānamiti nyāyaḥ |
[469,3]
tarhi vijñaptimātrasiddhāveṣa nyāyaḥ, prāgeva tu vyāpakānupalambhodaye tatsādhanamevānavakāśam | naivam, yadaiva nīlasya niḥsvabhāvatāṃ pratijānīte, tadaiva svavedanādhyakṣeṇa pratikṣepāduktakrameṇa | yadyevaṃ, prakāśamānatādisādhanabandhyatāprasaṅgaḥ | etadapi nāsti, vijñaptivyavahāramātropayogāt | nanu tathāpi paraprakāśyatāniṣedhena svaprakāśatā sādhyamānā vijñānavyavahāraṃ sādhayet, na ca sarvathā paravedyatābhāve niḥsvabhāvatve vā sādhyasādhanaṃ nāma kiñcit, tat kathaṃ vyavahārasiddhirapi ?
[469,4]
tadayuktam | saṃvṛtau hi sādhyasādhanāsthā | tadā ca dvayorapi tattvayorasiddhiḥ |
tatra ca yasya puro'paropādhiprakāśinyapi nīle nijābhisaṃskārikā'vidyābalāt paraprakāśyatāsaṃśayaḥ, tadvodhanāya nyāyasahaḥ sādhanopanyāsaḥ | tadā ca sa eva pratyakṣabādhādikaṃ nirūpayiṣyati | tatpratipādane ca jāte vijñaptivyavahāra iti | etāvataiva vijñānavādino vyāpārasamāptiḥ | parasya tu pratyakṣabādhaiva sādhanāvadhānaṃ niṣedhati | na cānumānānudayamapekṣya pratyakṣavṛttiḥ kvacidapi | anumānaṃ tadaviṣaya eva sarvadā pravṛttimaditi tena sādhite iva bādhite'pi nāvakāśamāsādayatīti sthitam |
[470,1]
tasmānna prameyabādhayā sāṃvṛtatvamātmavedanasya | tathaitadapi nāśaṅkanīyam, yadi nīlaṃ svavedanāt siddham, svavedanenāpi svavedanāntarāt seddhavyamityanavasthā, tasya svayaṃ siddhau nīlasyāpi svavedanena kiṃ kartavyamiti | tathāhi nīlasyāpi kiṃ svavedanena iti vedanaṃ vadataḥ svayameva vedanamastvityabhimatam | ayameva ca svasaṃvedanavāda ityaśvārūḍhanyāyaḥ | yadi tu bhinnaṃ tatsyāt, tadā nānavasthāmatikrāmeta, nāpi svavedanavādasparśa iti | yadi tarhi na bhinnaṃ prajñaptisat, tasyaiva ca dharmamātrametat, tadā tadvādhane svayameva na taṭasthamāsituṃ śaktam, tat kathaṃ pararakṣaṇakṣamam ? tadapi yatkiñcit |
[470,2]
nīlasyāpi prakāśatvaṃ prakāśasyāpi nīlatā | dharmadharmivyavasthānaṃ naikātmaniyataṃ matam ||
[470,3]
abheda eva rakṣāpi bhedo'smin niṣprayojanaḥ | svarakṣānāntarīyā hi pararakṣā bhavenna vā ||
[470,4]
yata eva svayaṃ bhāti tata eva na bādhyate | ityarthatattvaṃ kenāpi vyāhāreṇa nivedyate ||
[470,5]
yatpunaryuktivāditābhimānenocyate, svātmani kāritravirodhāt na svasaṃvedanam, na hi tadevāṅgulyagraṃ tenaivāṅgulyagreṇa spṛśyata iti, tatrāpi,
[470,6]
nāṅgulyagraṃ tadagreṇa spṛśyaṃ cenmasṛṇaṃ katham | svayaṃ masṛṇametacced virodhaḥ kiṃ na saṃprati ||
[470,7]
kiṃ na dhīrbhāsate svayaṃ vā svayameva masṛṇamidamasti jātaṃ veti pratītyā vākyārthaparyavasānādāyātaḥ kāritravirodhaḥ | tathā ca svayaṃ gacchati, svayaṃ gaura ityādipreraṇāṅgarāgajanitatvādipratikṣepeṇa sarvathā na vaktavyamevaṃ vādibhiḥ, tatsannidhau vā pareṇeti mahān viplavaḥ | atha sakarmikāyāṃ kriyāyāṃ ekameva karma kartā ca nocitam, jñānārthā ca sakarmikaiva kriyā nīlaṃ vetti caitra iti | evaṃ tarhi, svayaṃ prakāśate buddhirityādau tūṣṇīmāsyatām |
tataśca vedyata ityādi yat karmakartṛvivakṣayā paraiḥ prayujyate, tadasmābhirbhāsate ityasminnevārthe saṅketitamiti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ | atha svayambhūrbhagavānityādinā prakṛtīśvarādivyāpāranirāśena svahetoreva tādṛksvarūpotpattipratipādanamātrametat, na tu bhedadṛṣṭaḥ kriyākārakavyavahāro'tra mata ityucyate, buddhirapi tarhi svahetoreva prakāśarūpotpannā na pareṇa prakāśiteti saṃmatau ko vidveṣaḥ ? iyamevātmasaṃvittirasya yā jaḍarūpatā | kriyākārakabhāvena na svasaṃvittirasya tu ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[471,1]
yatpunaratroktamevaṃvādino loka eva bādhako bhaviṣyati iti, tadanenaiva nirastam, loke tathāvidhāyā vivakṣāyā dṛṣṭatvāt | atha buddhiviṣaye na dṛśyate, tatrāpi prakāśarūpavyavahāre svaparaprakāśavivakṣāyā dṛṣṭatvād dīpaghaṭavat | kevalaṃ bāhye dvayadarśane'pi buddhirūpādhikāreṇa paraprakāśyatāyā bādhanāt svaprakāśataiva vyavasthāpyate, na tu sarvathā vyavahāra evaivaṃ nāstīti ||
[471,2]
nanu, dīpaḥ prakāśata iti jñātvā jñānena kathyate | jñānaṃ prakāśata iti kenedaṃ suhṛdocyate || prakāśā vāprakāśā vā yadā dṛṣṭā na kenacit | bandhyāduhitṛlīleva kathyamānāpi sā mudhā ||
iti cet ? niravakāśametat ? idameva hi nīlādi svaprakāśasvabhāvaṃ jñānamiti vyavasthāpitam, tatkathaṃ kenedaṃ suhṛdocyata ityucyate ? na svasaṃvedye'rthe paropadeśo garīyān, ko'nyathā dharmī vyapakānupalambhādeḥ ? pradīpe'pi tarhi jñānameva kathaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ? satyam, lokāpekṣayā'loka eva bādhako bhaviṣyatītyapahastayitum | tadetad yuktikṣīṇasya viśrāmamātramatrāṇam, anyathā sarvaśūnyatāyāmeva kiṃ bādhako lokaḥ ?
saṃvṛttyā sarvasvīkārāditi cet ? tattvato na kiñcidastīti etadeva lokasya na kṣamaṃ, saṃvṛttyā tu nāstīti yadi syādastu | atha tattvato'pi nāstīti kimasmābhiḥ sādhyate, astināstivyatikramasyābhimatatvāditi cet — na | astiniṣedha eva, na hi nāstyarthaḥ |
[472,1]
na bhāvo yadi nīlāderabhāvaḥ kena vāryate | nābhāva iti vāde ca bhāva evāvatiṣṭhate ||
[472,2]
parasparaparīhāravyavasthitimatāṃ yataḥ | ekabādho'nyavidhaye nānicchāmātrato'nyathā ||
[472,3]
tṛtīyo vā prakāro'tra vaktavyo yadi vānayoḥ | ekatraiva vyavasthānaṃ dhīmatāṃ nāparā gatiḥ ||
[472,4]
syādetat, nāsmābhiḥ kasyacid vidhiḥ pratiṣedho vā sādhyate, sadasadubhayānubhayavādināṃ tu svābhyupagamenaiva tattallakṣaṇānupapattiriti pratipādyate | tatra yadi sallakṣaṇānupapattyā svayameva prāgapi sattvābhāvaḥ, tadā kimasmābhirapanītaṃ kimapi syāt ?
yadā cāsallakṣaṇānupapattyā prāgapyasattvābhāvaḥ, tadā kimabhāvābhāvena bhāvo nāma kasyacit kutaḥ ? yathā hi,
[472,5]
putrotpattivipattibhyāṃ kumāryāḥ prītidīnate | putrasaṅkalpataḥ svapne jāgratastu na vidyate ||
[472,6]
sa tasyāḥ sāvaśeṣaśokavinodanāya yadi tatprabandhamṛṣātvamāsādayati, tat kiṃ tena kasyacid vidhiḥ putrādyabhāvasya, niṣedho vā putrādibhāvasya kṛtaḥ, putrodayaniṣedhena vā abhāvaḥ kasyacit, maraṇaniṣedhena vā bhāvavidhiḥ, svayamāditaḥ putrasyaivābhāvāt ?
tadanuvādamātraṃ tu jāgrataḥ | evamāryānāryayorūhitavyam | etadeva cādiśāntatvaṃ prakṛtipariśuddhiścāgame gīyate iti |
[472,7]
atrocyate | kīdṛśau vidhiniṣedhau bhavatā parihriyete, utpādanavināśalakṣaṇau hastena gṛhītvopanayāpanayasvabhāvau vā ? yad vā vivādāspadībhūtasya kasyacit dharmasya pramāṇena sādhanalakṣaṇo vidhirbādhanalakṣaṇo vā niṣedhaḥ ? tatra,
[472,8]
ādyapakṣadvayaṃ tāvadanyasyāpi na vidyate | bhavatāpi tṛtīyastu parihartuṃ na śakyate ||
[473,1]
na hi bhagavataḥ prāmāṇyaṃ sthitameva prāgapanīyate, paścād vetīśvarādāvasadevopanīyata iti pare'pi manyante | tathā na dvayaṃ sthitamevāpanīyate, advayaṃ vā saṃpratyupanīyate, apareṇa sthita eva svabhāvo'nūdyate | yuktyā ca kayācit pratipādyata iti sarvasaṃmatiḥ | tacca bhavato'pyastīti ka evamatireka ukto bhavati ? tadayameva vidhiniṣedhaprakramo yadidamastīdaṃ nāstīti pratipādanaṃ, taccāyātaṃ vacanavyāpṛtasya, viśeṣato jigīṣayā parārthaśīlatayā vā vāde pravṛttasya | mūkībhūya tiṣṭatastu nāyaṃ paryanuyoga iti syāt | svapnadṛṣṭānto'pi sarvasādhāraṇaḥ, yo hi vastudharmaḥ kenacidādriyamāṇaḥ kenacinniṣedhyaḥ, tasya siddhyā tadguṇāropād vā prītiḥ, pareṇa tadabhāvapratipādane viṣādaḥ, taccitavinodanodyatena cādina eva tathā nāstītyanuvādamātraṃ kṛtamiti tulyam |
[473,2]
tatra ya eva tathā pratipādanakṣamastasyaiva svādhīnaḥ svapnadṛṣṭāntaḥ | tathā cādvayavāde'pi yathā svākāramātra eva putraṃ jāgaraṇakāle phalitamāropya harṣādistathā jāgraddaśāyāmapi jñānākāramātra eva bahirāropeṇeti na kṣatiḥ | tadubhayadaśayorapi nirvikalpapratibhāsaḥ svarūpamātraparyavasito'pi vikalpenābhūtāropastiraskriyata iti uktam | sa ca svarūpaṃ tirodhāya pararūpameva darśanena yojayati, yata evaṃ bhavati putro'dya svapne mayā dṛṣṭa iti, kiñcidvimarśe hi na putradarśanaṃ nāma, jñānamātraṃ mama tathodapādīti |
tatastadvyavasāyāpekṣayā sā putraṃ jātaṃ ca mṛtaṃ ca paśyatītyādyabhidhānam, tattvatastu kva putradarśanam anādivāsanāvaśāt tadabhiniveśaprasavayogyaviśiṣṭākārajñānamātrodayād anyatra ? kevalaṃ kimatra vastutattvamiti, vicāravyasanaṃ yasya hastāmarśena tasya kim | prītyābhiyogaḥ kriyatāṃ kīrtivārtikabhāṣyayoḥ || śraddhāvaśatve'pi varaṃ yuvarājanayāśrayaḥ | āryanāgārjunādīnāmapi yatra vyavasthitiḥ ||
iti pratipādayiṣyate | āgamapāṭhāḥ punaravicāracaturasya puṇyamātraprasavahetava eva |
vicāraprakrame ca bhāvābhāvayorekaniṣedhābhidhāyino dvitīyasvīkāraḥ sāmarthyādāyāta iti nānicchāmātreṇa trātuṃ śakyam | tathā hi svapne na putro nāmāsīditi putrābhāvo vihita eva bhāvaśca niṣiddhaḥ, tat kathaṃ jāgratā na vidhirna pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate ? āryasya tu na tathā darśanamityapi tadākāradarśanapratyanīkākārajñānodaya eva, na sarvathā saṃvittivilopa ityāstāṃ tāvat |
[474,1]
atha bhāvābhāvavikalpaniṣedho vivakṣitaḥ, sarvathā na pratibhāsamātralopaḥ, tadetadiṣṭameva, vikalpasya prakṛtibhrāntatvāt | atha vicārākṣamataiva śūnyatārthaḥ, tadā vicāro nāma saṃvṛtyāśrayaḥ, tatra ca niyamena pramāṇāvatāre na svasaṃvittimantareṇa pratyakṣāntaramanumānaṃ vā, svarūpasattayaiva viyogaprasaṅgāt | nāpi dharmidharmādipratipattiriti saṃvṛtau niyatasvākārāyāḥ svasaṃvidaḥ prameyapramāṇāntaravad bādhānupapatteḥ sthitereveti na sāṃvṛtatvaviśeṣaṇāvakāśaḥ |
[474,2]
yathā yathārthāścintyante vivicyante tathā tathā | svayaṃ tu vittiśchāyeva dhāvato duratikramā ||
[474,3]
tataśca svasaṃviditarūpasya kīdṛśī vicārākṣamatā ? kiyanto hi vicārāḥ pravartantām, na tu nīlaprakāśasya prakāśatā nīlatā vā atipātamātram, nāpyaprakāśadharmāntaraṃ paricayaviṣayaḥ | ya eva ca, svarūpamātrānubhavaḥ kalpitānāṃ parābhavaḥ |
sa eva, tataśca samatā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ ||
iti nyāyaḥ | tadetadādiśāntatvaṃ prakṛtyā ca viśuddhatā | vaimalyapariśuddhistu sarvāsatkalpanākṣayaḥ ||
ityuktameva | yadapīdaṃ tadabhyupagamenaiva tallakṣaṇānupapattiriti, tāvatāpi nānubhavasvabhāvaparibhavaḥ | yataḥ, bhautakalpitakalpānāṃ lakṣaṇānāṃ kṣatāvapi | sarvopādhiviviktasya vasturūpasya na kṣatiḥ ||
rājadvāri dviradamavalokya,
[475,1]
dantena mūlādakamandhakāraṃ prasrāvato nīradapotamāha | kaściccatustambhakamaṭṭamāsyaṃ dvāraṃ baliṃ piṇḍanibhātpurīṣāt ||
[475,2]
rājadvāre śmaśāne vā yastiṣṭhati sa bāndhavaḥ | iti gāḍhasmṛteranyo bhauto bāndhavameva tam ||
[475,3]
tato bhautairiva paraiḥ kalpitānyeva svarūpāṇi vigalantu puraḥprakāśinaḥ kimāyātaṃ bādhāyāḥ ? tataḥ,
[475,4]
yadyeṣa eva siddhānto na viśeṣastadāvayoḥ | bādhe tu sarvathā'bhāvaḥ kathaṃ lokādabādhanam || yadi lokānurakṣāpi dhīrūpe nāstitīcyatām | tattvena sarvathā nāstītyudvegaḥ kiṃ na gaṇyate ||
[475,5]
tasmālloka udvījatāṃ mā vā puruṣārthopayogitattvākhyānaṃ kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyamiti yadi svayamāśayaḥ paraḥ kimalīkamākulīkriyate ? ko hi saduttare'pi bhavatāṃ śaktipratibandhaṃ śraddhadhīta ? asti ca loke'pi svaprakāśavyavahāra iti kva lokabādhāpi ?
buddherevādhikāre sākṣāt na dṛṣṭa iti kimanenaḥ ? svaprakāśamapi vastvasti na ca kāritravirodha iti sāmānyāśrayeṇaiva dṛṣṭāntasya kṛtatvāt | api ca, sphuratyetādṛśo buddhirmametyādimatirna kim | mama svānubhavaścātra saṅkalpe tvadguṇaspṛśi ||
tasmādalamanena bālajanopalāpanena ||
[475,6]
yadapi smaraṇādanubhavasiddhimāśaṅkyārtha eva smaraṇamanubhavaśca na jñāna ityucyate, tatrāpyarthākārajñānameva, tacca svayaṃsphuritamanusmaryata iti na kṣatiḥ | arthe ca smaraṇamiti na tāvadananubhūte bhavitumarhati, atiprasaṅgāt | anubhūtaścārtho'nubhavānanubhave iti kathaṃ pratītamatra hṛdayena ? asaṃvittau vitterna khalu tadupādhivyavahṛtiḥ pratītāvanyena prasabhamanavasthā prasarati | anenaivāpāste'pyanumitimate liṅgaviraho na cādṛṣṭaṃ liṅgaṃ tadadhigatisiddhau ca vimatiḥ ||
ityantaraślokaḥ ||
[476,1]
kathaṃ tarhīdaṃtayā na nirdiśyate jñānamanubhūyamānam ? nanu nirdiṣṭameva,
[476,2]
antaḥ śātādiviṣayaṃ bahiḥ śītādigocaram | vedanaṃ tattadākāraṃ nānyo'pyasti tataḥ paraḥ || sphurattā nāma dharmo'yaṃ pratyātmaṃ durapahnavaḥ | iti sā yogyatā mānamātmā meyaḥ phalaṃ svavit ||
[476,3]
tato nirākārapakṣe syādeṣa doṣaḥ, sākārapakṣe tu śaṃkāpi nāsti | sākārapakṣa eva tu śāntidevapādānāmabhimataḥ | yadāhuḥ, yathā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ jñātaṃ neveha pratiṣidhyate | satyataḥ kalpanā tvatra duḥkhaheturnivāryate || (bo. a. 9. 26)
iti | atra hi satyatastattvato dṛṣṭādirna niṣidhyata iti dṛṣṭādikarmanirdeśāt prakāśamāno nīlakomalādiraśakyanihnava ityuktaṃ bhavati |
[476,4]
kasya tarhi nairātmyamityāha, kalpanaivābhūtānāṃ grāhyagrāhakahetuphalādīnāmityarthāt kalpanā śabdādeva | adṛṣṭe hi kalpanā | adṛṣṭaṃ cādṛṣṭatvādeva na saṃbhavati tattvata iti atrāpi saṃbadhyate | tena niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā ityādivacane'pi tattvataḥ kalpitarūpaniṣedha eveti bhāvaḥ | kimarthaṃ punarabhūtavikalpavāraṇam ? duḥkhasya hetutvāt | sa eva hi pravṛttinivṛttyādilakṣaṇaṃ saṃsāramākṣipati, tamantareṇa tadākārodayamātrasya tatrākiṃñcitkaratvāditi | yattu satyata iti satyatvena yā kalpaneti yojayanti, tatrāpi yadi satyatve'pi satyamidamiti vikalpavāraṇaṃ, pariniṣpattau ko doṣaḥ ?
[476,5]
atha saṃpratyapi satyādhimokṣavāraṇamasattvādityarthaḥ, tadā dṛṣṭādi na pratiṣidhyata iti vyāhatam, asatyaṃ cāpādyate dṛṣṭādi na ca pratiṣidhyata iti, asatyatāpādanasyaiva pratiṣedhārthatvāt | atha na pratiṣidhyate saṃvṛttyā, tattvatastu vāraṇam | tadapi nākṣarārūḍham | satyataḥśabdo'nyathāyojitaḥ kalpanāviśeṣaṇatvena, na ca tadā kalpanāśabdaḥ saṅgataḥ dṛṣṭāderevaikasya saṃvṛtiparamārthāpekṣayā vidhiniṣedhaviṣayatayā abhimatatvāt |
tathā hi, yathā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ jñātaṃ naiveha pratiṣidhyate | saṃvṛttyā tattvatastvetadduḥkhaheturnivāryate ||
iti vaktumucitam | tadatra śabdataḥ śabdasya punarāvṛttiḥ, saṃvṛtiśabdasyādhyāhāraḥ, kalpanāśabdasyānyārthateti kimakṣarāṇi kliśyante mahatām ? vyaktametat ṣaḍindriyavijñānagocarābhimatā ākārā na niṣidhyante svasaṃviditatvāt, kalpitasyaiva tu niṣedha iti | kathaṃ tarhi svasaṃvedananiṣedha eṣām ? yathā bhagavataḥ | bhagavata eva katham ?
bhinnaviṣayapratiṣedhāt | ekatrāpi citrākāre grāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ sūkṣme'pi sākṣāditi kriyākārakabhāvābhiprāyeṇa | na cāyaṃ nāśaṅkāyā viṣayaḥ sarvathā parihārayatnasya veti mantavyam | tathā hi kasyacit, ekatrāpi yathā bhāve kāryakāraṇakalpanam | ekatraiva tathā jñāne grāhyagrāhakadhīrbhavet ||
yathā bhagavataḥ, sa cāyamaṅkuro na svayaṃkṛta iti |
āryanāgārjunapādānāṃ vā, na svato nāpi parataḥ (mā. kā. 1. 1)
ityādinā niṣedhayatnaḥ, tathā, vibhuṃ cittaṃ na paśyati ityādi | yuktametat | niḥsīmā ca samāropaḥ sāṃsārikasya skandhā evātmetyādivat, kāruṇikena tasyāpyanupekṣaṇīyatvāt, grāhyagrāhakāropasya ca pradhānadoṣatvāt | kriyākārakabhāvena niṣedhastena yujyate | svasaṃviditarūpasya samutpādastu śasyate ||
yathoktamāryasandhinirmocane, na hi maitreya, tatra kaścid dharma pratyavekṣate, api tu tathā samutpannaṃ taccittaṃ yat tathā khyātīti | cittamarthābhāsaṃ pravartata ityapi svasaṃvedanameva nivedayati, vedyavedakayoḥ ekīkaraṇāt | tathā nīlajñānasamaṅgī puruṣo nīlaṃ jānātīti, agergatyarthatayā jñānārthatvāt | nīlajñānasaṃvedī sannityanena, apratyakṣopalambhasya nārthadṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati | (pramāṇaviniścaye)
iti vyaktamuktam | tadvedītyeva nīlavedīti yāvat |
[478,1]
uttaratantre ca, pratyātmavedyo dharmaḥ (u. ta. pṛḥ 10)
ityevākṣaram | na cābhūtaparikalpo'stīti bruvataḥ svasaṃvedanādanyaccharaṇam | tasmānna yuktyāgamābhyāṃ svabodhasiddhau pratibandhaḥ ||
[478,2]
astu nāma svasaṃvittiḥ svamalīkaṃ tu budhyatām | mānayorna virodhaśca kṣaṇinīlekṣaṇe yathā ||
[478,3]
anumānasiddhavyāvṛttyantaraviśiṣṭasya pratyakṣeṇa sākṣātkāre pramāṇayorapi na virodhaḥ, kṣaṇikavadalīkatve'pi niścayapratyayānudayād | viṣayabhedaśca vyaktaḥ | tadapi yatkiñcit |
nīlasattāgrāhiṇo hi pratyakṣasya kṣaṇabhaṅgasādhanaṃ sattāviśeṣasādhanameveti na virodhaḥ | sattābādhanaṃ tu prameyatvaṃ kūrmaromavaditi viruddhameva, bādhyate cādhyakṣeṇa tathā vyāpakānupalambho'pi |
tathā hi,
[478,4]
alīkamātmānamavaiti ko'rtho hyasatsvabhāvaḥ sphuratīti yo'rthaḥ | sphurattvamevāsya ca sattvamuktaṃ kathaṃ niṣedhaśca vidhiśca tasya ||
[479,1]
etena pratītyotpannatvamapi pratibimbavanniḥsvabhāvatāyāṃ svabhāvahetvabhimatam apāstam | api ca, pratītyotpannatā nāma kāryatāmātramucyate | sā ca nityaviruddheti nityatāmeva bādhatām ||
atha,
[479,2]
akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvo hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca | ityabhiprāyatastādṛksvabhāvasyaiva bādhanam ||
[479,3]
yena tarhīdṛśaṃ yatra rūpamāropi vastuni | tasyaiva bādho nirbādhaḥ kṣaṇabhaṅgavyavasthitaḥ ||
[479,4]
evaṃ hi sautrāntika eva mādhyamikaḥ prasakta iti mahatpauruṣam |
[479,5]
yatra cākṛtrimaṃ rūpaṃ vyomādāvabhyupeyate | na pratītyodayastatra pramāsiddhaḥ kathaṃcana ||
[479,6]
īpsitārthakriyāsaktā upalabdhā ghaṭādayaḥ | na santyātmādayaḥ santi vyatyayeneti kāpi dhīḥ ||
[479,7]
anupalambhādeva na te santīti cet ? upalambhastarhi sattāsādhana iti katham asantaḥ śailādayaḥ ? nopalabdhiranupalabdhirvā sattāsādhanīti cet ? etadeva parasamuttaraṃ kiṃ pratītyotpādena ? asattāsādhanamaneneti cet ? sarvathā sarvadā sattāyā asiddheḥ asattā siddhaiva | nānupalambho madīyo'yamasattāhetuḥ, kiṃ tu pareṇaiva tathābhyupagatatvāt upanyasyate | tannopalabdheḥ sattāsiddhiriti cet ? nātmādivādinānupalambhamātreṇābhāva iṣṭaḥ, tadanyeneṣṭatve'pi na tasya svopagamena doṣa ukto bhavati, tataśca svatantra evāyam anupalambho hetuḥ kartavyaḥ ||
[479,8]
sattā sādhurna saṃvittirasaṃvittistu bādhanī | viśeṣaṇānapekṣā ca setyayogaparamparā ||
[479,9]
na ca kāryatāniḥsvabhāvatayorviparyaye bādhakaṃ pratibandhasādhakaṃ kiñcidasti, na ca kvacidubhayadarśanamātreṇa vyāptisiddhiḥ, nāpi pratibimbe svābhimataniḥsvabhāvatāsaṃbhavaḥ, pratibhāsasyāśakyaniṣedhatvāt, prasādhya sādhyaṃ sādhyaśūnyatāparihāre sādhanāntarābhāvādanavasthā, adhyavasitaniṣedhopadarśane ca tenaiva vyāptiḥ pratibhāsināmiti siddhasādhanam, na ca kvacit hetuphalabhāvaḥ pramāṇasiddha iti sādhanaśūnyatā ca dṛṣṭāntasya | atha pakṣadharmasya hetorlokāśrayāt siddhiriti cet ? lokāśrayāt tarhi śūnyatāyai jalāñjalirdeyaḥ | na hīdamarddhajaratīyaṃ labhyaṃ sādhane lokāśrayo na sādhye iti |
[480,1]
pratibimbe lokāśrayeṇāpi śūnyatā dṛṣṭeti cet ? bimbe tarhi viparyayadarśanānna sādhanam | na ca pramāṇapratikṣiptasya pakṣīkaraṇamiti nyāyaḥ | viparyayādarśane darśanābhimāna iti cet ? pratibimbe'pi niḥsvabhāvatvādarśane darśanābhimāno bhavataḥ kevalaṃ lokaḥ pramāṇamāśritaḥ, bimbe viparyaye pramāṇamapi loka eva bimbe cāpramāṇībhavan pratibimbe'pi kathaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt ? pratibimbe saṃvādābhāva eva pramāṇamiti cet ? yatra tarhi saṃvādasaṃvāsastatra durvāraḥ śūnyatāvirahaḥ kṣmāruhādau | saṃvādābhimānamātramiti cet ? vaktavyastarhi saṃvādo'rtho yathā prasiddhādanyaḥ, yataḥ pratibimbe tadabhāvaḥ pratīyate |
[480,2]
pramāṇanirūpaṇāsahatvaṃ mahīdharādāvasaṃvāda iti cet ? kena punaḥ pramāṇena bhavān nirūpaṇamanusaratīti prakrame pratyakṣānumānopamānaśabdāni taditarāṇi vābhidadhīta, natvekasyāpi svasaṃvedanamantareṇa siddhiriti mahāntamāyāsamāviśet | tataḥ pramāṇāntaratiraskāre'pi svasaṃvedanādeva siddhaḥ sindhubhūdharādeḥ | yadi ca kvacit pramāṇanirūpaṇena saṃvādopalambhastadā tadabhāvānnivarteta, na ca tadasti | punarapi paracaraṇaparicaraṇameva śaraṇamiti ka eṣa nyāyaḥ, prasaṅgamātreṇa tadupagamāpekṣāyāḥ kṣamatvāt ? na ca sarvadā prasaṅga eva | viparyayārthameva hi prasaṅgasaṅgamaḥ, na ca kadācid asvātantryeṇa hetorupanyāsa eṣāṃ kṣamaḥ | kṣamāyāṃ vā sāṃvṛtaṃ tāttvikaṃ vā pramāṇam āśrayaṇīyamiti na bhūdharādeḥ siddhipratibandhaḥ | anyasya tu vijñaptimātravyavahāra eva adhiko na tu pratibhāsamānarūpasiddhipratibandhaḥ | yadi ca nirūpaṇākṣamatvaṃ kṣmādharādeḥ asaṃvādaḥ, tadeva tarhi niḥsvabhāvatvamiti kiṃ pratītyotpādena ?
[480,3]
kiṃ ca, śaktināntarīyakaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ, śaktireva ca sattvamiti niḥsvabhāvatvasādhane virodhaśca doṣaḥ | atha śūnyebhya eva dharmebhyaḥ śūnyā dharmāḥ prajāyanta iti na doṣaḥ, tat kimidānīṃ siddhāntapāṭhamātreṇa doṣaparihāraḥ ? evaṃ hyatiprasaṅgaḥ syāt | yasmādeva hi yajjanma śaktaṃ tatra tadeva tat | śakte'pi niḥsvabhāvatvakalpanā kvopayoginī ||
anyasya tu pūrvāparaviraha eva tatkalpanāpratighātaheturityanavadyam | kiṃ ca, sarvapratītimūlatvāddhanmo hetuphalasthitim | śūnyatākāṃkṣiṇo yatnādviparītastvayaṃ vidhiḥ ||
tadayamahetureva niḥsvabhāvatve pratītyotpādo nāma ||
[481,1]
atha pratītyotpāda eva niḥsvabhāvatvaṃ vyavahāramātrasādhanaṃ tu kadācit, tadāpi kāryatāmātraṃ śūnyatvamuktaṃ bhavatītyadharasthitipāta eva | samayamātraṃ vā kurvato na kaścit paripanthīti kimanena ? svayameva vā kṛtrime svabhāvatvamavakalpya tadabhāvena svabhāvahāniṃ bruvataḥ śṛṅgeṇāpi turaṅgatāmavakalpya tadabhāvena na turaṅga ityapi pratyeyam | kathaṃ tarhi, yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatā saiva te matā | (dra. a. a. ā. pṛḥ 153 praḥ)
ityādikaṃ saṅgaṃsyate | adharasthityapekṣayā tāvatāṅgena śūnyatāvatāramabhipretya tadetādṛśāni sādhanānyapi kvacinna prakṛtavādinyupayogabhāñji bhavanti | vyāpakānupalambhavad vā svasaṃvedanapratyakṣāpoḍhapauruṣāṇi nāṅganirūpaṇāyātamiti sthitam | tato niḥsvabhāvatayā na kathañcidapi svasaṃvedanasiddhiriti nirastam, tatsādhanapramāṇānavakāśāt, pratyakṣeṇa pratibandhādyabhāvācca, sādhanavinākṛtāyāṃ siddhāvatiprasaṅgāt | svaprakāśini tu nānyāpekṣitatathāsiddhireva svasaṃvedanasthitiḥ |
[481,2]
yadapyucyate, na cāpi jaḍasvabhāvatā madhyamakaṃ vādinaṃ prati kasyacit siddhā, yena tadvyāvṛttamajaḍaṃ svasaṃvedanaṃ syāditi | tadapi gātrābhreḍamātraṃ na trāṇāya | tathā hi,
[481,3]
yogācārasya nājñānaṃ nāśūnyā madhyamā vidaḥ | tathāpi jñānaśūnyādivyavahāro na bādhyate ||
[482,1]
yadi sarvathā nāstīti tadvyāvṛttinibandhanadhvaniniṣedhaḥ, hanta ! āditaḥ prabhṛti kṣaṇikanirātmānīśvarakṛtāprakṛtimayādiśabdonmūlanādavyavahāra evāyātaḥ | naño nirviṣayasyāsti na prayoga iti bruvan | paribhūtaḥ svavācaiva paraṃ vā bodhayet katham ||
antaraślokaḥ ||
[482,2]
tadāstāṃ tāvadatighṛṇākarametādṛśam | tasmānna svasaṃvedane dūṣaṇakaṇasyāpi saṃbhavaḥ |
tataḥ sāṃvṛtatvaviśeṣaṇamapanīya svasaṃvedanamastyeveti vyavasthānamanapetaṃ nyāyād yadyadyāpi nābhiniveśāveśi mānasamiti, svayamapi yadi bodhe bādhakasya pravṛttistadupanataviśeṣe kīdṛśī nirvṛtirvaḥ | atha kathamapi tatrāpattitaḥ kiṃ na sākṣādanubhuvi tadabādhā bodhibhittiḥ svavittiḥ ||
parabodhastu tattvato'sannapi abhimānamātrasiddhau yadyanumānāntareṇa bādhyate bādhyatām, svarūpaparyavasāyi tu tadā pratyakṣaṃ svarakṣāyāṃ na kṣamamiti na kṣamameveti |
[482,3]
sakala iha vicāraḥ saṃvṛtāveva yuktaḥ kvacidanubhavabādho na kṣamaḥ saṃvṛtau ca | na ca paramanubhūtaṃ kvāpi tadvodhabādhe kaliriva kalināyaṃ hanyatāmastu śāntiḥ ||
{11.6}
<ṣaṣṭhaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[483,1]
atha tathāvidhaślāghāspadaṃ madhyamāmupakramya, samyag yogācāradarśanametat pariniṣṭhitamiti ko'yaṃ kramaḥ ? naiṣa doṣaḥ, asyāpi bhagavataivoktasya nītaneyavibhāgakāritayā tadvyākṛtairāryairyuvarājaparyantaiḥ pratigṛhītasyācāryaiḥ prasādhitasyollāghaślāghatvāt |
sākārasiddhiśceyamupakrāntā | nanu tathāpi parasparavirodhidvayamapi na satyam, tatraikahṛdayo'pi svayaṃ daiśiko bhagavān vineyāpekṣayā neyamapyupadiśet, bhūmilābhinastu dṛṣṭasatyāḥ kathamekaikapakṣapātinaḥ ekaikamatadeśanāt ? viśiṣṭānyadeśane hi parānurodhādetaditi syāt |
paramagambhīraśca mantranayasamaya ete eva sthitī samāśritya yayoriyān virodha iti kathaṃ hṛdayanirvṛtiḥ samantabhadratve'pi ? ucyate,
[483,2]
virodhaḥ pauruṣeyo'tra vastvekamubhayasthitau | samāropāpavādāntamuktaṃ hi muniśāsanam ||
[483,3]
atra hi citraprakāśarāśau nāprakāśakaṇasyāropaḥ sahyo, nāpi prakāśaleśasyāpavādaḥ, śalyena viśatāṅgena cchidyamānena vā yathā | vyathāropāpavādābhyāṃ tatheha sphuradākṛtau || apavādo na saṃvṛttyā nāropastattvato yadi | na tau dvāvapi tattvena yadi kiṃ vā virudhyate ||
tathā sadasallakṣaṇanirdeśe āryasvāmī, abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate | śūnyatā vidyate tvatra tasyāmapi sa vidyate || (ma. vi. 1. 2) abhūtaparikalpastu cittacaittāstridhātukāḥ | (tatraiva 1. 9)
iti bruvan grāhyagrāhakayorevāropaniṣedhaṃ prati bhāsamānasyaivāpavādaniṣedhamāha | tatrābhūtaṃ grāhyagrāhakadvayaṃ parikalpyate'nenāsmin vā pṛṣṭhajavikalpadvāretyabhūtaparikalpaḥ | tadeva vistareṇa darśayan sabhāṣyaḥ sūtrālaṃkāraḥ,
[484,1]
yathā māyā tathābhūtaparikalpo nirucyate | yathā māyākṛtaṃ tadvad dvyabhrāntirnirucyate ||
[484,2]
yathā māyāmantraparigṛhītaṃ bhrāntinimittaṃ kāṣṭhaloṣṭādikaṃ tathā'bhūtaparikalpaḥ paratantrasvabhāve veditavyaḥ | yathā māyākṛtaṃ tasyāṃ māyāyāṃ hastyaśvasuvarṇādyākṛtistadbhāvena pratibhāsitā, tasminnabhūtaparikalpe dvayabhrāntirgrāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsitā parikalpitasvabhāvākāratā veditavyā | atra bhāṣye kāṣṭhaloṣṭādikamiti pravīṇaśilpiracitahastyādisaṃsthānaṃ citritaṃ ca samyakprayuktam | loṣṭaṃ mantrādiparigrahāt vikṛtendriyajñānadharmapītādyābhāsaparikaritam | ādiśabdānmṛṇmayapāṣāṇādiparigrahaḥ | yathā māyākṛtamiti vyākhyeyānuvādaḥ | tasyāṃ māyāyāmiti kṛtrimahastyādau | upalakṣaṇametad yathoktaloṣṭe ca | hastyādīnāmākṛtirvarṇasaṃsthānam | tadbhāvena hastyāditvena, pratibhāsitā adhyavasitā, asato'nubhavābhāvāt | marīciṣu jalasyevādhyavasānamātraṃ yat tatra hastyādīnāṃ tanmāyāmātrakṛtamuktamityarthaḥ | tathā dvayabhrāntiriti sambandhaḥ |
tasyā vyākhyānam parikalpitasvabhāvaṃ grāhyagrāhakameva, tasyaivākāra ullekho'syābhūtaparikalpasya khaṇḍadvayapratibhāsāt | tasya bhāvastattā | grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsitādhyavasitā | yathā māyādiṣu hastyādyavasāyastathā'bhūtaparikalpe dvayāvasāya ityevārthaḥ |
tathā ca,
[484,3]
yathā tasminna tadbhāvaḥ paramārthastatheṣyate | yathā tasyopalabdhistu tathā saṃvṛtisatyatā ||
[484,4]
yathā tasmin na tadbhāvo māyākṛte hastitvādyabhāvaḥ, tathā tasmin paratantre paramārtha iṣyate | parikalpitasya dvayalakṣaṇasyābhāvaḥ | yathā tasya māyākṛtasya hastyādibhāvenopalabdhiḥ, tathā tasyābhūtaparikalpasya saṃvṛtisatyavetnopalabdhiḥ | atra māyākṛtaṃ māyāracitaṃ mantavyam | hastyādibhāvenopalabdhirjñānamadhyavasāya ityarthaḥ | saṃvṛtisatyaṃ grāhyagrāhakaṃ tadbhāvenopalabdhiradhyavasāyaḥ | etena mūlena viṣayeṇa viṣayinirdeśa iti darśitam |
[485,1]
tadabhāve yathā vyaktistannimittasya labhyate | tathāśrayaparāvṛttāvasatkalpasya labhyate ||
[485,2]
yathā māyākṛtasyābhāve tasya tannimittasya kāṣṭhādikasya vyaktibhūtāya upalabhyate, tathāśrayaparāvṛttau dvayabhrāntyabhāvāt abhūtaparikalpasya bhūtārtha upalabhyate | mūle'satkalpa ityabhūtaparikalpa ukto bhūtārtho dvayavivekaḥ |
[485,3]
tannimitte yathā loko hyabhrāntaḥ kāmataścaret | parāvṛttāvaparyastaḥ kāmacārī tathā yatiḥ ||
[485,4]
yathā tannimitte kāṣṭhādāvabhrānto lokaḥ kāmataścarati svatantraḥ, tathāśrayaparāvṛttāvaviparyasta āryaḥ kāmacārī bhavati svatantraḥ | atra ca kāṣṭhādiyantramātrametad bhrāntajñānākāro vā na hastī na vā suvarṇamiti niścayāditi mantavyam |
[485,5]
tadākṛtiśca tatrāsti tadbhāvaśca na vidyate | tasmādastitvanāstitvaṃ māyādiṣu vidhīyate ||
[485,6]
eṣa śloko gatārthaḥ |
[485,7]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo nābhāvobhāva eva ca | bhāvābhāvāviśeṣaśca māyādiṣu vidhīyate ||
[485,8]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo yastadākṛtibhāvo nāsau na bhāvaḥ | nābhāvo bhāva eva ca, yo hasyādyabhāvo nāsau nābhāvaḥ | tayośca bhāvābhāvayoraviśeṣo māyādiṣu vidhīyate |
ya eva tatra tadākṛterbhāvaḥ, sa eva hastyādyabhāvaḥ | ya eva hastyādyabhāvaḥ, sa eva tadākṛtibhāvaḥ |
[485,9]
tathādvayābhatā cāsti tadbhāvaśca na vidyate | tasmādastitvanāstitvaṃ rūpādiṣu vidhīyate ||
[485,10]
tathātrābhūtaparikalpe'dvayābhatā cāsti dvayabhāvaśca nāsti | tasmādastitvanāstitvaṃ rūpādiṣu vidhīyate, abhūtaparikalpasvabhāveṣu | atra ca dvayamivābhātīti dvayābhastasya bhāvo'ntarbahīrūpapratibhāsī svabhāvaḥ |
[486,1]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo nābhāvo bhāva eva ca | bhāvābhāvāviśeṣaśca rūpādiṣu vidhīyate ||
[486,2]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo yā dvayābhāsatā | nābhāvobhāva eva ca yā taddvayabhāvanāstitā, bhāvābhāvāviśeṣaśca rūpādiṣu vidhīyate | ya eva hi dvayābhāsatayā bhāvaḥ sa eva dvayasyābhāva iti |
[486,3]
samāropāpavādāntapratiṣedhārthamiṣyate | hīnayānena yānasya pratiṣedhārthameva ca ||
[486,4]
kimarthaṃ punariha bhāvābhāvayoraikāntikatvamaviśeṣaśceṣyate, yathākramam ? samāropāpavādāntapratiṣedhārthamiṣyate, hīnayānagamanapratiṣedhārthaṃ ca | abhāvasya hyabhāvatvaṃ viditvā samāropaṇaṃ karoti | bhāvasya bhāvatvaṃ viditvāpavādaṃ na karoti | tayoścāviśeṣaṃ viditvā na bhāvādudvijate | tasmānna hīnayānena niryāti ityevaṃ vistaraḥ | tathābhisamayālaṅkāre tātparyam, sattā ca nāma dharmāṇāṃ jñeye cāvaraṇakṣayaḥ | yatparairucyate śāsturatra vismīyate mayā || (a. a. ā. pṛḥ 499)
iti prakaraṇāntaravat kalpitadharmaniṣedhābhiprāyeṇābhidhāya sāmānyavacanāt prakāśaniṣedhaśaṅkāsaṅkocārthamevāha, nāpaneyamataḥ kiñcit prakṣeptavyaṃ na kiñcana | draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate || (tatraiva pṛḥ 499; u. ta. 1. 154)
iti | tatrāta iti prakāśamānāt citrāt saṃkleśakālāpekṣayā'bhūtaparikalpaśabdavācyāt svasaṃvedyatayā na kiñcidapaneyam | prāgapyabhāvādasmābhirapanītaṃ kimatra cet | asattvāpādanādanyo nihnavo nāma kīdṛśaḥ ||
sa kiñcit prakṣeptavyamaprakāśaṃ grāhyagrāhakamanākāramātmādi vā, kiṃ tu yadbhūtaṃ tad bhūtenaiva grahītavyam, nābhūtatvenetyapavādaniṣedhaḥ, bhūtameva ca bhūtatvenādhimoktavyaṃ, nābhūtamiti samāropaniṣedhaḥ | kiṃ tadbhūtamabhūtaṃ veti viśeṣaniṣṭhāṃ netuṃ madhyāntavibhāge sadasallakṣaṇamanusaran dvayamabhūtam, dvayaśūnyatādharmiṇaṃ ca bhūtamavagacchatyekakartṛkatvāt |
atrāpi vā ata iti pratyakṣaparāmarśāt prakāśarāśerapratikṣepārhatvād bhūtatvamanyasya tu kalpitamātratvādabhūtatvam, tataśca tacchūnyatāyā api bhūtatvaṃ sūcitameva | tato bhūtasākṣātkārī vimucyate, bhūtagrāhī vā | śrutacintābhyāmabhyāsakrameṇa vimucyata ityarthaḥ |
samāropāpavādavinirmuktā ca madhyamā sthitiḥ | tadeva ca yogācāradarśanamiti na vastubhedaḥ |
na hi pratibhāsa evāropaḥ | nāpi bādhamarthāmītyuktam | ye tvatrāpi pratibhāsamānamapi pudgalanirākāravedanādi grāhyatādi cāropayanti, ye cāpratibhāsamānamapyapavadanti sarvataḥ, aṃśato vā tadubhayapuruṣāśrayo virodhaḥ parasparapratikṣepaheturanarthāya | tasmādayameva śūnyatānayaḥ | yathottaratantram,
[487,1]
tatra śūnyatāvikṣiptacittā ucyante | na ca yānasaṃprasthitā bodhisattvāstathāgatagarbhaśūnyatānayavipralabdhāḥ | ye bhāvavināśāya śūnyatāvimokṣasukhamicchanti sata eva dharmasyottarakālamucchedo vināśaḥ parinirvāṇamiti, ye vā punaḥ śūnyatopalambhena śūnyatāṃ pratisaranti, śūnyatā nāma rūpādivyatirekeṇa kaściddharmo'sti yamadhigamiṣyāmo bhāvayiṣyāma iti, tatra katamaḥ sa tathāgatagarbhaśūnyatānaya ucyate ? nāpaneyamataḥ kiñcidupaneyaṃ na kiñcana | draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate || (u. ta. 1. 154; a. a. ā. pṛḥ 499)
ityādi vistaraḥ | tatra sata evākārasyālīkatāmāsthāya paścāducchedānupagamānna prathamo vipralambhaḥ śūnyatārthe | nāpi dvitīyaḥ, nirākāravedanādivad vyatiriktānugamāt, nanvatra atastathāgatadhātorna kiñcidapaneyaṃ, saṃkleśanimittaṃ nātra kiñcidupaneyaṃ vyavadānanimittamiti vyākhyātam | satyam, kiṃ tu dharmeṇa dharminirdeśāt tathāgatadhātuśabdena śūnyatādharmā cittavivartagrāhya eva grāhyaḥ, kalpanāniveśini śūnyatāmātre kasyacit prakṣepādiśaṃkāvirahāt | tataśca saṃkleśavyavadānanimittayoḥ sadasatornirodhotpādapratiṣedhena yathoktāpavādasamāropaniṣedha eva vivakṣitaḥ, yato'nantaramāha, evaṃ yad yatra nāsti tattena śūnyamiti paśyati | yat punaratrāvaśiṣṭaṃ bhavati, tatsadihāstīti yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti, samāropāpavādānna parivarjanādaviparītaśūnyatālakṣaṇamanena paridīpitamiti |
tanna prakāśarūpaniṣedhaḥ | ayameva ca madhyamārthaḥ | athavā, śūnyaṃ nāpi na cāśūnyaṃ tasmāt sarvaṃ vidhīyate | sattvādasattvāt sattvācca madhyamāpratipacca sā || (ma. vi. 1. 3)
