ityanena, sanmadhyamākhyā pratipacca saivetyuvāca madhyāntavibhāgaśāstre | sākṣādakalpaṃ yuvarājamauliḥ kimatra pāṇḍityapariśrameṇa ||
tasmādiyameva sthitirmadhyamā yogācāranayaśca vastuta iti ||
[488,1]
enāmeva cābhisandhāyāryanāgārjunapādānāmapi, ātmagrahanivṛttyarthaṃ skandhadhātvādideśanā | sāpi dhvastā mahābhāgaiścitramātravyavasthayā ||
iti ślāghā | itaradigapakṣepāt tu, cittamātramidaṃ sarvamiti yā deśanā muneḥ | tattrāsaparihārārthaṃ bālānāṃ sā na tattvataḥ ||
ityuktam | prāyaso bahirivārthaśaktyaiva sattāṃ cittasyāpi prapanno janaḥ | tathā cādya yāvad vārtikabhāṣyakārayatnairapi na prabodhamāsādayati, pratyutānyābhiprāyadūṣaṇābhyāmupakramata iti | cittamātramiti sāmānyavacanaṃ prāyastvasūcanaparam, na tu sarvathā'niṣṭyaiva, ślāghāyā niravakāśatvaprasaṅgāt | na caiṣāṃ svapnavadanutpannāniruddhapratibhāsamātrādanyatra ślāghāsaṃbhavaḥ | dharmo notpadyate kaścinnāpi kaścinnirudhyate | utpadyante nirudhyante pratyayā eva kevalāḥ ||
iti vacanācca sākāranaya evaiṣām, saṃbhogakāyavarṇanācca, anyairivopacārāderavarṇanāt |
kathaṃ tarhi, na rakto harinmāñjiṣṭaḥ ityādyuktam ? dharmakāyābhiprāyeṇa | tathā cānantarameva, advayāya namo'stute ityuktaṃ prasajyavṛttimāśritya | kiṃ ca, vande pratyātmavedyaṃ dharmakāyamiti svasaṃvedanādare'pi viparītaśaṅketidhik svātantryam, svasaṃvedanasya citrākārapratibhāsa eva viśrāmāt | tacca dṛḍhīkṛtamiti na dharmakāyādyapalāpināṃ vilāpena kiñcit | tasmād yuvarājarucitaivāryāṇāṃ madhyameti sthitam ||
[489,1]
etena yairapi, rūpakāyamadhiṣṭhāya prakṛtibhramabhāvataḥ | nirodhaścittacaittānāṃ dharmakāyāptiriṣyate ||
teṣāmapi vyavasthā duḥstheti pratipāditam | tathā hi,
[489,2]
kva rūpamātrādhiṣṭhānaṃ sarvatraiva prasādhanāt | svasaṃvedanarūpasya bhramabhāvavirodhinaḥ ||
[489,3]
tasmāt tattvato jñānamapi na vicārasaham | saṃvṛttyā tu pañcāpi skandhāḥ santa iti kuta ekaniṣedho'nyasthāpanaṃ ceti na vācyametat | kiṃ ca, keyaṃ saṃvṛtirnāma ? yadyavicāraramyāpratītiḥ, hantānantatvāt saṃvṛteḥ kva pañcaskandhaniyamaḥ ? prakṛtīśvaraṣaṭpadārthādibuddhayo'pi vividhāḥ sahajābhisaṃskārikavyāmohabhājaḥ paryante bālasyāpi prāpyacandrabimbādigocarāḥ karapraṇidhānādyanumeyāstattadvastusaṃvṛtisatyatvena grāhayeyuḥ |
evamastviti cet ? kimidānīṃ nirodhāya mārgānveṣaṇena, vedeśvarāderapi gaveṣaṇīyatvāt ? atha saṃvṛtāvapi kvacideva paritoṣalābhānna sattāśrayaṇam, evaṃ tarhi yathāvihitalakṣaṇapratyakṣānumānarūpaiva saṃvṛtirāśrayaṇīyā | tathā ca satyavāntaravyavasthāmātrametat nāmarūpamiti |
[490,1]
pratyakṣādanumānād vā na rūpaskandhasādhanam | tābhyāmeva tu bādhāsya jñānamevākhilaṃ tataḥ ||
[490,2]
kevalaṃ tatrāpyanumānameva bādhakamiti kila tatrāpi na sthitiḥ | tathā sati jñānameva saṃvṛtisat, na rūpam | tasmādāsaṃsārasthāyi jñānameva saṃvṛtyā yuktam, bādhane'pi tasya prakāśāt, anyasyāprakāśāt | santu vā saṃvṛtyā pañcāpi skandhāḥ, svayaṃ vā buddhestu nivṛttitaḥ syāt, nivartanaprayatnena vā ? nādyaḥ pakṣaḥ, sthirasvabhāvatvasādhanāt cittasantateḥ | nirālambā praśāmyatīti cet ? nanu śāntiranupadrava ucyate iti kīdṛśo doṣaḥ ? nāśo vivakṣita iti cet ? tadāpi yadyālambanaṃ viṣaya idānīmapi nirviṣayaiva tattvataḥ kathaṃ prabandhena pravartate ? saṃvṛtyā tu na kadāpi viṣayavyāvṛttiḥ |
athādhāraḥ ? nāsyāḥ kiñcidādhāreṇa, gauravābhāvāt | atha kāraṇam ? tadedānīmapi samanantarapratyayaḥ kāraṇaṃ na tadāpi vicchidyate, viśeṣato'śeṣajagatkṛpāsahāyam | kleśābhāvānna pratisandhisaktiriti cet ? hitasukhecchayāśucisthānapātalakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāra eva mā bhūt, prabandhamātreṇa tu vṛttiḥ kena vāryate, viśeṣeṇa dayāloḥ ? tasmānna svayaṃ nivṛttiḥ, prayatnastu dvayorekasya sthāpane nivartane vānyasya guṇadoṣadarśinaḥ syāt |
[490,3]
tatra jaḍarāśeḥ kīdṛśo guṇo yo na caitanyasya ? kīdṛśo vāsya doṣo yo na jāḍyarāśeḥ ? prakṛtibhrāntatvāt cittacaittānāmiti cet ? jāḍyarāśitvādrūpasyeti kiṃ nocyate ? yadi ca tāvataiva bahumānaḥ, loṣṭeṣṭakāprabhṛtayo varaṃ bhavadbhya iti kimataḥparaṃ pareṇa kartavyam ? kiṃ ca keyaṃ bhrāntirnāma ? na tāvadalīkataiva, rūpe'pi prasaṅgāt | athālīkatve'pi na rūpe bhrāntivyavasthā kiṃ tu vijñāna eva ? evaṃ tarhi paribhāṣāmātrametat | svasaṃketānurodhācca vibhāge tyāgaparigrahau | tathā ca sati rūpe'pi tathā paribhāṣya tyāgo bhavet | yadi tu vijñānamātravādino bhagavataḥ prātikūlyena tasyaiva nirodha iṣṭo na rūpasya, tathāpi kiṃ bhramatvapoṣaṇena ? mā bhūjjaḍarūpasya pratyāsattyā bhrāntisaṃbhāvanā |
[490,4]
vijñānasya viparyāsa upalabdho na jaḍaikarūpasyeti cet ? nanu viparyāso bhrama ityeka evārthaḥ, tasyaiva ca svarūpanirūpaṇamidamiti kvedamuttaraṃ saṃbadhyate ? athātasmin tadgrahādiryathāsamayaṃ prasiddho bhramārthaḥ, tarhi tadvyatyayenābhrāntirapi vijñānasyopalabdhaiva | syādetat, bhramastāvadbhrama evobhayasiddheḥ | atra so'pi bhrama eva madvicāreṇa iti ? evaṃ tarhi sarva eva bhrama iti śūnyatājñānamapi bhramaḥ | nanu na śūnyatājñānaṃ nāma tattveneti cet ? tattvato nāstīti bhavatu, bhramastu śūnyatājñānamiti kāpīyaṃ vyavasthā | api ca,
[491,1]
tattvena kiñcinnāstīti śūnyatā nāma kathyate | tattvenaiva bhramo'stīha nābhramo'stīti kāpi dik ||
[491,2]
yato vicārādakhilabhramasthitiḥ sa eva kiṃ bhrāntirathābhramo bhavet | yadi bhramo'sāvakhilo bhramaḥ kathaṃ, na cet sa eva bhramabhāvavarjitaḥ ||
[491,3]
paramārthato na kaścid bhramo'pyabhrama iti cet ? yuktamapyetat | kevalaṃ saṃvṛtau yathā skandhapañcakam, tathā kaścid bhramaḥ, kaścidabhrama ityavaśyopeyam | na hi tadāpi nīle nīlabuddhirbhramaḥ, śvete tu syāt | evaṃ rajatabuddhyādayo dvidhābhidhātavyāḥ, anyathā na rūpaskandho nāma | saṃvṛtyā ca cittacaittanirodho rūpaskandhasthitiriti vivakṣitam, tatra ca bhrama eva | tasya tu na samyagbodhaḥ, tadarthameva sarvārambhāt |
[491,4]
saṃvṛttau dvayamapyasti tattvato dvayamapyasat | bhrama evākhila iti kvedaṃ saṃbadhyate vacaḥ ||
[491,5]
atha kadācijjñāna eva bhramo dṛṣṭo na rūpa ityucyate ? skandheṣveva dṛṣṭa ityapi syāt | śāstṛsaṃmateṣu vā doṣadarśanaṃ bhagavantamapi tyājayet | avāntarabhedastu sādhāraṇaḥ | prakṛtyā bhrāntirityapi yadi sarvavyaktyanuyāyitvaṃ vivakṣitaṃ, tadānenaiva pratyuktam | atha kvacid bhrāntirbhavantyapi vikṛtirevetyarthaḥ, tathāpi kathamayaṃ niścayaḥ, ubhayasyāpi darśanāt ? tatrāgamastāvaccittasya prakṛtapariśuddhatvam, āgantukatvaṃ tu doṣāṇāmasakṛdabhidhatte, anubhūyate ca viparyāsaśaṅkayā paripīḍyamānaṃ manaḥ, samyakparijñāne ca nirvṛtamiti vibhaktaṃ sarvajñasiddhau |
[491,6]
na ca savikalpāvikalpayoranyatarāpekṣayedamabhidhātuṃ śakyam, dvayordvayadarśanāt |
ekatra tathābhāve vā tasyaiva prahāṇirastu, bhedāpratipattau vā pratipattaye śāstrāntaramanveṣaṇīyam | tadayamalakṣaḥ kṣepaḥ prakṛtibhrāntāścittacaittā iti | kiṃ ca, cittacettanirodhaśca dharmakāyasākṣātkriyā ceti vyāhatam, cittadharmatvāt sākṣātkriyāyāḥ | sākṣātkāropacāro'sāviti cet ? kutaḥ ? gatyantarābhāvāditi cet ? tatra sākṣātkāricittasthitirevāstu, kiṃ nivartanayatneneti kathaṃ gatyantarābhāvaḥ ? tadetannetramutpāṭya darśanakautukavinodanaṃ na prekṣāvatāṃ kṣamate |
[492,1]
loṣṭādayo vā dharmakāyasākṣātkāriṇaḥ, teṣāṃ prabhāvātiśayābhāvāditi cet ?
na khalu tāvatā dharmakāyasākṣātkriyā kiṃ tvadhigamaviśeṣeṇa, anyathā mantrādīnāmapi sāmyād buddhatvaṃ ca | yadyevam, abhāvātiśayasaṃbhave sākṣātkriyayā kiṃ kartavyam, maṇyādivat ? yadyevaṃ lakṣaṇānuvyañjanairapi kiṃ kartavyam ? sāmarthyaviśeṣasya maṇimantrādivadanyathāpi saṃbhavāditi na dharmakāyo nāpi saṃbhogakāya iti pariśuddhā buddhasthitiḥ | athavā rūpavadadhigamasyāpi prabhāvaphalātiśayadarśanādrūpameva nivartyamastu, sthāpyaṃ vā, dvayamapi kasyacit kenacidarthasiddheḥ |
[492,2]
sarvasāmarthyasya rūpa evāropayituṃ śakyatvāditi cet ? vijñāna eva śakyatvād viparyayo'stu, neti kośapānaṃ pramāṇam | tathāpyekasya sthāpane kadāciccittabhāgasyaiva syāt, iti na rūpasyaiva sthitiḥ | rūpasāmarthyācca jñānasāmarthyasyaiva mahattvadarśanāt tatraiva bharanyāsa ucitaḥ | kathamanyathā vijñānamātraṃ jagaditi neyam ? tasmāt pañcaskandhakasaṃvṛtipakṣe'pi na cittacaittanirodhaḥ sādhuḥ | na ca saiva saṃvṛtiḥ sarvaśūnyatāpakṣe'pi | antimā saṃvṛtirvaktuṃ saṃvṛtitve na yujyate | antyā ca jñānarūpaiva no ced dravyaguṇādyapi ||
tasmāt sākāracittasyaiva sthitiḥ svasaṃvedanasiddhaśca dharmakāya iti ||
[492,3]
yadyevaṃ svasaṃvedanasya vastuviṣayatvāt kathaṃ prajñaptisat śūnyatābhidhānaṃ dharmamātraṃ dharmakāyo bhagavataḥ | tataḥ,
[492,4]
saṃbhogakāyāditarajñānameva nirākṛti | śūnyatālambanaṃ dharmakāya ityapare viduḥ ||
[493,1]
atrāpi pakṣe saṃbhogasaṃkhyātād buddhanāmataḥ | bhidyamānaṃ kathaṃ tasya svabhāvo bhavituṃ kṣamaḥ ||
[493,2]
tasyāpi buddharūpatve dvau buddhau bhinnnalakṣaṇau | tasyaiva buddharūpatve dharmakāyo'paraḥ punaḥ ||
[493,3]
sa eṣa buddho dharmaścet tasyeti na samanvayaḥ | na dharmidharmabhāvena na sāmānyaviśeṣataḥ ||
[493,4]
saṃbhogadharmo buddhaśced buddhaḥ prājñaptiko bhavet | tato'pyanyo'tha dharmātmā dravyaṃ cet sā paramparā ||
[493,5]
dharmatā cenna saṃvittiḥ saṃvittau nīlatādivat | anākāreṇa kiṃ sā'nyāsaṃbhogasyaiva dharmatā ||
[493,6]
kastarhi uttaratantre kleśopacayāpacayātyantāpacayāt sa evāyaṃ dharmakāyaḥ sattvadhāturbodhisattvo buddha iti cocyate iti darśitaḥ ? yastatraiva, dharmakāyo dvidhā jñeyo dharmadhātuḥ sunirmalaḥ | tanniṣyandaśca gāmbhīryavaicitryanayadeśanā || (u. ta. 1. 145)
ityena dharmadhāturityuktaḥ, sa eva ca prakṛto na tanniṣyandabhūtagambhīravicitranayadeśanākhyaḥ |
kastarhi dharmadhāturapi ? etadarthamadhīṣva madhyāntavibhāgameva | yaḥ, tathatābhūtakoṭiścānimittaṃ paramārthatā | dharmadhātuśca paryāyāḥ śūnyatāyāḥ samāsataḥ || (ma. vi. 1. 15)
ityuktaḥ, tādṛksaṃmohāpohāya | tathā śūnyatāpi dharmamātramityatrāpi yadi vipratipattiḥ, dvayābhāvo hyabhāvasya bhāvaḥ śūnyasya lakṣaṇam | (ma. vi. 1. 14)
ityādyanekaprakāramanusarattatraiva tatparihāreṇa nirākāravastu kiñciddharmakāyaśabdavācyamiti svātantryametat | nanu dharmamātraṃ saṃvṛtisat, kathaṃ svavedanaviṣayaḥ ? kathaṃ vā tasya pūrveṇa sadā rahitatā tu yā |
ityādi kvacid vidhirūpaḥ parāmarśaḥ ? ucyate,
[494,1]
prasajyaparyudāsābhyāṃ sarvabhāvasthitirdvidhā | dharmimānaṃ ca sarvasminnabhāve mānamiṣyate ||
[494,2]
yadā tāvat paryudāsaḥ, yathoktam — ya eva hi dvayābhāsatayā bhāvaḥ sa eva dvayābhāva iti, tadā na svasaṃvedanena grahābhāvaśaṃkā | dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate (ma. vi. 1. 2)
ityādi prasajyapakṣe'pi dharmisaṃvedanasya na dvayābhāvavikalpotpādanādanyad dvayābhāvasaṃvedanamiti | tadartha pradeśe ghaṭasya tādātmyatadādhāratāniṣedhaprastāvaḥ śāstre cintanīyaḥ |
ubhayathāpi tadevaikaṃ vasturūpamāpadyata iti prasajyapratiṣedhena paryudāsena vā vyavahāra itimātraṃ nirbandhaḥ | yathā vā bhāvamātrāpekṣayaikāntikabhedābhedaniṣedhe'pi digambaramatāvatāraḥ ṭīkākāreṇa niṣiddhaḥ, tathā vikalpapratibhāsini vidhirūpe'pi niṣedhyaḥ tasyāpi nityādirūpasyāvastutvāt, yadarthā ceyaṃ vyavasthā, tathoktaṃ prāk | yathā vā sa eva dharmakāya iti | na cānyathā samalāmalasarvatragādicintāyāḥ kaścidupayogaḥ |
niṣyandāgrārthe ṭīkā ca, dharmadhātuprabhāvitatvād buddhavacanasyeti prastutya, sarvākārapariśuddhasya dharmakāyākhyasya dharmadhātorādhipatyena pravṛttatvāditi | tasmāt prajñaptisan dharmakāya iti na sacetasastrāsaviṣayaḥ, tathaiva yuktyāgamābhyāṃ samarpaṇāt | athavā yatra niṣṭhā niṣedhasya, vidhirūpasya tu yadavasāyo'pi tad dharmirūpāpekṣayā vastusanneva bhagavān dharmakāya iti tyajyatāṃ trāsaḥ | yathā hi pradeśe ghaṭābhāvaḥ satya iti kevalaḥ pradeśa ityarthaniṣṭhā, tathā dvayābhāvo'treti dvayena dvayatvena vā rahitaṃ jñānarūpamityarthaḥ |
etadevābhisandhāya dvidhāpohaḥ, tasya ca vasturūpe niṣṭhā | dharmigrāhi ca dharme pramāṇam iti nirṇayaḥ śāstre | tena dharmadharmiṇoḥ,
[495,1]
kalpitaṃ bhedamāśritya buddho dharmaśca tāvubhau | saṃgho nirmāṇakāyābha iti ratnatrayasthitiḥ ||
[495,2]
vastutastu buddhadharmayostādātmyameva | etena yaḥ sabhāṣyaḥ sūtrālaṅkāraḥ,
[495,3]
samaḥ sūkṣmaśca saṃbaddhaḥ kāyaḥ svābhāviko mataḥ | svābhāvikaḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ nirviśiṣṭatayā samaḥ ||
[495,4]
sūkṣmo durjñānatayā, tena sābhogikena kāyena saṃbaddha iti | tatra tādātmyameva vāstavaḥ saṃbandho boddhavyaḥ | yadi tarhi saṃbhogabuddhatāheturiti vacanāttadutpattirevāstviti cet — na, madhyāntavibhāge āryadharmahetutvād dharmadhāturāryadharmāṇāṃ tadālambanaprabhavatvāditi vacanena tadāmukhīkaraṇasya tatra prabhāvāt tathā vyavahāra ityasyārthasya sphuṭīkṛtatvāt | tathā śūnyatāsvabhāvaprastāve ṭīkā, śūnyatābhāvanāyāḥ prayojanaṃ gatidvayaprāptimārabhya yāvad buddhadharmaprāptiḥ, svaparātmano rūpadharmakāyasampatprakarṣaḥ śūnyatābhāvanādevetyevamanyadapi | pūrvāvasthāpekṣayā vā tadaṅgasya tatrādhipatyavyavasthā, yathā vikramo'sya sarvārthasādhakaḥ, kṣaṇikatā ceti | na cākāramantareṇa kvacidarthakriyopalambhaḥ | samastaśukletaradharmotpattau tasyaiva sāmarthyadṛṣṭeḥ | tattvāmukhīkaraṇasya śukladharmajanmani sahakāritvam | tata eva nirākārāt sarvasaṃbhava iti cet ? nātrāgama iti darśitam, nāpi yuktiḥ kācit | api ca,
[495,5]
pratītyabhāvaprabhave'pyayaṃ janaḥ samakṣavṛtti śrayate'nyakāritam | tamaḥprakāraḥ katamo'yamīdṛśo yato'vipaśyan sadasannirīkṣate ||
[495,6]
kṛñaḥ kartṛkarmavivakṣāyāṃ ṇic | anyakāritamanyakriyāmityarthaḥ | ākāraleśo varaṃ hetuphalabhāvaṃ santaṃ na vipaśyati | anyaviṣayamasantamīkṣate | nanvayamātmavādādhikāreṇa sūtrālaṅkāraślokaḥ | kimato'pyanya ātmavādo nāma ? nityavibhutayoranaṅgīkāranneti cet — na, citratvādātmavādinām | yataḥ,
[495,7]
kartā bhoktā ca dṛṣṭebhyo bhinno'haṃkāragocaraḥ | nirañjanastadekāvaśeṣā muktiśca yoginām ||
[496,1]
kiṃ ca, pṛthaksvarūpanirbhāsābhāve'rthakriyāyāṃ kvacidupayogānanubhavād bhavān naiva kṣaṇikatāmasya svīkuryāt | tadayaṃ niṣkalātmavat jñānamātrārthakaraṇe'pyayogyam ityāderviṣayaḥ | yadā tu nityavibhutayorapi dharmakāyasya pratipādanamāgame, tadā kimuttaram ? na ca pravāhanityatā, prakṛtinityatāyā eva nirdeśāt | tathā ca tatraiva, prakṛtyāśraṃsanenāpi prabandhena ca nityatā |
iti | atra ca bhāṣyam, prakṛtinityatā svābhāvikasya, svabhāvenaiva nityatvāt |
aśraṃsane sāṃbhogikasya, dharmasaṃbhogāvicchedāt | prabandhena nairmāṇikasya, antarddhāpya punaḥpunarnirmāṇasaṃdarśanāditi | vibhutā coktaiva yathottaratantram, sarvatrānugataṃ yadvannirvikalpatayā nabhaḥ | cittaprakṛtivaimalyadhātuḥ sarvatragastathā || (u. ta. 1. 49)
anena kiṃ darśayati ? taddoṣaguṇaniṣṭhāsu vyāpi sāmānyalakṣaṇam | hīnamadhyaviśiṣṭeṣu vyoma rūpagateṣviva || (u. ta. 1. 50)
iti | rūpagateṣvityatra mṛdrajatasuvarṇabhājaneṣviti bhāṣyam | gataśabdaśca prakārārtho veditavyaḥ | haratergatatācchīlya ityatra patañjaliḥ gatavidhaprakārā ekārthā iti | gatatācchīlya iti rūḍhiḥ | nirvikalpatayetītthaṃbhūte tṛtīyā | cittasya prakṛtivaimanasyameva dhātustathatā | tasmānnityavyāpitvaṃ mukhyamevoktam | tato yadi dravyameva dharmakāyaḥ, kathamātmavādaparihāraḥ ?
[496,2]
dharmatāyāstu nityatvavyāpakatvādi sāṃvṛtam | svābhāvye'pi yathākalpaṃ prasiddhaṃ kṣaṇitādivat ||
[496,3]
atrāpi hīnamadhyaviśiṣṭeṣviti dharminirdeśaḥ | nāpi vyāpitvābhāvādanātmavādo digambaravat, na cātmavādatve'pi nirbandhaḥ, avipaśyan sadasannirīkṣate |
iti doṣasya tadvadevāparihārasiddheriti | sattve'pi ca śraddheyasyākārabhāgastāvat satya iti durvāraḥ | sattāprajñaptimātrametat, śraddheyameva tu vastusat | ata evālīkaḥ saṃbhogātmā na bhinna eva tadāśrayaprakāśatvācca nāsaṃbaddha evetyapetāgamayuktikaṃ kāvyamātram etat | sa ca buddhanāmārtho'līko yasyāsau dharmakāyaḥ satya iti sādhvī sthitiḥ |
[497,1]
api ca, evamāśritamātratvenopasarjanaṃ, buddhaḥ prabhustu dharmakāya iti dharmasya buddha ityāñjaso nirdeśaḥ syāt | athobhayaṃ buddhaḥ, tadāpi pratyekaṃ samudāyo veti vikalpe, eko buddhastadaṃśo vālīko bhrāntaśca ityapi sādhu, bhrāntibuddhayorvirodhāt | kathaṃ ca so'līkaḥ saṃbhogātmani nirmāṇaheturiṣṭaḥ ? yadāha sūtrālaṅkāraḥ, dvayordvayārthasampattiḥ sarvākārā pratiṣṭhitā |
iti | atra bhāṣyam, saṃbhogaḥ svārthasampattilakṣaṇakāyaḥ | nairmāṇikaḥ parārthasampattilakṣaṇaḥ |
seyaṃ parārthasampattiryathākramaṃ pratiṣṭhitā svābhāvike ca sāṃbhogike ceti | evaṃ ca sati phalaṃ dharmakāyasya, hetuśca nirmāṇasya parārthasampatteḥ | svārthasampattiścāsāvasatī ca khyātīti viplavaḥ sarvaḥ | tadayaṃ saṃbhoge svārthasampattivādo'līkatāpratijñānam ākāreṣu vidhurayati |
etena śraddheyasyaiva buddhatve satyatve'pi vā saṃbhogaḥ kāryārthamādriyata iti kalpanamapāstam |
tena phalasyāṇorapyabhāvāt, kalaṅkarūpatvāt ca,
[497,2]
doṣaṃ laghīyāṃsamupekṣya kaścidāsthīyate kāryamapekṣya bhūyaḥ | pradhānadoṣabhramarāśirarthaśūnyaḥ sthavīyān kathamādriyeta ||
[497,3]
karmavaśāt tadudaya iti na yuktam | ekāntatyājyasya hi hetuḥ karmaiva nārambham arhati, pātakāntaravat | karmāparādhād bhrāntistathāgatasyetyapi subhāṣitam | tadasya sarvathoparama evāyātaḥ | kiṃ ca bodhisattvābhidhānaiḥ, nirākāratayā puṃbhiḥ sarvathā syādasevyatā | ākāropagame mukhyaṃ gajasnānamidaṃ bhavet || nirākārapratijñānaṃ nirākāraprasiddhaye | svīkāraḥ punarākāre nikāraḥ ko'parastataḥ ||
ityantaraślokau |
[498,1]
yadarthalālasatayā ca tadvāraṇaṃ, tatra kaḥ śaktipratirodhaḥ śraddheyasya ? yadi tasya kvacicchaktiḥ śaktiḥ sarvatra gīyatām | nānvayavyatirekau hi śaraṇaṃ kāraṇasthiteḥ ||
tasmānnirākāravādināṃ kevalavimalānantavyomanibhāśeṣaśaktimati rūpaṃ sādhyamiti darśanāntaramastu kimanyānuṣaṅgeṇa ? āryamaitreyanāyakanayātikrame hi kīdṛśī bauddhatattvasthitiḥ ? saṃkṣepataḥ sa hi,
[498,2]
tredhātukaṃ dhiyamuvāca vicitramatra saṃvedyavedakamiti dvayameva mithyā | ropāpavādaniyataiva nudannunāva saṃbhogamanyahitahetunijārthalakṣmīm ||
[498,3]
na ca kvacillakṣaṇānuvyañjanādiprastāve tattvato na buddharūpamidamaupacārikaṃ veti darśitam | dharmakāyaprādhānyena buddhavyavahāraprastāve'pi nāsattvameva pratipāditamupacāro vā, lakṣaṇādikaṃ cakravartino'pīti darśanāt | sūtrālaṅkāre'pi, sarvaiścitrairlakṣaṇakairmaṇḍitagātraḥ ityatra bhāṣyam, citragrahaṇaṃ cakravartyādilakṣaṇebhyo viśeṣaṇārthamiti dṛḍhīkaraṇameva |
tadatikrame ca yadapīdaṃ likhitaṃ, bhagavāṃstu prahīṇajñeyāvaraṇatvādasaṃbhavadbhrāntirādarśanajñānarūpaḥ sakalajñeyabimbodayāt pratikṣaṇamekajñānacakrātmā | ata eva cakracihnaḥ |
sarvajñeyapratibimbasaṃvedanamevāsya sarvajñeyasaṃbodhaḥ | ata eva sarvadharmasvarūpāvabodhādatiśayena buddhirasyāstīti buddha ucyata iti | tataḥ svaparameva luptam, ākārasyaiva ca bhrāntivyavasthānāt, kva praśastabuddhiyogaḥ kva vā jñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇiriti | alīkamalīkameva vettīti atasmiṃstadgrahabhrāntivādaprasaṅgaḥ | nirākṛtāyāmiti saṃvidākṛtau na mantranītirna ca pāramīnayaḥ | tadastu saiva sthitirastadūṣaṇā manojñatā svarguṇaratnabhūṣaṇā ||
ityantaraślokaḥ |
[499,1]
atheṣyata eva saṃbhogakāyaḥ, alīkatve'pi tattadarthasamarthaśca | sāmarthye'pi vā viśuddhatvādeva tadupasaṃhāreṇa dharmakāyasākṣātkriyālakṣaṇaṃ nabhonibhamavasthāntaramiti na doṣaḥ ? na, evamapyaśraṃsananityatātikramāparihārāt | dharmakāyavirahitaścaivaṃ jagadarthakārī bhagavānityāyātam | tacca virudhyate, yadāha uttaratantram, mahākaruṇayā kṛtsnaṃ lokamālokya lokavit | dharmakāyādavicalannirmāṇaiścitrarūpibhiḥ || (u. ta. 2. 53)
iti | jātakādīni nirvāṇaparyantāni darśayatīti vistareṇa saṃbandhaḥ | punaśca, sarvatra devabhuvane brāhmyādavicalan padāt | pratibhāsaṃ yathā brahmā darśayatyaprayatnataḥ || tadvanmuniranābhogānnirmāṇaiḥ sattvadhātuṣu | dharmakāyādavicalan bhavyānāmeti darśanam || (u. ta. 4. 53–4)
ityādi punarvistareṇa | atha prakṛtipariśuddhyapekṣayā dharmakāyāvicalanamucyate, tadā sarvasyaiva prāṇinastulyametaditi ko'tiśayo bhagavata evamukto bhavati prabandhena ?
tasmād vaimalyaviśuddhyapekṣayaivāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ, kevalaṃ dharmakāyasākṣātkriyākāle na jagadarthakaraṇamābhogādyapekṣamataḥ samādhivyutthāne taditi śaṃkānivṛttyarthaḥ prayatnaḥ, tathā cānābhogānirmāṇairiti coktam | evaṃ ca dehatyāgenātmavādināṃ tattvādhigamapravādaniṣedhasiddhiḥ |
[499,2]
athāpi punaḥ punaḥ samādhivyutthānābhyāmapi calanaṃ vivakṣitaṃ, tathāpi kimanena pariśrameṇa ? nanu,
[499,3]
saṃbhogakāyāt parameti śuddhau saṃbhogakāyaṃ ca tato'rthasiddhau | nimajjanonmajjanasaktamūrttermadgoriva svāsthyamṛṣeḥ kadā syāt ||
[500,1]
na caivamakṣuṇṇavidhānaḥ parārthaḥ | nāpi śāśvatī śuddhirityāstāṃ tāvadetat |
mā bhūt tundivṛttāntasmṛtiḥ | yaccoktam, dharma eva buddha iti, tatra kalpitasyāpi bhedasyābhāvād bhinnapravṛttinimittatve'pi paryāyatvāt jinamunīndrādivat, kutaḥ kāyāntaravyavasthā ? kiṃ ca paryāyatvavirodhidharmajinayostadvākyam, dharmakāyādavicalan ityādi | na hi buddhādavicalan sugata iti yuktam, buddhatvāditi tu yuktameva | ekasya ca prajñaptisthitimāha, tacca vākyam, yathā brahmā brāhmyādavicalan padāditi nidarśanāt |
tatra hi brahmaiva paramārthasan | tatpadaṃ tu prajñaptisadeva, na hi tad vastvantaraṃ kiñcana, āśrayopakaraṇātmabhāvaviśeṣe padaprajñapteḥ |
[500,2]
yadāpyupādhiviśeṣāpekṣaṃ svarūpamevācāryapadavat padaśabdavācyam, tadāpi dharmiṇaḥ pṛthagiva kalpanayā nirdiśyamānaṃ prajñaptisadeva, tathātrāpi munidharmakāyaśabdavācyayorekasya prajñaptisattvamāyātam, dharmasyaiva tathāstu nāpi ca munerarthakriyābhāvato | bhāvaḥ so'pi nirākṛteryadi kathaṃ saṃbhogajanmocyate ||
iti svavacanavyāghātaḥ | kiṃ caivaṃ munirityapi nirākāra eva syāt, tataśca dharmakāyād avicalanniti saṃbhoga eva prajñaptisan dharmakāyaśabdavācyaḥ syāditi viparyayaḥ | tasya dvayaśūnyatā dharmakāya iti cet ? tadāpi kathaṃ saṃbhogasya janmocyate ? tāvataivārthaparisamāpterityāpāditam |
[500,3]
atha vibhāgo'stu kācitkāryakoṭiḥ, saṃbhogasya kācinnirākārasyeti cet ?
vibhāgena tvasahaḥ kriyābhāvo vyavasthāyāḥ, dvayorapi samānaprauḍhitayā brahmatatpadadṛṣṭāntānupapatteḥ, prakaraṇeṣvapi tathā pratipādanābhāvācca saṃbhoge tu yathā dharmakāyo heturuktaḥ, tathā darśitameva | astu vā saṃbhoge'nyatra vā kāryagrāme kiyatyapi nirākārasya vyāpāraḥ, saṃbhogasya tu siddha eva | tataścānalīkamubhayaṃ bhavediti paraṃ saṃbandhanīyam, tat kathaṃ saṃbhogasyālīkatā lokottaranirābhāsajñānasiddhirvā samudghuṣyate ? bādhakād alīkatvamiti cet ?
[501,1]
vihāya pratibimbādi brahmadṛṣṭāntato yadi | saṃbhogālīkatā sidhyet bādhaśaktistu cintitā ||
[501,2]
pratibhāsārthakriyayoravicchedena | etenopasarjanatāpi prāguktā pratyuktā | kiṃ ca, dvayorapi sāmarthyasthitau yadā dvayaśūnyatāmeva dharmadhātuṃ dharmakāyāparanāmikāmicchet, yuvarājānurodhād vā yathā darśitaṃ prāk, saṃpratyeva brahmapadadṛṣṭāntād vā, tadā
[501,3]
kāyaśca turyo bhavet
[501,4]
śraddheya eva nirmāṇasya pṛthaktvāt | sā ca dvayaśūnyatā saṃbhogasyaiva saṃbandhābhidhānāt, tasyaiva dharmasaṃbhogāvicchedapratipādanācca | na hi svasaṃvedanādanyā saṃbhuktiḥ |
sūtrālaṅkāre'pi, kvacid dharmya cakraṃ bahumukhaśatairdarśayati sa kvacij janmāntardhi kvacidapi ca citrāñjanavarām | kvacit kṛtsnāṃ bodhiṃ kvacidapi sanirmāṇamasakṛnna ca sthānāttasmādvicalati sa sarva ca kurute ||
iti | sthānādanāśravād dhātoriti bhāṣyam | sa cānāsravo dhāturdharmakāya iti |
tatsākṣātkārasthiratā cāvicalanārtha iti sa evārthaḥ | athavā, kāyaśca turyo bhavet iti nirākārasākārakalpitādisvabhāvatrayāccaturthaśca svabhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ, abhūtaparikalpākhyavicitracittacakrād bhinnatvāt | tadeva cittamabhūtaparikalpo veti cet — na, asyārthasyopāyakārairapyanudbheditatvāt | na cāprakāśaṃ cittamacittaṃ vā prakāśamānamiti |
uktaṃ ca prāk, rūpādiṣvabhūtaparikalpasvabhāveṣviti | tathākalpitavikalpitadharmatārūpādiprastāvo madhyāntavibhāge'nusartavyaḥ | vyākhyānamanyatheti cet ? bhavatu na tu nyāyākṣarānurodhīti ucyate | kiṃ ca, evamapyākārarāśireva pṛthaksvabhāvo'līkākhyaḥ syāt | kalpite'ntarbhavatīti cet ? kva kasya kalpanā ? nirākāre ākārasyeti cet ?
apratibhāsini pratibhāsamānaṃ kalpitamāropitaṃ veti kāryadṛṣṭiḥ, prakāśe tvaprakāśam ākāre'nākāramāropitamanyavaditi tasyaiva kalpite'ntarbhāvaḥ | tasmāt, dharmatvena vikalpabhāsivapuṣā bhedābhidāvarjitoniṣpannaḥ paratantradharmyanugato yaḥ śūnyatākhyo mataḥ | sa svābhāvika ucyate bhagavataḥ saṃbhogakāyodayedharmāṇāṃ prakṛtidhvanivyavahṛtaṃ dharmākhyametad vapuḥ ||
iti prakaraṇārthaḥ | tato yadi pravacanaprakīrṇārthasaṃkalanameva yuvarājanītiḥ, tadāsphuṭatarārthagatirvacasāmiyaṃ prakaraṇāntarasaṃgatirīdṛśī | pramitibhedabalaṃ ca vicintitaṃ vivṛtayastu bhavantu yathāruci ||
tasmānna nirākāravādavārtāpi | nanūttaratantre anuttaraṃ buddhaguṇamārabhya ślokaḥ, svārthaḥ parārthaḥ paramārthakāyatā tadāśritā saṃvṛtikāyatā ca | phalaṃ visaṃyogavipākabhāvādetaccatuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaprabhedam || (u. ta. 3. 1)
iti | tatra ca svārthaparārthau dharmasaṃbhogakāyāvanūdya paramārthakāyatā saṃvṛtikāyatā ca yathākramaṃ vihite, visaṃyogavipākaphalatve ca | tatra saṃbhogakāyasya sāṃvṛtatvapratipādanam anākāraṃ paramārthamupasthāpayatīti kathamucyate nirākāravārtāpi nāstīti ? tathā ca tatraiva vivṛtiḥ, ātmasampattyadhiṣṭhānaṃ śarīraṃ pāramārthikam | parasampattyadhiṣṭhānamṛṣeḥ sāṃketikaṃ vapuḥ || visaṃyogaguṇairyuktaṃ vapurādyaṃ balādibhiḥ | vaipākikairdvitīyaṃ tu mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ || (u. ta. 3. 2–3)
iti | tadetat hitakāmatāmātraprayuktaṃ vyākhyānamātram, apāstaṃ ca prāk dharmakāyasya dravyadharmarūpatānirūpaṇe | kathaṃ ca buddhaguṇamārabdho vaktuṃ nāthaḥ parārthasādhanamasādhāraṇaṃ nirmāṇakāyamanabhidhāya nirvṛṇīta ? kathaṃ vā tatraiva, ratnavigrahavajjñeyaḥ kāyaḥ svābhāvikaḥ śubhaḥ | akṛtrimatvāt prakṛterguṇaratnāśrayatvataḥ || mahādharmādhirājatvāt saṃbhogaścakravartivat | pratibimbopamatvācca nirmāṇaṃ hemabimbavat || (u. ta. 1. 151–2)
ityanena nirmāṇasya sāṃvṛtatvaṃ vyaktamuktaṃ vismṛtya dharmakāyādapyāyasthānīkṛtānmahādharmādhipatyena cakravartitulayotkarṣite saṃbhogakāye yojayet ? yadāryanāgārjunapādā api, vande saṃbhogakāyaṃ tamahamihamahādharmarājyapratiṣṭham |
iti | tadayaṃ ślokārthaḥ | svārthaparārthau dharmasaṃbhogāvanūdya paramārthakāyavyavahāra eva vidhīyate, paramajñānaviṣayatvāt paramasādhyatvācca tayoḥ | evaṃ paramārthasaṃgṛhītakāmadvayam abhidhāya tṛtīyamāha, tadāśritā saṃvṛtikāyatā ceti | pratibimbopamatvena nirmāṇasya sāṃvṛtatvapratipādanāt | āśritatvaṃ ca saṃbhoge sākṣāt, dharmakāye pāramparyeṇeti pratipāditaṃ prāk | vivṛtāvapi paramārthaśabdābhidheyakāyadvayamādimamanūdyātmasampattyadhiṣṭhānatvaṃ vihitam | tatra,
[503,1]
lokātītāmacintyāṃ svakṛtaśataphalāmātmano yo vibhūtiṃparṣanmadhye vicitrāṃ prathayati mahatīṃ dhīmatāṃ prītihetoḥ |
[503,2]
tasyāḥ saṃbhogakāyo'dhiṣṭhānamāśraya iti vyaktam | dharmakāyastu tadāśrayo darśita eva | tṛtīyaṃ paścārddhenāha, tatra bimbopamatvena lokaprasiddhyā sāṃvṛtaṃ padaṃ mūle |
vivṛtau tu tattvato buddha iti saṃketamātraṃ nirmāṇe | na tvasau buddha eveti sāṃketikaḥ śabdaḥ |
pauruṣaphalaṃ cāsya bāhyayogisādhāraṇamatipratītamiti na pṛthak kathyate | svarūpeṇa tu trayo'pyasādhāraṇaguṇā ityārabdham ||
[503,3]
athaivamapi paramārthaśabdaḥ śūnyatāyāṃ niveśitaḥ, kathaṃ saṃbhoge'pi vyākhyāyate ?
naivamanyārthatvāt | paramajñānaviṣayatvena hi śūnyatā paramārthaḥ paramaprayojanatvācca saṃbhogaḥ svārthasampattayaḥ | tathā ca, svārthaśabda eva saṃbhoge darśitaḥ punaradhunā dharmakāye'bhidhīyate, svārtho'rtho'smāditi kṛtvā | tataścārthabhedānna doṣaḥ | nanu dharmakāyo'pi sādhya ucyate, tataśca svo'rtha iti na kṣatiḥ | satyaṃ, kiṃ tu vyavasthāmātrametat, na tu saṃbhogavannirvartyatayā sādhyatvamasyeti siddho'rthabhedaḥ | tathā ca parārthatāpi nirmāṇe sākṣāt |
saṃbhoge tu taddvāreṇetyāgame | kevalo vā paramārthaśabdaḥ śūnyatāparyāyaḥ kṛtaḥ, paramārthakāya iti tu dharmadharmiṇoḥ pramāṇasiddhinibandhano'bhidhīyate iti na virodhaḥ | kiyad vā śakyaṃ nirbandhumevaṃvidhaśraddhāvilasiteṣu ityāstāṃ tāvat | sthitametat, na nirākāravādavārtāpīti |
kathaṃ tarhi ācāryadignāgapādāḥ piṇḍārthe, kalpitasya niṣedho'yamiti saṃgrahadarśanam | sarvo jñeyatayārūḍha ākāraḥ kalpito matau ||
iti | atrāyamarthaḥ, sarvo matāvārūḍha ākāro jñeyatayā kalpitaḥ | tasya jñeyatayā kalpitasya niṣedha iti grāhyatvaniṣedha ityarthaḥ | yathā, tadabhāvāt tadapyasat ityatrācāryasthiramatiḥ, arthābhāvād vijñātṛtvena vijñānamasat, na tvarthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsatayā | tadasattve hi sarvathā abhāvaprasaṅgaḥ, tadvyatirekeṇa vijñānasvabhāvānabhidhānāt |
tadvayatiriktasvabhāvatve vā kathaṃ tadvijñānaṃ, kathaṃ vā parasparato bhidyata iti ? atra tarhi kiṃ kartavyam ? asadeva yataḥ khyāti tadavidyāvinirmitam | asatkhyāpanaśaktau hi sāvidyeti nigadyate ||
iti | sa eṣa bandhakīmṛtyuvṛttāntaḥ samupāgataḥ | kathañcidekanistāre dustarāntarasaṅgateḥ ||
yātu | atrāpi tu bhavata eva bhrāntiḥ, pūrvāparāparāmarśāt | tathā hi, tena buddhaṃ tathā bodhiṃ na paśyāmyādivācakaiḥ | āsamāpteriha jñeyā kalpitānāṃ nirākṛtiḥ ||
ityatra tvayāpi kiṃ kartavyam, yadi prakāśasyāpi niṣedhaḥ kvacidiṣṭaḥ ? tasmādavidyāśabdena vikalpa evābhidhīyate, tayā nirmitaṃ darśitamasadeva rūpaṃ bāhyamityarthaḥ | rūpaśūnyatayorhi bhedābhedaniṣedhaprastāve uktametaditi na doṣaḥ | tadayaṃ khyātiradhyavasāyārthaḥ |
[505,1]
nijaṃ svarūpaṃ pracchādya tadavidyāvaśīkṛtam | māyāvadanyathā bhātītyatra bhātiryathāmataḥ ||
[505,2]
na hi māyāhastini hastī bhātyeva kiṃ tvavasīyate | tathābhyupagame rajatādayo'pi pratibhāntīti dvaividhyavilopaḥ | ataścaivam, prajñāpāramitāyāṃ hi trīn samāśritya deśanā | kalpitaṃ paratantraṃ ca pariniṣpannameva ca || nāstītyādipadaiḥ sarvaiḥ kalpitaṃ vinivāryate | māyopamādidṛṣṭāntaiḥ paratantrasya deśanā || caturdhā vyavadānena pariniṣpannakīrtanam | prajñāpāramitāyāṃ hi nānyā buddhasya deśanā ||
ityakṣuṇṇapāramitānayārthānugamāt | na cātra paratantrasyāpyākāro'san prakāśamātraṃ tu sadityuktam, yena pāramitānayādiyatā bheda iti syāt | na ca svābhimataṃ sphuṭīkṛtya tadartho'pyevaṃ draṣṭavya ityatideśaḥ kṛtaḥ | nāpi sādhye viśeṣapradarśanamasti yena tathā unnīyeta | prajñāpāramitājñānamadvayaṃ sā tathāgataḥ |
sādhyeti grāhyagrāhakamātraśūnyatāyāḥ pratipādanāt | anyathā nirābhāsatvameva vācyaṃ syāt |
na ca sa evākāro grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ bhavitumarhati tallakṣaṇāyogāditi kalpitameva tattvaṃ bhinnaṃ vā grāhyādi | saṃbhogakāyaśca laukika aupacāriko veti viśeṣeṇa nirdeśyeta, bhagavatyāḥ piṇḍārthasyārabdhatvāt, anyatra caivamanukteḥ | vārtikaṃ cādarśa eṣāṃ kimataḥ param ? tat kimātmano'śucinā lepanaṃ parasya ? svayameva vā, kvacid guṇā eva na rūpamuttamaṃ kvacicca rūpaṃ na guṇā viśeṣataḥ | amī tvasādhāraṇayogasaṃpado guṇāśca rūpaṃ ca bhavantamāśritāḥ ||
iti viśeṣābhivyakterityalaṃ bahunā | na cāsmākaṃ yāvatsaṃbhavaṃ granthakārāśayasamarthanayatnaḥ |
ekavaṃśasaṃmatāstveta iti | tathā hi,
[506,1]
āryāsaṅgamanaṅgajinnayavaho yad bhūpatīśo'nvaśād ācāryo vasubandhurudghuramatistasyājñayādidyutat | dignāgo'tha kumāranāthavihitāsāmānyasāhāyakastasmin vārtikabhāṣyakārakṛtinoradyānavadyā sthitiḥ ||
[506,2]
āryanāgārjunapādānāṃ tu bhinnavaṃśatve'pi sādhāraṇaiva sādhyatattvasthitiriti darśitam, abādhyasvasaṃvedanasvīkārāt | tadevam,
[506,3]
kecid buddhamalīkarūpavapuṣaṃ buddhyā vihīnaṃ viduḥ saṃvidrūpamarūpamambaranibhaṃ na bhrāntamanye punaḥ | saṃvidrūpamalīkasundaratanuṃ bhrāntyā vimuktaṃ pare kecit tvenamalīkatāvirahitaṃ yadbhāti tad gṛhyatām ||
[506,4]
tasmāt saṃbhogadharmasyaiva dharmakāyasya svasaṃvedanasiddheḥ kimapareṇa ?
sa hi bhavannapi bhedādbhinnavedanaḥ kathaṃ tasya svabhāvaḥ syāt, ekadeśatve'pi ārūpyadhātusattvavat ?
[506,5]
nanu ādarśādijñānacatuṣṭayasvabhāvo bhagavān pāramitānaya eva varṇitaḥ | tat kathaṃ prastute'pi vimatiriti cet ? tatrāpi citrādvaitasthityaiva nirvāhaḥ | nirākāre hi tāvat parasparaṃ bheda eva durlabhaḥ | yadāha, kathaṃ vā parasparato bhidyata iti | bhede'pi parasparāsaṃvedane sa eva doṣaḥ | citrādvaitasvīkāre ca kimapareṇa ? atha citrādvaitamapi noktamiti cet — na, sākārajñānavāditayā tadākṣepāt, sādhanavat | na hi vārtikaprameyarāśirapi tatsādhanaikaprabaṇastatroktaḥ | tasmāt tadvadeva taduktyaiva yāvatī tasya niṣṭhā sāpyākṣiptaiva | pradīpena vā pradīpānveṣaṇa eṣaḥ | eka eva bhagavān caturjñānasvabhāva iti prastauti ca citrādvaitaṃ ca gaveṣata iti | evaṃ citralakṣaṇādyuktayo'pi vācyāḥ |
[507,1]
ataeva yadapyuktaṃ sūtrālaṅkāre, ta eva vikalpā na punardvayābhāsāḥ pravartanta ityevaṃ vyavadānaṃ paryeṣitavyamiti tatrāpi dvayābhāsā iti dvayāvasāyina ityevārthaḥ vikalpaśabdaśca nābhūtaparikalpārthaḥ, kiṃ tu kalpanārthaḥ | ataeva bahuvacanam | yuktaṃ caitat | na hi grāhyagrāhakādṛte dvayaśabdasya kvacidanyo'rtha uktaḥ | na ca tayoḥ sākṣāt khyātiḥ, kiṃ tvavasāya eva, māyāhastini hastivat | anyathā ca yadaiva sarvākārakṣayastadaiva vyavadānamiti kathaṃ saṃbhogaḥ svārthasaṃpattiriti sarvavyavasthāvilopaḥ | ākārānākārayorasatyasatyatāpratipādanābhāvācca kathaṃ tatparihāraḥ ? ataevonnīyatāmiti cet — na, anyadarthatvāt | tathā pratipādane tu nānyārthakalpanā | tathā ca tatraiva, arthān sa vijñāya ca jalpamātrānsantiṣṭhate tannibhacittamātre |
ityatra bhāṣyam, manojanyamātrānarthān viditvā tadābhāse cittamātre vyavasthānamiyaṃ bodhisattvasya nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthā | tataḥ pareṇa dharmadhātoḥ pratyakṣatāgamanam, yo dvayalakṣaṇena vimukto grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇena | iyaṃ darśanamārgāvastheti | na cātra nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāpi, tasyākārasya darśanamārgāvasthāyāṃ bhraṃśa uktaḥ | nāpi kvacid bhāvanāmārge, grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇakṣayastu sarvatra | tasmād grāhyagrāhakasaṃgṛhītaprapañcakalpanā na punarbhavantīti vyavadānaparyeṣaṇārthaḥ |
[507,2]
nanu bhāvanāmārgasaṃgṛhītāyāṃ saptamyāṃ bhūmau sābhogamanābhogam, aṣṭamyāṃ nimittavarjanamuktam, nimittaṃ cākāra eva, kimiyaṃ nāgalokabhāṣā, ācāryamuṣṭirvā ?
athākāro bhrāntinimittaṃ prapañcanirmitamucyate bhrāntyavalambanatvāt ? nānvāstāṃ tāvadākāro bāhyasyāpi sato na bhrāntihetutāniyamaḥ vāsanāmātrānubaddhatvāt tasyāḥ |
yadyapi ca sādṛśyamapi sthirabhrānteḥ sādhanamuktam, tathāpyanāryasyeti vāsanāviśeṣa evāvaśiṣyate | yadi ca kadācid bhrāntisaṃvāsāt parihāraḥ, nirākārasyaiva prathamamastu |
yadeva vā kiñcid bhrāntinimittamupapādayituṃ śakyamanākāradarśanādivat tadeva nivartyaṃ nimittaśabdābhidheyamiti kathamasyāṃ bhaṇitāvāśvāsaḥ ? svayameva ca parikalpiteṣu dharmeṣu kāryakāraṇābhāvo niṣidhyate, teṣāmalīkatvādityucyate | alīkasaṃmatasya cākārasya bhrāntau śaktiriti suvyavastham | tadālambanavikalpadvāreṇa tasya śaktirucyata iti cet ? vikalpa eva heyo'stu | sa cākāraḥ svayameva bhramo bhavatāmiti kiṃ nimittavacanena ? prabandhāpekṣayā ca sarvaheyānāṃ nimittaśabdenaiva codanaprasaṅgaḥ | nirālambanasya ca bhrāntālambanatvaṃ, na tāvat tattvataḥ | saṃvṛttyā ca bhavadapi na heyatāheturiti kimanena pūtikuṣmāṇḍasthānīyena ?
[508,1]
tasmāt prasiddha eva bhedavyavahāraheturviprayuktasaṃskāro vastudharmasaṃmato nimittaśabdena gṛhyatāṃ yadudgrahaḥ saṃjñocyate heyaśca, bhinnasya tasyābhāvāt | yadi tarhi tasyāpi svālambanavikalpadvāreṇaiva bhedavyavahārakāraṇatvameṣṭavyam, tato vikalpa eva heyaḥ |
satyaṃ, tadeva tasya hānaṃ svayaṃ sphuraṇābhāvādākāravat | yadi cākāraparihāraḥ, tadā ataevāsyāṃ bhūmāvupāyapāramitātiriktatarā bhavati, yataḥ sarvanimittānyanimittatvena pratividhyati, tatkṛtaṃ ca vyavahāraṃ na virodhayatīti na vyākhyānavirodhaḥ | tatkṛto hi vyavahāro bhedavyavahāra eva bhāṣyaṭīkābhyāṃ darśitaḥ | sa cākāravirahiṇo manorathasyāpyaviṣayaḥ | na ca tadaivākāraparibhave bhagavatāmādarśajñānasaṃbhavaḥ | laukikaṃ taditi svakapolavilasitam, āryarājasmṛterabhāvāt | kathaṃ tarhi sūtrālaṃkāre, ādarśajñānanirdeśa eva sarvajñeyeṣvasaṃmūḍhaṃ, na ca teṣvāmukhaṃ sadetyatra bhāṣyam, na ca teṣvāmukhamanākāratvād iti | nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, vastujñānaprakārāṇāmākārā iti lakṣaṇamityabhiprāyeṇoktatvāt | tadgrahaṇaprakārābhāvānnāmukhamucyate jñeyapratibimbodaye'pītyarthaḥ | etaccādarśajñānatvādeva suvyaktam | tathā cānantarameva, saṃbhogabuddhatājñānapratibimbodayācca tat ityatra bhāṣyam, saṃbhogabuddhaśca tat, jñānapratibimbodayācca tadādarśajñānamityucyata iti | tasmādarthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvādityatrāpyagrāhakatvāditi yuktaṃ vibhaktamācāryasthiramatinā | tathā cāryavasubandhupādaiḥ svayamanābhāsaśabdasyāpyanyatra nirviṣayārthatvaṃ vyākhyātamiti darśitameva ||
[508,2]
kathaṃ punarjñeyābhāve jñeyapratibimbodaya eva ? ucyate, yathā yathā pūrvaṃ bāhyato vijñānamātrato vā viśvamabhiniviśya mahākaruṇayā parārthasaṃpādanābhiprāyasya pratiparamāṇupratikṣaṇasarvākārasarvavedanapraṇidhiḥ, tathā tathaiva jñānodayaḥ | tatra ca bahirarthābhāve'pi cittasantativivartabhedena bhinnabhinnā ākārāstāvat santi, tadākārotpattisaṃvedanameva tatsaṃvedanam | na ca bāhye jaḍe'pyeṣa prasaṅgaḥ, prakāśasyaiva sattāprasādhanāt |
tataḥ santānāntaramitarasyāprakāśamapi svaprakāśaṃ sadeva | jaḍasya tu naivaṃ, jaḍatvapracyutiprasaṅgāt | yuktametat, kevalaṃ santānāntarasya sattāyāmeva ka āśvāsaḥ ? nanu tadarthameva santānāntarasiddhiḥ, iha punaraprakṛtametat ||
[509,1]
nanu gambhīrastatrāśayo nāsmākamavadhāraṇasahaḥ, tatpratibimbasaṃvedanaṃ ca sārvajñyaṃ prakṛtameva | praṇidhānaṃ hi paracittākārāpekṣaṃ, tad yadi parastathā bhavatu mā vā, mayā tu evaṃrūpeṇa evaṃparivārabhājanopakaraṇena bhāvyamiti niyatarūpabhāvanādeva tadākārodayaḥ | tadeva ca sarvavedanaṃ, tadā na kṣatiḥ | yadā tu parasya praśnākārodayastadā hanta prativisarjanākāraḥ syāmiti praṇidhireva sādhanam, tadā tadīyasattāyāmeva tathā yujyate | evamapi praṇidhestāvanna kṣatiradhimokṣasaṃbhavāt | sati ca santānāntare tathā setsyati, asatyapi svarūpādhāropakaraṇasaṃpattireva śubhasañcayasacivasya bhaviṣyatīti na sādhyakṣatiḥ | ta eva ca svākārājñeyāropājñeyapratibimbaśabdavācyā iti ||
[509,2]
praṇidhirapi kathamaniścaye ? paropadeśāt sattvādhimokṣād bādhakābhāvācca |
na ca kaścid doṣaḥ | iyameva vā svārthasāmagrīti | atra ca citrādvaitavāditayā bhāṣyakāramate buddhabodhisattvādipratikṣepāt kva paropadeśa iti nirākārapakṣapātena dveṣaviṣadharāyitaṃ keṣāścit | tatrāyaṃ mantrapāṭhaḥ,
[509,3]
dharmādharmanirāśaṃsaḥ sarvāśī sukhamedhate | yuktāyuktavimarśena śūnyo yaśca yatheṣṭavāk ||
[509,4]
tathā hi, yuvarājaprabhṛtibhiḥ sākāravāditayā ākṣipta uktaśca sākṣāt |
vārtikakāreṇa ca sādhito'yaṃ citrādvaitavādaḥ | tadbhāṣyakāraśca dūṣyate | so'yaṃ caurāparādhena māṇḍavyanigrahaḥ | athavā, bhānuṃ paribhavatyeva vicakṣuḥ saṃmukhaḥ sthitaḥ | na sacakṣustadālokānmārgāmārgaṃ tu paśyati ||
evaṃ hi vadatā na tattvaṃ na saṃvṛtirna svapakṣo na parapakṣaścālocitaḥ | tathā hi, yogācārābhimānāt svavidi kṛtapado'pyanyasattāmavaiti nyakkāraḥ ko'paro'smānnanu bhavatu tato durlabhaḥ saṃśayo'pi | sandigdhāt kiṃ phalaṃ vo bhavatu kimapi cenniścayasyaiva kiṃ vai nāśaṃsā saṃśayo'pi svavidi kathamidaṃ viddhi dhāndhyaṃ vidhūya ||
na hi nirākāramityeva puruṣakāraḥ kaścidasya yena paravedanamupanayet, sthitihāniprasaṅgāt | nāpi tadvādyapajñamupādānābhedo'pyatra saṃbhavī | śeṣaṃ samānam |
[510,1]
saṃvṛtyapekṣā yadi saṃśayārthaṃ kiṃ nārthyate niścaya eva tasyāḥ | citrādvaye cedanumāpyaśakyā citrādvayaṃ tattvata eva gītam ||
[510,2]
vicitraṃ ca citrādvaitamādarśitam | tatra cekopādhiranyatra vacanādivijñaptyā anumīyamānamanyacetaḥ kimaṅga sākāravādavidveṣādaṅgamākarṣet ? ekopādhi tu saṃvṛtāvasadeva | saṃvṛttau cānumānamanveṣase ? athavā, yāvat saṃvṛtirasti tāvadanumābādhācca satsaṃvṛtirbāhye'sāvalasāpi nāparadhiyaḥ sattvaṃ vinā prāṇiti | āsaṃsāramato'numānaviṣayaḥ śāstā parastāt punaḥ pratyakṣasya padaṃ svavedanatanormānaṃ kimanyat tataḥ || sudṛṣṭatarametat syād dṛśyate svayameva yat iti nyāyaḥ | na tadā paropadeśāpekṣā, yadāpekṣā tadānumānamanivāritam | tannivāraṇamevādvayasākṣātkriyocyate | tadapi na dūramasmākam | ākāśībhāva eva hi bhavato'tiricyate, na ca tenānumānamanyad vā | tasmād gambhīra evāyaṃ viṣayaḥ tadaniścaye'pi sattādhimokṣe yathāśaktiparīkṣitāptopadeśena pravartamāno vyavahāraḥ kathaṃ parihartuṃ śakyaḥ ?
madhyamānaye'pyayameva nyāyaḥ, sāṃvṛtatvādātmaparatādeḥ | na ca tatra paro'pi saṃvṛtau pratibhāti tāvaditi śakyam, tadāpyanumānaikaśaraṇatvāt | na ca madhyamādhīmātravādayorbhedastattvata ityupapāditametat | api ca,
[510,3]
pratibhāsopamamakhilaṃ kecit pratibhāsameva viduranye | sakalārthaśaktiśūnyaṃ keṣāñcit kiyadantaraṃ tadiha ||
[510,4]
apūrvo'yaṃ śūnyatāvāda iti cet ? yuvarājenaikena darśite'vāntarapramāṇapuruṣasaṃvādo'pyatiricyate, kimanyasāhāyakena ? uktaṃ ca candrapradīpe, bahūjano bhāṣati skandhaśūnyatāṃ na ca prajānanti yathā nirātmakāḥ | te aprajānanta pare hi coditāḥ krodhābhibhūtāḥ paruṣaṃ vadanti ||
iti | tasmādvicāraḥ śaraṇamiti so'pi yathākathañcit kṛta eva ||
[511,1]
kathaṃ tarhi sthiticatuṣṭayavyavastheti cet— ucyate | nānayorbāhyavādavad dravyata eva bhedaḥ, kiṃ tvabhinna eva vastuni pratipādye vidhiniṣedhadvāravyavahāraḥ kṛtaḥ |
sa ca vineyabhedāt | dvividho hi saṃkṣepād vineyajanaḥ, āropacarito'pavādacaritaśca, tatrāpavādacaritāśayavaśāt pratibhāsamātraparyantasattollekhinī vidhimukhena bhagavato deśanā, tāvatā vijñānanayaprasiddhiḥ | āropacaritaṃ tu prati sarvadharmaśūnyatādeśanā pratiṣedhamukhena madhyamāsthitirityucyate | sarvāropavyavacchede'pi hi citrapratibhāsamātramidamidānīmaśakyāpahnavamiti svayamākṣepāt | ucchedacaritasyāpi vijñāne sattāṃ gṛhṇato pratibhāsamātrarūpaivāsyāpi sattetyekasiddhāntaniṣṭhā, sādharmyavaidharmyavākyavat |
āropacaritasya prāyaśaḥ saṃbhavāpekṣayā tanmukhadeśanāvistaraḥ | tathā hi,
[511,2]
prakṛtivimale sarvāropaprapañcavivekini sphurati yadiha nyastaṃ kiñcittadeva suduḥsaham | niravadhirayaṃ kṣipto bhārastathā tu vṛthā paraiściramiva yathā bhāvasyātmā talena talaṃ gataḥ ||
[511,3]
ataeva vikalpitaviśeṣaṇamanapekṣya sarvameva nāstītyapi sādhu samāropaśīlaṃ prati | sa hyalasa iva gāḍhaprerito bhittau sthāsyatīti bhāvaḥ | tadanayorekavaṃśatayā tattvato bāndhavatvādamūlakaḥ kalahaḥ | yathā,
[511,4]
sarvaśaktiviyuktena prakāśena satāpi kim | śaktyabhāvānna kāryaṃ syāt svarūpaṃ tu kva gacchatu ||
[511,5]
na cātra prameyabhedaḥ, anyatra sacchabdaprayogāprayogābhimānāt | na cecchācaritasya śabdasya prayoge'prayoge vopacayāpacayāviti kalahavāraṇamapi sukaram | ye tu pratibhāsamānamapyapavadanti, citrākāramaprakāśaṃ prakāśasaṃjñitamatiriktamāropayanti, arthaśaktyādikaṃ vā sādhyamapūrvam, te'rthaśaktimātrakalpakebhyo'pi vijñānavādibhyo dūramapakrāntatvāt na bandhutvabhājaḥ | kalahaścaikaparyavasāna iti | tasmād vastuto madhyamāyogācārayorapyadvaitameva | nāpi sthiticatuṣṭayavyavasthādauḥsthyam, sarvatrāvirodhācca samantabhadratve api nānirvṛtiḥ ||
[512,1]
yat tūktam, nocet nityamidamadvayameveti | chekoktiriyaṃ nirākāranirasanaparā, itaramādhyamikāpekṣayā vā | tattvatastu,
[512,2]
nāsatprakāśavapuṣā na ca sat tadanyaṃrekena na dvitayamadvitayaṃ na tābhyām | itthaṃ jagad yadi catuḥśikharīviyuktaṃ ko bhāṣyakāramatamadhyamayorviśeṣaḥ ||
[512,3]
arthakriyāpi paramārthata eva yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ prakāśavapuṣo'pi niṣedha eva | teṣāṃ bhidā bhavatu kiṃ tu nisargadurgo mārgo'yamātmavidi sāhasabhārasāraḥ ||
[512,4]
bhāṣyakārasya ca pratirājasthānīyasyotthāpanam, paraprasiddhyā vā |
nāyakastu vārtikakāra evātra yuvarājanītiprasādhanapade saṃpratītyabhivyaktametat | kiṃ ca bhūyaḥ, yanmadhyamāmavatarannapi na svavittimullaṃghate svarucimāha yadākṛtīnām | yatkāryakāraṇaguṇaṃ ca nirākaroti rītistato nayanidherapi saiva siddhā || krūrāsaṃkhyavipakṣarākṣasamukhād yaḥ śāsanasyāvane śāsturmūrta iva prabhāvamahimācāyaḥ stutistasya kā | kasyāmandavimardamandaragirivyāpāramāsādya vā dhanyānāṃ paramārthasampadi mude durgādhameyāmbudhiḥ || potenepsitamāpyate jalanidhāvityuktimātrānvayād ārabdhaṃ śiśunāpi cāpalabalācchrutvāpi bhītiryataḥ | tattīrāntamiyād vināśamaviśan yadyeṣa mukhyaḥ sudhāsindhorasya guṇaḥ sa vepitaviyadvelāvalīmālinaḥ || sākṣātkhyātakumāramūrtimahite mañjuśriyāṃ śāstari prāpyodbhedamidaṃ padaṃ prati śiśukrīḍānukāre'pi yat | śreyastena jano'yamastu parito niryantramaitrīmayajñānaśrīvaśitopanītaparamānandaikakandāṅkuraḥ ||
<sākārasaṃgrahasūtram>
{12.1}
<prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[47]
prajñā yena khalīkṛtāmbaradaśāmākṛṣya naḥ preyasī sāsūyaṃ sadasi sthiteṣu kṛtiṣu prakhyātakīrtiṣvapi | krūranyāyamayo nirākṛtinayo duḥśāsanaḥ sāmprataṃ so'yaṃ madbhujapañjare nipatitaḥ saṃrakṣyatāṃ kauravāḥ || 1 ||
[2]
sākāretaramadhyamāsu kṛtināmutthāpya nānāvidhā vikrāntīryuvarājanāyakanaye vyakte mamāyaṃ bharaḥ | śrīnāgārjunapādasaṃmatipade bhāṣyāntimairvaṇite tannyūnādhikacintanāya saphale madhyasthabuddheḥ śramaḥ || 2 ||
[3]
sākāratvaṃ matīnāṃ bhavaśamaniyamaḥ sundaraṃ buddharūpaṃ hetorvyāpteśca hānerna tu saditi sadityeva vāstu svavitteḥ | āryācāryāvirodhaḥ praguṇaparicayo dharmakāyo nayau ca muktau sthityorabhedaḥ parama iti paraṃ śāsti sākārasiddhiḥ || 3 ||
[4]
āveṇikākhilaguṇābharaṇābhirūparūpasvavittyadhigatāmaladharmadhātuḥ | dhātutrayīhitalatānikaraikakandakandarpaketuravatādakaniṣṭhaniṣṭhaḥ || 4 ||
[5]
tatsādhanapravaṇaśāstraparamparāyā yatnādvicitramatimātrajagatprasiddhyā | dhvasto'khilastadapavādiṣu tīrthikaughastanmārgasaṃgamaguṇaprathitāstvavāryāḥ || 5 ||
[6]
eketarātmavikalaḥ kila bhāsane'pi citrākṛtivyatikaro'yamasatya eva | tatrāpi satyamaparaṃ svabidabhyupetaṃ tanmātraśeṣamavadānamiti kva nāthaḥ || 6 ||
[7]
yuktyāgamoktiyuvarājanayānugo'yamadhveti sākṛtinaye nihitaḥ pravādaḥ | vādasthitāviva vivādimatakrameṇa lekhāvidhestu sa nayo'jani viprakīrṇaḥ || 7 ||
[8]
samāsatastena kariṣyate'yaṃ tadarthasaṃgrāhakasūtrakośaḥ | parārthacaryā hi bhavennaveyaṃ svārthastu tattvābhyasanādavāryaḥ || 8 ||
[9]
prakāśo nāma na svapne'pyanākāro'nubhūyate | tato'dṛśyamatasyākṣaṃ bādhakaṃ na tu sādhakam || 9 ||
[10]
jaḍatvena guṇādīnāmadṛṣṭiḥ saviśeṣaṇā | bādhane'pekṣate tāvanna vilambaḥ svasaṃvidaḥ || 10 ||
[11]
bodhātmani site bhāsamāne siddhātha bodhadhīḥ | pratīyamāne'jāṃ vetyagavi gotvagatirna kim || 11 ||
[12]
kiṃ ca pradeśo bhinnaścedabādhyo bhedaniścayaḥ | abhede tu pradeśasya svarūpābheda eva saḥ || 12 ||
[13]
na vātātapayorasti pratighātyaṇupuñjayoḥ | deśāvibhedo buddhistu tathānveti sthavīyasī || 13 ||
[14]
pratighātātyayāntena deśābhedo'stu vā siteḥ | avayavyaṇurūpatvavikalpe saiva dūṣaṇā || 14 ||
[15]
abhedabhāsane yathā kṣaṇayorbādhakād bhidā || 15 ||
[16]
abhedabhāsanānnāsti kṣaṇayorvyavasaiva tu | asti nīladhiyoḥ spaṣṭaṃ nānyathā kvacidekatā || 16 ||
[17]
na bādhāparyudāso'sti sādhakaṃ pramitidvayam | prasajyapakṣe bādhāyā hānistāvad duranvayā || 17 ||
[18]
kadācit kenacid bādhānnīlavad veditaiva sā | bādhāsphuraṇamātraṃ tu sandigdhe vitathe'pi sat || 18 ||
[19]
tato na bhedasiddhyaṅgaṃ bhedo dharmaḥ svato yataḥ | kṣaṇayostu satorbhedaḥ kāryakālabhidā bhavet || 19 ||
[20]
na caivamekakālatve kāryabhede'pyapoddhṛte | abhedabhāsino dīpapītasyeva prakāśinaḥ || 20 ||
[21]
kiṃ ca bādhātra nātreti pṛthagbhāse dvayorbhavet | bādhāyogyasvabhāvasya vibhāgenopalambhataḥ || 21 ||
[22]
na cānākārabhāgasya pṛthagbhāso'sti nīlataḥ | deśavyāptyavasāyastu bādhake'syaiva sādhakaḥ || 22 ||
[23]
siddho'pi tatra hetuścenna samarthaḥ prakalpyate | nūnaṃ na sādhyasaṃbandho nākāre'pi tataḥ kṣamaḥ || 23 ||
[24]
bhāsanaṃ bhāsa iti ca dharmo nīle'sti bhāsini | tasya svabhāvabhūtatvād bādhābādhau samau dvayoḥ || 24 ||
[25]
na nīlasya prakāśaścet sāhasaṃ kimataḥ param | parato'pi bhavannasya prakāśo'śakyavāraṇaḥ || 25 ||
[26]
nānyato'pi prakāśo'sya prakāśo'syānya eva cet | na tannīlaṃ prakāśeta prakāśe'nyasya kiṃ phalam || 26 ||
[27]
yataḥ kuto'pi vā tasmāt prakāśo'syānapahnavaḥ | dīpena bhāsamānasya ghaṭādeḥ kiṃ na bhāsanam || 27 ||
[28]
tasya bādhoktiraphalā dharmyabādhāvakāśataḥ | yatastadbhāsanaṃ tattu bhāsamānaṃ na dṛśyate || 28 ||
[29]
yadi prakāśo nīlādiḥ kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa vaḥ | athāprakāśo nīlādiḥ kiṃ prakāśāntareṇa vaḥ || 29 ||
[30]
dhvasto'nyena prakāśo hi prasiddhamaparaṃ na ca | kasyābādhaḥ kuto hetoḥ sarvasyāśrayasaṃśayāt || 30 ||
[31]
athāsti sphuraṇaṃ tāvannīladharmastu tanmatam | tasyābādhanato bhedasiddhau siddhaṃ samīhitam || 31 ||
[32]
bhāsamānasya nīlasya tāvaddharmeṇa bhāṣayā | avaśyabhāvyaṃ tadbhedapratijñānyā paṭuḥ sahā || 32 ||
[33]
kutaśca bhāsamātraṃ tadabādhyaṃ svavidā yadi | svavittāvapi nīlādi kiṃ na bādhābhidhāvati || 33 ||
[34]
svasaṃvittirna nīlasya yadi kiṃ na prakāśate | prakāśyatāṃ pareṇeti niṣiddhamidamīdṛśam || 34 ||
[35]
asattvānna paratvaṃ cet svaṃ netyeva kuto'sya vit | asvabhāsanaśaktiśca nimīlyākṣi nigadyate || 35 ||
[36]
atha kalpitatādātmyādetadanyonyasaṃśayaḥ | bhāsaḥ kalpitatādātmyādbhāsāt tādātmyakalpanam || 36 ||
[37]
kalpitaṃ kvacidarthe ca nopayogīti saṃmatam | iyantaṃ kālamadhunā śraddheyamidamapyabhūt || 37 ||
[38]
tenānyāsaṃbhavād bhrāntivāsanopaplavānmanaḥ | alīkarūpairbhātīti prakriyāmātrapoṣaṇam || 38 ||
[39]
sādhyaśūnyaśca dṛṣṭāntaḥ svapno'līkairitīha ca | svādiḥ sahārthānnānyārthābhāsanaṃ kena kasyacit || 39 ||
[40]
avidyayāpi nirbhāntaḥ ākārāḥ santu tatkṛtāḥ | prakāśāstu prajāyante yathā dīpaḥ svahetutaḥ || 40 ||
[41]
tathāpi hetvapekṣā cet svaprakāśatvabādhanī | bhinno'pyanubhavo'nyasmādudayan kiṃ svavedanaḥ || 41 ||
[42]
tat kvacit svavido'bhāvānnāsti vyavahatirbhavet | bhaved vākārapuñje'pi samānanyāyasaṃbhavāt || 42 ||
[43]
bhāsamānasya ca bhavet svaprakāśaḥ pareṇa vā | nīlādāviti cinteyaṃ na tvabhāsinyanākṛtau || 43 ||
[44]
na ca kāryatayā bhāsamātraṃ hetibhirākṛteḥ | svasaṃbhave'nyavyāpārāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ hi kathyate || 44 ||
[45]
śaktyabhāvācca kāryatvābhāvasteneva bādhitaḥ | ākārādākṛterjanmadṛṣṭeranyatra cintyatām || 45 ||
[46]
na vā śaktaṃ sitaṃ kāryaṃ kiṃ nānyāpekṣasaṃbhavāt | śaktyā vyāptaṃ taditi cecchaktirapyanumīyatām || 46 ||
[47]
kāryatve hi na sandehaḥ śaktiḥ sādhyā tu saṃśayāt | keśākāro'pi nākāryo'dhyastakeśastvaśaktikaḥ || 47 ||
[48]
dṛṣṭā ca prāgupādānābhāve kasya prakāśyatā | prakāśadharmā nīlo'yaṃ tasmājjāto'bhyupeyatām || 48 ||
[49]
abādhayā ca bhinnatve bādhābhāvaḥ kuto mataḥ | svasaṃvedanasāmarthyaṃ saṃpratyeva nirākṛtam || 49 ||
[50]
anāropitabhāvāccedanāropamatiḥ kutaḥ | abādhayānāropaścedetadanyonyasaṃśrayam || 50 ||
[51]
prakāśasya prakāśatvaṃ nāropyaṃ rūpameva tat | nīlasyāpi na nīlatvamāropyaṃ rūpameva tat || 51 ||
[52]
na prakāśaṃ vinā nīlaḥ prakāśastaṃ vināpi cet | anyo'pi vyāpako dharmaḥ kalpitaḥ ko na tādṛśaḥ || 52 ||
[53]
na ca prakāśaḥ pīte'pi nīla eva sthito hi yaḥ | sāmānyamanyathākasmādakasmādvinivāryate || 53 ||
[54]
anyatve ca yathā nīlaṃ na prakāśaṃ vinā tathā | narte nīlāt prakāśo'sau saprakāśo'tha sākṛtiḥ || 54 ||
[55]
mithaśced vyabhicāreṇa bhedo nīlotpalena kim | vastrodake'pi bhedaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na rūpanirūpaṇāt || 55 ||
[56]
bīje'pi kālabhedena tarjanyā bhedarūpaṇe | mānena bhedo'bhedo vā naivaṃ nīlaprakāśayoḥ || 56 ||
[57]
nīladharmaḥ prakāśo'smānna bhedyo bhedinaḥ punaḥ | kalpitasya sa evātmā bhaṇyate bhāsino na kim || 57 ||
[58]
kalpitaṃ tasya jātyāde rūpaṃ kiṃ na tadeva tat | pramāṇena tu tatsatyamasatyaṃ veti cintyate || 58 ||
[59]
tena bhāne'pi nīlādiralīko vastusanmataḥ | ayogād bādhakasyeti vibhāgaḥ kiṃ kṛto bhavet || 59 ||
[60]
na vā tasya pramāsiddhaḥ śaktiyogo'pi saṃbhavī | ākṛtiṃ vākṛtereva sāmarthyasyopalambhataḥ || 60 ||
[61]
viruddhadharmādhyāsācca na vinā bhedasādhanam | dharmau viruddhau bhinnādhikaraṇau yadi sidhyataḥ || 61 ||
[62]
deśakālākṛtikṛto bhedo'dhikaraṇasya ca | na saṃbhavī nīladhiyostat kva dharmavirodhivat || 62 ||
[63]
deśakālapratībhāsabhedābhāve'pi bhedanam | nīlotpalādāviva tad bhavato yadi sidhyati || 63 ||
[64]
antaḥ sphuratsukhādyeva svasaṃvedyaṃ mano yadi | nīlādyākāravirahādanākāraṃ ca saṃmatam || 64 ||
[65]
pratibhāsād yadi jñānaṃ sukhaṃ so'sti siterapi | abhedena prakāśaścet sukhasyaivaṃ siterapi || 65 ||
[66]
yathā bhinnaṃ sukhānnīlaṃ nīlād bhinnaṃ tathā sukham | yathā nāhaṃ mataṃ nīlaṃ tathā nāhaṃ mataṃ sukham || 66 ||
[67]
ahaṃ sukhīti vyavahṛnnāhaṃ nīlīti cenmatiḥ | vyavahārabhāvābhāvau nārthasādhanabādhanau || 67 ||
[68]
sādhāraṇyābhimānena na bhavedapi sā sthitiḥ | tathāpi kvacidastyeva gomān daṇḍī dukūlavān || 68 ||
[69]
antaḥ śātādiviṣayaṃ bahiḥ śītādigocaram | vedanaṃ tattadākāraṃ bādhakagrastameva ca || 69 ||
[70]
hānāddeśavitānasya bādhakāsaṃbhavaḥ kila | doṣo deśe'ṇumātre'pi kiyatyalpe vihanyate || 70 ||
[71]
kutrāpyavartamānasya kadācinna hi vartanam | tadasya vidyamānatvaṃ sukhādeḥ sādhu sādhitam || 71 ||
[72]
vidyate yadi kutrāpi deśastasya sa eva hi | śarīrādabahirbhūtā vedyante ca sukhādayaḥ || 72 ||
[73]
mānaṃ hastavitastyādi jñāyate niyataṃ na cet | tataḥ kiṃ bhūbhujāmeva bhūmānaniyamo'rthavān || 73 ||
[74]
sparśanāt spṛśyarūpābhyāṃ cānyatra viṣayendriye | na mānaniyamo'stīti tatrāpi kimabādhanam || 74 ||
[75]
yatrāpi niścayo māne śakyastatrāpi nāṇuśaḥ | niścaye'pyaṅgulādīnāṃ tattvato na mitistataḥ || 75 ||
[76]
taḍāgagāhane vyaktaṃ taptasyordhvādharāditaḥ | sukhamānaṃ sphuṭatvena tatrāropyo na cānyataḥ || 76 ||
[77]
tatsparśanendriyadvārā mitestaddeśatāmatiḥ | ityapi dhvastamiyatā bhramatvādasphuṭāptitaḥ || 77 ||
[78]
indriyabhrāntireṣā cet na tato'nyasukhātyayāt | idameva hi naḥ saukhyaṃ yatśātaṃ vedanaṃ sphuṭam || 78 ||
[79]
rūpādiṣvapi vā kāsthā cakṣurādīndriyāśrayāt | tathāpratīterākhyātuṃ śakyatvādaparaṃ samam || 79 ||
[80]
nirbhāsaniyamājñāne yadyadeśāḥ sukhādayaḥ | kṣaṇarūpāparijñānādakālaṃ sakalaṃ jagat || 80 ||
[81]
yathā niyatakālatvaṃ tathā niyatadeśatā | bādhakāvañcanāt tasmānnirākṛtigirātra kim || 81 ||
[82]
astu vā bādhakābhāvaḥ sattāśvāsastu kiṃkṛtaḥ | eketaratvayorekasthityasiddheradeśataḥ || 82 ||
[83]
na cādarśanamātreṇa bādhābhāvo'pi sidhyati | ekabādhaviyoge'pi syād vā bādhāntarodayaḥ || 83 ||
[84]
anumānādabādhyatvasādhane yadi sādhanam | kathañcidāśrayāsiddhidūṣaṇaṃ nātivartate || 84 ||
[85]
duḥkhadveṣādayo'pyevaṃ svabhāvāḥ sarvadehinām | hānaṃ svato'pyaniṣṭeścedasato'pīcchayā sthitiḥ || 85 ||
[86]
yad yathā bhāvyate cetaḥ tat tathaiva sphuṭībhavet | vyomākāramapi syāccenna prayojanahānitaḥ || 86 ||
[87]
saṃsāradoṣairaspṛṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇavyañjanojjvalam | ātmabhāvaṃ vihāya tvaṃ vihāyastvaṃ yadīcchasi || 87 ||
[88]
yadi tāvat khavad vyāpi tadvadevāsya dūṣaṇam | jyotsnātaḍinmaṇijvālāsphuliṅgāditulāsvapi || 88 ||
[89]
sāṃśe'vayavivad doṣo niraṃśe paramāṇuvat | na cāparaḥ prakāro'sti mudhaivādeśadhoṣaṇam || 89 ||
[90]
guṇāstadekaniyatāstadekaniyatā ruciḥ | tadekaniyataṃ mānaṃ bādhenaiva samaḥ paraḥ || 90 ||
[91]
para eva jino yeṣāṃ taiḥ svaśāstāpi hāritaḥ | śṛjukramagṛhīto ya āgamāllakṣaṇojjvalaḥ || 91 ||
[92]
yena rūpeṇa yannaikaṃ nānekaṃ tena tanna sat | yathā śātamaśātena bhāsaśca sitinā tathā || 92 ||
[93]
na dharmo dharmiṇo bhettuṃ śakya ityuktameva hi | na ca bhinnasya bhānasya nyāyenānena sādhanam || 93 ||
[94]
yadi nāma na nīlena prakāśasyāsti vastutā | tathāpi bhinnabhānasya vastutvaṃ kena sidhyati || 94 ||
[95]
bandhyāsuto'gnirūpeṇa naikāneko na tena san | tatastasyāpi vastutvaṃ kimastu bhavato miteḥ || 95 ||
[96]
na san bandhyāsutaḥ siddhaḥ prakāśaḥ siddha eva san | asiddho bheda evāsya sādhyate cet tadapyasat || 96 ||
[97]
tattvataḥ satyarūpeṇa siddhirbhedasya cenmatā | sā na siddhā na hi vyāpiviraho nāstyavastuni || 97 ||
[98]
pratītimātraṃ siddhiśced bhinno'pyevaṃ na tāttvikaḥ | vyāvahārikabhedastu kiṃ na pītasitasya te || 98 ||
[99]
yadi prakāśasattāṃ ca bādhakāvasaraṃ hanan | sādhayet tāvataivāstu bhedo mānamidaṃ vṛthā || 99 ||
[100]
tadaśaktāvapi vyarthametat śauṭīryajṛmbhitam | parasyopagamaḥ saṃpratyapramā kathamāśrayaḥ || 100 ||
[101]
nīlabhāsorabhedāvabhāsinoḥ prastutā ca bhit | na caivamanvayaḥ śakyastathā sādhyamataḥ katham || 101 ||
[102]
yena naikamanekaṃ yaditi sāmānyato'nvaye | pītena naikāneko'stu nīlabhāso na tena san || 102 ||
[103]
anukto'pīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhya ātmārthavanmataḥ | viśeṣeṇānvayastasmāt sāmānye siddhasādhanam || 103 ||
[104]
yathā śātamaśātena bhinnenaivātadātmakam | tajjātinaiva pītenanīlabhāso'stu tādṛśaḥ || 104 ||
[105]
naikānekaprakāśaśca nīleneti yadocyate | kastadāstu prakāśārtho dharmamātraṃ yadīṣyate || 105 ||
[106]
dharmirūpādabhinnasya tasya tenaiva sā sthitiḥ | aikyānaikyaṃ prakāśasya nīlenaivetyasiddhatā || 106 ||
[107]
tasyāpi naikyānaikyaṃ cedanekānto'pi vāñchate | piṇḍena naikānekaṃ sad vastusad gotvamastu kim || 107 ||
[108]
kartṛsādhanapakṣe'pi doṣa eva duruddharaḥ | prakāśamānarūpaṃ hi śūnyaṃ tenātmanā bhavet || 108 ||
[109]
arthāntaraṃ prakāśākhyaṃ yadi sānvayasaṃjñakam | nīlādibhyo'tiriktasya na sattāsya phalaṃ na ca || 109 ||
[110]
niranvaye ca hetūnāmāśrayāsiddhiratra te | vyāvṛttimātrasiddhau ca prastute'nupayogitā || 110 ||
[111]
pratyakṣaprativedyo'yaṃ prakāśo dharmakāri cet | pratyakṣagocaro dharmī nīlādanyo na vidyate || 111 ||
[112]
paratvameva cet sādhyaṃ tat siddhaṃ kathamarthyate | sādhyaṃ tava kimapyastu dharmī kāryastvidantayā || 112 ||
[113]
pariniṣṭhita evārtho vasturūpo yadā mataḥ | vyavacchedadvaye niṣṭhānapekṣāyāṃ phalaṃ na vaḥ || 113 ||
[114]
nanu prakāśaḥ sāmānyaṃ dharmi kiṃ bhedaniṣṭhayā | viśeṣaniṣṭhayā sādhyavidhūteśca na tacchramaḥ || 114 ||
[115]
sa niṣṭhitaviśeṣo'pi vivādapadameṣa yaḥ | dharmī tadekā vyāvṛttiranyā sādhyaṃ dhvanāviva || 115 ||
[116]
yukto vyāvṛttimātreṇa sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ | dharmirūpaṃ tu bhedena dṛṣṭamevopayujyate || 116 ||
[117]
sāmānyadharmayoreva vyāptiḥ śakyapratītikā | ayamevamitītthaṃ tu dharmī sarvatra bhedabhāk || 117 ||
[118]
sāmānyāśrayaṇaṃ yatra tatrāvaśyamapekṣate | viśeṣadarśanaṃ siddhiḥ sāmānyasyaiva nānyathā || 118 ||
[119]
na viśeṣaṃ vinā kvāpi sāmānyasya vyavasthitiḥ | no cedabandhyātanayavyāvṛtteśca samānatā || 119 ||
[120]
bhedaḥ sādhyasya dṛṣṭānte hetoḥ pakṣasapakṣayoḥ | sāmānyasyāpyavaśyopadeśyo dharmī tvidantayā || 120 ||
[121]
vyaktibhedāḥ kṣaṇitvāderapyamī eva saṃmatāḥ | prasiddhavyaktibhedaśca śabdo dharmī tathāparaḥ || 121 ||
[122]
aprakāśaparāvṛttistadvadevātra darśyatām | idantayā yadi puro darśyetākāra eva saḥ || 122 ||
[123]
tataḥ prakāśaḥ sāmānyaṃ nīlādyevetivādinā | svīkṛte vividiṣyante sasvātmādini dūṣake || 123 ||
[124]
siddhe dharmiṇi sandigdho dharmaḥ sādhanamarhati | dharmirūpaviśeṣasya niṣṭhāyāṃ tu hato hataḥ || 124 ||
[125]
kṣaṇikatvādirapyevaṃ yadi dharmiṇi niṣṭhite | hanyeta sādhayet kastaṃ saṃśayārthasya sādhanam || 125 ||
[126]
yena rūpeṇa yannaikaṃ nānekaṃ tena tanna sat | yathā śātamaśātena prakāśenāsitaṃ tathā || 126 ||
[127]
vidyududdyotasaṃkāśaḥ prakāśaḥ kasyacit kvacit | tamapekṣya sthiro bāhyaḥ prakāśe'līkatā tataḥ || 127 ||
[128]
alīkanīlajanane yathā śaktirmatā dhiyaḥ | alīkabodhajanane tathā śaktirna kiṃ bahiḥ || 128 ||
[129]
naikaṃ tvayāpyaniṣṭerityetaduktaṃ na labhyate | īdṛksādhanamajñātvā mamāniṣṭiryato'bhavat || 129 ||
[130]
prakāśaḥ kevalonāpi kvacit kenacidīkṣitaḥ | tato'numānapratyāśā pratyāśaiva hi kevalā || 130 ||
[131]
tenaikānekahāniścet svenaikānekasaṃbhavaḥ | tataḥ svena sthitiḥ sādhyā hetvasiddhistathāpi vaḥ || 131 ||
[132]
viparyayavivakṣā cet yad yad yenātmanā hi sat | tattat tenaikānekaṃ vā bhāsaśca svena sanniti || 132 ||
[133]
nādye dṛṣṭāntasadbhāvo bhāsa eva hi saṃmataḥ | na pakṣe copasaṃhāro vivādāt prakṛtaṃ na ca || 133 ||
[134]
yo bhramaḥ sarva evāsau dvicandrapratibhāsavat | satyasaṅgī bhramaścāyaṃ dvaitābhāsa itītare || 134 ||
[135]
khaṇḍadvayākāratayā janma vā dvaitabhāsanam | grāhyagrāhakarūpāvasāyau veti vivakṣitam || 135 ||
[136]
atasminnatadākārā vedye sati matirbhramaḥ | sarvathā vedyahānau tu na bhramo nāma tattvataḥ || 136 ||
[137]
yat kiñcidatathābhūtaṃ tathā bhāvena kalpyate | kīdṛk tasyāparādho'stu kalpakasya tu yujyate || 137 ||
[138]
kalpako'pi na kaściccedbhramo nāma na kaścana | tannāsiddhatayā heturvyavahārādatha bhramaḥ || 138 ||
[139]
vyavahārādavitathaṃ bahireva kathaṃ bhramaḥ | abahirvyavahāre tu yadāropastadā bhramaḥ || 139 ||
[140]
āropātikrame yasmāt tattva eva vyavasthitiḥ | bādhanād vitathatvena bhramastadapi kiṃ bhramaḥ || 140 ||
[141]
bhāsane'līkamityastu bhramatvaṃ vā kathaṃ bhavet | atasmiṃstadgrahābhāvādanalīkamateriva || 141 ||
[142]
dvicandrapratibhāse'pi bhramatvaṃ yacca viśrutam | dvicandragrāhicittasya tanna candradvayasya tu || 142 ||
[143]
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena kalpite'śadvaye dhiyaḥ | grāhakāṃśe pramāṇatvaṃ grāhyāṃśe bhramatā katham || 143 ||
[144]
vedyatve vedakatve ca vyatīte bhāsamātrakam | bodhakagrastamapyetadasatyaṃ syānna tu bhramaḥ || 144 ||
[145]
vedakābhimatatvena bhramatvaṃ vyāptamiṣyate | tadvirodhinyaveditve bhramatvaṃ dūrato hatam || 145 ||
[146]
anyathādhyavasāye tu bhramatve nirvikalpakam | na bhramastena tenaiva satyasaṅgitvamastu ca || 146 ||
[147]
yad yatrāvasthite'paiti tat tadbhinnaṃ paṭāmbuvat | prakāśe'vasthite'paiti nīlādīti pare viduḥ || 147 ||
[148]
yad yatrāvasthite'paiti tat tadbhinnaṃ paṭāmbuvat | gotve cāvasthite'paiti citrādītyapi gīyatām || 148 ||
[149]
atha gotvamago'pohastat taddharmo'nvayī katham | bhāso'pi bhāsināṃ dharmo nīlādīnāṃ kimanvayī || 149 ||
{12.2}
<dvitīyaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[1]
nāpyāgamād gamayituṃ śakyaṃ cittamanākṛti | na pratyakṣapratikṣipte pramāṇāntarasaṃgatiḥ || 1 ||
[2]
na ca pravacane'pyasya bodhakaṃ mukhyamakṣaram | lokaḥ svābhiniveśaṃ tu tatraiva pratibimbayet || 2 ||
[3]
vāsanāluṭhitaṃ cittamarthābhāsamiti śrutau | luṭhatiḥ śleṣaṇārtho'yaṃ nopaghātārthaloṭhitaḥ || 3 ||
[4]
vinārthamarthābhāsā dhīḥ kathamityatra kathyate | vāsanāyogata iti samanantaraśaktitaḥ || 4 ||
[5]
vyatirekīva nirdeśo na ca bhedasyavedakaḥ | suvarṇa kuṇḍalākāraṃ karotīti na kiṃ vacaḥ || 5 ||
[6]
vāsanopahatatvaṃ cāniṣṭarūpodayānmatam | pravṛttyākṣepi saṃkalpasūtisāmarthyagarbhataḥ || 6 ||
[7]
advaitaśikharārohe na pravṛttinivṛttayaḥ | tā eva saṃsāra iti taddhetuḥ kathamiṣyatām || 7 ||
[8]
vineyacittāmukhatāvasthāpekṣamidaṃ vacaḥ | tenārthābhāsamityetat sāmānyaṃ bhedadhiṣṭhitam || 8 ||
[9]
darpaṇe dṛśyate rūpamiti bālābhimānataḥ | anūdya vedanākāre tadāropanivāraṇam || 9 ||
[10]
tathā bhāveṣu bhāvatvaṃ jñānakāreṣu bāhyatā | yathā timiriṇā dṛṣṭaścandrayoścandratāsatī || 10 ||
[11]
nimnoccavirahād bāhyenaikatvaṃ nāsti darpaṇe | nāntaḥpraviṣṭanirbhāsāt pṛthaktvaṃ pratipātinā || 11 ||
[12]
bhāvairākārasaṃjñairvā lakṣyate bodharūpatā | sāmānyaṃ jñānasaṃkhyātamata evāpṛthagvacaḥ || 12 ||
[13]
loke rūḍhaṃ pṛthagiva jñānamādarśasannibham | ākārāḥ pratibimbābhā ubhayoḥ kalpitaṃ na sat || 13 ||
[14]
bodhasya naikatā bāhyaiḥ svarūpavirahāptitaḥ | nānyatvamagrahaprāpterna sattā cāprakāśinaḥ || 14 ||
[15]
śṛjukrameṇa cādarśe ekānekatvavarjitam | iti yuktaṃ na bhāvāśca yujyante darpaṇopamāḥ || 15 ||
[16]
sarvadharmāḥ svadhīreva sthitāścitte samāhite | abādhyāṃ kalpitairdharmaiḥ śūnyatāmāśritā yataḥ || 16 ||
[17]
tatprakāśatayā cittaṃ svamevaite sitādayaḥ | kalpitāstvaprakāśatvānna dharmā na ca dharmatā || 17 ||
[18]
śūnyatākhyā yathā bhāti vikalpe bhedinīva sā | bhinnayā hi tayā śūnyā dharmairdharmā na tairamī || 18 ||
[19]
bāhyagrāhasya hāne'pi grāhakasthitivāraṇam | tathatārambaṇe sthitvā cittamātravyatikramaḥ || 19 ||
[20]
āropyahānādāropaviṣayasyāpi mā sma bhūt | citrasyocchedadṛkpāta ityanābhāsavāraṇam || 20 ||
[21]
nirābhāse sthito yogītyābhāsaḥ kalpanā matā | ekāpohena yattasyāmīṣadābhāsate bahiḥ || 21 ||
[22]
samantabhāsādābhāsaḥ prapañco vā kadambavat | vicitrakalpanārūḍho heyaścitre'pi cetasi || 22 ||
[23]
tadāgantumaladhvaṃsāt tadākāśatalopamam | jñeyenābhitulā jñeyanirviśiṣṭatayā sphuṭā || 23 ||
[24]
prakāśamātraṃ tadidaṃ dīpasantānasannibham | aprakāśāṅgavirahānna svākāraprakāśanāt || 24 ||
[25]
aprakāśakaṇasyāpi na pūrvamapi saṃbhavaḥ | bhramavyavasthāpekṣā tu samalāmalatāsthitiḥ || 25 ||
[26]
bādhe nāma nimittānāmākārasya ca na kṣatiḥ | nāmamātraṃ munerdharmāḥ santu vā kalpitātmanā || 26 ||
[432]
dṛṣṭā vikalpākāre'pi dṛṣṭatākhyātibhātayaḥ | kathaṃ paśyasi saṃkhyāṃ bho bhāvite pratibhāsate || 27 ||
[28]
nirābhāse sthitivato'pyavikalpasthitirmatā | satokhyānamasatkhyānaṃ vyākhāta iyatā bhramaḥ || 28 ||
[29]
avaśyādeyametacca sato'khyānaṃ kimanyathā | parāsphūrtau na hi bhrāntiḥ svāsphūrtau ca na cittatā || 29 ||
[30]
agrāhyagrāhakasyātaḥ svasya nāvasitiḥ sataḥ | avasāyo'sato grāhyagrāhakasyāpyato bhramaḥ || 30 ||
[31]
tathācābhūtakalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate | na grāhyagrāhakādanyad dvayaśabdena cocyate || 31 ||
[32]
abhūtaparikalpāstu cittacaittāstridhātukāḥ | vihāya citrākāraṃ ca kā tridhātuvyavasthitiḥ || 32 ||
[33]
na cākārātirikto'ṃśaścittamāpāditaṃ kvacit | vaibhāṣikamatikramya sthitireṣā hi dūrataḥ || 33 ||
[34]
abhūtaṃ kalpyate yatra yena vā pṛṣṭhyakalpataḥ | abhūtaparikalpo'sau buddhiścitraiva yujyate || 34 ||
[35]
abhūtadvitayāropāpekṣayānvayasaṃgateḥ | adṛśye tvatiriktāṃśe nāropo nāma kasyacit || 35 ||
[36]
kalpitaṃ ca dvayaṃ tāvannīlameva na bhāsanāt | ataḥ svabhāvastu yo'pi vaktavyaḥ kalpitādiṣu || 36 ||
[37]
kalpitaṃ sphuradeveti sāhasaṃ kimataḥ param | marīciniścaye'pyambhaḥ kalpitaṃ sphuradastu kim || 37 ||
[38]
tathābhyupagame pāthaḥkāryaṃ tenābhidhīyatām | asattvānnaivamiti cet, yadasat tat kathaṃ payaḥ || 38 ||
[39]
āropāditi cet tarhi bhavatvāropamātrakam | na tu svabhāvasphuraṇaṃ sphuraṇe tatkriyāptitaḥ || 39 ||
[40]
satyataiva prasajyeta tathā bādhāpi kiṃkarī | bādhayā tatkriyāhānau, na payastatkriyaṃ hi tat || 40 ||
[41]
tatpāthaḥ kathamārope sphuratīti nigadyate | grāhyagrāhakayorevamāropaḥ sphuraṇaṃ na tu || 41 ||
[42]
svaprakāśasvabhāvatvād bhāgayorubhayorapi | kiṃ grāhyaṃ grāhi vā kiṃ syāt svasvalakṣaṇahānitaḥ || 42 ||
[43]
sphuradeva tato rūpaṃ svabhāvo'stu turīyakaḥ | adṛśyātmani dṛśyasya kalpanetyapi kāpi dhīḥ || 43 ||
[44]
citre ca paratantro'to dhīḥ kalpitavikalpitā | dharmatārūpanirṇītau vyaktametacca lakṣaya || 44 ||
[45]
kalpitasya dvayasyaiva paratantrasya bhāsinaḥ | ropāpavādau madhyāntavibhāge vihatāvataḥ || 45 ||
[46]
sūtrālaṃkāramāryīyaṃ bhāṣyayuktaṃ ca cintaya | yatra rūpādirākhyātaḥ paratantraparisphuṭaḥ || 46 ||
[47]
tadākṛtiśca tatrāsti tadbhāvaśca na vidyate | tasmādastitvanāstitvaṃ māyādiṣu vidhīyate || 47 ||
[48]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo nābhāvo bhāva eva ca | bhāvābhāvāviśeṣaśca māyādiṣu vidhīyate || 48 ||
[49]
tathādvayābhatā cāsti tadbhāvaśca na vidyate | tasmādastitvanāstitvaṃ rūpādiṣu vidhīyate || 49 ||
[50]
na bhāvastatra cābhāvo nābhāvo bhāva eva ca | bhāvābhāvāviśeṣaśca rūpādiṣu vidhīyate || 50 ||
[51]
samāropāpavādāntapratiṣedhārthamiṣyate | hīnayānena yānasya pratiṣedhārthameva ca || 51 ||
[52]
rūpādiṣviti cābhūtaparikalpātmakeṣviti | bhāṣyīyavivṛtiṃ paśya tasya vistarameva vā || 52 ||
[21]
nāpaneyamataḥ kiñcidupaneyaṃ na kiñcana | draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate || 53 ||
[54]
pratyakṣavastuviṣayo vimarśo'yaṃ yadīṣyate | na citrādanyadadhyakṣaṃ yatnaḥ śāstradvaye'pyayam || 54 ||
[55]
dharmadhātuvimarśoktau dharmī dharmagiroditaḥ | tathā cānantaragirā vyaktametaditīritam || 55 ||
[56]
ataeva ca dharmasya paścācchedo hi nirvṛtiḥ | doṣo'yaṃ svīkṛto'līkanāmnākārakṣayaspṛhaiḥ || 56 ||
[57]
śūnyatā nāma dharmo'sti rūpādivyatirekataḥ | yo bhāvya ityupālambhalābho'nākāravādinām || 57 ||
[58]
arthān sa vijñāya ca jalpamātrān santiṣṭhate tannibhacittamātre | ityāha nirvedhapathe'tha dṛṣṭau pratyakṣatāptiṃ khalu dharmadhātoḥ || 58 ||
[59]
grāhyagrāhakarūpeṇa yo dvayena vivarjitaḥ | iti tasya viśeṣaṃ ca na tvākārakṣayaṃ kvacit || 59 ||
[60]
dvayalakṣaṇahānistu sarvatreti parisphuṭam | na grāhyagrāhakatvaṃ cākṛtīnāmata eva ca || 60 ||
[61]
dvayābhāsāḥ pravartante na vikalpāḥ punaśca te | vyavadānārthanetyatrāpyābhāso'dhyavasāyitā || 61 ||
[62]
sarvajñeyeṣvasaṃmūḍhaṃ na ca teṣvāmukhaṃ sadā | ityatra vivṛtau heturanākāratayeti yaḥ || 62 ||
[63]
grāhyaprakārābhāvenetyartho bimbodaye'pi hi | etaccānantaraṃ mūlabhāṣyayorīkṣaṇe sphuṭam || 63 ||
[64]
evaṃ madhyāntabhāgasya mūle bhāṣye'pi īdṛśe | agrāhakatvādityartho vibhaktaḥ sādhu ṭīkayā || 64 ||
[65]
tathā ca tadbhāṣyakṛtādharmadharmatayonnaye | avikalpakavijñānalakṣaṇaprakrame svayam || 65 ||
[66]
arūpīti padaṃ grāhyagrāhitvenānirūpaṇāt | anābhāsamitīdaṃ cāgocaratvena varṇitam || 66 ||
[67]
na tvābhāsaviyogena grāhyābhāvena cet tathā | kimanena prayāsena mukhyamevocitaṃ vacaḥ || 67 ||
[68]
nāsminnābhāsate kiñcid gocaratvena saṃmatam | iti vyutpattiriṣṭeha tasmāt tantre'pi cottare || 68 ||
[69]
akiñcane nirābhāse nirālambe nirāśraye | cakṣuṣyathavyatikrānte'pyarūpiṇyanidarśane || 69 ||
[4]
yathā nimnonnataṃ vyomni dṛśyate na ca tattathā | buddheṣvapi tathā sarvaṃ dṛśyate na ca tattathā || 70 ||
[71]
atrāpi yadi dṛṣṭāntaviśeṣaṇagaṇo vibhau | avaśyayojyo'nābhāsarūpitve tadvadeva hi || 71 ||
[72]
ālambāśrayayorhānirūrdhvādho'pekṣayā samā | akiñcanatvamāgantvaśeṣadoṣaviyogataḥ || 72 ||
[73]
svaviśeṣaṇamātrāttu kṛtārtha padyamādimam | buddheṣviti tathā cedaṃ bahutvaṃ bhedakaṃ tataḥ || 73 ||
[74]
khasāmyānna ca nairūpyaṃ naiḥsvarūpyaṃ yathaiva na | ropāpavādasthānoccāvacahānyā tu tulyatā || 74 ||
[75]
vasturūpeṣu nīcoccabhāvasaṃbhāvanā bhavet | avasturūpe śaṅkāpi nāstīti khamudāhṛtam || 75 ||
[76]
yadi cānākṛtijñānamabhrāntirbhrāntirākṛtiḥ | trikāyavyavahāro'ntaḥsaṃbhogasya parābhavāt || 76 ||
[77]
bhrāntirākṛtipuñjo'sau yāvat tāvanna buddhatā | bodhe bhrāntivirodhitvādbuddhātmā saṃkathaṃ bhavet || 77 ||
[78]
nāpi saṃvṛtirevāsau kalpanaiva hi saṃvṛtiḥ | na copacārāt kāyatvaṃ tyāgasyaivopapattitaḥ || 78 ||
[79]
buddhādhipatyād dhanyānāṃ tadābhāsaśca nocitaḥ | nirākāratarāste hi buddhastu bhāmayādhikaḥ || 79 ||
[80]
buddhādhipatyaṃ sthāne ca sthāne teṣāṃ ca dhanyatā | aṇḍabhramāṇāṃ yadayaṃ tādṛksthūlabhramodayaḥ || 80 ||
[81]
yathā ca vyāptinityatve svābhiprāyeṇa varṇite | na saṃbhoge tathā vyākhyā tatsvātantryamidaṃ mahat || 81 ||
[82]
sarvaiśca lakṣaṇaiścitrairmaṇḍitātmeti citravāk | cakreśalakṣaṇagaṇādviśeṣāyeti bhāṣyakṛt || 82 ||
[83]
dharmakāyapradhānatvadarśanāyottareṇa yat | cakreśasyāpi bhāvīti nālīkatvādyavarṇayat || 83 ||
[84]
ayaṃ ca sūtrālaṃkāro viruddho yadyalīkatā | dvayordvayārthasaṃpattiḥ sarvākārā pratiṣṭhitā || 84 ||
[85]
saṃbhogaḥ svārthasaṃpattiḥ parārthaśrīstu nirmitiḥ | pratiṣṭhite te svābhāvye saṃbhoge ceti bhāṣyagīḥ || 85 ||
[86]
evaṃ ca dharmakāyasya kāyo nirmāṇakāraṇam | svārthasaṃpadasan khyātisaṃbhoga iti viplavaḥ || 86 ||
[87]
ākāśavāde dehatvānna bahutvaṃ muneriti | bahutvaṃ nākṛtivyāptaṃ cittacaittātmanāmiva || 87 ||
[88]
ṭīkā tvātmagrahābhāvānmuneḥ svaparahānitaḥ | na bhūmeti vadantyāha dehamātmagrahaṃ sphuṭam || 88 ||
[89]
svārthaḥ parārthaḥ paramārthakāyatā tadāśritā saṃvṛtikāyatā ca | phalaṃ visaṃyogavipākabhāvādityuttaretantravare'tha ko'rthaḥ || 89 ||
[90]
svārthaḥ svābhāviko'nyārthaḥ saṃbhogo mata eva naḥ | prastāve'tra tayoḥ kiṃ tu paramārthatvasaṃvidhiḥ || 90 ||
[91]
pāramparyeṇa sākṣād vā sāṃvṛtastau samāśritaḥ | nirmāṇakāyaḥ khyātaṃ ca nirmāṇaṃ sāṃvṛtaṃ phalam || 91 ||
[92]
vadaṃstathāgataguṇānnirmāṇaṃ hi tyajet katham | pāramārthikamityevaṃ vṛttau kāyāvanūdya tau || 92 ||
[93]
ātmasaṃpattyadhiṣṭhāne vidhiśca na virudhyate | ātmasaṃpat dvidhā rūpaniṣpattyābhyudayena ca || 93 ||
[94]
ādyāyāmādimādhiṣṭhā dvitīyasya dvitīyake | acintyalokātītādikhyātānekaviśeṣaṇe || 94 ||
[95]
athavātmani saṃbhoge saṃpattau ca tayorbalam | ratnavigrahavajjñeyaḥ kāyaḥ svābhāvikaḥ śubhaḥ || 95 ||
[96]
akṛtrimattvātprakṛterguṇaratnāśrayatvataḥ | mahādharmādhirājatvāt saṃbhogaścakravartivat || 96 ||
[97]
pratibimbasvabhāvatvānnirmāṇaṃ hemabimbavat | evaṃ vaktari nāthe tu svapakṣarasikaiḥ kṛtaḥ || 97 ||
[98]
saṃbhogaḥ sāṃvṛto hitvā nirmāṇaṃ dhik svatantratām | mahākaruṇayā kṛtsnaṃ lokamālokya lokavit || 98 ||
[99]
dharmakāyādavicalannirmāṇaiścitrarūpibhiḥ | ityādinā prabandhena yaccātraiva pradarśanam || 99 ||
[100]
uktaṃ nirvāṇaparyantajātakādeḥ punaśca yaḥ | sarvatra devabhavane brāhmyādavicalan padāt || 100 ||
[101]
pratibhāsaṃ yathā brahmā darśayedaprayatnataḥ | tadvanmuniranābhogānnirmāṇairlokadhātuṣu || 101 ||
[102]
dharmakāyādavicalan bhavyānāmeti darśanam | ityādi vistarastatra dharmakāyāt pṛthag girā || 102 ||
[103]
saṃbhogātmā na cet ko'nyaḥ kāryabhārakaro muniḥ || 103 ||
[104]
kvacid dharmyaṃ cakraṃ bahumukhaśatairdarśayati sa kvacijjanmāntardhi kvacidapi ca citrāñjanavidhim | kvacit kṛtsnāṃ bodhi kvacidapi sanirmāṇamasakṛnna ca sthānāt tasmādvicalati sa sarva ca kurute || 104 ||
[105]
ityāha sūtrālaṅkāre'pyatra sthānamanāśravaḥ | dhāturbhāṣyodito dharmakāyācalanameva tat || 105 ||
[106]
tathāpyalīka evātmā cākāraśca bhramo mataḥ | kāryabhārastadanyasmāditi lajjaiva lajjitā || 106 ||
[107]
astu cālīkabhāvena bhramaḥ sthūle nirarthakaḥ | avaśyaheyastvākārabhāraḥ syādiṣyate yadi || 107 ||
[108]
nirabbhragaganākārajñānasyevāvaśeṣaṇāt | trikāyasiddhimuddhūya paramevedamudgatam || 108 ||
[109]
saṃbhogabhaṅge taddharmo dharmakāyo na vidyate | tatkāryaṃ na ca nirmāṇaṃ sādhvī bauddhakṛtāntatā || 109 ||
[110]
nanvastametu saṃbhogo dharmakāyo'stvanākṛtiḥ | tata eva ca nirmāṇaṃ saṃbhogo'pi tadāśritaḥ || 110 ||
[111]
bhramatvādeva saṃbhogaṃ hitvānaṅgadaśāśrayaḥ | viśuddheḥ sa hi paryantastattrayī saṅgatirna kim || 111 ||
[112]
yuvarājanayenaitad virodhītyupapāditam | tathāpi yadi carcāyāṃ kautukaṃ kiñciducyate || 112 ||
[113]
anākāraprakāśaśced dharmakāyo'bhidhīyate | kastarhi buddhasaṃbhogo na praheyatayocitaḥ || 113 ||
[114]
kāryārthaṃ dhriyamāṇo'pi bhramatvāt sugataḥ katham | yadi kāryopayogī ca mṛṣālīkatvapoṣaṇam || 114 ||
[115]
tathā ca sati na bhrāntirabhrāntestyajanaṃ na ca | tato'nabbhravataḥ sāmyasiddhisiddhāntanirdhutiḥ || 115 ||
[116]
tadasyāvaśyaheyasya heturnārambhamarhati | tato'pi nāsau sugato dharma eva jino yadi || 116 ||
[117]
dharmakāyo jinasyeti vyavahāro na sidhyati | vyāvṛttibhedadvāreṇāpyekasyaivābhidhānataḥ || 117 ||
[118]
jinādināmabhedena kāyāḥ syuḥ śatamanyathā | na ca buddho jinasyeti vyavahāro'sti kutracit || 118 ||
[119]
dharmiṇo dharmavācī tu bhideva vyavahārabhāk | dhātryāstarorvā tarutā na tu dhātrī taroriti || 119 ||
[120]
dharmamātre mate buddhe buddho dharmasya yujyate | buddhasya dharmakāyastu dharmastasya guṇo yadi || 120 ||
[121]
tathā sati nirākāraḥ kāyasturyasamaśca te | gaṇanīyā na vā hānāt saṃbhogena tanutrayī || 121 ||
[122]
samaḥ sūkṣmaśca saṃbaddhaḥ kāyaḥ svābhāviko mataḥ | iti codyaṃ virudhyeta saṃbaddhapadavarṇane || 122 ||
[123]
sāṃbhogikena kāyena saṃbaddha iti bhāṣyataḥ | saṃbhoge sati taddharmastena saṃbandhamarhati || 123 ||
[124]
tadabhāve na tādātmyaṃ bhāve'pyatyantabhedataḥ | saṃbhogabuddhatāheturiti tatraiva kīrtanāt || 124 ||
[125]
kāryakāraṇabhāvaścet kārya nāvastu kasyacit | avastudharmatāmātraṃ kathaṃ heturapīti cet || 125 ||
[126]
na madhyāntanaye bhāṣye tadālambanatodgatā | taddhetutokto dharmāṇāṃ ṭīkaivaṃ tatra tatra ca || 126 ||
[127]
tadaṃśo vā pṛthakkṛtya san purāpi tathocyate | yathā vikrama evāsya rājñaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ || 127 ||
[128]
nirākārāt kvacijjanma kasyacinnoktamātmani | sūtrālaṃkāragaditaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ tulyamatra tu || 128 ||
[129]
pratītyabhāvaprabhave'pyayaṃ janaḥ samakṣavṛtti śrayate'nyakāritam | tamaḥprakāraḥ katamo'yamīdṛśo yato vipaśyan sadasannirīkṣate || 129 ||
[130]
kartā bhoktā ca dṛṣṭebhyo bhinno'haṅkāragocaraḥ | nirañjanastadekāvaśeṣā muktiśca yoginām || 130 ||
[131]
ityātmavāda evāyaṃ na ca nityo'kriyādṛśaḥ | svabhāvanityatā prāptā dharmakāyatayāsya ca || 131 ||
[132]
prakṛtyāśraṃsanenāpi prabandhena ca nityatā | atra svābhāvike tasyārthasya bhāṣyeṇa yojanāt || 132 ||
[133]
kāryabhramavyavasthāyāṃ yaḥ svābhāvika eva saḥ | dharmakāya iti prokto vyavadānavyapekṣayā || 133 ||
[134]
svabhāvaḥ śūnyatā dharmaḥ saṃbhogaḥ sugataḥ svayam | tasyāntaretaraguṇau bhittvā kāyacatuṣṭayī || 134 ||
[135]
trikāye dharmakāyoktirvakti svābhāvikaṃ vapuḥ | saṃbhogāṃśacatuṣṭve'ntarnirmāṇaṃ śeṣamatra ca || 135 ||
[49]
sarvatrānugataṃ yadvannirvikalpatayā nabhaḥ | cittaprakṛtivaimalyadhātuḥ sarvatragastathā || 136 ||
[137]
iti cottaratantreṇa mukhyaṃ vyāpitvamīritam | saṃpūrṇa ātmavādo'yaṃ vyakto vedāntavādinām || 137 ||
[138]
dharmatāyāstu nityatvavyāpakatvādi sāṃvṛtam | svābhāvye'pi yathākalpaṃ prasiddhaṃ kṣaṇitādivat || 138 ||
[139]
vinā viśeṣaṃ na nyāyo vastunastveṣa hīyate | ata evābhisamaye tacchaṃkāvāraṇaṃ vibhau || 139 ||
[140]
iti kāritravaipulyād buddho vyāpī nirucyate | anucchedācca tasyaiva nitya ityapi kathyate || 140 ||
[141]
yojyaṃ na ca tadevātra prakṛtyā nityatoditā | svābhāvikādhikāre hi vasturūpastato na saḥ || 141 ||
[142]
viśvakāryaṃ ca saṃbhoge śuddhistadvirahe yadā | prāgvad virodhaḥ saṃśuddhisattvārthau na ca śāśvatau || 142 ||
[143]
yadi nāsti nirākāra ātmanā cāsya tulyatā | sa evāyaṃ dharmakāya ityupakramya bhūbhujā || 143 ||
[144]
saṃkleśopacayadhvaṃsātyantadhvaṃsaiḥ ka uttare | tantre prakāśitaḥ sattvabodhisattvajinātmakaḥ || 144 ||
[145]
dharmakāyo dvidhā jñeyo dharmadhātuḥ sunirmalaḥ | tanniṣyandaśca gāmbhīryavaicitryanayadeśanā || 145 ||
[146]
iti vyākhyāpi tatraiva kiṃ tu dharmeṇa dharmigīḥ | prastuto dharmakāyastu dharmadhātuḥ sunirmalaḥ || 146 ||
[15]
tathātā bhūtakoṭiścānimittaṃ paramārthatā | dharmadhātuśca paryāyāḥ śūnyatāyāḥ samāsataḥ || 147 ||
[148]
iti madhyāntavībhāge dharmadhātuśca varṇitaḥ | jñeyaḥ sapariniṣpannastattvaṃ dhāturanāśravaḥ || 148 ||
[149]
śūnyatā ca dvayenoktā tatra kleśadaśāvaśāt | paratantraguṇo jñeyaḥ saṃbhogasya malakṣaye || 149 ||
[150]
sarvākārāṃ viśuddhiṃ ye dharmāḥ prāptā anāśravāḥ | svābhāviko muneḥ kāyasteṣāṃ prakṛtilakṣaṇaḥ || 150 ||
[151]
atrāpi cābhisamayālaṅkāre na virudhyate | prakṛtiḥ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt tattvaṃ ca pratipāditam || 151 ||
[152]
yad vā svabhāvaḥ pratipaddharmāṇāṃ śūnyataiva sā | sarveṣāṃ ca matā buddhaprastāvāttu viśuddhavāk || 152 ||
[153]
na śuddhisaṃgṛhīto'pi saṃbhogo gaṇito gaṇe | pṛthakkāyo hi vācyo'sau dharmastasya kathaṃ tadā || 153 ||
[154]
mukhyatvānna tu tasyaiva śeṣaḥ parikaro'sya hi | ekajñānātmakatvena tadgraheṇaiva gṛhyate || 154 ||
[155]
bhogaḥ pratiṣṭhākārau ca tato bhinnau na yadyapi | anyavadvyavahārastu sāṃvṛtaḥ puruṣādbhidā || 155 ||
{12.3}
<tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[1]
yadyevaṃ dharmatāmātraṃ pṛthakkṛtya vimucyate | buddho vā dharma eveti dvayābhāvaḥ svavitkatham || 1 ||
[2]
tadbodhāducyate buddho nojjvalairlakṣaṇādibhiḥ | na tadālambanaṃ hitvā sarvaśuklaguṇapriyaḥ || 2 ||
[3]
tadvodhaḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ sāmānyo nāparasya saḥ | tatsmṛtistāyināṃ pūjā tanniścayaphale prame || 3 ||
[4]
tasmāt svalakṣaṇaṃ buddho dharmaḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇam | tatprādhānye na buddhatvaṃ bhinno rāśirataḥ kutaḥ || 4 ||
[5]
ata evocyate buddho dharma eveti tadyathā | pratāpa eva rājeti tādātmyaṃ tattvatastayoḥ || 5 ||
[6]
yaccoktamādyācāryeṇa buddhaśabdasya gocaraḥ | viśuddhaścittasantāno dharmākhyāpi mahāmuneḥ || 6 ||
[7]
tatrāpi dharmakāyasya sākṣātkāreṇa sa dhvaniḥ | dharma eva jino yadvajjina eva tathā sa ca || 7 ||
[8]
āryeśanītivivṛterarūpyanābhāsavarṇanārīteḥ | dvayamātrahānigīterapi śaṅkā nāstyanākṛtinaḥ || 8 ||
[9]
ālayajñānayatne'pi na tadeva nirākṛti | tasya vyāvṛttirarhattve kathyate kathamanyathā || 9 ||
[10]
vyāvṛttiśced daśābhedo'nābhāsaḥ sādhyanirdhutiḥ | akaniṣṭhe hi saṃbodhiruktānārūpyadhātujā || 10 ||
[11]
ṭīkāpyāhāgame kvāpi noktā nākāradhīriti | khyātācāryasthiramaterāgamasyānusāriṇī || 11 ||
[12]
tannirākāramevoktamiti cenniścayo hataḥ | kimanyacintayāsmākaṃ prakṛtasya prasādhanāt || 12 ||
[13]
kvāpi vyavasthā kathamapyāgame kriyatāṃ jinaiḥ | ādyācāryeṇa vā sarvamidānīṃ prastutaṃ na tat || 13 ||
[14]
upekṣākārasadbhāvānnārūpye'pyākṛtikṣatiḥ | dhiyo vivarto hyākāraḥ kiṃcidrūpasya vā sthiteḥ || 14 ||
[15]
dhījātervyaktirākāro yadi nākanibhā na kim | kiṃ vādhunā vyavacchedyaṃ na kiñcid buddhisaṃbhave || 15 ||
[16]
nīlādau tu tadākārādanyā buddhirniṣidhyate | svapne'pyadarśanād dhīstu tathā kācit parānyathā || 16 ||
[17]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaiva vyavasthitam | tattadrūpāṅgamicchā cet pātramasyā niveditam || 17 ||
[18]
mohārūpavirāgeṇārūpyadhātuḥ śamāśayā | tasmānnīlādirātmaiva buddhīnāṃ dvayameva na || 18 ||
[19]
prasajyaparyudāsābhyāṃ sarvābhāvasthitirdvidhā | paryudāso dvayasyātra dharmirūpaṃ svalakṣaṇam || 19 ||
[20]
tasya vastutayā tāvat svavittirna virudhyate | dharmipratyakṣamevānyābhāve'pi vihitā mitiḥ || 20 ||
[21]
bhūtale kalasābhāvo bhūtalādhyakṣasādhanaḥ | saṃbhoge ca dvayābhāvaḥ saṃbhogādhyakṣasādhanaḥ || 21 ||
[22]
āryo'nyastadapekṣyedamadvayāya namo'stu te | na rakto harinmāñjiṣṭha ityādikamavarṇayat || 22 ||
[23]
pratyātmavedyamityevaṃ svavicca svagiroditā | tatparyudaste'pi samaṃ kalpe'pyavasitāśrayāt || 23 ||
[24]
avaseyasya niṣṭhāpi saṃbhogena sphuṭīkṛtā | ataeva ca sākārasvīkārastaiḥ prakāśitaḥ || 24 ||
[25]
dharmo notpadyate kaścinnāpi kaścinnirudhyate | utpadyante nirudhyante pratyayā eva kevalāḥ || 25 ||
[26]
iti cāṅkurabījādisthāne buddhiniveśanāt | tadābhāsaḥ sphuṭo yacca kalpitakṣayakīrtanam || 26 ||
[27]
mahābhūtādivijñāne proktaṃ samavarudhyate | tajjñāne vigamaṃ yāti nanu mithyā vikalpitam || 27 ||
[28]
tatrāsattvādhimokṣo'rthāvarodhaḥ śrutacintayoḥ | tajjñāna iti ca jñānarūpasākṣātkṛtau kṣayaḥ || 28 ||
[29]
ātmagrahanivṛttyartha skandhadhātvādideśanā | sāpi dhvastā mahābhāgaiścitramātravyavasthayā || 29 ||
[30]
iti ślāghāsamuddhārānniścayo'tra rucerapi | sthitidvayamapekṣyāyaṃ viśeṣaśced yathoditam || 30 ||
[31]
cittamātramidaṃ sarvamiti yā deśanā muneḥ | tattrāsaparihārārthaṃ bālānāṃ sā na tattvataḥ || 31 ||
[32]
ucchedābhiniviṣṭānāmicchāṃ dattvaiṣa saṃgrahaḥ | trāsahānena netyatra cchedastu paramārthataḥ || 32 ||
[33]
anyathā bālasaṃtrāsahānistulyā sthitidvaye | ko'tra bhedo yataḥ ślāghā prakṣepo vā tathāvidhaḥ || 33 ||
[34]
nāpaneyamataḥ kiñcidityādivacanasya ca | anvākhyānāt svayamapi vyākhyeyaṃ kimataḥ param || 34 ||
[35]
bhūtātmanā bhūtameva bhūtaṃ bhūtātmanaiva ca | draṣṭavyamiti vākyārtho neyatāṃ gīyate'tra kim || 35 ||
[36]
sarvanāstitvavāde hi na bhūtaṃ kiñcidasti yat | draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtarūpeṇetyapavādānta eṣa saḥ || 36 ||
[37]
samāropastavāpīti nāropaḥ kalpanā yataḥ | nirvikalpe sphuratyatrāropastu dvayakalpanā || 37 ||
[38]
apavādo na saṃvṛttyā nāropastattvato yadi | na tau dvāvapi tattvena yadi kiṃ vā virudhyate || 38 ||
[39]
saṃvṛttyānapavādo'pavāda eva hi tattvataḥ | sarvanāstitvavādo'taḥ prāpta uktaṃ ca dūṣaṇam || 39 ||
[40]
bhūtaṃ cet śūnyatā sādhu yatra yannāsti tena tat | śūnyaṃ gehaṃ yathā puṃbhirna bādhā dharmidharmayoḥ || 40 ||
[41]
abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate | śūnyatā vidyate tvatra tasyāmapi sa vidyate || 41 ||
[42]
sarvanāstitvavādastu dūṣya eva miterbalam | cintiṣyate'ta evāryāḥ kiñcinnekṣanta ityasat || 42 ||
[43]
vedyavedakabhāvena kalpitāpekṣayāthavā | niṣedha eṣa sadṛśo yadā cekṣāvikalpanam || 43 ||
[44]
yathā puṇyabalaṃ teṣāṃ citrajñānasamudbhave | etadetacca paśyantītyucyate vyavahāribhiḥ || 44 ||
[45]
astitvavāraṇaṃ kurmo nāstitvasya vidhirna tu | tasyāpi pratiṣedhyatvāt mahāneṣa manorathaḥ || 45 ||
[46]
niṣedha evāstitvasya nāstitvamabhidhīyate | naño'parārthavirahānnaikasya vidhibādhanam || 46 ||
[47]
parasparavyavacchedarūpayorekabādhanam | vidhiṃ vidhūya nānyasya sthātuṃ kṣaṇamapi kṣamam || 47 ||
[48]
bhautakalpitakalpānāṃ svabhāvānāmasaṃbhave | sarvopādhiviviktasya vasturūpasya na kṣatiḥ || 48 ||
[49]
tasmād rūpadvaye niṣṭhā naikatra vidhivādhayoḥ | bhāse'pavādo'nābhāse cāropastyajyatāmataḥ || 49 ||
[50]
