śalyena viśatāṅgena cchidyamānena vā yathā | vyathāropāpavādābhyāṃ tatheha sphuradākṛtau || 50 ||
[51]
śuddhamādhyamikastasmād yogācārānna bhidyate | samāropāpavādāntamuktireva hi madhyamā || 51 ||
[3]
śūnyaṃ nāpi na cāśūnyaṃ tasmāt sarvaṃ vidhīyate | sattvādasattvāt sattvācca madhyamāpratipacca sā || 52 ||
[53]
abhāvārtha paramate śūnyamādāya vāgiyam | āryarājasya yatno'yaṃ dṛṣṭidagdhairmudhākṛtaḥ || 53 ||
[54]
sattve'ta eva dharmāṇāṃ jñeyāvaraṇavāraṇe | vismayaḥ kalpitāpekṣo'sakṛcchāstreṣu kīrtanāt || 54 ||
[55]
svayaṃ vijñānavādyeva paraśabdena codayet | vijñānavādina iti vaiśasaṃ kimataḥ param || 55 ||
[56]
svo bhāvī yadi saṃbuddho vañcakaḥ kutra nirvṛtiḥ | vañcitā api tenaiva śobhābhājo manīṣiṇaḥ || 56 ||
[57]
parāśayājjñānanayo'tha nāthasyāryasya kiṃ nānyakathā tathaiva | yathā vineyāḥ khalu tasya kecid bhavādṛśo'pyasya tathā vineyāḥ || 57 ||
[58]
anuktiranyasya nijāśayasya sādhāraṇāyāśca narāntare'pi | ślāghāṃ tatānāryadharādhipasya yatnastu madhyāpratipañca seti || 58 ||
[59]
same'pi ced darśanamārgalābhe na bhāvanāthābhyadhiko'parādhaḥ | tadaikasatye sadṛśe dvidhā ced varaṃ dharādhīśapurapraveśaḥ || 59 ||
[60]
dharmānusāro yadivarṇataste pramāṇaśāstraikaparāyaṇaḥ syāḥ | śraddhānusāre tu mahājanīyaḥ sabhājanīyo yuvarājarājaḥ || 60 ||
[61]
jinoktimātraṃ vata pudgale'pi na sandhinirmocanamocanena | nītārthalābhastadanādare tu buddhe svayaṃ vaktari ko viśeṣaḥ || 61 ||
antaraślokāḥ ||
[62]
vineyabhedād bhittvaikāṃ gāmbhīryaparamārthataḥ | vidhibādhāmukhatayā caturdhā sthitirucyate || 62 ||
[63]
apavādaparā hyeke samāropaparāḥ pare | tatrādyānadhikṛtyoktā prathamā caramā parān || 63 ||
[64]
svayaṃ niṣedhanirateṣvabhisaṅgaṃ niṣidhya ye | cintāstitvavidhānena yogācāranayasthitiḥ || 64 ||
[65]
āroparakteṣu punarbādhadvāreṇa madhyamā | tadbhamnā ca niṣedhoktirbhūyasī nirupādhikā || 65 ||
[66]
paṅguvadgāḍhanunnāktibhittau sthāsyanti te svayam | sādharmyavaidharmyagiroraikārthye kiṃ na bhedanam || 66 ||
[67]
yogācārānna tattvena bhidyate śuddhamadhyamā | tasmādāryo'pi cāryeśanayastha iti sundaram || 67 ||
[68]
viśiṣṭayogyatādṛṣṭestaddvāreṇānyakarṣaṇāt | utsāhanācca sollāsavyākṛtirna virodhinī || 68 ||
[69]
tasmādeṣāmapi naye yāvaduktaniṣedhanam | kalpitasyaiva tajjñeyaṃ dvitīyācāryanītivat || 69 ||
[70]
kalpitasya niṣedho'yamiti saṃgrahadarśanam | sarvo jñeyatayā rūḍha ākāraḥ kalpito matau || 70 ||
[71]
matāvārūḍha ākāro jñeyarūpeṇa kalpitaḥ | tasyopalakṣaṇatvena jñānatvenāpi kaścana || 71 ||
[72]
kalpitasya niṣedhaśca grāhyāditvena gṛhyatām | vibhaktaṃ ṭīkayā yadvattadabhāvāt tadapyasat || 72 ||
[73]
asadeva yataḥ khyāti tadavidyāvinirmitam | asatkhyāpanaśaktau hi sāvidyeti nigadyate || 73 ||
[74]
khyātiradhyavasāyārtho vikalpe sphuratīti vā | avidyāvāsanāyātakalpasthastatkṛto mataḥ || 74 ||
[75]
prajñāpāramitāyāṃ hi trīn samāśritya deśanā | kalpitaṃ paratantraṃ ca pariniṣpannameva ca || 75 ||
[76]
nāstītyādipadaiḥ sarvaiḥ kalpitaṃ vinivāryate | māyopamādidṛṣṭāntaiḥ paratantrasya deśanā || 76 ||
[77]
caturdhā vyavadānena pariniṣpannakīrtanam | prajñāpāramitāyāṃ hi nānyā buddhasya deśanā || 77 ||
[78]
itthaṃ pāramitānīterakṣīṇārthānvayācca tat | tasyāṃ hi tāvat sākāravādaḥ sphurati nirmalaḥ || 78 ||
[79]
tato yadyanya evārtho mukhyamākhyāya bhāvikam | artha āryanaye'pyeṣa grāhya ityucitaṃ vacaḥ || 79 ||
[80]
atha tasmādiyatyaṃśe bhedaḥ sādhye tathāpi kim | dvayamātraniṣedhena nirvṛtiḥ kṛtinā kṛtā || 80 ||
[81]
vācyo bhāsaniṣedho'pi bhāsa eva ca na dvayam | lakṣaṇābhāvato bhāve tvabādhā sūcitā purā || 81 ||
[82]
saṃbhoge copacārādi varṇyeta viśadākṣaram | pradhānārthatayāryeṇa svānītau vā prakāśanāt || 82 ||
[83]
bhagavatyā hi piṇḍārthavākpravṛtte na kiṃ kṛtam | vihāya heyopādeyavyaktimīṣatkarāṃ girā || 83 ||
[84]
guṇarūpaviśeṣeṇa svastutirvā kimanyathā | yad vā vārtikamādarśastanmatasya pareṇa kim || 84 ||
[85]
tatra vārtikakāreṇa yatnād bāhye'pi sākṛtim | dhiyaṃ prasādhya tanmātraṃ śeṣitaṃ grāhyaviplavāt || 85 ||
[326]
ātmā sa tasyānubhavaḥ sa ca nānyasya kasyacit | pratyakṣaprativedyatvamapi tasya tadātmatā || 86 ||
[87]
tathā bruvāṇa āryeśa itthaṃ vārtikakṛd vadan | saṃmukho'pyanyathā kurvanna saṃpratyayagocaraḥ || 87 ||
[88]
yadyākāraṃ praveśyāpi citte cittamanākṛtiḥ | iṣṭamālīkyamākārasyāntarnyāso'sya kiṃphalaḥ || 88 ||
[89]
nirākāraṃ manaḥ siddhaṃ sarvayoḥ svānyavādinoḥ | jñānavad bahirārope'pyākṛterdūṣaṇaṃ samam || 89 ||
[90]
tataḥ prayāsaḥ kimiyān prakṣālya tyāga eva vā | ayatnasiddho vitathasphuraṇe vāsanānvayaḥ || 90 ||
[91]
grahasādhutayākāraṃ grāhye'ṅgīkāryadūṣite | sākāracittaniṣṭhāyāṃ yuktamākārasādhanam || 91 ||
[92]
grahaṇe karaṇatvena prakāśaikopalambhataḥ | vipratītiśatādhāraṃ prasādhyākāravanmanaḥ || 92 ||
[93]
mānameyaphalanyāyaṃ nirbandhena vidhāya ca | atṛpteḥ punarante'pi tadartho hi mahān śramaḥ || 93 ||
[94]
pratyutālīkamākāraṃ mudhā sādhayataḥ prati | pratyāsattiṃ grahe'nādyaḥ sa eva syānnidarśanam || 94 ||
[95]
tataḥ svabhāvato'nātmaprakāśabalavanmanaḥ | siddhamitthaphalaṃ grāhyalakṣaṇakṣaticintanam || 95 ||
[96]
sahopalambhaprākāśyahetudvayagirāpyalam | dvitīyācāryavaśyatvaṃ dharmottaravaducyatām || 96 ||
[97]
na ca vārtikakārīyamekānekātyayo'ñjasā | bāhye'pi dūṣaṇaṃ kvāpi paramāṇoradūṣaṇāt || 97 ||
[98]
yatnasādhitasākāre sthitvā grāhyaṃ tu dūṣitam | vaibhāṣikācca sūtrāntī varṇitastattvasannidheḥ || 98 ||
[99]
tato'līkamasad veti sarvatrāvaśitaṃ prati | na hyākārasvarūpeṇa gṛhyate kiṃ tu bāhyataḥ || 99 ||
[100]
dṛṣṭaminduyugaṃ tacca nāstītyuktirna cetasaḥ | dṛṣṭākṛtirmṛṣāveti na cendudvayameva tat || 100 ||
[101]
jalāropoditāddoṣāccittākārastu yujyate | asādhāraṇanirbhāsī prakāśo na parasya ca || 101 ||
[102]
iyaṃyathādhyavasiti vyavasthā tattvataḥ punaḥ | keśādayo na sāmānyamanarthābhiniveśataḥ || 102 ||
[103]
ityāha na tvanarthatvādityanyacca sphuṭābhatā | jñānarūpatayārthatvāt keśadīti matiḥ punaḥ || 103 ||
[104]
sāmānyaviṣayaṃ keśapratibhāsamanarthakam | indriyajñānasaṃkhyātamasadbāhyāvasāyataḥ || 104 ||
[105]
jñānarūpatayārthatve sāmānye cet prasajyate | tatheṣṭatvādadoṣo'rtharūpatvena samānatā || 105 ||
[106]
apratikṣepabhāgdharmī śabdārtha iti cāsakṛt | tasmād yathāpratītyuktaḥ śabdārthosāvasannapi || 106 ||
[107]
abhavannapi śabdārthaḥ śabdārtha iti kīrtitaḥ | jñānākāraśrute śabde tadbhāsāditi darśitam || 107 ||
[108]
yathāvasāyaṃ tu bahiḥ śabdārtha iti niścayaḥ | atadrūpaparāvṛttavastumātrasthiteriti || 108 ||
[109]
yathāpratīti sattvaṃ cet nāvasāyo'tra sāpi tu | bhāsanaṃ saiva sattāsya bāhye śaktestvapekṣaṇam || 109 ||
[110]
tasmājjñānatayaivokta ākāro'rtha iti sthitam | vyākhyātaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇa yacca tatra śrameṇa kim || 110 ||
[111]
sākārameva cetaścet paryante'pyadhikaṃ na hi | saṃkleśavyavadānaṃ cetyekamastu na tu dvayam || 111 ||
[112]
ākāra eva saṃkleśo vyavadānaṃ tu tatkṣayaḥ | ityanākāravāde syādubhayasya vyavasthitiḥ || 112 ||
[113]
atasmiṃstadgrahād bhrāntirvikalpastatkṣayaḥ samaḥ | samāpi ced vikalpo'pi satyākāraḥ kathaṃ bhramaḥ || 113 ||
[114]
avasāye prakāśyatvaṃ prakāśe ca tadātmatā | arthasya hānau na syācca nāma ityādivedanam || 114 ||
[115]
sarvātmaniścayaśca syāt spaṣṭo'rthaḥ syācca gauriti | svalakṣaṇe cāsaṃketāt kalpikaiva bhavenna dhīḥ || 115 ||
[116]
tasmādaśeṣagovyaktisāmānyena vibhāti dhīḥ | gotvena sābhilāpenālīkeneti tathā prathā || 116 ||
[117]
gavāvasāya ityastu naite doṣā bhavantyataḥ | svalakṣaṇasyābhāve'pi bhrāntyā tadavasāyataḥ || 117 ||
[118]
yathālīkasya gotvasya gobuddhau ca prakāśanam | tādātmyaṃ cāvyatirico'nāropo vastutāpi ca || 118 ||
[119]
tathā nīlādinirbhāse'līkasya dhavalādinaḥ | prakāśabhāvasiddhyaiva tādātmyaṃ siddhamiṣyatām || 119 ||
[120]
vastutāyāmanārope liṅgaṃ tādātmyagotrakam | gotvādibhiranekāntasamāropamasiddhakam || 120 ||
[121]
tadetat phalgu sakalaṃ yataḥ sākāravādinām | sato'pi bhānaṃ nārthasya kuta evāsato bhavet || 121 ||
[122]
svarūpasyaiva nirbhāsād bālasyāpyeṣa niścayaḥ | arthabhānāśrayāstasya kila doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ || 122 ||
[123]
kutra saṅketakaraṇaṃ śabdo yasyāvabodhakaḥ | kasyāvabodhakaḥ śabdo yatra saṃketakakriyā || 123 ||
[124]
vācoyuktiriyaṃ kīdṛśīdṛgeva yadīkṣase | vācyavācakatāṃ kvāpi mamāpi pratipādaya || 124 ||
[125]
alīko yasya cākāraḥ kiṃ tasyāpi viśiṣyate | alīke yadi saṃketaḥ satyākāre kathaṃ na saḥ || 125 ||
[126]
phalaṃ na satyapyākāre'līke suṣṭhu na vidyate | arthāropādalīke cet satye kena niṣidhyate || 126 ||
[127]
ko'rthāropo'tha satyatve'līkatve'pi sa kīdṛśaḥ | satyo'līko'thavākāro vastvāropastu kiṃkṛtaḥ || 127 ||
[128]
asatyagotvabhānād hi bhānāt satyākṛterna kim | satye'pi satyākāraścet satye'pyālīkyamākṛte || 128 ||
[129]
asatyabhānādāropo yuktaḥ satye kathaṃ bhavet | nanvasatye'pi saṃketo'satyatvāvasitau katham || 129 ||
[130]
tasmādarthakriyāśaktavastvāropātmanastanau | saṃketakaraṇaṃ satyāsatyayorna viśiṣyate || 130 ||
[131]
yathātathātve vākārasyāvasāyo na vidyate | na bhānamarthasya tato vācyatā kasya tatvataḥ || 131 ||
[132]
abhāne pratibhāne vā na cāropo'pi kasyacit | pratītyotpādabhedena vyavasthāmātramīdṛśaḥ || 132 ||
[133]
nirvikalpād vikalpasya bhāve leśānusāriṇaḥ | saṃketakārivacanād buddhyākāre viśeṣiṇi || 133 ||
[134]
saṃketaḥ kṛta ityāsthā tādṛkśabdasthitau punaḥ | pravṛttyākṣepabuddhyātmabhāve vācyavyavasthitiḥ || 134 ||
[135]
evaṃ pravṛtterākṣepivikalpākārajanmani | sato jalādirāropaḥ satyāsatyasamaśca saḥ || 135 ||
[136]
tato yadyapi tattvena nāropaḥ kasyacit kvacit | vyavahārakṛtastveṣa pratiṣeddhuṃ na śakyate || 136 ||
[137]
marīcau jalavad yāvadanātmanyātmakalpanam | bhramaḥ sa eva saṃsāro nirvāṇaṃ tatvasaṃsthitiḥ || 137 ||
[138]
tadatra yāvanna vicārasaṃbhavo bhavo'yamanyaḥ śama ityayaṃ nayaḥ | vicāralīlālulite tu mānase bhavaḥ śamo vā ka iheti kathyatām || 138 ||
tathā ca —
[139]
nacāntaraṃ kiñcana vidyate'nayoḥ sadarthavṛttyā śamajanmanoriha | tathāpi janmakṣayato vidhīyate śamasya lābhaḥ śubhakarmakāriṇām || 139 ||
tathā,
[140]
nirvāṇaṃ ca bhavaścaiva dvayametanna vidyate | parijñānaṃ bhavasyaiva nirvāṇamiti kathyate || 140 ||
[141]
jalabuddhāvalīkatvaṃ nākārasya prayojakam | bhramavyavasthitau tadvadgrāhyagrāhakaviplave || 141 ||
[142]
satye'satye'thavākāre nāparādho'sti cetasaḥ | yadi pravṛtterākṣepī bāhyāropo na jāyate || 142 ||
[143]
satyākāramapi jñānaṃ kalpakaṃ gocare tataḥ | pravṛttyākṣepaṇād duṣṭaṃ pravṛttiḥ saṃsṛtiryataḥ || 143 ||
[144]
pravṛttiravikalpe'pi vikalpe'pi na seti cet | viśeṣasaraṇe'pyeva tatrāniṣṭistato na kim || 144 ||
[145]
anādikālikābhyāsādyathā kiñcit kvacit kṣamam | tathā vikalpasyāpīyaṃ yogyatāniṣṭisādhanī || 145 ||
[146]
vikalpe kleśabhāvo'dhisattvānāmata eva hi | tadvāsanāhatau yatno yāvaddhetuphalasthitiḥ || 146 ||
[147]
alīkagotvākāreṇa khyātiḥ siddhā na gomateḥ | satyākāro'pi saṃkalpo'dhyavasāyaḥ pravartanāt || 147 ||
[148]
satyasya gotvākārasya gobuddhau bhāsanaṃ yathā | tādātmyaṃ cāvyatirico'nāropo vastutāpi ca || 148 ||
[149]
tathā nīlādinirbhāse satyasya dhavalādinaḥ | prakāśabhāvasiddhyaiva tādātmyaṃ satyamiṣyatām || 149 ||
[150]
yadvasturūpaṃ tadvastu govikalpe yathākṛtiḥ | prakāśavasturūpaṃ ca nīlaṃ na sphūrtiranyathā || 150 ||
[151]
tādātmyadvaidhanirdhūteḥ siddho bādhaśca vāstavaḥ | nekṣate ca sitādanyastathānāropasādhanam || 151 ||
[152]
śaktastvalīkaākāro nopakārāpakārayoḥ | kādācitkaḥ sphurannarthasamartho vā mṛṣā katham || 152 ||
[153]
etatsvarūpabādhe hi bādhako'pyasya kiṃkaraḥ | tataḥ svayaṃ prakāśātmā śuddho vā kliṣṭa eva vā || 153 ||
[154]
alīkamātraṃ sadapi na hi kvāpi vibandhakṛt | vibandhakatve'līkatvamevālīkaṃ prasajyate || 154 ||
[155]
gocarāntarasañcāro neṣṭa eva kva bandhakṛt | svasaṃvittau punastasya śatenāpi na bandhanam || 155 ||
[156]
svavittibandhe hi jaḍaḥ prakāśaśca svahetutaḥ | ityayuktamato'śakyaṃ svābhedenāpi vedanam || 156 ||
[157]
svahetośca tathotpattirvedanaṃ ca tadātmanā | bhāvaiḥ svīkṛtamekatvaṃ vādināṃ mahatī vyathā || 157 ||
[158]
tannālīko'yamākāraḥ spṛśatyenaṃ sphurannapi | tāvatāpyasya saṃkleśe santānāntarato na kim || 158 ||
[159]
vastusannapi santānabhedastasya na bādhakaḥ | asatyaḥ punarākāro bādhāyeti kimapyadaḥ || 159 ||
[160]
tatpravṛttinivṛttibhyāṃ saṃsāro nāma nāparaḥ | tattvāvasāyabhedeṣu pratibandhe prasādhite || 160 ||
[161]
viśeṣaścāvasāyānāmākārātparato na ca | jalākārād visaṃkalpājjala eva pravartate || 161 ||
[162]
jalākāravikalpo'pi jalākārādakalpataḥ | bhavannapi na tanmātrād vāsanāsacivā tvasau || 162 ||
[163]
tadvāsanāsamudghāte kevalānnāvikalpataḥ | grāhyagrāhakabhāvāderabhūtasya vikalpanam || 163 ||
[164]
nirvikalpamapi jñānaṃ hetuśced vāsanāśrayāt | yathāpravṛttākārasya tatkṣaye'stūdayakṣayaḥ || 164 ||
[165]
ā bodhicittagrahaṇād dānādyabhyāsataḥ kramāt | ativiśvavapurbhogapratiṣṭhākārasaṃbhavaḥ || 165 ||
[166]
āsaṃsāramaviśrāmaparārthasvārthasaṃpade | rucestadekaniṣṭhatvāttaddhetāvasamaḥ śramaḥ || 166 ||
[167]
mahākāruṇyasampannapuṇyajñānaśriyāntataḥ | viśuddhivāsanābandhaprabandhasthairyasādhanaḥ || 167 ||
[168]
tatrāsatkalpanā kālaḥ saṃkleśaḥ śuddhiruttaraḥ | sākāra eva vijñāne tasmādeṣā vyavasthitiḥ || 168 ||
[169]
advaitacitraguṇasaṃbhṛtaśātapūrṇasādhāradheyamayamaṇḍanacakrarūpam | sādhyaṃ vidhūya na ca santanayo'pi sāraḥ sākāranītiriti nītipugasya jīvaḥ || 169 ||
[170]
dṛṣṭaṃ śarmaviśiṣṭasādhanaparādhīnaṃ yathā bhāvanāpyasyodeti tathaiva yatsukharasākṛṣṭāṅganāderapi | niṣpattau ca tathā nirantarasukhasyandābhinandyākṛtau bādhābādhavidhau sametaratayā śarmaikaśeṣo'stu kim || 170 ||
antaraślokau ||
{12.4}
<caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ>
[1]
mā bhūdanyo'stu sākāra eva sādhyetarasthitiḥ | ekānekavivekena tvālīkyaṃ kena vāryate || 1 ||
[2]
ekānekaviveko'stu na tvālīkyaṃ prakāśinaḥ | bādhā hi rūpe'vasite nādhyakṣaviṣaye kvacit || 2 ||
[3]
rūpamātrasya nirbhāso dvicandre'pi na bādhyate | bādhā sparśādino rūpasyāpi tatsahacāriṇaḥ || 3 ||
[4]
evaṃsvapne'pi putrādiḥ kalpito'sanna dhītanuḥ | mantrādhipatyālloṣṭādau pītabhāso na bādhanam || 4 ||
[5]
rukmādi kalpitaṃ bādhyaṃ loṣṭādestu na bhāsanam | na cāvasāyastenāsya na vidhirna ca bādhanam || 5 ||
[6]
anyathākhyātirasyeti duṣṭaṃ tatkhyātyasaṃbhavāt | asatkhyātistu vikhyātā kalpitā sadapekṣayā || 6 ||
[7]
loṣṭamevānyathākhyātītyabhiprāyānna sāpi kim | vyavahāreṇa nirbandhaḥ tattvatastu na taddvayam || 7 ||
[8]
anyathaivāvabhāsante tadrūparahitā api | ityukterbhāvikastvatra boddhavyo'rtho yathoditaḥ || 8 ||
[9]
tathaivādarśanāt teṣāmanupaplutacakṣuṣā | kalpitatvamanenoktamābhāse kanakādinaḥ || 9 ||
[10]
na bādhaḥ kasyacit tattve saṃvṛttau kalpitasya tu | prakāśino'pi bādhaśced bādhe'pyāśvāsanaṃ kutaḥ || 10 ||
[11]
anumābādhikāśā ca na vastuviṣayeti cet | avaśyamasti vastvātmaniṣṭhāsau nānyathā pramā || 11 ||
[12]
bhātameva purā vastuvidhāvadhyavasīyate | niṣedho'pi svabhāvārthaḥ paryante paryavasyati || 12 ||
antaraślokau ||
[13]
pareṇa viṣayābhāvajñāpanaṃ sapadīṣyate | svārthe pravṛttimajjñānamabhāvaṃ gamayet katham || 13 ||
[14]
svagocaropasthānena viṣayāntarabādhane | svagocarasya tenāpi sthānāt kiṃ nāsya bādhanam || 14 ||
[15]
tadarthakarmahāneśced bhinnā sārthakriyā yadi | anyahāne'nyahāniḥ kimabhede tu sphuratyasau || 15 ||
[16]
rūpaṃ samīkṣya dāhādihāneḥ sparśasya bādhanam | na ca sparśaḥ sphuratyatra bādhā saivāsya kiṃ paraiḥ || 16 ||
[17]
viṣayīkṛtamanyadvā bādhyeta prathamaṃ yadi | sphuradeva kathaṃ bādhyamasphūrtau bādhakena kim || 17 ||
[18]
na bādhā bhinnakālatve svasvakāle spharattayā | tathaiva kālābhede'pi nīlapītasitādivat || 18 ||
[19]
tasmādāropavad bādhaḥ pratītyotpādabhedataḥ | kalpito na tu tattvena svavinmātre tu kā kathā || 19 ||
[20]
yāvanna siddhiḥ svavido bādhakaṃ tāvadastu cet | nirūpya svavido'siddhiṃ bādhastarhi pravartatām || 20 ||
[21]
pūrvaṃ pravartanārambhe pratijñābādhamakṣataḥ | yadi brūyāt parajñānaniṣedhe svavidāgatā || 21 ||
[22]
yathāyathārthāścintyante vivicyante tathā tathā | svayaṃ tu vittiśchāyeva dhāvato'pyanatikramā || 22 ||
[23]
ataeva niṣedhasya prakrame'pi jagau guruḥ | yadīdaṃ svayamarthānāṃ rocate tatra ke vayam || 23 ||
[24]
na bādhā cet pareṇāsti siddhirapyastu nānyataḥ | svavitsiddhirapīdānīṃ sādhanāntarataḥ katham || 24 ||
[25]
kutaścit kasyacit siddhirna tattve kiṃ tu saṃvṛtau | yathā dhūmādito'gnyādermatā siddhiriyaṃ tathā || 25 ||
[26]
svavitsiddhiratattve cet yāvat sādhyāṅgasaṃsthitiḥ | tāvat tadeva tattvaṃ yat siddhaṃ sādhanaśaktitaḥ || 26 ||
[27]
yatsādhanabalāt siddhe svavinmātre punaḥ param | siddhibādhanayorasti nāvakāśaḥ kutaścana || 27 ||
[28]
na bodhayan kiñcidanyat prastutatyajanakṣamaḥ | prastutaṃ vā tyajan nānyasyānyato grahaṇakṣamaḥ || 28 ||
[29]
ataeva parajñānaṃ gṛhyamāṇaṃ svabādhanam | svavittihetutrairūpyajñānasyāpyavakāśataḥ || 29 ||
[30]
tyaktaṃ tu teṣāṃ rūpāṇāmabodhe'pi na bādhakam | sādhyasiddheḥ prakāśo hi vidyate parato na tu || 30 ||
[31]
svato'pi mā bhūditi cet yadi bhāso na sarvathā | yuktametat prakāśastu sannāstyasmānna kiṃ svataḥ || 31 ||
[32]
prakāśo'sti na tu svasmādato'nyasmāt kathaṃ na cet | anyathā bādhakaṃ yadvat tadvannāsti svato matau || 32 ||
[33]
svātmanyatha kriyārodho dhārayoḥ svacchidā na hi | dhārāpi tīkṣṇā svayamityucyate kiṃ na sūriṇā || 33 ||
[34]
svahetoreva tīkṣṇā sā jāyate nānyato yadi | prakāśarūpajñānaṃ ca svahetoreva jāyate || 34 ||
[35]
upakāryopakāritvakṛtaṃ mā bhūt prakāśanam | tadrūpajanma rūpaṃ tu svayaṃśabdena śabditam || 35 ||
[36]
yathā pradīpapaṭayorupakārāt prakāśanam | dṛṣṭaṃ tathā pradīpasya svayaṃ kiṃ na samīkṣitam || 36 ||
[37]
akṣāpekṣāpi dīpe cet sā kumbhe kiṃ na vidyate | tatsattve'pi ghaṭo dīpaṃ dīpo nānyamapekṣate || 37 ||
[38]
yatnādau satyapi yathā parapreraṇavāraṇāt | svayaṃgamoktistajjātivāraṇaiva svabhāsane || 38 ||
[39]
āgame'pi svayaṃvitterbādhe ca pratibhāti yā | grāhyagrāhakabhāvasya sūkṣmasya tadapohanam || 39 ||
[40]
ekatra phalahetutvaṃ yathāśaṅkya nivāritam | grāhyagrāhakataikatra tathāśaṅkya nivāritā || 40 ||
[41]
na karmakartṛbhāvena svaprakāśamato matam | parānapekṣya bhāsantu svahetoruditaṃ manaḥ || 41 ||
[42]
sandhinirmocane vyaktaṃ tadarthapratipādanāt | arthābhāsapravṛttyādivacanairapi sūcanāt || 42 ||
[43]
tasmānna yuktyāgamayoḥ pratibodhi svavedanam | doṣaḥ sa evānyavidaṃ bādhate'gniriva drumam || 43 ||
[44]
na ca svavittivyāpāraṃ paravittigraho'rthitaḥ | yato'sya guṇadoṣābhyāṃ svavitteravalepanam || 44 ||
[45]
doṣo na sattāmātreṇa vyāpāreṇa tu sa smṛtaḥ | akāryakṛtikālasthā nigrāhyā kṣmādayo na hi || 45 ||
[46]
na svavitterato doṣaḥ paravittestu vistarāt | tadanyavittivyāvṛttaḥ prakāśo niyataḥ svayam || 46 ||
[47]
na svato nāpi parato bhāsaśced bhāsa eva na | nāloṣṭādisamānasya vaktumetacca sāmpratam || 47 ||
[48]
svato'nyataśca vyāvṛttāvapi bhāso yadīṣyate | ekānekaviyogo'pi vastunaḥ sattvamastu vaḥ || 48 ||
[49]
ekānekaviyoge'pi yadi vastu sadiṣyate | svato'nyataścābhāve'pi bhāvo bhāsasya kiṃ na vaḥ || 49 ||
[50]
bhāsamānāstathāpyete na bhāvāḥ śakyanihnavāḥ | asādhāraṇabhāsattvāt jñānatvaṃ ca bhaviṣyati || 50 ||
[51]
rūpanirbhāsato'dhyakṣarūpatāpyasti vāstavī | na ca svavittau doṣaścetyataḥ kiñcinna duṣyati || 51 ||
[52]
nanu svavittirnīlasyetyetadeva kuto bhavet | na hīdamekamātmānaṃ vetti yena svavedanam || 52 ||
[53]
antaḥ śātādirūpasya bahiḥ śītaśitādinaḥ | bhāsanāt kasya kenāstu kathaṃ vittirna caikatā || 53 ||
[54]
bhāsanaṃ tāvadastyeṣāṃ tanniṣeddhuṃ na śakyate | na bhede tacca yuktaṃ cedabhedo'stu dhiyastadā || 54 ||
[55]
bhinnākṛtīnāmeteṣāmabhedo'pi kathaṃ bhavet | tatkimiṣṭo dvayābhāvo bhāva eva dvayasya vā || 55 ||
[56]
bhedo'bhedo dvidhā'dvedhā dhīrūpe'stu yathā tathā | nālīkatvaṃ prakāśasya bādhagandhavirodhinaḥ || 56 ||
[57]
na hi svānubhavasyāsti bādhaḥ kvāpyupapattibhiḥ | sa eva tāsāṃ prabhavo niṣṭhā tatraiva vā yataḥ || 57 ||
[58]
bhedādireva cintyo'stu na prakāśasya vāraṇam | yatra prakāśaviśrāmaḥ svaḥ paro vā sa eva san || 58 ||
[59]
sattve ca svavidaḥ siddhe kimekānekacintayā | tadabhāvādabhāvena tasyāḥ kila phalasthitiḥ || 59 ||
[60]
prakāśamātre siddhe'pi svavittiḥ kathamucyate | tāvatā cārthasaṃsiddhau kiṃ svavittigirāpi naḥ || 60 ||
[61]
pratyakṣabādhā hi parapratijñā yā vivakṣitā | svarūpasya pareṇāpi prakāśe sā ca sidhyati || 61 ||
[62]
svarūpasākṣātkaraṇādadhyakṣatvaṃ na cāparam | pareṇāpi prakāśasya rūpaṃ tāvad vibhāti tat || 62 ||
[63]
tathāpi svavidastyeva kiṃ tu svasyeti na svayam | bādhāsiddhau tathānyena vittivāde'pi na kṣatiḥ || 63 ||
[64]
na siddhāparavittiśca svavittiśca na sidhyati | tataḥ pratyakṣatā nāma kīdṛśī bādhanaṃ yayā || 64 ||
[65]
sākṣātkārasvarūpasya pratyakṣatvamudīritam | viśeṣalakṣaṇasyāpi naiva kṣatiraniścaye || 65 ||
[66]
sāmānyena viśeṣāṇāṃ yathā vyāptistathāsya taiḥ | siddhe viśeṣaṃ sāmānyaṃ sāmānye'nyataraḥ sa ca || 66 ||
[67]
manuṣyaniścaye bhāvyaṃ śūriṇā vā'pareṇa vā | na ca taddvayasandehe manuṣyasya parābhavaḥ || 67 ||
[68]
niścite taddvayābhāve bhavenmānuṣyakakṣatiḥ | kiṃ tu mānuṣyake'siddhe siddhe vā na dvayakṣatiḥ || 68 ||
[69]
parokṣe vastuni tato dvidhābhāsakṣatisthitau | bhāsabhraṃśo'stu niśceyo bhāse tvekā sthitirdvayoḥ || 69 ||
[70]
na prakāśe'sti sandehaḥ sandehastu bhidābhidoḥ | bhidābhidoranyatarā prakāśe'vaśyamanvitā || 70 ||
[71]
bhedābhedasthitiryadvadupapattimapekṣate | naivaṃ prakāśo'pekṣāyāṃ prakāśaḥ kathamucyate || 71 ||
[72]
dvābhyāṃ vyāptiḥ prakāśasya syāccedekasthitirdvayoḥ | vyāptiśca na kvacit siddhā tathāpyakṣatirīritā || 72 ||
[73]
nābhinnena na bhinnena vedanena vidityataḥ | kathaṃ pratyakṣabādheti vyāptāvevedamapyalam || 73 ||
[74]
upapādyaṃ samakṣatvamatha ced bādhyavādinā | abhyupetapramāṇasya pratyakṣaṃ kīdṛśaṃ param || 74 ||
[75]
vyāpakānupalambhe'pi rūpatrayanirūpaṇe | pāramparyeṇa sākṣād vāpekṣāvaśyaṃ samakṣadhīḥ || 75 ||
[76]
tatra kīdṛk samakṣaṃ te yadyasmākaṃ na vidyate | tat sāṃvṛtaṃ ced bādhāpi sāṃvṛtādastu siddhivat || 76 ||
[77]
rūpāptau sāṃvṛtaṃ śaktaṃ na bādha iti kaḥ kramaḥ | yajjātikaṃ ca tatsiddhau tajjātyevāstu bādhakam || 77 ||
[78]
sāṃvṛtatvaṃ ca mānasya meyasya yadi saṃvṛteḥ | adyāpi cintyate saiva na siddhā sādhanaṃ katham || 78 ||
[79]
anyasyāsaṃvido'nyena yadi vyāptigraho hatiḥ | vipluto'nyagrahaścāstu svavitteḥ kiyatī kṣatiḥ || 79 ||
[80]
anupetapramāṇasya jyāyasī mūkataiva yat | bruvatā niyataṃ kiñcid bādhyaṃ vā sādhyameva vā || 80 ||
[81]
saṃvṛto mānamiṣṭaṃ ced vicāro'pyeṣa saṃvṛtiḥ | saṃvṛtāvapi neṣṭaṃ ced bruvan jetā yathātathā || 81 ||
[82]
na ca hetau prakāśādāvapyevaṃ bādhasaṃbhavaḥ | asādhāraṇanirbhāsavyatyayasyāprasādhanāt || 82 ||
[83]
amunāpi samakṣeṇa viṣayīkṛtimātrakam | na sattāsiddhirasyeti bādhakāvasaro na kim || 83 ||
[84]
vidhisādhanamānena viṣayīkaraṇātparam | na sattāsādhanaṃ kvāpi śaktiḥ sattā tu laukikī || 84 ||
[85]
sarvatra mānavihite sattābhedasya sādhanam | yuktaṃ nāśādivat sattābādhakaṃ tu virudhyate || 85 ||
[86]
tasmāt svaṃ vā paraṃ vā syāt pratyakṣaṃ viṣayasya tu | yasya svarūpanirbhāsaḥ sa evādhyakṣagocaraḥ || 86 ||
[87]
tadatadrūpavimatāvapi bodhyavapuḥ sthiram | jñānajñeyopanayanādeva sādhakabādhakam || 87 ||
[88]
na svarūpeṇa rūpaṃ tu gaveṣyaṃ bhrāntiśāntaye | pratibhāsini rūpe ca na bhrānterasti saṃbhavaḥ || 88 ||
[89]
kalpanāpoḍhamevāstu kimabhrāntapadaṃ tadā | bhrāntidvaividhyanirvāhanirbandho'pi mudheti cet || 89 ||
[90]
satyamācāryadignāgapādena kṛtameva tat | vārtike tu kṛtaṃ lokasyākāre bāhyaropaṇāt || 90 ||
[91]
ākāramākāratayā śuktiṃ śuktitayā tathā | yadi vidyājjanaḥ kvāpi kathaṃ syāt kasyacit bhramaḥ || 91 ||
[92]
atadātmani tādātmyavyavasāyastadā dvayoḥ | vikalpavarjanenaiva nivartya iti yujyate || 92 ||
[93]
yadā tvarthagraho jñānasyākāre sarvadehinām | dṛṣṭo'tispaṣṭavicchinnapratibhāse viśeṣataḥ || 93 ||
[94]
tadā mṛṣārthagrahaṇaṃ tadadhyakṣamakalpanāt | prāptaṃ gṛhītagrahavat taddvitīyaṃ viśeṣaṇam || 94 ||
[95]
lokabuddhimapekṣyaiva sataimiramitīritam | spaṣṭābhasyāsya kalpatvamohāpohāya cāparam || 95 ||
[96]
tat tattvacintāvasare kalpitāpekṣayaiva sā | bhramavyavasthā spaṣṭābhe na svākāravyapekṣayā || 96 ||
[97]
bhramatvamavikalpe'pi vikalpānna tataḥ param | ato vikalpe viśrāntamavikalpe'pi kathyate || 97 ||
[98]
vikalpakasya bhrāntatve bhramo'nyaḥ syānna vā bhavet | vikalpakasyābhrāntatve bhrama eva na vidyate || 98 ||
antaraślokau ||
[99]
nirbhāsinaḥ samakṣatvamasatyatvamapohati | ataḥ prakāśe mithyātvamarthasyaiva na dhītanoḥ || 99 ||
[100]
tasmānmāne bhidābhedavivāde'pi prakāśinaḥ | pratyakṣagocarāvasthā siddhā sattvaṃ tadeva ca || 100 ||
[101]
taccitrametadadvaitaṃ grāhyādivirahānmatam | sāṃvṛtī puṃvadekākhyānekavyavahṛtirmudhā || 101 ||
[102]
yāvadeva bahiradhyavasāyastāvadeva pṛthagetadidaṃ ca | tanmatistu sakaleti sa eva jñānapāṇicaraṇādirasau hi || 102 ||
[103]
nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk | aśakyadarśanastaṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || 103 ||
[104]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānubhūyate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākārasya cetasaḥ || 104 ||
saṃgrahaślokau ||
[105]
citravijñāna ityābhyāmekānekātyayaḥ kramāt | jñānopādhitayā bādhyaṃ vivicyāśakyadṛktayā || 105 ||
[106]
mudhānekadhvanistaṃ hītyādinā śeṣasaṃgrahaḥ | yad yathetyādinā yuktirekasaṃjñā tadekatā || 106 ||
[107]
pratyakṣānumayornāpi virodhe śaktisaṃśayaḥ | akṣāpekṣānumā nityaṃ nānumāpekṣamakṣajam || 107 ||
[108]
parihṛtya yathādhyakṣavirodhamanumodayaḥ | tathānumāvirodhaṃ na parihṛtyākṣasaṃbhavaḥ || 108 ||
[109]
parokṣe cānumānyatra virodha iti kaḥ kramaḥ | akṣeṇa bādhyate ko'rtho neyaṃ tadgocare pramā || 109 ||
[110]
svātmasattāsthitāvakṣādanumānād guṇāntaram | pratthakṣeṇāvyavahṛteḥ parokṣatvavyavasthiteḥ || 110 ||
[111]
tato'dhyakṣāntareṇāpi nānumāyāstulā kvacit | svasaṃvittyā tu yat siddhaṃ tatra cintaiva kīdṛśī || 111 ||
[112]
svavittirevāparamānayonirna cet pramāṇaṃ kimiha pramāṇam | atastayā sādhitabādhiteṣu na bādhasiddhyoraparasya śaktiḥ || 112 ||
antaraślokaḥ ||
[113]
ekānekātyaye'pyasmāt sphurataḥ kena vāraṇam | na ca tābhyāṃ sthitivyāptiḥ pratyakṣeṇaiva bādhanāt || 113 ||
[114]
lakṣaṇasya kriyākāle vyāptivicca hatāmunā | bahirevaiṣa niyamaḥ sāmarthyādavatiṣṭhate || 114 ||
[115]
dvaite'pi na bahirdharmaḥ sarvaḥ sādhāraṇo dhiyaḥ | sthairyāsthairyavadadvaite syānna yadyeṣa na kṣatiḥ || 115 ||
[116]
pūrvāparatayā vyāptaṃ sthairyādi na tadatyaye | ekānekatayāvyāptiḥ sthiterbuddhau na saṃvidaḥ || 116 ||
[117]
vyāptirevātha tadapi sattvādastyekamenayoḥ | sarvākārāvasāyo hi na pratyakṣe'pi vastuni || 117 ||
[118]
bhāsamāne ca nīlādau bhāsa eva samakṣadhīḥ | tato bhedo'tha nirbhedaśaṅkā pītādinaḥ punaḥ || 118 ||
[119]
tatrāpi vyatinirbhāsādevābhedavyavasthitiḥ | bhede hi bhedasantānajñānavanna prakāśanam || 119 ||
[120]
upādānābhido'nyonyaṃ prakāśa iti cedasat | upādānābhidapyeṣāṃ na hi bhedamapohati || 120 ||
[121]
pratyāsattiryadapyasti grahaṇārthastu ko bhavet | saiva cet sphuraṇaṃ sākṣāt na bhavet saiva hi prathā || 121 ||
[122]
tadbalācca grahe hetuphalayoḥ kiṃ na vedanam | sānnidhyatāratamyaṃ tu tatraivaitadapekṣayā || 122 ||
[123]
parasparagrahārtho'tra sāhityasphuraṇaṃ yadi | āsannadeśasphuraṇamagrahe'pi mitho na kim || 123 ||
[124]
tasmānna citrabhāsaḥ syāt saṃstu na kṣamate bhidām | anyonyasaṃvidāveśāt svabhāvābhedalakṣaṇāt || 124 ||
[125]
citrādeva sadotpattāvekopādānatāpi kā | na saṅkocadaśāyāmapyekāntāccitraniścayaḥ || 125 ||
[126]
yāvacca janma citrasya citrādevopalabhyate | bhinnopādānatā tāvat kṣamate na mithaḥ prathām || 126 ||
[127]
upādānasya yadi ca citrasyāpyekatāsthitiḥ | upādeyasya kiṃ neti citrādvaitamabādhitam || 127 ||
[128]
kathaṃ vā nīlamapyekamathāṇupratibhāsanam | tato'nekasthitibhraṃśe kena kasya sthiraikatā || 128 ||
[129]
ekānekatvaviraho'pyata eveti cenmatiḥ | astu sattvasya bādhā tu na śakyeti niveditam || 129 ||
[130]
etattu prakṛtaṃ bhede yuktaṃ nānyonyabhāsanam | upādānābhido nāma nottarasya balaṃ yataḥ || 130 ||
tasmāt,
[131]
sahopalambhaniyamādabhedo nīlapītayoḥ | svabhāvo hi tayoḥ saṃvidabhinneti bhidā kutaḥ || 131 ||
[132]
saṃvittiniyamo nāsti bhinnayornīlapītayoḥ | itthamarthe patet puṃbhyāmekaikasyāpi darśanāt || 132 ||
tadāha,
[133]
nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk | aśakyadarśanastaṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || 133 ||
[134]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānubhūyate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākāre'pi cetasi || 134 ||
[135]
bāhyavanna hi bodhe'pi puṃsorekaikadarśanam | yato'nyathāpi grahaṇānniyamasya parāhatiḥ || 135 ||
[136]
bhāsate yadyadekaṃ tad yathā citre sitākṛtiḥ | bhāsate cākhilaṃ citraṃ pītaśītasukhādikam || 136 ||
[137]
ekābhimataboddhāramapekṣyedamudīritam | nānaikāntikatā tasmāt santānāntarabhāsinā || 137 ||
[138]
dṛṣṭānte sādhyaśūnyatvaṃ na viparyayabādhakāt | bhāsaḥ sthūlatayā vyāpto na hyasāvaṇuśo bhidi || 138 ||
[139]
ekaikāṇunimagnatvāt saṃvittirna parasparam | na caikāṇuprakāśo'sti sthūlameva sphuratyataḥ || 139 ||
[140]
bāhyāṇūnāṃ pratībhāso buddhirekā sthavīyasī | jñānāṇūnāṃ ka ekastu pratibhāso bhaviṣyati || 140 ||
[141]
anekatrāpyavayavinyekā citrākṛtirmatiḥ | khaṇḍaśo vyavahārāya sādhvī buddhau tu kā gatiḥ || 141 ||
[142]
ekatrāpyaṃśini mitiḥ sākāraikā prasādhitā | vyavahāro'nyathā neti sthaulyaṃ jñānasya dustyajam || 142 ||
[143]
tasmāt sthūlatayā vyāpto nirbhāsastannivṛttitaḥ | nivartamāno'nekasmādekatve vinayasya te || 143 ||
[144]
yathā sajātīyamatād bhāgād bhedanirākriyā | anābhāsaprasaṅgena vijātīyamatāttathā || 144 ||
[145]
tannāstu sādhyo dṛṣṭānto na cāśaṅkāviparyaye | sādhyasyādhyakṣabādhāpi nādhyakṣasyāpratiṣṭhiteḥ || 145 ||
[146]
na mānamanyagrahaṇaṃ na bhedagrāhikā svavit | bhinnamasmādidamiti vikalpo vāsanānvayaḥ || 146 ||
[147]
yathā bāhyaṃ svato bhinnaṃ svatantraḥ kalpayatyayam | bāhyaṃ bāhyāntarādbhinnaṃ tathā kalpayati svayam || 147 ||
[148]
bāhye satyapi nānyasmādadhyakṣaṃ bhedavedanam | anyasyāpi grahaprāptestadviśiṣṭātmano grahāt || 148 ||
[149]
asmādbhinnamitīdaṃ cet svarūpaṃ grāhyavastunaḥ | sāvadherasya bhāsaḥ syānna vā grāhyaṃ tadātmanā || 149 ||
[150]
vināvadhiṃ pratīto hi bhedo'bhedaḥ kathaṃ na saḥ | bhedopacāramātraṃ syānna bhedastattvatastataḥ || 150 ||
[151]
parāsaṃkīrṇarūpasya grahaṇaṃ kila bhedavit | parāsaṃkīrṇamanyasmād bhinnamekārthamīdṛśam || 151 ||
[152]
na tvanyasaṃkīrṇagatāvanyasyāpyucito grahaḥ | anyāgrahe tvakīrṇasya kevalasyāgrahaḥ katham || 152 ||
[153]
kevalo yata evāyaṃ bhāti tenaiva nānyayuk | anyasyāpi prakāśe hi gṛhītaḥ kevalaḥ katham || 153 ||
[154]
kevalasya graho na syādanyasya sphuraṇe yathā | anyasyāsphuraṇe'pyevaṃ parāmiśro hi kevalaḥ || 154 ||
[155]
amiśro'yaṃ pareṇeti vivarto manaso yathā | tathaiva yadyanubhavaḥ paradhīḥ kena vāryate || 155 ||
[156]
parihṛtya paraṃ tāto yathā miśragraho na san | parihṛtya paraṃ tātastathā bhinnagraho na san || 156 ||
[157]
vastumātragrahastasmādadhyakṣeṇeti yujyate | na bhinnaṃ nāpi cābhinnaṃ grahītuṃ tena śakyate || 157 ||
[158]
na bhedyabhāsādavadherjñātaṃ nābhedyaśaṅkarāt | nānyacca bhedābhedābhyāṃ vastu vastugrahaḥ katham || 158 ||
[159]
sarvamarthāvyatibhidi jñānādapi bhidā kutaḥ | bhede cāvadhimāne'pi sarvaḥ sarvasya gocaraḥ || 159 ||
[160]
kiṃ tu bāhyagrahāveśe cintāyāṃ dūṣaṇaṃ samam | yathā bhedagrahāniṣṭau tathā satyavadhigrahe || 160 ||
[161]
tasmād bāhyagrahaścakṣunirmīlyāstu yathā tathā | bhedāgrahaṃ tvanuvadan tattvavid bādhyatāṃ katham || 161 ||
[162]
nādhyakṣaṃ bhedakṛt kalpaṃ taskarastviha tatkaraḥ | sa svāparādhamadhyakṣe kṣipatīti bhidaḥ sthitiḥ || 162 ||
[163]
nīlādiva tadekaṃ ca kathametat sametu cet | nīlamaṃśāntaraṃ caikamiti kiṃ bhāti saṅgatam || 163 ||
[164]
naikaṃ tadapi cet tarhi kvāṇuto bhidi bhāsanam | na parīkṣākṣamaścāṇuḥ kutaḥ kasya tadā bhidā || 164 ||
[165]
mā bhūdavastuto vā cet so'pyekatvahatau bhavet | nirbhāsādekatāsiddhau svavittervastutā sthitā || 165 ||
[166]
atha deśavitānāptirnāmāntaraviyoginaḥ | na deśabhānahānau ca bhāsa ityapi śakyate || 166 ||
[167]
na svātmāntaramanyātmā sa bāhyasyaiva yujyate | buddheḥ svavittiniṣṭhāyā yaḥ parastasya kā gatiḥ || 167 ||
[168]
bhinno'pi deśabhedena bāhyārtho gṛhyate dhiyā | dhīstu deśabhidā bhinnā kenāstu vyavahārabhāk || 168 ||
[169]
sthūladeśāpi tenaikyānna buddhirbhedamarhati | yathā na bhedo'syābhede bhedakastadvadākṛteḥ || 169 ||
[170]
citraṃ tadekamiti cedidaṃ citrataraṃ tataḥ | tataścitratamaṃ cedaṃ yadbhede vedanaṃ mithaḥ || 170 ||
[171]
citraikabuddhinirbhāse bāhyaḥ syād vā na vā bhavet | anābhāsaprasaṅge'syā na bāhyāni na buddhayaḥ || 171 ||
[172]
aṇutve tadabhāve vā na dhībhāsasya saṅgatiḥ | tasmādaṇutvābhāvābhyāṃ viruddhaṃ bhāsanaṃ dhiyaḥ || 172 ||
tadāha,
[173]
nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk | aśakyadarśanastaṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || 173 ||
[174]
yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaivānugamyate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākārasya cetasaḥ || 174 ||
[175]
jñānatvena viśiṣṭo'yaṃ nīlādiścitravedane | mithaḥ svarūpānāpanno'sthūlo draṣṭuṃ na śakyate || 175 ||
[176]
bhedasya pratthaṇu prāpternīlādi caya eva vā | aśakyo draṣṭumudita ekaikasya grahād dhiyā || 176 ||
[177]
anekākāra eko'ta eṣṭavyo'nubhavo yataḥ | asmādidaṃ bhinnamiti prakalpayati pṛṣṭajam || 177 ||
[178]
ata eva ca nīlādi bhindannartha vivecayet | na buddhirūpaṃ tadbhede na jñānaṃ na ca gocaraḥ || 178 ||
[179]
tasmād yena prakāreṇa karaṇena cakāsti dhīḥ | sthūlaikatvena tenaiva viśiṣṭā sopagamyate || 179 ||
[180]
viruddhadharmādhyāsaśca tatra bhedāya kalpate | yatrādhyakṣakṛto bhedo vyavahāraprasādhanāt || 180 ||
[181]
svayaṃ vedanamevātra pratyakṣaṃ na ca tadbhide | nīlāditve vikalpo'nuvartakastasya no bhidi || 181 ||
[182]
nirbhāsabhedād bhedaścet sa evākāra ucyate | bahirmeye pramāṇaṃ sa tatra meye svavit pramā || 182 ||
[183]
svavidekīkṛtasyāsya bhedād bhinnaṃ kathaṃ bahiḥ | yathā dhiyo'kṣād grahaṇaṃ svavidā bhedanaṃ tathā || 183 ||
[184]
sphuraṇaṃ pratibhāsaścet sā svavinna ca vidyate | meyabhūtākṛto bhedāvasāyo hanyate vidā || 184 ||
[185]
adhyakṣameva hi bhinatti śiteḥ sitaṃ cet tadbhidyamānamathavābhidameva bhindyāt | bhede'nyaleśamapi neti kuto bhinattu bhindyādabhedi mana ityapi kasya śakyam || 185 ||
[136]
bāhyaṃ na naśyati bhidāṇutayāpyabhede tvarthakriyāvirahasaṃkarato'śumātram | buddhistu naśyati bhidaiva vidaiva sattāccitrāpyato na bhidameti kimatra kurmaḥ || 186 ||
[187]
bhedastathāpyabudha buddhyanurodhataśced etāvatāpi tava heturasiddha eva | ekatvahāniratha buddhyanurodhabādho bādhastu nastadapi neti paroktametat || 187 ||
antaraślokāḥ ||
[188]
ekānekatayā vastuvyāptiḥ siddhā yadi kvacit | sarvaśūnyatvasamaye heturiṣṭavighātakṛt || 188 ||
[189]
atha lokaprasiddhau ca na sarvaṃ lokakalpitam | tattvavyavasthā śaraṇaṃ kiṃ tu mānena saṅgatam || 189 ||
[190]
na cādhyakṣānumānābhyāmanaṃśaṃ kvacidīkṣitam | yasya rāśiranekaṃ syānnāpi vastu ca kiñcana || 190 ||
[191]
sthūlamekaikamadhyakṣaṃ naikānekaṃ vyavasyati | vastutastu kimekaṃ tat nānā vā ko'tra niścayaḥ || 191 ||
[192]
na cānyopagamaḥ sādhuḥ svatantre sādhane satām | na prasaṅge ca mukhyārthaḥ tathātve ca matakṣatiḥ || 192 ||
[193]
yasya caikataratvābhyāṃ sattvavyāptiḥ sa hanyatām | abhrāntavittimātreṇa sattāvādī tu jitvaraḥ || 193 ||
[194]
sarvatra hetau vyāptistu pramāsiddhimapekṣate | vyāpakānupalambhādau sā ca jñeyā viparyaye || 194 ||
[195]
mānasiddhaṃ na ca vyāptivyāpyaṃ nopagataṃ svayam | paravit paravittyaiva bādhyate tviti kīrtitam || 195 ||
[196]
na ca svabhāvasvīkāro'vaśyamekādikarṣakaḥ | vyāpterasiddheradyāpi pramāṇavyāhataṃ ca tat || 196 ||
[197]
pramāṇavyastarūpeṇa vyāptimādāya taddhateḥ | yadi bhāvāsvabhāvatvaṃ kharaśṛṅgātyayānna kim || 197 ||
[198]
ekānekātyayāt tarhi bāhyasyāpi kathaṃ kṣatiḥ | tattvato'nupalambhena grāhyalakṣaṇahānitaḥ || 198 ||
[199]
na cānaśaikatā kiṃ tu vivicyāśabdadarśanam | tacca nāsti bahistasyābhāvatastatsamuccayaḥ || 199 ||
[200]
vivicyāśakyadarśitvamevaikatvamaṇāvapi | citrajñāne tadakṣīṇamaruciḥ kvopayoginī || 200 ||
[201]
buddhau tu citrarūpāyāmaśakyaikavivekadṛk | paracittavivekena tadekānekalakṣaṇam || 201 ||
[202]
tadāha nīlādītyādi sphuṭāto'nyadhiyo'nyatā | sā kuto'numiteḥ sā cet saṃvṛttyāstu yathā tathā || 202 ||
[203]
tathāpi kalpitaṃ nityamapekṣya kṣaṇitā yathā | dṛḍhaprakalpānyamano'pekṣyamekaṃ tathā dhiyaḥ || 203 ||
[204]
tarhyaśakyavivekaikābhāve'pyanyatayā tataḥ | śakyabhedamanekaṃ syād bāhye'pyekacayena kim || 204 ||
[205]
naivaṃ yathāṃśini hate tvaṇureko'vatiṣṭhate | tatastatpracayo'nekastaddoṣādeva dūṣitaḥ || 205 ||
[206]
tathā tatpratirūpe'sminnekānekātyaye kṛte | ekasaṃhatirevāyamaneko vādisaṃmataḥ || 206 ||
[207]
śakyamevamapi khyātumiti bāhyādhikārataḥ | avayavyaṇucintādyakṛtino'bhūtparāśayāt || 207 ||
[208]
yadā ca citrabuddhyaiva bādhakāntarahānitaḥ | ekānekatvayorbādhaḥ siddhiḥ kiṃ na tayā tayoḥ || 208 ||
[209]
ekatve citratābhāvo nānātve sutarāṃ yathā | citratvānnaikatā yadvadekānekasthitistathā || 209 ||
[210]
vinā viruddhopanayānna bādhā pratiyoginaḥ | tathānekahatāvekasvavidantargamād vada || 210 ||
[211]
tathā ca vyāpakābhāvaviplavaḥ syānmatasthiteḥ | asmākaṃ tu na doṣo'yaṃ dvayoścenmānasiddhatā || 211 ||
[212]
sarvāvakārahānena kimekaṃ na samaṃ kvacit | ekatānekatābhyāṃ tat sphurattābhyāṃ tadanvitam || 212 ||
[213]
syānnāma tata ekatvaṃ bhedābhedātmacitrake | athaikasyānyabādhāya sādhanaṃ sthitaye na tu || 213 ||
[214]
tasyāpi bādhanāt paścāt pratyāśā mahatīdṛśī | pramāṇādekasiddhiścet paścād bādhaḥ kathaṃ bhavet || 214 ||
[215]
pramāṇānnaikasiddhiścedanyabādhaḥ kathaṃ bhavet | ekātyayo nānyavidhiḥ syādvirodhaḥ svayaṃ yadi || 215 ||
[216]
vidhiśca citradhīrhanyādviruddhopanayāt param | udīryamāṇaḥ śaktaścedaho prāmāṇikasthitiḥ || 216 ||
[217]
kadāpi nobhayabhraṃśastathāpyekaikasaṃsthitiḥ | kadāpyekatayānekatayā bhāti kadāpi tat || 217 ||
[218]
tathāpi bhāva ekasyāmasiddhirvyāpakacyuteḥ || 218 ||
[219]
arthaśaktyādirūpaṃ ca yadi sattvaṃ niṣidhyate | kā kṣatirbhāsarūpaṃ tu brahmaṇāpi na bādhyate || 219 ||
[220]
bādhane dharmiṇastasya bādhā syādapi na svayam | yathā nīlamidaṃ tadvadbhāti satyaṃ na vā bhavet || 220 ||
[221]
sandehe dharmiṇo dharmasandeha iti cet kutaḥ | tādātmyāt tattvata iti tulyaṃ nāśikatādibhiḥ || 221 ||
[222]
athaikaniścayo'nyatra pravṛttamapi saṃśayaḥ | hanti vyāvṛttibhedena tadapi prastute samam || 222 ||
[223]
pratītireva sattāstu yadā bāhye'pi tattvataḥ | bhāsino dharmiṇastarhi kva bādhā kva ca saṃśayaḥ || 223 ||
[224]
kadācit kenacid dṛṣṭasyānumānatvamanyadā | apātraṃ sarvathā dṛṣṭeḥ pātraṃ kiṃ saditi sthiteḥ || 224 ||
[225]
vikalpa evānumiterabhāve'pi prakāśanam | tādṛśāṃ yādṛśī sattā pratītirapi tādṛśī || 225 ||
[226]
pratītimeva sattāṃ ca sphuṭayan vārtike kṛtī | apratītyaiva bāhyasya vinmātraṃ pratyapīpadat || 226 ||
[227]
tadbhāsamātrarūpeṇa bhātadravyāditā mudhā | citre bhāsaikabhāvaḥ syānna prapañco guṇādibhiḥ || 227 ||
[228]
sthitirhivijñānanaye tāttvikī ca phalāṅgatā | aho nairlajyamathavā sarva hi mahatāṃ mahat || 228 ||
[229]
pūrvāparaparijñāne parajñāne ca tadgrahaḥ | kutaḥ svavittiniṣṭhāyāmubhayasyāpyasaṃbhavāt || 229 ||
[230]
abhāse pūrvaparatājñānaṃ na jñānahānitaḥ | na bhāse pūrvaparatājñānamadvaitasaṃgateḥ || 230 ||
[231]
svaikarūpe dvayābhāvāt svānyayoḥ parayorna vā | phalāṅgabhāvaḥ paravit parihārāttu na dvidhā || 231 ||
[232]
tasmād yathā parajñānaṃ tathā hetuphalasthitiḥ | yathā svavittiviśrāmastathā saṃvṛtisatyasau || 232 ||
[233]
cittamātravyavasthānamanutpādaṃ vadantyataḥ | pratītyotpannatāpyasmādasiddherapyasādhanam || 233 ||
[234]
na ca pratītyotpannatvameva vācyā ca śūnyatā | adharasthitiyugmācca naivaṃ bhedo vṛthā śramaḥ || 234 ||
[235]
anutpannatvamevāstu heturna prācyadūṣaṇāt | hāne'pi hetuphalayoḥ sphuradrūpaṃ kva gacchatu || 235 ||
[236]
tasmāddharmaḥ kalpitaireva rūpaiḥ śūnyaḥ sarvo bhāsabhāgnaiva kaścit | citrādvaitaṃ citracakraṃ tadetad bhāvyaṃ bhāvyairaprapañcaṃ śivāya || 236 ||
[237]
sākṣātkāro na kāmaṃ bhavati bhavabhṛtāṃ yāvadasyā daśāyā heyopādeyasādhyaprabhavaparicayastāvadastyaprakampaḥ | tasmāt saṃbhārayugmābhyasanapariṇatau mūrticetoguṇābhyāṃ yogī yogīśvaro'sau nirupamanilaye labdhabodhiḥ prasiddhaḥ || 237 ||
[238]
yathā suvarṇa guṇarūpasaṃpadaḥ prakarṣaparyantamupetamakṣayam | vimuktamālīkyakalaṅkaśaṅkayā tathaiva bauddhaṃ vapurastu dehinām || 238 ||
